Matthew1:1 Igitabo kidondora ukuvuka kwa Yesu Kristo, umwana wa Dawidi, Dawidi wa Aburahamu." 
Matthew1:2 Aburahamu yavyaye Isaka, Isaka yavyaye Yakobo, Yakobo yavyaye Yuda n’abandi bavukana," 
Matthew1:3 Yuda yavyaye Peresi na Zera kuri Tamari, Peresi yavyaye Hesironi, Hesironi yavyaye Ramu," 
Matthew1:4 Ramu yavyaye Aminadabu, Aminadabu yavyaye Nahasoni, Nahasoni yavyaye Salumoni," 
Matthew1:5 Salumoni yavyaye Bowazi kuri Rahabu, Bowazi yavyaye Obedi kuri Rusi, Obedi yavyaye Isayi," 
Matthew1:6 Isayi yavyaye umwami Dawidi. Dawidi yavyaye Salomo kuri muka Uriya," 
Matthew1:7 Salomo yavyaye Rehobowamu, Rehobowamu yavyaye Abiya, Abiya yavyaye Asa," 
Matthew1:8 Asa yavyaye Yehoshafati, Yehoshafati yavyaye Yoramu, Yoramu yavyaye Uziya," 
Matthew1:9 Uziya yavyaye Yotamu, Yotamu yavyaye Ahazi, Ahazi yavyaye Hezekiya," 
Matthew1:10 Hezekiya yavyaye Manase, Manase yavyaye Amoni, Amoni yavyaye Yosiya," 
Matthew1:11 Yosiya yavyaye Yekoniya n’abandi bavukana, mu gihe co kwambukanwa i Babuloni." 
Matthew1:12 Kuva mu gihe co kwambukanwa i Babuloni Yekoniya yavyaye Shalutiyeli, Shalutiyeli yavyaye Zerubabeli," 
Matthew1:13 Zerubabeli yavyaye Abihudi, Abihudi yavyaye Eliyakimu, Eliyakimu yavyaye Azori," 
Matthew1:14 Azori yavyaye Sadoki, Sadoki yavyaye Akimu, Akimu yavyaye Elihudi," 
Matthew1:15 Elihudi yavyaye Eleyazari, Eleyazari yavyaye Matani, Matani yavyaye Yakobo," 
Matthew1:16 Yakobo yavyaye Yosefu, umugabo wa Mariya nyina wa Yesu yitwa Kristo." 
Matthew1:17 Nuko ba sekuruza bose guhera kuri Aburahamu gushitsa kuri Dawidi n’icumi na bane, kandi guhera kuri Dawidi gushitsa ku gihe co kwambukanwa i Babuloni n’icumi na bane, kandi guhera ku gihe co kwambukanwa i Babuloni gushitsa kuri Kristo n’icumi na bane nyene." 
Matthew1:18 Ukuvuka kwa Yesu Kristo kwabaye gurtya: nyina Mariya yar’ akowe na Yosefu ataramurongora bamubona afise inda yavuye kuri Mpwemu Yera. 
Matthew1:19 Ariko Yosefu, umugabo wiwe, kukw ar’ umugororotsi, kandi kukw atagomvye kumutetereza, yiyumvira kumubengera mu mpisho." 
Matthew1:20 Akivyiyumvira, umumarayika w’Umwami Imana amwiyerekera mu nzozi, aramubarira, ati Yosefu, mwana wa Dawidi, ntutinye kurongora Mariya umugeni wawe, kukw atwaye inda ya Mpwemu Yera." 
Matthew1:21 Azovyara umwana w’umuhungu, nawe uz’ umwite YESU, kukw ari we azokiza abantu biwe ivyaha vyabo." 
Matthew1:22 Ivyo vyose vyabaye birtyo ngw ivyo Umwami Imana yavugiye mu kanwa k’uwavugishwa na we biboneke," 
Matthew1:23 ngo Rāba, inkumi izotwara inda, ivyare umwana w’umuhungu, Bazomwita Imanuweli; risobanurwa ngw Imana iri kumwe natwe." 
Matthew1:24 Yosefu yikanguye aravyuka, agira nk’uk’ umumarayika w’Umwami Imana yamubariye, arongora umugeni wiwe." 
Matthew1:25 Kandi ntiyigera amwēgēra gushitsa aho yavyariye umwana w’umuhungu; araheza amwita YESU. 
Matthew2:1 Yesu amaze kuvukira i Betelehemu mu gihugu c’i Yudaya ku ngoma y’umwami Herode, haza abanyabgenge bavuye i burasirazuba, baja i Yerusalemu," 
Matthew2:2 barabaza, bat’ Umwami w’Abayuda yavutse ari hehe? Kuko twābonye inyenyeri yiwe, tur’ i burasirazuba, none tukaba tuzanywe no kumushengerera." 
Matthew2:3 Umwami Herode avyumvise, ahagarikana umutima n’ab’i Yerusalemu bose." 
Matthew2:4 Akoranya abaherezi bakuru n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe bose bo mur’ ubgo bgoko, arababaza, ati Kristo azovukira hehe?" 
Matthew2:5 Bati N’i Betelehemu mu gihugu c’i Yudaya, ni ko vyanditswe n’umuntu yavugishwa n’Imana," 
Matthew2:6 ngo Kandi wewe, Betelehemu mu ntāra ya Yuda, Nturi mutoya mu baganwa ba Yuda, Kuko kuri wewe hazova ūganza, Ni we azoragira abantu banje b’Abisirayeli." 
Matthew2:7 Buno Herode ahamagaza ba banyabgenge mu mpisho, abasiguza igihe iyo nyenyeri yabonekeye." 
Matthew2:8 Abatuma i Betelehemu, ati Mugende, mubaze mushirutse umwete ivy’ uwo mwana. Ni mwamubona muce muza kumbarira, ngo nanje nze kumushengerera." 
Matthew2:9 Na bo bumvise iry’ umwami, baragenda. Maz’ iyo nyenyeri bābonye i burasirazuba irabarōngōra, irinda ishika hejuru y’ah’ uwo mwana ari, ihagararaho." 
Matthew2:10 Babonye iyo nyenyeri banezerwa akaneza kenshi cane. 
Matthew2:11 Bashitse mu nzu babona uwo mwana na Mariya nyina wiwe; bikubita hasi, baramupfukamira, barumūra ibisimbo vyabo, bamushikanira amashikanwa, izahabu n’imibavu n’isenga." 
Matthew2:12 Babgiriwe n’Imana mu nzozi ngo ntibasubire guca kwa Herode, baca mu yindi nzira, bīsubirira mu gihugu c’i wabo." 
Matthew2:13 Bamaze kugenda, umumarayika w’Umwami Imana yiyerekera Yosefu mu nzozi, aramubgira, ati Vyuka, ujane umwana na nyina, uhungire muri Egiputa, ugumeyo gushitsa aho nzokubaririra, kuko Herode agira arondere umwana ngw amwice." 
Matthew2:14 Ahenga mw ijoro aravyuka, ajana umwana na nyina, aja muri Egiputa," 
Matthew2:15 agumayo gushitsa Herode amaze gutanga, ngw ivyo Umwami Imana yavugiye mu wavugishwa na we bishike, ngo Nahamagaye umwana wanje ngw ave muri Egiputa." 
Matthew2:16 Maze Herode abonye ko yahenzwe n’abo banyabgenge, arajingitwa cane. Atuma kugeseza abana b’abahungu bose b’i Betelehemu no mu misozi yose ihakikije, abamaze imyaka ibiri n’abatarayimara, yagerereje igihe yasigurije abanyabgenge." 
Matthew2:17 Ni ho ivyavuzwe na Yeremiya yavugishwa n’Imana vyashikiye," 
Matthew2:18 ngw Induru yumvikana i Rama, Amarira n’amaborogo menshi; Rakeli aririra abana biwe, Yanka kwīrūrwa, kuko batakiriho." 
Matthew2:19 Herode amaze gutanga, umumarayika w’Umwami Imana yiyerekera Yosefu mu nzozi ari muri Egiputa," 
Matthew2:20 aramubgira, ati Vyuka, ujane umwana na nyina, uje mu gihugu c’i Bgisirayeli, kukw abārondera kwica umwana bāpfuye." 
Matthew2:21 Avyutse, ajana umwana na nyina, aragenda, ashika mu gihugu c’i Bgisirayeli." 
Matthew2:22 Ariko yumvise yuko Arukelayo yimye i Yudaya, asubiye ku ngoma ya se Herode, atinya kujayo. Abgiriwe mu nzozi, aja mu bihugu vy’i Galilaya." 
Matthew2:23 Ashitseyo, agerēra mu gisagara citwa Nazareti, ngw ivyavuzwe n’abāvugishwa n’Imana bishike, ngw Azokwitwa Umunyanazareti." 
Matthew3:1 Mur’ iyo misi haza Yohana Umubatizi, yigishiriza mu bugaragwa bg’i Yudaya," 
Matthew3:2 ati Mwihane, kuk’ ubgami bgo mw ijuru buri hafi." 
Matthew3:3 Uyo ni we yavuzwe na Yesaya yavugishwa n’Imana, at’ Ijwi ry’ūsemererera mu bugaragwa, Ati Ni mutegure inzira y’Uhoraho, Mugorore iz’ ibihamo ziwe." 
Matthew3:4 Yohana uyo, imyambaro yiwe yar’ iy’ ubgoya bg’ingamiya, yayikenyeza umukanda w’urusato mu rukenyerero; indya ziwe zar’ inzige n’ubūki bgo mw ishamba." 
Matthew3:5 Maz’ ab’i Yerusalemu n’ab’i Yudaya bose n’igihugu giherereye kuri Yorodani cose, bava i wabo baza kuri we," 
Matthew3:6 babatizwa na we mu ruzi Yorodani, bātura ivyaha vyabo." 
Matthew3:7 Abonye benshi bo mu Bafarisayo no mu Basadukayo bazanywe no kugira ngw ababatize, arababaza, ati Mwa bana b’inzoka mwe, ni nde yababūriye ngo muhunge uburake buzoza?" 
Matthew3:8 Nuko mwame imbuto zikwiranye n’ukwihana. 
Matthew3:9 Mwoye kwiyumvira mu mitima, muti Dufise Aburahamu, ni we sogokuruza. Ndababgira yukw aya mabuye Imana ishobora kuyavyuramw’ abana ba Aburahamu." 
Matthew3:10 Arikw incabiti igenekerejwe ku bitsina vy’ibiti; nuko rer’ igiti cose kitāma ivyiza kiracibga, kigatererwa mu muriro." 
Matthew3:11 N’ukuri jeho ndababatiza mu mazi ngo mwihane; arik’ ūzoza hanyuma yanje andusha ubushobozi, ntibimbereye no kumutwaza inkweto. Uyo azobabatiza muri Mpwemu Yera no mu muriro." 
Matthew3:12 Urutaro rwiwe ruri mu kuboko kwiwe, kand’ azokubūra imbuga yiwe neza, yimburire ingano ziwe mu kigega, maz’ umuguruka awuturire mu muriro utazima." 
Matthew3:13 Ico gihe Yesu ava i Galilaya, aja kuri Yorodani aje kuri Yohana, azanywe no kubatizwa na we." 
Matthew3:14 Ariko Yohana agomba kumwankira, ati Kw ari jewe nkwiye kubatizwa nawe: non’ uje kuri jewe?" 
Matthew3:15 Yesu aramwishura, ati Bikunde: kukw ari vyo bidukwiye, ngo dushitse ukugororoka kwose. Bun’ aramukundira;" 
Matthew3:16 Yesu amaze kubatizwa, aca ava mu mazi: maz’ ijuru riruguruka, abona Mpwemu w’Imana, amanuka asa n’inuma, amugwako." 
Matthew3:17 Buno rer’ ijwi riva mw ijuru, rit’ Uyu ni we Mwana wanje nkunda, akampimbara." 
Matthew4:1 Buno Yesu adūganwa na Mpwemu mu bugaragwa ngw ageragezwe n’Umurwanizi. 
Matthew4:2 Amaze imisi mirongwine n’amajoro mirongwine yisonzesheje, abona gusonza." 
Matthew4:3 Umugeragezi aza kuri we, ati Ni waba ur’ Umwana w’Imana, bgira aya mabuye acike imitsima." 
Matthew4:4 Aramwishura, ati Vyanditswe ng’ Umuntu ntatungwa n’umutsima gusa, arikw atungwa n’ijambo ryose riva mu kanwa k’Imana." 
Matthew4:5 Bun’ Umurwanizi amujana mu gisagara cera, amuhagarika ku gatwe k’urusengero," 
Matthew4:6 aramubgira, ati Ni waba ur’ Umwana w’Imana, ikororere hasi, kuko vyanditswe, ngw Azokuragiza abamarayika biwe, Na bo bazokuramira mu maboko yabo, Ngo kumbure ntutsitare kw ibuye." 
Matthew4:7 Yesu aramubgira, ati Vyongeye haranditswe, ngo Ntukagerageze Uhoraho, Imana yawe." 
Matthew4:8 Umurwanizi yongera kumujana ku musozi uhagaze cane, amwereka ubgami bgose bgo mw isi n’ubgiza bgabgo," 
Matthew4:9 at’ Ivyo vyose ndabiguha, ni wampfukamira, ukansenga." 
Matthew4:10 Buno Yesu aramubgira, ati Mvako, Satani, kuko vyanditswe, ng’ Uhoraho, Imana yawe, abe ari yo usenga, kand’ abe ari yo usaba yonyene." 
Matthew4:11 Maz’ Umurwanizi aramureka, kand’ abamarayika baraza, baramukorera." 
Matthew4:12 Yumvise ko Yohana yashizwe mw ibohero, aja i Galilaya." 
Matthew4:13 Yimuka i Nazareti, aja kuba i Kaperinawumu hafi y’ikiyaga mu rugabano rwa Zebuloni na Nafutali," 
Matthew4:14 ngw ivyanditswe na Yesaya yavugishwa n’Imana bishike," 
Matthew4:15 ngw Igihugu ca Zebuloni n’igihugu ca Nafutali, Aherekeye ku kiyaga, hakurya ya Yorodani, I Galilaya h’abanyamahanga," 
Matthew4:16 Abantu bāri bicaye mu mwiza, Babonye umuco mwinshi, Kand’ abāri bicaye mu gihugu c’urupfu no mu gitutu carwo, Umuco urasiye kuri bo." 
Matthew4:17 Guhera ubgo, Yesu atangura kwigisha, ati Mwihane, kuk’ ubgami bgo mw ijuru buri hafi." 
Matthew4:18 Aciye i ruhande y’ikiyaga c’i Galilaya, abona abavukana babiri, Simoni yitwa Petero, na Andereya mwene nyina, bariko baraterera urusenga mu kiyaga, kuko bār’ abarovyi." 
Matthew4:19 Arababgira, ati Ni munkurikire, nzobagira abaroba abantu." 
Matthew4:20 Baca bareka insenga, baramukurikira." 
Matthew4:21 Yīgiye imbere yaho, abona abavukana bandi babiri, Yakobo mwene Zebedayo, na mwene nyina Yohana, bari kumwe na se Zebedayo mu bgato, bariko barasana insenga zabo, arabahamagara." 
Matthew4:22 Baca bareka ubgato na se, baramukurikira." 
Matthew4:23 Yesu agendagenda i Galilaya hose, yigisha mu masinagogi yabo, ababgira ubutumwa bgiza bg’ubgami, akiza indwara n’ubumuga vy’uburyo bgose mu bantu." 
Matthew4:24 Inkuru yiwe ikwira i Siriya hose, bamuzanira abarwaye bose bātewe n’indwara zitari zimwe n’ibibasheshereje, n’abinjiwemwo n’abadayimoni, n’abarwaye intandara, n’ibimuga; arabakiza." 
Matthew4:25 Kand’ ishengero ryinshi riramukurikira bavuye i Galilaya n’i Dekapoli n’i Yerusalemu n’i Yudaya no hakurya ya Yorodani. 
Matthew5:1 Abonye iryo shengero, adūga umusozi. Amaze kwicara, abigishwa biwe baramwēgēra." 
Matthew5:2 Yanzika kuvuga, arabigisha," 
Matthew5:3 ati Hahirwa aboro mu mitima yabo, kuk’ ubgami bgo mw ijuru ar’ ubgabo." 
Matthew5:4 Hahirwa abatuntuye, kukw ari bo bazokwirurwa." 
Matthew5:5 Hahirwa abatekereza, kukw ari bo bazoragwa isi." 
Matthew5:6 Hahirwa abafise inzara n’inyota vyo kugororoka, kukw ari bo bazohāzwa." 
Matthew5:7 Hahirwa abagira imbabazi, kukw ari bo bazozigirirwa." 
Matthew5:8 Hahirwa abafise imitima itanduye, kukw ari bo bazobona Imana." 
Matthew5:9 Hahirwa ababanguranya, kukw ari bo bazokwitwa abana b’Imana." 
Matthew5:10 Hahirwa abahamwa bahōrwa ukugororoka, kuk’ ubgami bgo mw ijuru ar’ ubgabo." 
Matthew5:11 Namwe muzoba muhiriwe aho bazobatuka bakabahama bakabarementaniriza ibibi vyose babampōye. 
Matthew5:12 Munezerwe, muhimbarwe, kukw impēra zanyu ari nyinshi mw ijuru: kukw ari ko bāhama abāvugishwa n’Imana ba mbere." 
Matthew5:13 Mur’ umunyu w’isi. Arik’ umunyu, iy’ ushize uburyohe, uba ukiryoshwa n’iki? Nta co uba ukimaze atar’ ugutabga hanze ugakandagirwa n’abantu." 
Matthew5:14 Mur’ umuco w’isi. Igisagara cubatswe ku mpinga y’umusozi ntigishobora guhishwa. 
Matthew5:15 Nta bodomeka itara ngo baryubikekw igisimbo, ariko barishira ku gitereko caryo, ngo riboneshereze abari mu nzu bose." 
Matthew5:16 Abe ari k’umuco wanyu ubonesha imbere y’abantu, ngo babone ibikorwa vyanyu vyiza, bahimbaze So wo mw ijuru." 
Matthew5:17 Ntimugire ngo naje gusenyura ivyagezwe cank’ amajambo y’abavugishwa n’Imana. Sinaje kubisenyura, naje kubishitsa." 
Matthew5:18 Ndababgire ukuri, Gushitsa ah’ ijuru n’isi bizoviraho, nta kanyuguti na kamwe canke n’akazatsa bizova ku vyagezwe, gushitsa aho vyose bizoheraherezwa." 
Matthew5:19 Nuk’ ūzorenga ibgirizwa na rimwe ryo mu yoroshe hanyuma y’ayandi, akigisha abantu ngo bagire bartyo, mu bgami bgo mw ijuru azokwitwa muto hanyuma y’abandi. Arik’ ūyitondera, akayigisha, uyo we azokwitwa mukuru mu bgami bgo mw ijuru." 
Matthew5:20 Ariko ndababgira yuk’ ukugororoka kwanyu ni kutaruta ukw’ abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe n’ukw’ Abafarisayo, mutazoruha mwinjira mu bgami bgo mw ijuru." 
Matthew5:21 Mwarumvise kw aba kera bābgiwe, ngo Ntukice: uwica aba ashikiwe no gutsindwa n’urubanza." 
Matthew5:22 Ariko jeho ndababgira yuk’ umuntu wese azorakira mugenzi we azoba ashikiwe no gutsindwa n’urubanza; ūzotuka mugenzi we, ngo Wa kijuju we! azoba ashikiwe no gucirwakw iteka; ūzomutuka, ati Wa gipfu we! azoba ashikiwe no gutabga mu muriro wa Gehinomu." 
Matthew5:23 Ni wajana ishikanwa ryawe ku gicaniro, ukahībukira ko har’ ico upfa na mugenzawe," 
Matthew5:24 usige ishikanwa ryawe imbere y’igicaniro, ubanze ugende wikiranure na mugenzawe, uce ugaruka, ushikane ishikanwa ryawe." 
Matthew5:25 Wuzure vuba n’ūkurega mukiri mu nzira; ūkurega ntagushikirize umucamanza, umucamanza akaguha umusoda, ugashirwa mw ibohero." 
Matthew5:26 Ndakubgira ukuri yuk’ utazohava na gatoya utishuye n’ikuta ry’imperēra. 
Matthew5:27 Mwarumvise ko vyāvuzwe, ngo Ntugasambane." 
Matthew5:28 Ariko jeho ndababgira yuk’ umuntu wese arāba umugore akamwifuza, aba amaze gusambana na we mu mutima wiwe." 
Matthew5:29 Ijisho ryawe ry’i buryo ni ryagutsitaza, urinogore, urite kure: vyokubera vyiza gupfa ijisho ryawe rimwe, hak’ umubiri wawe wose wotabga muri Gehinomu." 
Matthew5:30 N’ukuboko kwawe kw’i buryo ni kwagutsitaza, uguce igikonjo, ugite kure: vyokubera vyiza gupfa urugingo rwawe rumwe, hak’ umubiri wawe wose woja muri Gehinomu." 
Matthew5:31 Kandi vyaravuzwe, ng’ Umuntu wese yirukana umugore wiwe n’amuhe icete co kuvāvānura." 
Matthew5:32 Ariko jeho ndababgira yuk’ umuntu wese yirukana umugore wiwe atamuhōye ubusambanyi, aba amusambanishije: kand’ uwābīra uwahukanye azoba asambanye." 
Matthew5:33 Mwarumvise kandi kw aba kera bābgiwe, ngo Ntukarahire ngo wirahuruze, arik’ uz’ ukorere Uhoraho ivyo wamusezeraniye:" 
Matthew5:34 ariko jeho ndababgire: Ntukarahire na mba; nturahire ijuru, kukw ar’ intebe y’Imana;" 
Matthew5:35 cank’ isi, kukw ari yo ndava y’ibirenge vyayo; cank’ i Yerusalemu, kukw ar’ umurwa w’Umwami ahambaye." 
Matthew5:36 Nturahire umutwe wawe, kuk’ udashobora guhindura agashatsi na kamwe ngo kēre canke ngo kirabure." 
Matthew5:37 Arikw ijambo ryanyu ribe Ego, ego; Oya, oya: ikirenze ivyo kiva kuri wa Mubi." 
Matthew5:38 Mwarumvise ko vyāvuzwe, ngw Ijisho rihōrwe irindi, n’iryinyo rihōrwe irindi;" 
Matthew5:39 ariko jeho ndababgire: Ntimurwanye umunyakibi: ūgukubise urushi mu musaya w’i buryo umuhindukirize n’uwundi; 
Matthew5:40 umuntu ni yagomba kukubūranya ngw akunyage ipfundo, umuhebere n’umutamana;" 
Matthew5:41 ūgufata ng’ umurenze umusozi umwe, umurenze n’uwa kabiri." 
Matthew5:42 Ūgusaba, umuhe, ūgomba kukugurana, ntumutere ibitugu." 
Matthew5:43 Mwarumvise ko vyāvuzwe, ngo Mukunde bagenzi banyu, mwanke abansi banyu." 
Matthew5:44 Ariko jeho ndababgire: Mukunde abansi banyu, musabire ababahama," 
Matthew5:45 kugira ngo mube abana ba So wo mw ijuru, kukw atuma izuba ryiwe rirasira ababi n’abeza, kand’ aha imvura abagororotsi n’abagabitanya." 
Matthew5:46 Ni mwakunda ababakunda, muri n’impēra ki? Mbeg’ abatozakori bo si ko bagira?" 
Matthew5:47 Ni mwaramukanya n’incuti zanyu gusa, abandi muzoba mubarusha iki? Abanyamahanga bo si ko bagira?" 
Matthew5:48 Mwebge ni mube agahore, nk’uko So wo mw ijuru ar’ agahore." 
Matthew6:1 Mwirinde ntimugakorere ivyiza vyanyu mu maso y’abantu kugira ngo babarābe: ni mwagira murtyo, ntimuzogira impēra kuri So wo mw ijuru." 
Matthew6:2 Ni wagira ubuntu, ntuz’ uvugishe inzamba imbere yawe, nk’ukw indyarya zikora mu masinagogi no mu nzira, ngo bashimwe n’abantu: ndababgire ukuri: Baramaze guhabga impēra zabo." 
Matthew6:3 Ariko weho ni wagira ubuntu, ntumenyeshe ukubamfu kwawe ico ukuryo kwawe gukora," 
Matthew6:4 kugira ng’ ubuntu bgawe bugirirwe mu mpisho: kandi So, abona ibihishijwe, azoguhēra." 
Matthew6:5 Iyo musenga ntimukabe nka za ndyarya, kuko bakunda gusenga bahagaze mu masinagogi no mu mayirabiri, ngo biyerekane imbere y’abantu; ndababgire ukuri: Baramaze guhabga impēra zabo." 
Matthew6:6 Ariko weho, iy’ usenga, uje haruguru mu nzu yawe, wugare urugi, usenge So aba mu mpisho, kandi So, akuboneye mu mpisho azoguhēra." 
Matthew6:7 Kandi ni mwasenga, ntimukabomboranye amanwa nk’ukw abanyamahanga bagira: biyumvira yuko bazokwumvirwa kubg’ amajambo yabo menshi." 
Matthew6:8 Ntimuze muse na bo; kuko So azi ivyo mukennye mutaramusaba. 
Matthew6:9 Nuko musenge murtya, muti Data wa twese wo mw ijuru, izina ryawe ryubahwe," 
Matthew6:10 ubgami bgawe buze, ivyo ugomba bibe mw isi nk’uko biba mw ijuru." 
Matthew6:11 Uduhe ivyo kurya dukwiranye uyu musi; 
Matthew6:12 uduhebere imyenda yacu, nk’uko natwe twahebeye abari mu myenda yacu;" 
Matthew6:13 kandi ntutujane mu bitwosha nabi, arik’ udukize wa Mubi. [Kuk’ ubgami n’ubushobozi n’icubahiro ar’ ivyawe ibihe bidashira. Amen.]" 
Matthew6:14 Kuko ni mwaharira abantu ivyaha vyabo, na So wo mw ijuru azobaharira namwe." 
Matthew6:15 Ariko ni mutāharira abantu ivyaha vyabo, na So na we ntazobaharira ivyaha vyanyu." 
Matthew6:16 Kand’ iyo mwisonzesha, ntimwijirwe nk’uko za ndyarya zigira. Kuko bīyoberanya mu maso ngo babonwe n’abantu ko bisonzesheje. Ndababgire ukuri: Baramaze guhabga impēra zabo." 
Matthew6:17 Ariko weho, ni wisonzesha, wīsīge amavuta mu mutwe, wiyuhagire mu maso," 
Matthew6:18 ngo ntubonwe n’abantu ko wisonzesheje, arik’ ubonwe na So aba mu mpisho, kandi So, abona ivyo mu mpisho, azoguhēra." 
Matthew6:19 Ntimukīrundanirize ubutunzi mw isi, ah’ inyenzi n’ingese bibumara, n’ibisuma bikīmba bikabgiba." 
Matthew6:20 Ariko mwirundanirize ubutunzi mw ijuru, ah’ inyenzi n’ingese bitabumara, hatariyo n’ibisuma vyimba ngo vyibe." 
Matthew6:21 Kukw ah’ ubutunzi bgawe buri, ari ho umutima wawe uzoba." 
Matthew6:22 Itara ry’umubiri n’ijisho. Ijisho ryawe iy’ ari ryiza, umubiri wawe wose uba uri n’umuco." 
Matthew6:23 Arikw ijisho ryawe iy’ ari ribi, umubiri wawe wose uba uri n’umwiza. Nuko wa muco uba muri wewe, woramuka ubaye umwiza, uwo mwiza wongana ute!" 
Matthew6:24 Nta wusaba abami babiri: kuko yokwanka umwe, agakunda uwundi, canke yoguma kur’ umwe, akagaya wa wundi. Ntimushobora gusaba Imana n’Itunga." 
Matthew6:25 Ni co gitumye ndababarira, nti Ntimukaganyire amagara yanyu ku vyo muzorya canke ku vyo muzonywa, cank’ umubiri wanyu ku vyo muzokwambara. Mbeg’ amagara ntaruta ivyo kurya, cank’ umubiri nturuta ivyambarwa?" 
Matthew6:26 Ni murābe ibiguruka vyo mu kirēre, ntibibiba, ntibishwabura, kandi ntivyimburira mu bigega, ariko So wo mw ijuru arabitunga; mbega mwebge ntimubiruta cane?" 
Matthew6:27 Ni nde muri mwebge yoshobozwa n’amaganya kwisumvya uko yareha nk’ukuboko kumwe? 
Matthew6:28 Ikibaganyisha impuzu n’iki? Ni murābe amashurwe yo ku misozi ingen’ akura, ntiyirirwa aratama, ntajisha impuzu;" 
Matthew6:29 ariko ndababgira yuko na Salomo mu bgiza bgiwe bgose atar’ ashajije nka rimwe mur’ ayo. 
Matthew6:30 Non’ Imana ko yambika ivyatsi vyo ku misozi irtyo, birih’ uyu musi, ariko nk’ejo bigatererwa mu ziko, mbega ntizorushiriza kubambika, mwebge ab’ ukwizera guke mwe?" 
Matthew6:31 Nuko ntimukiganyire, ngo Tuzorya iki? canke Tuzonywa iki? canke Tuzokwambara iki?" 
Matthew6:32 Kukw ivyo vyose abanyamahanga ari vyo bitwaririka; ariko So wo mw ijuru arazi kw ivyo vyose mubikena. 
Matthew6:33 Ariko mubanze mwitwaririke ubgami bg’Imana n’ukugororoka kwayo, ni ho ivyo vyose muzovyongerwa." 
Matthew6:34 Ntimukiganyire ivy’ ejo, kuk’ umusi w’ejo uzoba wiganyira ivyawo; umusi ukwiranye n’amagorwa yawo." 
Matthew7:1 Ntimugahinyurire mu mitima yanyu, namwe mukazohinyurwa." 
Matthew7:2 Kuko, uko muhinyura abandi, ari ko muzohinyurwa namwe; kand’ ingero mugeramwo muzoyigererwa namwe." 
Matthew7:3 Urābira iki akabango kari mu jisho rya mugenzawe, kand’ inkingi iri mu jisho ryawe ntuyitegereze?" 
Matthew7:4 Wobgira ute mugenzawe, uti Zana ngutosore akabango kari mu jisho ryawe, nawe ufise inkingi mu jisho ryawe?" 
Matthew7:5 Wa ndyarya we, banza witosore inkingi iri mu jisho ryawe, uheze ubone neza gutosora akabango kari mu jisho rya mugenzawe." 
Matthew7:6 Ivyera vy’Imana ntimukabihe imbga, kand’ imaragarita zanyu ntimuziterere ingurube, kugira ngo ntizizihonyange n’inzāra zazo, maze zikabahindukirira, zikabatabagura." 
Matthew7:7 Musabe, muzohabga; murondere, muzoronka; muramutse, muzokwugururirwa." 
Matthew7:8 Kuk’ ūsaba wese ahabga; ūrondera aronka; ūramutsa yugururirwa. 
Matthew7:9 Har’ umuntu muri mwebge, umwana wiwe yomusaba umutsima, akamuha ibuye?" 
Matthew7:10 Canke yomusaba ifi, akamuha inzoka?" 
Matthew7:11 None mwebge, ko muzi guha abana banyu ingabire nziza muri babi, mbega So wo mw ijuru ntazorushiriza rwose guha ivyiza abamusavye?" 
Matthew7:12 Nukw ivyo mugomba kw abantu babagirira vyose mube ari ko mubagirira namwe; kukw ivyo ar’ ivyagezwe n’ivy’ abavugishijwe n’Imana. 
Matthew7:13 Muce mw irembo ripfunganye; kukw irembo ryagutse, n’inzira y’igihamo, ari vyo bijana abantu mu mahonero, kand’ abahaca ni benshi." 
Matthew7:14 Arikw irembo ripfunganye, n’inzira ntoya, ni vyo bija mu bugingo, kand’ abahabona ni bake." 
Matthew7:15 Mwirinde abīgira abavugishwa n’Imana; baza kuri mwebge bambaye nk’intama; arikw imbere ar’ amabingira y’inkazi. 
Matthew7:16 Muzobamenyera ku vyo bama. Mbega har’ uwokwamura inzabibu ku munyinya, cank’ insukoni ku bitovu?" 
Matthew7:17 Nukw igiti ciza cose cama ivyiza, arikw igiti kibi cama ibibi." 
Matthew7:18 Igiti ciza ntigishobora kwama ibibi, kand’ igiti kibi ntigishobora kwama ivyiza." 
Matthew7:19 Igiti cose kitama ivyiza kiracibga, kigatererwa mu muriro." 
Matthew7:20 Nuko muzobamenyera ku vyo bama. 
Matthew7:21 Umuntu wese amvumereza, ati Mwami, Mwami; si we azokwinjira mu bgami bgo mw ijuru, atar’ ūkora ivyo Data wo mw ijuru agomba." 
Matthew7:22 Benshi bazombgira kuri wa musi, ngo Mwami, Mwami, ntitwavugishwa n’Imana mw izina ryawe, ntitwasenda abadayimoni mw izina ryawe, ntitwakora ibitangaza vyinshi mw izina ryawe?" 
Matthew7:23 Ni ho nzobajinjiburira, nti Nta ho nigeze mbamenya; mviraho, mwa bakora ibizira mwe." 
Matthew7:24 Uwumva ayo majambo yanje wese, akayakora, asa n’umuntu w’ubgenge yubatse inzu yiwe ku rutare." 
Matthew7:25 Isegenya iragwa, inkukūra iratwaza, igihuhuta kirahuhuta, bisūrira kuri nya nzu, ntiyagwa, kuko yar’ imase ku rutare." 
Matthew7:26 Arik’ uwumva ayo majambo yanje wese, ntayakore, asa n’umuntu w’imburabgenge, yubatse inzu yiwe ku musenyi." 
Matthew7:27 Isegenya iragwa, inkukūra iratwaza, igihuhuta kirahuhuta, bisūrira kuri nya nzu, irasenyuka, kand’ isenyerana ryayo riba irikomeye." 
Matthew7:28 Yesu arangije ayo majambo yose, ishengero ritangazwa n’inyigisho ziwe," 
Matthew7:29 kuko yabigisha nk’ūfise ububasha, ntase n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe babo." 
Matthew8:1 Amanutse uwo musozi, ishengero ryinshi riramukurikira." 
Matthew8:2 Maz’ umunyamibembe aza kuri we, aramupfukamira, ati Mugenzi, ukunze, woshobora kumpumanura." 
Matthew8:3 Aramvura ukuboko, amukorako, ati Ndakunze, humanuka." 
Matthew8:4 Bun’ aca akira imibembe yiwe. Yesu aramubgira, ati Wirinde, ntugire uwo ubgira, ariko genda wiyereke umuherezi, utange ishikanwa ryagezwe na Mose, ribe ikimenyetso kibabere icabona." 
Matthew8:5 Ashitse i Kaperinawumu, haza umugabisha w’abasoda ijana, aramwinginga," 
Matthew8:6 ati Mushingantahe, umuhungu wanje n’ikimuga, aryamye mu nzu, arasinzikaye cane." 
Matthew8:7 Aramubgira, ati Ndaje kumukiza." 
Matthew8:8 Umugabisha aramwishura, ati Mugenzi, ntibimbereye ko winjira mu nzu yanje; vuga ijambo gusa, uwo muhungu arakira." 
Matthew8:9 Kuko nanje nd’umuntu agendera musi y’abanganza, mfise abasoda ntwara: iyo mbariye umwe, nti Genda, aragenda; n’uwundi nti Ngwino, akaza; nabarira umushumba wanje, nti Kora iki, akagikora." 
Matthew8:10 Yesu avyumvise, biramutangaza, abgira abamukurikiye, ati Ndababgire ukuri: Sinaribgabone ukwizera kungana gurtyo no mu Bisirayeli." 
Matthew8:11 Ndababgira yuko benshi bazoza, bavuye i burasirazuba n’i burengerazuba, bazokwicarana na Aburahamu na Isaka na Yakobo mu bgami bgo mw ijuru;" 
Matthew8:12 arikw abana b’ubgo bgami bazohindirwa hanze mu mwiza, ni ho hazoba amarira no kuryanya insya z’amenyo." 
Matthew8:13 Yesu abgira uwo mugabisha, at’ Igīre, bikubere nk’uko wizeye. Nuko wa muhungu akira uno mwanya." 
Matthew8:14 Yesu yinjiye mu nzu kwa Petero, abona inabukwe aryamye afashwe n’umururumbo." 
Matthew8:15 Amukora ku kuboko, umururumbo urazima; aravyuka, aramuzimana." 
Matthew8:16 Ku kagoroba, bamuzanira benshi binjiwemwo n’abadayimoni; izo mpwemu mbi azirukanisha ijambo, akiza abāri barwaye bose," 
Matthew8:17 ngw ivyavuzwe n’uwavugishwa n’Imana Yesaya biboneke, ng’ Ubgiwe ni we yatwara ubumuga bgacu, akikorera n’indwara zacu." 
Matthew8:18 Yesu abonye ishengero ryinshi rimukikije, agera ko bajabuka hakurya." 
Matthew8:19 Haza umunyabgenge w’ivyanditswe, aramubgira, ati Mwigisha, ndagukurikira ah’ uja hose." 
Matthew8:20 Yesu aramubgira, at’ Imbgebge ziri n’imyobo, n’ibiguruka mu kirēre biri n’ivyari; arik’ Umwana w’umuntu we ntagira ah’ arambika umusaya." 
Matthew8:21 Uwundi mu bigishwa aramubgira, ati Mugenzi, banza undekure, ngende mpambe data." 
Matthew8:22 Ariko Yesu aramubgira, ati Nkurikira, reka abapfuye bahambe abapfuye babo." 
Matthew8:23 Atambukira mu bgato, abigishwa biwe baramukurikira." 
Matthew8:24 Haza igihuhuta gikomeye mu kiyaga, bituma ubgato buzimirira mu mipfunda: ariko we yar’ asinziriye." 
Matthew8:25 Baraza baramukangura, bati Mugenzi, dukize, turapfuye." 
Matthew8:26 Arababaza, ati N’iki kibateye ubgoba, mwa bafise ukwizera guke mwe? Bun’ aravyuka azibiza ingunza n’ikiyaga, haba agahwekere rwose." 
Matthew8:27 Maz’ abo bantu baratangara, bat’ Uyu n’umuntu ki, umuyaga n’ikiyaga ko bimwumvira?" 
Matthew8:28 Afashe hakurya mu gihugu c’Abagadareni, babiri binjiwemwo n’abadayimoni baramusanganira bava mu masenga y’imva, bari bakaze cane, bituma ata wushobora guhita mur’ iyo nzira." 
Matthew8:29 Barasemerera, bati Duhuriye hehe ga Mwana w’Imana? Uje hano kutubabaza agashinyaguro igihe cacu kitarashika?" 
Matthew8:30 Kure yabo hār’ umukuku w’ingurube nyinshi zirisha. 
Matthew8:31 Abadayimoni baramwinginga, bati Namb’ udusenda, uturungike mur’ uriya mukuku w’ingurube." 
Matthew8:32 Arababgira, ati Ni mugende. Babasokorokamwo, baragenda, baja mur’ izo ngurube. Wa mukuku wose wirukira ku gatembge, zīsuka mu kiyaga, zihonera mu mazi." 
Matthew8:33 Abāziragira barahunga; bashitse mu gisagara bavuga ivyo babonye vyose n’ivy’ abāri binjiwemwo n’abadayimoni. 
Matthew8:34 Abo mur’ ico gisagara bose baja gusanganira Yesu. Bamubonye, baramwinginga ngw ave mu ntāra yabo." 
Matthew9:1 Aja mu bgato, arajabuka, ashika mu gisagara c’i wabo." 
Matthew9:2 Bamuzanira ikimuga bagiteruye mu nderuzo. Yesu abonye ukwizera kwabo, abgira ico kimuga, ati Hūmura mwana wanje, ivyaha vyawe urabihariwe." 
Matthew9:3 Bamwe mu banyabgenge b’ivyanditswe baribgira, bat’ Uyo ararogose." 
Matthew9:4 Yesu amenye ivyo biyumvira arababaza, ati N’iki kibateye kwiyumvira nabi mu mitima yanyu?" 
Matthew9:5 Non’ icoroshe n’ikihe, n’ukuvuga nt’ Uhariwe ivyaha vyawe; canke n’ukuvuga nti Vyuka, ugende?" 
Matthew9:6 Ariko kugira ngo mumenye k’Umwana w’umuntu afise ububasha mw isi bgo guharira ivyaha — bun’ abgira ikimuga, ati Vyuka, wikorere inderuzo yawe, utahe." 
Matthew9:7 Aravyuka arataha. 
Matthew9:8 Ishengero ribibonye, riratinya, rihimbaza Imana yahaye abantu ububasha ben’ ubgo." 
Matthew9:9 Yesu ahavuye, abona umuntu yitwa Matayo, yicaye aho yatoreza ikibuguro. Aramubarira, ati Nkurikira. Ava hasi, aramukurikira." 
Matthew9:10 Kandi Yesu acicaye mu nzu arikw ararya, haza benshi mu batozakori n’abanyavyaha, basangira na Yesu n’abigishwa biwe." 
Matthew9:11 Abafarisayo babibonye, babaza abigishwa biwe, bati N’iki gitumye umwigisha wanyu asangira n’abatozakori n’abanyavyaha?" 
Matthew9:12 Avyumvise, aravuga, at’ Abakomeye nta co bagombera umuvūzi, atar’ abarwaye." 
Matthew9:13 Mugende mwige iri jambo, muritahure, ngw Imbabazi ni zo ngomba, s’ibimazi: kuko ntaje guhamagara abagororotsi, atar’ abanyavyaha." 
Matthew9:14 Kuri we haza abigishwa ba Yohana, bati N’iki gituma twebge n’Abafarisayo twisonzesha kenshi, abigishwa bawe ntibisonzeshe?" 
Matthew9:15 Yesu arababaza, at’ Abātowe bobabara bate bakiri kumwe n’umukwe? Har’ imisi izoza umukwe akūrwe muri bo, ni ho bazokwisonzesha." 
Matthew9:16 Nta wokwomeka ikiremo c’igitambara gisha ku mpuzu y’umushire, kukw ico kiremo gica impuzu, intoboro ikarushiriza kuba nini." 
Matthew9:17 Nta wotara umutobe wa vino mu mikuza y’insato ibōmbōtse: imikuza yoturika, vino igashirira hasi, imikuza igapfa. Arik’ umutobe wa vino bawutara mu mikuza misha, vyompi bikarama." 
Matthew9:18 Akibabgira ivyo, haza umukuru w’isinagogi aramupfukamira, at’ Umwana wanje w’umukobga aradēndūtse, n’uze se, umurambikekw ikiganza, asubire abe muzima." 
Matthew9:19 Yesu ava hasi, aramukurikira, bo n’abigishwa biwe." 
Matthew9:20 Bun’ umugore arwaye ubutinyanka, yar’ abimaranye imyaka cumi n’ibiri, amuturuka inyuma, akora ku buyonga bg’impuzu yiwe;" 
Matthew9:21 yari yiyumviriye mu mutima, ati N’iyo nokora ku mpuzu yiwe gusa, nokira." 
Matthew9:22 Buno Yesu arakebuka aramubona, aramubgira, ati Hūmura, mwana wanje, ukwizera kwawe kuragukijije. Nya mugore akira uwo mwanya." 
Matthew9:23 Yesu ashikiriye inzu y’uwo mukuru, abona abavuza imyironge n’abantu benshi bakoma induru," 
Matthew9:24 arababgira, ati Ni muhave, kuk’ umukobga atāhwereye, arikw arasinziriye. Baramutwenga bamushinyagurira." 
Matthew9:25 Abantu bamaze guhindirwa hanze, arinjira, amufata ukuboko, umukobga aravyuka." 
Matthew9:26 Iyo nkuru ikwira mur’ ico gihugu cose. 
Matthew9:27 Yesu avayo, akirikw aragenda impumyi zibiri ziramukurikira zisemerera, ziti Tugirire imbabazi, mwana wa Dawidi." 
Matthew9:28 Ashitse mu nzu, za mpumyi ziza kuri we. Maze Yesu arazibaza, ati Murizeye ko nshobora kubikora? Na zo zit’ Ego me, Mushingantahe." 
Matthew9:29 Aca akora ku maso yabo, ati Bibabere nk’uko mwizeye." 
Matthew9:30 Amaso yabo arahumūka. Yesu arabihanikiriza, ati Murumva, ntihagire umuntu abimenya." 
Matthew9:31 Ariko basohotse bamukwiza mur’ ico gihugu cose. 
Matthew9:32 Bano bagisohoka, bamuzanira ikiragi cinjiwemwo na dayimoni." 
Matthew9:33 Dayimoni amaze gusendwa ico kiragi kiravuga. Kand’ ishengero riratangara, riti Mu Bisirayeli ntiharibgaboneke ibimeze birtyo." 
Matthew9:34 Arikw Abafarisayo baravuga, bat’ Umukuru w’abadayimoni ni we amushoboza gusenda abadayimoni." 
Matthew9:35 Yesu agendagenda mu bisagara vyose no mu mihana yose, yigisha mu masinagogi yabo, avuga ubutumwa bgiza bg’ubgami, akiza indwara zose n’ubumuga bgose." 
Matthew9:36 Abonye ishengero, rimutera akagongwe, kuko bāri bagowe, basābagiye nk’intama zitagira umwungere." 
Matthew9:37 Maz’ abgira abigishwa biwe, at’ Ivyimburwa ni vyinshi, arikw abimbuzi ni bo bake." 
Matthew9:38 Nuko ni mwinginge Nyen’ ivyimburwa arungike abimbuzi mu vyimburwa vyiwe. 
Matthew10:1 Ahamagara abigishwa biwe cumi na babiri, abaha ububasha ku mpwemu zihumanye n’ubgo kuzisenda, no gukiza indwara zose n’ubumuga bgose." 
Matthew10:2 Amazina y’izo ntumwa cumi na zibiri n’aya: Uwa mbere ni Simoni, yitwa Petero, na mwene nyina Andereya, na Yakobo mwene Zebedayo na mwene nyina Yohana," 
Matthew10:3 na Filipo na Barutolomayo na Toma na Matayo umutozakori, na Yakobo mwene Alufayo, na Tadayo," 
Matthew10:4 na Simoni Umunyakananayo, na Yuda Isikaryota, umwe yamugura." 
Matthew10:5 Abo cumi na babiri Yesu arabatuma ababarira, ati Ntimuze mujane inzira ija mu banyamahanga, canke mu bisagara vy’Abasamariya." 
Matthew10:6 Ariko muje mu ntama zazimiye zo mu muryango wa Isirayeli. 
Matthew10:7 Uko mugenda kwose mwigishe, mut’ Ubgami bgo mw ijuru buri hafi." 
Matthew10:8 Mukize abarwaye, muzure abapfuye, mukize abanyamibembe, musende abadayimoni. Mubiherewe ubusa, mubitangire ubundi." 
Matthew10:9 Ntimutekere izahabu cank’ ifeza cank’ amahera mu mipfuko yanyu," 
Matthew10:10 cank’ isaho y’impamba, kandi ntimujane amapfundo abiri, cank’ inkweto cank’ inkoni, kuk’ umukozi akwiye impembo yiwe." 
Matthew10:11 Igisagara cose cank’ imihana muzoshikamwo, muhabaze ūbereye, mumurārire gushitsa aho muzovirayo." 
Matthew10:12 Mucinjira mu nzu muyiramutse; 
Matthew10:13 nya nzu ni yaba ibereye, amahoro yanyu azoyizako. Ni yaba itabereye, amahoro yanyu azobagarukako." 
Matthew10:14 Kand’ umuntu n’atabākīra, canke ngo yumve amajambo yanyu, mukiva mur’ ino nzu canke muri nya gisagara, muze mukunkumure umukungugu wo mu birenge vyanyu." 
Matthew10:15 Ndababgire ukuri, ku musi w’amateka igihugu c’i Sodomu n’i Gomora kizogira agahengekezo kurusha nya gisagara." 
Matthew10:16 Rāba mbatumye muri nk’intama mu mabingira hagati. Nuko mugire ubgenge nk’inzoka, mumere nk’inuma ata karohe." 
Matthew10:17 Mwirinde abantu. Bazobashengerana mu manza, babatonagurire mu masinagogi yabo." 
Matthew10:18 Bazobajana imbere y’abaganza n’abami babampōra, muzoba ikimenyetso kibabere icabona, bo n’abanyamahanga." 
Matthew10:19 Ariko babashengeranye, ntimuze muhagarikire imitima ico muyuga n’ingene muzokivuga, kukw ivyo muvuga muzobihabga mur’ ako kanya." 
Matthew10:20 Kukw atazoba ari mwebge muvuga, azoba ari Mpwemu wa So avugira muri mwebge." 
Matthew10:21 Umuntu azoshengerana uwo bavukana ngo bamwice, na se w’umwana azomushengerana, n’abana bazogābagābira abavyeyi babicishe." 
Matthew10:22 Muzoba mwanswe na bose babahōra izina ryanje; arik’ uwihangana agashitsa iherezo ni we azokira. 
Matthew10:23 Ni babahama mu gisagara kimwe, muhungire mu kindi: kuko mbabgira ukuri yuko mutazohetura ibisagara vyose vy’i Bgisirayeli, Umwana w’umuntu ataraza." 
Matthew10:24 Umwigishwa ntaruta umwigisha; kandi n’umushumba ntaruta shebuja. 
Matthew10:25 Umwigishwa biramubereye kumera nk’umwigisha wiwe, n’umushumba nka shebuja. Nyen’ urugo ko bamwise Beyezebuli, non’ abo mu rugo rwiwe ntibazorushiriza kubīta bartyo?" 
Matthew10:26 Nuko ntimuze mubatinye, kukw ata catwikiriwe kitazotwikururwa, canke kinyegejwe kitazomenyekana." 
Matthew10:27 Ico mbabaririra mu mwiza muze mukivugire mu muco, kand’ ico mwongorewe mu gutwi muze mukivugire ku mazu hejuru." 
Matthew10:28 Ntimuze mutinye abica umubiri, badashobora kwica ubugingo: cane‐cane mutinye ūshobora guhonereza ubugingo n’umubirimuri Gehinomu." 
Matthew10:29 Mbeg’ utunyoni tubiri ntitugurwa ikuta? Ariko muri two nta na kamwe gakorokera hasi, So atabizi." 
Matthew10:30 Ariko n’umushatsi wo ku mitwe yanyu wose waraharūwe. 
Matthew10:31 Nuko ntimutinye: mwebge muruta utunyoni twinshi. 
Matthew10:32 Umuntu wese azonyaturira imbere y’abantu, nanje nzomwaturira imbere ya Data wo mw ijuru." 
Matthew10:33 Arik’ umuntu wese azonyihakanira imbere y’abantu, nanje nzomwihakanira imbere ya Data wo mw ijuru." 
Matthew10:34 Mwoye kwiyumvira ngo naje gutera amahoro mw isi: sinaje gutera amahoro, atar’ inkota." 
Matthew10:35 Kuko naje guteranya umwana na se, n’umukobga na nyina, n’umukazana na inabukwe." 
Matthew10:36 Kand’ abansi b’umuntu bazoba abo mu rugo rwiwe. 
Matthew10:37 Ūkunze se canke nyina akabandutisha, ntaba ankwiye: kand’ ūkunze umuhungu wiwe cank’ umukobga wiwe akabandutisha, ntaba ankwiye." 
Matthew10:38 Kand’ ūtikoreye umusaraba wiwe ngw ankurikire, ntaba ankwiye." 
Matthew10:39 Ūrokora ubugingo bgiwe azobubura; n’ūheba ubugingo bgiwe kubganje azoburonka. 
Matthew10:40 Ūbākiriye aba anyakiriye, kand’ ūnyakiriye aba yākiriye uwantumye." 
Matthew10:41 Uwākīra umuntu avugishwa n’Imana kukw avugishwa na yo azohabga impēra nk’iy’ ūvugishwa n’Imana; uwākīra umuntu agororotse kukw agororotse azohabga impēra nk’iy’ umugororotsi. 
Matthew10:42 Kand’ ūzoha umwe mur’ abo bato urwato rw’amazi apfutse gusa kukw ar’ umwigishwa, ndababgira ukuri yukw atazobura impēra yiwe." 
Matthew11:1 Yesu arangije gutuma abigishwa biwe cumi na babiri, avayo, aja kwigisha abantu no kuvuga ivy’ Imana mu bisagara vyabo." 
Matthew11:2 Ariko Yohana ari mu nzu y’imbohe, yumva ivyo Kristo akora, atuma abigishwa biwe kumubaza," 
Matthew11:3 ati Mbeg’ uri wa wundi akwiye kuza, canke twitege uwundi?" 
Matthew11:4 Yesu arabishura, ati Ni mugende mubarire Yohana ivyo mwumva n’ivyo mubona." 
Matthew11:5 Impumyi zirahumūka, abacumbagira bagenda neza, abanyamibembe barakizwa, ibipfamatwi birumva, abapfuye barazurwa, aboro barabgirwa ubutumwa bgiza." 
Matthew11:6 Kandi hahirwa uwo ivyanje bitazotsitaza. 
Matthew11:7 Abo bagiye, Yesu atangura kubgira ishengero ivya Yohana, ati Mwagiye mu bugaragwa kurāba iki? Mbega n’irenga rihungabanywa n’umuyaga?" 
Matthew11:8 Ariko mwagiye kurāba iki? Mbega n’umuntu yambaye impuzu ziremvye? Ereg’ abambaye impuzu ziremvye baba mu ngo z’abami. 
Matthew11:9 Ariko mwajanywe n’iki? Mbega kwar’ ukurāba umuntu avugishwa n’Imana? Ego me ni co; kandi ndababgire, Aruta ūvugishwa n’Imana cane." 
Matthew11:10 Uyo ni we yanditswe, ng’ Umve ngira ntume integuza yanje imbere y’amaso yawe, Ikuroranirize inzira imbere yawe." 
Matthew11:11 Ndababgire ukuri: Mu bāvyawe n’abagore ntihigeze kuboneka umuntu aruta Yohana Umubatizi. Arik’ umutoya mu bgami bgo mw ijuru aramuruta. 
Matthew11:12 Uhereye mu gihe ca Yohana Umubatizi ugashitsa n’ubu barabandanira ubgami bgo mw ijuru, ababandana babunyakurisha ubuhizi." 
Matthew11:13 Kukw abavugishwa n’Imana bose bāvugishijwe, bo n’ivyagezwe, gushitsa igihe ca Yohana," 
Matthew11:14 kandi ni mwaba mugomba kuvyemera, uwo ni we Eliya yavuzwe kw azoza." 
Matthew11:15 Ūri n’amatwi yumva, ni yumve." 
Matthew11:16 Arikw ab’uru runganwe ndabagereranye n’iki? Basa n’abana bicaye mu tuguriro, bahamagara bagenzi babo," 
Matthew11:17 bati Twavugije imyironge ntimwahamiriza; twakomye induru, ntimwaboroga." 
Matthew11:18 Kuko Yohana yaje, atarya, atanywa, bavuga bat’ Ahagazweko na dayimoni." 
Matthew11:19 Umwana w’umuntu yaje, arya, anywa, baravuga bati Nguyu umukunzi w’inda n’umunoho wa vino, incuti y’abatozakori n’abanyavyaha. Kand’ ubgenge burangwa ko bugororotse n’ibikorwa vyabgo." 
Matthew11:20 Bun’ atangura guhambarira ibisagara yakoreyemw’ ibikomeye vyinshi, kuko batihannye." 
Matthew11:21 At’ Uzobona ibara, Korazini; uzobona ibara, Betsayida; kukw ibikomeye vyakorewe muri mwebge iyo biba vyarakorewe muri Tiro n’i Sidoni, baba barihannye kera, bakambara amagunira, bakīsīga iminyota." 
Matthew11:22 Ariko ndababgire: muri Tiro n’i Sidoni hazogira agahengekezo ku musi w’amateka kurusha mwebge. 
Matthew11:23 Nawe, Kaperinawumu, mbeg’ uzoshirwa hejuru ushike kw ijuru? Oya, uzocokezwa i kuzimu; kukw ibikomeye vyakorewe muri wewe, iyo biba vyarakorewe i Sodomu, haba hakiriho na bugingo n’ubu." 
Matthew11:24 Ariko ndababgira yukw igihugu c’i Sodomu kizogira agahengekezo ku musi w’amateka kurusha wewe. 
Matthew11:25 Mur’ ico gihe Yesu aravuga, ati Ndaguhimbaza, Data, Mwami w’ijuru n’isi, kukw ivyo wabihishije abanyabgenge n’abahanga, ukabihishurira inzoya." 
Matthew11:26 Ego me, Data, kuko washimye ko biba birtyo imbere yawe." 
Matthew11:27 Vyose nabihawe na Data, kandi nta wuzi Umwana, atari Data, na Data, nta wumuzi, atar’ Umwana, n’uwo Umwana agomba kumuhishurira." 
Matthew11:28 Ni muze kuri jewe mwese abananiwe n’abaremerewe, ndabaruhura;" 
Matthew11:29 mwikoreze ingata yanje, munyigireko; kuko nd’ umugwaneza, niyoroheje mu mutima; namwe muzoronka uburuhukiro bg’imitima yanyu." 
Matthew11:30 Kukw ingata yanje itababaza, n’umutwaro wanje uhwahutse." 
Matthew12:1 Mur’ ico gihe Yesu aca mu mirima y’ingano kw isabato. Abigishwa biwe bashonje, batangura kumyoza ingano, barazihekenya." 
Matthew12:2 Abafarisayo babibonye, baramubgira, bati Mbeg’ abigishwa bawe ko bakora ikizira gukorwa kw isabato!" 
Matthew12:3 Na we arababaza, ati Nta ho murasoma ico Dawidi yakoze, aho yar’ asonzanye n’abāri kumwe na we;" 
Matthew12:4 ingene yinjiye mu nzu y’Imana, akarya imitsima y’ibiterekērwa, yar’ umuziro kuri we no ku bāri kumwe na we, ukūye abaherezi bonyene?" 
Matthew12:5 Canke nta ho murasoma mu vyagezwe ingene kw isabato abaherezi, iyo bari mu rusengero, bazirura isabato, ntibabekw igicumuro?" 
Matthew12:6 Ariko ndababgira yuko hano har’ ūruta urusengero. 
Matthew12:7 Iyo muba mwari muzi iri jambo ico rivuga, ngw Imbabazi ni zo ngomba, s’ibimazi; ntimuba mutsindishije abatarikw igicumuro." 
Matthew12:8 Kuk’ Umwana w’umuntu ar’ Umwami w’isabato. 
Matthew12:9 Avayo, yinjira mw isinagogi yabo." 
Matthew12:10 Kandi hārimw’ umuntu anyunyutse ukuboko. Baramubaza, bati Mbega birēmerwa gukiza kw isabato? Ngo baronke uko bomurega." 
Matthew12:11 Arabishura, ati Ni nde muri mwebge yoba afise intama imwe ikagwa mu cobo kw isabato, ntayifate ngw ayikūreyo?" 
Matthew12:12 Mbega non’ umuntu ntaruta intama cane? None rero birēmerwa gukora ivyiza kw isabato. 
Matthew12:13 Maz’ abgira uwo muntu, ati Ramvura ukuboko kwawe. Arakuramvura, kurakira, gukomera nk’ukundi." 
Matthew12:14 Abafarisayo barasohoka, bamugīra inama ngo babone ingene bomwica." 
Matthew12:15 Yesu abimenye, arahava. Benshi baramukurikira, abakiza bose." 
Matthew12:16 Arabihaniza ngo ntibagende baramwandagaza," 
Matthew12:17 ngw ivyavuzwe n’uwavugishwa n’Imana Yesaya bishike," 
Matthew12:18 ngo Nguyu umushumba wanje natoranije, Nkunda, ahimbara umutima wanje; Nzoshira Mpwemu wanje kuri we, Azomenyesha abanyamahanga amateka azocibga." 
Matthew12:19 Ntazosinda, kandi ntazoyogora, Kandi nta wuzokwumva ijwi ryiwe mu nzira:" 
Matthew12:20 Ntazohohosha irenga rivunitse, N’urumuri ruyenga ntazoruzimya, Gushitsa ah’ azogomorera amateka akanesha;" 
Matthew12:21 Kand’ izina ryiwe ni ryo abanyamahanga bazokwizigira. 
Matthew12:22 Maze bamuzanira impumyi y’ikiragi yinjiwemwo na dayimoni, arayikiza; ico kiragi kiravuga, kirahumūka." 
Matthew12:23 Ishengero ryose rirumirwa, riti Mbeg uyu yoba wa mwana wa Dawidi?" 
Matthew12:24 Arikw Abafarisayo bavyumvise baravuga, bat’ Uyu ntashobozwa n’ikindi gusenda abadayimoni, atari Beyezebuli, umukuru w’abadayimoni." 
Matthew12:25 Amenye ivyo biyumvira, arababgira, at’ Ubgami bgose iyo bgitandukanije ubgabgo burahona. Igisagara cose n’umuryango wose iyo vyitandukanije ntibirama." 
Matthew12:26 Na Satani, yosenda Satani, yoba yitandukanije ubgiwe; non’ ubgami bgiwe bgorama bute?" 
Matthew12:27 Ariko jewe namba Beyezebuli ari we anshoboza gusenda abadayimoni, abana banyu bashobozwa na nde kubasenda? Ni co gituma ari bo bazobatsindisha." 
Matthew12:28 Ariko Mpwemu w’Imana ni yaba ari we anshoboza gusenda abadayimoni, noneh’ ubgami bg’Imana burabashikiriye." 
Matthew12:29 Non’ umuntu yoshobora ate kwinjira mu nzu y’umuntu w’inkomezi kumusahura ibintu atabanje kuboha wa munyenkomezi? Maz’ akabona kumusahura ivyo mu nzu yiwe. 
Matthew12:30 Ūtamperereyeko n’umwansi wanje, kand’ ūdasukiranya nanje arasanzaza." 
Matthew12:31 Kubg’ ivyo ndababgira yukw icaha cose n’ukurogota, abantu bazobiharirwa; ariko kurogota kuri Mpwemu n’icaha kitazoharirwa." 
Matthew12:32 Umuntu wese azodedemba ku Mwana w’umuntu azobiharirwa, arik’ ūdedemba kuri Mpwemu Yera ntazobiharirwa, naho hoba mur’ iki gihe canke mu gihe kizoza." 
Matthew12:33 Ni mube muvuga igiti kw ari ciza n’ivyo camye kw ari vyiza, canke mube muvuga igiti kw ari kibi n’ivyo camye kw ari bibi; kukw igiti kimenyekanira ku vyo camye." 
Matthew12:34 Mwa bana b’inzoka mwe, mwoshobora mute kuvuga ivyiza muri babi? Ibibōgabōga mu mutima ni vyo akanwa kavuga." 
Matthew12:35 Umunyangeso nziza akūra ivyiza mw itunga ryiwe ryiza; umunyangeso mbi akūra ibibi mw itunga ryiwe ribi. 
Matthew12:36 Kandi ndababgira yukw ijambo ryose risunitswe n’impwemu abantu bavuga bazoribazwa ku musi w’amateka. 
Matthew12:37 Amajambo yawe ni yo azotuma utsinda cank’ amajambo yawe ni yo azotuma utsindwa. 
Matthew12:38 Abafarisayo n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe bamwe baramubgira, bati Mwigisha, turagomba kurāba ikimenyetso ukora." 
Matthew12:39 Arabishura, at’ Ab’ urunganwe rubi rw’ubumaka barondera ikimenyetso; kandi nta kimenyetso bazohabga, atar’ ikimenyetso c’uwavugishwa n’Imana Yona." 
Matthew12:40 Nk’uko Yona yamaze imisi itatu n’amajoro atatu mu nda y’urufi, ni ko n’Umwana w’umuntu azomara imisi itatu n’amajoro atatu i kuzimu." 
Matthew12:41 Abagabo b’i Ninewe bazovana hasi n’ab’ uru runganwe ku musi w’amateka, babatsindishe: kuko bihannye aho bumviye ubutumwa buvuzwe na Yona; kandi rāba, ūruta Yona ari hano." 
Matthew12:42 Umugabekazi w’igihugu c’i bumanuko azovana hasi n’ab’ iki gihe ku musi w’amateka, abatsindishe: kuko yavanywe ku mpera y’isi no kwumva ubgenge bga Salomo; kandi rāba, ūruta Salomo ari hano." 
Matthew12:43 Impwemu ihumanye iy’ ivuye mu muntu, ica ahatagira amazi, irondera uburuhukiro, ikabubura." 
Matthew12:44 Ikavuga, iti Reka nsubire mu nzu yanje navuyemwo. Ihashitse, igasanga igaragara, ikubuye, iteguritse." 
Matthew12:45 Igaca igenda, ikazana izindi mpwemu ndwi ziyirusha ububi, zikinjira, zikahaba. Ivya nyuma vy’uwo muntu bikarusha ivya mbere ububi. Ni ko bizoba no ku b’iki gihe kibi." 
Matthew12:46 Akivugana n’ishengero, nyina na bene nyina bāri bahagaze hanze, bagomba kubonana na we." 
Matthew12:47 Umwe aramubgira, at’ Ereg’ umuvyeyi wawe na barumuna bawe bahagaze hanze, baragomba ko mubonana." 
Matthew12:48 Yishura uno abimubgiye, ati Mama ni nde? Canke bene mama ni ba nde?" 
Matthew12:49 Atunga urutoke abigishwa biwe, ati Ngaba mama na bene mama." 
Matthew12:50 Kuk’ umuntu wese akora ivyo Data wo mw ijuru agomba ari we murumunanje na mushikanje na mama. 
Matthew13:1 Kur’ uwo musi Yesu asohoka ava mu nzu, yicara ku nkombe y’ikiyaga." 
Matthew13:2 Ishengero ryinshi rikoranira kuri we, bimutera gutambukira mu bgato, yicaramwo; ishengero ryose rihagarara i musozi." 
Matthew13:3 Ababgira vyinshi mu migani, aravuga, at’ Umubivyi yasohoye imbuto." 
Matthew13:4 Akibiba, zimwe zigwa i ruhande y’inzira, inyoni ziraza, zirazinobagura." 
Matthew13:5 Izindi zigwa ku rutare, hatar’ ivu ryinshi; zica zimera vuba, kukw ata vu ryinshi ririho." 
Matthew13:6 Izuba rirashe, ziraraba, kukw ata mizi zifise, zirūma." 
Matthew13:7 Izindi zigwa mu mahwa, amahwa arakura, arazinyoha." 
Matthew13:8 Izindi zigwa mw ivu ryiza, zihunda impeke, zimwe ijana, izindi mirongwitandatu, izindi mirongwitatu birtyo birtyo." 
Matthew13:9 Ūri n’amatwi ni yumve. 
Matthew13:10 Abigishwa baramwēgēra, baramubaza, bati Mbeg’ ikigutera kubigishiriza mu migani n’iki?" 
Matthew13:11 Arabishura, ati Mwebge mwahawe kumenya amabanga y’ubgami bgo mw ijuru, ariko bo ntibābihawe." 
Matthew13:12 Kuk’ ūfise azohabga, bikamucagatira; arik’ ūdafise azokwakwa n’ico yar’ asanzwe afise." 
Matthew13:13 Igituma mbabgirira mu migani, n’ukw iyo barāba batabona; kand’ iyo bumva batumva, badatahura." 
Matthew13:14 Kand’ ivyo uwavugishwa n’Imana Yesaya yavuze, bibashitseko, ngo Kwumva muzokwumva, ariko ntimuzoruha mubitahura; Kurāba muzorāba, ariko ntimuzoruha muvyihweza." 
Matthew13:15 Kuk’ umutima w’ubu bgoko ucuramye, Amatwi yabo akaba ari bihurugutwi, Amaso yabo bakayahumiriza: Ngo ntibarābishe amaso, Ntibumvishe amatwi, Ntibatahurishe imitima, Ngo bahindukire, Mbakize." 
Matthew13:16 Arikw amaso yanyu arahiriwe, kukw abona, n’amatwi yanyu, kuko yumva." 
Matthew13:17 Ndababgira ukuri yukw abavugishwa n’Imana benshi n’abagororotsi benshi bāhahamiye kubona ivyo mubona, ntibābibona, no kwumva ivyo mwumva, ntibāvyumva." 
Matthew13:18 Nuko mweho ni mutahure umugani w’umubivyi. 
Matthew13:19 Uwumva wese ijambo ry’ubgami ntarimenye, wa Mubi araza, agasahura ikibibge mu mutima wiwe. Uwo ni we yabibge i ruhande y’inzira." 
Matthew13:20 Uwabibge ku rutare ni we yumva ijambo, agaca aryakirana umunezero;" 
Matthew13:21 ariko ntagira imizi muri we, ahagarara umwanya muto; iyo yadutsweko n’amarushwa bo n’akadenderezo azira iryo jambo, bica bimutsitaza." 
Matthew13:22 Uwabibge mu mahwa ni we yumva iryo jambo, arik’ umwitwaririko w’ivy’ isi n’uruhendo rw’ubutunzi bikanyoha iryo jambo, akaba ikirumbirane." 
Matthew13:23 Uwabibge mw ivu ryiza ni we yumva iryo jambo, akaritahura, uwo ni we rero yama imbuto, umwe akagira ijana, uwundi mirongwitandatu, uwundi mirongwitatu, birtyo birtyo." 
Matthew13:24 Abacira uwundi mugani, at’ Ubgami bgo mw ijuru busa n’umuntu yabivye imbuto nziza mu ndimiro yiwe." 
Matthew13:25 Abantu basinziriye, haza umwansi wiwe abiba urwamfu mu buro hagati, arīgīra." 
Matthew13:26 Bumaze gusēsa no kuyangika, urwamfu ruca ruraboneka." 
Matthew13:27 Abashumba ba nyen’ urugo baraza baramubaza, bati Mbega mutungwa, ntiwabivye imbuto nziza mu ndimiro yawe? Non’ urwamfu rwavuye hehe?" 
Matthew13:28 Na we ati N’umuntu w’umwansi yagize artyo. Ba bashumba baramubaza, bati Non’ uragomba ko tugenda kurutororokanya?" 
Matthew13:29 At’ Oyaye, kuko kumbure mu kurandura urwamfu mworandurana n’uburo." 
Matthew13:30 Mureke bikurane vyompi gushitsa mw igenya. Maze mu gihe c’igenya nzobgira abagenyi, nti Mubanze mutororokanye urwamfu, muruhambire imikama, muruturire; arik’ uburo mubgimburire mu kigega canje." 
Matthew13:31 Abacira uwundi mugani, at’ Ubgami bgo mw ijuru busa n’akabuto ka sinapi, umuntu yābiriye akagatera mu ndimiro yiwe." 
Matthew13:32 Kandi ni kanzinya hanyuma y’imbuto zose, arikw iyo gakuze kaba kanini kakaruta ibirimwa vyose, kakaba igiti. Maz’ inyoni zo mu kirere zikaza zikārika mu mashami yaco." 
Matthew13:33 Abacira uwundi mugani, at’ Ubgami bgo mw ijuru busa n’umwambiro, umugore yābiriye akawuvanga n’ingero zitatu z’ifu, gushitsa ah’ iribututumbire yose." 
Matthew13:34 Ivyo vyose Yesu yabibgiye ishengero mu migani, nta co yababgiye atabaciriye umugani." 
Matthew13:35 Ni co catumye ivyo umuntu yavugishwa n’Imana yavuze biboneka, ngo Nzoteranura akanwa kanje, nce imigani, Nzovuga ivyahishijwe uhereye ku kuremwa kw’isi." 
Matthew13:36 Maz’ asezera ishengero, yinjira mu nzu. Abigishwa biwe baza kuri we, bati Dusobanurire umugani w’urwamfu rwo mu ndimiro." 
Matthew13:37 Na we arabishura, at’ Ūbiba imbuto nziza n’Umwana w’umuntu." 
Matthew13:38 Indimiro n’isi. Imbuto nziza ni bo bana b’ubgami. Urwamfu n’abana ba wa Mubi. 
Matthew13:39 Umwansi yarubivye ni wa Murwanizi. Igenya n’umuhero w’isi. Abagenyi n’abamarayika. 
Matthew13:40 Nk’uk’ urwamfu rutororokanywa rugaturirwa mu muriro, ni ko bizoba ku muhero w’isi." 
Matthew13:41 Umwana w’umuntu azotuma abamarayika biwe, na bo bazotororokanya ibitsitaza vyose n’abakoze ibizira, babikūre mu bgami bgiwe." 
Matthew13:42 Bazobaterera mw itanure ry’umuriro, ni ho hazoba amarira no kuryanya insya z’amenyo." 
Matthew13:43 Bun’ abagororotsi bazokwaka nk’izuba mu bgami bga Se. Ūri n’amatwi ni yumve. 
Matthew13:44 Ubgami bgo mw ijuru busa n’izahabu zanyegejwe mw itongo. Umuntu yazubutseko, arazihisha, aragenda, umunezero umutera gushōra ivy’ afise vyose, agura iryo tongo." 
Matthew13:45 Kand’ ubgami bgo mw ijuru busa n’umudandaza arondera imaragarita nziza. 
Matthew13:46 Abonye imaragarita imwe, y’igiciro kinini, aragenda, ashōra ivy’ afise vyose, arayigura." 
Matthew13:47 Kand’ ubgami bgo mw ijuru busa n’urusenga runiniya rwaterewe mu kiyaga, rukoranya ifi z’amoko yose." 
Matthew13:48 Rwuzuye, barukwegera i musozi, baricara barobanurira nziza mu gisangaza, mbi barazita." 
Matthew13:49 Uko ni ko bizoba ku muhero w’isi. Abamarayika bazoza, barobanure ababi mu bagororotsi," 
Matthew13:50 babaterere mw itanure ry’umuriro; ni ho hazoba amarira no kuryanya insya z’amenyo. 
Matthew13:51 Mbeg’ ivyo murabitahuye vyose? Baramwishura, bat’ Ego me." 
Matthew13:52 Na we arababgira, ati Ni co gituma umunyabgenge w’ivyanditswe wese, amaze guhinduka umwigishwa w’ivy’ ubgami bgo mw ijuru asa na nyen’ urugo asokorora mu vyo atunze ibintu bisha n’ivya kera." 
Matthew13:53 Yesu amaze guca iyo migani, avayo." 
Matthew13:54 Aja mu ntāra y’i wabo, yigishiriza mw isinagogi yabo, bituma batangara, bat’ Ubu bgenge n’ivyo bitangaza mbeg’ uyu yabikūye hehe?" 
Matthew13:55 Mbega si wa mwana w’umubāji? Nyina ntiyitwa Mariya, kand’ abavukana na we si Yakobo na Yosefu na Simoni na Yuda?" 
Matthew13:56 Bashiki biwe ntibar’i wacu bose? Non’ ivyo vyose yabikūye hehe? 
Matthew13:57 Ivyiwe birabatsitaza. Yesu arababgira, at’ Umuntu avugishwa n’Imana ntabura icubahiro, atari mu ntāra y’i wabo no mu nzu y’i wabo." 
Matthew13:58 Kandi nta bitangaza vyinshi yahakoreye, kubg’ ukutizera kwabo." 
Matthew14:1 Mur’ ico gihe umwami Herode yumva inkuru za Yesu. 
Matthew14:2 Abgira abagendanyi biwe, at’ Uwo ni Yohana Umubatizi yazutse mu bāpfuye; ni co gituma ivyo bitangaza bikorera muri we." 
Matthew14:3 Kuko Herode yari yarafashe Yohana, akamuboha, akamushira mw ibohero kubga Herodiya, muka Filipo mwene se." 
Matthew14:4 Kuko Yohana yari yarabgiye Herode, ati N’ikizira k’umwābiriye." 
Matthew14:5 Agomba kumwica, arikw atinya abantu, kuko bāmwiyumvira kw ar’ umuntu avugishwa n’Imana." 
Matthew14:6 Umusi wo kwibutsa ukuvuka kwa Herode ushitse, umukobga wa Herodiya atambira hagati ya bose, anezereza Herode." 
Matthew14:7 Ni co catumye amwemerera amurahiye kw amuha ico yomusaba cose. 
Matthew14:8 Na we amaze kwoshwa na nyina, ati Mpēra ngaha ku mubehe umutwe wa Yohana Umubatizi." 
Matthew14:9 Bun’ umwami arijirwa; ariko kubga za ndahiro, no kubg’ abāsangira na we, abgiriza ko bawumuha;" 
Matthew14:10 atuma mw ibohero ngo bace izosi Yohana. 
Matthew14:11 Bazana umutwe ku kibehe, bawuha wa mwigeme, awushīra nyina." 
Matthew14:12 Abigishwa biwe baraza, bajana ikiziga, baragihamba, maze baja kubikira Yesu." 
Matthew14:13 Yesu avyumvise, arahava, agenda mu bgato, aja ahantu h’agahinga kwiherērayo. Ishengero rivyumvise, riva mu bisagara, rimukurikira rijanye inkōkoro." 
Matthew14:14 Avuye mu bgato, abona ishengero ryinshi, rimutera akagongwe, abakiriza abarwaye." 
Matthew14:15 Bugorovye, abigishwa baramwēgēra, bati Mbega hano hantu kw ari mu gahinga, kandi bukaba buriko burīra: sezera abantu baje mu mihana kwirondereray’ ivyo kurya." 
Matthew14:16 Yesu arababgira, ati Ntibarinda kugenda: mube ari mwebge mubagaburira." 
Matthew14:17 Baramwishura, bati Nta vyo dufise hano atar’ udutsima dutanu n’udufi tubiri." 
Matthew14:18 Na we ati Ni mubinzanire hano. 
Matthew14:19 Abgira abantu kwicara hasi ku vyatsi, yābīra ya mitsima itanu na za fi zibiri, ararangamiza, arāba mw ijuru, arabihezagira; amanyagura ya mitsima, ayiha abigishwa, abigishwa bagaburira ishengero." 
Matthew14:20 Bararya bose, barahāga. Batororokanya utumanyagu tw’imisigazwa twuzura ibisimbo cumi na bibiri." 
Matthew14:21 Kand’ abāriye bār’ abagabo nk’ibihumbi bitanu, ukūyemw’ abagore n’abana." 
Matthew14:22 Uwo mwanya agōbēra abigishwa ngo batambukire mu bgato bītangire kujabuka hakurya, abanze gusezera ishengero." 
Matthew14:23 Ahejeje gusezera ishengero, adūga umusozi gusenga yiherereye. Bgagorovye ariyo ari wenyene gusa." 
Matthew14:24 Arik’ ubgato bushitse hagati mu kiyaga bāri batamijwe n’imipfunda, kuk’ umuyaga war’ ubaturutse imbere." 
Matthew14:25 Ku muteramyi agira kane, aza aho bari, agendesha amaguru hejuru ku kiyaga." 
Matthew14:26 Abigishwa bamubonye agendesha amaguru hejuru ku kiyaga, basimbga n’umutima, bati N’igihūme; baturishwa ubuku n’ubgoba." 
Matthew14:27 Uwo mwanya Yesu arababgira, ati Hūmura, ni jewe, ni mureke gutinya." 
Matthew14:28 Petero aramwishura, ati Mushingantahe, asangwa ari wewe, mbarira nze ah’ uri ku mazi." 
Matthew14:29 Na we ati Ngo. Petero yururuka mu bgato, agendesha amaguru ku mazi, ngw aje aho Yesu ari." 
Matthew14:30 Abonye igihuhuta, aratinya, atanguye kuroka arataka, ati Ntabara Mugenzi." 
Matthew14:31 Buno Yesu aramvura ukuboko, aramucakira, aramubgira, ati Yewe w’ukwizera guke, n’iki cagukekeranishije?" 
Matthew14:32 Būriye mu bgato, umuyaga uraca." 
Matthew14:33 Abāri mu bgato baramupfukamira, bati N’ukuri ur’ Umwana w’Imana." 
Matthew14:34 Bamaze kujabuka hakurya, bafata i musozi mu ntāra y’i Genesareti." 
Matthew14:35 Abantu b’aho hantu baramumenya, batumatumanako mur’ ico gihugu cose, bamuzanira abarwaye bose," 
Matthew14:36 baramwinginga ngo bakore ku buyonga bg’impuzu yiwe gusa, ababukozeko bose barakira." 
Matthew15:1 Maz’ Abafarisayo n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe baza kuri Yesu bavuye i Yerusalemu, baramubaza," 
Matthew15:2 bati N’iki gitumye abigishwa bawe barenga imigenzo twabgirijwe n’aba kera, ntibakarabe iyo bagira barye?" 
Matthew15:3 Na we arababaza, ati None mweho, n’iki catumye murenga icagezwe c’Imana kubg’ imigenzo yanyu?" 
Matthew15:4 Kukw Imana yavuze, iti Wubahe so na nyoko; kand’ it’ Ūtutse se canke nyina ntaz’ abure kwicwa." 
Matthew15:5 Ariko mweho, mugira mut’ Umuntu wese abgira se canke nyina, at’ Ico nari kugufashisha ni co nzoshikanira Imana," 
Matthew15:6 ntiyubahe se canke nyina. None mwatītūye ijambo ry’Imana kubg’ imigenzo yanyu. 
Matthew15:7 Mwa ndyarya mwe, Yesaya yavuze neza ivyo yavugishwa n’Imana kuri mwebge," 
Matthew15:8 at’ Aba bantu banyubahisha iminwa yabo, Arikw imitima yabo iri kure yanje." 
Matthew15:9 Bansengera ubusa, Kukw inyigisho bigisha ar’ ivyagezwe n’abantu." 
Matthew15:10 Ahamagara ishengero araribgira, ati Ni mwumve, mubitahure." 
Matthew15:11 Ikija mu kanwa si co gihumanya umuntu; arikw ikiva mu kanwa ni co kimuhumanya. 
Matthew15:12 Bun’ abigishwa baramwēgēra, baramubarira, bat’ Urazi yukw Abafarisayo bumvise iryo jambo bakavunika umutima?" 
Matthew15:13 Arabishura, at’ Igitewe cose, Data wo mw ijuru atāteye, kizorandurwa." 
Matthew15:14 Ni mubareke! N’impumyi zijana izindi. Arikw impumyi yojana iyindi mpumyi zompi zogwa mu cobo. 
Matthew15:15 Petero aramwishura, ati Dusobanurire uwo mugani." 
Matthew15:16 Na we aramubaza, ati Mbega namwe muracar’ imburabgenge?" 
Matthew15:17 Ntimutahura yukw ikintu cose kigiye mu kanwa kija mu nda kigaca mu nzira yaco? 
Matthew15:18 Arikw ibiva mu kanwa biba biturutse mu mutima, ni vyo bimuhumanya." 
Matthew15:19 Kuko mu mutima havamw’ ivyiyumviro bibi: ubgicanyi, ubusambanyi, ubushakanyi, ubgivyi, kwagiriza abandi ibinyoma, ibitutsi." 
Matthew15:20 Ivyo vyose ni vyo bihumanya umuntu. Ariko kurisha intoke zidakaravye si vyo bimuhumanya. 
Matthew15:21 Yesu arahava, aja ahegereye muri Tiro n’i Sidoni." 
Matthew15:22 Umunyakananikazi ava mu ntāra yaho aratakamba, ati Ngirira imbabazi se Mugenzi, Mwana wa Dawidi: umukobga wanje afashwe nabi na dayimoni." 
Matthew15:23 Na we ntiyamwishura ijambo na rimwe. Abigishwa biwe baza kuri we, baramwinginga, bati Murungike, kukw agenda aradusemerera inyuma." 
Matthew15:24 Arabishura, ati Sinatumwe ku bandi, atari ku ntama zazimiye z’inzu ya Isirayeli." 
Matthew15:25 Amushikiriye aramupfukamira, ati Ntabara se Mugenzi." 
Matthew15:26 Aramwishura, ati Si vyiza kwābira umutsima w’abana ukawuterera utubga." 
Matthew15:27 Na we ati Nka ko, Mugenzi, kuk’ utubga na two twīrīra utuvunguka dukorokera musi y’ameza ya ba nyene two." 
Matthew15:28 Buno Yesu aramwishura, at’ Ukwizera kwawe ni kwinshi nyina wanje: bikubere nk’uk’ ugomba. Umukobga wiwe aca akira uwo mwanya." 
Matthew15:29 Yesu arahava, aja ku kiyaga c’i Galilaya, adūga umusozi, yicaraho." 
Matthew15:30 Abantu benshi baza kuri we bazanye abacumbagira n’ibimuga n’impumyi n’ibiragi, n’abandi benshi, babashira imbere y’ibirenge vyiwe, arabakiza." 
Matthew15:31 Bituma ishengero ritangara ribonye ibiragi bivuga n’ibimuga bikomera n’abacumbagira bagenda neza n’impumyi zibona; bahimbaza Imana y’Abisirayeli. 
Matthew15:32 Yesu ahamagara abigishwa biwe, at’ Ishengero rinteye akagongwe, kuk’ uyu ar’ umusi ugira gatatu turi kumwe, none ntibagira ico barya. Ariko singomba kubasezera bashonje, ntibagwīre isari mu nzira." 
Matthew15:33 Abigishwa baramubaza, bati Twokūra hehe mur’ aka gahinga imitsima ingana irtyo yo guhāza iri shengero ringaho?" 
Matthew15:34 Yesu arababaza, ati Mufise imitsima ingahe? Na bo bati N’indwi, n’udufi dukeya." 
Matthew15:35 Abarira ishengero ngo ryicare hasi. 
Matthew15:36 Yābīra ya mitsima ndwi na za fi, arabishimira, arabimanyagura, abihereza abigishwa biwe, babigaburira ishengero." 
Matthew15:37 Bararya bose, barahāga; batororokanya imisigazwa y’utumanyagu, yuzura ibivumvu ndwi." 
Matthew15:38 Abāriye bar’ abagabo ibihumbi bine, ukūyemw’ abagore n’abana." 
Matthew15:39 Asezera ishengero, atambukira mu bgato, aja mu gihugu c’i Magadani." 
Matthew16:1 Abafarisayo n’Abasadukayo baraza, barondera kw abereka ikimenyetso kiva mw ijuru, bamugeza." 
Matthew16:2 Na we arabishura, at’ Iyo bugorovye, muravuga muti Buca haba umuco, kukw ijuru ryirasiye." 
Matthew16:3 Mu mutwenzi, muravuga muti Hagira hafurungane, kukw ijuru ryirasiye, kandi ryiraburaniwe. Murazi kugenzura ijuru uko risa, arikw ibimenyetso vy’ibihe ntimuzi kubigenzura." 
Matthew16:4 Ab’ igihe kibi c’ubumaka barondera ikimenyetso, kandi nta kimenyetso bazohabga, atar’ ikimenyetso ca Yona. Abasigaho, arīgīra." 
Matthew16:5 Abigishwa bafata hakurya, bāri bibagiye gutekera imitsima." 
Matthew16:6 Yesu arababgira, ati Mumenye, mwirinde umwambiro w’Abafarisayo n’Abasadukayo." 
Matthew16:7 Bībūranya bati Ntitwatekeye imitsima. 
Matthew16:8 Yesu arabimenya, arababaza, ati Yemwe ab’ukwizera guke, n’iki gitumye mwībūranya ngo nta mitsima mufise?" 
Matthew16:9 Ntimuraruha mubimenya, ntimwibutse ya mitsima itanu ku bihumbi bitanu, n’ibisimbo mwatororokanije uko vyangana?" 
Matthew16:10 Canke ya mitsima ndwi ku bihumbi bine, n’ibivumvu mwatororokanije uko vyangana?" 
Matthew16:11 N’iki kibabujije gutahura ko ntababgiye imitsima? Ariko mwirinde umwambiro w’Abafarisayo n’Abasadukayo. 
Matthew16:12 Buno batahura kw atababgiye kwirinda umwambiro w’umutsima butsima, ariko kw ar’ inyigisho z’Abafarisayo n’Abasadukayo." 
Matthew16:13 Yesu aja mu misozi ihera i Kayisariya mu bga Filipo, abaza abigishwa biwe, at’ Abantu bagira ng’ Umwana w’umuntu ndi nde?" 
Matthew16:14 Na bo bati Bamwe bagira ng’ uri Yohana Umubatizi, abandi ng’ uri Eliya, abandi ng’ uri Yeremiya cank’ umwe mu bavugishwa n’Imana." 
Matthew16:15 Arababaza, at’ Ariko mweho, mugira ngo ndi nde?" 
Matthew16:16 Simoni Petero aramwishura, at’ Uri Kristo, Umwana w’Imana nzima." 
Matthew16:17 Yesu aramwishura, at’ Ur’ umuhirwe, Simoni mwene Yona, kukw ata w’inyama n’amaraso yabiguhishuriye, ariko ni Data wo mw ijuru." 
Matthew16:18 Nanje ndakubgira yuk’ uri Petero, kandi kur’ urwo rutare nzorwubakakw ishengero ryanje, kand’ amarembo y’i kuzimu ntazorishobora." 
Matthew16:19 Nzoguha impfunguzo z’ubgami bgo mw ijuru: kand’ ico uzohambira mw isi kizoba gihambiriwe mw ijuru; n’ico uzohamburura mw isi kizoba gihamburuwe mw ijuru. 
Matthew16:20 Maze yihanikiriza abigishwa ngo ntihagire umuntu babgira kw ari we Kristo. 
Matthew16:21 Kuva ubgo Yesu atangura guserurira abigishwa biwe kw akwiye kuzoja i Yerusalemu no kuzobabazwa uburyo bginshi n’abashingantahe n’abaherezi bakuru n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe, no kuzokwicwa, no kuzozurwa ku musi ugira gatatu." 
Matthew16:22 Petero aramwihererana, atangura kumwamira, ati Ntibikāze, Mwami wanje, ntibize bikubeko na gato." 
Matthew16:23 Ahindukirira Petero, ati Herēra inyuma yanje, Satani; ur’ ikintsitaza, kukw ivy’ Imana atari vyo ubabaye, ubabaye ivy’ abantu." 
Matthew16:24 Buno Yesu abgira abigishwa biwe, at’ Umuntu ni yagomba kunkurikira, ni yiyanke, yikorere umusaraba wiwe, ankurikire." 
Matthew16:25 Kuk’ ūgomba gukiza ubugingo bgiwe azobubura, arik’ ūzoheba ubugingo bgiwe kubganje azoburonka." 
Matthew16:26 Kand’ umuntu vyomumarira iki kwunguka ivyo mw isi vyose ni yākwa ubugingo bgiwe kw icīru? Cank’ umuntu yotanga iki ngw acungure ubugingo bgiwe? 
Matthew16:27 Kuk’ Umwana w’umuntu azohava aza afise ubgiza bga Se, azananye n’abamarayika biwe; ni ho azoca yishura umuntu wese ibikwiranye n’ivyo yakoze." 
Matthew16:28 Ndababgire ukuri: Mur’ aba bahagaze hano harimwo bamwe batazobona urupfu gushitsa aho bazobonera Umwana w’umuntu aje mu bgami bgiwe. 
Matthew17:1 Imisi itandatu ishize, Yesu ajana Petero na Yakobo na mwene nyina Yohana, abadūgana igisozi kirekire ari bonyene." 
Matthew17:2 Ahinduka ukundi imbere yabo, mu maso hiwe haka nk’izuba, impuzu ziwe zera nk’umuco." 
Matthew17:3 Maze Mose na Eliya barababonekera, bavugana na we." 
Matthew17:4 Petero abgira Yesu, ati Mugenzi, bitubereye vyiza ko turi hano: ni wabigomba ndaca insago zitatu hano, rumwe rwawe, urundi rwa Mose, urundi rwa Eliya." 
Matthew17:5 Akivuga, haza igicu gikayangana, kibatera igitūtu; kand’ ijwi riva muri nya gicu, riti Nguyu Umwana wanje nkunda, akampimbara; ni mumwumve." 
Matthew17:6 Abigishwa bavyumvise, bubama hasi baratinya cane." 
Matthew17:7 Yesu arabēgēra, abakorako, ati Ve hasi, ntimutinye." 
Matthew17:8 Bunamuye amaso, ntibagira uwundi babona, atari Yesu wenyene." 
Matthew17:9 Bariko baramanuka ico gisozi, Yesu arabihanikiriza, ati Ntihagire umuntu mubgira ivyo mweretswe, gushitsa ah’ Umwana w’umuntu azozukira avuye mu bāpfuye." 
Matthew17:10 Abigishwa baramubaza, bati None rero n’iki gituma abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe bavuga yuko Eliya akwiye kubanza kuza?" 
Matthew17:11 Arabishura, ati Eliya azoza koko, aroranye vyose neza." 
Matthew17:12 Ariko ndababgira yuko Eliya yamaze kuza, yamara ntibāmumenye, ariko bamwigiriye uko bagomba kwose. Uko ni ko n’Umwana w’umuntu agira ababazwe na bo." 
Matthew17:13 Bun’ abigishwa batahura ko yababgiye Yohana Umubatizi. 
Matthew17:14 Bashikiriye ishengero, umuntu araza aramupfukamira," 
Matthew17:15 ati Mwami wanje, girira ikigongwe umwana wanje, kukw arwaye intandara, arasinzikaye cane. Kuko kenshi na kenshi agwa mu muriro no mu mazi." 
Matthew17:16 Namuzaniye abigishwa bawe, ariko vyabananiye kumukiza." 
Matthew17:17 Yesu arishura, ati Yemwe ab’ iki gihe mutizera b’ibidambidambi, nzogeza ryari kubana namwe; nzogeza ryari kubihanganira? Ni mumunzanire hano." 
Matthew17:18 Yesu aramukankamira, dayimoni amuvamwo, umuhungu aca akira uwo mwanya." 
Matthew17:19 Maz’ abigishwa baza kuri Yesu biherereye, baramubaza, bati Tweho n’iki catumye bitunanira kumusenda?" 
Matthew17:20 Arabishura, ati N’ukwizera kwanyu guke. Ndababgire ukuri: Namba mufise ukwizera kungana n’akabuto ka sinapi, mwobgira kino gisozi, mut’ Imuka aha, uje harya, kandi cokwimuka. Kandi nta kitazobashobokera. [" 
Matthew17:21 Ariko ben’ urya ntakūrwamwo n’ikindi atar’ ugusenga no kwisonzesha.] 
Matthew17:22 Bakigendagenda i Galilaya, Yesu arababgira, at’ Umwana w’umuntu azoshirwa mu maboko y’abantu," 
Matthew17:23 kandi bazomwica, maze ku musi ugira gatatu azozurwa. Barababara cane." 
Matthew17:24 Bashitse i Kaperinawumu, abatoza ikori ry’urusengero baza kuri Petero, baramubaza, bati Harya Umwigisha wanyu ntatanga ikigabane ca shekeli? Na we at’ Ego me, aragitanga." 
Matthew17:25 Binjiye mu nzu, Yesu aramwitanga, aramubaza, at’ Ugira ngw iki ga Simoni? Abami bo mw isi babugurisha canke batoza abahe? N’ababo canke n’abandi?" 
Matthew17:26 Aramwishura, ati N’abandi. Yesu aramubgira, ati Noneh’ ababo baracuna." 
Matthew17:27 Ariko twoye kubatsitaza, genda ku kiyaga, uteremw’ igera, wābīre ifi iribubanze gufatwa, uyasamike, urasangamwo shekeli; abe ari yo ujana, uyitange kubganje nawe." 
Matthew18:1 Mur’ uwo mwanya abigishwa baza kuri Yesu, baramubaza, bat’ Umukuru mu bgami bgo mw ijuru ni nde?" 
Matthew18:2 Ahamagara akana, agahagarika hagati yabo," 
Matthew18:3 arababgira, ati Ndababgire ukuri: Ni mutirimbura ngo mucike nk’abana bato, ntimuzoruha mwinjira mu bgami bgo mw ijuru." 
Matthew18:4 Nuk’ ūzokwicisha bugufi nk’aka kana ni we mukuru mu bgami bgo mw ijuru. 
Matthew18:5 Kand’ ūzokwākīra akana kamwe nk’aka mw izina ryanje azoba anyakiriye. 
Matthew18:6 Arik’ ūzotsitaza n’umwe mur’ abo bato banyizera, icoroshe n’uko yohambirirwa urusyo ruremereye kw izosi, akadobezwa i bgina mu kiyaga." 
Matthew18:7 Isi izobona ibara kubg’ ibitsitaza, kukw ivyo bitsitaza bitazobura kuza, arik’ uyo muntu azana igitsitaza azobona ibara." 
Matthew18:8 Ukuboko kwawe cank’ ikirenge cawe ni hagira ikigutsitaza muri vyo, ugice, ugite kure; vyokubera vyiza kwinjira mu bugingo ucitse igikonjo cank’ ikirenge, hak’ utererwa mu muriro utazima ufise amaboko yompi n’ibirenge vyompi." 
Matthew18:9 Kand’ ijisho ryawe ni ryagutsitaza, urinogore urite kure; vyokubera vyiza kwinjira mu bugingo upfuye ijisho, hak’ utererwa muri Gehinomu y’umuriro ufise amaso yompi." 
Matthew18:10 Mwirinde ntimukēngēre n’umwe mur’ aba bana bato: ndababgira yuko mw ijuru abamarayika babo bama barāba mu nyonga ha Data wo mw ijuru. [ 
Matthew18:11 Kand’ Umwana w’umuntu yaje gukiza icari cazimiye.] 
Matthew18:12 Mugira ngw iki? Umuntu afise intama ijana, imwe yozimira, ntiyosiga zimwe mirongwicenda n’icenda, akagenda mu misozi kurondera iyazimiye?" 
Matthew18:13 Kand’ iy’ ayibonye, ndababgira ukuri yukw ayinezererwa kuyirutisha zimwe mirongwicenda n’icenda zitāzimiye." 
Matthew18:14 Ni ko bidakundwa mu nyonga za So wo mw ijuru k’umwe mur’ abo bato apfa rubi. 
Matthew18:15 Mugenzawe ni yakugirira nabi, ugende umuhishuke mwiherereye; ni yakwumvira, uzoba wigaruriye mugenzawe." 
Matthew18:16 Ariko n’atakwumvira, ujane umwe canke babiri, kugira ngw ijambo ryose rize riringanizwe, bivuye mu kanwa k’ivyabona bibiri canke bitatu." 
Matthew18:17 N’atabumvira ubgire ishengero; ni yanka kwumvira ishengero na ryo, kuri wewe azoba nk’umunyamahanga n’umutozakori." 
Matthew18:18 Ndababgire ukuri: Ivyo muzohambira mw isi vyose bizoba bihambiriwe mw ijuru; kand’ ivyo muzohamburura mw isi vyose bizoba bihamburuwe mw ijuru. 
Matthew18:19 Kandi ndababgira ukuri yukw ababiri muri mwebge ni bahuriza inama mw isi gusaba ikintu cose, Data wo mw ijuru azokibakorera" 
Matthew18:20 Kukw aho babiri canke batatu bazoba bakoraniye mw izina ryanje, nanje nzoba ndi hagati muri bo." 
Matthew18:21 Maze Petero aza kuri we, aramubgira, ati Mushingantahe, incuti yanje ni yangirira nabi, nzomuharira ngeze kangahe? Ngeze indwi?" 
Matthew18:22 Yesu aramubgira, ati Jeho sinkubgira yuk’ ugeza indwi, arik’ ugeze indwi‐indwi gushitsa ibihetangabo mirongwirindwi." 
Matthew18:23 Ni co gituma ubgami bgo mw ijuru busa n’umwami yagomvye gusuzuma ivyo yabīkije abantu biwe. 
Matthew18:24 Atanguye guharūra, bamuzanira uwamurīriye umwenda w’italanto ibihumbi cumi." 
Matthew18:25 Ariko kukw atar’ afise ico yishura, shebuja agera ko bamugura, n’umugore, n’abana, n’ivy’ afise vyose, ng’ umwenda wishurwe." 
Matthew18:26 Wa muntu yikubita hasi, amwitembagaza imbere, ati Mwami, nyihanganira, nzokwishura vyose." 
Matthew18:27 Shebuja w’uyo muntu amugirira akagongwe, aramurekura, amuhebera wa mwenda amufitiye." 
Matthew18:28 Uno muntu asohotse, abona mugenzi we yamurīriye umwenda w’idenariyo ijana; aramufata, amugwa mu gahogo, ati Nyishura ivyo umperaniye." 
Matthew18:29 Uyo mugenzi we yikubita hasi, aramutakambira, ati Nyihanganira, nzokwishura vyose." 
Matthew18:30 Wa wundi aranka, aragenda, amushirisha mw ibohero, gushitsa ah’ azomwishurira ivy’ amufitiye." 
Matthew18:31 Bagenzi biwe babonye ibibaye, barababara cane, baragenda babgira shebuja ibibaye vyose." 
Matthew18:32 Buno shebuja aramuhamagaza, aramubgira, ati Wa muntu mubi we, naguhebeye wa mwenda wose aho wantakambira:" 
Matthew18:33 none nawe ntiwar’ ukwiye kugirira imbabazi mugenzawe, nk’uko nanje nazikugiriye?" 
Matthew18:34 Shebuja araraka, amuhereza abasoda, gushitsa ah’ azokwishurira ivy’ amufitiye vyose." 
Matthew18:35 Na Data wo mw ijuru ni kw azobagirira, ni mutāharirana, umuntu wese ngw aharire mugenzi we bivuye mu mutima." 
Matthew19:1 Yesu arangije ayo majambo, ava i Galilaya, aja mu gihugu c’i Yudaya hakurya ya Yorodani." 
Matthew19:2 Ishengero ryinshi riramukurikira, abakirizayo." 
Matthew19:3 Abafarisayo baza kuri we bamugeza, baramubaza, bati Mbega biremerwa k’umuntu yirukana umugore kubg’ inyanduruko y’ikintu cose?" 
Matthew19:4 Na we arabishura, ati Nta ho murasoma yuk’ uhereye mbere na mbere Rurema yabaremye bar’ uburyo bubiri," 
Matthew19:5 ikavuga, iti Ni co gituma umuntu azosiga se na nyina, akabana n’umugore wiwe akaramata, bompi bakaba umubiri umwe?" 
Matthew19:6 Bituma batakiri babiri, ariko baba babaye umubiri umwe. Nukw ico Imana yamatanije, umuntu ntaz’ akimature." 
Matthew19:7 Baramubaza, bati None se, n’iki catumye Mose agera ko bamuha icete co kuvāvānura, akamwirukana?" 
Matthew19:8 Arabishura, ati Mose yabarekuye kwirukana abagore banyu kukw imitima yanyu ikomantaye. Arik’ uhereye ubga mbere hose ntivyari bimeze birtyo." 
Matthew19:9 Ariko ndababgire: Umuntu wese yirukana umugore wiwe atamuhōye ubusambanyi, akābīra uwundi, aba asambanye; kand’ uwābīra uwahukanye aba asambanye." 
Matthew19:10 Abigishwa baramubgira, bat’ Ivy’ umugabo n’umugore asangwa bimeze birtyo, noneho kurongora n’ikigoye." 
Matthew19:11 Na we arababgira, ati Si bose bashobora kwemera iryo jambo, atar’ abābihawe." 
Matthew19:12 Kuko har’ inkone zavutse zirtyo uhereye kuva mu nda za ba nyina, kandi har’ inkone zakonwe n’abantu, kandi har’ inkone zīkona ubgazo kubg’ ubgami bgo mw ijuru. Ūshobora kuvyemera n’avyemere." 
Matthew19:13 Bamuzanira abana bato, ngw abarambikekw ibiganza, abasabire. Arikw abigishwa barabakankamira." 
Matthew19:14 Yesu arababgira, ati Ni mureke abana bato, ntimubabuze kuza aho ndi, kuk’ ubgami bgo mw ijuru ar’ ubg’ abameze bartyo." 
Matthew19:15 Abarambikakw ibiganza, avayo." 
Matthew19:16 Haza umuntu kuri we, aramubaza, ati Mwigisha, nkore iciza ki ngo ndonke ubugingo budashira?" 
Matthew19:17 Aramubaza, at’ Umbariza iki iciza? Inziza n’Imwe. Arikw asangw’ ugomba kwinjira mu bugingo, witondere ivyagezwe." 
Matthew19:18 Aramubaza, ati N’ibihe? Yesu aramwishura, ati Ntukice, ntugasambane, ntukibe, ntukāgirize abandi ibinyoma," 
Matthew19:19 wubahe so na nyoko, kand’ ukunde mugenzawe nk’uko wikunda." 
Matthew19:20 Wa musore aramubgira, at’ Ivyo vyose naravyitondeye; har’ ikindi mpajije?" 
Matthew19:21 Yesu aramubgira, at’ Asangw’ ugomba kuba agahore, genda ushōre ivyo utunze, ugabire aboro, ni ho uzogira itunga mw ijuru, utek’ uze, unkurikire." 
Matthew19:22 Uwo musore yumvise iryo jambo, agenda ababaye, kuko yar’ afise itunga ryinshi." 
Matthew19:23 Yesu abgira abigishwa biwe, ati Ndababgire ukuri: Biragoye k’umutunzi yinjira mu bgami bgo mw ijuru." 
Matthew19:24 Kandi ndababgira yukw icoroshe ar’ ingamiya guca mu zuru ry’urushinge biruta k’umutunzi yinjira mu bgami bg’Imana. 
Matthew19:25 Abigishwa bavyumvise baratangara cane, bati None rero, ni nde ashobora gukizwa?" 
Matthew19:26 Yesu arabītegereza, arababgira, ati Kubg’ abantu ico ntigishoboka, ariko ku Mana vyose birashoboka." 
Matthew19:27 Buno Petero aramubaza, ati Mbega twebge ko twaretse vyose tukagukurikira; none tuzohabga iki?" 
Matthew19:28 Yesu arababgira, ati Ndababgira ukuri yuko mwebge abankurikiye, ah’ Umwana w’umuntu azovyagirira ku ntebe y’ubgiza bgiwe, igihe co kuvyarwa ukundi gusha, namwe muzokwicara ku ntebe cumi na zibiri, mucire imanza imiryango cumi n’ibiri y’Abisirayeli." 
Matthew19:29 Umuntu wese yasize urugo canke bene nyina canke bashiki be canke se canke nyina cank’ abana cank’ itongo kubg’ izina ryanje, azobishumbushwa umurengera, kand’ azoragwa ubugingo budashira." 
Matthew19:30 Ariko benshi b’imbere bazoba ab’ inyuma, kand’ ab’ inyuma bazoba ab’ imbere." 
Matthew20:1 Ubgami bgo mw ijuru busa na nyen’ urugo azindutse kurondera abamukorera mu ruzabibu rwiwe. 
Matthew20:2 Ategeranya n’abakozi ku musi kubaha idenariyo, abarungika mu ruzabibu rwiwe." 
Matthew20:3 Nko kw isaha zitatu aragenda, abona abandi bīhagarariye mu kaguriro ata co bakora." 
Matthew20:4 Na bo arababgira, ati Namwe ni mugende mu ruzabibu, ndabagerera ivyo mukwiranye. Baragenda." 
Matthew20:5 Yongera kugenda kw isaha zitandatu no ku y’icenda, agira kuno." 
Matthew20:6 Kandi nko kw isaha cumi n’imwe aragenda, abona abandi bīhagarariye; arababgira, ati Mbega ko mwahagaze hano umusi wose ata co mukora?" 
Matthew20:7 Baramwishura, bati N’ukw ata waturaritse. Arababgira, ati Namwe ni mungīre mu ruzabibu." 
Matthew20:8 Bugorovye, nyen’ uruzabibu abgira umukoresha wiwe, ati Hamagara abakozi, ubagerere ingero zabo, utangurire mu bo hanyuma gushitsa ku ba mbere." 
Matthew20:9 Abaje kw isaha cumi n’imwe bahabga idenariyo imwe‐imwe. 
Matthew20:10 Abātanguye kare bāje, bagira ngo bagererwa ibirenze. Ariko bahabga idenariyo imwe‐imwe na bo." 
Matthew20:11 Bayahawe bidodombera nyen’ uruzabibu," 
Matthew20:12 bat’ Abaherutse kuza, bagakora isaha imwe gusa, none k’ubaringanije natwe twacumukuye umurango wose no mu ndugumba!" 
Matthew20:13 Na we yishura umwe muri bo, ati Mugenzi wanje, sinkugiriye nabi; ntitwemeranije idenariyo imwe?" 
Matthew20:14 Fata iyawe, ugende. Uyo wo hanyuma nagomvye kumugerera nkawe." 
Matthew20:15 Har’ ikimbuza kugira uko ngomba mu vyanje? Cank’ ugize ijisho ribi kuko jewe ndi mwiza? 
Matthew20:16 Uko ni kw ab’ inyuma bazoba ab’ imbere, kand’ ab’ imbere bazoba ab’ inyuma." 
Matthew20:17 Yesu agira adūge i Yerusalemu, yihererana na ba bigishwa cumi na babiri, maze bari mu nzira arababgira," 
Matthew20:18 at’ Ehe turadūze i Yerusalemu, kand’ Umwana w’umuntu azoshirwa mu maboko y’abaherezi bakuru n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe, bazomucira urubanza rwo gupfa," 
Matthew20:19 kandi bazomuha abanyamahanga ngw ashinyagurirwe, atonagurwe, abambge, kandi ku musi ugira gatatu azozurwa." 
Matthew20:20 Buno nyina wa bene Zebedayo aza kuri we, ari kumwe n’abahungu biwe, aramupfukamira, amusaba ijambo." 
Matthew20:21 Aramubaza, at’ Uragomba iki? Na we ati Bivuge, aba bahungu banje babiri ngo baze bicare umwe i buryo bgawe uwundi i bumoso mu bgami bgawe." 
Matthew20:22 Yesu arishura, ati Ntimuzi ico musaba. Mwoshobora kunywera ku gikombe jewe ngira nnywereko? Na bo bati Turashobora." 
Matthew20:23 Arababgira, at’ Igikombe canje koko muzokinywerako, ariko gutanga ivyicaro i buryo bganje n’i bumoso, s’ivyanje, atar’ abo Data yabiteguriye." 
Matthew20:24 Bamwe cumi bavyumvise, bitonganiriza ivy’ abo babiri bavukana." 
Matthew20:25 Yesu arabahamagara, arababgira, ati Murazi yukw abaganwa b’amahanga bayatwaza amanyama, kandi n’abakuru bayo bayagirak’ ububasha." 
Matthew20:26 Muri mwebge si ko biri. Arik’ ūgomba kuba mukuru muri mwebge az’ abe umukozi wanyu; 
Matthew20:27 kand’ ūgomba kuba uw’ imbere az’ abe umuja wanyu," 
Matthew20:28 nk’uk’ Umwana w’umuntu atāzanywe no gukorerwa, atar’ ugukorera abandi, no gutanga ubugingo bgiwe kw incungu ya benshi." 
Matthew20:29 Bakiva i Yeriko ishengero ryinshi riramukurikira. 
Matthew20:30 Impumyi zibiri zari zicaye i ruhande y’inzira, zumvise yuko Yesu ahaciye ziratakamba, ziti Mwami, mwana wa Dawidi, tugirire imbabazi." 
Matthew20:31 Ishengero rirazizibiranya ngo zihore. Zirushiriza gutakamba, ziti Mwami, mwana wa Dawidi, tugirire imbabazi." 
Matthew20:32 Yesu arahagarara, arazihamagara, arazibaza, ati Mugomba ko mbakorera iki?" 
Matthew20:33 Ziti Tugomba kw amaso yacu ahumūka Mwami. 
Matthew20:34 Yesu azigirira akagongwe, akora ku maso yazo, zica zirahumūka, baramukurikira." 
Matthew21:1 Bageze hafi y’i Yerusalemu, bashikira i Betifage ku musozi wa Elayono, Yesu atuma abigishwa babiri," 
Matthew21:2 arababarira, ati Mugende mur’ iriya mihana ir’ imbere yanyu, muca mubona indogoba iziritseho n’inyana yayo; muziziture, muzinzanire." 
Matthew21:3 Ni hagira ūbabaza, mumubgire, muti Databuja ni we azigomba. Aca azirungika." 
Matthew21:4 Ivyo vyabayeho ngw ivyavuzwe n’uwavugishwa n’Imana bishike," 
Matthew21:5 ngo Mubgire umukobga w’i Siyoni, Muti Rāba, Umwami wawe aje kuri wewe, Ar’ umutekerezi, agendera ku ndogoba, Mbere ni ku mukangara, inyana y’indogoba." 
Matthew21:6 Abigishwa baragenda, babigenza nk’uko Yesu yababgiye," 
Matthew21:7 bazana indogoba n’inyana yayo, bazisasakw impuzu zabo, yicarako." 
Matthew21:8 Abenshi mw ishengero basasa impuzu zabo mu nzira, abandi baca amashami y’ibiti, bayasasa mu nzira." 
Matthew21:9 Kand’ ishengero rimugiye imbere n’irimukurikiye rirasemerera, riti Hoziyana, mwana wa Dawidi, hashemezwe ūje mw izina ry’Uhoraho, hoziyana mw ijuru." 
Matthew21:10 Ashitse i Yerusalemu, igisagara cose kirashwabaduka, barabaza, bat’ Uyo ni nde?" 
Matthew21:11 Abo mw ishengero barabishura, bat’ Uyo n’ūvugishwa n’Imana, Yesu w’i Nazareti i Galilaya."
