Matthew21:12 Yesu yinjira mu rusengero rw’Imana, ahindira hanze abadandariza mu rusengero n’abaruguriramwo bose, ahenura ameza y’abavunja amahera n’intebe z’abāriko baragurwakw inuma." 
Matthew21:13 Arababgira, ati Handitswe ngw Ingoro yanje izokwitwa inzu yo gusengeramwo, ariko mwebge mwayihinduye nk’isenga ry’abambuzi." 
Matthew21:14 Maz’ impumyi n’abacumbagira baza kuri we mu rusengero, arabakiza." 
Matthew21:15 Abaherezi bakuru n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe babonye ibitangaza akoze, n’abana basemererera mu rusengero, ngo Hoziyana mwana wa Dawidi; baritonganya," 
Matthew21:16 baramubaza, bat’ Urumva ivyo bavuga? Yesu arabishura, at’ Ego me; nta ho murasoma, ngo Mu kanwa k’abana bato n’abonka waroranijemw’ ishimwe?" 
Matthew21:17 Abasigaho, asokoroka mu gisagara, aja i Betaniya, arārayo." 
Matthew21:18 Kare mu gatondo arikw arasubira mu gisagara, yumva arashonje." 
Matthew21:19 Abonye umusukoni ku nzira, arawēgēra, ntiyagira ico awubonako, atar’ amababi gusa, arawubarira, ati Ntugapfe wamye insukoni uhereye ubu ugashitsa ibihe bidashira. Uwo musukoni uca ukabirana uwo mwanya." 
Matthew21:20 Abigishwa babibonye, baratangara, bati Mbeg’ uyu musukoni uyu mwanya ukabiranijwe n’iki?" 
Matthew21:21 Yesu arabishura, ati Ndababgire ukuri: Iyo muba muri n’ukwizera, mudakekeranya, ntimwokora ic’ uyu musukoni gusa, ariko mwobgira n’uyu musozi, muti Shingūka, utabge mu kiyaga; vyoba ko." 
Matthew21:22 Kand’ ivyo muzosaba vyose musenze, mwizeye, muzobihabga." 
Matthew21:23 Yinjiye mu rusengero, arikw arigisha, abaherezi bakuru n’abashingantahe b’ubgo bgoko baza kuri we, baramubaza, bati N’ububasha ki bugutera gukora ivyo? Kandi ni nde yaguhaye ubgo bubasha?" 
Matthew21:24 Yesu arabishura, ati Nanje hinge ndababaze ijambo rimwe; ni mwarinyishura nanje mpeze ndababarire ububasha bunkoresha ivyo." 
Matthew21:25 Non’ ukubatiza kwa Yohana kwaturutse hehe? Ni mw ijuru, canke ni mu bantu? Bībūranya muri bo, bati Ni twavuga tuti Ni mw ijuru; ahava atubaza, ati N’iki cababujije kumwemera?" 
Matthew21:26 Kandi ni twavuga tuti Ni mu bantu; n’uko dutinya ishengero, kuko bose bavuga yuko Yohana yar’ ūvugishwa n’Imana." 
Matthew21:27 Bishura Yesu, bati Ntituhazi. Na we ati Nuko rero nanje simbabgira ububasha bunkoresha ivyo." 
Matthew21:28 Mugira ngw iki? Hābaye umuntu yar’ afise abahungu babiri: aragenda abarira umukuru, ati Genda, mwana wanje, uyu musi uje gukora mu ruzabibu." 
Matthew21:29 Aramwishura, at’ Eka singenda. Maze hanyuma aririmbura, aragenda." 
Matthew21:30 Aja ku wa kabiri, amubgira kuno. Aramwishura, ati Ndagiye muvyeyi; ntiyajayo." 
Matthew21:31 None mur’ abo bompi n’uwuhe yakoze ivyo se agomba? Baramwishura, bati N’uwa mbere. Yesu arababgira, ati Ndababgira ukuri yukw abatozakori n’abasambanyikazi babatanga kwinjira mu bgami bg’Imana." 
Matthew21:32 Kuko Yohana yaje muri mwebge agendera mu nzira yo kugororoka, kandi ntimwamwemera. Arikw abatozakori n’abasambanyikazi baramwemeye. Namwe mubibonye, no hanyuma ntimwirimbura ngo mumwemere." 
Matthew21:33 Ni mwumvīre uwundi mugani: Hābaye nyen’ urugo yateye uruzabibu; aruzitirira uruzitiro, yimbamw’ ubgato bg’ikinogo, yubakamw’ umutara, arusigarana abarimyi, aja mu mahanga." 
Matthew21:34 Nukw igihe c’iyera kigomba kugera, atuma abakozi biwe kuri ba barimyi ngo babahe inzabibu ziwe." 
Matthew21:35 Maz’ abo barimyi bafata ba bakozi biwe, umwe baramushishagura, uwundi baramwica, uwundi bamutera amabuye." 
Matthew21:36 Yongera gutuma abandi bakozi barengeye aba mbere; babagira kuno. 
Matthew21:37 Hanyuma abatumak’ umwana wiwe, ati Bazosonera umwana wanje." 
Matthew21:38 Abo barimyi babonye wa mwana wiwe, baravugana, bat’ Urya ni we samuragwa: ni muze tumwice, tuze twegukire umwandu wiwe." 
Matthew21:39 Baramufata bamuhindira inyuma y’uruzabibu, baramwica." 
Matthew21:40 None nyen’ uruzabibu ni yiyizira azobagira ate, abo barimyi?" 
Matthew21:41 Baramwishura, bat’ Abo babi azobica rubi, uruzabibu arusigarane abandi barimyi, bazohora bamuha inzabibu igihe cazo." 
Matthew21:42 Yesu arababaza, ati Nta ho murasoma mu vyanditswe, ngw Ibuye abubatsi bāgaye Ni ryo ryahindutse irigumya imfuruka: Ivyo vyavuye k’Uhoraho, Kandi n’igitangaza mu maso yacu?" 
Matthew21:43 Ni co gitumye mbabgira yuk’ ubgami bg’Imana muzobgakwa, bugahabga ihanga ryama imbuto zabgo." 
Matthew21:44 Arik’ ūzogwa kur’ iryo buye azovunagurika; arik’ uwo rizogwako rizomuvungura. 
Matthew21:45 Maz’ abaherezi bakuru n’Abafarisayo bumvise iyo migani yiwe, bamenya kw ari bo avuga." 
Matthew21:46 Barondeye ingene bomufata, batinya abantu, kuko bamwiyumvira kw ar’ ūvugishwa n’Imana." 
Matthew22:1 Yesu yongera kuvuganira na bo mu migani," 
Matthew22:2 at’ Ubgami bgo mw ijuru busa n’umwami atahisha ubukwe bg’umwana wiwe arongora. 
Matthew22:3 Atuma abagendanyi biwe, ngo bahamagare abātōrewe gutaha ubukwe, banka kuza." 
Matthew22:4 Yongera gutuma abandi bagendanyi, ati Mubgire abatowe, muti Rāba amazimano yiwe yayiteguye, n’amapfizi n’amagumba vyiwe vyābāzwe, kandi vyose biriteguwe: ni muze mutahe ubukwe." 
Matthew22:5 Ariko barirengagiza barīgīra, umwe aja mw itongo ryiwe, uwundi mu bidandazwa vyiwe." 
Matthew22:6 Abasigaye bafata abo bagendanyi biwe, babakorera ibara, barabica." 
Matthew22:7 Uwo mwami araraka, agomora ingabo ziwe, ahonnya abo bicanyi, ayigiza igisagara cabo." 
Matthew22:8 Maz’ abgira abagendanyi biwe, at’ Ubukwe buriteguwe, arikw abābutorewe ntibāri babukwiye." 
Matthew22:9 Nuko ni mugende mu mayirabiri, abo muribuboneyo bose mubahamagare, baze babutahe." 
Matthew22:10 Abo bagendanyi baragenda baja mu nzira bakoranya abo babonye bose, ababi n’abeza; mu bukwe huzura ababutorewe." 
Matthew22:11 Umwami yinjiye kurāba abatowe abonamw’ umuntu atambaye impuzu y’ubukwe; 
Matthew22:12 aramubaza, ati Mugenzi wanje, winjiye ute hano utambaye impuzu y’ubukwe? Arajorerwa." 
Matthew22:13 Maz’ umwami abgira abakozi biwe, ati Ni mumubohe amaboko n’amaguru, mumuterere hanze mu mwiza; ni ho hazoba amarira n’ukuryanya insya z’amenyo." 
Matthew22:14 Kukw abatowe ari benshi, arikw abatoranijwe bakaba bake." 
Matthew22:15 Bun’ Abafarisayo baragenda baja inama, ngo baronke ingene bomutegera mu majambo yovuga." 
Matthew22:16 Bamutumakw abigishwa babo hamwe n’abantu ba Herode, bati Mwigisha, turazi yuk’ ur’ umunyakuri, kandi ko wigisha inzira y’Imana vy’ukuri, kandi k’udatinya umuntu n’umwe ku kigohe; kuk’ udatinya ijunja ry’abantu:" 
Matthew22:17 non’ utubgire, wiyumvira ute? Biremerwa gutanga ikori rya Kayisari, canke ntivyemerwa?" 
Matthew22:18 Ariko Yesu amenya ububi bgabo, arababaza, ati Mungereza iki ga mwa ndyarya mwe?" 
Matthew22:19 Ni munyereke ihera ry’ikori. Bamuzanira idenariyo. 
Matthew22:20 Arababaza, at’ Iki gishushanyo n’ibi vyanditsweko n’ivya nde?" 
Matthew22:21 Bati N’ivya Kayisari. Bun’ arababgira, ati Nuko rer’ ivya Kayisari ni mubihe Kayisari, ivy’ Imana mubihe Imana." 
Matthew22:22 Bavyumvise baratangara, bamusigaho barīgīra." 
Matthew22:23 Nya musi Abasadukayo baza kuri we, abahakana yukw ata kuzuka kuriho, baramubaza," 
Matthew22:24 bati Mwigisha, Mose yavuze ng’umuntu ni yapfa adasize abana, mwene nyina acūre umugore wiwe, ngw ahonore mwene nyina." 
Matthew22:25 I wacu hār’ abavukana ndwi. Uwa mbere yararongoye, arapfa, maze kukw adasize umwana umugore wiwe amuraga mwene nyina." 
Matthew22:26 Nuko n’uwa kabiri, n’uwa gatatu biba birtyo gushitsa ku wa ndwi." 
Matthew22:27 Hanyuma ya bose nya mugore arapfa. 
Matthew22:28 None mw izuka azoba muka nde mur’ abo ukw ar’ indwi? Ko bari bamufise bose! 
Matthew22:29 Yesu arabishura, ati Mwarazimiye, ko mutāmenye ivyanditswe n’ubushobozi bg’Imana." 
Matthew22:30 Mw izuka ntibazorongora kandi ntibazoshingirwa: bazoba nk’abamarayika bo mw ijuru. 
Matthew22:31 Arikw ivyo kuzuka kw’abapfuye nta ho murasoma ico Imana yababgiye," 
Matthew22:32 iti Ni jewe Mana ya Aburahamu, Imana ya Isaka, Imana ya Yakobo? Imana s’iy’ abapfuye, n’iy’ abariho." 
Matthew22:33 Ishengero rivyumvise, ritangazwa n’inyigisho ziwe." 
Matthew22:34 Abafarisayo bumvise ko Yesu yajoreje Abasadukayo, bakoranira hamwe." 
Matthew22:35 Umwe muri bo w’umwigisha w’ivyagezwe aramubaza amugeza," 
Matthew22:36 ati Mwigisha, ibgirizwa risumba ayandi mu vyagezwe n’irihe?" 
Matthew22:37 Aramwishura, ati Mukundishe Uhoraho Imana yanyu imitima yanyu yose n’ubugingo bganyu bgose n’ubgenge bganyu bgose." 
Matthew22:38 Iryo ni ryo rihambaye rya mbere. 
Matthew22:39 Har’ irindi rya kabiri rimeze nka ryo, n’iri: Mukunde bagenzi banyu nk’uko mwikunda." 
Matthew22:40 Kur’ ayo mabgirizwa yompi ivyagezwe vyose n’amajambo y’abavugishwa n’Imana ni yo vyenenako. 
Matthew22:41 Abafarisayo bagikoraniye hamwe, Yesu arababaza," 
Matthew22:42 at’ Ivya Kristo muvyiyumvira mute? Ni mwene nde? Baramwishura, bati Ni mwene Dawidi." 
Matthew22:43 Na we arababaza, ati None Dawidi mu vya Mpwemu yamwitiye iki Umwami?" 
Matthew22:44 at’ Uhoraho yabariye Umwami wanje, At’ Icara i buryo bganje, Ushitse aho nzoshirira abansi bawe musi y’ibirenge vyawe." 
Matthew22:45 None Dawidi ko yamwise Umwami, yoshobora ate kuba umwana wiwe?" 
Matthew22:46 Ntihāgira ūshobora kumwishura ijambo na rimwe, kand’ uhereye kur’ uwo musi nta muntu yubahutse gusubira kumubaza ikindi." 
Matthew23:1 Maze Yesu abarira ishengero n’abigishwa biwe," 
Matthew23:2 at’ Abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe n’Abafarisayo bicaye ku ntebe ya Mose. 
Matthew23:3 Nukw ivyo bababgira vyose mubikore, muvyitondere. Ariko ntimukurikire ibikorwa vyabo, kukw ivyo bavuga atari vyo bakora." 
Matthew23:4 Kandi bahambira imitwaro iremereye igoye itwara, bakayikoreza abantu ku bitugu, arik’ ubgabo ntibagomba kuyikozako n’urutoke." 
Matthew23:5 Arikw ibikorwa vyabo vyose babikora kugira ngo barābge n’abantu, kukw amambe yabo yanditswemw’ amajambo y’Imana bayagira manini, ubuyonga bg’ impuzu zabo bakabgongereza." 
Matthew23:6 Bakunda ivyicaro vyo haruguru aho batumiwe, n’intebe z’icubahiro mu masinagogi," 
Matthew23:7 no kugirwako bgakeye mu tuguriro, no kwitwa n’abantu: Rabi." 
Matthew23:8 None, ntimukitwe Rabi, kuk’ umwigisha wanyu ar’ umwe, namwe mwese mur’ abavukana." 
Matthew23:9 Kandi ntimukīte umuntu wo mw isi Data, kuko So ar’ umwe, ar’ uwo mw ijuru." 
Matthew23:10 Kandi ntimukīyite umuranzi, kuk’ umuranzi wanyu ar’ umwe, ari Kristo." 
Matthew23:11 Arik’ umukuru muri mwebge az’ abe umukozi wanyu. 
Matthew23:12 Ūzokwishira hejuru azocishwa bugufi, kand’ ūzokwicisha bugufi azoshirwa hejuru." 
Matthew23:13 Muzobona ibara, mwebge abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe n’Abafarisayo, mwa ndyarya mwe, kuko mwugarirana ubgami bgo mw ijuru imbere y’abantu: kandi ntimubginjiramw’ ubganyu, n’abagomba kubginjiramwo ntimubakundira. [" 
Matthew23:14 Muzobona ibara, mwebge abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe n’Abafarisayo, mwa ndyarya mwe, kuko mukirya ingo z’abapfakazi musengesha menshi muhumba: ni co gituma muzocirwa urubanza ruruta izindi.]" 
Matthew23:15 Muzobona ibara, mwebge abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe n’Abafarisayo, mwa ndyarya mwe, kuko mukwiragira mu kiyaga no ku misozi ngo muhindure n’umwe abe uw’ idini yanyu; iy’ ahindutse, mutuma abarusha kabiri kuba umwana wa Gehinomu." 
Matthew23:16 Muzobona ibara, mwa ndongozi zihumye mwe, muvuga mut’ Ūzorahira urusengero s’ikigoye, arik’ ūzorahira izahabu yo mu rusengero azoba yikwegeye umwenda." 
Matthew23:17 Mwa bipfu n’impumyi mwe, non’ igihambaye n’ikihe: n’izahabu canke n’urusengero rweza izahabu?" 
Matthew23:18 Kandi ng’ Ūzorahira igicaniro s’ikigoye, arik’ ūzorahira ishikanwa ririko azoba yikwegeye umwenda." 
Matthew23:19 Mwa mpumyi mwe, non’ igihambaye n’ikihe, n’ishikanwa, canke n’igicaniro ceza ishikanwa?" 
Matthew23:20 Nuk’ ūrahiye igicaniro aba akirahiranye n’ibiriko vyose," 
Matthew23:21 kand’ ūrahiye urusengero aba arurahiranye n’Īrubamwo," 
Matthew23:22 kand’ ūrahiye ijuru aba arahiye intebe y’Imana n’Iyivyagirako. 
Matthew23:23 Muzobona ibara, mwebge abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe n’Abafarisayo, mwa ndyarya mwe, mutanga ikigiracumi c’imbgija na anisi na kumino, ariko mwaretse ibihambaye vyo mu mabgirizwa, guca izibereye, n’imbabazi, n’ukwizera; arikw ivyo mwari mukwiye kubikora, vya bindi na vyo ntimubireke." 
Matthew23:24 Mwa ndongozi zihumye mwe, muramimina agatūku, arikw ingamiya murayiyongobeza." 
Matthew23:25 Muzobona ibara, mwebge abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe n’Abafarisayo, mwa ndyarya mwe, kuko mwoza igikombe n’inkōko inyuma, arikw imbere vyuzuye ubgambuzi n’ukutigarura." 
Matthew23:26 Wa Mufarisayo uhumye we, banza woze imbere mu gikombe no mu nkōko, inyuma havyo na ho habone kwera." 
Matthew23:27 Muzobona ibara, mwebge abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe n’Abafarisayo, mwa ndyarya mwe, kuko musa n’imva zihomeshejwe ingwa, ziboneka inyuma zīkuyengeje, arikw imbere zuzuye amagufa y’abapfuye n’ibihumanya vyose." 
Matthew23:28 Namwe ni ko muri: inyuma mubonekera abantu mur’ abagororotsi, arikw imbere mwuzuye uburyarya n’ubugarariji." 
Matthew23:29 Muzobona ibara, mwebge abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe n’Abafarisayo, mwa ndyarya mwe, kuko mwubakira imva z’abāvugishwa n’Imana, mugashariza ivyibutso vy’abagororotsi," 
Matthew23:30 mukavuga mut’ Iyo tuba twariho mur’ ico gihe ca ba sogokuruza, ntitwari gufatanya na bo kuvisha amaraso y’abāvugishwa n’Imana." 
Matthew23:31 Uko ni ko mwiyagiriza ko mur’ abana b’abishe abāvugishwa n’Imana. 
Matthew23:32 None ni mwuzurize ingero ya ba sogokuruza banyu. 
Matthew23:33 Mwa nzoka mwe, mwa bana b’inzoka, muzohunga mute urubanza rwa Gehinomu?" 
Matthew23:34 Ehe ngira ntume abavugishwa n’Imana n’abanyabgenge bo n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe; bamwe muri bo muzobica, mubabambe, abandi muzobatonagurira mu masinagogi yanyu, mubatuza mu bisagara vyose;" 
Matthew23:35 bitayeko muzokorwa n’amaraso yose y’abagororotsi yaviriye kw isi, uhereye ku maraso ya Abeli umugororotsi ukageza ku maraso ya Zakariya mwene Barakiya mwiciye hagati y’ahēra h’urusengero n’igicaniro." 
Matthew23:36 Ndababgire ukuri: Ivyo vyose bizoshika ku b’iki gihe. 
Matthew23:37 Ewe Yerusalemu! Ewe Yerusalemu! Wica abavugishwa n’Imana, ugatera amabuye abagutumweko, ni kangahe nagomvye gukoranya abana bawe, nk’ukw inkoko ikoranya imiswi yayo iyibundikira mu vyubi vyayo, ntimwakunda!" 
Matthew23:38 Rāba inzu yanyu muyitānywe ar’ umusaka. 
Matthew23:39 Kuko mbabgira yuko mutazosubira kumbona kuva ubu, kugeza aho muzovugira, muti Hashemezwe ūje mw izina ry’Uhoraho." 
Matthew24:1 Yesu arasohoka ava mu rusengero; akigenda abigishwa biwe baramwēgēra ngo bamwereke inyubako y’urusengero. 
Matthew24:2 Arababgira, ati Ntimubona ivyo vyose? Ndababgire ukuri: Aha ntihazosigazwa ibuye rigeretse ku rindi, ridasamburiwe hasi." 
Matthew24:3 Yicaye ku musozi wa Elayono, abigishwa biwe baramwēgēra bihereranye, baramubaza, bati Tubgire, ivyo bizobaho ryari, kand’ ikimenyetso kizoba iki c’ukuza kwawe n’ic’ umuhero w’isi?" 
Matthew24:4 Yesu arabishura, ati Mwirinde, ntihagire ūbazimiza." 
Matthew24:5 Kuko benshi bazoza mw izina ryanje, bati Ni jewe Kristo, kandi bazozimiza benshi." 
Matthew24:6 Muzokwumva intambara n’impuha z’intambara: mwirinde, ntimugahagarike imitima; kuko bitazobura kubaho, arik’ umuhero uzoba utaraza." 
Matthew24:7 Kukw ihanga rizotera irindi hanga, n’ubgami buzotera ubundi bgami; amapfa no kunyiganyiga kw’isi bizobaho henshi;" 
Matthew24:8 arikw ivyo vyose n’itanguriro ryo kuramukwa. 
Matthew24:9 Ni ho bazobatanga ngo muzigirizwe, bazobica, kandi muzokwankwa n’amahanga yose, abahōra izina ryanje." 
Matthew24:10 Ni ho benshi bizobatsitaza, bazoryarukana, bazokwankana." 
Matthew24:11 Kandi hazokwaduka abīgira abavugishwa n’Imana benshi, bazimize benshi." 
Matthew24:12 Maze kuk’ ubugarariji buzogwira urukundo rw’abenshi ruzotimba. 
Matthew24:13 Arik’ uwihangana, agashitsa kw iherezo, ni we azokira." 
Matthew24:14 Kand’ ubu butumwa bgiza bg’ubgami buzovugwa mw isi yose, ngo bube ikimenyetso kibere icabona amahanga yose, maz’ umuhero uzoca uza." 
Matthew24:15 Nukw aho muzobonera ca kizira c’ubuyobe bg’ubugesera, gihagaze ahantu hēra, cavuzwe na Daniyeli yavugishwa n’Imana — ūsoma ni yiyubare —" 
Matthew24:16 ico gihe abazoba bar’ i Yudaya baze bahungire ku misozi miremire," 
Matthew24:17 ūzoba ari hejuru ku nzu ntaze yururutswe no gusahura ibiri mu nzu yiwe," 
Matthew24:18 ūzoba ari mu mirima ntaz’ asubizwe inyuma no gusahura umutamana wiwe. 
Matthew24:19 Ariko mur’ iyo misi abazoba batwaye inda n’abonsa bazobona ibara. 
Matthew24:20 Kandi muze musenge kugira ng’ uruhungo rwanyu ntiruze rube mu rushana canke kw isabato. 
Matthew24:21 Kuko mur’ iyo misi hazoba amarushwa ahambaye atigeze kubaho kuva kw itanguriro ry’isi ugashitsa n’ubu, kandi ntazokwongera kubaho." 
Matthew24:22 Kand’ iyo misi iy’ itagerurwa ntihorokotse umuntu n’umwe; ariko kubg’ abatoranijwe iyo misi izogerurwa. 
Matthew24:23 Ico gihe ni hāgira umuntu ababgira, at’ Ehe Kristo ari hano, canke, at’ Ari hariya: ntimuze muvyemere." 
Matthew24:24 Kuko hazokwaduka abīgira Kristo n’abīgira abavugishwa n’Imana, bagakora ibimenyetso bihambaye n’ibitangaza, kugira ngo bazimize n’abātoranijwe ni vyashoboka." 
Matthew24:25 Rāba ndabibabgiye bitaraba. 
Matthew24:26 Nuko ni bababgira, bat’ Eh’ ari mu bugaragwa, ntimuze mujeyo; canke, ngw Ari haruguru mu mpete, ntimuze muvyemere." 
Matthew24:27 Nk’uk’ umuravyo urabiriza i burasirazuba ukabonekera iyo rirengera, ni k’ukuza kw’Umwana w’umuntu kuzomera." 
Matthew24:28 Ah’ umuvyimba uri hose, ni ho ibinyakabaka bizokoranira." 
Matthew24:29 Hanyuma y’ayo marushwa y’ico gihe, uwo mwanya izuba rizocura umwiza, n’ukwezi ntikuzoba kucaka umuco wakwo, n’inyenyeri zizokoragurika zive kw ijuru, n’ivy’ inkomezi vyo mu majuru bizonyiganyizwa." 
Matthew24:30 Bun’ ikimenyetso c’Umwana w’umuntu kizobonekera kw ijuru, ni ho amoko yose yo mw isi azoboroga, bazobona Umwana w’umuntu aje mu bicu vyo kw ijuru ari n’ububasha n’ubgiza bginshi." 
Matthew24:31 Azotuma abamarayika biwe n’ijwi rirenga ry’inzamba, bakoranye abatoranijwe biwe, bave mu birēre bine, guhēra iy’ ijuru ritangurira kugeza iyo riherera." 
Matthew24:32 Ni mwigire ku musukoni umugani wawo: ishami ryawo iyo ritoshe, amababi agatutuza, mumenya yukw agatāsi kari hafi." 
Matthew24:33 Nuko namwe, ni mwabona ivyo vyose bishitse, muze mumenye kw ari hafi, ku rugi." 
Matthew24:34 Ndababgire ukuri: Ab’ iki gihe ntibazorangira, ivyo vyose bitarashika." 
Matthew24:35 Ijuru n’isi bizorangira, arikw amajambo yanje nta co azoba." 
Matthew24:36 Arik’ uwo musi cank’ iyo saha nta wubizi, n’iyo boba abamarayika bo mw ijuru, cank’ Umwana w’Imana, atari Data gusa." 
Matthew24:37 Kand’ uko vyari biri mu misi ya Nowa ni ko bizoba mu kuza kw’Umwana w’umuntu. 
Matthew24:38 Kukw ari ko bāri bameze mu misi umwuzure utaribgatere: bārarya, bāranywa, bārarongora, bārashingira, bageza kuri wa musi Nowa yinjiye muri bga bgato," 
Matthew24:39 ntibagira ico bamenya kugeza ah’ umwuzure waziye ubatwara bose; ni k’ukuza kw’Umwana w’umuntu kuzomera. 
Matthew24:40 Ico gihe abagabo babiri bazoba mu murima, umwe azojanwa, uwundi arekwe." 
Matthew24:41 Abagore babiri bazoba bariko barasēra hamwe ku rusyo, umwe azojanwa, uwundi arekwe." 
Matthew24:42 Nuko mwame mugavye, kuko mutazi umusi Umwami wanyu azozako." 
Matthew24:43 Arikw ibi mubimenye: iyaba nyen’ urugo yar’ asanzwe azi igihe igisuma kiziramwo, yogavye, ntiyokunze kw inzu yiwe yimbga." 
Matthew24:44 Nuko namwe mwame mwiteguye, kuk’ Umwana w’umuntu azoza mu gihe mutiyumviriye." 
Matthew24:45 None ni nde mushumba wo kwizigirwa w’ubgenge shebuja yosigarana abo mu rugo rwiwe, ngw abagaburire igihe kigeze?" 
Matthew24:46 Hahirwa uwo mushumba shebuja agarutse azosanga akora artyo. 
Matthew24:47 Ndababgira ukuri yukw azomuha kugaba ivy’ afise vyose. 
Matthew24:48 Arik’ umushumba mubi ni yibgira mu mutima wiwe, ati Databuja aracatevye:" 
Matthew24:49 maz’ agatangura gukubita abashumba bagenzi biwe no gusangira n’ababorerwa; 
Matthew24:50 shebuja w’uwo mushumba azoza ku musi atamwiteze no mu gihe atazi: 
Matthew24:51 azomucamwo kubiri, amusangize umugabane wiwe n’indyarya: ni ho hazoba amarira no kuryanya insya z’amenyo." 
Matthew25:1 Ico gihe ubgami bgo mw ijuru buzosa n’inkumi cumi, zajanye amatara yazo, zija gusanganira umukwe." 
Matthew25:2 Batanu muri bo bār’ ibijuju, bandi batanu bār’ abanyabgenge." 
Matthew25:3 Kuko vya bijuju, mu kujana amatara yavyo, bitajananye n’amavuta." 
Matthew25:4 Arikw abanyabgenge bo, bajananye n’amavuta mu macupa yabo hamwe n’amatara yabo." 
Matthew25:5 Umukwe agitebaganye bose barahūnyiza, barasinzira." 
Matthew25:6 Mu gicugu humvikana urwamo, ngo Nguyu umukwe, ni musohoke mumusanganire." 
Matthew25:7 Buno za nkumi zose zirazanzamuka, zitunganya amatara yazo." 
Matthew25:8 Vya bijuju bibgira abanyabgenge, biti Ni muduhe se ku mavuta yanyu, kukw amatara yacu arikw arazima." 
Matthew25:9 Arikw abanyabgenge barabishura, bati Kumbure ntiyodukwira twese: ivyiza ni muje ku badandaza mwigurire." 
Matthew25:10 Bakigiye kugura umukwe arashika; abiteguye binjirana na we mu bukwe, urugi rurugarwa." 
Matthew25:11 Mu nyuma za nkumi zindi na zo ziraza, ziti Mupfasoni, mupfasoni, n’utwugururire." 
Matthew25:12 Na we arabishura, ati Ndababgire ukuri: Simbazi." 
Matthew25:13 Nuko mwame mugavye kuko mutazi umusi cank’ isaha. 
Matthew25:14 Bizoba nk’ivy’ umuntu agira agende mu mahanga, ahamagara abantu biwe, abasigarana ivyo atunze." 
Matthew25:15 Umwe amuha italanto zitanu, uwundi zibiri, uwundi imwe, uk’ umuntu wese ashobora, aja mu mahanga." 
Matthew25:16 Uwo mwanya uwahawe italanto zitanu aragenda arazicurūza, yungukamw’ izindi talanto zitanu." 
Matthew25:17 N’uwa zibiri abigenza artyo, yungukamw’ izindi zibiri." 
Matthew25:18 Arik’ uwahawe imwe arīgīra, yimba mu kuzimu, ahisha amahera ya shebuja." 
Matthew25:19 Hashize igihe kirekire, shebuja w’abo bantu aragaruka, asuzuma ivyo yabasigaranye." 
Matthew25:20 Uwari yahawe italanto zitanu araza, azana italanto zindi zitanu, ati Mugenzi, wari wansigaranye italanto zitanu, ehe nungutsemw’ izindi talanto zitanu." 
Matthew25:21 Shebuja aramubgira, ati Wagize neza, muntu wanje mwiza wo kwizigirwa, wizigiwe kuri bike, nzoguha kugaba vyinshi. Injira mu munezero wa shobuja." 
Matthew25:22 Haza uwari yahawe italanto zibiri, ati Mugenzi, wari wansigaranye italanto zibiri, ehe nungutsemw’ izindi talanto zibiri." 
Matthew25:23 Shebuja aramubgira, ati Wagize neza, muntu wanje mwiza wo kwizigirwa, wizigiwe kuri bike, nzoguha kugaba vyinshi. Injira mu munezero wa shobuja." 
Matthew25:24 Kandi haza uwahawe italanto imwe, ati Mugenzi, nari nkuzi k’ur’ umuntu w’ingāre, wimbura ivyo utārimye, ukumakuma ivyo utāsanzaje;" 
Matthew25:25 ndatinya, ndagenda mpisha italanto yawe mu kuzimu: ehe ngibi ivyawe." 
Matthew25:26 Shebuja aramwishura, ati Wa muntu wanje mubi we, wa kinebge we, war’ uzi ko nimbura ivyo ntārimye, nkumakuma ivyo ntāsanzaje." 
Matthew25:27 Nuko war’ ukwiye kujana amahera yanje mu bayacurūza, nanje nagaruka nkaronka ayanje n’inyungu yayo." 
Matthew25:28 Nuko ni mumwake italanto, muyihe ūfise italanto cumi." 
Matthew25:29 Kuk’ ūfise wese azohabga, asesekarizwe: arik’ ūdafise azokwakwa n’ico yar’ afise." 
Matthew25:30 N’uyo muntu wanje w’imburakimazi ni mumute hanze mu mwiza, ni ho hazoba amarira no kuryanya insya z’amenyo." 
Matthew25:31 Arik’ Umwana w’umuntu ah’ azozira afise ubgiza bgiwe ari kumwe n’abamarayika biwe bose, ni ho azovyagira ku ntebe yiwe y’ubgiza:" 
Matthew25:32 amahanga yose azokoranirizwa mu nyonga ziwe, na we azobarobanura, nk’uk’ umwungere arobanura intama mu mpene." 
Matthew25:33 Intama azoziherereza i buryo bgiwe, impene na zo i bumoso." 
Matthew25:34 Maz’ Umwami azobgira abar’ i buryo bgiwe, ati Ni muze, abo Data yahezagiye, muragwe ubgami mwateguriwe, uhereye ku kuremwa kw’isi." 
Matthew25:35 Nari nshonje, murangaburira, nari mfise inyota, mumpa ico nnywa; nar’ ingenzi, mumpa indāro;" 
Matthew25:36 nagenda gusa, muranyambika; nari ndwaye, muza kurāba uko mmeze; nari mw ibohero, muza kundāba." 
Matthew25:37 Maz’ abagororotsi bazomubaza, bati Mwami, twakubonye ryari ushonje, tukakugaburira; cank’ ufise inyota, tuguha ico unywa?" 
Matthew25:38 Twakubonye ryari ur’ ingenzi, tuguha indāro; cank’ ugenda gusa tukakwambika?" 
Matthew25:39 Twakubonye ryari urwaye, cank’ uri mw ibohero, tuza kukurāba?" 
Matthew25:40 Umwami na we azobishura, ati Ndababgire ukuri: Ko mwabigiriye umwe mur’ aba bene Data bari hanyuma y’abandi, ni jewe mwabigiriye." 
Matthew25:41 Maz’ azobgira n’abar’ i bumoso, ati Mva i ruhande, mwa bivume mwe, muje mu muriro utazima wateguriwe wa Murwanizi n’abamarayika biwe." 
Matthew25:42 Nari nshonje, ntimwangaburira; nari mfise inyota ntimwampa ico nnywa;" 
Matthew25:43 nar’ ingenzi, ntimwampa indāro; nagenda gusa, ntimwanyambika; nari ndwaye, nari mw ibohero, ntimwaza kundāba." 
Matthew25:44 Maze na bo bazomwishura, bati Mwami, twakubonye ryari ushonje, cank’ ufise inyota, cank’ ur’ ingenzi, cank’ ugenda gusa, cank’ urwaye, cank’ uri mw ibohero, ntitwagira ico tugukorera?" 
Matthew25:45 Maz’ azobishura, ati Ndababgire ukuri: Ko mutabigiriye umwe mur’ aba bari hanyuma y’abandi, nanje ntimwabingiriye." 
Matthew25:46 Abo bazoja mu gihano kidashira, arikw abagororotsi bazoja mu bugingo budashira." 
Matthew26:1 Yesu arangije ayo majambo yose, abgira abigishwa biwe," 
Matthew26:2 ati Murazi yukw imisi ibiri ni yashira, hazoba Pasika, kand’ Umwana w’umuntu azotangwa abambge." 
Matthew26:3 Maz’ abaherezi bakuru n’abakuru b’ubgo bgoko bakoranira mu rugo rw’umuherezi mukuru yitwa Kayafa," 
Matthew26:4 baja inama yo gusuka Yesu ngo bamufate, bamwice." 
Matthew26:5 Ariko, bati Ntitumufate mu misi mikuru, hoye kuvyuka umugūmūko mu bantu." 
Matthew26:6 Yesu ar’ i Betaniya mu nzu kwa Simoni umunyamibembe," 
Matthew26:7 umugore aza kuri we afise ikebano ry’amavuta atāmirana y’igiciro kinini cane, ayamusuka ku mutwe, arikw ararya." 
Matthew26:8 Arikw abigishwa babibonye, baritonganya, bati Mbeg’ ubu buhombe n’ubg’ iki?" 
Matthew26:9 Aya yoshoboye kugurwa vyinshi bigahabga aboro. 
Matthew26:10 Yesu avyumvise arababgira, ati Mubabariza iki uyu mugore? Ankoreye igikorwa ciza." 
Matthew26:11 Aboro muramana imisi yose, ariko jeho ntituja kwamana imisi yose." 
Matthew26:12 Igitumye ansuka ayo mavuta ku mubiri n’ukuntegurira guhambga. 
Matthew26:13 Ndababgire ukuri: Ah’ ubu butumwa bgiza buzovugwa hose mw isi yose, n’ico uyu akoze na co kizovugwa kibe icibutso ciwe." 
Matthew26:14 Maz’ umwe muri bamwe cumi na babiri, yitwa Yuda Isikaryota, aja ku baherezi bakuru," 
Matthew26:15 arababaza, ati Mwompēra iki, nkazomubaronkera? Bamugerera intete z’ifeza mirongwitatu." 
Matthew26:16 Aherakw arondera uburyo bgo kumubaronkera. 
Matthew26:17 Ku musi w’intangamarāra wo kurya imitsima itambiwe abigishwa baza kuri Yesu, baramubaza, bat’ Ugomba ko tugutegurira hehe ah’ uriburīre ivya Pasika?" 
Matthew26:18 Arabishura, ati Ni muje mu gisagara kwa ntuze, mumubarire, mut’ Umwigisha agize ngw Igihe ciwe kiri hagufi, agira asangirire ivya Pasika n’abigishwa biwe i wawe." 
Matthew26:19 Abigishwa bagira nk’uko Yesu yababariye, bategura ivya Pasika." 
Matthew26:20 Bugorovye, yicarana n’abigishwa biwe cumi na babiri ngo basangire." 
Matthew26:21 Bariko bararya, arababgira, ati Ndababgira ukuri yuk’ umwe muri mwebge agira angure." 
Matthew26:22 Barababara cane, batangura kumubaza umwe‐umwe, bati Ni jewe ga Mugenzi?" 
Matthew26:23 Arabishura, at’ Uwo duhūje amaboko mu gukoza mu mubehe, ni we angura." 
Matthew26:24 Umwana w’umuntu agira agende, uko vyanditswe kuri we; arik’ uwo muntu agura Umwana w’umuntu azobona ibara: uwo muntu ivyomubereye vyiza iyaba atāvutse." 
Matthew26:25 Yuda amugura aramubaza, ati Ni jewe ga Mwigisha? Na we at’ Urarivuze." 
Matthew26:26 Bariko bararya, Yesu yābīra umutsima, awuhezagiye arawumanyagura, awuha abigishwa, ati Ni mwābīre, murye, uyu n’umubiri wanje." 
Matthew26:27 Yābīra igikombe, agishimira Imana, arakibaha, ati Ni mukinywereko mwese," 
Matthew26:28 kukw iki ar’ amaraso yanje y’isezerano, aviriye benshi ngo baharirwe ivyaha." 
Matthew26:29 Ariko ndababgira yuk’ uhereye none ntazokwongera kunywa kur’ izi nzabibu ugashitsa kuri wa musi nzosangirira namwe umutobe wazo musha mu bgami bga Data. 
Matthew26:30 Bahejeje kuririmba, barasohoka baja ku musozi wa Elayono." 
Matthew26:31 Maze Yesu arababgira, ati Mwebge mwese mur’ iri joro ivyanje bihava bibatsitaza; kuko handitswe, ngo Nzokubita umwungere, intama z’umukuku zisanzare." 
Matthew26:32 Ariko ni namara kuzurwa, nzobītangira imbere kuja i Galilaya." 
Matthew26:33 Maze Petero aramwishura, at’ Ivyawe n’iyo vyotsitaza bose, jeho nta ho bizontsitaza." 
Matthew26:34 Yesu aramubgira, ati Ndakubgira ukuri yuko mur’ iri joro inkoko itarabika, uhava unyihakana gatatu." 
Matthew26:35 Petero aramubgira, ati N’iyo noba nkwiye gupfana nawe, sinokwihakana. N’abigishwa bose bavuga bartyo." 
Matthew26:36 Maze Yesu ashikana na bo ahantu hitwa i Getsemane, abgira abigishwa biwe, ati Ba muricaye hano, mbanze nje harya gusenga." 
Matthew26:37 Ajana Petero na bene Zebedayo bompi, atangura kubabara no guhagarika umutima cane." 
Matthew26:38 Arababgira, at’ Umutima wanje uri n’akabonge kagomba kunyica: ba muragumye aha, mubane maso nanje." 
Matthew26:39 Yunguruza imbere gatoya, arubama, arasenga, ati Data, asangwa vyoshoboka, iki gikombe ni kindēngāne: ariko ntibibe uko jewe ngomba, yamara bibe uko wewe ugomba." 
Matthew26:40 Agaruka ku bigishwa, asanga basinziriye, abaza Petero, at’ Ubgo ntimurushe mubana maso nanje n’isaha n’imwe?" 
Matthew26:41 Ni mube maso, musenge, ntimuje mu mosha mabi. Umutima ni wo ukunze, arik’ umubiri ufise intege nke." 
Matthew26:42 Yongera kugenda ubga kabiri, arasenga, ati Data, asangwa bidashoboka yukw iki kindēngāna, shiti nkinywereyeko, ni bibe nk’uk’ ugomba." 
Matthew26:43 Yongera kugaruka asanga basinziriye, kukw amaso yabo yar’ aremerewe." 
Matthew26:44 Yongera kubasigaho, aragenda, asenga ubga gatatu, avuga amajambo amwe n’aya mbere." 
Matthew26:45 Maz’ agaruka ku bigishwa, arababarira, ati Ni mwisinzirire noneho, muruhuke. Eh’ igihe kirashitse, Umwana w’umuntu ashizwe mu maboko y’abanyavyaha." 
Matthew26:46 Ni muvyuke, tugende, eh’ ūnguze ari hafi." 
Matthew26:47 Akivuga, Yuda, umwe muri bamwe cumi na babiri, araza, azananye n’igitero cinshi, kizanye inkota n’amahiri, kivuye ku baherezi bakuru n’abashingantahe b’ubgo bgoko." 
Matthew26:48 Arik’ ūmugura yari yabahaye ikimenyetso, at’ Uwo nja gusoma azoba ari we; mumufate." 
Matthew26:49 Ako kanya ashikīra Yesu, aramubgira, ati N’amahoro ga Mwigisha? Maz’ aramusomagura." 
Matthew26:50 Yesu aramubarira, ati Mugenzi wanje, ikikuzanye n’ugikore. Buno baraza, bashōrera amaboko kuri Yesu, baramufata." 
Matthew26:51 Maz’ umwe mu bāri kumwe na Yesu atuma ukuboko, asokōra inkota yiwe, ayikubita umushumba w’umuherezi mukuru, amuca ugutwi." 
Matthew26:52 Buno Yesu aramubarira, ati Subiza inkota yawe ahayo; kukw ababanguye inkota bose bazokwicwa n’inkota." 
Matthew26:53 Ugira ngo sinoshobora kwinginga Data, na we akandungikira ubu nyene abamarayika basāga legiyono cumi na zibiri?" 
Matthew26:54 Non’ ivyanditswe vyoshika bite kw ari ko bikwiye kuba? 
Matthew26:55 Uwo mwanya Yesu abaza ico gitero, ati Mbega munziye kumfata nk’umwambuzi, muzanye inkota n’amahiri? Ko nicara mu rusengero nigisha imisi yose ntimumfate?" 
Matthew26:56 Arikw ivyo vyose bibaye, kugira ngw ivyanditswe n’abāvugishwa n’Imana bishike. Bun’ abigishwa bose baramuta, barahunga." 
Matthew26:57 Abāfashe Yesu bamujana kwa Kayafa, umuherezi mukuru, ni ho abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe n’abashingantahe bāri bakoraniye." 
Matthew26:58 Ariko Petero amuja inyuma barenga arenguka, gushitsa ku rugo rw’umuherezi mukuru, ashika imbere, yicarana n’abagendanyi ngw arābe amaherezo." 
Matthew26:59 Abaherezi bakuru n’abashingantahe b’amakombe bose baronderera Yesu ibirego vy’ibinyoma, ngo babone ingene bomwica." 
Matthew26:60 Ariko barabibura, naho haje abīgize ivyabona benshi. Ubuheruka haza babiri," 
Matthew26:61 bat’ Uyo yagize ngo yoshobora gusambura urusengero rw’Imana, akarwubaka mu misi itatu." 
Matthew26:62 Umuherezi mukuru arahaguruka, aramubaza, ati Nta co wiregura? Aba bakwagirije iki?" 
Matthew26:63 Ariko Yesu arihorera. Umuherezi mukuru aramubgira, ati Ndakurahiye Imana nzima, tubarire kw ari wewe Kristo, Umwana w’Imana." 
Matthew26:64 Yesu aramwishura, at’ Urarivuze; yamara ndababgira yuk’ uhereye ubu muzobona Umwana w’umuntu yicaye i buryo bg’Ububasha, aje mu bicu vyo kw ijuru." 
Matthew26:65 Bun’ umuherezi mukuru yitantamurirakw impuzu ziwe, at’ Ararogose; turacaronderera iki ivyabona? Ehe murīyumviye ingen’ arogose:" 
Matthew26:66 mugira ngw iki? Na bo baramwishura, bat’ Akwiye gupfa." 
Matthew26:67 Buno bamuvuma amate mu maso, bamukubita ibipfunsi, abandi baramubīngūra," 
Matthew26:68 bati Yewe Kristo, dupfindūre: ni nde agukubise?" 
Matthew26:69 Ariko Petero yari yicaye hanze mu rugo. Incoreke iza ah’ ari, iti Nawe nyene mwari kumwe na Yesu Umunyagalilaya." 
Matthew26:70 Na we abihakanira mu maso ya bose, at’ Ico uvuze sindanakizi." 
Matthew26:71 Yungururije mu bikingi vy’irembo, iyindi ncoreke iramubona, ibarira abar’ aho, iti N’uyu nyene yari kumwe na Yesu Umunyanazareti." 
Matthew26:72 Yongera kubihakana arahira, at’ Uyo muntu sindanamuzi." 
Matthew26:73 Hahise akanya, abahagazeho baramwēgēra, babgira Petero, bati N’ivy’ ukuri nawe ur’ uwo muri bo; bitayeko n’imvugo yawe iraguhinyuza." 
Matthew26:74 Bun’ atangura kurahira arīsiba, at’ Uyo muntu sindanamuzi. Uwo mwanya inkoko irabika;" 
Matthew26:75 Petero yibuka ijambo Yesu yamubgiye, at’ Inkoko itarabika uja kunyihakana gatatu. Arenga irembo, araturika ararira." 
Matthew27:1 Umutwenzi utambitse abaherezi bakuru bose n’abashingantahe b’ubgo bgoko bagīra inama Yesu ngo bamwice. 
Matthew27:2 Baramuboha baramujana, bamushikiriza Pilato, icēgēra ca Kayisari." 
Matthew27:3 Maze Yuda yamuguze, abonye Yesu ko bamutsindishije, aricuza, asubiza abaherezi bakuru n’abashingantahe za ntete z’ifeza mirongwitatu," 
Matthew27:4 ati Nācumuye, naguze amaraso y’ūtagira icaha. Na bo baramwishura, bati Bidutwaye iki? N’ivyawe." 
Matthew27:5 Aterera izo ntete z’ifeza ahēra h’urusengero, aragenda, arīmanika." 
Matthew27:6 Abaherezi bakuru bāndūra zino feza, bati Ntizemerwa gushirwa mu mashikanwa, kukw ar’ ibiguze amaraso." 
Matthew27:7 Baja inama, bazigura ubgatsi n’umubumvyi, ngo baze bahahambe injabuka." 
Matthew27:8 Ni co catumye ubgo bgatsi bgitwa Ubgatsi bg’amaraso, na bugingo n’ubu." 
Matthew27:9 Ni ho ivyavuzwe na Yeremiya yavugishwa n’Imana vyashikiye, ngo Bābiriye za ntete z’ifeza mirongwitatu, ni zo giciro yaciriwe, uwo bamwe mu Bisirayeli baciriye," 
Matthew27:10 bazigura ubgatsi n’umubumvyi, nk’uk’ Uhoraho yambariye." 
Matthew27:11 Ariko Yesu yar’ ahagaze mu maso ya ca cēgēra ca Kayisari; ico cēgēra kiramubaza, kiti Ni wewe Mwami w’Abayuda? Yesu aramwishura, at’ Urarivuze." 
Matthew27:12 Ariko mu vyo arezwe n’abaherezi bakuru n’abashingantahe ntiyishura na rimwe. 
Matthew27:13 Pilato aramubaza, ati Ntiwumva ingene bakwagiriza vyinshi?" 
Matthew27:14 Ariko ntiyamwishura n’ijambo na rimwe, bituma ico cēgēra gitangara cane." 
Matthew27:15 Mur’ iyo misi mikuru icēgēra camenyereye kurekurira abantu imbohe imwe, iyo bagomba." 
Matthew27:16 Kandi bāri n’imbohe imwe yari rurangiranwa yitwa Baraba. 
Matthew27:17 Bakoranye, Pilato arababaza, at’ Uwo mugomba ko ndabarekurira ni nde? Ni Baraba, canke ni Yesu yitwa Kristo?" 
Matthew27:18 Kuko yamenye yukw ishari ari ryo rimubatangishije. 
Matthew27:19 Acicaye ku ntebe y’imanza umugore wiwe amutumako, ati Ntihagire ico ugira uwo mugororotsi; kuko narāye ndose mbona mbabazwa vyinshi kubgiwe." 
Matthew27:20 Arikw abaherezi bakuru n’abashingantahe bosha ishengero ngo rimusabe Baraba, ryicishe Yesu." 
Matthew27:21 Ico cēgēra kirababaza, kiti Mur’ abo bompi uwo mugomba ko ndabarekurira ni nde? Na bo baramwishura, bati Ni Baraba." 
Matthew27:22 Pilato arababaza, ati None Yesu yitwa Kristo, we ndamugire nte? Bose bati N’abambge." 
Matthew27:23 Arababaza, ati Ku ki? Yakoze ikibi ki? Ariko barushiriza gusemerera cane, bati N’abambge." 
Matthew27:24 Maze Pilato abonye kw arushwa n’ubusa, ariko ko barushirije kuvyura umugūmūko, yābīra amazi akarabira imbere y’ishengero, ati Jeho ndacuna kubg’ amaraso y’uyu mugororotsi: n’ivyanyu." 
Matthew27:25 Abantu bose baramwishura, bat’ Amaraso yiwe araba ari twebge akora n’abana bacu." 
Matthew27:26 Maz’ abarekurira Baraba, ariko Yesu aramutonagura, amutanga ngw abambge." 
Matthew27:27 Maz’ abasoda b’ico cēgēra ca Kayisari bajana Yesu mw iboma, bateraniriza ingabo zose kuri we." 
Matthew27:28 Bamwambura iziwe mpuzu bamwambika umutamana w’agahama," 
Matthew27:29 batsiba igitsibo c’amahwa, bakimwambika mu mutwe, bashira n’irenga mu kuryo kwiwe; baramupfukamira, baramucurīra, bati Ndagize bgakeye Mwami w’Abayuda!" 
Matthew27:30 Bamuvuma amate, bamushikura rya renga, barimukubita mu mutwe." 
Matthew27:31 Bamaze kumucurīra, bamwambura wa mutamana, bamwambika iziwe mpuzu, bamujana kumubamba." 
Matthew27:32 Bakirenga irembo bahūra n’Umunyakurene yitwa Simoni, uyo baramufata kugira ngw amutwaze umusaraba." 
Matthew27:33 Bashitse ahantu hitwa i Gologota, risobanurwa ngw Ahantu h’agahanga," 
Matthew27:34 bamuha vino ivanze n’umuti w’umururazi, ngw ayinywe; ayumvirije yanka kuyinywa." 
Matthew27:35 Bamaze kumubamba, bagabura impuzu ziwe, barazipfindira," 
Matthew27:36 bicara hano baramurinda. 
Matthew27:37 Hejuru y’umutwe wiwe bahashira ikirego ciwe, canditswe ng’ UYU NI YESU, UMWAMI W’ABAYUDA." 
Matthew27:38 Maze babambana na we abambuzi babiri, umwe i buryo, uwundi i bumoso." 
Matthew27:39 Abahahita baramutuka, bazunguza imitwe," 
Matthew27:40 bat’ Ewe usambura urusengero, ukarwubaka mu misi itatu, ni wikize: ni waba ur’ Umwana w’Imana imanure ku musaraba." 
Matthew27:41 N’abaherezi bakuru n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe n’abashingantahe bamucurīra bartyo na bo," 
Matthew27:42 bati Yakijije abandi, we ntashobora kwikiza. N’Umwami w’Abisirayeli, ni yīmanure ku musaraba ubu nyene, duheze tumwizere." 
Matthew27:43 Yizigiye Imana, n’imukize ubu nyene ni yaba imubabaye: kuko yīgira ngo Nd’ Umwana w’Imana." 
Matthew27:44 N’abambuzi babambanywe na we na bo barabimutuka. 
Matthew27:45 Uhereye kw isaha ya gatandatu ubgirakabiri bukorana mu gihugu cose gushitsa kw isaha y’icenda. 
Matthew27:46 Nko kw isaha y’icenda Yesu asemerera n’ijwi rirenga, ati Eli, Eli, lama sabakatani? risobanurwa ngo Mana yanje, Mana yanje, n’iki kikumpebesheje?" 
Matthew27:47 Bamwe mu bahahagaze bavyumvise, baravuga, bat’ Uyo ahamagaye Eliya." 
Matthew27:48 Umwe muri bo aca arirukanga yābīra sipongo, ayuzuza inkarisha ayirungikisha irenga, arayimusomesha." 
Matthew27:49 Arikw abandi bati Banza ugume: turābe ko Eliya yoza kumukiza. 
Matthew27:50 Yesu yongera gusemerera n’ijwi rirenga, umutima uraca." 
Matthew27:51 Igihuzu gikingiriye ahēra cane h’urusengero gitantamukamwo kubiri, uhereye hejuru ugashitsa hasi; isi iratigita; ibitandara birasaduka;" 
Matthew27:52 imva ziruguruka, imivyimba myinshi y’abera bāri basinziriye irazurwa;" 
Matthew27:53 bava mu mva amaze kuzuka, bashika mu gisagara cera, babonekera benshi." 
Matthew27:54 Umugabisha w’abasoda ijana n’abāri kumwe na we barinda Yesu, babonye isi itigita n’ibibaye, baratinya cane, bati N’ivy’ ukuri, uyo yar’ Umwana w’Imana." 
Matthew27:55 Hāriho n’abagore benshi bāri kure babirāba; ni bo bākurikiye Yesu ava i Galilaya, bamukorera." 
Matthew27:56 Muri bo hārimwo Mariya Magadalene na Mariya nyina wa Yakobo na Yose, na nyina wa bene Zebedayo." 
Matthew27:57 Ariko bugorovye haza umutunzi w’i Arimataya yitwa Yosefu, kandi na we yar’ umwigishwa wa Yesu;" 
Matthew27:58 uyo aja kuri Pilato asaba ikiziga ca Yesu. Maze Pilato avuga ko bakimuha. 
Matthew27:59 Yosefu ajana ico kiziga, akizingira mu mpuzu yera nziza," 
Matthew27:60 agishira mu mva yiwe nsha, yari yarimbishije mu bitandara; atembagaza ikibuye kinini acugaza umuryango w’imva, aragenda." 
Matthew27:61 Mariya Magadalene na Mariya wundi ni ho bāri bari, bicaye berekeye ku mva." 
Matthew27:62 Bukeye bgaho, ni wo musi wakurikira uwo Kwitegura, abaherezi bakuru n’Abafarisayo bakoranira kwa Pilato," 
Matthew27:63 baramubgira, bati Mugenzi, twibutse yuko wa muhumvyi akiriho yagize ngw imisi itatu ishize azozuka." 
Matthew27:64 Nuko n’ugere barinde imva cane gushitsa ku musi ugira gatatu, kugira ngw abigishwa biwe ntibaze kumwiba, bakabgira abantu ngo yazutse mu bapfuye; maz’ ubuhumvyi bga nyuma bgoruta ubga mbere." 
Matthew27:65 Pilato arababgira, at’ Abarinzi ngabo: ni mubajane; muyīrindishirize uko muzi." 
Matthew27:66 Nuko baragenda barindisha imva, ca kibuye bagihomakw ishashara, bayidomamw’ ikimenyetso, abo barinzi babona." 
Matthew28:1 Umusi w’isabato ushize, ku wa mbere w’imisi ndwi, umutwenzi ugomba gutambika, Mariya Magadalene na Mariya wundi baja kurāba imva." 
Matthew28:2 Habaho kunyiganyiga kw’isi gukomeye, kuk’ umumarayika w’Umwami Imana yar’ amanutse ava mw ijuru, araza akūra ca kibuye agitembagaje, acicarako." 
Matthew28:3 Ishusho yiwe yasa n’umuravyo, impuzu ziwe zera nka shelegi." 
Matthew28:4 Ubgoba yateye abarāririzi bubashira mu gatengo, bamera nk’abapfuye." 
Matthew28:5 Arik’ umumarayika abgira ba bagore, ati Mweho ntimutinye, kuko nzi ko murondera Yesu, umwe yabambga;" 
Matthew28:6 ntari hano, kuko yazutse, nk’uko yavuze. Ngo murābe ah’ Umwami yar’ aryamye." 
Matthew28:7 Ni mukwakwanye mubgire abigishwa biwe yuko yazutse mu bapfuye, kand’ azobītangira imbere kuja i Galilaya, iyo ni ho muzomubonera. Nuko n’ivyo, ndabibabgiye." 
Matthew28:8 Bava ku mva n’ingoga, bari n’ubgoba n’akanyamuneza kenshi, birukanga kubibgira abigishwa biwe." 
Matthew28:9 Maze Yesu ahwana na bo, ati N’amahoro. Baramwēgēra, bamufata ku birenge, baramusenga." 
Matthew28:10 Maze Yesu arababgira, ati Ntimutinye: ni mugende mubgire bene Data ngo baje i Galilaya, ni ho tuzobonanira." 
Matthew28:11 Bakigenda, bamwe muri ba barinzi baja mu gisagara, babgira abaherezi bakuru ivyabaye vyose." 
Matthew28:12 Na bo bakoranira hamwe n’abashingantahe baja inama, bahēra abo basoda amahera menshi," 
Matthew28:13 bati Muze muvuge, mut’ Abigishwa biwe baje mw ijoro, baramutwibana dusinziriye." 
Matthew28:14 Icēgēra ca Kayisari ni caramuka kivyumvise, tuzomuhwamika, namwe tuzobakiza amagorwa." 
Matthew28:15 Bābīra ya mahera, bagira nk’uko bohejwe; kand’ iryo jambo ryandagara mu Bayuda na bugingo n’ubu." 
Matthew28:16 Maze ba bigishwa cumi n’umwe baja i Galilaya ku musozi Yesu yabarangiye; 
Matthew28:17 bamubonye, baramusenga, ariko bamwe barakekeranya." 
Matthew28:18 Yesu arabēgēra, arababgira, ati Jewe nahawe ububasha bgose mw ijuru no mw isi." 
Matthew28:19 Nuko ni mugende, muhindure amahanga yose abigishwa, mubabatiza mw izina rya Data wa twese n’iry’ Umwana n’irya Mpwemu Yera;" 
Matthew28:20 mubigishe kwitondera ivyo nabageze vyose. Umve, ndi kumwe namwe imisi yose, gushitsa ku muhero w’isi." 
Mark1:1 Itanguriro ry’ubutumwa bgiza bga Yesu Kristo, Umwana w’Imana." 
Mark1:2 Nk’uko vyanditswe na Yesaya yavugishwa n’Imana, Ng’ Umve, ngira ntume integuza yanje imbere y’amaso yawe, Ikuroranirize inzira." 
Mark1:3 Ijwi ry’ūsemererera mu bugaragwa, Ati Ni mutegure inzira y’Uhoraho, Mugorore iz’ ibihamo ziwe." 
Mark1:4 Ni ko Yohana yaje, abatiriza mu bugaragwa, yigisha ukubatizwa kwo kwihana, ngo babohorwe ivyaha." 
Mark1:5 Igihugu c’i Yudaya cose n’ab’i Yerusalemu bose bava i wabo, baza kuri we: ababatiriza mu ruzi Yorodani, bātuye ivyaha vyabo." 
Mark1:6 Kandi Yohana yambara ubgoya bg’ingamiya, akabukenyeza umukanda w’urusato mu rukenyerero, kandi yarya inzige n’ubūki bgo mw ishamba." 
Mark1:7 Yaravuga, at’ Ūndusha ubushobozi azoza mu nyuma yanje, ntibimbereye no kwunama ngo mpfundurure utugozi tw’inkweto ziwe." 
Mark1:8 Jeho ndababatirishije amazi, ariko we azobabatirisha Mpwemu Yera." 
Mark1:9 Mur’ iyo misi Yesu ava i Nazareti i Galilaya, araza, abatizwa na Yohana muri Yorodani." 
Mark1:10 Avuye mu mazi, aca abona ijuru ritandukanye, Mpwemu aramanuka amugwako, asa n’inuma." 
Mark1:11 Ijwi riva mw ijuru, riti Ni wewe Mwana wanje nkunda ukampimbara." 
Mark1:12 Mpwemu aca amushorera mu bugaragwa. 
Mark1:13 Amaray’ imisi mirongwine, ageragezwa na Satani; kandi yaba hamwe n’ibikōko, abamarayika bakamukorera." 
Mark1:14 Yohana amaze gushirwa mw ibohero, Yesu aja i Galilaya, ababgira ubutumwa bgiza bg’Imana," 
Mark1:15 at’ Igihe kirashitse, ubgami bg’Imana buri hafi: mwihane, mwemere ubutumwa bgiza." 
Mark1:16 Aciye i ruhande y’ikiyaga c’i Galilaya, abona Simoni na Andereya mwene nyina baterera urusenga mu kiyaga, kuko bār’ abarovyi." 
Mark1:17 Yesu arababarira, ati Ni munkurikire, nzobagira abaroba abantu." 
Mark1:18 Baca bareka insenga, baramukurikira." 
Mark1:19 Yīgiye imbere gato, abona Yakobo mwene Zebedayo na Yohana mwene nyina, na bo bari mu bgato basana insenga." 
Mark1:20 Aca arabahamagara, basiga se Zebedayo mu bgato hamwe n’abakozi biwe, baramukurikira." 
Mark1:21 Bashika i Kaperinawumu, aca yinjira mw isinagogi kw isabato, arabigisha." 
Mark1:22 Batangazwa n’inyigisho ziwe, kuko yabigisha nk’ūfise ububasha, ntase n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe." 
Mark1:23 Uwo mwanya mw isinagogi yabo hār’ umuntu yinjiwemwo n’impwemu ihumanye, arasemerera," 
Mark1:24 ati Duhūriye hehe ga Yesu Munyanazareti? Uje kuduhonnya? Ndakuzi uw’ uri we, ur’ Uwera w’Imana." 
Mark1:25 Yesu aramuzibiza, ati Hora, muvemwo." 
Mark1:26 Iyo mpwemu ihumanye iramujegeza, irasemerera, ivuga n’ijwi rirenga, imuvamwo." 
Mark1:27 Bose baratangara, bituma babazanya, bat’ Iki n’iki? N’ukwigisha gusha! N’ububasha agera n’impwemu zihumanye na zo, zikamwumvira." 
Mark1:28 Inkuru yiwe ica ikwira hose mu gihugu cose c’i Galilaya kihakikije. 
Mark1:29 Bavuye mw isinagogi, baca bajana na Yakobo na Yohana mu nzu kwa Simoni na Andereya." 
Mark1:30 Kandi inabukwe wa Simoni yar’ aryamye, afashwe n’umururumbo, baca bamubarira ivyiwe." 
Mark1:31 Araza, amufata ukuboko, aramuvyutsa, umururumbo urazima, arabazimana." 
Mark1:32 Ku kagoroba, ku kirengazuba, bamuzanira abarwaye bose n’abinjiwemwo n’abadayimoni." 
Mark1:33 Igisagara cose gikoranira kw irembo. 
Mark1:34 Akiza benshi bāri barwaye indwara zitari zimwe, asenda abadayimoni benshi, ntiyakundira abo badayimoni ko bavuga, kuko bāri bamuzi." 
Mark1:35 Mw ijoro rishīra ubuca aravyuka, arasohoka, aja mu gahinga, asengerayo." 
Mark1:36 Simoni n’abandi bāri kumwe na we baramukurikira: 
Mark1:37 bamubonye baramubgira, bati Bose bariko barakurondera." 
Mark1:38 Arabishura, ati Tuje ahandi mu bisagara biri hafi, na ho nyene nigisheyo, kukw ari co canzanye." 
Mark1:39 Yinjira mu masinagogi yabo i Galilaya hose, avuga ijambo ry’Imana, asenda abadayimoni." 
Mark1:40 Haza umunyamibembe kuri we, amwinginga amupfukamiye, at’ Ukunze, woshobora kumpumanura." 
Mark1:41 Amugirira akagongwe, aramvura ukuboko, amukorako, ati Ndakunze, humanuka." 
Mark1:42 Imibembe ica imuvako, arakira." 
Mark1:43 Aramwihanikiriza rwose, aca amurungika uwo mwanya," 
Mark1:44 aramubarira, ati Wirinde, ntugire uwo ubikerukiriza, ariko genda, wiyereke umuherezi, utange ivy’ uguhumanurwa kwawe, nk’uko Mose yageze, bibe ikimenyetso kibabere icabona." 
Mark1:45 Maz’ avaho, atangura kwandagaza no gukwiza ivyabaye; ni co catumye Yesu atābaye agishobora kuja mu gisagara abandi babizi, arikw aguma inyuma yaco mu gahinga: abava hose baza kuri we." 
Mark2:1 Hashize imisi, asubira i Kaperinawumu, bimenyekana kw ari mu nzu." 
Mark2:2 Bakoraniraho benshi, ntibakwirwa mu nzu, eka n’imbere y’umuryango hose; ababgira ijambo ry’Imana." 
Mark2:3 Haza abazanye ikimuga, bagiteruye ari bane." 
Mark2:4 Babuze ingene bamushikīra kubg’ ishengero, basambura inzu hejuru y’ah’ atumbereye; bahejeje kuhatobora, bururukirizamw’ inderuzo, iryamyemw’ ico kimuga." 
Mark2:5 Yesu abonye ukwizera kwabo, abgira ico kimuga, ati Mwana wanje, ivyaha vyawe urabihariwe." 
Mark2:6 Ariko hārih’ abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe bamwe bicayeho, bībūranya mu mitima," 
Mark2:7 bati N’iki gitumye uyo avuga artyo? Ararogose: ni nde ashobora guharira ivyaha, atar’ umwe, ni we Mana?" 
Mark2:8 Yesu amenye mu mutima wiwe yuko bībūranya muri bo bartyo, aca arababaza, ati N’iki gitumye mwībūranya ivyo mu mitima yanyu?" 
Mark2:9 Icoroshe n’ikihe, n’ukubarira ikimuga, nt’ Uhariwe ivyaha vyawe; canke n’ukukibarira, nti Vyuka, wikorere inderuzo yawe, ugende?" 
Mark2:10 Ariko kugira ngo mumenye k’Umwana w’umuntu afise ububasha mw isi bgo guharira ivyaha — abgira ikimuga," 
Mark2:11 ati Ndakubariye nti Vyuka, wikorere inderuzo yawe, utahe." 
Mark2:12 Aravyuka, aca yikorera inderuzo, asohoka imbere ya bose: nuko bose barumirwa, bahimbaza Imana, bati Ntitwaribgabone ben’ ibi." 
Mark2:13 Arasohoka, yongera kuja i ruhande y’ikiyaga: ishengero ryose riza kuri we, arabigisha." 
Mark2:14 Nukw arikw aragenda abona Lewi mwene Alufayo, yicaye aho yatoreza ikibuguro, aramubarira, ati Nkurikira. Ava hasi, aramukurikira." 
Mark2:15 Kandi yicaye mu nzu y’uwo, arikw ararya, haza benshi mu batozakori n’abanyavyaha basangira na Yesu n’abigishwa biwe: bāri benshi, kandi bāramukurikira." 
Mark2:16 Abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe bo mu Bafarisayo babonye asangira n’abanyavyaha n’abatozakori babgira abigishwa biwe, bati Mbega kw asangira n’abatozakori n’abanyavyaha!" 
Mark2:17 Yesu avyumvise, arababgira, at’ Abakomeye nta co bagombera umuvūzi, atar’ abarwaye. Sinaje guhamagara abagororotsi, atar’ abanyavyaha." 
Mark2:18 Kand’ abigishwa ba Yohana bo n’Abafarisayo bāri bisonzesheje. Baraza, baramubaza, bati N’iki gituma abigishwa ba Yohana n’abigishwa b’Abafarisayo bisonzesha, abigishwa bawe ntibisonzeshe?" 
Mark2:19 Yesu arababaza, ati Mbeg’ abātowe bokwisonzesha bate, bakiri kumwe n’umukwe? Umukwe akiri kumwe na bo ntibashobora kwisonzesha." 
Mark2:20 Har’ imisi izoza, umukwe akūrwe muri bo, bazoca bisonzesha uwo musi." 
Mark2:21 Nta wobarīra ikiremo c’igitambara gisha ku mpuzu y’umushire; kukw ico kiremo coyitabura, igisha kikavana n’umushire, ikarushiriza gutabuka." 
Mark2:22 Kandi nta wotara umutobe wa vino mu mikuza y’insato ibōmbōtse; kuko vino yoturitsa iyo mikuza, vino n’imikuza bigapfana. Arik’ umutobe wa vino bawutara mu mikuza misha." 
Mark2:23 Kandi kw isabato, agenda aca mu mirima y’ingano; abigishwa biwe bakigenda batangura kumyōza ingano." 
Mark2:24 Abafarisayo baramubaza, bati N’iki gitumye bakora ikizira gukorwa kw isabato?" 
Mark2:25 Na we arababaza, ati Nta ho murasoma ico Dawidi yakoze, aho yar’ aburaniwe ashonje, bo n’abāri kumwe na we?" 
Mark2:26 Ingene yinjiye mu nzu y’Imana, mu misi ya Abiyatari umuherezi mukuru, akarya imitsima y’ibiterekērwa, ar’ umuziro kuribga, ukūye abaherezi, akayihako n’abāri kumwe na we?" 
Mark2:27 Kand’ arababgira, at’ Isabato yabayeho kubg’ umuntu, arik’ umuntu si we yabayeho kubg’ isabato." 
Mark2:28 Ni co gituma Umwana w’umuntu ar’ umwami w’isabato na yo. 
Mark3:1 Yongera kwinjira mw isinagogi; kandi hār’ umuntu anyunyutse ukuboko; 
Mark3:2 baramugenza ngo barābe kw amukiza kw isabato, ngo bamurege." 
Mark3:3 Abarira uwo muntu anyunyutse ukuboko, ati Va hasi, uhagarare hagati." 
Mark3:4 Arababaza, ati Mbeg’ ivyemerwa n’ugukora ivyiza kw isabato canke n’ugukora ibibi? Gukiza umuntu canke kumwica? Barihorera." 
Mark3:5 Aberaguzamw’ amaso, aratse, ababazwa n’ukw imitima yabo ikomantaye, abarira uwo muntu, ati Ramvura ukuboko kwawe. Arakuramvura, kurakira." 
Mark3:6 Abafarisayo barasohoka, baca bamugīra inama n’abantu ba Herode ngo babone ingene bomwica." 
Mark3:7 Maze Yesu n’abigishwa biwe bavayo, baja ku kiyaga: ishengero ryinshi riramukurikira, bavuye i Galilaya n’i Yudaya" 
Mark3:8 n’i Yerusalemu no muri Idumaya no hakurya ya Yorodani, n’abahereranye no muri Tiro n’i Sidoni, ishengero ryinshi ryumvise ivyo yakoze riza kuri we." 
Mark3:9 Abarira abigishwa biwe ngo bagumishe ubgato butoya hafi kubg’ ishengero, ngo ntirimubānde." 
Mark3:10 Kuko yakijije benshi, ni co catumye abāri bafise ivyago bose bamuhenukirako, ngo bamukoreko." 
Mark3:11 Impwemu zihumanye na zo uko zimubonye zamwikubita imbere, zigasemerera zit’ Ur’ Umwana w’Imana." 
Mark3:12 Arazihanikiriza cane, ngo ntizigende ziramwandagaza." 
Mark3:13 Maz’ adūga umusozi muremure, ahamagara abo agomba, baza kuri we." 
Mark3:14 Atoranya icumi na babiri bo kubana na we, maze ngw abatume kwigisha," 
Mark3:15 no kugira ububasha bgo gusenda abadayimoni. 
Mark3:16 Nukw atoranya aba cumi na babiri: Simoni, amwita Petero;" 
Mark3:17 atoranya na Yakobo mwene Zebedayo, na Yohana mwene nyina wa Yakobo, na bo abita Bowanerige, risobanurwa ngw Abana b’inkuba;" 
Mark3:18 atoranya na Andereya, na Filipo, na Barutolomayo, na Matayo, na Toma, na Yakobo mwene Alufayo, na Tadayo, na Simoni Umunyakananayo," 
Mark3:19 na Yuda Isikaryota, ni we yamuguze. Aja mu nzu:" 
Mark3:20 ishengero ryongera gukoranira kuri we, bituma babura ingene botamira n’agatsima." 
Mark3:21 Ab’i wabo bavyumvise barasohoka ngo baje kumufata, kuko bāgira ngo Yasaze." 
Mark3:22 Kand’ abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe bavuye i Yerusalemu baravuga, bat’ Arimwo Beyezebuli: kandi bat’ Umukuru w’abadayimoni ni we amushoboza gusenda abadayimoni." 
Mark3:23 Arabahamagara, abacira umugani, ati Satani yoshobora ate gusenda Satani?" 
Mark3:24 Ubgami iyo bgitandukanije ubgabgo, ubgo bgami ntibushobora kurama." 
Mark3:25 Inzu ni yitandukanya ubgayo, iyo nzu ntizoshobora kurama." 
Mark3:26 Kandi Satani, namba yīhagurukiye, akitandukanya, ntashobora guhangama, arahera." 
Mark3:27 Kandi nta muntu yoshobora kwinjira mu nzu y’umuntu w’inkomezi kumusahura ibintu, atabanje kuboha wa munyenkomezi, maz’ akabona kumusahura ivyo mu nzu yiwe." 
Mark3:28 Ndababgire ukuri: Abana b’abantu bazoharirwa ivyaha vyabo vyose n’ibirogotano vyose bazorogota," 
Mark3:29 arik’ umuntu wese azorogota kuri Mpwemu Yera nta ho azoharirwa, kand’ azoba akoze icaha c’ibihe bidashira." 
Mark3:30 Icatumye avuga artyo n’uko bavuze ngw Arimw’ impwemu ihumanye. 
Mark3:31 Maze nyina na bene nyina baraza, batuma kumuhamagara, bahagaze hanze." 
Mark3:32 Ishengero ryari ryicaye rimukikije; maze baramubgira, bat’ Ereg’ umuvyeyi wawe na barumuna bawe bari hanze, barakurondera." 
Mark3:33 Na we arababaza, ati Mama ni nde, canke bene mama ni ba nde?" 
Mark3:34 Yeraguza amaso abari bicaye impande zose bamukikije, ati Ngaba mama na bene mama:" 
Mark3:35 umuntu wese akora ivyo Imana igomba ni we murumunanje, ni we mushikanje, ni we mama." 
Mark4:1 Atangura ukundi gusha kwigishiriza ku nkombe y’ikiyaga. Ishengero ryinshi cane rikoranira kuri we, bimutera gutambukira mu bgato buri mu kiyaga, yicaramwo, ishengero ryose riguma ku nkombe y’ikiyaga." 
Mark4:2 Abigisha vyinshi mu migani, ababgira mur’ ukwo kwigisha kwiwe," 
Mark4:3 ati Ni mwumve; umubivyi yasohoye imbuto. 
Mark4:4 Akibiba, zimwe zigwa i ruhande y’inzira; inyoni ziraza, zirazinobagura." 
Mark4:5 Izindi zigwa ku rutare, hatar’ ivu ryinshi; zica zimera vuba, kukw ata vu ryinshi ririho:" 
Mark4:6 izuba rirashe, ziraraba, kukw ata mizi zifise, zirūma." 
Mark4:7 Izindi zigwa mu mahwa, amahwa arakura, arazinyoha, ntizama." 
Mark4:8 Izindi zigwa mw ivu ryiza, ziramera, zirakura, zihunda impeke, zimwe mirongwitatu, izindi mirongwitandatu, izindi ijana, birtyo birtyo." 
Mark4:9 Kand’ at’ Ūri n’amatwi yumva, ni yumve." 
Mark4:10 Bīherereye, abāri kumwe na we na bamwe cumi na babiri bamubaza iyo migani;" 
Mark4:11 arabishura, ati Mwebge mwahawe ibanga ry’ubgami bg’Imana, arikw abo hanze babarirwa vyose mu migani:" 
Mark4:12 ngo kurāba barābe, yamara ntibavyitegereze; kwumva bavyumve, yamara ntibabitahure; ngo kumbure bohindukira bagaharirwa." 
Mark4:13 Kand’ arababaza, ati Ntimuzi uwo mugani? Non’ imigani yose muzoyitahura mute?" 
Mark4:14 Umubivyi abiba ijambo ry’Imana. 
Mark4:15 Ab’i ruhande y’inzira, ah’ iryo jambo ribibga, iyo bahejeje kwumva, Satani aca aza uwo mwanya, akabakūramw’ iryo jambo ryabibge muri bo." 
Mark4:16 N’aba n’uko, ni bo bābibge ku rutare; iyo bumvise iryo jambo, baca baryākīrana umunezero," 
Mark4:17 ntibagire imizi muri bo, ariko bahagarara umwanya muto, maz’ iyo bādutsweko n’amarushwa bo n’akadenderezo bazira iryo jambo, bica bibagwisha." 
Mark4:18 Abandi ni bo bābibge mu mahwa, abo ni bo bumva iryo jambo," 
Mark4:19 maz’ umwitwaririko w’ivy’ isi n’uruhendo rw’ubutunzi no kwifuza ibindi, iyo bibinjiyemwo, binyoha iryo jambo, rikaba ikirumbirane." 
Mark4:20 Abābibge mw ivu ryiza, abo ni bo bumva iryo jambo bakaryemera, bagahunda impeke, umwe mirongwitatu, uwundi mirongwitandatu, uwundi ijana, birtyo birtyo." 
Mark4:21 Kand’ arababaza, ati Mbeg’ itara rizanwa ngo baryubikekw igisimbo canke barishire mu rutara, ntirishirwa ku gitereko caryo?" 
Mark4:22 Kukw ata canyegejwe kitazoserurwa, cank’ icagizwe ibanga kitazoja ahabona." 
Mark4:23 Ūri n’amatwi yumva, ni yumve." 
Mark4:24 Kand’ arababarira, ati Mwiyubare mu vyo mwumva. Ingero mugeramwo ni yo muzogererwamwo, kandi muzorengerezwa:" 
Mark4:25 kuk’ ūfise azohabga, arik’ ūdafise azokwakwa n’ico yar’ asanzwe afise." 
Mark4:26 Yongera kubabgira, at’ Ubgami bg’Imana busa n’umuntu yabivye imbuto mw ivu," 
Mark4:27 bgije agasinzira, bugaca akavyuka, imbuto zikamera, zigakura, atazi ingene zakuze." 
Mark4:28 Ivu rimeza ryonyene, habanza kuba ibironge, hanyuma hakaba imiyange, hanyuma hakaba amahundo atēngēngeye impeke." 
Mark4:29 Maz’ imirima yeze, aca ayitemesha umuhoro, kukw igihe c’ishwābūra kigeze." 
Mark4:30 Kand’ arababaza, at’ Ubgami bg’Imana tubushushanye n’iki? Canke tubusobanurishe umugani ki?" 
Mark4:31 Busa n’akabuto ka sinapi, iyo gatewe mw ivu, nah’ ari kanzinya hanyuma y’imbuto zose ziri mw isi;" 
Mark4:32 arikw iyo gatewe, karakura, kakaba kanini, kakaruta ibirimwa vyose, kagashamika amashami manini, kand’ inyoni zo mu kirere zishobora kwārika ivyāri mu gitūtu cako." 
Mark4:33 Kand’ ababgira ijambo ry’Imana mu migani myinshi imwe n’iyo, uko bashobora kwumva." 
Mark4:34 Kand’ atabaciriye umugani nta co yababgira, ariko yihereranye n’abiwe bigishwa akabibasobanurira vyose." 
Mark4:35 Kur’ uwo musi bugorovye, arababgira, ati Tujabuke tuje hakurya." 
Mark4:36 Basiga abantu hano, bamujana mu bgato yahozemwo, kand’ ayandi mato yari kumwe na bo." 
Mark4:37 Nuko haza inkūbi ikomeye y’umuyaga, imipfunda yisuka mu bgato, bgariko buruzura." 
Mark4:38 Ariko we yar’ aryamye mu mutwe w’inyuma, yiseguye umusego yisinziriye. Baramukangura, baramubaza, bati Mwigisha, ntubabaye ko turiko turapfa?" 
Mark4:39 Arikangura, azibiza ingunza, abarira ikiyaga, ati Hora, utekereze. Umuyaga uraca, haba agahwekere rwose." 
Mark4:40 Arababaza, ati N’iki kibateye ubgoba? Ntimurizera?" 
Mark4:41 Baratinya, bagira ubgoba bginshi, barabazanya, bati Mbeg’ uyu n’umuntu ki, umuyaga n’ikiyaga ko bimwumvira?" 
Mark5:1 Bafata hakurya y’ikiyaga mu gihugu c’Abageraseni. 
Mark5:2 Avuye mu bgato, umuntu yinjiwemwo n’impwemu ihumanye ava mu masenga y’imva, aca aramusanganira." 
Mark5:3 Yaba mur’ ayo masenga, ntihāgira ūba akibona ico ashobora kumubohesha, n’iyo woba umunyororo:" 
Mark5:4 kuko bāmubohesheje iminyororo ku maguru no ku maboko kenshi, iy’ amaboko akayicagagura, iy’ amaguru akayivutagura: ntihāgira umuntu afise inkomezi zomutururuza." 
Mark5:5 Maz’ imisi yose ku murango no mw ijoro yama mur’ ayo masenga no ku misozi, ataka, yikebesha amabuye." 
Mark5:6 Abonye Yesu akiri kure, arirukanga, arunama," 
Mark5:7 asemerera n’ijwi rirenga, ati Duhūriye hehe ga Yesu Mwana w’Imana isumba vyose? Ndakurahiye Imana, ntumbabaze agashinyaguro." 
Mark5:8 Kuko yar’ amubariye, ati Va mu muntu, wa mpwemu ihumanye." 
Mark5:9 Aramubaza, ati Witwa nde? Aramwishura, ati Gitero ni ryo zina ryanje kuko turi benshi." 
Mark5:10 Aramwinginga cane ngo ntazirukane mur’ ico gihugu. 
Mark5:11 Kandi kur’ uwo musozi hār’ umukuku mwinshi w’ingurube zirisha: 
Mark5:12 ziramwinginga, ziti Turungike muri ziriya ngurube, tuzinjiremwo." 
Mark5:13 Arazemerera. Izo mpwemu zihumanye zimusokorotsemwo, zinjira muri nya ngurube, umukuku wirukira ku gatembge, zisuka mu kiyaga, zāri nk’ibihumbi bibiri, amazi araziniga." 
Mark5:14 Abāziragira barahunga, babivuga mu gisagara no mu misozi: na bo baza kurāba ibibaye ivy’ ari vyo." 
Mark5:15 Bashika aho Yesu ari, basanga uwari yinjiwemwo n’abadayimoni yicaye, yambaye, ubgenge bgāgarutse, umwe nyene yari yinjiwemwo na ca gitero; baratinya." 
Mark5:16 Abābibonye babadondera ivy’ uwari yinjiwemwo n’abadayimoni n’ivy’ ingurube. 
Mark5:17 Batangura kumwinginga ngw ave mu ntāra yabo. 
Mark5:18 Arikw aratambukira mu bgato, uwari yinjiwemwo n’abadayimoni aramwinginga ngw agume kuri we." 
Mark5:19 Ntiyamukundira, arikw aramubarira, ati Ja i muhira i wawe mu b’i wanyu, ubabarire ivyo Umwami Imana igukoreye vyose, kand’ ingen’ ikugiriye ikigongwe." 
Mark5:20 Aragenda, atangura gukwiza i Dekapoli ivyo Yesu yamukoreye vyose, abantu bose baratangara." 
Mark5:21 Nuko Yesu agenda mu bgato, asubira hakurya, ishengero ryinshi rikoranira kuri we; yar’ i ruhande y’ikiyaga." 
Mark5:22 Haza umwe mu bakuru b’isinagogi, yitwa Yayiro, amubonye amwitembagaza imbere y’ibirenge," 
Mark5:23 aramwinginga cane, at’ Akana kanje k’agakobga kari ku mpfiro, ndakwinginze, n’uze se, umurambikekw ibiganza, akire, abeho." 
Mark5:24 Aragenda, ajana na we. Ishengero ryinshi riramukurikira rimubanda." 
Mark5:25 Kand’ umugore arwaye ubutinyanka yar’ abimaranye imyaka cumi n’ibiri," 
Mark5:26 yababajwe cane n’abavūzi benshi bamumarisha ibintu vyiwe vyose abitangamw’ ingemu, ntihāgira ico bamumarira, mber’ arushiriza kurwara;" 
Mark5:27 yumvise ivya Yesu, araza, aca hagati y’ishengero, amuturuka inyuma, akora ku mpuzu yiwe." 
Mark5:28 Yari yibgiye, ati N’iyo nokora ku mpuzu ziwe gusa, nokira." 
Mark5:29 Uwo mwanya isōko y’amaraso irakama, amenya mu mubiri wiwe yukw akize ico cago." 
Mark5:30 Ako kanya Yesu yumva muri we ubushobozi bumuvamwo, ahindukira abāndana n’ishengero, arababaza, ati Ni nde akoze ku mpuzu zanje?" 
Mark5:31 Abigishwa biwe baramwishura, bat’ Ubone abantu bariko barakubānda, nawe ukagira uti Ni nde ankozeko?" 
Mark5:32 Aberaguzamw’ amaso, ngw abone ūmukozeko." 
Mark5:33 Uwo mugore aratinya, ahinda agashitsi, kukw azi ikimubayeko, araza amwikubita imbere, amubarira ivy’ ukuri vyose." 
Mark5:34 Yesu aramubgira, ati Mwana wanje, ukwizera kwawe kuragukijije, genda amahoro, ukire rwose icago cawe." 
Mark5:35 Akivuga, haza abavuye kwa wa mukuru w’isinagogi, bati Wa mwana wawe aracīkānye, uracagorera iki Umwigisha?" 
Mark5:36 Ariko Yesu ntiyashira umutima kw ijambo rivuzwe, abarira uwo mukuru w’isinagogi, ati Ntutinye, wizere gusa." 
Mark5:37 Ntiyakundira uwundi muntu kujana na we, atari Petero na Yakobo na Yohana mwene nyina wa Yakobo." 
Mark5:38 Bashitse ku nzu y’uwo mukuru w’isinagogi, asanga bariko barakoma induru barira baboroga cane." 
Mark5:39 Yinjiye arababaza, ati N’iki gitumye mukoma induru murira? Umwana ntahwereye, arikw arasinziriye." 
Mark5:40 Baramutwenga bamushinyagurira. Arabakumīra bose, ajana se w’umwana na nyina n’abāri kumwe na we, yīgira haruguru ah’ ikiziga kiri," 
Mark5:41 afata ukuboko kw’ikiziga, arakibarira, ati Talisa kumi; bisobanurwa ngo Gakobga, ndakubariye, nti Vyuka." 
Mark5:42 Umukobga aca avyuka uwo mwanya, aragendagenda, kuko yar’ amaze imyaka cumi n’ibiri avutse: baca baratangara cane." 
Mark5:43 Arabihanikiriza cane, ngo ntihagire umuntu n’umwe abimenya, arababarira ngo bamugaburire." 
Mark6:1 Avayo, aja mu ntāra y’i wabo, abigishwa biwe baramukurikira." 
Mark6:2 Isabato ishitse, aca yigishiriza mw isinagogi: benshi bamwumvise baratangara, bat’ Ivyo vyose uyu yabikūye hehe? Kandi n’ubgenge ki yahawe, n’ivyo bitangaza bingaho bikorwa n’amaboko yiwe n’ibiki?" 
Mark6:3 Mbega si wa mubāji, mwene Mariya, mwene nyina wa Yakobo na Yose na Yuda na Simoni? Bashiki biwe na bo ntibari hano i wacu? Ivyiwe birabatsitaza." 
Mark6:4 Yesu arababgira, at’ Umuntu avugishwa n’Imana ntabura icubahiro, atari mu ntāra y’i wabo, no mu muryango w’i wabo, no mu nzu y’i wabo." 
Mark6:5 Maze ntiyashobora gukoreray’ igitangaza na kimwe, atar’ abarwaye bake yarambitsekw ibiganza, akabakiza." 
Mark6:6 Atangazwa n’ukutizera kwabo. Agendagenda mu mihana ihakikije, yigisha." 
Mark6:7 Ahamagara bamwe cumi na babiri, atangura kubatuma babiri-babiri, abaha ububasha ku mpwemu zihumanye." 
Mark6:8 Ababuza ngo ntibagire ico bajana ku nzira, atar’ inkoni gusa, ati Ntimujane impamba cank’ isaho cank’ amahera mu mipfuko yanyu," 
Mark6:9 ariko mwambare inkweto, kandi ntimwambare amapfundo abiri." 
Mark6:10 Kand’ arababgira, at’ Inzu yose muzokwinjiramwo, abe ari yo mugumamwo, kugeza aho muzovira aho hantu." 
Mark6:11 Ahantu hose aho bazokwanka kubākīra ntibabumve, mukivayo muze mukunkumure umukungugu wo mu birenge vyanyu, kibe ikimenyetso kibabere icabona." 
Mark6:12 Baragenda, bigisha kw abantu bakwiye kwihana." 
Mark6:13 Basenda abadayimoni benshi, basīga amavuta abarwaye benshi, barakira." 
Mark6:14 Umwami Herode aravyumva, kukw izina rya Yesu ryari ribaye rurangiranwa, aravuga, ati Yohana Umubatizi yāzutse mu bapfuye, ni co gituma ivyo bitangaza bikorera muri we." 
Mark6:15 Arikw abandi baravuga, bati Ni Eliya; abandi bati N’umuntu avugishwa n’Imana, nka ba bandi bāvugishwa na yo." 
Mark6:16 Ariko Herode avyumvise, aravuga, ati Yohana uwo naciye izosi ni we yazutse." 
Mark6:17 Kuko Herode ubgiwe ari we yari yatumye ngo bafate Yohana, aramuboha, amushira mw ibohero, kubga Herodiya muka Filipo mwene se, kuko Herode yamucikije." 
Mark6:18 Kandi Yohana yari yarabgiye Herode, ati N’ikizira k’ufise muka mwene so." 
Mark6:19 Ni co catumye Herodiya amugirira akazīka, agomba kumwica, ntiyaronka uburyo:" 
Mark6:20 kuko Herode yatinya Yohana, amuzi kw agororotse kand’ ar’ umuntu yera, aramurinda: iy’ amwumvise hose, ivyiwe vyaramuzazanira, yamara yanezererwa kumwumva." 
Mark6:21 Maz’ umusi uragera, uburyo buraboneka: war’ umusi wo kwibutsa ukuvuka kwa Herode; atumira abaganwa biwe, n’abakuru b’abagabisha b’abasoda, n’abapfasoni b’i Galilaya, ngo baze abatereke." 
Mark6:22 Umukobga wa Herodiya nyene arinjira aratamba, Herode n’abashitsi biwe baramushima. Umwami abgira uwo mukobga, ati Nsaba ico ugomba cose, ndakiguha." 
Mark6:23 Aramurahira, at’ Ico unsaba cose ndakiguha, n’iyo coba igisate c’ubgami bganje." 
Mark6:24 Arasohoka, abaza nyina, ati Nsabe iki? Aramwishura, ati Saba umutwe wa Yohana Umubatizi." 
Mark6:25 Aca aza ah’ umwami ari n’ingoga, aramusaba, ati Ndagomba k’umpa nonaha umutwe wa Yohana Umubatizi ku mubehe." 
Mark6:26 Umwami arababara cane, ariko kubga za ndahiro ziwe, no kubg’ abāsangira na we, bimunanira kuwumwima." 
Mark6:27 Uwo mwanya umwami atuma umushibamyi, amubarira kuzana umutwe wa Yohana. Aragenda, amucira izosi mw ibohero," 
Mark6:28 azana umutwe wiwe ku kibehe, awuha wa mwigeme, na we awuha nyina." 
Mark6:29 Abigishwa biwe bavyumvise baraza, bajana ikiziga ciwe, bagihamba mu cobo." 
Mark6:30 Nuko za ntumwa zikoranira aho Yesu ari, zimudondera ivyo zakoze vyose n’ivyo zigishije." 
Mark6:31 Arababgira, ati Ni muze mwebge mwenyene ahiherereye mu gahinga, muruhuke gatoya. Kuko hāri benshi banyurana, babura n’ingene botamira utwo kurya." 
Mark6:32 Bagenda mu bgato, baja ahantu h’agahinga kwiherērayo." 
Mark6:33 Bababona bagenda, benshi barabamenya, bava mu bisagara vyose, barirukanga, bajana inkōkoro y’ikiyaga, babatangayo." 
Mark6:34 Avuye mu bgato, abona ishengero ryinshi, rimutera akagongwe kuko bameze nk’intama zitagira umwungere: atangura kubigisha vyinshi." 
Mark6:35 Umusi ukuze, abigishwa biwe baramwēgēra, bati Mbega hano hantu kw ari mu gahinga, umusi ukaba ukuze;" 
Mark6:36 basezere, baje mu misozi no mu mihana impande zose, kwirondereray’ ivyo kurya." 
Mark6:37 Arabishura, ati Mube ari mwebge mubagaburira. Baramubaza, bati Tugende tugure imitsima y’idenariyo amajana abiri, tuyibahe ga barye?" 
Mark6:38 Na we arababaza, ati Mufise imitsima ingahe? Ni mugende muyirābe. Babimenye baramwishura, bati Ni dutanu, n’udufi tubiri." 
Mark6:39 Ababarira ko bose bicara ku vyatsi bibisi bīcīye intēko. 
Mark6:40 Bicara imirongo‐imirongo, hamwe ijana‐ijana, ahandi mirongwitanu‐mirongwitanu, bartyo bartyo." 
Mark6:41 Yābīra ya mitsima itanu na za fi zibiri, ararangamiza, arāba mw ijuru, arabihezagira, amanyagura iyo mitsima, ayiha abigishwa ngo bayishire imbere y’abantu, n’ifi zompi na zo arazibagaburira bose." 
Mark6:42 Bararya bose barahāga. 
Mark6:43 Batororokanya utumanyagu tw’imitsima n’utw’ ifi, twuzura ibisimbo cumi na bibiri." 
Mark6:44 Abāriye iyo mitsima bār’ abagabo ibihumbi bitanu. 
Mark6:45 Uwo mwanya agōbēra abigishwa biwe ngo batambukire mu bgato, bitangire kujabuka hakurya i Betsayida, aheze gusezera rya shengero." 
Mark6:46 Ahejeje gusezerana na bo avayo, adūga umusozi gusenga." 
Mark6:47 Bgagorovye, bga bgato bushitse mw idamba, ariko we yar’ i musozi wenyene." 
Mark6:48 Abonye ko batamijwe no gusōza, kuk’ umuyaga war’ ubaturutse imbere, ku muteramyi agira kane aza aho bari, agendesha amaguru hejuru ku kiyaga, yagira abarengane." 
Mark6:49 Ariko babonye agendesha amaguru hejuru ku kiyaga, bagira ngo n’igihūme, batura ubuku." 
Mark6:50 Bose baramubona, basimbga n’umutima. Arik’ uwo mwanya arabavugisha, ati Hūmura ni jewe, ni mureke gutinya." 
Mark6:51 Aratambuka, aja mu bgato bārimwo: umuyaga uraca. Barumirwa cane mu mitima yabo:" 
Mark6:52 kuko batātahuye ivya ya mitsima, arikw imitima yabo yar’ ikomantaye." 
Mark6:53 Bamaze kujabuka hakurya, bafata i musozi mu ntāra y’i Genesareti, bazirika ubgato ku nkombe." 
Mark6:54 Bavuye mu bgato, abaho baca baramumenya." 
Mark6:55 Birukanga impande zose mur’ ico gihugu cose, batangura guterura abarwaye mu nderuzo, babakwiragirana aho bamwumvise hose." 
Mark6:56 Kand’ aho yaja, mu mihana canke mu bisagara canke mu misozi, bāshira abarwaye mu tuguriro, bakamwinginga ngo bamukore naho hoba ku buyonga bg’impuzu yiwe gusa; abamukozeko bose bagakira." 
Mark7:1 Abafarisayo bakoranira kuri we n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe bamwe bavuye i Yerusalemu. 
Mark7:2 Babona abigishwa biwe bamwe barisha ivyo kurya intoke zihumanye, bisobanurwa ngo zidakaravye." 
Mark7:3 Arikw Abafarisayo n’Abayuda bose, iyo batīfyikinyuye mu gukaraba ntibārya, kuko bākurikiye imigenzo bābgirijwe n’aba kera." 
Mark7:4 Kandi bavuye mu kaguriro, iyo batīmijagiye amazi ntibārya, kandi harih’ ibindi vyinshi bābgirijwe n’aba kera ngo bavyumireko, nko kwoza mu buryo bginshi ibikombe n’inzavya n’inkono zikozwe mu miringa." 
Mark7:5 Abafarisayo n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe baramubaza, bati N’iki gitumye abigishwa bawe badakurikira ingeso twabgirijwe n’aba kera, bagapfa kurisha ivyo kurya intoke zihumanye?" 
Mark7:6 Arabishura, ati Yesaya yavuze neza ivyo yavugishijwe n’Imana kuri mwebge indyarya, nk’uko handitswe, ngw Aba bantu banyubahisha iminwa yabo, Arikw imitima yabo iri kure yanje." 
Mark7:7 Bansengera ubusa, Kukw inyigisho bigisha ar’ ivyagezwe n’abantu." 
Mark7:8 Ico Imana yageze murakireka ngo mwumire ku migenzo mwābgirijwe n’abantu. 
Mark7:9 Kand’ ati Nka ko mwagize neza gukēngēra icagezwe c’Imana, ngo muziririze iyo migenzo yanyu!" 
Mark7:10 Kuko Mose yavuze, ati Wubahe so na nyoko: kand’ at’ Ūtutse se canke nyina, ntaz’ abure kwicwa." 
Mark7:11 Ariko mweho mugira mut’ Umuntu ni yabgira se canke nyina, at’ Ico nari kugufashisha ni Korubani, risobanurwa ngo Ni co nzoshikanira Imana;" 
Mark7:12 ntimuba mukimukundira kugira ico yofasha se canke nyina; 
Mark7:13 ijambo ry’Imana mukaritituza imigenzo yanyu mwigishije: kandi mukora n’ibindi vyinshi ben’ ivyo. 
Mark7:14 Kandi yongera guhamagara ishengero, araribarira, ati Munyumve mwese, mubitahure:" 
Mark7:15 nta kintu kir’ inyuma, iyo kigiye imbere mu muntu gishobora kumuhumanya, arikw ibivuye mu muntu ni vyo bimuhumanya. [" 
Mark7:16 Namba har’ ūfise amatwi yumva, ni yumve.]" 
Mark7:17 Yinjiye mu nzu asize ishengero hanze, abigishwa biwe bamusiguza uwo mugani." 
Mark7:18 Na we arababaza, ati Mbega namwe mur’ imburabgenge murtyo? Ntimutahura yukw ata kintu kir’ inyuma iyo kigiye imbere mu muntu gishobora kumuhumanya," 
Mark7:19 kuko kitagiye mu mutima wiwe, ariko kija mu nda, kigaca mu nzira yaco? Ivyo yabivugiye kuzirura ivyo kurya vyose." 
Mark7:20 Kand’ aravuga, at’ Ibiva imbere mu muntu, ni vyo bimuhumanya:" 
Mark7:21 kukw imbere mu mitima y’abantu havamw’ ivyiyumviro bibi, ubushakanyi," 
Mark7:22 ubgivyi, ubgicanyi, ubusambanyi, ukwifuza, kugira nabi, ubugunge, ivy’ isoni nke, ijisho ribi, ibitutsi, ubgibone, ubupfu:" 
Mark7:23 ivyo bibi vyose biva imbere ni vyo bihumanya umuntu. 
Mark7:24 Ava aho hantu, aja mu ntāra yo muri Tiro n’i Sidoni. Yinjira mu nzu atagomba ko hogira umuntu abimenya, ariko ntiyashobora kuyoberana." 
Mark7:25 Arik’ uwo mwanya, umugore afise akigeme kinjiwemwo n’impwemu ihumanye, amwumvise, araza, yikubita imbere y’ibirenge vyiwe." 
Mark7:26 Uwo mugore yar’ Umugirikikazi, amamo yiwe n’i Sirofoyinike: aramwinginga ngw asende dayimoni mu mukobga wiwe." 
Mark7:27 Aramubgira, ati Reka abana babanze guhāga, kukw atari vyiza kwābīra umutsima w’abana ukawuterera utubga." 
Mark7:28 Na we aramwishura, ati Nka ko, Mugenzi, utubga na two turi musi y’ameza twīrīra utuvunguka tw’abana." 
Mark7:29 Aramubgira, ati K’uvuze urtyo ni wīgīre, dayimoni avuye mu mukobga wawe." 
Mark7:30 Arīgīra, ashitse mu nzu yiwe asanga umwana aryamye ku buriri, dayimoni amuvuyemwo." 
Mark7:31 Yongera kuva mu ntāra yo muri Tiro, araza aca i Sidoni, ashika ku kiyaga c’i Galilaya, aciye hagati y’intāra y’i Dekapoli." 
Mark7:32 Bamuzanira igipfamatwi kidatobora neza, baramwinginga ngw akirambikekw ikiganza." 
Mark7:33 Agikūra mw ishengero, aracihererana, agishira intoke mu matwi, acira amate, agikora ku rurimi." 
Mark7:34 Ararangamiza, arāba mw ijuru, yitsa umutima, arakibarira, ati Efata, risobanurwa ngo Zibūka." 
Mark7:35 Amatwi yiwe arazibūka, inkingi z’ururimi rwiwe zirabohoka, avuga neza." 
Mark7:36 Arabihanikiriza ngo ntihagire umuntu babibarira, arikw iy’ abihanikirije barushiriza gukwiza inkuru yiwe rwose." 
Mark7:37 Baratangara cane, baravuga, bat’ Akoze vyose neza: azibūra n’ibipfamatwi, kand’ avugisha ibiragi." 
Mark8:1 Mur’ iyo misi hongera kuba ishengero ryinshi, babura ivyo kurya; ahamagara abigishwa, arababarira," 
Mark8:2 at’ Ishengero rinteye akagongwe, kuk’ uyu ar’ umusi ugira gatatu turi kumwe, none ntibagira ico barya." 
Mark8:3 Nobasezera ngo basubire i wabo bashonje, bogwira isari mu nzira, kandi bamwe ar’ aba kure." 
Mark8:4 Abigishwa biwe baramubaza, bat’ Umuntu yokūra hehe imitsima yo guhāza aba bantu, ko hano ari mu gahinga?" 
Mark8:5 Arababaza, ati Mufise imitsima ingahe? Na bo bati N’indwi." 
Mark8:6 Abarira ishengero ngo ryicare hasi; yābīra ya mitsima ndwi, arayishimira, arayimanyagura, ayihēreza abigishwa biwe, ngo bayibagaburire: bayigaburira ishengero." 
Mark8:7 Kandi bāri bafise udufi duke; araduhezagira, avuga ko batubagaburira na two." 
Mark8:8 Bararya, barahāga, batororokanya utumanyagu tw’imisigazwa, twuzura ibivumvu ndwi." 
Mark8:9 Bāri nk’ibihumbi bine; arabasezera. 
Mark8:10 Uwo mwanya atambukira mu bgato, bo n’abigishwa biwe, aja ahēgereye i Dalamanuta." 
Mark8:11 Haza Abafarisayo, batangura kumuhāririza, bamuronderakw ikimenyetso kiva mw ijuru, bamugeza." 
Mark8:12 Yitsa umutima cane, ati N’iki gitumye ab’iki gihe barondera ikimenyetso? Ndababgira ukuri ab’iki gihe bakazohabga ikimenyetso?" 
Mark8:13 Abasiga hano, yongera gutambukira mu bgato, ajabuka hakurya." 
Mark8:14 Kandi bāri bibagiye gutekera imitsima, nta yo bāri bafise mu bgato, atar’ irobe rimwe." 
Mark8:15 Arabihanikiriza, ati Mumenye, mwirinde umwambiro w’Abafarisayo n’umwambiro wa Herode." 
Mark8:16 Bībūranya muri bo, bati Ntidufise imitsima." 
Mark8:17 Yesu arabimenya, arababaza, ati N’iki gitumye mwībūranya ngo nta mitsima mufise? Ntimuraruha mubimenya canke mubitahura? Mbega mufise imitima ikomantaye?" 
Mark8:18 Amaso ko muyafise ntimuruha mubona? Mufise amatwi, ntimwumva, kandi ntimwibuka?" 
Mark8:19 Hamwe namanyagurira ya mitsima itanu ibihumbi bitanu, mwatororokanije ibisimbo bingahe vyuzuye utumanyagu? Baramwishura, bati N’icumi na bibiri." 
Mark8:20 Ati Kandi hamwe namanyagurira ya mitsima ndwi ibihumbi bine, mwatororokanije ibivumvu bingahe vyuzuye utumanyagu? Baramwishura, bati N’indwi." 
Mark8:21 Arababaza, ati Ntimuraruha mubitahura?" 
Mark8:22 Baraza bashika i Betsayida. Bamuzanira impumyi, baramwinginga ngw ayikoreko." 
Mark8:23 Afata iyo mpumyi ukuboko, ayikūra mu mihana, acira amate mu maso yayo, ayirambikakw ibiganza, arayibaza, ati Har’ ico ubona?" 
Mark8:24 Iraramura amaso, iramwishura, iti Ndabona abantu kuko mbona ibisa n’ibiti bigendagenda." 
Mark8:25 Yongera kurambika ibiganza ku maso yayo, iritegereza, irakira, yihweza vyose neza." 
Mark8:26 Amurungika i we, ati Ntuje no mur’ iyi mihana." 
Mark8:27 Yesu avanayo n’abigishwa biwe, aja mu mihana y’i Kayisariya mu bga Filipo: bari mu nzira, abaza abigishwa biwe, at’ Abantu bagira ngo ndi nde?" 
Mark8:28 Baramwishura, bati Bagira ng’ uri Yohana Umubatizi, abandi ng’ uri Eliya, abandi ng’ ur’ umwe mu bavugishwa n’Imana." 
Mark8:29 Na we arababaza, at’ Ariko mweho mugira ngo ndi nde? Petero aramwishura, at’ Uri Kristo." 
Mark8:30 Arabihanikiriza ngo ntihagire umuntu babgira ivyiwe. 
Mark8:31 Atangura kubigisha, at’ Umwana w’umuntu akwiye kuzobabazwa uburyo bginshi, no kuzokwankwa n’abashingantahe n’abaherezi bakuru n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe, no kuzokwicwa, maze hashize imisi itatu akazuka." 
Mark8:32 Avuga iryo jambo adakingitiranije. Petero aramwihererana, atangura kumwāmira." 
Mark8:33 Arahindukira, abona abigishwa biwe, akankamira Petero, ati Herēra inyuma yanje, Satani, kukw ivy’ Imana atari vyo ubabaye, ariko n’ivy’ abantu." 
Mark8:34 Ahamagara ishengero bo n’abigishwa biwe, arababgira, at’ Umuntu ni yagomba kunkurikira, ni yiyanke, yikorere umusaraba wiwe, ankurikire;" 
Mark8:35 kuk’ ūgomba gukiza ubugingo bgiwe azobubura, arik’ ūzoheba ubugingo bgiwe kubganje no kubg’ ubutumwa bgiza, azobukiza." 
Mark8:36 Kand’ umuntu vyomumarira iki kwunguka ivyo mw isi vyose, ni yakwa ubugingo bgiwe kw iciru?" 
Mark8:37 Mbeg’ umuntu yotanga iki ngw acungure ubugingo bgiwe? 
Mark8:38 Kuk’ umuntu wese bizotera isoni kunyemera no kwemera amajambo yanje mur’ iki gihe c’ubusambanyi kandi c’ikinyavyaha, n’Umwana w’umuntu bizomutera isoni kumwemera, ah’ azozira afise ubgiza bga Se, azananye n’abamarayika bera." 
Mark9:1 Arababgira, ati Ndababgira ukuri: mur’ aba bahagaze hano harimwo bamwe batazobona urupfu gushitsa aho bazobonera ubgami bg’Imana buzananye n’ubushobozi." 
Mark9:2 Imisi itandatu ishize, Yesu ajana Petero na Yakobo na Yohana, abadūgana igisozi kirekire ari bonyene. Ahinduka ukundi imbere yabo," 
Mark9:3 impuzu ziwe zirakayangana, zera derere, kandi nta mumesuzi kw isi yoshoboye kuzeza artyo." 
Mark9:4 Maze Eliya na Mose barabiyereka, bavugana na Yesu." 
Mark9:5 Petero abgira Yesu, ati Mwigisha, bitubereye vyiza ko turi hano, nuko duce insago zitatu, rumwe rwawe, urundi rwa Mose, urundi rwa Eliya." 
Mark9:6 Ntiyar’ azi ico akwiye kuvuga, kuko bari baguye igihūmura." 
Mark9:7 Maz’ igicu kiraza kibatera igitūtu, ijwi riva muri nya gicu, riti Nguyu Umwana wanje nkunda, ni mumwumve." 
Mark9:8 Maze bakebaguza vuba, ntibaba bakigira uwundi babona, atari Yesu wenyene, ari kumwe na bo." 
Mark9:9 Bariko baramanuka ico gisozi, arabihanikiriza ngo ntihagire umuntu badondera ivyo babonye, Umwana w’umuntu atarazuka avuye mu bapfuye." 
Mark9:10 Babīka iryo jambo, basiguzanya ivy’ ukuzuka mu bapfuye ivy’ ari vyo." 
Mark9:11 Baramubaza, bati Mbeg’ abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe ko bavuga yuko Eliya akwiye kubanza kuza?" 
Mark9:12 Arabishura, ati Eliya abanza kuza koko, akaroranya vyose neza. Ariko vyanditswe bite ku Mwana w’umuntu yukw azobabazwa vyinshi, agatiturwa?" 
Mark9:13 Ariko ndababgira yuko Eliya yamaze kuza, kandi bamwigiriye uko bagomba kwose, nk’uko vyanditswe kuri we." 
Mark9:14 Bariko barashikīra abigishwa, babona ishengero ryinshi ribajiguje, n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe bahārīra na bo." 
Mark9:15 Uwo mwanya ishengero ryose rimurabutswe riratangara rwose, barirukanga baramusanganira, baramuramutsa." 
Mark9:16 Arababaza, ati Mwariko murabahāririza ibiki?" 
Mark9:17 Umwe mur’ iryo shengero aramwishura, ati Mwigisha, nari nakuzaniye umwana wanje, yinjiwemwo n’impwemu y’ikiragi." 
Mark9:18 Ah’ imufatiye hose, imutūra hasi, akabimba ifuro, akazyegenya amenyo, akagenda ashira umunywera; mbarira abigishwa bawe ngo bayisende, irabananira." 
Mark9:19 Arabishura, ati Yemwe ab’iki gihe mutizera, nzogeza ryari kubana namwe? Nzogeza ryari kubihanganira? Ni mumunzanire." 
Mark9:20 Baramuzana. Iyo mpwemu imubonye ica iramujegeza cane, aratemba, arigaragura, abimba ifuro." 
Mark9:21 Yesu abaza se, at’ Amaze igihe kingana iki bimutera birtyo? Aramwishura, at’ Uhereye mu bgana bgiwe." 
Mark9:22 Kenshi cane imuta mu muriro no mu mazi ngw imwice. Ariko namba har’ ico woshobora, tugirire akagongwe udutabare." 
Mark9:23 Yesu aramwishura, at’ Uvuze uti Namba wobishobora? Erega vyose bishobokera uwizeye."
