Mark9:24 Se w’uwo mwana aca aturika cane, ati Ndizeye, fasha ukutizera kwanje." 
Mark9:25 Yesu abonye abantu bagwirirana biruka, akankamira iyo mpwemu ihumanye, ati Yewe mpwemu y’ikiragi kandi y’igipfamatwi, ubganje ndakubariye muvemwo, ntukamugarukemw’ ukundi." 
Mark9:26 Irataka, iramujegeza cane, imuvamwo, amera nk’ūhwereye, bituma abenshi bavuga bat’ Arahwereye." 
Mark9:27 Yesu amufata ukuboko, aramuvyura, arahagarara." 
Mark9:28 Yinjiye mu nzu, abigishwa biwe bamubaza biherereye, bati Tweho mbega ko vyatunaniye kuyisenda?" 
Mark9:29 Arabishura, ati Ben’ irya ntikūrwamwo n’ikindi atar’ ugusenga no kwisonzesha." 
Mark9:30 Bavayo, baca i Galilaya, agomba ko hatogira ūbimenya." 
Mark9:31 Kuko yigisha abigishwa biwe, at’ Umwana w’umuntu azoshirwa mu maboko y’abantu, bazomwica, hashize imisi itatu bamwishe, azozuka." 
Mark9:32 Ariko bayoberwa iryo jambo, batinya kurimubaza." 
Mark9:33 Bashika i Kaperinawumu. Yinjiye mu nzu arababaza, ati Mwāhārīra ibiki mu nzira?" 
Mark9:34 Barīhorera, kuko mu nzira bāhārīra umukuru wabo uw’ ari we." 
Mark9:35 Aricara, ahamagara bamwe cumi na babiri, arababgira, at’ Umuntu ni yagomba kuba uw’ imbere, n’abe inyuma ya bose, n’abe n’umukozi wa bose." 
Mark9:36 Yābīra akana, agahagarika hagati yabo; arakarera, arababgira," 
Mark9:37 at’ Ūzokwākīra umwe mu twana nk’aka mw izina ryanje, azoba anyakiriye; kand’ ūnyakīra, si jewe yākīra, ariko yākīra uwantumye." 
Mark9:38 Yohana aramubgira, ati Mwigisha, twabonye umuntu asenda abadayimoni mw izina ryawe, turamubuza, kukw atadukurikira." 
Mark9:39 Yesu aramwishura, ati Ntimumubuze, kukw ata muntu azokora igitangaza mw izina ryanje, azoshobora guca amvuga nabi." 
Mark9:40 Kuk’ ūtar’ umwansi wacu ari mu ruhande rwacu. 
Mark9:41 Umuntu wese azobaha n’urwato rw’amazi kuko muri mw izina rya Kristo, ndababgire ukuri, ntazobura impēra yiwe." 
Mark9:42 Kand’ ūzotsitaza n’umwe mur’ abo bato banyizera, iciza n’uko yohambīrirwa urusyo ruremereye kw izosi, agatererwa mu kiyaga." 
Mark9:43 Ukuboko kwawe ni kwagutsitaza, uguce igikonjo; vyokubera vyiza kwinjira mu bugingo ucitse igikonjo, hak’ uja muri Gehinomu mu muriro utazima, ufise amaboko yompi: [" 
Mark9:44 ah’ inyo zabo zidapfa, kandi n’umuriro utazima.]" 
Mark9:45 N’ikirenge cawe ni cagutsitaza, ugice; vyokubera vyiza kwinjira mu bugingo ucitse ikirenge, hak’ utererwa muri Gehinomu, ufise ibirenge vyompi: [" 
Mark9:46 ah’ inyo zabo zidapfa, kandi n’umuriro utazima.]" 
Mark9:47 N’ijisho ryawe ni ryagutsitaza, urinogore; vyokubera vyiza kwinjira mu bgami bg’Imana upfuye ijisho, hāk’ utererwa muri Gehinomu ufise amaso yompi:" 
Mark9:48 ah’ inyo zabo zidapfa, kandi n’umuriro utazima." 
Mark9:49 Kand’ umuntu wese azoryoshwa n’umuriro, nk’uk’ umunyu uryosha." 
Mark9:50 Umunyu ni mwiza, arik’ umunyu woshira uburyohe, mwoba mukiwuryohesha iki? Mugire umunyu mu mitima yanyu, kandi mubane amahoro." 
Mark10:1 Arīkora avayo, aja mu gihugu c’i Yudaya no hakurya ya Yorodani, ishengero ryongera gukoranira kuri we, yongera kubigisha nk’uko yamenyereye." 
Mark10:2 Abafarisayo baza kuri we, baramugeza, bati Mbega biremerwa k’umuntu yirukana umugore wiwe?" 
Mark10:3 Na we arababaza, ati Mose yabagereye iki?" 
Mark10:4 Baramwishura, bati Mose yemeye ko handikwa icete co kuvāvānura, akamwirukana." 
Mark10:5 Yesu arababgira, ati Gukomantara kw’imitima yanyu ni kwo kwamwandikishije ico cagezwe." 
Mark10:6 Arik’ uhereye kw itanguriro ry’ukuremwa, Imana yabaremye bar’ uburyo bubiri." 
Mark10:7 Ni co gituma umuntu azosiga se na nyina, akabana n’umugore wiwe akaramata," 
Mark10:8 bompi bakaba umubiri umwe. Bituma batakiri babiri, ariko baba babaye umubiri umwe." 
Mark10:9 Nukw ico Imana yamatanije umuntu ntaz’ akimature. 
Mark10:10 Yinjiye mu nzu abigishwa bongera kumubaza iryo jambo. 
Mark10:11 Arababgira, at’ Umuntu wese yirukana umugore wiwe, akābīra uwundi, aba asambanye kand’ amuhemukiye." 
Mark10:12 Kandi na we ubgiwe, ni yāhukana n’umugabo wiwe, akābīrwa n’uwundi, azoba asambanye." 
Mark10:13 Maze bamuzanira abana bato, ngw abakoreko: abigishwa barabakankamira." 
Mark10:14 Maze Yesu abibonye, araraka, arababarira, ati Ni mureke abana bato baze aho ndi, ntimubabuze: kuk’ ubgami bg’Imana ar’ ubg’ abameze bartyo." 
Mark10:15 Ndababgire ukuri, ūtazokwākīra ubgami bg’Imana nk’umwana muto, ntazobginjiramwo na gatoya." 
Mark10:16 Arabarera, arabahezagira, abarambitsekw ibiganza." 
Mark10:17 Agisohoka ngw akomeze urugendo, haza umuntu kuri we yirukanga, aramupfukamira, aramubaza, ati Mwigisha mwiza, nkore iki, ngo nze ndagwe ubugingo budashira?" 
Mark10:18 Yesu aramubaza, at’ Unyitira iki mwiza? Nta mwiza, atar’ umwe, ni we Mana." 
Mark10:19 K’uzi ivyagezwe, ngo Ntukice, ntugasambane, ntukibe, ntukāgirize abandi ibinyoma, ntukagunge, wubahe so na nyoko." 
Mark10:20 Aramubgira, ati Mwigisha, ivyo vyose naravyitondeye, mpereye mu buto bganje." 
Mark10:21 Yesu amwitegereje aramukunda, aramubgira, at’ Uhajije kimwe: genda, ushōre ivy’ utunze vyose, ugabire aboro, ni ho uzogira itunga mw ijuru, utek’ uze, unkurikire." 
Mark10:22 Yumvise iryo jambo arijirwa, agenda ababaye, kuko yar’ afise itunga ryinshi." 
Mark10:23 Yesu yeraguza amaso, abgira abigishwa biwe, at’ Erega biragoye kw aba vyinshi binjira mu bgami bg’Imana!" 
Mark10:24 Abigishwa batangazwa n’amajambo yiwe. Yesu yongera kubabgira, ati Bana banje, erega biragoye kw abizigiye ubutunzi binjira mu bgami bg’Imana!" 
Mark10:25 Icoroshe n’ingamiya guca mu zuru ry’urushinge biruta umutunzi ko yinjira mu bgami bg’Imana. 
Mark10:26 Baratangara rwose, bati None rero, ni nde ashobora gukizwa?" 
Mark10:27 Yesu arabitegereza, arababgira, ati Kubg’ abantu ntigishoboka, ariko ku Mana s’uko, kuko vyose bishobokera Imana." 
Mark10:28 Maze Petero atangura kumubgira, ati Rāba, twebge twaretse vyose turagukurikira." 
Mark10:29 Yesu arababgira, ati Ndababgire ukuri, Nta waretse inzu, canke bene nyina, canke bashiki biwe, canke nyina, canke se, cank’ abana, cank’ itongo, kubganje no kubg’ ubutumwa bgiza," 
Mark10:30 atazobishumbushwa ijana mur’ iki gihe ca none, amazu, na bene nyina, na bashiki biwe, na ba nyina, n’abana, n’itongo, bisukiranijwe no guhamwa, kandi mu gihe kizoza azohabga ubugingo budashira." 
Mark10:31 Ariko benshi b’imbere bazoba ab’ inyuma, kand’ ab’ inyuma bazoba ab’ imbere." 
Mark10:32 Bāri mu nzira badūga i Yerusalemu. Yesu yar’ abagiye imbere, baratangara, abāmukurikira baratinya. Yongera kujana bamwe cumi na babiri bar’ ukwabo, atangura kubabarira ibigira bimubeko," 
Mark10:33 at’ Ehe, turadūze i Yerusalemu, kand’ Umwana w’umuntu azoshirwa mu maboko y’abaherezi bakuru n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe, bazomucira urubanza rwo gupfa, bamuhe abanyamahanga," 
Mark10:34 bamushinyagurire, bamuvume amate, bamutonagure, bamwice, maz’ imisi itatu ishize azozuka." 
Mark10:35 Yakobo na Yohana bene Zebedayo baramwēgēra baramubgira, bati Mwigisha, turagomba k’uduha ico tugusaba cose." 
Mark10:36 Arababaza, ati Mugomba ko mbaha iki?" 
Mark10:37 Baramwishura, bat’ Uduhe ngo tuze twicare, umwe i buryo bgawe uwundi i bumoso, mu bgiza bgawe." 
Mark10:38 Maze Yesu arabishura, ati Ntimuzi ico musaba. Mwoshobora kunywera ku gikombe nnywerako, canke kubatizwa umubatizo mbatizwa jewe?" 
Mark10:39 Baramwishura, bati Turashobora. Yesu arababgira, at’ Igikombe nnywerako, muzokinywerako, kandi muzobatizwa umubatizo mbatizwa jewe." 
Mark10:40 Ariko gutanga ivyicaro i buryo bganje cank’ i bumoso, s’ivyanje, shit’ abo vyateguriwe." 
Mark10:41 Bamwe cumi bavyumvise batangura kwitonganiriza ivya Yakobo na Yohana. 
Mark10:42 Yesu arabahamagara, arababgira, ati Murazi yukw abavugwa ko baganza amahanga bayatwaza amanyama, kandi n’abakuru bayo bayagirak’ ububasha." 
Mark10:43 Ariko muri mwebge si ko biri. Yamar’ ūgomba kuba mukuru muri mwebge, az’ abe umukozi wanyu:" 
Mark10:44 kand’ ūgomba kuba uw’ imbere, az’ abe umuja wa mwese." 
Mark10:45 Kuko na none Umwana w’umuntu atāzanywe no gukorerwa, atar’ ugukorera abandi, no gutanga ubugingo bgiwe kw incungu ya benshi." 
Mark10:46 Nuko bashika i Yeriko: akivana i Yeriko n’abigishwa biwe n’ishengero ryinshi, mwene Timayo yitwa Barutimayo, umusēzi w’impumyi, yari yicaye i ruhande y’inzira." 
Mark10:47 Yumvise kw ari Yesu Umunyanazareti atangura gutakamba, ati Yesu, mwana wa Dawidi, ngirira imbabazi." 
Mark10:48 Abantu benshi baramuzibiranya ngw ahore: arikw arushiriza cane gutakamba, ati Mwana wa Dawidi, ngirira imbabazi." 
Mark10:49 Yesu arahagarara, arababarira, ati Ni mumuhamagare. Bahamagara iyo mpumyi, barayibgira, bati Hūmura, va hasi, araguhamagaye." 
Mark10:50 Na yo ita impuzu yayo, irabaduka, yēgēra Yesu." 
Mark10:51 Yesu arayibaza, at’ Ugomba ko ngukorera iki? Ino mpumyi iramwishura, iti Ndagomba guhumūka, Mwigisha." 
Mark10:52 Yesu arayibgira, ati Genda, ukwizera kwawe kuragukijije. Aca arahumūka, amukurikira ku nzira." 
Mark11:1 Bageze hafi y’i Yerusalemu, bashikira i Betifage n’i Betaniya ku musozi wa Elayono, atuma babiri bo mu bigishwa biwe," 
Mark11:2 arababarira, ati Muje mur’ iriya mihana ir’ imbere yanyu; ni mwayishikamwo, muca mubona inyana y’indogoba iziritse, ata muntu yigeze kuyigenderako: muyiziture muyizane." 
Mark11:3 Kandi ni hagira ūbabaza, at’ Ivyo mubikoreye iki? Mumwishure, muti Databuja ni we ayigomba. Uwo mwanya arayirungika ino." 
Mark11:4 Baragenda, basanga inyana y’indogoba iziritse i ruhande y’irembo ku nzira, barayizitura." 
Mark11:5 Bamwe mu bahahagaze barababaza, bati Mukora iki ko muzitura iyo nyana?" 
Mark11:6 Na bo babishura nk’uko Yesu yababariye: barabareka. 
Mark11:7 Bazana iyo nyana aho Yesu ari, bayishirakw impuzu zabo, ayicarako." 
Mark11:8 Benshi basasa impuzu zabo mu nzira, abandi basasa amashami y’ibiti, ayo baciye mu matongo." 
Mark11:9 Abar’ imbere yiwe n’abamukurikiye barasemerera, bati Hoziyana, hashemezwe ūje mw izina ry’Uhoraho," 
Mark11:10 ubgami buje bushimwe, ni bgo bga sogokuruza Dawidi; Hoziyana mw ijuru." 
Mark11:11 Ashika i Yerusalemu, yinjira mu rusengero, maz’ ahejeje kweraguza vyose, kuko bgari bugorovye, arasohoka, aja i Betaniya, ajanye na bamwe cumi na babiri." 
Mark11:12 Bukeye bamaze kuva i Betaniya, yumva arashonje." 
Mark11:13 Akiri kure, abona umusukoni urikw amababi, arawēgēra ngo kumbure yogira ic’ awusangako: awushitseko ntiyagira ic’ awubonako, atar’ amababi: kuko kitār’ igihe co kwama c’umusukoni." 
Mark11:14 Arawubgira, ati Ntugapfe har’ ūriye ku nsukoni zawe uhereye ubu ugashitsa ibihe bidashira. Abigishwa biwe baravyumva." 
Mark11:15 Bashika i Yerusalemu. Yinjira mu rusengero, atangura guhindira hanze abarudandarizamwo n’abaruguriramwo, ahenura ameza y’abāvunja amahera n’intebe z’abāriko baragurwakw inuma," 
Mark11:16 ntiyakundira umuntu n’umwe guhita mu rusengero atwaye ikintu co mu mbombovu. 
Mark11:17 Arigisha arababgira, ati Mbega ntivyanditswe, ngw Ingoro yanje izokwitwa inzu yo gusengerwamwo n’amahanga yose? Ariko mwebge mwayihinduye nk’isenga ry’abambuzi." 
Mark11:18 Abaherezi bakuru n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe bavyumvise barondera ingene bomwica, kuko bāmutinya, kukw abantu bose batangazwa n’inyigisho ziwe." 
Mark11:19 Iyo bugorovye, yama ava mu gisagara." 
Mark11:20 Bukeye kare‐kare bariko barahita babona wa musukoni, wahereye ku mizi wakabiranye." 
Mark11:21 Petero yibutse aramubgira, ati Mwigisha, ehe wa musukoni wavumye wakabiranye." 
Mark11:22 Yesu aramwishura, arababgira, ati Mwamane ukwizera Imana." 
Mark11:23 Ndababgira ukuri yuk’ umuntu wese yobgira uyu musozi, ati Shingūka utabge mu kiyaga: ntabikekeranye mu mutima, arikw akizera yukw ico avuze gikorwa, azokibona." 
Mark11:24 Ni co gitumye mbabgira yukw ivyo musenga canke musaba vyose, mwizere yuko mubihawe, kandi muzobibona." 
Mark11:25 Kandi ni mwahagarara musenga, ni haba har’ ico mupfa n’uwundi, mukimuharire, ngo So wo mw ijuru na we abaharire ivyaha vyanyu: [" 
Mark11:26 ariko ni mutāharira abandi, na So wo mw ijuru ntazobaharira ivyaha vyanyu.]" 
Mark11:27 Bongera kuja i Yerusalemu. Akigendagenda mu rusengero, abaherezi bakuru n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe n’abashingantahe baza kuri we," 
Mark11:28 baramubaza, bati N’ububasha ki bugutera gukora ivyo? Canke ni nde yaguhaye ubgo bubasha bgo kubikora?" 
Mark11:29 Yesu arabishura, ati Nanje hinge ndababaze ijambo rimwe, munyishure; mpeze ndababarire ububasha bunkoresha ivyo." 
Mark11:30 Non’ ukubatiza kwa Yohana kwaturutse mw ijuru, canke se mu bantu? Ni munyishure." 
Mark11:31 Bībūranya muri bo, bati Ni twavuga tuti Ni mw ijuru; ahava atubaza, ati N’iki cababujije kumwemera?" 
Mark11:32 Ariko mbega tuvuge tuti Ni mu bantu? Batinya abantu, kuko bose biyumvira badakekeranya yuko Yohana yavugishwa n’Imana." 
Mark11:33 Bishura Yesu, bati Ntituhazi. Yesu arababgira, ati Nuko rero nanje simbabgira ububasha bunkoresha ivyo." 
Mark12:1 Atangura kubabgira mu migani, ati Hābaye umuntu yateye uruzabibu, aruzitirira uruzitiro, yimbamw’ ubgato bg’ikinogo, yubakamw’ umutara, arusigarana abarimyi, aja mu mahanga." 
Mark12:2 Hageze mw iyera atuma umukozi ku barimyi, ngw aze yake abo barimyi ivyāmūwe mu ruzabibu." 
Mark12:3 Baramufata, baramushishagura, bamurungika gusa." 
Mark12:4 Yongera kubatumak’ uwundi mukozi, uwo bamukubita uruguma mu mutwe, baramutetereza." 
Mark12:5 Atuma uwundi, uwo we baramwica: atuma n’abandi benshi, bamwe barabashishagura, abandi barabica." 
Mark12:6 Yar’ agisigaranye umwe, umwana wiwe akunda: hanyuma amubatumako, ati Bazosonera umwana wanje." 
Mark12:7 Maz’ abo barimyi baravugana, bat’ Urya ni we samuragwa; ni muze tumwice, umwandu uz’ ube uwacu." 
Mark12:8 Baramufata, baramwica, bamukwegera inyuma y’uruzabibu." 
Mark12:9 None nyen’ uruzabibu azogenza ate? Abo barimyi azoza abice rubi, uruzabibu arusigarane abandi." 
Mark12:10 Mbega nta ho murasoma iki canditswe, ngw Ibuye abubatsi bāgaye Ni ryo ryahindutse irigumya imfuruka;" 
Mark12:11 Ivyo vyavuye k’Uhoraho, Kandi n’igitangaza mu maso yacu?" 
Mark12:12 Barondera ingene bomufata, batinya abantu: kuko bamenye yukw ari bo yaciyek’ uwo mugani; bamusiga hano, baragenda." 
Mark12:13 Bamutumako bamwe mu Bafarisayo n’abantu ba Herode, ngo bamutegeshe amajambo." 
Mark12:14 Bāje baramubgira, bati Mwigisha, turazi yuk’ ur’ umunyakuri, kandi k’udatinya umuntu wese ku kigohe, kuk’ udatinya ijunja ry’abantu, ariko ko wigisha inzira y’Imana vy’ukuri. Mbega biremerwa gutanga ikori rya Kayisari, canke ntivyemerwa?" 
Mark12:15 Turitange, canke dusigeho? Maz’ amenye uburyarya bgabo arababaza, ati Mungereza iki? Ni munzanire idenariyo, ndayirābe." 
Mark12:16 Barayizana. Arababaza, at’ Iki gishushanyo n’ibi vyanditsweko n’ivya nde? Baramwishura, bati N’ivya Kayisari." 
Mark12:17 Yesu arababarira, at’ Ivya Kayisari ni mubihe Kayisari, ivy’ Imana mubihe Imana. Baramutangarira cane." 
Mark12:18 Maz’ Abasadukayo baza kuri we, abahakana yukw ata kuzuka kuriho, baramubaza," 
Mark12:19 bati Mwigisha, Mose yatwandikiye yuko mwene nyina w’umuntu ni yapfa, agasiga umugore wiwe, adasize umwana, mwene nyina akwiye gucūra uwo mugore, ngw ahonore mwene nyina." 
Mark12:20 Hābaye abavukana ndwi: uwa mbere ararongora, arapfa, ntiyasiga abana;" 
Mark12:21 uwa kabiri acūra umupfakazi wiwe, na we apfa adasize abana; n’uwa gatatu aba artyo;" 
Mark12:22 bose ukw ar’ indwi ntibāsiga abana. Hanyuma ya bose, na wa mugore arapfa." 
Mark12:23 Mbega mw izuka azoba muka nde muri bo? Ko bāri bamufise bose ukw ar’ indwi! 
Mark12:24 Yesu arabishura, at’ Igituma muzimira mbega s’uko mutāmenye ivyanditswe cank’ ubushobozi bg’Imana?" 
Mark12:25 Aho bazozukira mu bapfuye ntibazorongora kandi ntibazoshingirwa: bazoba nk’abamarayika bo mw ijuru. 
Mark12:26 Arikw ivy’ abapfuye yuko bazurwa, nta ho murasoma mu gitabo ca Mose hamwe havuga ivy’ Igisaka c’amahwa, ingen’ Imana yamubgiye, iti Ni jewe Mana ya Aburahamu, Imana ya Isaka, Imana ya Yakobo?" 
Mark12:27 Imana s’iy’ abapfuye, n’iy’ abariho: mwarazimiye cane." 
Mark12:28 Haza umwe mu banyabgenge b’ivyanditswe yumva babazanya, amenye kw abishuye neza, aramubaza, at’ Ibgirizwa ry’imbere muri yose n’irihe?" 
Mark12:29 Yesu aramwishura, at’ Iry’ imbere n’iri, ngo Ni mwumve, yemwe Bisirayeli: Uhoraho Imana yacu ni we Uhoraho wenyene." 
Mark12:30 Kandi mukundishe Uhoraho Imana yanyu imitima yanyu yose, n’ubugingo bganyu bgose, n’ubgenge bganyu bgose, n’inkomezi zanyu zose." 
Mark12:31 Irya kabiri ngiri, Mukunde bagenzi banyu nk’uko mwikunda; nta rindi bgirizwa risumba ayo." 
Mark12:32 Uno munyabgenge w’ivyanditswe aramubgira, ati Ni koko, Mwigisha, uvuze ivy’ ukuri yukw ar’ Imwe, nta yindi, atari yo yonyene:" 
Mark12:33 kandi kuyikundisha umutima wose, n’ugutahura kwose, n’inkomezi zose, bo n’ugukunda mugenzawe nk’uko wikunda, biruta cane ibimazi vyose vyoshejwe n’ibitoshejwe." 
Mark12:34 Yesu abonye amwishuranye ubgenge, aramubgira, ati Nturi kure y’ubgami bg’Imana. Ntihāgira ūsubira kwubahuka kugira ico amubaza." 
Mark12:35 Kandi Yesu yigishiriza mu rusengero, arababaza, at’ Abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe bavuga bate yuko Kristo ari mwene Dawidi?" 
Mark12:36 Dawidi ubgiwe yavugishijwe na Mpwemu Yera, aravuga, at’ Uhoraho yabariye Umwami wanje, At’ Icara i buryo bganje, Ushitse aho nzoshirira abansi bawe musi y’ibirenge vyawe." 
Mark12:37 Dawidi kw ari we amwita Umwami, non’ ivyo kuba umwana wiwe vyavuye hehe? Abenshi mw ishengero banezererwa kumwumva." 
Mark12:38 Kand’ ababarira mu kwigisha kwiwe, ati Mwirinde abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe, bakunda kugenda bambaye imvune, no kugirwako bgakeye mu tuguriro," 
Mark12:39 no kwicara ku ntebe z’icubahiro mu masinagogi, n’ivyicaro vyo haruguru aho batumiwe." 
Mark12:40 Barya ingo z’abapfakazi, kandi basengesha menshi bahumba: abo bazocirwa urubanza ruruta izindi." 
Mark12:41 Yicara yerekeye ku masandugu y’amahera, abona ingen’ ishengero rishikana amahera, bayaterera mur’ ayo masandugu: benshi b’abatunzi batereramwo menshi." 
Mark12:42 Haza umupfakazi w’umworo, atereramw’ amasenge abiri, ni yo kuta." 
Mark12:43 Ahamagara abigishwa biwe, arababgira, ati Ndababgire ukuri, Uyu mupfakazi w’umworo ashikanye ibirengeye ivyo bose batereye mu masandugu:" 
Mark12:44 kuko bose bashikanye ku bibasāgutse, ariko we ku bgoro bgiwe ashikanye ivyo yar’ afise vyose, n’ibimutunze vyose." 
Mark13:1 Arikw arasohoka mu rusengero, umwe mu bigishwa biwe aramubgira, ati Mwigisha, rāba aya mabuye ukw ari, n’iyi nyubako ukw iri!" 
Mark13:2 Yesu aramubaza, at’ Urarāba iyi nyubako ihambaye? Ntihazosigazwa ibuye rigeretse ku rindi, ridasamburiwe hasi." 
Mark13:3 Yicaye ku musozi wa Elayono yerekeye ku rusengero, Petero na Yakobo na Yohana na Andereya baramubaza bihereranye," 
Mark13:4 bati Tubgire, ivyo bizobaho ryari, ikimenyetso kizoba iki, c’igihe ivyo vyose bizoba bigira bishike?" 
Mark13:5 Yesu atangura kubabgira, ati Mwirinde ntihagire ūbazimiza." 
Mark13:6 Benshi bazoza mw izina ryanje, bati Ndi we; kandi bazozimiza benshi." 
Mark13:7 Kandi ni mwumva intambara n’impuha z’intambara, ntimuze muhagarike imitima: ntibizobura kubaho, arik’ umuhero uzoba utaraza." 
Mark13:8 Kukw ihanga rizotera irindi hanga, n’ubgami buzotera ubundi bgami, isi izonyiganyiga henshi, amapfa azotera. Ivyo n’itanguriro ryo kuramukwa." 
Mark13:9 Ariko mwiyubare: kuko bazobashengerana mu manza, muzoshishagurirwa mu masinagogi, kandi muzohagarara imbere y’abaganza n’abami babampōra, mube ikimenyetso kibabere icabona." 
Mark13:10 Ubutumwa bgiza bukwiye kubanza kuvugwa mu mahanga yose. 
Mark13:11 Kandi ni babajana babashengeranye, ntimuze muhagarikire imitima ico muzovuga; ico muzohabga cose mur’ ako kanya, muze mube ari co muvuga: kukw atazoba ari mwebge muvuga, azoba ari Mpwemu Yera." 
Mark13:12 Umuntu azoshengerana uwo bavukana ngo bamwice, na se w’umwana azomushengerana, n’abana bazogābagābira abavyeyi babicishe." 
Mark13:13 Muzoba mwanswe na bose, babahōra izina ryanje: arik’ uwihangana, agashitsa iherezo, ni we azokira." 
Mark13:14 Ariko, aho muzobonera ca kizira c’ubuyobe bg’ubugesera gihagaze aho kidakwiye, (ūsoma ni yiyubare), ico gihe abazoba bar’ i Yudaya baze bahungire ku misozi miremire," 
Mark13:15 ūzoba ari hejuru ku nzu ntaze yururutswe no kwinjira gusahura ikintu cose mu nzu yiwe: 
Mark13:16 ūzoba ari mu mirima ntaz’ asubizwe inyuma no gusahura umutamana wiwe. 
Mark13:17 Ariko mur’ iyo misi abazoba batwaye inda n’abonsa bazobona ibara: 
Mark13:18 kandi muze musenge kugira ngo ntibize bibe mu rushana. 
Mark13:19 Kukw iyo misi izoba iy’ amarushwa atigeze kubaho, kuva kw itanguriro ry’ibiremwa Imana yaremye ugashitsa n’ubu, kand’ atazokwongera kubaho." 
Mark13:20 Iyaba Umwami Imana itogeruye iyo misi, ntihorokotse umuntu n’umwe, ariko kubg’ abatoranijwe yatoranije, yarayigeruye." 
Mark13:21 Ico gihe ni hagira umuntu ababgira, at’ Ehe Kristo ari hano; cank’ at’ Ari hariya: ntimuze muvyemere." 
Mark13:22 Kuko hazokwaduka abīgira Kristo n’abīgira abavugishwa n’Imana, bagakora ibimenyetso n’ibitangaza, kugira ngo bazimize n’abatoranijwe, ni vyashoboka." 
Mark13:23 Ariko mweho mwiyubare: rāba ndabibabgiye vyose bitaraba. 
Mark13:24 Ariko mur’ iyo misi, hanyuma y’ayo marushwa, izuba rizocura umwiza, n’ukwezi ntikuzoba kucaka umuco wakwo," 
Mark13:25 n’inyenyeri zizoba ziriko zirakoragurika ziva kw ijuru, n’ivy’ inkomezi vyo mu majuru bizonyiganyizwa." 
Mark13:26 Ni ho bazobona Umwana w’umuntu aje mu bicu, ari n’ububasha bginshi n’ubgiza." 
Mark13:27 Ni ho azotuma abamarayika, akoranye abatoranijwe biwe, bave mu birēre bine, guhēra ku mpera y’isi kugeza impera y’ijuru." 
Mark13:28 Ni mwigire ku musukoni umugani wawo: ishami ryawo iyo ritoshe, amababi agatutuza, mumenya yukw agatāsi kari hafi:" 
Mark13:29 nuko namwe ni mwabona ivyo bibaye, muze mumenye kw ari hafi, ku rugi." 
Mark13:30 Ndababgire ukuri: Ab’iki gihe ntibazorangira, ivyo vyose bitarashika." 
Mark13:31 Ijuru n’isi bizorangira, arikw amajambo yanje nta co azoba." 
Mark13:32 Arik’ uwo musi cank’ iyo saha, nta wubizi, n’iyo boba abamarayika bo mw ijuru, cank’ Umwana w’Imana, atari Data gusa." 
Mark13:33 Mwiyubare, mube maso, musenge; kuko mutazi igihe bizoshikira." 
Mark13:34 Ni nk’umuntu yasize urugo rwiwe, aja mu kindi gihugu, asigarana abashumba biwe urugo, kand’ ahejeje kugerera umuntu wese igikorwa ciwe, abarira umuteramyi ngo yame agavye." 
Mark13:35 Nuko mwame mugavye, kuko mutazi igihe nyen’ urugo azozamwo, namb’ ari ku mugoroba, canke mu gicugu, canke mu nkoko, cank’ umutwenzi ukītse:" 
Mark13:36 kugira ngo ni yaza giturumbuka, ntasange musinziriye." 
Mark13:37 Arikw ico mbabariye, ndakibarira bose, nti Mwame mugavye." 
Mark14:1 Hāri hasigaye imisi ibiri, imisi mikuru ya Pasika ikagera, ni yo yo kurya imitsima itambiwe. Abaherezi bakuru n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe barondera uburyo bgo gusuka Yesu ngo bamufate bamwice:" 
Mark14:2 kuko bāvuga, bati Ntitumufate mu misi mikuru, abantu bogūmūka." 
Mark14:3 Ar’i Betaniya mu nzu kwa Simoni umunyamibembe, yicaye arikw ararya, haza umugore afise ikebano ry’amavuta atāmirana, y’igiciro kinini cane, y’agati kitwa narada: amena iryo kebano, amavuta ayamusuka ku mutwe." 
Mark14:4 Bamwe muri bo barītonganya, bati Mbeg’ ubu buhombe bg’aya mavuta n’ubg’ iki?" 
Mark14:5 Kuko yoshoboye kugurwa idenariyo amajana atatu arenga, zigahabga aboro: baramwidodombera." 
Mark14:6 Yesu arababarira, ati Ni mumureke! Mumubabariza iki? Ankoreye igikorwa ciza." 
Mark14:7 Aboro murāmana imisi yose; aho mwogombera mwobagirira neza; ariko jeho ntituja kwamana imisi yose. 
Mark14:8 Akoze ukw ashoboye, ansutse amavuta ku mubiri kuwutegurira guhambga bitaraba." 
Mark14:9 Ndababgire ukuri: Ah’ ubutumwa bgiza buzovugwa hose mw isi yose, n’ico uyu akoze kizovugwa, kibe icibutso ciwe." 
Mark14:10 Kandi Yuda Isikaryota, yar’ umwe muri bamwe cumi na babiri, aja ku baherezi bakuru, ngw az’ amubaronkere." 
Mark14:11 Bavyumvise baranezerwa, basezerana kumuha amahera y’ifeza. Arondera uburyo bgo kumubaronkera." 
Mark14:12 Ku musi w’intangamarāra wo kurya imitsima itambiwe, uwo bābāgak’ umwagazi w’intama wa Pasika, abigishwa biwe baramubaza, bat’ Ugomba ko twoja hehe gutegura ivya Pasika ng’ ubirye?" 
Mark14:13 Atuma babiri mu bigishwa biwe, arababarira, ati Ni muje mu gisagara, umugabo muribuhūre yikoreye umubindi w’amazi mumukurikire." 
Mark14:14 Ah’ aja kwinjira mubgire nyen’ urwo rugo, mut’ Umwigisha agize ngw Indāro yiwe iri hehe, ah’ asangirira ivya Pasika n’abigishwa biwe?" 
Mark14:15 Ubgiwe aribubereke inzu nini yo hejuru, isēzeye, iteguritse; abe ari yo muduteguriramwo." 
Mark14:16 Ba bigishwa baragenda, baja mu gisagara, babisanga uko yabibabariye: bategura ivya Pasika." 
Mark14:17 Bugorovye azanana na bamwe cumi na babiri. 
Mark14:18 Bicaye bariko bararya, Yesu arababgira, ati Ndababgire ukuri: Umwe muri mwebge, uwo dusangira, agira angure." 
Mark14:19 Batangura kubabara, bamubaza umwe‐umwe, bati Mbega ni jewe?" 
Mark14:20 Arabishura, at’ Umwe muri mwebge cumi na babiri, uwo turiko turakoreza amaboko rimwe mu mubehe, ni we." 
Mark14:21 Umwana w’umuntu agira agende uko vyanditswe kuri we: arik’ uwo muntu agura Umwana w’umuntu azobona ibara; uwo muntu ivyomubereye vyiza iyaba atāvutse. 
Mark14:22 Maze bariko bararya, yābīra umutsima; awuhezagiye arawumanyagura, arawubaha, ati Ni mwābīre, uyu n’umubiri wanje." 
Mark14:23 Yābīra igikombe; agishimiye Imana arakibaha, bakinywerako bose." 
Mark14:24 Arababarira, at’ Ico n’amaraso yanje y’isezerano, aviriye benshi." 
Mark14:25 Ndababgire ukuri: Sinzokwongera kunywa ku nzabibu, gushitsa kuri wa musi nzonywera umutobe wazo musha mu bgami bg’Imana." 
Mark14:26 Bahejeje kuririmba, barasohoka, baja ku musozi wa Elayono." 
Mark14:27 Maze Yesu arababgira, ati Mwese muhava mutsitazwa: kuko handitswe, ngo Nzokubita umwungere, intama zisanzare." 
Mark14:28 Ariko ni namara kuzurwa, nzobītangira imbere kuja i Galilaya." 
Mark14:29 Maze Petero aramubgira, ati N’iyo vyotsitaza bose, urakūra jeho." 
Mark14:30 Yesu aramubgira, ati Ndakubgira ukuri yuko wewe ubgawe uyu musi mur’ iri joro nyene, inkoko itaragereka uhava unyihakana gatatu." 
Mark14:31 Arikw arīhanukīra cane, ati N’iyo noba nkwiye gupfana nawe, sinokwihakana. N’abandi na bo bavuga bartyo bose." 
Mark14:32 Maze bashika ahantu hitwa i Getsemane, abarira abigishwa biwe, ati Ba muricaye hano, mbanze nje gusenga." 
Mark14:33 Ajana Petero na Yakobo na Yohana, atangura kwumirwa no guhagarika umutima cane." 
Mark14:34 Arababgira, at’ Umutima wanje uri n’akabonge kagomba kunyica; ba muragumye hano, mube maso." 
Mark14:35 Yunguruza imbere gatoya, yubama hasi arasenga ngw ico gihe kimurengāne, asangwa bishoboka." 
Mark14:36 Ati Abba, Data, vyose biragushobokera: kūra iki gikombe kindēngāne: ariko ntibibe uko jewe ngomba, yamara bibe uko wewe ugomba." 
Mark14:37 Aragaruka, asanga basinziriye, abaza Petero, ati Simoni, urasinziriye? Nturushe uba maso n’isaha n’imwe?" 
Mark14:38 Ni mube maso, musenge, ntimuje mu mosha mabi. Umutima ni wo ukunze, arik’ umubiri ufise intege nke." 
Mark14:39 Yongera kugenda, arasenga, avuga amajambo amwe n’aya mbere." 
Mark14:40 Yongera kugaruka, asanga basinziriye, kukw amaso yabo yar’ aremerewe cane, ntibāmenya ico bamwishura." 
Mark14:41 Agaruka ubugira gatatu, arababarira, ati Ni mwisinzirire noneho, muruhuke: biraheze. Igihe kirashitse; rāba Umwana w’umuntu ashizwe mu maboko y’abanyavyaha." 
Mark14:42 Ni muvyuke, tugende: eh’ ūnguze ari hafi." 
Mark14:43 Buno nyene akivuga, Yuda, umwe muri bamwe cumi na babiri, araza, azananye n’igitero kizanye inkota n’amahiri, kivuye ku baherezi bakuru n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe n’abashingantahe." 
Mark14:44 Arik’ ūmugura yari yabahaye ikimenyetso, at’ Uwo nja gusoma azoba ari we, mumufate, mumujane mumugumije." 
Mark14:45 Ashitse, aca aramwēgēra, ati Mwigisha: maz’ aramusomagura." 
Mark14:46 Bamushōrerakw amaboko, baramufata." 
Mark14:47 Maz’ umwe mu bahagazeho asokora inkota, ayikubita umushumba w’umuherezi mukuru, amuca ugutwi." 
Mark14:48 Yesu arababaza, ati Mbega munziye kumfata nk’umwambuzi, muzanye inkota n’amahiri?" 
Mark14:49 Ko nāmana namwe mu rusengero nigisha imisi yose, ntimumfate: arikw ibi bibaye kugira ngw ivyanditswe bishike." 
Mark14:50 Maze bose baramuta barahunga. 
Mark14:51 Kand’ umuhungu umwe w’umusore amuja inyuma, yikuvyekw impuzu imwe gusa, baramufata:" 
Mark14:52 abatāna impuzu yiwe, ahunga amēnya." 
Mark14:53 Bajana Yesu ku muherezi mukuru, abaherezi bakuru bose n’abashingantahe n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe bakoraniraho." 
Mark14:54 Petero amuja inyuma barenga arenguka, ashika imbere mu rugo rw’umuherezi mukuru; yicarana n’abagendanyi yota umuriro." 
Mark14:55 Maz’ abaherezi bakuru n’abashingantahe b’amakombe bose baronderera Yesu ibirego vyomwicisha, barabibura." 
Mark14:56 Nah’ abāmurega ibinyoma bāri benshi, ibirego vyabo ntivyari bihūye." 
Mark14:57 Bamwe bava hasi, baramubeshera," 
Mark14:58 bati Twebge twaramwumvise avuga, ati Nzosambura uru rusengero rwubatswe n’intoke nubake urundi mu misi itatu, rutubatswe n’intoke." 
Mark14:59 Ariko na ho nyene amagambo yabo ntiyar’ ahūye. 
Mark14:60 Umuherezi mukuru arahaguruka, ahagarara hagati, abaza Yesu, ati Nta co wiregura? Aba bakwagirije iki?" 
Mark14:61 Arihorera, ntiyamwishura na rimwe. Umuherezi mukuru yongera kumubaza, ati Ni wewe Kristo, Umwana w’Īshimwa?" 
Mark14:62 Yesu aramwishura, ati Ndi we; kandi muzobona Umwana w’umuntu yicaye i buryo bg’Ububasha, azananye n’ibicu vyo kw ijuru." 
Mark14:63 Maz’ umuherezi mukuru yitantamurirakw imyambaro yiwe, aravuga, ati Turacaronderera iki ivyabona?" 
Mark14:64 Murīyumviye ingen’ arogose: mugira ngw iki? Bose bamucira urubanza ngw akwiye gupfa. 
Mark14:65 Bamwe batangura kumuvuma amate, bamupfuka mu maso, bamukubita ibipfunsi, bati N’udupfīndūre. Abagendanyi bamushikizakw inshi." 
Mark14:66 Petero akiri mu rugo ahahera hepfo, haza umwe mu ncoreke z’umuherezi mukuru," 
Mark14:67 abonye Petero yota umuriro, aramwitegereza, aramubgira, ati Nawe nyene mwari kumwe na wa Munyanazareti Yesu." 
Mark14:68 Na we arabihakana, ati Sinzi ico uvuze, singitahuye. Maz’ arunguruza, ashika mu bikingi vy’irembo; inkoko irabika." 
Mark14:69 Ya ncoreke imubonye, itangura kwongera kubgira abahagazeho, it’ Uyu n’uwo muri bo." 
Mark14:70 Na we yongera kubihakana. Maze hahise akanya, abahagazeho bongera kubgira Petero, bati N’ivy’ ukuri ur’ uwo muri bo, bitayeko ur’ Umunyagalilaya." 
Mark14:71 Na we atangura kurahira arīsiba, at’ Uyo muntu muvuga sindanamuzi." 
Mark14:72 Uwo mwanya inkoko ibika ubugira kabiri. Petero yibuka rya jambo Yesu yamubgiye, at’ Inkoko itaragereka, uja kunyihakana gatatu; avyiyumviriye, ararira." 
Mark15:1 Umutwenzi utambitse, uwo mwanya abaherezi bakuru n’abashingantahe n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe n’abashingantahe b’amakombe bose baja inama, baboha Yesu, baramujana, bamushikiriza Pilato." 
Mark15:2 Pilato aramubaza, ati Ni wewe Mwami w’Abayuda? Na we aramwishura, at’ Urarivuze." 
Mark15:3 Abaherezi bakuru bamurega vyinshi. 
Mark15:4 Pilato yongera kumubaza, ati Nta co wiregura? Umve ivyo bakwagiriza ingen’ ari vyinshi." 
Mark15:5 Maze Yesu ntiyasubira kwishura ijambo na rimwe, bituma Pilato atangara." 
Mark15:6 Mur’ iyo misi mikuru yahora abarekurira imbohe imwe, uwo bamusavye." 
Mark15:7 Hārih’ umwe yitwa Baraba, yabohanywe n’abāgararije, bishe abantu mur’ ukwo kugarariza." 
Mark15:8 Ishengero riradūga, ritangura gusaba kw abagirira nk’uko yamenyereye." 
Mark15:9 Pilato arababaza, ati Muragomba ko mbarekurira Umwami w’Abayuda?" 
Mark15:10 Kuko yamenye yukw ishari ari ryo ryatumye abaherezi bakuru bamutanga. 
Mark15:11 Maz’ abaherezi bakuru bosha ishengero gusaba ngw ivyoba vyiza abarekurire Baraba. 
Mark15:12 Pilato yongera kubabaza, ati Non’ uwo mwita Umwami w’Abayuda, we ndamugire nte?" 
Mark15:13 Bongera kuyogora, bati Mubambe." 
Mark15:14 Pilato arababaza, ati Ku ki? Yakoze ikibi ki? Maze barushiriza kuyogora cane, bati Mubambe." 
Mark15:15 Pilato agomvye kumara ishavu ishengero, abarekurira Baraba, maz’ atanga Yesu ngw abambge, amaze kumutonagura." 
Mark15:16 Maz’ abasoda bamujana imbere mu rugo, ari rwo boma, bahamagara ingabo zose, ziraterana." 
Mark15:17 Bamwambika impuzu y’ishigisha, batsiba igitsibo c’amahwa, bakimwambika mu mutwe;" 
Mark15:18 batangura kumuramutsa, bati Ndagize bgakeye, Mwami w’Abayuda." 
Mark15:19 Bamukubita irenga mu mutwe, bamuvuma amate, barapfukama, bamukomera amashi." 
Mark15:20 Bamaze kumucurīra, bamwambura ya mpuzu y’ishigisha, bamwambika iziwe mpuzu, bamurengana irembo bamushoreye kumubamba." 
Mark15:21 Bafata umuntu ahita, Simoni Umunyakurene, avuye mu misozi, ni se wa Alekisandero na Rufo, ngw amutwaze umusaraba." 
Mark15:22 Bamushikana ahitwa i Gologota, risobanurwa ngw Ahantu h’agahanga." 
Mark15:23 Bamuha vino ivanze n’umuti w’umururazi, ntiyayinywa." 
Mark15:24 Baramubamba, bagabura impuzu ziwe, barazipfindira, ngo bamenye iyo umuntu wese atwara." 
Mark15:25 Igihe bāmubamba zar’ isaha zitatu. 
Mark15:26 Icandiko c’ikirego candikwa hejuru yiwe ng’ UMWAMI W’ABAYUDA. 
Mark15:27 Kandi babambana na we abambuzi babiri, umwe i buryo bgiwe, uwundi i bumoso. [" 
Mark15:28 Nukw ivyanditswe birashika, ngo Yaharūranywe n’abanyavyaha.]" 
Mark15:29 Abahahita baramucurīra, bazunguza imitwe, bati Yō, wewe usambura urusengero, ukarwubaka mu misi itatu," 
Mark15:30 ni wikize, wimanure ku musaraba." 
Mark15:31 N’abaherezi bakuru bamucurīra bartyo, banwengurana n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe, bati Yakijije abandi, we ntashobora kwikiza:" 
Mark15:32 Kristo Umwami w’Abisirayeli ni yimanure ku musaraba ubu nyene, tubibone twizere. N’abāri babambanywe na we na bo baramutuka." 
Mark15:33 Maz’ isaha zitandatu zishitse, ubgīrakabiri bukorana mu gihugu cose, bushitsa kw isaha y’icenda." 
Mark15:34 Kw isaha y’icenda Yesu asemerera n’ijwi rirenga, ati Eloi, Eloi, lama sabakatani? Risobanurwa ngo Mana yanje, Mana yanje, n’iki kikumpebesheje?" 
Mark15:35 Maze bamwe mu bahahagaze bavyumvise baravuga, bat’ Umve, ahamagaye Eliya." 
Mark15:36 Umwe arirukanga, yābīra sipongo, ayuzuza inkarisha, ayirungikisha irenga; arayimusomesha, ati Hinge turābe ko Eliya yoza kumubambūra." 
Mark15:37 Maze Yesu avuga n’ijwi rirenga, aracīkāna." 
Mark15:38 Igihuzu gikīngiriza ahēra cane h’urusengero gitantamukamwo kubiri, uhereye hejuru ugashitsa hasi." 
Mark15:39 Umugabisha w’abasoda ijana yar’ ahahagaze bahanganye, abonye acīkānye artyo, aravuga, ati N’ivy’ ukuri, uyu muntu yar’ Umwana w’Imana." 
Mark15:40 Hāriho n’abagore bāri kure babirāba, muri bo hārimwo Mariya Magadalene, na Mariya nyina wa Yakobo mutoya na Yose, hārimwo na Salome." 
Mark15:41 Abo bagore, aho yaba i Galilaya, bāramukurikira bakamukorera: kandi hāriho n’abandi bagore benshi bāri badūganye na we i Yerusalemu." 
Mark15:42 Bugorovye, kuko war’ umusi wo Kwitegura, ni wo musi utangurira isabato," 
Mark15:43 haza Yosefu w’i Arimataya, umunyekombe w’icubahiro, kandi na we yar’ areretse ubgami bg’Imana, ararinduka aja kuri Pilato, asaba ikiziga ca Yesu." 
Mark15:44 Ariko Pilato biramutangaza ko yoba amaze gupfa; ahamagaza wa mugabisha w’abasoda, amubaza yukw amaze umwanya apfuye." 
Mark15:45 Maze yumvise ivy’ uwo mugabisha amubgiye, aha Yosefu ikiziga." 
Mark15:46 Agura impuzu yera, arakibambūra akizingira mur’ ino mpuzu, agishira mu mva yimbge mu bitandara, atembagaza ikibuye acugaza umuryango w’imva." 
Mark15:47 Mariya Magadalene na Mariya nyina wa Yose babona ah’ ahambge. 
Mark16:1 Maz’ isabato ishize, Mariya Magadalene, na Mariya nyina wa Yakobo, na Salome bagura ibimota neza, ngo baje kubimusīga." 
Mark16:2 Kandi mu mutwenzi ku wa mbere w’imisi ndwi barazinduka, bashika ku mva izuba rimennye ijuru." 
Mark16:3 Barabazanya, bati Ni nde adutembagariza ikibuye co ku munwa w’imva?" 
Mark16:4 Maze bunamuye amaso babona ca kibuye catembagajwe cavuyeho, kandi cari kinini cane." 
Mark16:5 Maze binjiye mu mva, babona umusore yicaye mu ruhande rw’i buryo, yambaye imvune yera, barūmirwa cane." 
Mark16:6 Arababgira, ati Nta co mwumirwa: ndazi yuko murondera Yesu Umunyanazareti umwe yabambga: none yazutse, ntari hano: ehe, rāba aho bāri bamushize!" 
Mark16:7 Ariko ni mugende mubgire abigishwa biwe na Petero, mut’ Arabītangira imbere kuja i Galilaya, iyo ni ho muzomubonera, nk’uko yababgiye." 
Mark16:8 Bava mu mva, barahunga, kuko bari bafashwe n’agatengo n’akumiza, maze ntibāgira ico babgira umuntu n’umwe, kuko batinye. [" 
Mark16:9 Yesu amaze kuzuka mu mutwenzi ku wa mbere w’imisi ndwi, abanza kwiyereka Mariya Magadalene, uwo yasenzemw’ abadayimoni ndwi." 
Mark16:10 Uwo aragenda, abibarira abābana na we, asanga bababaye barira." 
Mark16:11 Na bo bumvise kw ari muzima, kandi ko yamwiboneye, ntibāvyemera." 
Mark16:12 Hanyuma y’ivyo yiyereka babiri muri bo, afise iyindi shusho, bagenda baja mu misozi." 
Mark16:13 Na bo nyene baragenda, babibgira abasigaye, maze ntibābemerera na bo." 
Mark16:14 Hanyuma yiyereka bamwe cumi n’umwe, bicaye bariko bararya, abagaya ukutizera kwabo no gukomantara kw’imitima yabo, kuko batemereye abāmubonye, amaze kuzuka." 
Mark16:15 Arababarira, ati Mugende muje mu bihugu vyose, mubgire abāremwe bose ubutumwa bgiza." 
Mark16:16 Uwizera akabatizwa azokizwa, arik’ ūtizera azotsindwa n’urubanza." 
Mark16:17 Kand’ ibimenyetso bizokwama biboneka ku bizera n’ibi: bazosenda abadayimoni mw izina ryanje; bazovuga indimi nsha; 
Mark16:18 bazofata inzoka; ni banywa ikintu cica, nta co kizobagira na gatoya; bazorambika ibiganza ku barwaye, bakire." 
Mark16:19 Kand’ Umwami Yesu ahejeje kubibabarira, adūzwa mw ijuru, avyagira i buryo bg’Imana." 
Mark16:20 Abo bavayo, bigisha hose, Umwami Yesu akorana na bo, ijambo ryiwe arishingishiriza intahe ibimenyetso birikurikira. Amen.]" 
Luke1:1 Abantu benshi bāgerageje kwandika amajambo adonda ivyābaye muri twebge," 
Luke1:2 nk’uko twabirazwe n’abāhereye ubga mbere ar’ivyabona vyavyo n’abasuku b’ijambo ry’Imana. 
Luke1:3 Nuko nanje, mpejeje gukurikiranya vyose neza mpereye ku vya mbere, nabonye kw ari vyiza kubikwandikira uko bikurikirana, wewe Teyofilo umwubahwa," 
Luke1:4 kugira ng’ umenye neza yukw amajambo wigishijwe ar’ ay’ ukuri adakekeranywa. 
Luke1:5 Ku ngoma ya Herode, umwami w’i Yudaya, hārih’ umuherezi yitwa Zakariya, wo mu mutigiri wa Abiya, kandi yar’ afise umugore wo mu nzu ya Aroni, yitwa Elisabeti." 
Luke1:6 Bompi bāgororoka imbere y’Imana, bāgendera mu vyagezwe n’amabgirizwa vy’Umwami Imana vyose, batagawa." 
Luke1:7 Ariko ntibagira umwana, kuko Elisabeti yar’ ingumba, kandi bompi bāri bageze mu zabukuru." 
Luke1:8 Maze yarikw arakora igikorwa c’ubuherezi imbere y’Imana, ukw imbu zabo zikurikirana;" 
Luke1:9 kandi nk’uk’ umugenzo w’abaherezi war’ uri, ni we yari yatoranijwe n’ubupfindo kwinjira ahēra h’urusengero rw’Umwami Imana, kwosa imibavu:" 
Luke1:10 kand’ ishengero ryose ry’ubgo bgoko ryariko rirasengera hanze mu gihe co kwosa. 
Luke1:11 Maz’ umumarayika w’Umwami Imana aramwiyereka, ahagaze i buryo bg’igicaniro boserezakw imibavu." 
Luke1:12 Zakariya amubonye ahagarika umutima, aterwa n’ubgoba." 
Luke1:13 Umumarayika aramubgira, ati Nta co utinya, Zakariya, kukw ivyo wasavye vyumviswe, umugore wawe Elisabeti azokuvyarira umuhungu, uz’ umwite Yohana:" 
Luke1:14 uzonezerwa, uzohimbarwa, kandi benshi bazonezererwa ukuvuka kwiwe;" 
Luke1:15 kukw azoba mukuru mu nyonga z’Umwami Imana; ntazonywa vino cank’ ikiboreza na kimwe; azokwuzuzwa Mpwemu Yera, ahereye ku kuva mu nda ya nyina," 
Luke1:16 kand’ azosanganya benshi bo mu Bisirayeli n’Umwami Imana yabo. 
Luke1:17 Azoyiza imbere ari n’umutima wa Eliya n’ubushobozi bgiwe, ngw asanganye imitima ya ba se n’iy’ abana, n’intabarirwa azisubize ku bgenge bg’abagororotsi, ategurire Umwami Imana ubgoko burorane." 
Luke1:18 Zakariya abaza umumarayika, at’ Ivyo nzovyerekwa n’iki, ko nd’umutāma, n’umugore wanje akaba ageze mu zabukuru?" 
Luke1:19 Umumarayika aramwishura, ati Ndi Gaburiyeli, nama mpagaze mu nyonga z’Imana, kandi natumwe kubonana nawe no kukubgira ubgo butumwa bgiza." 
Luke1:20 Umve, uragobga ururimi, kandi ntuzoshobora kuvuga, kugeza ku musi ivyo bizoberako, kuk’ utemeye ijambo ryanje, rizoshika mu gihe caryo." 
Luke1:21 Abantu bāri barorereye Zakariya batangazwa n’ukw atevye ahēra h’urusengero. 
Luke1:22 Maz’ asohotse ntiyagira ico ashobora kuvugana na bo, bamenya yuko har’ ico yerekewe ahēra h’urusengero: arabagereraniriza, agumya kuba ikiragi." 
Luke1:23 Maz’ imisi yo gusasa kwiwe ishize, asubira i we." 
Luke1:24 Iyo misi ishize, umugore wiwe Elisabeti asama inda, atinya abantu amezi atanu," 
Luke1:25 at’ Uku ni k’Umwami Imana inkoreye mu misi yandābiyemwo kunteturura mu bantu. 
Luke1:26 Kandi mu kwezi kwa gatandatu, umumarayika Gaburiyeli atumwa n’Imana mu gisagara c’i Galilaya citwa Nazareti," 
Luke1:27 ku nkumi ikowe n’umugabo yitwa Yosefu, wo mu nzu ya Dawidi, izina ry’iyo nkumi ni Mariya." 
Luke1:28 Yinjira ah’ ari, aramubgira, ati N’amahoro, ugiriwe ubuntu, Umwami Imana ari kumwe nawe." 
Luke1:29 Ariko we ahagarika umutima cane w’iryo jambo, yibaza iyo ndamukanyo iy’ ari yo." 
Luke1:30 Umumarayika aramubgira, ati Nta co utinya, Mariya, kuk’ ugiriwe ubuntu n’Imana." 
Luke1:31 Umve, uzosama inda, uvyare umuhungu, kand’ uz’ umwite YESU." 
Luke1:32 Azoba mukuru, azokwitwa Umwana w’Īsumba vyose, kand’ Umwami Imana azomuha intebe y’ubgami ya sekuruza Dawidi," 
Luke1:33 ahangame mu nzu ya Yakobo ibihe bidashira; ubgami bgiwe ntibuzogira iherezo. 
Luke1:34 Mariya abaza umumarayika, at’ Ivyo bizobaho bite, ko ntaramenya icitwa umugabo?" 
Luke1:35 Umumarayika aramwishura, ati Mpwemu Yera azokuzako, ubushobozi bg’Īsumba vyose buzogutera igitūtu: ni co gituma uwera azovuka azokwitwa Umwana w’Imana." 
Luke1:36 Kand’ umve, Elisabeti mwene wanyu na we atwaye inda y’umuhungu mu butāmakazi bgiwe, uwitwa ingumba uku n’ukwezi kwiwe kwa gatandatu:" 
Luke1:37 kukw ata jambo rivuye ku Mana ribura ububasha. 
Luke1:38 Mariya aramubgira, at’ Ehe nd’ umugurano w’Umwami Imana, bimbere ukw ijambo ryawe rivuzwe. Maz’ umumarayika ava ah’ ari, aragenda." 
Luke1:39 Mur’ iyo misi Mariya arikora, agenda yihuta, aja mu mugamba mu gisagara c’i Yudaya," 
Luke1:40 yinjira mu nzu kwa Zakariya, aramukanya na Elisabeti." 
Luke1:41 Maze Elisabeti yumvise indamukanyo ya Mariya, inda ikinagira muri we, Elisabeti yuzuzwa Mpwemu Yera," 
Luke1:42 avuga n’ijwi rirenga, ati Mu bagore urahiriwe, n’imbuto yo mu nda yawe irahiriwe." 
Luke1:43 Kand’ iki kimbereyekw iki, nyina w’Umwami wanje kuza aho ndi?" 
Luke1:44 Kukw ijwi ry’indamukanyo yawe ryinjiye mu matwi yanje, inda igakinagizwa muri jewe n’umunezero." 
Luke1:45 Kandi hahirwa wewe wizeye, kukw ivyo wabgiwe n’Umwami Imana bizoshika." 
Luke1:46 Mariya aravuga, at’ Ubugingo bganje butazira Umwami Imana," 
Luke1:47 Umutima wanje unezererewe Imana Umukiza wanje: 
Luke1:48 Kuko yabonye ubufafara bg’umugurano wayo, Kand’ uhereye none, ab’ ibihe vyose bazonyita umuhirwa." 
Luke1:49 Kukw Iy’ ubushobozi inkoreye ibikomeye, Kand’ izina ryayo n’iryera." 
Luke1:50 Imbabazi zayo ziri ku bayubaha ku buzukuru no ku buzukuruza‐kuruza babo: 
Luke1:51 Yerekanishije ubushobozi ukuboko kwayo, Yasābagije abībona mu vyo biyumvira mu mitima yabo." 
Luke1:52 Yirukanye abaganza ku ntebe zabo, Yashize hejuru abafafara." 
Luke1:53 Abashonje yabahāgije ivyiza, Yirukanye abatunzi bagenda imvumure." 
Luke1:54 Yatabaye Isirayeli umusavyi wayo, Maze ngw imbabazi zayo izibuke," 
Luke1:55 Nk’uko yabgiye ba sogokuruza, Kuzigirira Aburahamu n’uruvyaro rwiwe, ibihe bidashira." 
Luke1:56 Kandi Mariya amarana na we amezi nk’atatu, asubira i wabo." 
Luke1:57 Igihe co kuvyara kwa Elisabeti kirashika, avyara umuhungu." 
Luke1:58 Ababanyi biwe n’incuti ziwe bumva yuk’ Umwami Imana yamugiriye imbabazi nyinshi, banezeranwa na we." 
Luke1:59 Ku musi ugira umunani baza gukeba uwo mwana, bagomba kumwitiranya na se Zakariya." 
Luke1:60 Nyina arababgira, at’ Oya, ni yitwe Yohana." 
Luke1:61 Baramubgira, bati Mu muryango wanyu kw ata witwa iryo zina." 
Luke1:62 Bagereraniriza se, bamubaza ukw agomba ko yitwa." 
Luke1:63 Yaka ico kwandikako, arandika, at’ Izina ryiwe ni Yohana." 
Luke1:64 Bose baratangara. Uwo mwanya akanwa kiwe karazibūka, n’ururimi rwiwe ruragobodoka, aravuga, ashima Imana." 
Luke1:65 Ababanyi babo bose baterwa n’ubgoba: ayo majambo yose akwira mu mugamba wose w’i Yudaya. 
Luke1:66 Abavyumvise bose babishira mu mitima yabo, bati Mbe non’ uyo mwana azoba umuntu ki? Kuk’ ukuboko kw’Umwami Imana kwari kumwe na we." 
Luke1:67 Se Zakariya yuzuzwa Mpwemu Yera, avugishwa n’Imana," 
Luke1:68 at’ Umwami ashimwe, Imana y’Abisirayeli, Kukw igendeye abantu bayo, ikabacungura;" 
Luke1:69 Kand’ iduhagurukirije ihembe ry’agakiza Mu nzu ya Dawidi umusavyi wayo," 
Luke1:70 Nk’uko yavugiye mu kanwa k’abera yavugisha, bāhereye mbere na mbere," 
Luke1:71 Ngw idukize abansi bacu n’amaboko y’abatwanka bose: 
Luke1:72 Kand’ igirire ba sogokuruza imbabazi, Yibuke isezerano ryayo ryera," 
Luke1:73 Indahiro yarahiye sogokuruza Aburahamu," 
Luke1:74 Kw izoduha gukizwa amaboko y’abansi bacu, Tukayisenga ata bgoba," 
Luke1:75 Tur’ abera tugororoka mu nyonga zayo imisi yacu yose. 
Luke1:76 Kandi nawe, mwana, uzokwitwa umuntu avugishwa n’Īsumba vyose, Kuk’ uzokwītangira imbere y’Umwami Imana gutegūra inzira ziwe:" 
Luke1:77 Kumenyesha abantu biwe agakiza, Kw ar’ uguharirwa ivyaha vyabo," 
Luke1:78 Kubg’ umutima w’imbabazi w’Imana yacu, Ni wo uzotuma umutwenzi utugendera, uvuye mw ijuru," 
Luke1:79 Ng’utambikire abicaye mu mwiza no mu gitūtu c’urupfu, Urōngōrere ibirenge vyacu mu nzira y’amahoro." 
Luke1:80 Nya mwana arakura, agwiza inkomezi z’umutima, aba mu bugaragwa kugeza umusi yerekewekw Abisirayeli." 
Luke2:1 Mur’ iyo misi icagezwe kiva kwa Kayisari Augusito, ngw abo mw isi bose bandikwe." 
Luke2:2 Ukwo ni kwo kwandikwa kwa mbere kwabayeho Kureniyo akir’ icēgēra ca Kayisari i Siriya. 
Luke2:3 Bose baja kwiyandikisha, umuntu wese aja mu gisagara cabo." 
Luke2:4 Yosefu na we ava i Galilaya mu gisagara c’i Nazareti, aja i Yudaya mu gisagara ca Dawidi, citwa Betelehemu, kuko yakomotse mu nzu ya Dawidi mu muryango wiwe:" 
Luke2:5 aja kwiyandikishanya na Mariya uwo yakoye, yar’ akuriwe." 
Luke2:6 Bakiriyo, igihe ciwe co kuvyara kirashika." 
Luke2:7 Avyara umuhungu w’uburiza, amuzingirakw impuzu y’uruyoya, amuryamika mu bgato bg’inka, kuko bāri babuze umwanya mu ndāro." 
Luke2:8 Mur’ iyo ntāra hār’ abungere bārāra mu gahinga barāririye umukuku w’intungwa zabo. 
Luke2:9 Umumarayika w’Umwami Imana ahagarara i ruhande yabo, ubgiza bg’Umwami bubakayanganira irya n’ino, baterwa n’ubgoba bginshi." 
Luke2:10 Umumarayika arababgira, ati Nta co mutinya, umve ndababarira ubutumwa bgiza bg’akanyamuneza kenshi kazoba ku bgoko bganyu bgose." 
Luke2:11 Uyu musi Umukiza abavukiye mu gisagara ca Dawidi, ni we Kristo Umwami." 
Luke2:12 Iki ni co kimenyamenya canyu, murasanga umwana w’uruyoya azingiriwekw impuzu y’uruyoya, aryamitswe mu bgato bg’inka." 
Luke2:13 Uwo mwanya hamwe n’uwo mumarayika haboneka ingabo nyinshi zo mw ijuru, zihimbaza Imana," 
Luke2:14 zit’ Icubahiro ni kibe ku Mana ahasumba ijuru, No mw isi amahoro abe mu b’inezererwa." 
Luke2:15 Ba bamarayika bahejeje kuva aho bari, basubiye mw ijuru, nya bungere baravugana, bati Ngo rero tuje i Betelehemu, turābe ico kintu cabayeyo, ico Umwami Imana atumenyesheje." 
Luke2:16 Bagenda banyaruka, babona Mariya na Yosefu n’uruyoya rubīkiriwe mu bgato bg’inka." 
Luke2:17 Babibonye bababarira ijambo bābgiwe kur’ uwo mwana. 
Luke2:18 Abavyumvise bose batangazwa n’ivyo ba bungere bababgiye. 
Luke2:19 Ariko Mariya abīka ayo majambo yose, ayiyumvira mu mutima wiwe." 
Luke2:20 Maze ba bungere bahindukira bahimbaza Imana, bayishimira ivyo bumvise vyose n’ivyo babonye, nk’uko bābibgiwe." 
Luke2:21 Kand’ imisi munani ishitse ngw akebge, bamwita YESU, rya zina ryavuzwe n’umumarayika, atarasamwa inda." 
Luke2:22 Imisi ishize yo guhumanurwa kwabo, nk’ukw ivyagezwe vya Mose biri, bamujana i Yerusalemu kumushikanira Umwami Imana," 
Luke2:23 nk’uko vyanditswe mu vyagezwe n’Umwami Imana, ng’ Umuhungu wese w’ubuzibūra aze yitwe uwera k’Uhoraho;" 
Luke2:24 kandi ngo batange ikimazi, nk’uko vyavuzwe mu vyagezwe n’Umwami Imana, ngw Intunguru zibiri cank’ ivyana vy’inuma bibiri." 
Luke2:25 Kandi muri Yerusalemu hār’ umuntu yitwa Simeyoni; uyo yar’ umuntu agororotse kandi yubaha Imana, yar’ arorereye uguhumurizwa kw’Abisirayeli, Mpwemu Yera yari kuri we." 
Luke2:26 Yari yarabgiwe na Mpwemu Yera yukw atazopfa, atarabona Kristo w’Umwami Imana." 
Luke2:27 Ajanwa na Mpwemu mu rusengero; abavyeyi bajanye uwo mwana Yesu ngo bamugenze nk’uk’ umugenzo w’ivyagezwe war’ uri," 
Luke2:28 aramwākira, aramukikira, ashima Imana," 
Luke2:29 ati Databuja, noneh’ urasezeye umusavyi wawe amahoro, Nk’uko wavuze:" 
Luke2:30 Kukw amaso yanje abonye agakiza kawe," 
Luke2:31 Ako wateguye mu maso y’amoko yose," 
Luke2:32 Kuba umuco wākira amahanga, No kuba ubgiza bg’abantu bawe b’Abisirayeli." 
Luke2:33 Se na nyina batangazwa n’ayo majambo avuzwe kuri we. 
Luke2:34 Simeyoni arabahezagira, abgira nyina Mariya, at’ Umve, uyu ashiriweho kugira ngo benshi mu Bisirayeli bagwe, benshi bavyuke, no kuzoba ikimenyetso kigawa," 
Luke2:35 kandi nawe inkota izogucumita mu mutima, ngw ivyiyumviro vy’imitima myinshi bize biserurwe." 
Luke2:36 Kandi hāriho Ana, uwavugishwa n’Imana, umukobga wa Fanuweli, wo mu muryango wa Asheri, yar’ umutāmakazi wa kera, yabanye n’umugabo wiwe imyaka ndwi, uhereye ku kurongorwa kwiwe," 
Luke2:37 kandi yamaze imyaka mirongumunani n’ine ar’ umupfakazi, ntiyava mu rusengero gusenga, yisonzesha yinginga, ku murango no mw ijoro." 
Luke2:38 Ako kanya aca araza, ashima Imana, avuga ivya Yesu, abibgira abāri barorereye ugucungurwa kw’i Yerusalemu bose." 
Luke2:39 Banonosoye vyose nk’ukw ivyagezwe n’Umwami Imana bivuga, basubira i Galilaya mu gisagara cabo i Nazareti." 
Luke2:40 Kand’ uno mwana arakura, agwiza inkomezi, yuzuzwa ubgenge, ubuntu bg’Imana bgari kuri we." 
Luke2:41 Kand’ uk’ umwaka utashe, abavyeyi biwe bāja i Yerusalemu mu misi mikuru ya Pasika." 
Luke2:42 Nukw amaze imyaka cumi n’ibiri avutse, baradūga, nk’uk’ umugenzo w’iyo misi mikuru war’ uri." 
Luke2:43 Banonosoye ivy’ iyo misi, barahindukira, uwo muhungu Yesu asigara i Yerusalemu, abavyeyi biwe ntibābimenya." 
Luke2:44 Ariko bībgiye yukw ari mw igugu ry’abo bagendanye, bagenda urugendo rw’umusi wose, maze bamurondera mu ncuti no mu bo bazinanyi:" 
Luke2:45 bamubuze basubira i Yerusalemu bamurondera. 
Luke2:46 Hashize imisi itatu bamubona mu rusengero, yicaye mu bigisha hagati, abumva, kand’ ababaza." 
Luke2:47 Abamwumvise bose batangazwa n’ubgenge bgiwe n’ivy’ abishura. 
Luke2:48 Bamubonye baratangara, nyina aramubaza, ati Mwananje, n’iki catumye utugirira urtyo? Urabona twe na so aho twakurondereye tubabaye." 
Luke2:49 Arababaza, ati N’iki cabateye kundondera? Ntimwari muzi yuko bikwiye ko mba kwa Data?" 
Luke2:50 Ntibāmenya iryo jambo ababgiye. 
Luke2:51 Amanukana na bo, aja i Nazareti, yama abumvira. Nyina abīka ayo majambo yose mu mutima wiwe." 
Luke2:52 Kandi Yesu agwiza ubgenge no gukura no gushimwa n’Imana n’abantu. 
Luke3:1 Mu mwaka ugira icumi na gatanu Kayisari Tiberiyo ari ku ngoma, Pontiyo Pilato ar’ icēgēra ciwe i Yudaya, Herode na we ar’ umwami w’i Galilaya, na Filipo mwene se ar’ umwami w’igihugu co muri Ituraya n’i Tirakoniti, na Lusaniya ar’ umwami w’i Abilene," 
Luke3:2 na Anasi na Kayafa ar’ abaherezi bakuru, mur’ uwo mwaka ijambo ry’Imana rishika kuri Yohana mwene Zakariya, ari mu bugaragwa." 
Luke3:3 Aja mu gihugu cose giherereye kuri Yorodani, yigisha abantu ukubatizwa kwo kwihana ngo bakūrwekw ivyaha:" 
Luke3:4 nk’uko vyanditswe mu gitabo c’amajambo y’uwavugishwa n’Imana Yesaya, ngw Ijwi ry’ūsemererera mu bugaragwa, Ati Ni mutegure inzira y’Uhoraho, Mugorore iz’ ibihamo ziwe." 
Luke3:5 Umwonga wose uzokwuzuzwa, N’umusozi wose n’akarambi bizoringanizwa, Ibigoramye bizogororoka, N’inzira z’ubukiru zizosenwa," 
Luke3:6 Maz’ abafise umubiri bose bazobona agakiza k’Imana. 
Luke3:7 Nukw abgira ishengero ryari rivuye i wabo rije kubatizwa na we, ati Mwa bana b’inzoka mwe, ni nde yababūriye ngo muhunge uburake buzoza?" 
Luke3:8 Nuko mwame imbuto zikwiranye n’ukwihana: kandi ntimutangure kwiyumvira mu mitima, muti Ko dufise Aburahamu, ni we sogokuruza. Ndababgira yukw aya mabuye Imana ishobora kuyavyuramw’ abana ba Aburahamu." 
Luke3:9 Arikw incabiti igenekerejwe ku bitsina vy’ibiti; nuko rero, igiti cose kitama ivyiza kiracibga, kigatererwa mu muriro." 
Luke3:10 Ishengero riramubaza, riti None tugire dute?" 
Luke3:11 Arabishura, at’ Ūfise amapfundo abiri, rimwe n’arihe ūtarifise, n’ūfise ivyo kurya n’agire artyo." 
Luke3:12 Kandi haza n’abatozakori kubatizwa, baramubaza, bati Mwigisha, tugire dute?" 
Luke3:13 Arabishura, ati Ntimugatoze abantu ibiruta ivyo mwagezwe." 
Luke3:14 N’abasoda baramubaza, bati Tweho tugire dute? Arabishura, ati Ntihakagire umuntu mutangisha impongano canke mwagiriza ibinyoma, kand’ ingero zanyu zibabumbe." 
Luke3:15 Kand’ abantu bāri barorereye ibizoba, bose bakabūranisha imitima ngo kumbure Yohana yoba Kristo." 
Luke3:16 Yohana ababarira bose, ati N’ukuri jeho ndababatirisha amazi, ariko hazoza ūndusha ubushobozi, ntibimbereye no gupfundurura utugozi tw’inkweto ziwe: uyo azobabatiza muri Mpwemu Yera no mu muriro." 
Luke3:17 Urutaro rwiwe ruri mu kuboko kwiwe, ngw akubure imbuga yiwe neza, yimburire ingano mu kigega ciwe, maz’ umuguruka awuturire mu muriro utazima." 
Luke3:18 Kand’ abarira abantu ubutumwa bgiza, abahanūrisha ibindi vyinshi;" 
Luke3:19 maz’ ahishutse umwami Herode ku vya Herodiya muka mwene se, no ku vy’ ibindi bibi vyose Herode yakoze," 
Luke3:20 kur’ ivyo vyose Herode agerekakw iki, yugaranira Yohana mw ibohero." 
Luke3:21 Nukw abantu bose babatijwe, na Yesu ahejeje kubatizwa, arikw arasenga, ijuru rirakinguruka," 
Luke3:22 Mpwemu Yera aramanuka amugwako, afise ishusho y’umubiri usa n’inuma; ijwi riva mw ijuru, riti Ni wewe Mwana wanje nkunda ukampimbara." 
Luke3:23 Aho Yesu yatangura kwigisha, yar’ amaze imyaka nka mirongwitatu avutse, kandi biyumvira ko yari mwene Yosefu, Yosefu mwene Heli," 
Luke3:24 Heli mwene Matati, Matati mwene Lewi, Lewi mwene Meluki, Meluki mwene Yanayi, Yanayi mwene Yosefu," 
Luke3:25 Yosefu mwene Matatiya, Matatiya mwene Amosi, Amosi mwene Nahumu, Nahumu mwene Esili, Esili mwene Nagayi," 
Luke3:26 Nagayi mwene Mati, Mati mwene Matatiya, Matatiya mwene Semeyini, Semeyini mwene Yoseki, Yoseki mwene Yoda, Yoda mwene Yohanani," 
Luke3:27 Yohanani mwene Resa, Resa mwene Zerubabeli, Zerubabeli mwene Shalutiyeli, Shalutiyeli mwene Neri," 
Luke3:28 Neri mwene Meluki, Meluki mwene Adi, Adi mwene Kosamu, Kosamu mwene Elumadamu, Elumadamu mwene Eri, Eri mwene Yesu," 
Luke3:29 Yesu mwene Eliyezeri, Eliyezeri mwene Yorimu, Yorimu mwene Matati, Matati mwene Lewi," 
Luke3:30 Lewi mwene Simeyoni, Simeyoni mwene Yuda, Yuda mwene Yosefu, Yosefu mwene Yonamu, Yonamu mwene Eliyakimu, Eliyakimu mwene Meleya," 
Luke3:31 Meleya mwene Mena, Mena mwene Matata, Matata mwene Natani, Natani mwene Dawidi," 
Luke3:32 Dawidi mwene Isayi, Isayi mwene Obedi, Obedi mwene Bowazi, Bowazi mwene Salumoni, Salumoni mwene Nahasoni," 
Luke3:33 Nahasoni mwene Aminadabu, Aminadabu mwene Aruni, Aruni mwene Hesironi, Hesironi mwene Peresi," 
Luke3:34 Peresi mwene Yuda, Yuda mwene Yakobo, Yakobo mwene Isaka, Isaka mwene Aburahamu, Aburahamu mwene Tera, Tera mwene Nahori," 
Luke3:35 Nahori mwene Serugi, Serugi mwene Reyu, Reyu mwene Pelegi, Pelegi mwene Eberi, Eberi mwene Shela, Shela mwene Kayinani," 
Luke3:36 Kayinani mwene Arupakisadi, Arupakisadi mwene Shemu, Shemu mwene Nowa," 
Luke3:37 Nowa mwene Lameki, Lameki mwene Metusela, Metusela mwene Henoki, Henoki mwene Yeredi, Yeredi mwene Mahalaleyeli," 
Luke3:38 Mahalaleyeli mwene Kayinani, Kayinani mwene Enoshi, Enoshi mwene Seti, Seti mwene Adamu, Adamu w’Imana." 
Luke4:1 Yesu yuzuzwa Mpwemu Yera, ava kuri Yorodani, agendagendeshwa mu bugaragwa na Mpwemu, amaray’ imisi mirongwine," 
Luke4:2 ageragezwa n’Umurwanizi. Kandi mur’ iyo misi nta co yariye; ishize arasonza. 
Luke4:3 Umurwanizi aramubgira, ati Ni waba ur’ Umwana w’Imana, bgira iri buye ricike umutsima." 
Luke4:4 Yesu aramwishura, ati Vyanditswe ng’ Umuntu ntatungwa n’umutsima gusa." 
Luke4:5 Aramudūgana, amwereka ubgami bgose bgo mw isi mu kanya gato." 
Luke4:6 Umurwanizi aramubgira, ati Ndaguha ubu bubasha bgose n’ubgiza bgabgo, kuko jewe nabuhawe, kandi mbuha uwo ngomba wese:" 
Luke4:7 nuko ni wampfukamira, ukansenga, ubgo bgose buraba ubgawe." 
Luke4:8 Yesu aramwishura, ati Vyanditswe ng’ Usenge Uhoraho, Imana yawe, abe ari yo usaba yonyene." 
Luke4:9 Amujana i Yerusalemu, amuhagarika mu gatwe k’urusengero, aramubgira, ati Ni waba ur’ Umwana w’Imana, ikororere hasi," 
Luke4:10 kuko vyanditswe, ngw Azokuragiza abamarayika biwe, ngo bakuzigame:" 
Luke4:11 kandi ngo Bazokuramira mu maboko yabo, Ngo kumbure ntutsitare kw ibuye." 
Luke4:12 Yesu aramwishura, ati Vyaravuzwe, ngo Ntukagerageze Uhoraho, Imana yawe." 
Luke4:13 Umurwanizi arangije ivy’ amugerageresha vyose, amara igihe amuretse." 
Luke4:14 Maze Yesu asubira i Galilaya, ari n’ubushobozi bga Mpwemu, inkuru yiwe ikwira mu gihugu cose kihakikije." 
Luke4:15 Yigishiriza mu masinagogi yabo, bose baramushima." 
Luke4:16 Aja i Nazareti, iyo yakuriye; ku musi w’isabato yinjira mw isinagogi, nk’uko yamenyereye, ava hasi ngw asome." 
Luke4:17 Bamuha igitabo c’uwavugishwa n’Imana Yesaya, arakizingurura, abona ahantu handitswe," 
Luke4:18 ngo Mpwemu w’Uhoraho ari kuri jewe, Ni co catumye andobanuza amavuta kugira ngo mbgire aboro ubutumwa bgiza: Yantumye kumenyesha abarindwa ko barekuwe, N’impumyi ko zihumūka, No kubohora abanywagutse imitima," 
Luke4:19 No kumenyesha abantu umwaka wo kwemererwamwo n’Uhoraho. 
Luke4:20 Azinga igitabo, agisubiza umusanzi w’inzu, aricara; abantu bose bāri mw isinagogi bamuhanga amaso." 
Luke4:21 Atangura kubabgira, at’ Ivyo vyanditswe birashitse uyu musi, nk’ukw amatwi yanyu yiyumviye." 
Luke4:22 Bose baramushima, batangazwa n’amajambo y’igikundiro avuye mu kanwa kiwe, bati Mbeg’ uyu si we mwene Yosefu?" 
Luke4:23 Arababgira, ati Ntimuzobura kuncirak’ uyu mugani, muti Muvūzi, wivūre. Ivyo twumvise vyose ko wakoreye i Kaperinawumu, ubikorere n’ino mu ntāra y’i wanyu." 
Luke4:24 Kand’ ati Ndababgire ukuri, Nta muntu avugishwa n’Imana yemerwa mu ntāra y’i wabo." 
Luke4:25 Ariko ndababgire ukuri, Hārih’ abapfakazi benshi mu Bisirayeli mu gihe ca Eliya, hamwe ijuru ryakingwa, imvura igatara imyaka itatu n’amezi atandatu, ikigoyi cinshi kigatera mu gihugu cose;" 
Luke4:26 yamara Eliya ntiyatumwa kuri n’umwe muri bo, arikw atumwa i Zarefati mu gihugu c’i Sidoni ku mugore w’umupfakazi." 
Luke4:27 Kandi hārih’ abanyamibembe benshi mu Bisirayeli mu gihe c’uwavugishwa n’Imana Elisa, ntihākizwa n’umwe muri bo, atari Namani Umusiriya." 
Luke4:28 Abo mw isinagogi bose bumvise ivyo barashungumirwa," 
Luke4:29 bava hasi, baramushika bamukūra mu gisagara cabo, bamujana ku manga y’umusozi wubatswekw igisagara cabo, ngo bamutembagarizeyo:" 
Luke4:30 arikw aca hagati muri bo, arīgīra." 
Luke4:31 Aramanuka aja i Kaperinawumu, igisagara c’i Galilaya: kand’ arikw arabigisha kw isabato," 
Luke4:32 batangazwa n’inyigisho ziwe, kukw ijambo ryiwe ryari n’ububasha." 
Luke4:33 Kandi mw isinagogi hār’ umuntu yinjiwemwo n’impwemu ya dayimoni ahumanye, asemerera n’ijwi rirenga," 
Luke4:34 ati Yō! Duhūriye hehe ga Yesu Munyanazareti? Uje kuduhonnya? Ndakuzi uw’ uri we, ur’ Uwera w’Imana." 
Luke4:35 Yesu aramuzibiza, ati Hora, muvemwo. Dayimoni amutūye hasi hagati yabo, amuvamwo, atagize ico amugira." 
Luke4:36 Bose baratangara, barabazanya, bat’ Iryo n’ijambo ki? N’ububasha n’ubushobozi agera impwemu zihumanye zigasohoka." 
Luke4:37 Inkuru yiwe ikwira hose mu ntāra ihakikije. 
Luke4:38 Ava hasi, arasohoka ava mw isinagogi, yinjira mu nzu kwa Simoni. Kandi inabukwe wa Simoni yar’ afashwe n’umururumbo ukomeye, baramumwingingira." 
Luke4:39 Amuhagarara i ruhande, akankamira umururumbo, urazima; avyuka uwo mwanya, arabazimana." 
Luke4:40 Kandi ku kirengazuba, abari bafise abarwaye bose barwaye indwara zitari zimwe barabamuzanira. Abarambikakw ibiganza umwe‐umwe, arabakiza." 
Luke4:41 Kandi n’abadayimoni bava muri benshi, basemerera, bat’ Ur’ Umwana w’Imana. Arabazibiza, ntiyabakundira ko bavuga, kuko bāri bazi yukw ari Kristo." 
Luke4:42 Kand’ ijoro rikeye, arasohoka, aja mu gahinga: ishengero riramurondera, bashika ah’ ari, bageza kumubuza ngo ntave muri bo." 
Luke4:43 Maz’ arababgira, ati Nkwiye kuvuga ubutumwa bgiza bg’ubgami bg’Imana no mu bindi bisagara, kukw ari co natumwe." 
Luke4:44 Nukw avugira ijambo ry’Imana mu masinagogi y’i Galilaya. 
Luke5:1 Nukw ishengero ririko riramubanda ryumva ijambo ry’Imana, yar’ ahagaze ku musenyi w’ikiyaga c’i Genesareti." 
Luke5:2 Abona amato abiri aziritswe ku nkombe y’ikiyaga, arikw abarovyi bāri bayavuyemwo, boza insenga." 
Luke5:3 Atambukira mu bgato bumwe, bgar’ ubga Simoni, aramusaba ngw abgigizeyo buve ku nkombe gatoya: aricara, yigisha ishengero, ari mu bgato." 
Luke5:4 Ahejeje kuvuga, abarira Simoni, at’ Igira mw idamba, muterere insenga zanyu murobe." 
Luke5:5 Simoni aramwishura, at’ Erega Mwigisha, twakesheje ijoro ryose twātamye, nta co twafashe: ariko kubg’ ijambo ryawe ndaterera insenga." 
Luke5:6 Babigize, baroba ifi nyinshi cane, insenga zabo zigomba gucika." 
Luke5:7 Bākura abagenzi babo bāri mu bundi bgato, ngo baze babafashe: baraza, buzuza amato yompi, agomba kudobera." 
Luke5:8 Ariko Simoni Petero abibonye yikubita imbere y’amavi ya Yesu, ati Va aho ndi, Mugenzi, kuko nd’ umunyavyaha." 
Luke5:9 Kukw atangaye, n’abāri kumwe na we bose, babonye ifi barovye." 
Luke5:10 Na Yakobo na Yohana bene Zebedayo na bo baratangara, bari bafatanije na Simoni. Yesu abgira Simoni, ati Nta co utinya, uhereye none uzoroba abantu." 
Luke5:11 Bahejeje gushikana amato yabo ku nkombe, basiga vyose, baramukurikira." 
Luke5:12 Ikindi gihe ari mu gisagara kimwe muri vyo, haza umuntu ajejeta imibembe: abonye Yesu yikubita hasi yubamye, aramwinginga, ati Mugenzi, ukunze, woshobora kumpumanura." 
Luke5:13 Aramvura ukuboko, amukorako, ati Ndakunze, humanuka. Imibembe ica imuvako." 
Luke5:14 Aramwihanikiriza, ngo ntagire umuntu abibarira, at’ Ariko genda, wiyereke umuherezi, utange ivy’ uguhumanurwa kwawe, nk’uko Mose yabgirije, bibe ikimenyetso kibabere icabona." 
Luke5:15 Arikw inkuru yiwe irushiriza gukwira, ishengero ryinshi rikoranira kumwumva no gukizwa indwara zabo." 
Luke5:16 Ariko we yigunga mu bugaragwa, asenga." 
Luke5:17 Ku musi umwe muri yo yarigisha. Abafarisayo n’abigisha ivyagezwe bāri bicayeho, bavuye mu mihana yose y’i Galilaya n’i Yudaya n’i Yerusalemu; kand’ ubushobozi bg’Umwami Imana bgari muri we bgo gukiza indwara." 
Luke5:18 Maze haza abagabo bazanye ikimuga, bagiteruye mu nderuzo, barondera ingene bacinjiza ngo bagishire imbere yiwe." 
Luke5:19 Babuze aho bocinjiriza kubg’ ishengero, būrira hejuru ku nzu, bagicisha mu mategura ayisakaye, bacururutsa mu nderuzo hagati y’abantu imbere ya Yesu." 
Luke5:20 Abonye ukwizera kwabo, aravuga, at’ Ewe muntu, ivyaha vyawe urabihariwe." 
Luke5:21 Abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe n’Abafarisayo batangura kwibūranya, bat’ Uyo ni nde arogose? Ni nde ashobora guharira ivyaha atar’ Imana yonyene?" 
Luke5:22 Maze Yesu, amenye ivyo bibūranya, arababaza, ati Mwibūranya ibiki mu mitima yanyu?" 
Luke5:23 Icoroshe n’ikihe, n’ukuvuga nt’ Uhariwe ivyaha vyawe; canke n’ukuvuga nti Vyuka ugende?" 
Luke5:24 Ariko kugira ngo mumenye k’Umwana w’umuntu afise ububasha mw isi bgo guharira ivyaha — abgira ico kimuga, ati Ndakubariye, nti Vyuka, wikorere inderuzo yawe, utahe." 
Luke5:25 Aca avyuka imbere yabo, yikorera inderuzo yar’ aryamyemwo, arataha, ahimbaza Imana." 
Luke5:26 Bose barumirwa cane, bahimbaza Imana, baterwa n’ubgoba bginshi, bat’ Uyu musi tubonye ibitangaza." 
Luke5:27 Ivyo bishize, arasohoka, abona umutozakori yitwa Lewi, yicaye aho yatoreza ikibuguro, aramubarira, ati Nkurikira." 
Luke5:28 Asiga vyose, ava hasi, aramukurikira." 
Luke5:29 Lewi amurondereza izimano ryinshi mu nzu yiwe: kandi hār’ abantu benshi b’abatozakori n’abandi bicaranye na bo basangira. 
Luke5:30 Abafarisayo n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe bafatanye na bo bidodombera abigishwa ba Yesu, bati N’iki gitumye musangira n’abatozakori n’abanyavyaha?" 
Luke5:31 Yesu arabishura, at’ Abakomeye nta co bagombera umuvūzi, atar’ abarwaye." 
Luke5:32 Sinaje guhamagara abagororotsi, ariko naje guhamagara abanyavyaha ngo bihane." 
Luke5:33 Na bo baramubgira, bat’ Abigishwa ba Yohana barisonzesha kenshi bagasenga, n’ab’ Abafarisayo n’uko, arikw abawe barīrīra, barīnywera." 
Luke5:34 Yesu arababaza, ati Mbega mwoshobora mute kugera abātowe ngo bisonzeshe, bakiri kumwe n’umukwe?" 
Luke5:35 Ariko har’ imisi izoza; kand’ umukwe ni yabakūrwamwo, bazoca bisonzesha mur’ iyo misi." 
Luke5:36 Kand’ abacira umugani, ati Nta wotabura ikiremo ku mpuzu nsha, ngw acomeke ku mpuzu y’umushire: uwogira artyo yoba atabuye nsha, kand’ ikiremo atabuye kuri nsha nticomatana n’iy’ umushire." 
Luke5:37 Kandi nta wotara umutobe wa vino mu mikuza y’insato ibōmbōtse; kuko vino yoturitsa iyo mikuza, igashirira hasi, imikuza igapfa." 
Luke5:38 Arikw igikwiye n’ugutara umutobe wa vino mu mikuza misha. 
Luke5:39 Kandi nta muntu yanyoye vino ihiye yogomba umutobe: kukw avuga, at’ Īhiye ni yo nziza." 
Luke6:1 Kw isabato agenda aca mu mirima y’ingano; abigishwa biwe bamyoza ingano, barazihekenya, bazivunze mu minwe." 
Luke6:2 Bamwe mu Bafarisayo barababaza, bati N’iki gitumye mukora ikizira gukorwa kw isabato?" 
Luke6:3 Yesu na we arababaza, ati Nta ho murasoma iki, ico Dawidi yakoze, aho yar’ ashonje, asonzanye n’abari kumwe na we;" 
Luke6:4 ingene yinjiye mu nzu y’Imana, akābīra imitsima y’ibiterekērwa, akayirya, akayihako n’abari kumwe na we, ar’ umuziro kurībga, ukūye abaherezi bonyene?" 
Luke6:5 Kand’ arababgira, at’ Umwana w’umuntu n’Umwami w’isabato." 
Luke6:6 Ku yindi sabato yinjira mw isinagogi, arigisha: kandi hār’ umuntu anyunyutse ukuboko kw’i buryo." 
Luke6:7 Abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe bo n’Abafarisayo baramugenza ngo barābe kw akiza kw isabato, ngo baronke ingene bomurega." 
Luke6:8 Na we amenya ivyo biyumvira; abarira uwo muntu anyunyutse ukuboko, ati Va hasi, uhagarare hagati. Ava hasi, arahagarara." 
Luke6:9 Yesu arababgira, ati Ndababaze: mbeg’ ivyemerwa n’ugukora ivyiza kw isabato, canke n’ugukora ibibi; gukiza umuntu, canke kumwica?" 
Luke6:10 Abēraguzamw’ amaso bose, aramubarira, ati Ramvura ukuboko kwawe. Arabigira, ukuboko kwiwe kurakira." 
Luke6:11 Ariko bo birabasaza rwose, baja inama y’ico bogira Yesu." 
Luke6:12 Mur’ iyo misi avayo, aja ku musozi gusenga: akesha ijoro asenga Imana." 
Luke6:13 Ijoro rikeye, ahamagara abigishwa biwe, atoranyamw’ icumi na babiri, abita intumwa;" 
Luke6:14 Simoni, uwo yise Petero, na Andereya mwene nyina, na Yakobo, na Yohana, na Filipo, na Barutolomayo," 
Luke6:15 na Matayo, na Toma, na Yakobo mwene Alufayo, na Simoni yitwa Zelote," 
Luke6:16 na Yuda mwene Yakobo, na Yuda Isikaryota yabaye umuguranyi." 
Luke6:17 Amanukana na bo, ahagarara ahateze, kandi hārih’ ishengero ryinshi ry’abigishwa biwe, n’ishengero ryinshi ry’abantu bavuye i Yudaya hose n’i Yerusalemu no mu gihugu co muri Tiro n’i Sidoni gihereranye n’ikiyaga kinini, baje kumwumva no gukizwa indwara zabo." 
Luke6:18 Kandi n’abababazwa n’impwemu zihumanye barakizwa. 
Luke6:19 Kand’ ishengero ryose rigerageza kumukorako, kuk’ ubushobozi bgāmuvamwo bukabakiza bose." 
Luke6:20 Yunamurira abigishwa biwe amaso, arababgira, ati Hahirwa mwebge aboro; kuk’ ubgami bg’Imana ar’ ubganyu." 
Luke6:21 Hahirwa mwebge mushonje none, kuko muzohāzwa. Hahirwa mwebge murira none, kuko muzotwenga." 
Luke6:22 Muzoba muhiriwe abantu ni babanka bakabaca, bakabatuka, bakanegura izina ryanyu nk’ah’ ari ribi, babahōye Umwana w’umuntu." 
Luke6:23 Uwo musi muze munezerwe mwitere hejuru, kukw impēra yanyu ari nyinshi mw ijuru: kukw ari ko ba sekuruza babo bāgize abāvugishwa n’Imana." 
Luke6:24 Ariko muzobona ibara, mwebge abatunzi; kuko muhejeje gutunganirwa." 
Luke6:25 Muzobona ibara, mwebge muhāze none; kuko muzosonza. Muzobona ibara, mwebge mutwenga none; kuko muzoboroga murira." 
Luke6:26 Muzobona ibara, ah’abantu bose bazobashemagiza; kukw ari ko ba sekuruza babo bāshemagije abīgira abavugishwa n’Imana." 
Luke6:27 Ariko mwebge mwumva ndababgire: Mukunde abansi banyu, mugirire neza ababanka," 
Luke6:28 muhezagire ababavuma, musabire ababagirira nabi." 
Luke6:29 Ūgukubise mu musaya, umuhindukirize n’uwundi; ūkwaka umutamana, ntumwime n’ipfundo." 
Luke6:30 Ūgusaba wese umuhe, ūnyaga ivyawe ntuz’ ubimwake ukundi." 
Luke6:31 Kand’ uko mugomba kw abantu babagirira, mube ari ko mubagirira namwe." 
Luke6:32 Kandi ni mwakunda ababakunda, muzoshimwa iki? Kukw abanyavyaha na bo bagira bartyo." 
Luke6:33 Kandi ni mwagirira neza ababagirira neza, muzoshimwa iki? Kukw abanyavyaha na bo bagira bartyo." 
Luke6:34 Kandi ni mwagurana abo muziga ko bazobaguranura, muzoshimwa iki? Abanyavyaha na bo bagurana abandi banyavyaha, ngo baguranurwe nk’ivyabo." 
Luke6:35 Ariko mukunde abansi banyu, mubagirire neza, mugurane abantu, mutaziga ko muzoguranurwa; kand’ impēra zanyu zizoba nyinshi, namwe muzoba abana b’Īsumba vyose; kukw igirira neza intashima n’ababi." 
Luke6:36 Mugire imbabazi, nk’uko So agira imbabazi." 
Luke6:37 Kandi ntimugahinyurire mu mitima yanyu, namwe mukazohinyurwa; kandi ntimugatsindishe, namwe mukazotsindishwa; mubohore, namwe muzobohorwa; mutange, namwe muzohabga;" 
Luke6:38 ingero nziza, itsindagiye, inyingishe, isēsekaye, ni yo bazobaha mu co muteze. Kukw ingero mugeramwo ari yo muzosubirizwamwo namwe." 
Luke6:39 Kand’ abacira umugani, ati Mbeg’ impumyi yoshobora kujana iyindi mpumyi? Zompi ntizogwa mu cobo?" 
Luke6:40 Umwigishwa ntaruta umwigisha wiwe, arik’ umwigishwa wese arangije azoba nk’umwigisha wiwe." 
Luke6:41 Urābira iki akabango kari mu jisho rya mugenzawe, inkingi iri mu jisho ryawe ntuyītegereze?" 
Luke6:42 Woshobora ute kubgira mugenzawe, uti Zana mugenzi ngutosore akabango kari mu jisho ryawe; nawe ubgawe nturābe inkingi iri mu jisho ryawe? Wa ndyarya we, banza witosore inkingi iri mu jisho ryawe, uheze ubone neza gutosora akabango kari mu jisho rya mugenzawe." 
Luke6:43 Kukw ata giti ciza cama ibibi, kandi nta giti kibi cama ivyiza." 
Luke6:44 Igiti cose kimenyekanira ku vyo camye: nta bokwamura insukoni ku munyinya, cank’ inzabibu ku mukēre." 
Luke6:45 Umunyangeso nziza akūra ivyiza mw itunga ryiza ryo mu mutima wiwe, n’umunyangeso mbi akūra ibibi mw itunga ribi: ibibōgabōga mu mutima ni vyo akanwa kiwe kavuga." 
Luke6:46 Kandi munyitira iki Mwami, Mwami; ntimukore ivyo mvuga?" 
Luke6:47 Umuntu wese aza aho ndi, akumva amajambo yanje, akayakora, ndabereka ukw asa." 
Luke6:48 Asa n’umuntu yubaka inzu, yimvye hasi cane, akubaka itanguriro ku rutare: maz’ umugezi wuzuye usūrira kur’ iyo nzu, ntiwashobora kuyinyiganyiza, kuko yubatswe neza." 
Luke6:49 Arik’ uwumva, ntabikore, asa n’umuntu yubatse inzu kw ivu, atimvye itanguriro: maz’ umugezi uyisūrirako, ica irasenyuka, uguhomvoka kw’iyo nzu kwabaye ugukomeye." 
Luke7:1 Kand’ ahereje ayo majambo yiwe yose mu matwi y’abantu, aja i Kaperinawumu." 
Luke7:2 Hāriy’ umugabisha w’abasoda ijana, umushumba wiwe akunda cane yar’ arwaye, ari ku mpfiro." 
Luke7:3 Yumvise inkuru ya Yesu, amutumakw abashingantahe b’Abayuda kumwinginga, ngw aze gukiza umushumba wiwe." 
Luke7:4 Na bo bashitse aho Yesu ari, baramwinginga cane, bati Birabereye k’umugirira urtyo," 
Luke7:5 kukw akunda ubgoko bgacu, n’isinagogi yacu ni we yayitwubakiye." 
Luke7:6 Yesu ajana na bo. Atakiri kure y’inzu, wa mugabisha amutumakw incuti ziwe, ati Mugenzi, nturinde kwigora, kuko bitambereye ko winjira mu nzu yanje:" 
Luke7:7 ni co catumye niyumvira ko bitambereye ko noza ah’ uri: ariko vuga ijambo gusa, uwo muhungu arakira." 
Luke7:8 Kuko nanje nd’umuntu agendera musi y’abanganza, mfise abasoda ntwara: iyo mbariye umwe nti Genda, aragenda; n’uwundi nti Ngwino, akaza; nabarira umushumba wanje nti Kora iki, akagikora." 
Luke7:9 Yesu yumvise ivyo, aramutangarira, ahindukirira ishengero rimukurikiye, ati Ndababgire, Sinaribgabone ukwizera kungana gurtyo no mu Bisirayeli." 
Luke7:10 Abātumwe basubiye mu nzu, basanga wa mushumba akomeye." 
Luke7:11 Hashize igihe gitoya, aja mu gisagara citwa Nayini: abigishwa biwe n’ishengero ryinshi bajana na we." 
Luke7:12 Ashitse hafi y’irembo ry’igisagara, hasokoroka abajanye umuvyimba kuwuhamba, ariko yar’ ikinege, kandi nyina yar’ umupfakazi: abantu benshi bo mur’ ico gisagara bari kumwe na we." 
Luke7:13 Umwami Yesu amubonye amutera akagongwe, aramubarira, ati Nta co urira." 
Luke7:14 Yigira hafi y’ikigagara, agikorako, abahamvyi barahagarara. Aravuga, ati Muhungu, ndakubariye nti Vyuka." 
Luke7:15 Uwari yapfuye aravyuka, aricara, atangura kuvuga; Yesu amuha nyina." 
Luke7:16 Bose baterwa n’ubgoba, bahimbaza Imana, bat’ Ūvugishwa n’Imana ahambaye aserutse muri twebge; kandi bat’ Imana igendeye abantu bayo." 
Luke7:17 Iyo nkuru yiwe ikwira i Yudaya hose no mu gihugu cose gihereranye na ho. 
Luke7:18 Yohana abigishwa biwe bamudondera ivyo vyose. 
Luke7:19 Yohana ahamagara babiri mu bigishwa biwe, abatuma ku Mwami Yesu, ati Muti Mbeg’ uri wa wundi akwiye kuza, canke twitege uwundi?" 
Luke7:20 Abo bagabo bamushikiriye, baramubgira, bati Yohana Umubatizi yakudutumyeko, ngo Mbeg’ uri wa wundi akwiye kuza, canke twitege uwundi?" 
Luke7:21 Mur’ ako kanya akiza benshi indwara n’ivyago n’impwemu mbi; n’impumyi nyinshi arazihumūra. 
Luke7:22 Maz’ arabishura, ati Ni mugende, mubarire Yohana ivyo mubonye n’ivyo mwumvise. Impumyi zirahumūka, abacumbagira bagenda neza, abanyamibembe barakizwa, ibipfamatwi birumva, abāpfuye barazurwa, aboro barabgirwa ubutumwa bgiza." 
Luke7:23 Kandi hahirwa uwo ivyanje bitazotsitaza. 
Luke7:24 Abatumwa ba Yohana bagiye, atangura kubgira ishengero ivya Yohana, ati Mwagiye mu bugaragwa kurāba iki? Mbega n’irenga rihungabanywa n’umuyaga?" 
Luke7:25 Ariko mwagiye kurāba iki? Mbega n’umuntu yambaye impuzu ziremvye? Ereg’ abambara impuzu zishajije n’abinibanibira baba mu ngo z’abami. 
Luke7:26 Ariko mwajanywe no kurāba iki? Umuntu avugishwa n’Imana? Ego me ni co; kandi ndababgire, Aruta ūvugishwa n’Imana cane." 
Luke7:27 Uyo ni we yanditswe, ng’ Umve, ngira ntume integuza yanje imbere y’amaso yawe, Ikuroranirize inzira imbere yawe." 
Luke7:28 Ndababgire, Mu bāvyawe n’abagore nta wuruta Yohana: arik’ umutoya mu bgami bg’Imana aramuruta." 
Luke7:29 Kand’ abantu bose n’abatozakori bumvise Yohana bemeye ukugororoka kw’ Imana, kuko bābatijwe na Yohana:" 
Luke7:30 arikw Abafarisayo n’abigisha ivyagezwe bībujije inama z’Imana, kuko batābatijwe na we." 
Luke7:31 Nukw abantu b’iki gihe ndabagereranya n’iki, kandi basa n’iki?" 
Luke7:32 Basa n’abana bicaye mu kaguriro bahamagarana, bati Twavugije imyironge, ntimwahamiriza; twakomye induru, ntimwarira." 
Luke7:33 Yohana Umubatizi yaje atarya umutsima, atanywa vino, mugira mut’ Ahagazweko na dayimoni." 
Luke7:34 Umwana w’umuntu yaje arya, anywa, mugira muti Nguyu umukunzi w’inda n’umunoho wa vino, incuti y’abatozakori n’abanyavyaha." 
Luke7:35 Kand’ ubgenge burangwa ko bugororotse n’abana babgo bose. 
Luke7:36 Maz’ umwe mu Bafarisayo aramuhamagara ngw amuzimane. Yinjira mu nzu y’uwo Mufarisayo, aricara ngw arye." 
Luke7:37 Umugore wo mur’ ico gisagara, yar’ umunyavyaha, amenye yukw arīra mu nzu y’uwo Mufarisayo, azana ikebano ry’amavuta atāmirana," 
Luke7:38 ahagarara inyuma yiwe, hafi y’ibirenge vyiwe, arira, atangura kumutonyangiriza amosozi ku birenge, abihanaguza umushatsi wiwe, arabisomagura, abisīga ya mavuta." 
Luke7:39 Wa Mufarisayo yamuhamagaye abibonye, aribgira, at’ Uyu muntu iy’aba ūvugishwa n’Imana, yari kumenya uyu mugore amukozeko, ukw ari kand’ ukw asa, kw ar’ umunyavyaha." 
Luke7:40 Yesu aramubgira, ati Simoni, mfise ico ngomba kukubgira. Aramwishura, ati Mbarira, Mwigisha." 
Luke7:41 Aramubgira, ati Hābaye umuntu yagurāna, yar’ afise abari mu mwenda wiwe babiri. Umwe yar’ amufitiye idenariyo amajana atanu, uwundi mirongwitanu." 
Luke7:42 Maze badafise ico kumwishura, azibahebera bompi. Mbeg’ ūzorushiriza kumukunda n’uwuhe?" 
Luke7:43 Simoni aramwishura, ati Ngira ngo n’uwo yahebeye nyinshi. Na we aramubgira, at’ Uvuze ukuri." 
Luke7:44 Ahindukiriye wa mugore, abgira Simoni, at’ Urabona uyu mugore? Ninjiye mu nzu yawe, ntiwampa amazi yo kwoga ibirenge: arik’ uyu antonyangirije amosozi ku birenge, abihanaguza umushatsi wiwe." 
Luke7:45 Ntiwansomye; arik’ uyu uhereye aho ninjiriye ntiyasizeho kunsomagura ibirenge. 
Luke7:46 Ntiwansutse amavuta ku mutwe: arik’ uyu ansīze amavuta atāmirana ku birenge. 
Luke7:47 Iki ni co gitumye nkubgira yukw ahariwe vya vyaha vyiwe vyinshi; kuko yagize urukundo rwinshi: arik’ ūhariwe bike agira urukundo ruke. 
Luke7:48 Abgira wa mugore, at’ Urahariwe ivyaha vyawe." 
Luke7:49 Maz’ abasangira na we batangura kwibaza, bat’ Uyo ni nde, kw aharira n’ivyaha?" 
Luke7:50 Abgira wa mugore, at’ Ukwizera kwawe kuragukijije, genda amahoro." 
Luke8:1 Hashize igihe gitoya, agendagenda mu bisagara no mu mihana, ababgira ijambo ry’Imana, avuga ubutumwa bgiza bg’ubgami bgayo; bamwe cumi na babiri bajana na we," 
Luke8:2 n’abagore bamwe bākijijwe impwemu mbi n’indwara, Mariya ari we Magadalene, abadayimoni ndwi bāri baramuvuyemwo," 
Luke8:3 na Yowana muka Kuza, umubgiriza wa Herode, na Susana, n’abandi bagore benshi, bābafashisha ivyabo." 
Luke8:4 Ishengero ryinshi rirakorana, kand’ abāvuye mu bisagara vyose baza kuri we, abacira umugani," 
Luke8:5 at’ Umubivyi yasohoye imbuto ziwe; akibiba, zimwe zigwa i ruhande y’inzira, barazikandagira, inyoni zo mu kirēre zirazinobagura." 
Luke8:6 Izindi zigwa ku rutare, zihejeje kumera zirūma, kuko zibuze ahabomvye." 
Luke8:7 Izindi zigwa mu mahwa hagati, amahwa amerana na zo, arazinyoha." 
Luke8:8 Izindi zigwa mw ivu ryiza, ziramera, zihunda impeke, imwe ijana, iyindi ijana, birtyo birtyo. Avuze ivyo, avuga n’ijwi rirenga, at’ Ūri n’amatwi yumva ni yumve." 
Luke8:9 Maz’ abigishwa biwe bamubaza uwo mugani, uw’ ari wo." 
Luke8:10 Arababgira, ati Mwebge mwāhawe kumenya amabanga y’ubgami bg’Imana: arikw abasigaye babibarirwa mu migani; ngo barābe, yamara ntibavyitegereze; bumve, yamara ntibabitahure." 
Luke8:11 Umugani n’uyu. Imbuto n’ijambo ry’Imana. 
Luke8:12 Abo i ruhande y’inzira n’abaryumvise, maz’ Umurwanizi yaza, agakūra iryo jambo mu mitima yabo, kugira ngo ntibizere ngo bakizwe." 
Luke8:13 Abo ku rutare n’aba: iyo bumvise iryo jambo, baryākīrana umunezero, ariko ntibagira imizi, bizera akanya gato, maze mu gihe c’igeragezwa bakarireka." 
Luke8:14 Izaguye mu mahwa n’abaryumvise, maze bariko barīgīra umwitwaririko wo mur’ ubu bugingo, bo n’ubutunzi n’ibihimbaro vyo muri bgo, bikabanyoha, ntibame imbuto nziza." 
Luke8:15 Izo mw ivu ryiza n’abumvise iryo jambo bakarigumya mu mitima myiza itunganye, bakāmishwa imbuto n’ukwihangana." 
Luke8:16 Kandi nta wodomeka itara, ngw aryubikekw ikintu, canke ngw arishire mu rutara, arikw arishira ku gitereko caryo, ngw abinjira basange habona." 
Luke8:17 Kukw ata canyegejwe kitazozanwa ahabona, cank’ icagizwe ibanga kitazomenyekana kikaja ahabona." 
Luke8:18 Mwiyubare uburyo mwumva: kuk’ ūfise azohabga, kand’ ūdafise azokwakwa n’ico yiyumvira kw afise." 
Luke8:19 Maze nyina na bene nyina baza ah’ ari, ntibāshobora kumushikīra kubg’ ishengero." 
Luke8:20 Baramubgira, bat’ Umuvyeyi wawe na barumuna bawe bahagaze hanze bagomba kubonana nawe." 
Luke8:21 Na we arabishura, ati Mama na bene mama n’aba bumva ijambo ry’Imana bakarikora." 
Luke8:22 Ku musi umwe mur’ iyo atambukira mu bgato, bo n’abigishwa biwe, arababgira, ati Tujabuke, tuje hakurya y’ikiyaga. Baterera ubgato, bava ku nkombe." 
Luke8:23 Bariko baragenda, arasinzira; hamanuka inkūbi y’umuyaga mu kiyaga, ubgato bgariko buruzura amazi, bari mw irinde." 
Luke8:24 Baraza, baramukangura, bati Mwigisha, Mwigisha, turapfuye! Ari angura, azibiza ingunza n’ugusūriranya kw’amazi: birahora, haba agahwekere." 
Luke8:25 Arababaza, ati Mbeg’ ukwizera kwanyu kuri hehe? Baratinya baratangara, barabazanya, bati Mbeg’ uyu n’umuntu ki, kw abarira n’umuyaga n’amazi bikamwumvira?" 
Luke8:26 Bafata hakurya mu gihugu c’Abageraseni, kirābana n’i Galilaya." 
Luke8:27 Ashitse i musozi, umuntu yavuye mu gisagara, yinjiwemwo n’abadayimoni, aramusanganira. Yar’ amaze imisi myinshi ata mpuzu acambara; nta nzu yabamwo, yaba mu masenga y’imva." 
Luke8:28 Abonye Yesu arasemerera, amwikubita imbere, avuga n’ijwi rirenga, ati Duhūriye hehe ga Yesu, Mwana w’Imana isumba vyose? Ndakwinginze, ntumbabaze agashinyaguro." 
Luke8:29 Kuko yar’ abariye iyo mpwemu ihumanye kuva mur’ uwo muntu. Yahora imutera kenshi, kandi bāmubohesha iminyororo ku maboko no ku maguru, bakamurinda, agacagagura ibimuboshe, dayimoni akamukubebera mu bugaragwa." 
Luke8:30 Yesu aramubaza, ati Witwa nde? Aramwishura, ati Ndi Gitero. Kukw abadayimoni benshi bāri baramwinjiyemwo."
