Luke8:31 Baramwinginga ngo ntababarire kuja i kuzimu. 
Luke8:32 Kandi hār’ umukuku w’ingurube nyinshi zirisha kur’ uwo musozi; baramwinginga ngw abemerere kuzinjiramwo: arabemerera. 
Luke8:33 Abadayimoni basokoroka mur’ uno muntu, binjira muri nya ngurube, umukuku wirukira ku gatembge, zīsuka mu kiyaga, amazi araziniga." 
Luke8:34 Abāziragira babibonye barahunga, babivuga mu gisagara no mu misozi." 
Luke8:35 Na bo bavayo, baza kurāba ivyābaye, bashika aho Yesu ari, basanga wa muntu yavuwemwo n’abadayimoni, yicaye i ruhande y’ibirenge vya Yesu, yambaye, ubgenge bgāgarutse; baratinya." 
Luke8:36 Abābibonye babīgānira ingen’ uwari yinjiwemwo n’abadayimoni yakijijwe. 
Luke8:37 Abantu bose bo mu gihugu c’Abageraseni gikikije aho baramwinginga ngw ave i wabo, kuko bāri batewe n’ubgoba bginshi. Atambukira mu bgato, asubira inyuma." 
Luke8:38 Ariko wa muntu avuwemwo n’abadayimoni aramwinginga ngw agume kuri we. Arikw aramusezera," 
Luke8:39 ati Subira i muhira i wawe, ubadondere ivyo Imana igukoreye vyose. Aragenda, akwiza mu gisagara cose ivyo Yesu yamukoreye vyose." 
Luke8:40 Yesu agarutse, ishengero riramusanganira, kuko bose bāri bamurorereye." 
Luke8:41 Maze haza umuntu yitwa Yayiro, umukuru w’isinagogi: yitembagaza imbere y’ibirenge vya Yesu, aramwinginga ngw aze i muhira i we," 
Luke8:42 kuko yar’ afise umukobga w’ikinege, yar’ amaze imyaka nka cumi n’ibiri avutse, kandi yarikw arahwera. Arikw aragenda, ishengero riramubānda." 
Luke8:43 Umugore arwaye ubutinyanka, yar’ abimaranye imyaka cumi n’ibiri, yamariye utwiwe twose ku bavūzi adutangamw’ ingemu, ntihāgira ūshobora kumukiza," 
Luke8:44 amuturuka inyuma, akora ku buyonga bg’impuzu yiwe, ako kanya umugende w’amaraso urakama." 
Luke8:45 Yesu arabaza, ati Ni nde ankozeko? Bose bahakanye, Petero n’abāri kumwe na we baramwishura, bat’ Erega Mwigisha, n’ishengero rigutaye hagati rikubānda." 
Luke8:46 Yesu aramubgira, ati Har’ ūnkozeko, kuko numvise ubushobozi bumvuyemwo." 
Luke8:47 Wa mugore abonye yukw atayoberanye, aza ahinda agashitsi, amwikubita imbere, amubgirira mu maso y’abantu bose icatumye amukorako, n’ukw akize uwo mwanya." 
Luke8:48 Aramubgira, ati Mwana wanje, ukwizera kwawe kuragukijije, genda amahoro." 
Luke8:49 Akivuga, haza umuntu avuye kwa wa mukuru w’isinagogi, ati Wa mwana wawe aracikanye, ureke kugora umwigisha." 
Luke8:50 Maze Yesu avyumvise aramubgira, ati Ntutinye, wizere gusa, arakira." 
Luke8:51 Ashitse ku nzu, ntiyagira uwundi muntu akundira kwinjirana na we, atari Petero na Yohana na Yakobo, na se wa nya mukobga na nyina." 
Luke8:52 Asanga bamuririra bose, bīshishitira. Arababarira, ati Nta co murira, ntahwereye, arikw arasinziriye." 
Luke8:53 Baramutwenga bamushinyagurira, kuko bari bazi ko yapfuye." 
Luke8:54 Amufata ukuboko, avuga n’ijwi rirenga, ati Mukobga, vyuka." 
Luke8:55 Ubugingo bgiwe buragaruka, aca ava hasi uwo mwanya; Yesu ababarira ngo bamugaburire." 
Luke8:56 Abavyeyi biwe baratangara, arikw arabīhanikiriza ngo ntihagire umuntu n’umwe babgira ibibāye." 
Luke9:1 Akoranya bamwe cumi na babiri, abaha ubushobozi n’ububasha ku badayimoni bose no gukiza indwara." 
Luke9:2 Abatuma kubarira abantu ivy’ ubgami bg’Imana, no gukiza abarwaye:" 
Luke9:3 arababarira, ati Ntimugire ico mujana ku nzira, ar’inkoni cank’ isaho, cank’ impamba, cank’ amahera: kandi ntimugire amapfundo abiri." 
Luke9:4 Kand’ inzu yose muzokwinjiramwo, abe ari yo mugumamwo, kugeza aho muzovira aho hantu." 
Luke9:5 Abazokwanka bose kubākīra, mukiva mur’ ico gisagara, muze mukunkumure umukungugu wo mu birenge vyanyu, kibe ikimenyetso kibabere icabona." 
Luke9:6 Baragenda, bagendagenda mu mihana, bavuga ubutumwa bgiza, bakiriza abarwaye hose." 
Luke9:7 Maz’ umwami Herode, yumvise ivyābaye vyose, arazazanirwa, kuko bamwe bāvuga, bati Yohana yazutse mu bapfuye;" 
Luke9:8 abandi bati Ni Eliya yiseruye; abandi bati N’umwe mu bāvugishwa n’Imana ba kera yazutse. 
Luke9:9 Herode aravuga, ati Yohana ni jewe namwiciriye izosi; mbeg’ uwo ni nde, numvakw ibimeze birtyo? Arondera uko yomubona." 
Luke9:10 Za ntumwa zigarutse zidondera Yesu ivyo zākoze vyose. Arabajana, abīhererana mu gisagara citwa Betsayida." 
Luke9:11 Maz’ ishengero ribimenye riramukurikira: arabākīra, ababgira ivy’ ubgami bg’Imana, kand’ abāgomba kuvūrwa arabakiza." 
Luke9:12 Umusi ukuze, bamwe cumi na babiri baramwēgēra, bati Sezera abantu, baje mu mihana no mu misozi impande zose bāke indāro, baronke ivyo kurya, kuko hano turi mu gahinga." 
Luke9:13 Arababarira, ati Mube ari mwebge mubagaburira. Baramubgira, bati Nta kindi dufise, atar’ udutsima dutanu n’udufi tubiri, shiti tugiye gusumira aba bantu bose." 
Luke9:14 Kuko bār’ abagabo nk’ibihumbi bitanu. Abarira abigishwa biwe, ati Ni mubicarike bīcīye intēko z’abantu nka mirongwitanu‐mirongwitanu." 
Luke9:15 Babigira bartyo, barabīcarika bose." 
Luke9:16 Yābīra ya mitsima itanu na za fi zibiri, ararangamiza, arāba mw ijuru, arabihezagira, arabimanyagura, abiha abigishwa ngo babishire imbere y’abantu." 
Luke9:17 Bararya, barahāga bose, batororokanya utumanyagu tw’ imisigazwa, twuzura ibisimbo cumi na bibiri." 
Luke9:18 Maze yarikw arasenga yiherereye, abigishwa biwe bāri kumwe na we; arababaza, at’ Abantu bagira ngo ndi nde?" 
Luke9:19 Baramwishura, bati Bagira ng’ uri Yohana Umubatizi; abandi ng’ uri Eliya; abandi ng’ ur’ umwe mu bāvugishwa n’Imana ba kera yazutse." 
Luke9:20 Arababaza, at’ Ariko mweho mugira ngo ndi nde? Petero aramwishura, at’ Uri Kristo w’Imana." 
Luke9:21 Arabihanikiriza, ababarira kutagira umuntu babgira ivyo;" 
Luke9:22 at’ Umwana w’umuntu akwiye kuzobabazwa uburyo bginshi, no kuzokwankwa n’abashingantahe n’abaherezi bakuru n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe, no kuzokwicwa, no kuzozurwa ku musi ugira gatatu." 
Luke9:23 Abgira bose, at’ Umuntu ni yagomba kunkurikira, ni yiyanke, yikorere umusaraba wiwe uko bukeye, ankurikire." 
Luke9:24 Kuk’ ūgomba gukiza ubugingo bgiwe azobubura; arik’ ūzoheba ubugingo bgiwe kubganje azobukiza. 
Luke9:25 Kand’ umuntu vyomumarira iki kwunguka ivyo mw isi vyose, ni yabura ubugingo bgiwe, canke ni yabgakwa kw icīru?" 
Luke9:26 Kuk’ umuntu wese bizotera isoni kunyemera no kwemera amajambo yanje, n’Umwana w’umuntu bizomutera isoni kumwemera, ah’ azozira afise ubgiza bgiwe n’ubga Se n’ubg’ abamarayika bera." 
Luke9:27 Ariko ndababgire ukuri: Mur’ aba bahagaze hano, harimwo bamwe batazobona urupfu gushitsa aho bazobonera ubgami bg’Imana." 
Luke9:28 Hanyuma y’ayo majambo, hashize imisi nka munani, ajana Petero na Yohana na Yakobo, adūga igisozi, aja gusenga." 
Luke9:29 Arikw arasenga, ishusho yo mu maso hiwe ihinduka ukundi, imyambaro yiwe yera derere, irakayangana." 
Luke9:30 Abagabo babiri bavugana na we, yari Mose na Eliya," 
Luke9:31 baboneka bafise ubgiza, bavuga ivyo kuzotāmbūra kwiwe, agira anonosorere i Yerusalemu." 
Luke9:32 Petero n’abāri kumwe na we bāri baremerewe n’itiro, bikanguye rwose babona ubgiza bgiwe na ba bagabo babiri bahagararanye na we." 
Luke9:33 Bagira batandukane na we, Petero abgira Yesu, ati Mwigisha, bitubereye vyiza ko turi hano; nuko duce insago zitatu, rumwe rwawe, urundi rwa Mose, urundi rwa Eliya. Ntiyar’ azi ico avuga." 
Luke9:34 Akibivuga, igicu c’igipfungu kiraza, kibatera igitūtu; ico gipfungu kikibashikako, baratinya." 
Luke9:35 Ijwi riva muri nya gicu, riti Nguyu Umwana wanje natoranije, ni mumwumve." 
Luke9:36 Iryo jwi rishize, Yesu aboneka ar’ umwe. Barabihora, ntihāgira umuntu mur’ iyo misi babgira na kimwe mu vyo bābonye." 
Luke9:37 Bukeye bg’aho bamanutse ico gisozi, ishengero ryinshi riramusanganira." 
Luke9:38 Kand’ umugabo wo muri bo avuga n’ijwi rirenga, ati Mwigisha ndakwinginze, ndābira umwana, kuko namuvyaye ar’ ikinege," 
Luke9:39 kandi har’ impwemu imufata, agatura akaborogo, ikamujegeza, akabimba ifuro, kand’ ihejeje kumukungagura ikagora cane kumuvamwo." 
Luke9:40 Nanje ninginze abigishwa bawe kuyisenda, irabananira." 
Luke9:41 Yesu arishura, ati Yemwe ab’iki gihe mutizera b’ibidambidambi, nzogeza ryari kubana namwe no kubihanganira? Zana hano umwana wawe." 
Luke9:42 Arikw araza, dayimoni amutūra hasi, aramujegeza cane; Yesu akankamira iyo mpwemu ihumanye, akiza uwo muhungu, amusubiza se." 
Luke9:43 Bose batangazwa n’icubahiro gihambaye c’Imana. Ariko bose bagitangarira ivyo yakoze vyose, abarira abigishwa biwe," 
Luke9:44 ati Mushire aya majambo mu matwi yanyu: Umwana w’umuntu azoshirwa mu maboko y’abantu. 
Luke9:45 Bayoberwa iryo jambo, kandi bararihishwa ngo ntibarimenye, batinya kurimubaza iry’ ari ryo." 
Luke9:46 Kandi havyuka ibihāri muri bo, vy’umukuru wabo uw’ ari we." 
Luke9:47 Ariko Yesu abonye ivyo bihāri vyo mu mitima yabo, yābīra akana, agahagarika i ruhande yiwe," 
Luke9:48 arababgira, at’ Ūzokwākīra aka kana mw izina ryanje, azoba anyakiriye; kand’ ūnyakīra aba yākiriye uwantumye: kuk’ umuto muri mwebge hanyuma ya mwese ari we mukuru." 
Luke9:49 Yohana aramwishura, ati Mwigisha, twabonye umuntu asenda abadayimoni mw izina ryawe, turamubuza, kukw atadukurikira." 
Luke9:50 Yesu aramubgira, ati Ntimumubuze, kuk’ ūtar’ umwansi wanyu ari mu ruhande rwanyu." 
Luke9:51 Maz’ imisi yiwe yo kudūzwa mw ijuru igira ishike, yerekeza i Yerusalemu amaramaje kujayo," 
Luke9:52 atuma integuza imbere yiwe. Ziragenda, zija mu mihana y’Abasamariya kumuteguriza." 
Luke9:53 Ntibāmwākīra, kuko yerekeje i Yerusalemu." 
Luke9:54 Abigishwa biwe Yakobo na Yohana, babibonye, baramubaza, bati Mugenzi, ugomba ko tubarira umuriro ng’ utibuke uve mw ijuru, ubayigize, nk’uko Eliya yakoze?" 
Luke9:55 Maz’ arahindukira, arabakankamira, at’ Erega ntimuzi umutima wanyu uk’ usa; kuk’ Umwana w’umuntu ataje guhonnya ubugingo bg’abantu, ariko yaje kubukiza." 
Luke9:56 Nuko baja mu yindi mihana. 
Luke9:57 Bariko baragenda mu nzira, umuntu aramubgira, ati Ndagukurikira ah’ uja hose." 
Luke9:58 Yesu aramubgira, at’ Imbgebge ziri n’imyobo, n’ibiguruka mu kirēre biri n’ivyāri; arik’ Umwana w’umuntu we ntagira ah’ arambika umusaya." 
Luke9:59 Maz’ abarira uwundi muntu, ati Nkurikira. Na we, ati Mugenzi, banza undekure ngende mpambe data." 
Luke9:60 Ariko Yesu aramubarira, ati Reka abāpfuye bahambe abāpfuye babo, ariko weho genda, ukwize ivy’ ubgami bg’Imana." 
Luke9:61 Uwundi muntu aramubgira, ati Mugenzi, ndagukurikira, ariko banza undekure, nje gusezera abo mu rugo i wanje." 
Luke9:62 Ariko Yesu aramubgira, ati Nta muntu afashe isuka irimishwa n’inka, arāba inyuma, abereye ubgami bg’Imana." 
Luke10:1 Mu nyuma y’ivyo, Umwami Yesu atoranya abandi mirongwirindwi, atuma babiri‐babiri, ngo bagende imbere yiwe mu bisagara vyose n’ahantu hose ah’ agira ace." 
Luke10:2 Arababgira, at’ Ivyimburwa ni vyinshi, arikw abimbuzi ni bo bake: nuko ni mwinginge Nyen’ ivyimburwa, arungike abimbuzi mu vyimburwa vyiwe." 
Luke10:3 Ni mugende; rāba mbatumye muri nk’abana b’intama mu mabingira hagati. 
Luke10:4 Ntimujane umupfuko w’amahera, cank’ isaho, cank’ inkweto: kandi ntihagire n’uwo muramukanya mu nzira." 
Luke10:5 Inzu yose muzokwinjiramwo, muze mubanze muvuge, mut’ Amahoro abe mur’ iyi nzu." 
Luke10:6 Ni yaba irimw’ umunyamahoro, amahoro yanyu azoba kuri we: ni bitāmera birtyo, azobagarukako." 
Luke10:7 Kand’ iyo nzu nyene muze muyigumemwo, murya munywa ivyo babahaye; kuk’ umukozi akwiye ingero yiwe. Ntimugende murarāraguza." 
Luke10:8 Kand’ igisagara cose mujamwo bakabākīra, muze murye ivyo babahaye," 
Luke10:9 mukize abarwaye baho, mubabgire mut’ Ubgami bg’Imana burabēgereye." 
Luke10:10 Arikw igisagara cose mujamwo ntibabākīre, muze musohoke muje mu nzira zaco," 
Luke10:11 muti N’umukungugu wo mu gisagara canyu, ufashe mu birenge vyacu, turawubakunkumuriye: ariko mumenye iki, yuk’ ubgami bg’Imana buri hafi." 
Luke10:12 Ndababgire, Kur’ uwo musi uzoza, Sodomu hazogira agahengekezo kurusha nya gisagara." 
Luke10:13 Uzobona ibara, Korazini; uzobona ibara, Betsayida; kukw ibikomeye vyakorewe muri mwebge iyo biba vyarakorewe muri Tiro n’i Sidoni, baba bārihannye kera, bicaye bambaye amagunira, bīsīze umunyota." 
Luke10:14 Ariko muri Tiro n’i Sidoni hazogira agahengekezo ku musi w’amateka kurusha mwebge. 
Luke10:15 Nawe, Kaperinawumu, mbeg’ uzoshirwa hejuru, ushike kw ijuru? Oya, uzocokezwa i kuzimu." 
Luke10:16 Ūbumviye ni jewe aba yumviye; ūbanse, ni jewe aba yanse; ūnyanse, aba yanse uwantumye." 
Luke10:17 Nuko bamwe mirongwirindwi bagarukana umunezero, bati Mugenzi, abadayimoni na bo baratwumvira mw izina ryawe." 
Luke10:18 Arababgira, ati Nabonye Satani, avuye mw ijuru, akoroka nk’umuravyo." 
Luke10:19 Ehe mbahaye ububasha bgo gukandagira inzoka na sikorupiyo, n’ubgo kunesha ubushobozi bga wa Mwansi bgose, kandi nta kintu kizogira ico kibagira na gatoya." 
Luke10:20 Ariko ntimunezerezwe n’ukw izo mpwemu zibumvira, yamara munezerezwe n’ukw amazina yanyu yanditswe mw ijuru." 
Luke10:21 Uwo mwanya anezererwa cane muri Mpwemu Yera, aravuga, ati Ndaguhimbaza Data, Mwami w’ijuru n’isi, kukw ivyo wabihishije abanyabgenge n’abahanga, ukabihishurira inzoya. Ego me Data, kuko washimye ko biba birtyo imbere yawe." 
Luke10:22 Vyose nabihawe na Data; kandi nta wuzi Umwana uw’ ari we, atari Data: na Data nta wumuzi uw’ ari we atar’ Umwana, n’uwo Umwana agomba kumuhishurira." 
Luke10:23 Ahindukirira abigishwa, ababgira biherereye, ati Hahirwa amaso abona ivyo mubona." 
Luke10:24 Ndababgira yukw abāvugishwa n’Imana benshi n’abami benshi bāgomvye kubona ivyo mubona ntibābibona, no kwumva ivyo mwumva, ntibāvyumva." 
Luke10:25 Maz’ umwe mu bigisha ivyagezwe ava hasi, aramugeza, ati Mwigisha, nkore iki, ngo nze ndagwe ubugingo budashira?" 
Luke10:26 Na we aramubaza, ati Vyanditswe bite mu vyagezwe, kand’ usoma iki?" 
Luke10:27 Aramwishura, ati Ngo Mukundishe Uhoraho, Imana yanyu, imitima yanyu yose, n’ubugingo bganyu bgose, n’inkomezi zanyu zose, n’ubgenge bganyu bgose; kandi mukunde bagenzi banyu nk’uko mwikunda." 
Luke10:28 Aramubgira, ati Wishuye neza, gira urtyo, uzogira ubugingo." 
Luke10:29 Maz’ uwo agomvye kwiyerekana nk’ūgororotse, abaza Yesu, ati Mbega mugenzanje ni nde?" 
Luke10:30 Yesu aramwishura, ati Hābaye umuntu yar’ avuye i Yerusalemu, arikw aramanuka aja i Yeriko, agwa mu bambuzi, baramukoba, baramukubita, barīgīra, basiga ashigaje gatoya agahwera." 
Luke10:31 Hāriho n’umuherezi amanuka mur’ iyo nzira, amurengukako, amubonye aca i ruhande." 
Luke10:32 Kandi n’Umulewi ahashitse agira kuno, amubonye aca i ruhande." 
Luke10:33 Maz’ Umusamariya yari mu nzira ashika kuri we, amubonye amutera akagongwe:" 
Luke10:34 aramwēgēra, amupfuka inguma, amusomōza amavuta ya elayo na vino, amushira ku ndogoba yiwe, amujana mu ndāro y’abahita, aramurwaza." 
Luke10:35 Bukeye agoborora idenariyo zibiri, aziha nyen’ indāro, at’ Umurwaze, kand’ ivy’ uzotanga vyose birenze ivyo ni nagaruka nzobikwishura." 
Luke10:36 Mur’ abo batatu ugira ngo ni nde yabonetse kw ari mugenzi w’uwaguye mu bambuzi? 
Luke10:37 Aramwishura, ati N’uwamugiriye imbabazi. Yesu aramubarira, ati Nawe genda ugire urtyo." 
Luke10:38 Maze bariko baragenda bashika mu mihana: umugore yitwa Marita aramwākīra amushikiza mu nzu yiwe. 
Luke10:39 Uwo yar’ afise mwene nyina yitwa Mariya, yicara imbere y’ibirenge vy’Umwami Yesu, yumva ijambo ryiwe." 
Luke10:40 Ariko Marita ahagarikira umutima kuzimana vyinshi; aramwēgēra, aramubgira, ati Mugenzi, ntibikubabaje yuko mwene mama yantereranye ibikorwa? Nuko mubarire amfashe." 
Luke10:41 Umwami Yesu aramwishura, ati Marita, Marita, urīganyira wigora muri vyinshi:" 
Luke10:42 arikw ibikwiye rwose ni kimwe: kuko Mariya ahisemw’ umugabane mwiza, atazokwakwa." 
Luke11:1 Maz’ ar’ ahantu, asenga; ahejeje, umwe mu bigishwa biwe aramubgira, ati Mugenzi, twigishe gusenga, nk’uko Yohana yigishije abigishwa biwe." 
Luke11:2 Arababarira, ati Ni mwasenga, muvuge muti Data, izina ryawe ryubahwe, ubgami bgawe buze;" 
Luke11:3 imisi yose uduhe ivyo kurya vyayo; 
Luke11:4 uduharire ivyaha vyacu, kuko natwe duhebera abari n’imyenda yacu bose; kandi ntutujane mu bitwosha nabi." 
Luke11:5 Arababgira, ati Ni nde muri mwebge afise incuti yoja i we mu gicugu, akayibgira, ati Ncuti yanje, ngurana udutsima dutatu," 
Luke11:6 kuko haje incuti yanje ivuye ku rugendo, nanje ntagira ico ndayizimana:" 
Luke11:7 uwo mu nzu yomwishura, ati Sigaho kungora, namaze kwugara, kandi turi kumwe n’abana banje ku buriri, sinshoboye kuvyuka ngo ndayiguhe." 
Luke11:8 Ndababgire: Nah’ atovyurwa n’ukw ar’ incuti yiwe ngw ayimuhe, ariko kukw atagize isoni zo kumuhambira, aravyuka, akamuha ivy’ agomba vyose." 
Luke11:9 Nanje ndababgire: Musabe muzohabga; murondere muzoronka; muramutse muzokwugururirwa. 
Luke11:10 Kuk’ ūsaba wese ahabga; ūrondera aronka; ūramutsa yugururirwa. 
Luke11:11 Kandi ni nde muri mwebge w’umuvyeyi, umwana wiwe yomusaba umutsima, akamuha ibuye; canke yomusaba ifi, akamuha inzoka;" 
Luke11:12 canke yomusaba irigi, akamuha sikorupiyo?" 
Luke11:13 None mwebge, ko muzi guha abana banyu ingabire nziza muri babi, mbega So wo mw ijuru ntazorushiriza rwose guha Mpwemu Yera abamumusavye?" 
Luke11:14 Kand’ asenda dayimoni atera uburagi: dayimoni amuvuyemwo, uno muntu w’ikiragi aravuga; ishengero riratangara." 
Luke11:15 Ariko bamwe muri bo baravuga, bati Beyezebuli, umukuru w’abadayimoni, ni we amushoboza gusenda abadayimoni." 
Luke11:16 Abandi bamuronderakw ikimenyetso kiva mw ijuru, bamugeza." 
Luke11:17 Na we amenye ivyo biyumvira, arababgira, at’ Ubgami bgose iyo bgitandukanije ubgabgo burahona, n’inzu, iyo yitandukanije, iragwa." 
Luke11:18 Na Satani, namba yitandukanije ubgiwe, ubgami bgiwe buzorama bute? Kuko muvuga yuko Beyezebuli ari we anshoboza gusenda abadayimoni." 
Luke11:19 Ariko jewe namba Beyezebuli ari we anshoboza gusenda abadayimoni, abana banyu bashobozwa na nde kubasenda? Ni co gituma ari bo bazobatsindisha." 
Luke11:20 Arik’ urutoke rw’Imana ni rwaba ari rwo runshoboza gusenda abadayimoni, noneh’ ubgami bg’Imana burabashikiriye." 
Luke11:21 Umuntu w’inkomezi afise ibirwanishwa iy’ ateramiye urugo rwiwe, ibintu vyiwe biba amahoro;" 
Luke11:22 arik’ ūmurusha inkomezi iy’ aramutse amuteye, akamunesha, amwaka ivy’ arwanisha vyose yari yizigiye, akanyaga ibintu vyiwe, akabigaba." 
Luke11:23 Ūtamperereyeko aba ar’ umwansi wanje, kand’ ūdafatanije nanje kwegeranya aba asanzaje." 
Luke11:24 Iy’ impwemu ihumanye ivuye mu muntu, ica ahatagira amazi, irondera uburuhukiro, ikabubura, ikavuga, iti Reka nsubire mu nzu yanje navuyemwo." 
Luke11:25 Ihashitse, igasanga ikubuye, iteguritse." 
Luke11:26 Igaca igenda, ikazana izindi mpwemu ndwi ziyirusha ububi, zikinjira, zikahaba. Ivya nyuma vy’uwo muntu bikarusha ivya mbere ububi." 
Luke11:27 Akivuga ivyo, umugore wo mw ishengero ashira hejuru, aramubgira, ati Hahirwa inda yakuvyaye, n’amabere yakwonkeje." 
Luke11:28 Na we aramwishura, ati Cane‐cane hahirwa abumva ijambo ry’Imana bakaribungabunga." 
Luke11:29 Ishengero rikoraniye kuri we, atangura kubabgira, at’ Iki gihe n’igihe kibi; kirondera ikimenyetso, ariko nta kimenyetso kizohabga, atar’ ikimenyetso ca Yona." 
Luke11:30 Nk’uko Yona yabaye ikimenyetso ku Banyaninewe, ni k’Umwana w’umuntu azoba ku b’iki gihe." 
Luke11:31 Umugabekazi w’igihugu c’i bumanuko azovana hasi n’abagabo b’iki gihe ku musi w’amateka, azobatsindisha; kuko yavanywe ku mpera y’isi no kwumva ubgenge bga Salomo; kandi rāba, ūruta Salomo ari hano." 
Luke11:32 Abagabo b’i Ninewe bazovana hasi n’ab’ iki gihe ku musi w’amateka, babatsindishe; kuko bihannye aho bumviye ubutumwa buvuzwe na Yona; kandi rāba, ūruta Yona ari hano." 
Luke11:33 Nta wodomeka itara ngw arishire mu mwobo, canke ngw aryubikekw igisimbo, arikw arishira ku gitereko caryo, ngw abinjira basange habona." 
Luke11:34 Itara ry’umubiri wawe n’ijisho ryawe. Ijisho ryawe iy’ ari ryiza, umubiri wawe wose uba uri n’umuco: arikw iy’ ari ribi, umubiri wawe uba uri n’umwiza." 
Luke11:35 Nuko wirābe yuk’ umuco uri muri wewe atar’ umwiza. 
Luke11:36 Kand’ umubiri wawe wose ni waba uri n’umuco, ata gice na kimwe gifise umwiza, wose uzoba uri n’umuco, nk’uk’ ukwaka kw’itara kukuboneshereza." 
Luke11:37 Akibivuga, Umufarisayo aramuhamagara ngw amuzimane: arinjira, aricara ngw arye." 
Luke11:38 Wa Mufarisayo abibonye biramutangaza, kukw atabanje gukaraba atararya." 
Luke11:39 Umwami Yesu aramubgira, at’ Erega mwebge Abafarisayo mwoza inyuma y’igikombe n’inkōko, arikw imbere muri mwebge mwuzuye ubgambuzi n’ububi." 
Luke11:40 Mwa bijuju mwe, iyaremye urukoba si yo yaremye n’imbere?" 
Luke11:41 Ariko mutange ibir’ imbere mu gikombe no mu nkōko mubitangishijwe n’ubuntu, kand’ umve, vyose bizobabera ibiziruwe." 
Luke11:42 Ariko muzobona ibara, Bafarisayo, kuko mutanga ikigiracumi c’imbgija n’isogi n’imboga zose, ariko guca izibereye no gukunda Imana mukavyirengagiza. Ivyo mwari mukwiye kubikora, vya bindi na vyo ntimubireke." 
Luke11:43 Muzobona ibara, Bafarisayo, kuko mukunda intebe z’icubahiro mu masinagogi, no kugirwako bgakeye mu tuguriro." 
Luke11:44 Muzobona ibara, kuko musa n’imva zitamenyekana, abantu bakazicako batabizi." 
Luke11:45 Umwe mu bigisha ivyagezwe aramwishura, ati Mwigisha, k’uvuze urtyo, natwe uradututse." 
Luke11:46 Na we, ati Namwe abigisha ivyagezwe muzobona ibara, kuko mwikoreza abantu imitwaro itokwikorerwa, namwe ubganyu iyo mitwaro ntimuyikozek’ urutoke na rumwe." 
Luke11:47 Muzobona ibara, kuko mwubakira imva z’abāvugishwa n’Imana, ba sogokuruza banyu ari bo bābīshe." 
Luke11:48 Uko ni ko mwiyagirije, kandi mwemeye ivyo ba sogokuruza banyu bākoze, kukw ari bo bābīshe, namwe mububakira imva." 
Luke11:49 Ni co catumye Imana ivugisha ubgenge bgayo, iti Nzobatumakw abo mvugisha n’intumwa, bamwe muri bo bazobica, abandi bazobahama," 
Luke11:50 ngw amaraso y’abāvugishwa n’Imana bose yavishijwe, uhereye ku kuremwa kw’isi, aronderwe ku b’iki gihe," 
Luke11:51 uhereye ku maraso ya Abeli, ukageza ku maraso ya Zakariya yīciwe hagati y’igicaniro n’ahēra h’urusengero: ni koko, ndababgire, azoronderwa ku b’iki gihe." 
Luke11:52 Muzobona ibara, abigisha ivyagezwe, kuko mwatwaye urupfunguzo rw’ubgenge: ntimwinjiye ubganyu, n’abāgomba kwinjira mwarababujije." 
Luke11:53 Maz’ asohotse, abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe n’Abafarisayo batangura kumusugereza no kumwiyandagazako ngo bamuvugishe vyinshi," 
Luke11:54 bamutega ngo bafate ijambo ryomukorokana. 
Luke12:1 Mur’ ico gihe, ishengero ry’abantu ibihumbi vyinshi rikoranira kuri we, bakandagirana, ahēra ku bigishwa biwe, arababarira, ati Mwirinde umwambiro w’Abafarisayo, ni wo buryarya." 
Luke12:2 Nta catwikiriwe kitazotwikururwa, canke kinyegejwe kitazomenyekana." 
Luke12:3 Nukw ivyo mwavugiye mu mwiza vyose bizokwumvikanira mu muco, n’ico mwongoreraniye mu mazu haruguru kizovugirwa ku mazu hejuru." 
Luke12:4 Kandi ndabgira mwebge abakunzi banje: Ntimugatinye abica umubiri, hanyuma batagira ikindi bazobagira." 
Luke12:5 Ariko ndabereka iyo mukwiye gutinya: mutinye Iyiheza kwica umuntu, ikagira ububasha bgo kumukororera muri Gehinomu. Ni koko, ndababgire, abe ari yo mutinya." 
Luke12:6 Mbeg’ utunyoni dutanu ntitugurwa amakuta abiri? Ariko kamwe muri two ntigahundukwa imbere y’Imana. 
Luke12:7 Ariko n’umushatsi wo ku mitwe yanyu wose waraharūwe. Ntimutinye; muruta utunyoni twinshi. 
Luke12:8 Kandi ndababgire; Umuntu wese azonyaturira imbere y’abantu, Umwana w’umuntu azomwaturira imbere y’abamarayika b’Imana." 
Luke12:9 Arik’ ūnyihakanira imbere y’abantu, azokwihakanirwa imbere y’abamarayika b’Imana." 
Luke12:10 Kand’ umuntu wese azodedemba ku Mwana w’umuntu, azobiharirwa; arik’ ūzorogota kuri Mpwemu Yera ntazobiharirwa." 
Luke12:11 Kandi ni bābajana mu masinagogi bakabashīra abakuru n’abaganza, ntimuze muhagarikire imitima ico mwireguza n’ingene mwiregura, n’ico muvuga." 
Luke12:12 Kuko Mpwemu Yera mur’ ako kanya nyene azobategekera ivyo mukwiye kuvuga. 
Luke12:13 Maz’ umuntu wo mw ishengero aramubgira, ati Mwigisha, mbaririra mwene mama tugabure umwandu." 
Luke12:14 Aramubaza, ati Mbega wa mugabo, ni nde yanshizeho kuba umucamanza wanyu, canke kubagaburira ivyanyu?" 
Luke12:15 Kand’ arababarira, ati Murumva, mwirinde ukwifuza kwose, kuk’ ubugingo bg’umuntu butava mu bihinda vy’ibintu atunze." 
Luke12:16 Kand’ abacira umugani, ati Hābaye umuntu w’umutunzi yar’ afise itongo rimera cane." 
Luke12:17 Yiyumvira mu mutima wiwe, ati Ndagira nte, ko ntagira aho nimburira imirima yanje?" 
Luke12:18 Ati Ndabigenza ntya: ndasambura ibigega vyanje, nubake ibindi binini‐binini, abe ari ho nimburira imirima yanje yose n’ibintu vyanje vyose." 
Luke12:19 Nzobgira umutima wanje, nti Mutima, ufise ibintu vyinshi bizohitikirana imyaka myinshi, ruhuka, urye, unywe, unezerwe." 
Luke12:20 Maz’ Imana iramubgira, iti Wa gipfu we, mur’ iri joro barakwaka ubugingo bgawe: non’ ivyo wohitikiranije bizoba ivya nde?" 
Luke12:21 Umuntu yishingurira ni kw amera, atar’ umutunzi mu vy’Imana." 
Luke12:22 Abgira abigishwa biwe, ati Ni co gitumye ndababarira, nti Ntimukaganyire amagara yanyu ku vyo muzorya, cank’ umubiri wanyu ku vyo muzokwambara." 
Luke12:23 Kukw amagara aruta ivyo kurya, n’umubiri uruta ivyambarwa." 
Luke12:24 Ni mwitegereze ibikōna, ingene bitabiba, ntibishwabure, ntibigire ububīko cank’ ikigega, kand’ Imana irabitunga: erega mwebge muruta ibisīga cane." 
Luke12:25 Ni nde muri mwebge yoshobozwa n’amaganya kwisumvya uko yareha nk’ukuboko kumwe? 
Luke12:26 Nuko ni mutāshobora gukora igito rwose, n’iki gituma mwiganyira ibindi?" 
Luke12:27 Ni mwitegereze amashurwe, ingen’ akura: ntiyīrirwa aratama, ntajisha impuzu: ariko ndababgire: Na Salomo mu bgiza bgiwe bgose ntiyar’ ashajije nka rimwe mur’ ayo." 
Luke12:28 Non’ Imana ko yambika ivyatsi vyo ku misozi irtyo, birih’ uyu musi, ariko nk’ejo bigatererwa mu ziko, mbega ntizorushiriza kubambika, mwebge ab’ ukwizera guke mwe?" 
Luke12:29 Kandi ntimukītwaririke ivyo murya n’ivyo munywa, ntimukiganyire." 
Luke12:30 Kukw ivyo vyose abanyamahanga bo mw isi ari vyo bitwaririka, ariko So arazi ko mukena ivyo." 
Luke12:31 Ariko mwitwaririke ubgami bgiwe, ni ho ivyo muzovyongerwa." 
Luke12:32 Yemwe mwa busho buto, ntimutinye: kuko So bimuhimbara kubaha ubgami." 
Luke12:33 Mugure ivyo mufise, mutange ibiguzi vyavyo kubg’ ubuntu; mwibarīrire imipfuko idashira, ubutunzi budashira buri mw ijuru, ahatēgērwa n’igisuma, ata n’inyenzi zōnōna:" 
Luke12:34 kukw ah’ ubutunzi bganyu buri ari ho imitima yanyu izoba. 
Luke12:35 Mwame mukenyeye, kand’ amatara yanyu yame yaka:" 
Luke12:36 namwe muse n’abantu barorereye shebuja, igihe agarukira ava mu bukwe, ngo ni yaza, akaramutsa, bace bamwugururira." 
Luke12:37 Hahirwa abo bashumba, abo shebuja azoza agasanga bari maso: ndababgire ukuri: Azokenyera, abicarike, aze, abagaburire." 
Luke12:38 Ni yaza mu gicugu canke mu nkoko, akabasanga artyo, bazoba abahirwe." 
Luke12:39 Kandi mumenye iki, yukw iyaba nyen’ urugo yar’ asanzwe azi igihe igisuma kiziramwo, yogavye, ntiyokunze kw inzu yiwe yimbga." 
Luke12:40 Namwe mwame mwiteguye, kuk’ Umwana w’umuntu azoza mu gihe mutiyumviriye." 
Luke12:41 Petero aramubaza, ati Mbega Mugenzi, uwo mugani ni twebge twenyene uwuciriye, canke n’abandi bose?" 
Luke12:42 Umwami Yesu na we aramubaza, ati Ni nde mubgiriza wo kwizigirwa w’ubgenge, shebuja yosigarana abo mu rugo rwiwe, ngw abagaburire ku ngero yabo igihe kigeze?" 
Luke12:43 Hahirwa uwo mushumba shebuja agarutse azosanga akora artyo. 
Luke12:44 Ndababgira ukuri yukw azomuha kugaba ivy’ afise vyose. 
Luke12:45 Arik’ uwo mushumba ni yibgira mu mutima wiwe, ati Databuja aracatevye kuza; maz’ agatangura gukubita abashumba n’incoreke, no kurya no kunywa no kuborerwa," 
Luke12:46 shebuja w’uwo mushumba azoza ku musi atamwiteze, no mu gihe atazi, azomucamwo kubiri, amusangize umugabane wiwe n’abatizera." 
Luke12:47 Kand’ uwo mushumba yar’ azi ivyo shebuja agomba, ntiyitegure, ntakore ivyo agomba, azokubitwa nyinshi." 
Luke12:48 Arik’ ūtar’ abizi, agakora ibikwiye kumukubitisha, azokubitwa nkeya. Uwahawe vyinshi wese azobazwa vyinshi; uwabīkijwe vyinshi ni we bazorushiriza kwaka vyinshi." 
Luke12:49 Naje guta umuriro mw isi, non’ iyaba war’ umaze gufatwa, mba nkigomba iki kandi?" 
Luke12:50 Ndi n’umubatizo, uwo nkwiye kubatizwa; emwe uko mbabazwa kugeza ah’ uzoherera!" 
Luke12:51 Mbega mwiyumvira ko naje kuzana amahoro mw isi? 
Luke12:52 Ndababgire, si ko biri, ariko naje kuzana umucano. Kuk’ uhereye none hazobaho batanu mu nzu imwe batandukanye, batatu na babiri, na babiri na batatu." 
Luke12:53 Umwana azotandukana na se, na se n’umwana n’uko; umukobga azotandukana na nyina, na nyina n’umukobga n’uko; inabukwe azotandukana n’umukazana wiwe, n’umukazana na inabukwe n’uko." 
Luke12:54 Kand’ abgira ishengero, at’ Iyo mubonye igicu kivuye i burengerazuba, muca mugira ngw Imvura iraguye; kandi ni ko biba." 
Luke12:55 Iyo mubonye umuyaga uturutse i bumanuko mugira ngo Haraba indugumba, kandi ni ko biba." 
Luke12:56 Mwa ndyarya mwe, murazi kugendeza isi n’ijuru, n’iki kibabuza kugendeza iki gihe?" 
Luke12:57 Kandi namwe ubganyu n’iki kibabuza kugenzura ivyo kugororoka? 
Luke12:58 Ni wajana n’ūkurega muja ku mushingantahe, mukiri mu nzira ushishikare kwikiranura na we, ngo ntagukwegere ku mucamanza, umucamanza akaguha umusoda, akagushira mw ibohero." 
Luke12:59 Ndakubgire, Ntuzohava na gatoya, utishuye n’isenge ry’imperēra." 
Luke13:1 Ico gihe abantu bār’ aho bamwīgānira ivy’ Abanyagalilaya, abo Pilato yavanganije amaraso yabo n’ibimazi vyabo." 
Luke13:2 Arababaza, ati Mbega mwiyumvira yukw abo Banyagalilaya bārusha abandi Banyagalilaya kuba abanyavyaha, kuko bāgizwe bartyo?" 
Luke13:3 Ndababgire, Si ko biri; ariko ni mutihana, namwe muzohona murtyo mwese." 
Luke13:4 Canke ba bandi cumi n’umunani, abo umutara muremure w’amatafari w’i Silowamu wahomvokeyeko, ukabica, mwiyumvira yuko bārusha abandi b’i Yerusalemu bose kuba abanyabicumuro?" 
Luke13:5 Ndababgire, Si ko biri; ariko ni mutihana, namwe muzohona murtyo mwese." 
Luke13:6 Kand’ abacira uyu mugani, ati Hābaye umuntu yar’ afise umusukoni watewe mu ruzabibu rwiwe, araza awuronderakw insukoni arazibura." 
Luke13:7 Abgira umukozi w’uruzabibu, ati Rāba, none n’imyaka itatu nza kurondera insukoni kur’ uyu musukoni, sinzibone; uwuce: ugasarira iki aha hantu?" 
Luke13:8 Na we aramwishura, at’ Enda mugenzi, wureke uyu mwaka na wo, ndaworohereze, ndawutabirire:" 
Luke13:9 hanyuma ni wama insukoni bizoba ari vyiza; ariko n’utama, uzowuca." 
Luke13:10 Ku musi w’isabato yigishiriza mur’ imwe mu masinagogi. 
Luke13:11 Hār’ umugore yinjiwemwo n’impwemu itera ubumuga, yar’ amaze imyaka cumi n’umunani ahetamye, adashobora kwunamuka na gatoya." 
Luke13:12 Yesu amubonye aramuhamagara, aramubgira, ati Nyina wanje, urabohowe ubumuga bgawe." 
Luke13:13 Amurambikakw ibiganza, uwo mwanya aragororoka, ahimbaza Imana." 
Luke13:14 Arik’ umukuru w’isinagogi yitonganiriza ivy’ uko Yesu akijije umuntu kw isabato, abgira abantu, ati Harih’ imisi itandatu, ikwiye gukorwakw ibikorwa; abe ari yo muzako mukizwe, ariko hatari ku musi w’isabato." 
Luke13:15 Umwami Yesu aramwishura, ati Mwa ndyarya mwe, mbeg’ umuntu wese muri mwebge ntazitura inka yiwe cank’ indogoba yiwe mu ruhongore kw isabato, akayijana, akayishōra?" 
Luke13:16 Non’ uyu, ar’ umukobga wa Aburahamu, yaboshwe na Satani iyo myaka cumi n’umunani yose, ntakwiye kubohorwa iyo ngoyi ku musi w’isabato?" 
Luke13:17 Akivuga ivyo, abamurwanya bose baramāramāra, ishengero ryose rinezererwa ivyiza vy’agahebuza yakora vyose." 
Luke13:18 Kand’ aravuga, at’ Ubgami bg’Imana busa n’iki, kandi ndabushushanye n’iki?" 
Luke13:19 Busa n’akabuto ka sinapi, umuntu yābiriye, akagatera mu ntabire yiwe, kagakura, kakaba igiti, inyoni zo mu kirēre zikārika mu mashami yaco." 
Luke13:20 Yongera kuvuga, at’ Ubgami bg’Imana ndabushushanye n’iki?" 
Luke13:21 Busa n’umwambiro umugore yābiriye akawuvanga n’ingero zitatu z’ifu, gushitsa ah’ iribututumbire yose." 
Luke13:22 Ari mu nzira, ahita mu bisagara no mu mihana, yigisha, ari ku rugendo aja i Yerusalemu." 
Luke13:23 Umuntu aramubaza, ati Mugenzi, mbeg’ abakizwa ni bake? Na we arababarira," 
Luke13:24 ati Mushishikare guca mw irembo ripfunganye: ndababgira yuko benshi bazogomba kuricamwo, ntibabishobore." 
Luke13:25 Nyen’ inzu ni yaheza guhaguruka, akugara urugi, mugatangura gukomanga muhagaze hanze, mukavuga, muti Mupfasoni, n’utwugururire: ni ho azobishura, ati Simbazi, sinzi n’iyo muvuye." 
Luke13:26 Ni ho muzotangura kuvuga, mut’ Erega twarīra, twanywera imbere yawe, kandi wigishiriza mu nzira z’i wacu." 
Luke13:27 Azobabgira, ati Ndababgire, sinzi iyo muvuye; mviraho, mwa bakora ibizira mwese mwe." 
Luke13:28 Aho ni ho hazoba amarira no kuryanya insya z’amenyo, aho muzobonera Aburahamu na Isaka na Yakobo n’abāvugishwa n’Imana bose bari mu bgami bg’Imana, namwe muhindiwe hanze." 
Luke13:29 Hazoza abava i burasirazuba n’i burengerazuba n’i burārūko n’i bumanuko, bazokwicara mu bgami bg’Imana." 
Luke13:30 Kandi har’ ab’ inyuma bazoba ab’ imbere, n’ab’ imbere bazoba ab’ inyuma." 
Luke13:31 Uwo mwanya haza Abafarisayo bamwe, baramubarira, bati Va hano ugende, kuko Herode agomba kukwica." 
Luke13:32 Arababarira, ati Genda mubgire iyo mbgebge, mut’ Umve, arasenda abadayimoni, arakiza abantu uyu musi n’ejo, ku musi ugira gatatu azotunganywa rwose." 
Luke13:33 Ariko nkwiye kugenda uyu musi n’ejo na hirya y’ejo, kuko bidashoboka k’ūvugishwa n’Imana yicwa, atar’ i Yerusalemu." 
Luke13:34 Ewe Yerusalemu, ewe Yerusalemu, wica abavugishwa n’Imana, ugatera amabuye abagutumweko! Ni kangahe nagomvye gukoranya abana bawe, nk’ukw inkoko ikoranya imiswi yayo iyibundikira mu vyubi vyayo, ntimwakunda." 
Luke13:35 Rāba, inzu yanyu muyitānywe ar’ umusaka. Kandi ndababgire, Ntimukimbona kugeza aho muzovugira, muti Hashemezwe ūje mw izina ry’Uhoraho." 
Luke14:1 Yinjiye mu nzu y’umwe mu bakuru b’Abafarisayo kw isabato kurya, baramugenza." 
Luke14:2 Imbere yiwe hār’ umuntu arwaye urusina. 
Luke14:3 Yesu abaza abigisha ivyagezwe n’Abafarisayo, ati Mbega biremerwa gukiza umuntu kw isabato, canke ntivyemerwa?" 
Luke14:4 Maze barihorera. Aramufata, aramukiza, aramusezera." 
Luke14:5 Kand’ arababaza, ati Ni nde muri mwebge afise umwana cank’ inka, hogira igikorokera mw iriba, ntiyoca agikūrayo kw isabato?" 
Luke14:6 Ntibāshobora kumwishura mur’ ivyo. 
Luke14:7 Kand’ acira umugani abātumiwe, abonye ingene bitoraniriza ivyicaro vy’abakuru;" 
Luke14:8 arababgira, at’ Umuntu ni yagutorera ubukwe, ntuze wicare mu cicaro c’abakuru: ngo kumbure ntihabeh’ umuntu akurusha igitinyiro yatowe," 
Luke14:9 kand’ uwabatoye mwempi akaza akakubgira, ati Habise uyu: ni ho uzomāramāra, ukagenda, ukicara inyuma y’abandi bose." 
Luke14:10 Ariko ni watorwa, ugende, wicare inyuma y’abandi bose, kugira ng’uwagutoye aje, akubgire, at’ Igira ino haruguru mugenzi; ni ho uzobona icubahiro imbere y’abo mwicaranye musangira bose." 
Luke14:11 Kuk’ umuntu wese yishira hejuru azocishwa bugufi, kand’ uwicisha bugufi azoshirwa hejuru." 
Luke14:12 Kand’ abgira uwamutumiye, ati Ni wagira amazimano ku murango canke mw ijoro, ntuz’ utumire abagenzi bawe cank’ abo muvukana cank’ incuti zawe cank’ ababanyi bawe b’abatunzi; kuko kumbure na bo bogutumira, bakakwishura." 
Luke14:13 Ariko ni wagira amazimano, upfume utumira aboro n’ibirema n’abacumbagira n’impumyi: ni ho uzoba uhiriwe;" 
Luke14:14 kuko badafise ivyo kukwishura, arik’ uzokwishurwa mw izuka ry’abagororotsi." 
Luke14:15 Maz’ umwe mu bicaranye na we avyumvise, aramubgira, ati Hahirwa ūzorīra mu bgami bg’Imana." 
Luke14:16 Na we aramubgira, ati Hābaye umuntu yarondeje amazimano menshi, atora benshi:" 
Luke14:17 igihe co kurya gishitse, atuma umushumba wiwe kubarira abātowe, ngo Ni muze, kuko bihejeje gutegurwa." 
Luke14:18 Bose batangura kuzangazanga n’umutima uhūye. Uwa mbere, ati Naguze itongo, nkwiye kuja kurirāba; ndakwinginze, uramvugira antunge." 
Luke14:19 Uwundi, ati Naguze inka cumi, ngiye kuzirimisha ngo ndābe; ndakwinginze, uramvugira antunge." 
Luke14:20 Uwundi, ati Nārongoye, ni co kimbujije kuza." 
Luke14:21 Maze wa mushumba agarutse, abgira shebuja uko vyagenze. Nyen’ urugo araraka, abarira umushumba wiwe, ati Genda n’ingoga, uje mu nzira z’ibihamo no mu nzira nto‐nto zo mu gisagara, uzane hano aboro n’ibirema n’impumyi n’abacumbagira." 
Luke14:22 Umushumba wiwe, ati Mugenzi, ico umbariye ndagikoze, arikw imyanya iracasigaye." 
Luke14:23 Shebuja abarira uno mushumba wiwe, ati Genda uje mu nzira z’iroro no mu mihōra, ubagōbēre baze, kugira ngw inzu yanje yuzure." 
Luke14:24 Ndababgira yukw ata muntu n’umwe wo mur’ abo natumiye aza kugira ico atamira mu vyo nabateguriye. 
Luke14:25 Kand’ ishengero ryinshi ryari rijanye na we: arahindukira, arababgira," 
Luke14:26 at’ Umuntu ni yaza kuri jewe, ntiyanke se, na nyina, n’umugore wiwe, n’abana biwe, na bene nyina, na bashiki biwe, mbere n’amagara yiwe na yo, ntashobora kuba umwigishwa wanje." 
Luke14:27 Ūtikorera umusaraba wiwe ngw ankurikire, ntashobora kuba umwigishwa wanje." 
Luke14:28 Ni nde muri mwebge agomba kwubaka umutara w’amatafari muremure, ntiyobanza kwicara, akarimbura igitigiri c’amahera yowubaka, ngw amenye yukw afise ayowunonosora?" 
Luke14:29 Ngo kumbure yoba ahejeje kwubaka amatafari y’itanguriro, ntashobore kuwuzuza; ababibonye bose bagatangura kumutwenga," 
Luke14:30 bat’ Uyu yatanguye kwubaka, ntashobora kwuzuza." 
Luke14:31 Canke har’ umwami yoba agiye guhūra n’uwundi ngo barwane, ntiyobanza kwicara, akaja inama, ko yoshobora kujana ingabo ibihumbi cumi guhwana n’ūmuteye ari n’ingabo ibihumbi mirongwibiri?" 
Luke14:32 Bisanzwe atari ko biri, wa wundi akiri kure cane, amutumakw intumwa, akamubaza ico yomuhongera ngo babane amahoro." 
Luke14:33 Ni ko biri, umuntu wese muri mwebge adaheba ivy’ afise vyose ntashobora kuba umwigishwa wanje." 
Luke14:34 Umunyu ni mwiza; arik’ umunyu wo, woshira uburyohe, woba ukiryoshwa n’iki?" 
Luke14:35 Nta co umaze mu ndimiro canke mw icukiro: bapfa kuwuta. Ūri n’amatwi yumva ni yumve. 
Luke15:1 Abatozakori bose n’abanyavyaha bāriko baramwēgēra, ngo bamwumve." 
Luke15:2 Abafarisayo n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe barīdodomba, bat’ Uyo yiyegereza abanyavyaha, agasangira na bo." 
Luke15:3 Abacira uyu mugani," 
Luke15:4 ati Hogira umuntu muri mwebge afise intama ijana, yozimiza imwe muri zo, ntiyosiga izindi mirongwicenda n’icenda mu gahinga, akaja kurondera iyazimiye, kugeza ah’ ayibonera?" 
Luke15:5 Iy’ ayibonye, ayiterera ku bitugu anezerewe;" 
Luke15:6 yashika mu rugo, agahamagara incuti ziwe n’ababanyi biwe, akababgira, ati Tunezeranwe, kuko mbonye intama yanje yari yāzimiye." 
Luke15:7 Ndababgira yuko mw ijuru bazonezererwa bartyo umunyavyaha umwe yihannye, bakamurutisha abagororotsi mirongwicenda n’icenda batarinda kwihana." 
Luke15:8 Cank’ umugore yogira amahera cumi, akabura rimwe, ntiyodomeka itara, agakubura inzu, akarondera ashishikaye kugeza ah’ aribonera?" 
Luke15:9 Iy’ aribonye, ahamagara incuti ziwe n’ababanyi biwe, akababgira, ati Tunezeranwe, kuko mbonye ihera nari nājimije." 
Luke15:10 Ndababgire, Uko ni ko haba umunezero imbere y’abamarayika b’Imana kubg’ umunyavyaha umwe yihannye." 
Luke15:11 Kand’ arababgira, ati Hābaye umuntu yar’ afise abahungu babiri." 
Luke15:12 Umuhererezi abgira se, ati Data, mpa umugabane w’ibintu notwaye. Abagaburira itunga ryiwe." 
Luke15:13 Imisi mike ishize, umuhererezi akoranya ibintu vyiwe vyose, aragenda, aja mu kindi gihugu ca kure; ashitseyo yayisha ibintu vyiwe ubuhumbu." 
Luke15:14 Abimaze vyose, ikigoyi gikomeye gitera mur’ ico gihugu, atangura gufutana." 
Luke15:15 Aragenda, ashumba ku muntu wo mur’ ico gihugu, amurungika ku gasozi kiwe kuragira ingurube." 
Luke15:16 Yifuza guhāzwa n’ibishishwa ingurube zārya, ntihāgira ūmunūtsa." 
Luke15:17 Yisubiyemwo, aribgira, at’ Abacangero ba data bangana kuriya, kandi bahāzwa n’ivyo kurya bakabisigaza, nanje jeho inzara irikw iranyicira hano." 
Luke15:18 Mve hasi, nje kwa data, mmubgire, nti Data, nacumuye ku Yo mw ijuru no mu maso yawe," 
Luke15:19 singikwiye kwitwa umwana wawe: pfuma ungira umucangero wawe. 
Luke15:20 Ava hasi, aja kwa se. Se amubona akiri kure, amutera akagongwe, arirukanga, amugwa mw izosi, aramugumbira." 
Luke15:21 Wa muhungu aramubgira, ati Data, nacumuye ku Yo mw ijuru no mu maso yawe, singikwiye kwitwa umwana wawe." 
Luke15:22 Maze se abarira abashumba biwe, ati Ni muzane n’ingoga imvune iruta izindi, muyimwambike, mumwambike n’impeta ku rutoke n’inkweto mu birenge," 
Luke15:23 muzane ya shūri inuze, muyibāge, turye tunezerwe:" 
Luke15:24 kuk’ uyu mwana wanje yari yarapfuye, non’ arazutse; yari yarahavye, non’ arahabutse. Nuko batangura kunezerwa." 
Luke15:25 Arik’ umwana wiwe w’imfura yari mu ndimiro; arikw araza, agira ashike ku nzu, yumva inanga n’imihamirizo." 
Luke15:26 Ahamagara umwe mu bashumba, amubaza ibibaye ivy’ ari vyo." 
Luke15:27 Aramwishura, ati Murumunāwe yaje, so yamubāgiye ya shūri inuze, kukw amubonye agikomeye." 
Luke15:28 Araraka, yanka kwinjira: se arasohoka, aramwinginga." 
Luke15:29 Maz’ abgira se, ati Rāba iyi myaka ingana irtya ngukorera, nta ho nigeze kwanka ico wangezeko, nanje nta ho wigeze kumpa n’agasuguru, ngo nnezeranwe n’abagenzi." 
Luke15:30 Maz’ uyo mwana wawe aje, yakomvye ivyawe abisambanisha, umubāgira ishūri inuze." 
Luke15:31 Na we aramubgira, ati Mwana wanje, tubana imisi yose, kand’ ivyanje vyose n’ivyawe:" 
Luke15:32 arikw akanyamuneza no guhimbarwa biratubereye: kuko murumunāwe uyu yari yarapfuye, non’ arazutse; yari yarahavye, non’ arahabutse." 
Luke16:1 Maz’ abgira abigishwa biwe, ati Hābaye umuntu w’umutunzi yar’ afise umubgiriza wiwe, bamumuregako ko yaya ibintu vyiwe." 
Luke16:2 Aramuhamagaza, aramubaza, at’ Ivyo nkwumvako n’ibiki? Harūra igitigiri c’ivyo wabīkijwe, kuk’ utagikwiye kuba umubgiriza wanje." 
Luke16:3 Uwo mubgiriza aribaza, ati Mbe ngira nte, ko databuja agira ansohore mu bubgiriza bganje? Sinshobora kurima, binteye isoni ko nosēgerereza." 
Luke16:4 Ndazi ico nkora, ngo ni nasohorwa mu bubgiriza baze bantunge mbe mu ngo zabo." 
Luke16:5 Ahamagara abāri n’imyenda ya shebuja bose umwe‐umwe, abaza uwa mbere, ati Harya databuja umufitiye ibingana iki?" 
Luke16:6 Aramwishura, at’ Ingero ijana z’amavuta ya elayo. Na we at’ Abīra icete cawe, wicare vuba, wandike mirongwitanu." 
Luke16:7 Kand’ abaza uwundi, ati Harya weho umufitiye ibingana iki? Aramwishura, at’ Ingero ijana z’ingano. Aramubarira, at’ Abīra icete cawe, wandike mirongumunani." 
Luke16:8 Nuko shebuja ashima uwo mubgiriza agabitanya, kuko yakoze ivy’ ubgenge: kukw abana b’iki gihe bagira ubgenge mu vy’ubu bugingo kurusha abana b’umuco." 
Luke16:9 Nanje ndababgire, Itunga ribi muryironkeshereze incuti, ngo ni ryabura baze babatunge mube muri za ngo zitazoshira." 
Luke16:10 Ūkora ivyo yizigiweko ku coroshe cane, agira artyo no ku gikomeye: ūgabitanya ku coroshe cane, agabitanya no ku gikomeye." 
Luke16:11 Namba mutabaye abizigirwa kw itunga ribi mubīkijwe, ni nde azobabītsa itunga nyaryo?" 
Luke16:12 Kandi namba mudakora ivyo mwizigiweko ku vy’ abandi mwabīkijwe, ni nde azobaha ivyo mwokwiganzira?" 
Luke16:13 Nta muntu asaba abami babiri; yokwanka umwe, agakunda uwundi, canke yoguma kur’ umwe, akagaya wa wundi. Ntimushobora gusaba Imana n’Itunga." 
Luke16:14 Abafarisayo, bār’ abakunzi b’ubutunzi, bumvise ivyo vyose, baramutwenga cane." 
Luke16:15 Arababgira, ati Mwebge mugomba kwiyerekana nk’abagororotse mu maso y’abantu, arikw Imana irazi imitima yanyu: kukw igishizwe hejuru mu bantu ar’ igisesema mu nyonga z’Imana." 
Luke16:16 Ivyagezwe, bo n’amajambo y’abāvugishwa n’Imana, vyabayeho gushitsa igihe ca Yohana: uhereye ico gihe ubutumwa bgiza bg’ubgami bg’Imana ni ho bgavugiwe, umuntu wese akabubandanira." 
Luke16:17 Icoroshe n’ukw ijuru n’isi vyovaho, hakw akazatsa na kamwe kova ku nyuguti imwe yo mu vyagezwe." 
Luke16:18 Umuntu wese yirukana umugore wiwe, akābīra uwundi, aba asambanye; kandi n’uwābīra umugore yahukanye n’umugabo wiwe aba asambanye." 
Luke16:19 Hābaye umuntu w’umutunzi yambara impuzu z’inyambarabami n’izera nziza, yama adibamye mu vyiza imisi yose." 
Luke16:20 Kandi hāriho n’umworo yitwa Lazaro, yatembagara kw irembo ryiwe yatonyanga ibisebe." 
Luke16:21 Yifuza guhāzwa n’udukorokera musi y’ameza y’uno mutunzi; kand’ imbga na zo zāraza zikamurigata ibisebe. 
Luke16:22 Hanyuma rero wa mworo arapfa, abamarayika bamujana mu gikiriza ca Aburahamu: na nya mutunzi arapfa, arahambga." 
Luke16:23 Ar’i kuzimu, ararangamiza, ababazwa cane, abona Aburahamu ari kure, na Lazaro ari mu gikiriza ciwe." 
Luke16:24 Aratabaza, ati Aburahamu muvyeyi, ngirira ikigongwe, rungika Lazaro, akoze isonga y’urutoke mu mazi, ampfuvye ururimi, kuko nsesererejwe mur’ uru rubeya." 
Luke16:25 Aburahamu aramubgira, ati Mwana wanje, ibuka yuko wahawe ivyiza vyawe ukiriho, Lazaro na we yahawe ibibi: non’ amariwe imibabaro hano, nawe uraseserezwa." 
Luke16:26 Mber’ ukūye n’ivyo, hagati yacu namwe harih’ imanga ihambaye yashizweho kugira ngo ni hagira abagomba kuva ino bakaja aho muri ntibabishobore, kandi ngo ntibave iyo ngo bashike aho turi." 
Luke16:27 Na we ati Ndakwinginze se muvyeyi, umurungike mu rugo kwa data," 
Luke16:28 kuko mfise bene mama batanu; ababgire uko bimeze, ngo na bo ntibaze baze hano hantu ho kubabarizwa." 
Luke16:29 Aburahamu aramubgira, ati Bafise ivya Mose n’ivy’ abāvugishwa n’Imana, ni babumvire." 
Luke16:30 Na we at’ Oyaye, Aburahamu muvyeyi, ariko ni hājayo ūvuye mu bāpfuye, bazokwihana." 
Luke16:31 Aramubgira, ati Ni batumvira Mose n’abāvugishwa n’Imana, ntibokwemera nah’ umuntu yozuka mu bāpfuye." 
Luke17:1 Kand’ abgira abigishwa biwe, at’ Ibitsitaza abantu ntibizobura kuza, arik’ ūbizana azobona ibara." 
Luke17:2 Ivyoba vyiza n’uko yohambīrirwa urusyo ruremereye kw izosi, agatererwa mu kiyaga, hakw atsitaza n’umwe mur’ aba bato." 
Luke17:3 Mwirinde; mugenzawe ni yakora icaha, umuhanūre; ni yihana, umuharire." 
Luke17:4 Kandi ni yakugirira nabi indwi ku musi umwe, agahindukira ibihetangabo ndwi, akubgira, ati Ndihannye; uz’ ubimuharire." 
Luke17:5 Kandi za ntumwa zibgira Umwami Yesu, ziti N’utwongere ukwizera." 
Luke17:6 Umwami arabishura, ati Namba mufise ukwizera kungana n’akabuto ka sinapi, mwobarira iki giti c’umusukamino, muti Randuka, ubadikwe mu kiyaga, kandi cobumvira." 
Luke17:7 Ariko ni nde muri mwebge afise umugurano amurimira cank’ amuragirira intama, iyo yinjiye avuye ku kivi canke kuragira, mbega yomubarira, ati Ngwino n’ingoga wicare urye?" 
Luke17:8 Ariko ntiyomubarira, at’ Arura ivyo kurya vyanje, ukenyere, ungaburire, gushitsa aho mpereza kurya no kunywa, nawe hanyuma ubone kurya no kunywa?" 
Luke17:9 Mbeg’ akengurukira uwo mugurano kuko yakoze ivyo yamugezeko? 
Luke17:10 Abe ari ko namwe mugira, ni mwaheza gukora ivyo mwagezweko vyose, muvuge, muti Tur’ abagurano b’imburakimazi, twakoze ivyo dukwiye gukora gusa." 
Luke17:11 Maze bari mu nzira baja i Yerusalemu, aca hagati y’i Samariya n’i Galilaya." 
Luke17:12 Ashitse mu mihana, asanganirwa n’abanyamibembe cumi, bahagarara kure," 
Luke17:13 baratabaza cane, bati Yesu, Mwigisha, tugirire imbabazi." 
Luke17:14 Ababonye arababgira, ati Ni mugende, mwiyereke abaherezi. Bariko baragenda barakira, barahumanuka." 
Luke17:15 Umwe muri bo, abonye akize, agaruka ahimbaza Imana n’ijwi rirenga;" 
Luke17:16 yikubita imbere y’ibirenge vyiwe, aramushima: kand’ uwo yar’ Umusamariya." 
Luke17:17 Yesu arabaza, ati Ntibahumanutse bose ukw ar’ icumi? Abandi cenda bari hehe?" 
Luke17:18 Nta bandi babonetse ngo bagaruke guhimbaza Imana, atar’ uyu munyamahanga?" 
Luke17:19 Kand’ aramubarira, ati Va hasi, ugende; ukwizera kwawe kuragukijije." 
Luke17:20 Abafarisayo bamubajije igihe ubgami bg’Imana buzozira, arabishura, at’ Ubgami bg’Imana ntibuzoza bgerekanwa," 
Luke17:21 kandi ntibazovuga, bat’ Ehe ngubu: canke bati Nguburiya; kuk’ ubgami bg’Imana buri muri mwebge." 
Luke17:22 Abgira abigishwa biwe, ati Hazoza imisi muzokwifurizamwo kubona umusi umwe musa w’Umwana w’umuntu, ntimuzowubona." 
Luke17:23 Kandi bazobabgira, bat’ Ehe nguriya: canke bat’ Ehe nguyu. Ntimuze mujeyo, kandi ntimubakurikire." 
Luke17:24 Kuko nk’uk’ umuravyo urabiriza mu ruhande rumwe rw’ijuru, ukarabagiranira mu rundi, uko ni k’Umwana w’umuntu azoba ku musi wiwe." 
Luke17:25 Arikw akwiye kuzobanza kubabazwa uburyo bginshi no kwankwa n’ab’ iki gihe. 
Luke17:26 Kand’ uko vyari biri mu misi ya Nowa, ni ko bizoba mu misi y’Umwana w’umuntu:" 
Luke17:27 bārarya, bāranywa, bārarongora, bārashingira, bageza kuri wa musi Nowa yinjiye muri bga bgato, umwuzure ukaza ukabahonnya bose." 
Luke17:28 No mu misi ya Loti vyabaye birtyo: bārarya, bāranywa, bāradandaza, bāragura, bāratera, bārubaka;" 
Luke17:29 maz’ umusi Loti yaviriye i Sodomu, umuriro n’amazuku biratibuka bivuye mw ijuru, birabahonnya bose." 
Luke17:30 Ni ko bizoba, umusi Umwana w’umuntu azoserukirako." 
Luke17:31 Uwo musi, ūzoba ari hejuru ku nzu, ibintu vyiwe biri mu nzu, ntaze yururutswe no kubisahura, n’ūri mu mirima n’uko, ntaz’ asubire inyuma." 
Luke17:32 Mwibuke muka Loti. 
Luke17:33 Ūzogerageza gukiza ubugingo bgiwe azobubura; arik’ ūzoheba ubugingo bgiwe azoburokora. 
Luke17:34 Ndababgire, Mur’ iryo joro abantu babiri bazoba ku buriri bumwe, umwe azojanwa, uwundi arekwe;" 
Luke17:35 ah’ abagore babiri bazoba bariko barasēra hamwe, umwe azojanwa, uwundi arekwe; [" 
Luke17:36 aho babiri bazoba mu mirima, umwe azojanwa, uwundi arekwe.]" 
Luke17:37 Baramubaza, bati Bizoba hehe ga Mushingantahe? Arabishura, at’ Ah’ umuvyimba uri hose, ni ho ibinyakabaka bizokoranira." 
Luke18:1 Abacira umugani wo kubigisha ko bakwiye guhora basenga, ntibarambirwe," 
Luke18:2 arababgira, ati Mu gisagara habaye umucamanza, adatinya Imana, ntagire udusoni ku bantu." 
Luke18:3 Mur’ ico gisagara hār’ umupfakazi, aza kuri we kenshi, aramubarira, ati Ncira urubanza runkiza umwansi wanje." 
Luke18:4 Amara imisi atemera, ariko hanyuma aribgira, ati Naho ntatinya Imana, kandi singire isoni z’abantu," 
Luke18:5 ariko kuk’ uwo mupfakazi angoye, ndamucira urubanza rumukiza, ngo ntiyame aza imisi yose, akanzigiriza." 
Luke18:6 Kand’ Umwami Yesu aravuga, ati Ni mwumve ivyo uyo mucamanza agabitanya yavuze." 
Luke18:7 None mbeg’ Imana ntizocira abo yatoranije urubanza rubakiza, bayiborogera ku murango no mw ijoro, nah’ ibatevya?" 
Luke18:8 Ndababgira yukw izorubacira vuba. Arik’ Umwana w’umuntu ni yaza, mbeg’ azosanga ukwizera mw isi?" 
Luke18:9 Uyu mugani na wo awucira abiyizigira ubgabo ko bagororotse, bagakēngēra abandi bose." 
Luke18:10 At’ Abantu babiri bādūze baja mu rusengero gusenga, umwe yar’ Umufarisayo, uwundi yar’ umutozakori." 
Luke18:11 Umufarisayo ahagaze asengera ku mutima wiwe, ati Mana, ndagushimye yuko ntameze nk’abandi bose, abanyazi, cank’ abagabitanya, cank’ abasambanyi, canke n’abameze nk’urya mutozakori." 
Luke18:12 Mu misi ndwi yose nisonzesha kabiri, ntanga ikigiracumi c’ivyo ndonka vyose." 
Luke18:13 Ariko wa mutozakori, ahagaze kure, ntiyagomba no kurangamiza ngw arābe mw ijuru, arikw arishishitira, ati Mana, ngirira ikigongwe, nd’ umunyavyaha." 
Luke18:14 Ndababgire, Uwo muntu yamanutse aja i we, atsindanishirijwe kuruta wa wundi; kuk’ uwishira hejuru wese azocishwa bugufi, arik’ uwicisha bugufi azoshirwa hejuru." 
Luke18:15 Maze bamuzanira abana babo b’inzoya ngw abakoreko: abigishwa babibonye barabakankamira. 
Luke18:16 Maze Yesu arabahamagara, ati Ni mureke abana bato baze aho ndi, ntimubabuze: kuk’ ubgami bg’Imana ar’ubg’ abameze bartyo." 
Luke18:17 Ndababgire ukuri: Ūtazokwākīra ubgami bg’Imana nk’umwana muto ntazobginjiramwo na gatoya. 
Luke18:18 Umukuru w’isinagogi aramubaza, ati Mwigisha mwiza, nkore iki, ngo nze ndagwe ubugingo budashira?" 
Luke18:19 Yesu aramubaza, at’ Unyitira iki mwiza? Nta mwiza atar’ umwe, ni we Mana." 
Luke18:20 K’uzi ivyagezwe, ngo Ntugasambane, ntukice, ntukibe, ntukāgirize abandi ibinyoma, wubahe so na nyoko." 
Luke18:21 Aramubgira, at’ Ivyo vyose naravyitondeye, mpereye mu buto bganje." 
Luke18:22 Yesu avyumvise aramubgira, ati Na non’ uhajije kimwe; shōra ivy’ ufise vyose, ugabire aboro, ni ho uzogira itunga mw ijuru, utek’ uze, unkurikire." 
Luke18:23 Maze yumvise ivyo, arababara cane, kuko yar’ umutunzi cane." 
Luke18:24 Yesu amwitegereje aravuga, at’ Erega biragoye kw aba vyinshi binjira mu bgami bg’Imana!" 
Luke18:25 Kukw icoroshe ar’ ingamiya guca mu zuru ry’urushinge biruta umutunzi ko yinjira mu bgami bg’Imana. 
Luke18:26 Abavyumvise baravuga, bati None rero, ni nde ashobora gukizwa?" 
Luke18:27 Maz’ arababgira, at’ Ibidashobokera abantu bishobokera Imana." 
Luke18:28 Petero aravuga, ati Rāba, twebge twaretse ivyacu, turagukurikira." 
Luke18:29 Arababgira, ati Ndababgire ukuri, Nta waretse inzu, cank’ umugore, canke bene nyina, cank’ abavyeyi, cank’ abana, kubg’ ubgami bg’Imana," 
Luke18:30 atazobishumbushwa umurengera mur’ iki gihe, no mu gihe kizoza atazohabga ubugingo budashira." 
Luke18:31 Yihererana bamwe cumi na babiri, arababgira, at’ Ehe turadūze i Yerusalemu, kand’ ivyanditswe n’abāvugishwa n’Imana vyose bizoshika ku Mwana w’umuntu." 
Luke18:32 Azoshirwa mu maboko y’abanyamahanga, ashinyagurirwe, ateterezwe, avumwe amate;" 
Luke18:33 kandi bazomutonagura, bamwice, ku musi ugira gatatu azozuka." 
Luke18:34 Ntibāgira ico batahura mur’ ivyo, kand’ iryo jambo bāri barihishijwe, ntibāmenya ivyo babgiwe." 
Luke18:35 Ageze hafi y’i Yeriko, hār’ impumyi yicaye i ruhande y’inzira, isēgerereza." 
Luke18:36 Yumvise ishengero rihita, ibaza ivy’ ari vyo." 
Luke18:37 Barayibgira, bati Ni Yesu Umunyanazareti ahita." 
Luke18:38 Irasemerera, iti Yesu, mwana wa Dawidi, ngirira imbabazi." 
Luke18:39 Abagiye imbere barayizibiranya ngw ihore: arikw irushiriza cane gutakamba, iti Mwana wa Dawidi, ngirira imbabazi." 
Luke18:40 Yesu arahagarara, avuga ko bayimuzanira: ishitse hafi, arayibaza," 
Luke18:41 at’ Ugomba ko ngukorera iki? Iramwishura, iti Ndagomba guhumūka, Mwami wanje." 
Luke18:42 Yesu arayibgira, ati Humūka, ukwizera kwawe kuragukijije." 
Luke18:43 Aca ahumūka buno nyene, amukurikira ahimbaza Imana: abantu bose babibonye bashima Imana." 
Luke19:1 Ashika i Yeriko, arikw arahaca." 
Luke19:2 Hār’ umuntu yitwa Zakayo, yar’ umutozakori mukuru, kandi yar’ umutunzi." 
Luke19:3 Ageza kurāba Yesu, ngw amenye ukw asa, bimwankira kubg’ ishengero, kuko yari mugufi." 
Luke19:4 Arirukanga, aja imbere, yūrira igiti citwa umusukomora ngw amurābe, kuko yagira ace mur’ iyo nzira." 
Luke19:5 Yesu ahashitse, ararangamiza, aramubarira, ati Zakayo, ururuka vuba, kuk’ uyu musi nkwiye kurāra i wawe." 
Luke19:6 Yururuka vuba, amwākīrana akanyamuneza." 
Luke19:7 Babibonye, bose baridodomba, bati Ko yinjiye kurārira umuntu w’umunyavyaha!" 
Luke19:8 Zakayo arahagarara, abgira Umwami Yesu, ati Rāba Mugenzi, umugabane w’itunga ryanje ngira ndawuhe aboro; kand’ umuntu wese nagunze ndabimurihe kane." 
Luke19:9 Yesu amuvugako, at’ Uyu musi agakiza gashitse mur’ iyi nzu, kuk’ uyu na we ar’ umwana wa Aburahamu." 
Luke19:10 Kand’ Umwana w’umuntu yazanywe no kurondera no gukiza icari cazimiye. 
Luke19:11 Bakiriko barumva ivyo, avyongerak’ umugani, kuko yari hafi y’i Yerusalemu, kandi kuko biyumvira yuk’ ubgami bg’Imana bugira buboneke uwo mwanya;" 
Luke19:12 nukw aravuga, ati Hābaye umuganwa yagiye mu gihugu ca kure kwimikirwayo, ngw agaruke." 
Luke19:13 Ahamagara icumi bo mu bishikira biwe, abaha amahera cumi yitwa mina, arababarira, ati Muyacuruze, mugeze aho nzozira." 
Luke19:14 Arikw abantu biwe bāramwanka, bamukurikiza intumwa, bat’ Uyo ntitugomba kw atuganza." 
Luke19:15 Agarutse, amaze kwimikwa, ahamagaza ba bishikira yasigaranye ya mahera, ngw amenye inyungu umuntu wese yungutsemwo mu kuyacuruza." 
Luke19:16 Uwa mbere arengutse, aravuga, ati Mugenzi, mina yawe yungutsemw’ izindi mina cumi." 
Luke19:17 Aramubgira, ati Wagize neza, muntu wanje mwiza, ko wabaye umwizigirwa no kuri gito cane, n’ube umutware w’ibisagara cumi." 
Luke19:18 Uwa kabiri arengutse, aravuga, ati Mugenzi, mina yawe yungutsemw’ izindi mina zitanu." 
Luke19:19 Uwo na we aramubarira, ati Nawe twara ibisagara bitanu." 
Luke19:20 Uwundi arengutse, aravuga, ati Mugenzi, ngiyi mina yawe, nabītse itekeye mu kiremo:" 
Luke19:21 kuko nagutinye k’ur’ umuntu w’umuhambazi, uterura ivyo utāhateretse, wimbura ivyo utārimye." 
Luke19:22 Aramubgira, ati Ndagucira urubanza ku vyakuvuye mu kanwa, wa muntu wanje mubi we. Ko war’ uzi yuko nd’ umuntu w’umuhambazi, nterura ivyo ntāhateretse, nimbura ivyo ntārimye:" 
Luke19:23 none se n’iki cakubujije guha abacurūza amahera yanje, nanje nagaruka nkayakwaka n’inyungu yayo?" 
Luke19:24 Abarira abahagazeho, ati Ni mumwake ya mina, muyihe ūfise mina cumi." 
Luke19:25 Baramubgira, bati Mugenzi, mbega kw afise icumi!" 
Luke19:26 Ndababgire, Ūfise wese azohabga, arik’ ūdafise azokwakwa n’ico yar’ afise." 
Luke19:27 Arikw abo bansi banje batākunze ko mbaganza ni mubazane hano, mubīcire imbere yanje." 
Luke19:28 Yesu ahejeje kuvuga ivyo, aja imbere, adūga aja i Yerusalemu." 
Luke19:29 Ageze hafi y’i Betifage n’i Betaniya, ku musozi witwa Elayono, atuma babiri bo mu bigishwa," 
Luke19:30 arababarira, ati Muje mur’ iriya mihana ir’ imbere yanyu, ni mwayishikamwo, murabona inyana y’indogoba iziritse, ata muntu yigeze kuyigenderako: muyiziture muyizane." 
Luke19:31 Kandi ni hāgira ūbabaza, ati N’iki gitumye muyizitura? mumwishure, muti Databuja ni we ayigomba." 
Luke19:32 Abātumwe baragenda, babisanga uko yabibabgiye." 
Luke19:33 Bariko barazitura ya nyana y’indogoba, bene yo barababaza, bati Ko muzitura iyo nyana n’iki?" 
Luke19:34 Barabishura, bati Databuja ni we ayigomba." 
Luke19:35 Bayizanira Yesu, bayishirakw impuzu zabo, bayiterekako Yesu." 
Luke19:36 Arikw aragenda, basasa impuzu zabo mu nzira." 
Luke19:37 Agira ashike, ageze ku kamanuko k’umusozi wa Elayono, ishengero ryose ry’abigishwa ritangura kunezerwa no guhimbaza Imana n’ijwi rirenga, bayishimira ibitangaza babonye vyose," 
Luke19:38 bati Hashemezwe Umwami, aje mw izina ry’Uhoraho, Amahoro abe mw ijuru, Icubahiro kibe ahasumba ijuru." 
Luke19:39 Abafarisayo bamwe bo mw ishengero baramubarira, bati Mwigisha, zibiza abigishwa bawe." 
Luke19:40 Arabishura, ati Ndababgire, Aba ni bahora, amabuye arasemerera." 
Luke19:41 Ashitse hafi, abona igisagara, arakiririra," 
Luke19:42 at’ Uyu musi iy’ umenya ivy’ amahoro! Ariko none bihishijwe amaso yawe. 
Luke19:43 Kukw imisi izokuzako, ah’ abansi bawe bazokurundira ikirundo c’ivu kigukikije, na bo ubgabo bakagukikiza, bakakwugariza impande zose," 
Luke19:44 bakagukekana n’abana bawe bo muri wewe; kandi ntibazogusigariza ibuye na rimwe rigeretse ku rindi, kuk’ utāmenye igihe wagendewemwo." 
Luke19:45 Yinjira mu rusengero, atangura guhindira hanze abārudandarizamwo," 
Luke19:46 arababgira, ati Vyanditswe, ngw Ingoro yanje izoba inzu yo gusengeramwo; ariko mwebge mwayihinduye nk’isenga ry’abambuzi." 
Luke19:47 Kandi yigishiriza mu rusengero imisi yose. Arikw abaherezi bakuru n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe n’abantu bakuru‐bakuru bo mur’ ubgo bgoko barondera ingene bomwica," 
Luke19:48 babura uko bamugira; kukw abantu bose bāri bamumaseko, bamwumva." 
Luke20:1 Umusi ur’ izina, yigishiriza abantu mu rusengero, avuga ubutumwa bgiza, abaherezi bakuru n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe bazanana kuri we n’abashingantahe:" 
Luke20:2 baramubaza, bati Tubgire, n’ububasha ki bugutera gukora ivyo, canke ni nde yaguhaye ubgo bubasha?" 
Luke20:3 Arabishura, ati Nanje hinge ndababaze ijambo, mumbgire:" 
Luke20:4 non’ ukubatiza kwa Yohana kwāturutse mw ijuru, canke se mu bantu?" 
Luke20:5 Bībūranya muri bo, bati Ni twavuga tuti Ni mw ijuru; ahava atubaza, ati N’iki cababujije kumwemera?" 
Luke20:6 Ariko ni twavuga tuti Ni mu bantu, abantu bose baradutera amabuye, kuko bemeye badakekeranya yuko Yohana yavugishwa n’Imana." 
Luke20:7 Bamwishura yuko batazi aho kwavuye. 
Luke20:8 Yesu arababgira, ati Nuko rero nanje simbabgira ububasha bunkoresha ivyo." 
Luke20:9 Atangura gucira abantu uyu mugani, ati Hābaye umuntu yateye uruzabibu, arusigarana abarimyi, aja mu mahanga, amaray’ igihe kirekire." 
Luke20:10 Igihe c’iyera kigeze, atuma umukozi kuri ba barimyi, ngo bamwamurire inzabibu z’uruzabibu: abo barimyi baramushishagura, bamurungika gusa." 
Luke20:11 Yongera gutuma uwundi mukozi; uwo na we baramushishagura, baramutetereza, bamurungika gusa." 
Luke20:12 Atuma n’uwa gatatu; uwo na we baramukomeretsa, baramuhinda." 
Luke20:13 Nyen’ uruzabibu aribaza, ati Ngire nte? Ndatuma umwana wanje nkunda, kumbure bazomusonera." 
Luke20:14 Arikw abo barimyi bamubonye baja inama, bat’ Urya ni we samuragwa; tumwice, kugira ng’ umwandu uz’ ube uwacu." 
Luke20:15 Bamuhindira inyuma y’uruzabibu, baramwica. None nyen’ uruzabibu azobagira ate?" 
Luke20:16 Azoza yice rubi abo barimyi, uruzabibu arusigarane abandi. Bavyumvise baravuga, bati Biragahera." 
Luke20:17 Arabitegereza, arababaza, ati None rer’ aya majambo yanditswe n’amaki, ngw Ibuye abubatsi bāgaye, Ni ryo ryahindutse irigumya imfuruka?" 
Luke20:18 Ūzogwa kur’ iryo buye wese azovunagurika, arik’ uwo rizogwako wese rizomuvungura." 
Luke20:19 Abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe bo n’abaherezi bakuru ako kanya barondera ingene bomushōrerakw amaboko, ariko batinya abantu: kuko bamenye yukw ari bo yaciyek’ uwo mugani." 
Luke20:20 Baramugenza, batuma abo kumudaha bīgira intungane, ngo bakūre urwitwazo mu vyo avuga, bamushīre segaba nyen’ ububasha, ari we cēgēra ca Kayisari." 
Luke20:21 Baramubaza, bati Mwigisha, turazi yuk’ uvuga kandi wigisha neza, kandi k’udatinya ijunja ry’abantu, ariko ko wigisha inzira y’Imana vy’ukuri:" 
Luke20:22 mbega biremerwa ko dutanga ikori rya Kayisari, canke ntivyemerwa?" 
Luke20:23 Maz’ amenya ubugunge bgabo, arababgira," 
Luke20:24 ati Ni munyereke idenariyo; igishushanyo n’ivyanditswe kuri yo n’ivya nde? Bati N’ivya Kayisari. 
Luke20:25 Arababarira, ati Nuko rer’ ivya Kayisari ni mubihe Kayisari, ivy’ Imana mubihe Imana." 
Luke20:26 Ntibāshobora gukūra urwitwazo mur’ ayo majambo imbere y’abantu, batangazwa n’ivyo abishuye, barahora." 
Luke20:27 Abasadukayo bamwe baza kuri we, ni bo bahakana yukw ata kuzuka kuriho, baramubaza," 
Luke20:28 bati Mwigisha, Mose yatwandikiye yuko mwene nyina w’umuntu ni yapfa ar’ imponnyi, agasiga umugore, mwene nyina akwiye gucūra uwo mugore, ngw ahonore mwene nyina." 
Luke20:29 Nuko rero hābaye abavukana ndwi: uwa mbere arongora umugore, apfa ar’ imponnyi:" 
Luke20:30 uwa kabiri aramucūra," 
Luke20:31 n’uwa gatatu nyene, nuko bose ukw ar’indwi baramucūra, bapfa badasize impfuvyi." 
Luke20:32 Hanyuma na wa mugore arapfa. 
Luke20:33 None mw izuka azoba muka nde muri bo? Ko bāri bamufise bose ukw ar’indwi! 
Luke20:34 Yesu arabishura, at’ Ab’ iyi si bararongora, kandi barashingirwa," 
Luke20:35 arikw abemerewe gushika muri ya si yindi no kuzuka mu bapfuye ntibarongora kandi ntibashingirwa; 
Luke20:36 kandi ntibaba bagishobora gupfa, kuko baringaniye n’abamarayika, kand’ ar’ abana b’Imana, kukw ar’ abana b’ukuzuka." 
Luke20:37 Arikw abāpfuye ko bazuka na Mose yabimenyekanishije hamwe havuga ivy’ Igisaka c’amahwa, aho yita Uhoraho Imana ya Aburahamu n’Imana ya Isaka n’Imana ya Yakobo." 
Luke20:38 Ereg’ Imana s’iy’ abāpfuye, ariko n’iy’ abariho: kuko kuri yo bose bariho." 
Luke20:39 Bamwe mu banyabgenge b’ivyanditswe baramwishura, bati Mwigisha, uvuze neza." 
Luke20:40 Ntibāba bacubahuka kumubaza irindi jambo. 
Luke20:41 Arababaza, ati Bavuga bate yuko Kristo ari mwene Dawidi?" 
Luke20:42 Ko Dawidi ubgiwe avuga mu gitabo ca Zaburi, at’ Uhoraho yabariye Umwami wanje, At’ Icara i buryo bganje," 
Luke20:43 Ushitse aho nzohindurira abansi bawe indava yo musi y’ibirenge vyawe. 
Luke20:44 Dawidi ko yamwise Umwami, non’ ashobora ate kuba umwana wiwe?" 
Luke20:45 Maz’ abarira abigishwa biwe, abantu bose bumva," 
Luke20:46 ati Mwirinde abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe, bakunda kugenda bambaye imvune, bagakunda kugirwako bgakeye mu tuguriro, no kwicara ku ntebe z’icubahiro mu masinagogi, n’ivyicaro vyo haruguru aho batumiwe." 
Luke20:47 Barya ingo z’abapfakazi, kandi basengesha menshi bahūmba; abo bazocirwa urubanza ruruta izindi." 
Luke21:1 Yunamura amaso, abona abatunzi bashikana, baterera amashikanwa yabo mu masandugu y’amahera." 
Luke21:2 Abona umupfakazi w’umworo ateramw’ amasenge abiri. 
Luke21:3 Arababgira, ati Ndababgire ukuri, Uyu mupfakazi w’umworo ashikanye ibirengeye ivy’ abandi bose:" 
Luke21:4 kukw abo bose batereye mu mashikanwa ku bibasāgutse, ariko we ku bgoro bgiwe ashikanye ibimutunze vyose." 
Luke21:5 Kandi bamwe bavuga urusengero, ingene rwasharijwe amabuye meza n’amashikanwa; arababgira," 
Luke21:6 at’ Ivyo mubona ivyo, mu misi izoza ntihazosigara ibuye rigeretse ku rindi ridasamburiwe hasi." 
Luke21:7 Baramubaza, bati Mwigisha, non’ ivyo bizobaho ryari? Ikimenyetso kizoba iki c’igihe ivyo bizogira bishike?" 
Luke21:8 Arababarira ati Mwirinde ntimuzimizwe: kuko benshi bazoza mw izina ryanje, bati Ndi we; kandi bat’ Igihe kiri hafi: ntimuze mubakurikire." 
Luke21:9 Kandi ni mwumva intambara n’imivurungano, ntimuze mucike ivutu; kukw ivyo bitazobura kubanza kubaho, arik’ umuhero ntuzoca ushika." 
Luke21:10 Maz’ arababgira, at’ Ihanga rizotera irindi hanga, n’ubgami buzotera ubundi bgami." 
Luke21:11 Kand’ isi izonyiganyiga cane henshi, kandi hamwe‐hamwe hazotera amapfa, hatere n’ikīza, habeho n’ibiteye ubgoba n’ibimenyetso bihambaye biva mw ijuru." 
Luke21:12 Arikw ivyo vyose bitarabaho bazobashōrerakw amaboko, babahame, babashengerane mu masinagogi, babashirishe mu mabohero, babashengeze ku bami no ku baganza, babahōra izina ryanje:" 
Luke21:13 bicike ikimenyetso kibere mwebge icabona. 
Luke21:14 Nukw ibi mubishirekw imitima, yuko mudakwiye kubanza kwiyumvira ivyo muzokwireguza:" 
Luke21:15 kukw ari jewe nzobaha ururimi n’ubgenge, ivyo ababarwanya bose batazoshobora gutsinda canke gutururuza." 
Luke21:16 Ariko muzoshengezwa n’abavyeyi banyu na bo, na bene nyoko n’incuti n’abakunzi, bamwe muri mwebge bazobicisha." 
Luke21:17 Muzoba mwanswe na bose babahōra izina ryanje. 
Luke21:18 Kandi ntihazohara agashatsi na kamwe ko mu mitwe yanyu. 
Luke21:19 Ukwihangana kwanyu ni kwo kuzotuma mukiza ubugingo bganyu. 
Luke21:20 Ariko ni mwabona i Yerusalemu hakikijwe n’ibitero, muze mumenye yuk’ ubuyobe bgaho bugira bushike." 
Luke21:21 Ico gihe abazoba bar’i Yudaya baze bahungire ku misozi miremire, kand’ abazoba bari hagati muri Yerusalemu baze bahasokoroke, kand’ abazoba bari mu misozi ntibaze baje i Yerusalemu." 
Luke21:22 Kukw iyo misi izoba iyo guhōra, kugira ngw ivyanditswe vyose bishike." 
Luke21:23 Mur’ iyo misi abazoba batwaye inda n’abonsa bazobona ibara; kuko hazoba umubabaro mwinshi mu gihugu, kand’ uburake buzoba kur’ ubu bgoko." 
Luke21:24 Bazokwicwa n’ubugi bg’inkota, bazojanwa mu mahanga yose ar’inyagano: kand’ i Yerusalemu hazosiribangwa n’abanyamahanga, kugeza ah’ ibihe vy’abanyamahanga bizoshirira." 
Luke21:25 Kandi hazoba ibimenyetso ku zuba no ku kwezi no ku nyenyeri, kandi no mw isi hazoba imibabaro mu mahanga, bazotegekanishwa n’ukubomborana kw’ikiyaga n’imipfunda;" 
Luke21:26 kand’ abantu bazogwishwa igihūmura n’ubgoba no kwitega ibigira bibe mw isi; kukw ivy’ inkomezi vyo mw ijuru bizonyiganyizwa. 
Luke21:27 Ni ho bazobona Umwana w’umuntu aje mu gicu, ari n’ububasha n’ubgiza bginshi." 
Luke21:28 Arikw ivyo ni vyatangura kubaho, muze murangamize, muraramike imitwe yanyu kuko gucungurwa kwanyu kuzoba kugira gushike." 
Luke21:29 Kand’ abacira umugani, ati Ni murābe umusukoni n’ibiti vyose." 
Luke21:30 Iyo bitoshe, murabibona, mukamenya ubganyu yukw agatāsi kari hafi:" 
Luke21:31 nuko namwe ni mwabona ivyo bibaye, muze mumenye yuk’ ubgami bg’Imana buri hafi." 
Luke21:32 Ndababgire ukuri: Ab’ iki gihe ntibazorangira, ivyo vyose bitarashika." 
Luke21:33 Ijuru n’isi bizorangira, arikw amajambo yanje nta co azoba." 
Luke21:34 Ariko mwirinde, kugira ngw imitima yanyu ntīremērwe no kudandahirwa no kuborerwa n’umwitwaririko w’ivy’ ubu bugingo, ng’uwo musi ntubazeko giturumbuka, nk’umutego:" 
Luke21:35 kukw ari k’uzoshika ku bantu bose bashagaje mw isi yose. 
Luke21:36 Mwame mugavye, musenge mu bihe vyose, kugira ngo muze mushobore guhunga ivyo vyose bigira bibeho, ngo muhagarare imbere y’Umwana w’umuntu." 
Luke21:37 Imisi yose Yesu yirirwa mu rusengero yigisha, ariko bgira, agasohoka, akaja kurāra ku musozi witwa Elayono." 
Luke21:38 Abantu bose bakazindukira kuri we mu rusengero kumwumva. 
Luke22:1 Imisi mikuru y’imitsima itambiwe, yitwa Pasika, yagira ishike." 
Luke22:2 Abaherezi bakuru n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe barondera uburyo bgo kumwica, kuko batinya abantu." 
Luke22:3 Satani yinjira muri Yuda ari we Isikaryota, yari mu gitigiri ca bamwe cumi na babiri." 
Luke22:4 Aragenda, aja inama n’abaherezi bakuru n’abakuru b’abashibamyi b’urusengero, y’uburyo bgo kumubaronkera." 
Luke22:5 Baranezerwa, basezerana kumuha amahera y’ifeza." 
Luke22:6 Na we aremera, arondera uburyo bgo kumubaronkera, ishengero ritariho." 
Luke22:7 Umusi w’imitsima itambiwe urashika, uwo bakwiye kubāgak’ umwagazi w’intama wa Pasika." 
Luke22:8 Atuma Petero na Yohana, arababarira, ati Ni mugende, mudutegurire ivya Pasika, kugira ngo turye." 
Luke22:9 Baramubaza, bat’ Ugomba ko tubitegurira hehe?" 
Luke22:10 Arabishura, at’ Umve, mumaze gushika mu gisagara, murahūra n’umugabo yikoreye umubindi w’amazi; mumukurikire mu rugo ajamwo." 
Luke22:11 Mubgire nyen’ urugo, mut’ Umwigisha agize ngw Indāro iri hehe, ah’ asangirira ivya Pasika n’abigishwa biwe?" 
Luke22:12 Na we arabereka icumba kinini co mu nzu yo hejuru gitunganijwe: abe ari co muteguriramwo. 
Luke22:13 Baragenda, babisanga uko yabibabariye: bategura ivya Pasika." 
Luke22:14 Igihe gishitse, aricara ngw arye, kand’ intumwa na zo zicarana na we." 
Luke22:15 Arababgira, ati Kwifuza nifuje cane gusangira namwe ivy’ iyi Pasika, ntarababazwa." 
Luke22:16 Ndababgire, Sinzokwongera kuyiryako, kugeza ah’ izoshikira mu bgami bg’Imana." 
Luke22:17 Yābīra igikombe, agishimira Imana, arababarira, ati Mwābīre iki, mugisangire:" 
Luke22:18 kuko mbabgira yuk’ uhereye none ntazokwongera kunywa ku nzabibu, kugeza ah’ ubgami bg’Imana buzozira." 
Luke22:19 Yābīra umutsima, awushimira Imana, arawumanyagura, arawubaha, arababgira, at’ Uyu n’umubiri wanje ubatangiwe: murakore murtya kugira ngo kibe icibutso canje." 
Luke22:20 N’igikombe akigenza artyo bahejeje kurya, arababgira, at’ Iki gikombe n’isezerano risha ryo mu maraso yanje, abaviriye." 
Luke22:21 Kandi rāba, ukuboko kw’ ūngura kuri kumwe nanje ku meza." 
Luke22:22 N’ukuri, Umwana w’umuntu aragenda, nk’uko vyashinzwe: arik’ uwo muntu amugura azobona ibara." 
Luke22:23 Batangura kubazanya, ngo ni nde muri bo agira akore ico kintu." 
Luke22:24 Maze havyuka impāri muri bo, z’uwo bagereranyako kw ar’ umukuru uw’ ari we." 
Luke22:25 Arababgira, at’ Abami b’amahanga bayatwaza amanyama, n’abafise ububasha bgo kuyaganza bitwa ba rutungaboro." 
Luke22:26 Ariko mwebge s’uko: mugab’ umukuru muri mwebge abe nk’umuto, n’ūganza abe nk’ūbakorera." 
Luke22:27 Umukuru ni nde, n’ūkorerwa, canke n’ūmukorera? Mbega s’ūkorerwa? Ariko jeho ndi hagati muri mwebge mmeze nk’ūbakorera." 
Luke22:28 Ni mwebge mwamanye nanje mu vyo nageragejwe. 
Luke22:29 Nanje mbabīkiye ubgami, nk’uko Data yabumbīkiye," 
Luke22:30 ngo muze murīre, munywere ku meza yanje mu bgami bganje: kandi muzokwicara ku ntebe z’icubahiro, mucire imanza imiryango y’Abisirayeli, ukw ar’icumi n’ibiri." 
Luke22:31 Ati Simoni, Simoni, rāba Satani yabasavye ngw abagosore nk’ingano;" 
Luke22:32 ariko wewe nagusengeye ng’ukwizera kwawe ntiguhere. Nawe ni wamara guhinduka, uz’ uremeshe bagenzi bawe." 
Luke22:33 Aramubgira, ati Mugenzi, niteguye kujana nawe no mw ibohero no mu rupfu." 
Luke22:34 Aramubgira, ati Petero, ndakubgire, Inkoko itarabika uyu musi, uhava unyihakana gatatu ngo ntunzi." 
Luke22:35 Kand’ arababaza, ati Hamwe nabatuma mudafise umupfuko w’amahera cank’ isaho cank’ inkweto, har’ ico mwabuze? Baramwishura, bati Nta co twabuze." 
Luke22:36 Arababgira, at’ Ariko noneho, ūfise umupfuko w’amahera awujane, n’ūfise isaho ayijane; kand’ ūdafise inkota, ashōre impuzu yiwe ayigure." 
Luke22:37 Ndababgire, Ibi vyanditswe bikwiye kunshikako, ngo Yaharūranywe n’abanyabicumuro. Kukw ivyanje bigira bishike." 
Luke22:38 Baramubgira, bati Mushingantahe, ehe, ngizi inkota zibiri. Arababgira, ati Ziramaze." 
Luke22:39 Arasohoka, aja ku musozi wa Elayono, nk’uko yamenyereye: abigishwa biwe na bo baramukurikira." 
Luke22:40 Ashitse aho hantu, arababarira, ati Ni musenge, kugira ngo ntimuje mu mosha mabi." 
Luke22:41 Atandukana na bo, ashika nk’ahoterwa ibuye, arapfukama, arasenga," 
Luke22:42 ati Data, asangw’ ubigomba, kūra iki gikombe, kindēngāne: ariko ntibibe uko jewe ngomba, yamara bibe uko wewe ugomba." 
Luke22:43 Umumarayika aramwiyereka, avuye mw ijuru, amuha intege." 
Luke22:44 Arushirije kwicwa n’umubabaro, ashishikara gusenga cane, icuya ciwe kiba nk’ibitonyanga binini vy’amaraso bitonyanga hasi." 
Luke22:45 Amaze gusenga, ava hasi aja ah’abigishwa bari, asanga basinzirijwe n’umubabaro." 
Luke22:46 Arababaza, ati N’iki gitumye musinzira? Ni muvyuke, musenge, ntimuje mu mosha mabi." 
Luke22:47 Akivuga, haza igitero kizanywe n’uwitwa Yuda, umwe muri bamwe cumi na babiri, abagiye imbere: yēgēra Yesu, ngw amusome." 
Luke22:48 Yesu aramubaza, ati Yuda, mbeg’ utangisha Umwana w’umuntu kumusoma?" 
Luke22:49 Abāri kumwe na we babonye ibigira bibeho, baramubaza, bati Mugenzi, tubakubite inkota?" 
Luke22:50 Umwe muri bo ayikubita umusavyi w’umuherezi mukuru, amuca ugutwi kw’i buryo." 
Luke22:51 Yesu arababarira, ati Geza aho. Akora ku gutwi kwiwe, aramukiza." 
Luke22:52 Yesu abaza abaherezi bakuru n’abakuru b’abashibamyi b’urusengero n’abashingantahe bamuziye, ati Mbega munziye nk’umwambuzi, muzanye inkota n’amahiri?" 
Luke22:53 Imisi yose nāmana namwe mu rusengero ko mutāramvuye amaboko ngo mumfate; arikw iki n’igihe canyu n’ic’ ububasha bg’umwiza. 
Luke22:54 Baramufata, baramujana, bamwinjiza mu nzu y’umuherezi mukuru, ariko Petero amuja inyuma barenga arenguka." 
Luke22:55 Bacanye umuriro mu rugo hagati, bicaye hamwe, Petero yicara hagati muri bo." 
Luke22:56 Incoreke imubona yicaye ahabona, imwitegereje iravuga, iti N’uyu yari kumwe na we." 
Luke22:57 Na we arabihakana, at’ Eka nyina wanje, sindanamuzi." 
Luke22:58 Hashize akanya gato, uwundi aramubona, aramubgira, ati Nawe nyene ur’ uwo muri bo. Petero aramwishura, at’ Eka wa muntu, si jewe." 
Luke22:59 Hashize umwanya nk’isaha imwe, uwundi abivuga yigumiye, ati N’ivy’ ukuri, uyu yari kumwe na we, bitayeko n’Umunyagalilaya." 
Luke22:60 Petero aramubgira, at’ Eka wa muntu, sinzi n’ivy’ uvuze. Akivuga, uwo mwanya inkoko irabika." 
Luke22:61 Umwami Yesu arakebuka, yitegereza Petero. Petero yibuka rya jambo ry’Umwami, ingene yamubgiye, at’ Uyu musi inkoko itarabika, uja kunyihakana gatatu." 
Luke22:62 Arenga irembo, araturika ararira." 
Luke22:63 Abagabo bāri bafashe Yesu baramushinyagurira, baramutonagura," 
Luke22:64 bamupfuka mu maso, baramubaza, bati Pfīndūra: ni nde agukubise?" 
Luke22:65 N’ibindi vyinshi babimuvuga bamutuka. 
Luke22:66 Iryo joro rikeye, hakorana abashingantahe b’ubgo bgoko, ni bo baherezi bakuru n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe, bamujana mw ikombe ryabo, baramubaza," 
Luke22:67 bati Namb’ uri Kristo, tubgire. Arababgira, ati N’iyo nobabgira, ntimwovyemera;" 
Luke22:68 n’iyo nobabaza, ntimwonyishura." 
Luke22:69 Arik’ uhereye none Umwana w’umuntu azoba yicaye i buryo bg’ububasha bg’Imana. 
Luke22:70 Bose baramubaza, bati None rer’ ur’ Umwana w’Imana? Arabishura, ati Murarivuze ko ndi we." 
Luke22:71 Bati Turacaronderera iki ivyabona? Kuk’ ubgacu tuvyīyumviye mu kanwa kiwe. 
Luke23:1 Iryo koraniro ryose riva hasi, bamujana kwa Pilato." 
Luke23:2 Batangura kumwagiriza, bat’ Uyu twamubonye agomesha ubgoko bgacu, ababuza gutanga ikori rya Kayisari, yivuga ngo ni Kristo, Umwami." 
Luke23:3 Pilato aramubaza, ati Ni wewe Mwami w’Abayuda? Na we aramwishura, at’ Urarivuze." 
Luke23:4 Pilato abgira abaherezi bakuru n’ishengero, ati Nta caha mbona kur’ uyu muntu." 
Luke23:5 Na bo barashimika, bat’ Asibanganya igihugu, yigisha i Yudaya hose; yahereye i Galilaya ageza n’ino." 
Luke23:6 Pilato avyumvise, abaza yuk’ uwo muntu ar’ Umunyagalilaya." 
Luke23:7 Amenye yukw ar’ uwo mu gihugu ca Herode, amurungika kwa Herode, kuko na we yar’ i Yerusalemu mur’ iyo misi." 
Luke23:8 Herode abonye Yesu aranezerwa cane, kuko yahereye kera yifuza kumurāba, kuko yahora yumva ivyiwe, kandi yaziga ko yobona ikimenyetso yokora." 
Luke23:9 Amubaza amajambo menshi, ntiyamwishura na rimwe." 
Luke23:10 Abaherezi bakuru n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe barahagarara, bakovya kumwagiriza cane." 
Luke23:11 Herode aramutitura, hamwe n’abasoda biwe, aramushinyagurira, maz’ amwambika impuzu y’inyambarabami, amusubiza kwa Pilato." 
Luke23:12 Herode na Pilato baca buzura uwo musi nyene, kuko bāri basanzwe bankana." 
Luke23:13 Pilato akoranya abaherezi bakuru n’abashingantahe n’abantu," 
Luke23:14 arababgira, ati Mwanzaniye uyu muntu ngw agomesha abantu; none jewe namucunagurije imbere yanyu, nta caha mbona kuri we ku vyo mwamureze." 
Luke23:15 Na Herode n’uko, kuko yamudushubije: kandi rāba nta co yakoze gikwiye kumwicisha." 
Luke23:16 Nuko ndamukubita, ndamurekure. [" 
Luke23:17 Kuko yar’ akwiye kubarekurira imbohe imwe mur’ iyo misi mikuru.] 
Luke23:18 Ariko bose basemererera icarimwe, bati Kūrah’ uyo, uturekurire Baraba." 
Luke23:19 Uwo yari yashizwe mw ibohero bamuhōye ukugarariza kwabaye mur’ ico gisagara, bo n’ubgicanyi." 
Luke23:20 Pilato yongera kubabgira, kukw agomba kurekura Yesu." 
Luke23:21 Ariko bo barayogora, bati Mubambe, mubambe." 
Luke23:22 Ababaza ubugira gatatu, ati Ku ki? Uyu yakoze ikibi ki? Simmubonakw igikwiye kumwicisha; nuko ndamukubita, ndamurekure." 
Luke23:23 Ariko barīhambīra bavuga n’amajwi arenga, bamusaba kw abambga, amajwi yabo aramunesha." 
Luke23:24 Nuko Pilato aca urubanza nk’uko bamusavye. 
Luke23:25 Arekura uwashizwe mw ibohero bamuhōye ubugarariji n’ubgicanyi, uwo basavye; maz’ atanga Yesu ngw agirwe uko bagomba." 
Luke23:26 Bakimujana, bafata umuntu yitwa Simoni Umunyakurene, avuye mu misozi, bamukorera umusaraba, ngw awikorere akurikiye Yesu." 
Luke23:27 Ishengero ry’abantu ryinshi riramukurikira, ririmwo n’abagore bishishitira, bamuborogera." 
Luke23:28 Yesu arabakebuka, ati Yemwe bakobga b’i Yerusalemu, ntimundirire, ariko mwiririre n’abana banyu," 
Luke23:29 kukw imisi izoza bazovuga, bati Hahirwa abāgumbashe n’inda zitigeze kuvyara n’amabere atigeze kwonsa." 
Luke23:30 Ni ho bazotangura kubarira imisozi, bati Ni mutugweko; n’imirambi, bati Ni mudupfuke." 
Luke23:31 Ko bagirira bartyo igiti kibisi, non’ icumye kizogirirwa gite?" 
Luke23:32 N’abandi babiri, b’inkozi z’ibibi, bajananwa na we kwicanwa na we." 
Luke23:33 Bashitse ahantu hitwa Nyagihanga, bamubambanaho na za nkozi z’ibibi, umwe i buryo bgiwe, uwundi i bumoso." 
Luke23:34 Yesu aravuga, ati Data, n’ubaharire, kuko batazi ico bakora. Bagabura impuzu ziwe, barazipfindira." 
Luke23:35 Abantu bahagarara barāba. Abashingantahe na bo bamutwengera mw ijigo, bati Yakijije abandi, ni yikize, namb’ ari Kristo w’Imana, uwatoranijwe na yo." 
Luke23:36 N’abasoda baramucurīra, baramwēgēra, bamuha inkarisha," 
Luke23:37 baramubarira, bati Ni waba ur’ Umwami w’Abayuda, ni wikize." 
Luke23:38 Hejuru yiwe kandi hār’ icandiko canditswe, ng’ UYU N’UMWAMI W’ABAYUDA." 
Luke23:39 Umwe mu nkozi z’ibibi babambge aramutuka, ati Si wewe Kristo? Ni wikize, natwe udukize." 
Luke23:40 Arik’ uwa kabiri amwishura amuhana, ati No kwubaha Imana ntuyubaha, kand’ uciriwe urubanza rumwe n’urwiwe?" 
Luke23:41 Tweho turishuye, kuko tugiriwe ibihwanye n’ivyo twākoze: arik’ uyu nta kibi yakoze." 
Luke23:42 Kand’ aravuga, at’ Urahava uz’ unyibuke Yesu, ah’ uzozira mu bgami bgawe." 
Luke23:43 Aramwishura, ati Ndakubgire ukuri: Uyu musi urabana nanje muri Paradiso." 
Luke23:44 Kandi hāri nk’isaha zitandatu, ubgirakabiri bukorana mu gihugu cose, bushitsa mw isaha y’icenda," 
Luke23:45 izuba ryazimanganye; igihuzu gikingiriza ahēra cane h’urusengero gitantamukamwo kubiri. 
Luke23:46 Yesu amaze gusemerera n’ijwi rirenga, aravuga, ati Data, mu maboko yawe ni ho nshize ubugingo bganje. Ahejeje kuvuga artyo aracīkāna." 
Luke23:47 Umugabisha w’abasoda ijana abonye ibibaye, ahimbaza Imana, ati N’ukuri uyu muntu yar’ umugororotsi." 
Luke23:48 Ishengero ryose ryari ribikungereye, babonye ibibaye basubira inyuma bishishitira." 
Luke23:49 Abazinanyi na Yesu bose n’abagore bāri bavanye i Galilaya na we bāri bahagaze kure barāba ivyo. 
Luke23:50 Maze hār’ umuntu yitwa Yosefu, yar’ umunyekombe, kandi yar’ umunyangeso nziza agororotse." 
Luke23:51 Uwo ntiyari yafatanije inama n’abandi n’ivyo bākoze; yar’ Umunyarimataya, igisagara c’Abayuda, yar’ areretse ubgami bg’Imana." 
Luke23:52 Uyo aja kuri Pilato, asaba ikiziga ca Yesu." 
Luke23:53 Arakibambūra, akizingira mu mpuzu yera, agishira mu mva yimbge mu bitandara, itarahambgamw’ umuntu." 
Luke23:54 War’ umusi wo Kwitegura, isabato igira ishike."
