Luke23:55 Abagore bāri bavanye na Yesu i Galilaya bakurikira Yosefu, babona iyo mva, n’ingen’ ikiziga ciwe gishizwemwo." 
Luke23:56 Basubira inyuma, bategura ibimota neza n’amavuta atāmirana. Kandi kw isabato bararuhuka, nk’uko vyagezwe." 
Luke24:1 Ku wa mbere w’imisi ndwi kare mu mutwenzi baja kuri ya mva, bajanye vya bimota neza bāteguye." 
Luke24:2 Basanga ikibuye gitembagajwe kivuye ku mva; 
Luke24:3 binjirayo ntibāsangamw’ ikiziga c’Umwami Yesu. 
Luke24:4 Ivyo bikibazazaniye, abagabo babiri bahagarara i ruhande yabo, bambaye impuzu zikayangana." 
Luke24:5 Bagitinye, bunamitse amaso hasi, barababaza, bati N’iki gitumye muronderera ūriho, ahantu h’abāpfūye?" 
Luke24:6 Ntari hano, ariko yāzutse. Mwibuke uko yababgiye, akir’ i Galilaya," 
Luke24:7 at’ Umwana w’umuntu akwiye gushirwa mu maboko y’abanyavyaha, no kubambga, no kuzuka ku musi ugira gatatu." 
Luke24:8 Bibuka ya majambo yiwe," 
Luke24:9 bava mu mva, basubira inyuma, ivyo vyose babibarira bamwe cumi n’umwe n’abandi bose." 
Luke24:10 Abo bagore ni Mariya Magadalene na Yowana na Mariya nyina wa Yakobo: kandi n’abandi bagore bāri kumwe na bo, babarira intumwa ivyo." 
Luke24:11 Ayo majambo ababera nk’umuyaga, ntibābemera." 
Luke24:12 Ariko Petero ava hasi, yirukira ku mva, arunama, arungurukamwo, abona impuzu zera ziri zonyene: asubira i we, atangajwe n’ibibaye." 
Luke24:13 Uwo musi nyene babiri muri bo bari mu nzira baja mu mihana ahītwa Emawusi, ni kure y’i Yerusalemu nk’urugendo rwa stadiyo mirongwitandatu," 
Luke24:14 bavugana ivyabaye vyose. 
Luke24:15 Bakivugana babazanya, Yesu ubgiwe arabēgēra, ajana na bo." 
Luke24:16 Arikw amaso yabo atabgamw’ uruhuni ngo ntibamumenye. 
Luke24:17 Arababaza, ati Mbeg’ ivyo mugenda murabazanya n’ibiki? Barahagarara, bijiriwe." 
Luke24:18 Umwe muri bo yitwa Kileyopa aramwishura, ati Mbega ni wewe gusa watse indāro i Yerusalemu, utazi ivyabayeyo mur’ iyi misi?" 
Luke24:19 Arababaza, ati N’ibiki? Baramwishura, bati N’ivya Yesu Umunyanazareti, yar’ umuntu avugishwa n’Imana, akaba umunyabushobozi bginshi mu vyo yakora no mu vyo yavuga, imbere y’Imana n’imbere y’abantu bose:" 
Luke24:20 n’ivy’ ukw abaherezi bakuru n’abashingantahe bacu bāmutanze ngw acirwe urubanza rwo gupfa, bakamubamba." 
Luke24:21 Kandi twari twishimiye yukw ari we azocungura Abisirayeli. Kand’ ikigeretseko, uyu n’umusi ugira gatatu uhereye ah’ ivyo vyabereye." 
Luke24:22 Kandi n’abagore bo muri twebge badutangaje, bazindutse baja ku mva;" 
Luke24:23 babuze ikiziga ciwe, baraza batubarira yukw abamarayika babiyeretse bavuga yukw ariho." 
Luke24:24 Kandi na bamwe mu bari kumwe natwe bagiye ku mva basanga ari ko biri, ukw abo bagore batubariye; ariko we ntibamubona." 
Luke24:25 Arababgira, ati Yemwe mwa mburabgenge, imitima yanyu itevye cane kwizera ivyo abāvugishwa n’Imana bāvuze vyose!" 
Luke24:26 Mbega Kristo ntiyar’ akwiye kubabazwa artyo ngw abone kuja mu bgiza bgiwe? 
Luke24:27 Atangurira kuri Mose no ku bāvugishwa n’Imana bose, abasobanurira mu vyanditswe vyose ivyanditswe kuri we." 
Luke24:28 Bashitse hafi y’umuhana bajako, amera nk’ūgomba kuwurēngāna." 
Luke24:29 Baramugōbēra, bati Gumana natwe, kuko bugira bgire kand’ umusi ukuze cane. Arinjira ngw agumane na bo." 
Luke24:30 Yicaye ngw asangire na bo, yābīra umutsima, arawuhezagira, arawumanyagura, arawubaha." 
Luke24:31 Uruhuni rubava ku maso, baramumenya: maz’ arakamangana, ntibāba bakimubona." 
Luke24:32 Baravugana, bati Mbeg’ imitima yacu ko yarikw iragurugumba, aho yarikw aravugana natwe mu nzira, aduhishurira ivyanditswe!" 
Luke24:33 Ako kanya barīkora, basubira i Yerusalemu, basanga bamwe cumi n’umwe bakoranye, bo n’abāri kumwe na bo," 
Luke24:34 kandi bavuga, bati N’ukuri Umwami Yesu yāzutse, kandi yabonywe na Simoni." 
Luke24:35 Na bo babadondera vya bindi vyo mu nzira, kandi yuko bamumenyeshejwe n’uko yamanyaguye umutsima." 
Luke24:36 Bariko baravuga ivyo, Yesu ubgiwe ahagarara hagati muri bo, arababgira, at’ Amahoro abe muri mwebge." 
Luke24:37 Ariko bafatwa n’ubgoba bacika ivutu, bagira ngo n’umuzimu babonye." 
Luke24:38 Arababaza, at’ Ikibahagaritse imitima n’iki? Kandi n’iki gitumye mubūranisha imitima?" 
Luke24:39 Ni murābe ibiganza vyanje n’ibirenge vyanje, mumenye kw ari jewe ubganje: ni munkorakore, murābe, kuk’ umuzimu utagira inyama n’amagufa, nk’ivyo mumbonana." 
Luke24:40 Avuze ivyo, abereka ibiganza vyiwe n’ibirenge." 
Luke24:41 Akanyamuneza kakibabujije kuvyemera, bariko baratangara, arababaza, ati Har’ utwo kurya mufise hano?" 
Luke24:42 Bamuha igihimba c’ifi yokeje," 
Luke24:43 aracābīra, akirīra imbere yabo." 
Luke24:44 Arababgira, at’ Aya n’amajambo yanje nababgira nkiri kumwe namwe, y’ingen’ ivyanditswe kuri jewe vyose mu vyagezwe vya Mose no mu majambo y’abāvugishwa n’Imana no muri Zaburi bikwiye gushika." 
Luke24:45 Maz’ abungura ubgenge ngo batahure ivyanditswe. 
Luke24:46 Arababgira, ati Ni ko vyanditswe yuko Kristo akwiye kubabazwa no kuzuka mu bāpfuye ku musi ugira gatatu," 
Luke24:47 kandi yuk’ ukwihana no guharirwa ivyaha bikwiye kuvugwa mw izina ryiwe mu mahanga yose, uhereye i Yerusalemu." 
Luke24:48 Namwe mur’ ivyabona vyo kuvuga ivyo. 
Luke24:49 Umve, ngira mbarungikire ico Data yasezeranye; ariko mugume mu gisagara, kugeza aho muzokwambikirwa ubushobozi buvuye mw ijuru." 
Luke24:50 Abavanaho, abashitsa aharābana n’i Betaniya, aterura amaboko, arabahezagira." 
Luke24:51 Akibahezagira, atandukanywa na bo, adūzwa mw ijuru." 
Luke24:52 Na bo baramusenga, basubira i Yerusalemu bafise akanyamuneza kenshi," 
Luke24:53 bama mu rusengero ubudasība bashima Imana. 
John1:1 Ubga mbere na mbere Jambo yariho, kandi Jambo yahoranye n’Imana, kand’ uwo Jambo yar’ Imana." 
John1:2 Uwo yahoranye n’Imana ubga mbere na mbere; 
John1:3 vyose vyaremwe na we, mu vyaremwe vyose nta kintu na kimwe kitaremwe na we." 
John1:4 Muri we hārimw’ ubugingo, kand’ ubgo bugingo bgar’ umuco w’abantu." 
John1:5 Uwo muco wākira mu mwiza, arik’ umwiza ntiwawākiriye." 
John1:6 Haje umuntu yatumwe n’Imana, izina ryiwe ni Yohana;" 
John1:7 uwo yazanywe no kuba igishingantahe, ngw ashingire intahe umuco, kugira ngo bose bizere kubgiwe." 
John1:8 Uwo si we wa muco, ariko kwar’ ugushingira intahe umuco." 
John1:9 Umuco w’ukuri, wākira umuntu wese, warik’ uraza mur’ iyi si." 
John1:10 Yari mw isi, kand’ isi yaremwe na we, arikw isi ntiyamumenya;" 
John1:11 yaje mu vyiwe, arikw abiwe ntibāmwākiriye." 
John1:12 Arikw abāmwākiriye bose yabahaye ububasha bgo gucika abana b’Imana, ni bo bizeye izina ryiwe," 
John1:13 ni bo batāvyawe n’amaraso, canke n’ukwifuza kw’ umubiri, canke n’ukwifuza kw’ umugabo, ariko bāvyawe n’Imana." 
John1:14 Kand’ uwo Jambo yihaye umubiri, abana natwe, twitegereza ubgiza bgiwe, n’ubgiza bumeze nk’ubg’ Umwana w’ikinege ava kwa Se, yuzuye ubuntu n’ukuri." 
John1:15 Yohana amushingira intahe, arasemerera, at’ Uwo ni we navuze, nt’ Ūza inyuma yanje ni we yar’ uwa mbere kuri jewe, kuko yariho ntarabaho." 
John1:16 Kukw ibibōgabōga muri we ari vyo twahaweko twese, n’ubuntu bugerekeranye n’ubundi." 
John1:17 Kukw ivyagezwe vyazanywe na Mose, ubuntu n’ukuri vyazanywe na Yesu Kristo." 
John1:18 Nta muntu yigeze kubona Imana na rimwe; Umwana w’ikinege aba mu gikiriza ca Se ni we yayimenyekanishije. 
John1:19 Uku ni kwo gushinga intahe kwa Yohana, ah’ Abayuda bāmutumakw abaherezi n’Abalewi bavuye i Yerusalemu, ngo bamubaze, bat’ Uri nde?" 
John1:20 Na we aravyatura, ntiyahisha ukuri, aravyatura, ati Si jewe Kristo." 
John1:21 Baramubaza, bati None se bimeze bite? Uri Eliya? Ati Sindi we. Bat’ Uri wa muntu avugishwa n’Imana? At’ Oya." 
John1:22 Baramubaza, bati Non’ uri nde, ngo tuje kwishura abādutumye? Kuri wewe wivuga ute?" 
John1:23 Ati Nd’ ijwi ry’ūsemererera mu bugaragwa, ati Ni mugorore inzira y’Uhoraho, nk’uk’ uwavugishwa n’Imana Yesaya yavuze." 
John1:24 Kand’ abo bātumwe bār’ Abafarisayo; 
John1:25 baramubaza, bati Non’ ubatiriza iki, k’utari Kristo, ntube Eliya canke wa muntu avugishwa n’Imana?" 
John1:26 Yohana arabishura, ati Jeho mbatiza mu mazi; hagati muri mwebge hahagaze uwo mutazi," 
John1:27 ni we aza inyuma yanje, kandi jewe ntibimbereye gupfundurura akagozi k’inkweto yiwe." 
John1:28 Ivyo vyabereye i Betaniya, hakurya ya Yorodani aho Yohana yabatiriza." 
John1:29 Bukeye bg’aho abona Yesu aza kuri we, aravuga, ati Nguyu Umwagazi w’intama w’Imana ukūrah’ icaha c’abari mw isi." 
John1:30 Uyo ni we navuze, nt’ Inyuma yanje hazoza umuntu yar’ uw’ imbere kuri jewe, kuko yariho ntarabaho." 
John1:31 Nanje sinaribgamumenye, ariko kugira ngo yerekwe Abisirayeli, ni co catumye nanje nza mbatiza mu mazi." 
John1:32 Kandi Yohana ashinga intahe, ati Nabonye Mpwemu amanuka ava mw ijuru asa n’inuma, aguma kuri we;" 
John1:33 kandi jewe sinaribgamumenye, arik’ Uwantumye kubatiza mu mazi, ni we yambariye, at’ Uwo uzobona Mpwemu amanuka aja kuri we, akamugumako, ni we abatiza muri Mpwemu Yera." 
John1:34 Nanje narabibonye, narabishingiye intahe yuk’ uyo ar’ Umwana w’Imana." 
John1:35 Bukeye bg’aho, Yohana yongeye guhagararana na babiri mu bigishwa biwe," 
John1:36 yitegereza Yesu agendagenda, aravuga, ati Nguyu Umwagazi w’intama w’Imana." 
John1:37 Abo bigishwa babiri bumvise ukw avuga, bakurikira Yesu." 
John1:38 Yesu akebutse, abona bamukurikiye, arababaza, ati Murondera iki? Baramubgira, bati Rabi (risobanurwa ngo Mwigisha), usembereye hehe?" 
John1:39 Arababgira, ati Ni muze muharābe. Nuko baragenda, babona ah’ asembereye, basībira ah’ ari uno musi, hāri nk’isaha cumi." 
John1:40 Andereya mwene nyina wa Simoni Petero, yar’ umwe mur’ abo babiri bumvise Yohana, bagakurikira Yesu." 
John1:41 Uyo abanza kurondera mwene nyina Simoni, aramubgira, ati Twabonye Mesiya (risobanurwa ngo Kristo)." 
John1:42 Amujana kuri Yesu. Yesu aramwitegereza, aramubgira, at’ Uri Simoni mwene Yohana; uzokwitwa Kefa (risobanurwa ngo Petero)." 
John1:43 Bukeye bg’aho Yesu agomba kuvayo ngw aje i Galilaya, abona Filipo, aramubarira, ati Nkurikira." 
John1:44 Kandi Filipo uyo, i wabo n’i Betsayida, igisagara c’i wabo wa Andereya na Petero." 
John1:45 Filipo abona Natanayeli, aramubgira, at, Uwo Mose yanditse mu vyagezwe, n’abāvugishwa n’Imana bakamwandika, twamubonye, ni Yesu w’i Nazareti, mwene Yosefu." 
John1:46 Natanayeli aramubaza, ati Mbeg’ i Nazareti hova iciza? Filipo aramubgira, ati N’uze urābe." 
John1:47 Yesu abona Natanayeli aza kuri we, amuvugako, at’ Ehe Umwisirayeli vy’ukuri, atarimw’ ubugunge." 
John1:48 Natanayeli aramubaza, ati Wammenyeye hehe? Yesu aramwishura, ati Filipo ataraguhamagara, aho wari musi y’umusukoni, nakubonye." 
John1:49 Natanayeli na we aramwishura, ati Mwigisha, ur’ Umwana w’Imana, ni wewe Mwami w’Abisirayeli." 
John1:50 Yesu aramwishura, ati Wijejwe n’uko nkubgiye yuko nakubonye uri musi y’umusukoni? Uzobona ibiruta ivyo." 
John1:51 Arongera aramubgira, ati N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndababgira yuko muzobona ijuru rikingurutse, kand’ abamarayika b’Imana badūga bamanuka ku Mwana w’umuntu." 
John2:1 Ku musi ugira gatatu haba ubukwe i Kana i Galilaya, kandi nyina wa Yesu ni ho yar’ ari." 
John2:2 Yesu na we atorerwa ubukwe, bo n’abigishwa biwe." 
John2:3 Maze vino ikamye, nyina wa Yesu aramubarira, ati Nta vino bafise." 
John2:4 Yesu aramwishura, ati Duhūriye hehe ga nyina wanje? Igihe canje ntikiragera." 
John2:5 Nyina abgira abasuku, at’ Ic’ ababgira cose mugikore." 
John2:6 Hārih’ impange z’intango zitandatu z’amazi zabājwe mu mabuye, zateretsweho kubg’ ukwihumānura nk’uk’ umugenzo w’Abayuda war’ uri, imwe‐imwe yuzuzwa n’ibibindi bibiri canke bitatu." 
John2:7 Yesu arababarira, ati Ni mwuzuze izo ntango amazi. Bazuzuza kugeza ku mbiga." 
John2:8 Arababarira, ati Mudahe ubu nyene, mushīre umuteretsi mukuru. Baramushīra." 
John2:9 Umuteretsi yumvirije amazi yāhindutse vino, ntiyamenye iy’ ivuye, arikw abasuku bādashe amazi bari babizi; uwo muteretsi ahamagara umukwe," 
John2:10 aramubgira, at’ Umuntu wese ahora abanza gutereka vino ziryoshe, maze bāhimba akabaha izitaryoshe: ariko weho iziryoshe ni zo wabītse gushitsa ubu." 
John2:11 Iryo ni ryo tanguriro ry’ibimenyetso Yesu yakoze ar’i Kana i Galilaya, yerekana ubgiza bgiwe; kand’ abigishwa biwe baramwizera." 
John2:12 Hanyuma y’ivyo amanuka i Kaperinawumu, bo na nyina na bene nyina n’abigishwa biwe, amaray’ imisi itari myinshi." 
John2:13 Kandi Pasika y’Abayuda yari hafi; Yesu adūga i Yerusalemu. 
John2:14 Asanga mu rusengero abadandarizah’ inka n’intama n’inuma, n’abavunja amahera bicaye." 
John2:15 Atsiba imigozi ayigira nk’ikimoko, abahinda mu rusengero bose, n’intama n’inka, asēsa amahera y’abariko baravunja, ahenura ameza yabo." 
John2:16 Abarira abadandaza inuma, ati Ni mukūreh’ ivyo, nta co muhindura inzu ya Data kuba inzu y’akaguriro." 
John2:17 Abigishwa biwe bibuka ko handitswe, ngw Ishaka ry’inzu yawe rizondya." 
John2:18 Abayuda baramubaza, bat’ Utwereka ikimenyetso ki, gituma ukora ivyo?" 
John2:19 Yesu arabishura, ati Musambure uru rusengero, nanje nzoruhagarika mu misi itatu." 
John2:20 Maz’ Abayuda bat’ Uru rusengero rwubatswe imyaka mirongwine n’itandatu: none wewe uzoruhagarika mu misi itatu? 
John2:21 Ariko we yavuga urusengero rw’umubiri wiwe. 
John2:22 Nukw amaze kuzurwa mu bāpfuye, abigishwa biwe bibuka yuko yari yaravuze ivyo, bemera icanditswe, na rya jambo Yesu yavuze." 
John2:23 Kandi yar’i Yerusalemu mu misi mikuru ya Pasika, benshi bizera izina ryiwe, babonye ibimenyetso akora." 
John2:24 Ariko Yesu we ntiyabīshimira, kuko yar’ azi abantu bose," 
John2:25 ntiyarinda ko hogira ūshingira intahe ivy’ umuntu, kuk’ ubgiwe yar’ azi ibiri mu muntu." 
John3:1 Hār’ umuntu mu Bafarisayo, yitwa Nikodemo, yar’ umukuru wo mu Bayuda;" 
John3:2 uwo aza kuri we mw ijoro, aramubgira, ati Mwigisha, turazi yuk’ ur’ umwigisha yavuye ku Mana, kukw ata muntu ashobora gukora ibimenyetso nk’ivyo ukora, shit’ Imana iri kumwe na we." 
John3:3 Yesu aramwishura, ati N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndakubgire: Iy’ umuntu atavyawe ubga kabiri, ntashobora kubona ubgami bg’Imana." 
John3:4 Nikodemo aramubaza, at’ Umuntu ashobora ate kuvyarwa ashaje? Mbega yoshobora gusubira mu nda ya nyina akavuka?" 
John3:5 Yesu aramwishura, ati N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndakubgire: Iy’ umuntu atavyawe n’amazi na Mpwemu, ntashobora kwinjira mu bgami bg’Imana." 
John3:6 Ikivyawe n’umubiri na co n’umubiri; ikivyawe na Mpwemu na co n’impwemu. 
John3:7 Ntutangazwe n’uko nkubgiye, nti Murakwiye kuvyarwa ubga kabiri." 
John3:8 Umuyaga uhuhuta ah’ ugomba, nawe ukumva igihuhuta cawo, ariko ntumenye ah’ uva, n’ah’ uja; uko ni kw amera, ūvyawe na Mpwemu wese." 
John3:9 Nikodemo aramubaza, at’ Ivyo bishoboka bite?" 
John3:10 Yesu aramwishura, ati Ni wewe mwigisha w’Abisirayeli, kandi ntutahura ivyo?" 
John3:11 N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndakubgire: Twebge tuvuga ico tuzi, kandi dushingira intahe ico twabonye; ariko ntimwemera igishingantahe cacu." 
John3:12 Ko nababgiye ivy’ isi ntimwemere, none muzokwemera mute ni nababgira ivy’ ijuru?" 
John3:13 Nta wadūze mw ijuru, atar’ uwamanutse ava mw ijuru, ni we Mwana w’umuntu wo mw ijuru." 
John3:14 Kand’ uko Mose yamanitse inzoka mu bugaragwa, ni k’Umwana w’umuntu akwiye kumanikwa," 
John3:15 ng’ ūmwizera wese ahabge ubugingo budashira. 
John3:16 Kuk’ urukundo Imana yakunze abari mw isi ari rwo rwatumye itanga Umwana wayo w’ikinege, ng’ ūmwizera wese ntaz’ apfe rubi, arikw ahabge ubugingo budashira." 
John3:17 Kukw Imana itātumye Umwana wayo gucira abari mw isi urubanza, ariko ngw abari mw isi bakizwe na we." 
John3:18 Ūmwizeye ntazotsindwa n’urubanza, arik’ ūtamwizeye aramaze gutsindwa, kukw atizeye izina ry’Umwana w’Imana w’ikinege." 
John3:19 Uku ni kwo gutsindwa, kuk’ umuco waje mw isi, arikw abantu bagakunda umwiza kuruta umuco, kukw ibikorwa vyabo ari bibi." 
John3:20 Kuk’ ūkora ibibi wese yanka umuco, kandi ntaza ku muco, kugira ngw ibikorwa vyiwe ntibihanwe." 
John3:21 Arik’ ūkora ivy’ ukuri aza ku muco, kugira ngw ibikorwa vyiwe biseruke ko vyakorewe mu Mana." 
John3:22 Hanyuma y’ivyo Yesu ajana n’abigishwa biwe mu gihugu c’i Yudaya, atebanayo na bo, abatiza." 
John3:23 Kandi Yohana na we yabatiriza ahitwa Ayinoni, hafi y’i Salimu, kukw aho har’ amazi menshi, abantu bāraza bakabatizwa," 
John3:24 kuko Yohana atāribgashirwe mw ibohero. 
John3:25 Havyuka ibihāri ku bigishwa ba Yohana n’Umuyuda ku vyo kwihumanura. 
John3:26 Baza aho Yohana ari, baramubgira, bati Mwigisha, uwo mwari kumwe hakurya ya Yorodani, umwe washingira intahe, erega na we arikw arabatiza, kandi bose baza kuri we." 
John3:27 Yohana arabishura, ati Nta co umuntu ashobora kuronka ubgiwe, atagihawe kivuye mw ijuru." 
John3:28 Ni mwebge ubganyu munshingira intahe yuko navuze, nti Si jewe Kristo, ariko natumwe kumwītangira imbere." 
John3:29 Ūhawe umugeni ni we mukwe, arik’ umugenzi w’uno mukwe amuhagaraye i ruhande amwumva, anezerwa cane n’ijwi ry’umukwe; nukw ako kanyamuneza kanje karashitse." 
John3:30 Urya akwiye gukuzwa, nanje ngirwe muto." 
John3:31 Uwavuye hejuru ni we asumba bose, uwo mw isi aba ar’ uwo mw isi nyene, avuga ivy’ isi; uwavuye mw ijuru ni we asumba bose." 
John3:32 Ico yabonye, kandi yumvise, ni co ashingira intahe, arik’ ugushinga intahe kwiwe nta wukwemera." 
John3:33 Uwemeye ugushinga intahe kwiwe aba ateye igikumu ngw Imana n’iy’ ukuri. 
John3:34 Uwo Imana yatumye, ni we avuga amajambo y’Imana, kukw idatanga Mpwemu ku ngero." 
John3:35 Se arakunda Umwana, kandi yamuhaye vyose, abishira mu kuboko kwiwe." 
John3:36 Uwizeye Umwana arafise ubugingo budashira, arik’ ūtumvira Umwana ntazobona ubugingo, arik’ uburake bg’Imana buguma kuri we." 
John4:1 Umwami Yesu amenye kw Abafarisayo bumvise yukw aronka abigishwa benshi, kand’ abatiza benshi, arusha Yohana," 
John4:2 (ariko Yesu ubgiwe si we yabatiza, bār’ abigishwa biwe)," 
John4:3 ava i Yudaya, asubira i Galilaya." 
John4:4 Yumva akwiye guca i Samariya. 
John4:5 Nukw ashika ku gisagara c’i Samariya citwa Sukara, hafi y’umusozi Yakobo yahaye Yosefu, umuhungu wiwe," 
John4:6 kand’ aho hār’ iriba rya Yakobo. Yesu ananijwe n’urugendo apfa kwicara kw iriba, hāri nk’isaha zitandatu." 
John4:7 Haza umugore w’Umusamariyakazi kuvoma: Yesu aramubgira, at’ Umpe utwo kunywa." 
John4:8 Kukw abigishwa biwe bari bagiye mu gisagara kugura indya. 
John4:9 Uno Musamariyakazi aramubaza, ati Wewe ur’ Umuyuda, non’ unsaba amazi ute, jewe nd’ Umusamariyakazi? (Ni kukw Abayuda n’Abasamariya bānēnana.)" 
John4:10 Yesu aramwishura, at’ Iy’ uba war’ uzi ingabire y’Imana, ukamenya n’ūgusavye ngo Mpa utwo kunywa uw’ ari we, nawe uba umusavye, na we akaguha amazi y’ubugingo." 
John4:11 Wa mugore aramwishura, ati Mugenzi, kw ata co kuvomesha ufise, kand’ iriba rikaba ari rirerire, non’ ayo mazi y’ubugingo uyakūra hehe?" 
John4:12 Mbeg’ uruta sogokuruza wacu Yakobo, yaduhaye iri riba, yanywa amazi yaryo, ubgiwe n’abana biwe, n’amasho yiwe?" 
John4:13 Yesu aramwishura, at’ Ūnywa kur’ ayo mazi wese azosubira kugira inyota;" 
John4:14 arik’ ūnywa amazi nzomuha, ntazoba akigira inyota na mba gushitsa ibihe vyose, arikw amazi nzomuha azohinduka muri we imbizi y’amazi yiburuka azana ubugingo budashira." 
John4:15 Uwo mugore aramubgira, ati Mugenzi, mpa se ayo mazi, sinze ngire inyota, kandi sinze ngaruke kuvoma ino hose." 
John4:16 Yesu aramubgira, ati Genda uhamagare umugabo wawe, uheze ugaruke ino." 
John4:17 Uwo mugore aramwishura, ati Nta mugabo mfise. Yesu aramubgira, at’ Uvuze ko, k’ugize ngo nta mugabo ufise," 
John4:18 kuko war’ ufise abagabo batanu, arik’ uwo ufise ubu s’umugabo wawe; ivyo ubivuze ukuri." 
John4:19 Uno mugore aramubgira, ati Mugenzi, ndabona k’ur’ umuntu avugishwa n’Imana." 
John4:20 Ba sogokuruza bacu bāsengera kur’ uyu musozi, ariko mweho mugira ngw i Yerusalemu ni ho hantu hakwiye gusengerwa." 
John4:21 Yesu aramubgira, ati Nyizera nyina wanje; igihe kija kuza, si kur’ uyu musozi cank’ i Yerusalemu muzosengera Data." 
John4:22 Mwebge musenga ico mutazi; tweho dusenga ico tuzi, kukw agakiza gaturuka mu Bayuda." 
John4:23 Arikw igihe kiza, kandi kirashitse, ni ho abasenga b’ukuri bazosengera Data mu mpwemu no mu kuri, kuko Data arondera abamusenga bameze bartyo." 
John4:24 Imana ni Mpwemu, kand’ abayisenga bakwiye kuyisenga mu mpwemu no mu kuri." 
John4:25 Nya mugore aramubgira, ati Ndazi ko Mesiya azoza yitwa Kristo; uwo ah’ azozira ni we azoduserurira vyose." 
John4:26 Yesu aramubgira, ati Ni jewe nyene turiko turavugana." 
John4:27 Bun’ abigishwa biwe barashika, batangazwa n’ukw avugana n’umugore: ariko nta wavuze, at’ Urondera iki? Canke ngo Muvuganira na we iki?" 
John4:28 Maz’ uno mugore asiga umubindi wiwe hano, asubira mu gisagara, abgira abantu," 
John4:29 ati Ni muze murābe umuntu ambariye ivyo nakoze vyose: namb’ ari we Kristo? 
John4:30 Bava mu gisagara ngo bamusange iy’ ari. 
John4:31 Batarashika, abigishwa baramwinginga, bati Mwigisha, enda fungura." 
John4:32 Arabishura, ati Jewe mfise ivyo kurya mwebge mutazi." 
John4:33 Abigishwa barabazanya, bati Mbega har’ uwamuzaniye ivyo kurya?" 
John4:34 Yesu arababgira, at’ Indya zanje n’ugukora ico uwantumye agomba, no guheraheza igikorwa ciwe." 
John4:35 Mbega mwebge ntimuvuga ngo hasigaye amezi ane iyimbura rikagera? Ehe ndababgire: Ni mwunamure amaso yanyu murābe imirima, irēze igeze kwimbura." 
John4:36 Umwimbuzi aragererwa, yegeraniriza ivyimburwa mu bugingo budashira; kugira ng’ ūbiba n’uwimbura banezeranwe." 
John4:37 Kuko mur’ ivyo ari ho iri jambo rimenyekanira kw ar’ iry’ ukuri, ngo Habiba umwe, hakimbura uwundi." 
John4:38 Nabatumye kwimbura ibitābatamije; abandi bāratamye, namwe mwashikiye mu vy’ubutame bgabo." 
John4:39 Benshi mu Basamariya bo mur’ ico gisagara bamwizera kubg’ amajambo ya wa mugore, yavuze ashinga intahe, at’ Ambariye ivyo nakoze vyose." 
John4:40 Maz’ Abasamariya baje ah’ ari, baramwinginga ngw agume i wabo; asībirayo kabiri." 
John4:41 Hizera abandi benshi baruta aba mbere, kuko bīyumviye ijambo ryiwe;" 
John4:42 maze babgira uwo mugore, bat’ Ubu ho ntitwizeye kubg’ amajambo yawe gusa, kuko natwe twīyumviye kandi tumenye k’uyu ar’ Umukiza w’isi vy’ukuri." 
John4:43 Iyo misi ibiri ishize, avayo aja i Galilaya." 
John4:44 Kandi Yesu ubgiwe yashinze intahe yuk’ umuntu avugishwa n’Imana atagira icubahiro mu ntāra y’i wabo. 
John4:45 Ashitse i Galilaya, Abanyagalilaya baramwākīra, kuko babonye ivyo yakoreye i Yerusalemu vyose muri ya misi mikuru, kuko na bo bari bagiyeyo mu misi mikuru." 
John4:46 Maz’ asubira kuja i Kana i Galilaya, hamwe yahindurira amazi agacika vino. Hār’ umutware atwarira umwami, umwana wiwe w’umuhungu yar’ arwariye i Kaperinawumu;" 
John4:47 uyo yumvise ko Yesu avuye i Yudaya ashitse i Galilaya, aza kuri we, aramwinginga ngw amanuke gukiza umwana wiwe, kuko yari ku mpfiro." 
John4:48 Yesu aramubgira, at’ Iyo mutabonye ibimenyetso n’ibitangaza nta ho mwizera na mba." 
John4:49 Uwo mutware ati Mugenzi, ngwino se umanuke umwana wanje atarapfa." 
John4:50 Yesu aramubarira, ati Ni wīgīre, umwana wawe ni muzima. Uwo muntu yizera ijambo Yesu amubgiye, aragenda." 
John4:51 Arikw aramanuka abantu biwe baramusanganira, bat’ Umwana wawe ni muzima." 
John4:52 Abasiguza cane igihe yatanguye kworoherwa. Baramubgira, bat’ Ejo, kw isaha ndwi, ni ho umururumbo wamuvuyeko." 
John4:53 Maze se aca amenya ko hāri muri nya saha nyene Yesu yamubgiriyemwo, at’ Umwana wawe ni muzima. Arizera ubgiwe n’abo mu rugo rwiwe bose." 
John4:54 Ico ni co kimenyetso ca kabiri Yesu yakoze, avuye i Yudaya ashitse i Galilaya." 
John5:1 Hanyuma y’ivyo haba imisi mikuru y’Abayuda; Yesu adūga i Yerusalemu. 
John5:2 Kand’ i Yerusalemu hafi y’irembo ry’intama, hār’ ikidengeri, mu Giheburayo citwa Betesida, carikw amabaraza atanu." 
John5:3 Muri yo hari haryamye abantu benshi barwaye, n’impumyi, n’abacumbagira, n’abanyunyutse. [Bāri barorereye kw amazi azīkuruka." 
John5:4 Kuko rimwe‐rimwe umumarayika yamanuka aja muri kino kidengeri, akazīkurura amazi. Maz’ uwītangiye gutambukiramwo, amazi azīkurutse, ni we yakira indwara yamufashe iy’ ari yo yose.]" 
John5:5 Hārih’ umuntu yar’ afise indwara ayimaranye imyaka mirongwitatu n’umunani. 
John5:6 Yesu amubonye aryamyeho, kand’ amenye kw amaze igihe kirekire, aramubaza, ati Wumva ugomba gukira?" 
John5:7 Uno arwaye aramwishura, ati Mugenzi, nta muntu mfise wo kunyinikīra mu kidengeri iy’amazi azīkurutse: kuko ngira ngo ndaza uwundi akantanga gushungurukiramwo." 
John5:8 Yesu aramubgira, ati Va hasi, ikorere ikirago cawe, ugende." 
John5:9 Buno nyene uwo muntu arakira, yikorera ikirago ciwe, aragenda. Arik’ uwo musi hari kw isabato." 
John5:10 Nukw Abayuda babgira uwakijijwe, bat’ Erega ni kw isabato: ntivyemerwa ko wikorera ikirago cawe." 
John5:11 Na we arabishura, at’ Uwankijije ni we yambariye at’ Ikorere ikirago cawe, ugende." 
John5:12 Baramubaza, bat’ Uyo muntu ni nde yakubariye ngw Ikorere ugende?" 
John5:13 Arik’ uwakijijwe ntiyar’ azi uw’ ari we, kuko Yesu yaciye yīgīra, kukw aho hantu hār’ abantu benshi." 
John5:14 Hanyuma y’ivyo Yesu amubona mu rusengero, aramubgira, ati Rāba wakize; ntugasubire gukora icaha, kugira ngo ntuz’ ubone ibiruta ivya mbere." 
John5:15 Uno muntu aragenda, abgira Abayuda kw ari Yesu yamukijije." 
John5:16 Ni co catumye Abayuda bahama Yesu, kuko yakoze ivyo kw isabato." 
John5:17 Yesu arababgira, ati Data arakora kugeza n’ubu, nanje ndakora." 
John5:18 Ni co catumye Abayuda barushiriza kurondera ingene bomwica, kukw atākēngereye isabato gusa, arikw agatakw akīta Imana kw ari Se bgite, akīringaniza n’Imana." 
John5:19 Nuko Yesu asubira kubabgira, ati N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndababgire: Nta co Umwana ashobora kwigenera, atabonye Se agikora, kukw ivyo Se akora vyose n’Umwana aca abikora kuno." 
John5:20 Kuko Se akunda Umwana, akamwereka ivy’ akora vyose ubgiwe, kand’ azomwereka ibikorwa biruta ivyo, kugira ngo mwebge mutangare." 
John5:21 Nk’uko Se azura abapfuye akabaha ubugingo, ni ko n’Umwana aha ubugingo abo agomba." 
John5:22 Kuko Se ata n’umwe acira urubanza, arikw imanza zose yazishikirije Umwana," 
John5:23 ngo bose bubahe Umwana nk’uko bubaha Se; ūtubaha Umwana ntaba yubaha Se yamutumye. 
John5:24 N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndababgire: Uwumva ijambo ryanje, akizera uwantumye, ni we afise ubugingo budashira, kandi ntazoshirwa mu rukinja, arikw aba avuye mu rupfu, ashitse mu bugingo." 
John5:25 N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndababgire: Igihe kiza, kandi kirashitse, ah’ abapfuye bazokwumvira ijwi ry’Umwana w’Imana, kand’ abazoryumva bazoba bazima." 
John5:26 Nk’uko Se ari n’ubugingo muri we, ni ko yahaye Umwana kugira ubugingo muri we na we." 
John5:27 Yamuhaye ububasha bgo guca imanza, kukw ar’ Umwana w’umuntu." 
John5:28 Ntimutangazwe n’ico; kukw igihe kija kuza, ah’ abari mu mva bose bazokwumvira ijwi ryiwe," 
John5:29 bakazivamwo; abākoze ivyiza bakazukira ubugingo, abākoze ibibi bakazukira gucirwakw iteka." 
John5:30 Nta co nshobora gukora nigeneye; uko numvise ni ko nca urubanza, kand’ urubanza nca rurabereye, kuko ntarondera ivyo nigombera, ariko ndondera ivyo uwantumye agomba." 
John5:31 Asangwa nishingira intahe, intahe yanje ntizoba ar’ iy’ ukuri;" 
John5:32 ariko har’ Uwundi anshingira intahe, nanje nzi yukw intahe yiwe anshingira ar’ iy’ ukuri." 
John5:33 Mwebge mwatumye kuri Yohana, ashingira ukuri intahe," 
John5:34 mugabo jewe sindinda gushingirwa intahe n’umuntu; arikw ico mvugiye ivyo n’ukugira ngo mukizwe. 
John5:35 Uwo yar’ itara ryaka rikabonesha, kandi namwe mwamaze igihe muhimbawe n’ukwaka kwiwe." 
John5:36 Ariko jewe mfise ikinshingira intahe kuruta Yohana, kukw ibikorwa Data yampaye ngo mbiheraheze, ivyo bikorwa nyene nkora ni vyo binshingira intahe yuko Data ari we yantumye." 
John5:37 Kandi Data yantumye ni we anshingira intahe. Nta ho murumva ijwi ryiwe, kandi ntimurabona ishusho yiwe," 
John5:38 bitayeko ntimufise ijambo ryiwe riguma muri mwebge, kuk’ uwo yatumye mutamwizeye." 
John5:39 Mwebge murasesa mu vyanditswe, kuko mugira ngo muri vyo ni ho mufise ubugingo budashira, kand’ ari vyo binshingira intahe," 
John5:40 ariko mukanka kuza kuri jewe ngo muronke ubugingo. 
John5:41 Singomba gushimwa n’abantu," 
John5:42 ariko mwebge ndabazi yuko mutagira urukundo rw’Imana mu mitima yanyu. 
John5:43 Jewe naje mw izina rya Data, ntimwanyakīra: ni hagira uwundi aza mw izina ryiwe ubgiwe, we muzomwākīra." 
John5:44 Mwoshobora kwizera mute, ari mwebge mwubahana, arikw icubahiro kiva ku Mana imwe nsa mutakirondera?" 
John5:45 Ntimugire ngo nzobarega kuri Data: harih’ ūbarega, ni Mose uwo mwishimiye." 
John5:46 Iyo mwizera Mose, nanje muba munyizeye, kukw ar’ ivyanje yanditse." 
John5:47 Ariko ni mutizera ivy’ uwo yanditse, amajambo yanje muzoyizera mute?" 
John6:1 Hanyuma y’ivyo Yesu avayo, yīgira hakurya y’ikiyaga c’i Galilaya citwa Tiberiya." 
John6:2 Ishengero ryinshi riramukurikira kuko ribonye ibimenyetso akora ku barwaye. 
John6:3 Yesu adūga umusozi, yicaranayo n’abigishwa biwe." 
John6:4 Kandi Pasika, imisi mikuru y’Abayuda, yari hafi." 
John6:5 Yesu yunamuye amaso, abona ishengero ryinshi riza kuri we, abaza Filipo, ati Tugurira hehe imitsima, ngo barye bose?" 
John6:6 Icatumye avuga artyo kwār’ ukumugeza, kuk’ ubgiwe yar’ azi ico agira akore." 
John6:7 Filipo aramwishura, at’ Imitsima y’idenariyo amajana abiri ntiyobakwira, nah’ umuntu wese yohabga gatoya." 
John6:8 Umwe mu bigishwa biwe, ni Andereya mwene nyina wa Simoni Petero, aramubgira," 
John6:9 ati Hano har’ umuhungu ari n’udutsima dutanu twa sayiri, n’udufi tubiri, ariko tumaze iki mu bantu bangaho?" 
John6:10 Yesu aravuga, ati Ni mwicarike abantu. Kand’ aho hantu hār’ ivyatsi vyinshi: nukw abantu baricara, igitigiri cabo cari nk’ibihumbi bitanu." 
John6:11 Maze Yesu yābīra ya mitsima, arayihezagira, ayigaburira abicaye, n’ifi na zo nk’uko bagomba." 
John6:12 Bamaze guhāga, abgira abigishwa biwe, ati Ni mutororokanye utumanyagu tw’ imisigazwa, hoye kugira igipfa ubusa." 
John6:13 Baradutororokanya, buzuza ibisimbo cumi na bibiri vy’utumanyagu twa ya mitsima itanu ya sayiri, utw’ abāriye bashigaje." 
John6:14 Bano bantu babonye ikimenyetso akoze, baravuga, bati N’ukuri uyu ni wa muntu avugishwa n’Imana yar’ akwiye kuza mw isi." 
John6:15 Yesu amenye ko bagira baze kumufata ngo bamwimike, asubira ku musozi ari wenyene gusa." 
John6:16 Buhwibiriye, abigishwa biwe bamanuka ku kiyaga," 
John6:17 batambukira mu bgato, bajabuka baja hakurya y’ikiyaga i Kaperinawumu. Bgateranye Yesu atarabashikīra;" 
John6:18 ikiyaga gitangura kuzungazunga, kuk’ umuyaga mwinshi uhuhuta." 
John6:19 Bamaze gusōza nka stadiyo mirongwibiri na zitanu canke mirongwitatu, babona Yesu agendesha amaguru hejuru ku kiyaga, arikw arēgēra ubgato, na bo baratinya." 
John6:20 Maz’ arababgira, ati Ni jewe, nta co mutinya." 
John6:21 Bumva bakunze kumushira mu bgato, buno nyene buca bushika i musozi aho bāja." 
John6:22 Bukeye bg’aho, rya shengero ryari rihagaze hakurya y’ikiyaga, rimenye kw ata bundi bgato bgāriho atari bumwe, kandi yuko na Yesu atājanye n’abigishwa biwe mu bgato, arikw abigishwa biwe ni bo bāri bījanye:" 
John6:23 (mugabo hār’ amato ajabuka ava i Tiberiya, afata hafi ya ha hantu bārīriye imitsima ihezagiwe n’Umwami Yesu)." 
John6:24 Nukw iryo shengero ribonye ko Yesu atari ho ari, n’abigishwa biwe na bo ar’ uko, rija mur’ ano mato na ryo, rijabuka i Kaperinawumu rirondera Yesu." 
John6:25 Bamubonye hakurya y’ikiyaga baramubaza, bati Mwigisha, waje ino ryari?" 
John6:26 Yesu arabishura, ati N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndababgire: Ntimundondera kuko mwabonye ibimenyetso, ariko n’uko mwariye kuri ya mitsima, mugahāga." 
John6:27 Ntimukorere ivyo kurya biyoka, ariko mukorere ivyo kurya bihoraho bizana ubugingo budashira, ni vyo Umwana w’umuntu azobaha, kukw ari we Imana Data yashizekw ikimenyetso." 
John6:28 Baramubaza, bati Tugire dute ngo dukore ibikorwa vy’Imana?" 
John6:29 Yesu na we arabishura, at’ Igikorwa c’Imana ngiki: n’uko mwizera uwo yatumye." 
John6:30 Nuko baramubaza, bati Non’ ukora ikimenyetso ki, ngo tukirābe tukwizere? Ukora ikimeze gite?" 
John6:31 Ba sogokuruza bacu bārīra manu mu bugaragwa, nk’uko vyanditswe ngo Yabahaye umutsima wo kurya uvuye mw ijuru." 
John6:32 Yesu arababgira, ati N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndababgire: Si Mose yabahaye umutsima uvuye mw ijuru; Data ni we abaha umutsima w’ukuri uvuye mw ijuru." 
John6:33 Kuk’ umutsima w’Imana ar’ ūmanuka uva mw ijuru, ugaha abari mw isi ubugingo." 
John6:34 Baramubgira, bati Mugenzi, na ntaryo uz’ uhore uduha uwo mutsima." 
John6:35 Yesu arababgira, ati Ni jewe mutsima w’ubugingo: ūza kuri jewe ntazosonza na mba, kand’ ūnyizera nta ho azogira inyota na mba." 
John6:36 Ariko narababgiye yuko mwāmbonye, muraheza ntimwizera." 
John6:37 Ico Data ampa cose kiranshikīra, kand’ uwoza kuri jewe sinomuhinda na gatoya." 
John6:38 Kuko ntākūwe mw ijuru no gukora ivyo nigombera, ariko nazanywe no gukora ivy’ uwantumye agomba." 
John6:39 Kand’ ic’ uwantumye agomba ngiki: agomba yuko mu vyo yampaye vyose hatagira na kimwe kinzimirana, ariko ngo nze nkizure ku musi w’iherezo." 
John6:40 Kukw iki ari co Data agomba: agomba yuk’ ūbona Umwana wese akamwizera, agira ubugingo budashira, nanje nkazomuzura ku musi w’iherezo." 
John6:41 Bun’ Abayuda baramwidodombera, kuko yavuze, ati Ni jewe mutsima wamanutse uva mw ijuru." 
John6:42 Bat’ Uyu si we Yesu mwene Yosefu? Na se na nyina turabazi: non’ avuga ate ngo Namanutse mva mw ijuru? 
John6:43 Yesu arabishura, ati Nta co mugira imyidodombo muri mwebge." 
John6:44 Nta n’umwe ashobora kuza kuri jewe Data yantumye atamukwegereye; nanje nzomuzura ku musi w’iherezo. 
John6:45 Mu majambo y’abavugishwa n’Imana handitswe, ngo Bose bazoba abigishijwe n’Imana. Uwumvise ivya Data wese akavyiga, aza kuri jewe." 
John6:46 S’ukugira ngo har’ uwabonye Data, atar’ uwavuye ku Mana: uwo ni we yabonye Data." 
John6:47 N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndababgire: Uwizera afise ubugingo budashira." 
John6:48 Ni jewe mutsima w’ubugingo. 
John6:49 Ba sogokuruza banyu bārīra manu mu bugaragwa, barapfa:" 
John6:50 uyu ni wo mutsima umanuka uva mw ijuru, ng’ umuntu awuryako ntapfe." 
John6:51 Ni jewe mutsima w’ubugingo wamanutse uvuye mw ijuru; ni hagira ūrya kur’ uwo mutsima azohorah’ ibihe bidashira: kand’ umutsima nzobaha n’umubiri wanje, utangirwa abari mw isi ngo bagire ubugingo." 
John6:52 Abayuda batanakw ibirake, bat’ Uyu ashobora ate kuduha umubiri wiwe ngo tuwurye?" 
John6:53 Yesu arababgira, ati N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndababgire: Ni mutarya umubiri w’Umwana w’umuntu, ngo munywe amaraso yiwe, nta bugingo mwogira muri mwebge." 
John6:54 Ūrya umubiri wanje akanywa amaraso yanje, ni we afise ubugingo budashira, nanje nzomuzura ku musi w’iherezo." 
John6:55 Kuk’ umubiri wanje ar’ ico kurya c’ukuri, n’amaraso yanje ar’ ico kunywa c’ukuri." 
John6:56 Ūrya umubiri wanje akanywa amaraso yanje, aguma muri jewe, nanje nkaguma muri we." 
John6:57 Nk’uko Data w’ubugingo yantumye, nanje ndiho kubga Data, ni k’ūndya na we azobaho kubganje." 
John6:58 Uwo ni wo mutsima wamanutse uvuye mw ijuru, si nk’uwo ba sogokuruza banyu bāriye, ariko bagapfa; ūrya uwo mutsima azohorah’ ibihe bidashira." 
John6:59 Ivyo yabivugiye mw isinagogi yigisha i Kaperinawumu. 
John6:60 Nuko benshi mu bigishwa biwe bavyumvise, baravuga, bat’ Iryo jambo riragoye: har’ uworyumva akarishobora?" 
John6:61 Yesu amenye mu mutima kw abigishwa biwe bidodomba ivyo, arababaza, ati Mbeg’ ivyo birabatsitaje?" 
John6:62 None bizomera bite ni mwabona Umwana w’umuntu adūga aja iyo yahora ubga mbere? 
John6:63 Impwemu ni zo zitera ubugingo, umubiri nta co umaze: amajambo mbabgiye n’impwemu n’ubugingo." 
John6:64 Ariko muri mwebge hariho bamwe batizera. Kuko Yesu yahereye ubga mbere azi abatizera ab’ ari bo, n’ūzomugura uw’ ari we." 
John6:65 Kand’ aravuga, ati Ni co catumye mbabgira kw ata wushobora kuza kuri jewe atabihawe na Data." 
John6:66 Kuva ico gihe benshi mu bigishwa biwe bamuva inyuma, ntibāba bakijana na we." 
John6:67 Yesu abaza bamwe cumi na babiri, ati Mbega namwe muragomba kwīgīra?" 
John6:68 Simoni Petero aramwishura, ati Tuje kwa nde ga Mugenzi? Kw ari wewe ufise amajambo y’ubugingo budashira," 
John6:69 natwe twarizeye, tumenya yuko wewe ur’ Uwera w’Imana." 
John6:70 Yesu aramwishura, ati Mbega si jewe nabatoranije uko mur’ icumi na babiri? Arik’ umwe muri mwebge n’umurwanizi." 
John6:71 Yavuga Yuda Isikaryota, mwene Simoni, kukw ari we yagira az’ amugure, yar’ uwo muri bamwe cumi na babiri." 
John7:1 Hanyuma y’ivyo Yesu agendagenda i Galilaya: ntiyashaka kugendagenda i Yudaya, kukw Abayuda bārondera ingene bomwica." 
John7:2 Imisi mikuru y’Abayuda yitwa iy’ Insago yarikw irashika. 
John7:3 Nuko bene nyina baramubgira, bati N’uve ino, uje i Yudaya, abigishwa bawe na bo barābe ibikorwa ukora;" 
John7:4 kukw ata wogira ico akora mu mpisho, na we ngw arondere kumenyekana. K’ukora ivyo, ni wiserure mu b’isi." 
John7:5 Kuko na bene nyina na bo batāmwizera. 
John7:6 Maze Yesu arabishura, at’ Igihe canje ntikiragera, arikw igihe canyu co, cama kiriho." 
John7:7 Ab’ isi ntibabanka, ariko jewe baranyanka, kuko mbavugira ibikorwa vyabo kw ari bibi." 
John7:8 Mwebge ni mudūge kumara iyo misi mikuru, ariko jeho sindayidūgako, kukw igihe canje kitaragera." 
John7:9 Ababgiye ivyo, aguma i Galilaya." 
John7:10 Bene nyina bamaze kudūga i Yerusalemu kumara iyo misi mikuru, na we aradūga, ntiyibonekeza, arikw agenda nk’uwomba." 
John7:11 Maz’ Abayuda bamurondera mur’ iyo misi mikuru, bati Mbega wa wundi ari hehe?" 
John7:12 Haba ivyongoshwe vyinshi mw ishengero bamuvuga: bamwe bati N’umuntu mwiza, abandi bat’ Oya, arazimiza abantu." 
John7:13 Ariko nta n’umwe yamuvuze atobora, kuko batinya Abayuda." 
John7:14 Ya misi mikuru igeze hagati, Yesu adūga mu rusengero, arigisha." 
John7:15 Abayuda baratangara, bati Mbeg’ uyu yakūye ubgenge hehe, atigishijwe?" 
John7:16 Maze Yesu arabishura, at’ Izi nyigisho zanje s’izanje, n’iz’ uwantumye." 
John7:17 Ni hāba har’ ūgomba gukora ivyo uwo akunda, azomenya izi nyigisho, ko zavuye ku Mana, canke ko mbivuga mvyigeneye." 
John7:18 Ūvuga ivyo yigeneye aba yironderera icubahiro; arik’ ūrondera icubahiro c’uwamutumye, ni we w’ukuri, kandi nta kugabitanya kuba kuri muri we." 
John7:19 Mbega Mose si we yabahaye ivyagezwe? Ariko muri mwebge nta n’umwe yitondera ivyo vyagezwe. Muronderera iki kunyica? 
John7:20 Ishengero riramwishura, rit’ Urimwo dayimoni! Ni nde ashaka kukwica?" 
John7:21 Yesu arabishura, ati Nakoze igikorwa kimwe, mwese muratangara." 
John7:22 Mose yabahaye ugukebga — mugabo ntikwavuye kuri Mose, ni kuri ba sogokuruza banyu — kandi murakeba umuntu kw isabato." 
John7:23 None se, k’umuntu akebga kw isabato, kugira ngw icagezwe ca Mose ntimukirenge, none jewe mumpōra iki ko kw isabato nakijije umuntu yiramvuriye?" 
John7:24 Ntimupfe guca imanza ku biboneka, ariko muce imanza z’ukuri." 
John7:25 Bamwe mu b’i Yerusalemu baravuga, bati Mbeg’ uwo si we bashaka kwica?" 
John7:26 Ehe avuga akararamango, nta co baruha bamubgira. Mbega harya abakuru bemeye vy’ ukuri k’uyo ari we Kristo?" 
John7:27 Uyo ko tuzi aho yaturutse, ariko Kristo ah’azozira, nta wuzi ah’ azoturuka." 
John7:28 Nuko Yesu arasemerera yigisha mu rusengero, ati Jewe muranzi, n’aho naturutse murahazi, kandi sinaje nitumye, arik’ uwantumye n’uw’ ukuri, mwebge ntimumuzi;" 
John7:29 jeho ndamuzi, kuko navuye kuri we, kand’ ari we yantumye." 
John7:30 Buno barondera ingene bomufata, ariko ntihagira ūmukozako n’intoke, kukw igihe ciwe kitaribgagere." 
John7:31 Benshi mw ishengero baramwizera baravuga, bati Kristo ni yaza, mugira ngw azokora ibimenyetso vyinshi birengeye ivyo uyu akora?" 
John7:32 Abafarisayo bumvise kw ishengero rimuvugana ivyo mu twongoshwe, abaherezi bakuru n’Abafarisayo batuma abagendanyi kumufata." 
John7:33 Maze Yesu aravuga, ati Hasigaye igihe gito nkiri kumwe namwe, nkaja ku wantumye." 
John7:34 Muzondondera, ariko ntimuzombona, kand’ iyo nzoba ndi ntimuzoshobora gushikayo." 
John7:35 Maz’ Abayuda baravugana, bati Mbeg’ uyo agira aje hehe, aho twebge tutazoshobora kumubona? Agira aje mu bāsābagiriye mu Bagiriki, ngw aze yigishe Abagiriki?" 
John7:36 Mbeg’ iryo jambo atubgiye n’iriki, ngo Muzondondera, ariko ntimuzombona, kandi ngw Iyo nzoba ndi mwebge ntimuzoshobora gushikayo?" 
John7:37 Nuko ku musi uherūkira ya misi mikuru, ni wo musi uruta iyindi, Yesu arahagarara, arasemerera, ati Namba har’ ūfise inyota, n’aze kuri jewe, anywe." 
John7:38 Ūnyizera, inzūzi z’amazi y’ubugingo zizotemba ziva mu nda yiwe, nk’ukw ivyanditswe bivuga." 
John7:39 Arikw ivyo yabivuze kuri Mpwemu, uwo abamwizera bāgira bahabge; kuko Mpwemu ataribgatangwe, kuko Yesu ataribgashike mu bgiza bgiwe." 
John7:40 Bamwe mw ishengero bumvise ayo majambo, bati N’ukuri uyu ni wa muntu avugishwa n’Imana." 
John7:41 Abandi bat’ Uyu ni we Kristo. Abandi bat’ Oya, mbega Kristo yova i Galilaya?" 
John7:42 Mbeg’ icanditswe ntikivuga ko Kristo azova mu ruvyaro rwa Dawidi, i Betelehemu, wa musozi Dawidi yabako?" 
John7:43 Ishengero riramupfa," 
John7:44 bamwe muri bo bashaka kumufata, ariko ntihāgira n’umwe amukozako n’intoke." 
John7:45 Nuko ba bagendanyi basubira ku baherezi bakuru n’Abafarisayo, na bo barababaza, bati Ko mutamuzanye?" 
John7:46 Abagendanyi barabishura, bat’ Erega ntihigeze kuboneka umuntu avuga nka we." 
John7:47 Abafarisayo barababaza, bati Mbega namwe mwajimijwe?" 
John7:48 Har’ umukuru n’umwe yamwizeye, cank’ Umufarisayo?" 
John7:49 Arikw abo bantu batazi ivyagezwe n’ibivume. 
John7:50 Nikodemo, umwe yaza kuri we mbere, yar’ umwe muri bo, arababaza," 
John7:51 ati Mbeg’ ivyagezwe vyacu biratsindisha umuntu batabanje kumwumva no kumenya ico yakoze? 
John7:52 Baramwishura, bati Mbega nawe ur’ uw’ i Galilaya? Sesa urābe yuko har’ ūvugishwa n’Imana yova i Galilaya. [" 
John7:53 Bose baca baritahira. 
John8:1 Yesu aja ku musozi wa Elayono. 
John8:2 Mu gaturuturu asubira mu rusengero, abantu bose baza ah’ ari, aricara arabigisha." 
John8:3 Abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe bo n’Abafarisayo bamuzanira umugore, afashwe asambana, bamushira hagati," 
John8:4 baramubgira, bati Mwigisha, uyu mugore bamuturumbukiyeko arikw arasambana." 
John8:5 Kandi Mose mu vyagezwe yatugeze kwicisha amabuye ben’ abo. None weho uvuga iki? 
John8:6 Arikw ivyo bābivuga ar’ ukumugeza, ngo bamukūrek’ urwitwazo rwo kumurega. Ariko Yesu arunama, yandikisha urutoke hasi." 
John8:7 Maze bakobeje kumubaza, arunamuka, arababgira, at’ Ūtagira icaha muri mwebge n’abe ari we abanza kumutera ibuye." 
John8:8 Asubira kwunama yandika hasi. 
John8:9 Na bo bavyumvise basohoka isorōsoro, uhereye k’ūkuze ugashitsa ku muto, Yesu asigara wenyene, bo na wa mugore yar’ ahagaze hagati." 
John8:10 Yesu yunamutse aramubaza, ati Yewe mugore, bamwe bakureze bari hehe? Nta n’umwe aguciriye urubanza?" 
John8:11 Na we ati Nta n’umwe, Mugenzi. Yesu aramubgira, ati Nanje singucira urubanza. Ni wīgīre, guhēra ubu ntuz’ usubire gukora icaha.]" 
John8:12 Yesu yongera kubabgira, ati Jewe nd’ umuco w’isi, ūnkurikira nta ho azogenda mu mwiza, arikw azogira umuco w’ubugingo." 
John8:13 Abafarisayo baramubgira, bat’ Ereg’ urishingira intahe, intahe yawe s’iy’ ukuri." 
John8:14 Yesu arabishura, ati Naho jewe nishingira intahe, intahe yanje n’iy’ ukuri, kuko nzi iyo navuye, n’iyo nja, ariko mweho ntimuzi iyo navuye cank’ iyo nja." 
John8:15 Mwebge muca urubanza nk’abantu, jeho nta n’umwe ncira urubanza." 
John8:16 Kandi naho jewe noca urubanza, urubanza rwanje rwoba urw’ ukuri, kuko ntari jenyene, ndi kumwe na Data yantumye." 
John8:17 Kandi no mu vyagezwe vyanyu handitswe kw intahe ishinzwe n’abantu babiri ar’ iy’ ukuri. 
John8:18 Jewe nd’ uwishingira intahe, kandi na Data yantumye aranshingira intahe na we." 
John8:19 Na bo baramubaza, bati So ari hehe? Yesu arabishura, ati Nta jewe, nta Data, nta we muzi; iyo muba munzi, na Data muba mumuzi." 
John8:20 Ayo majambo yayavugiye mw iyakīriro ry’amashikanwa, arikw arigisha mu rusengero; kandi nta n’umwe yamufashe, kukw igihe ciwe kitaribgashike." 
John8:21 Nuko yongera kubabgira, ati Jewe ndi mu kuhava, namwe muzondondera, kandi muzopfira mu vyaha vyanyu: jewe iyo nja mwebge ntimuzoshobora gushikayo." 
John8:22 Abayuda barabazanya, bati Mbeg’ azokwiyahura, kw agize ngw iy’ aja ntituzoshobora gushikayo?" 
John8:23 Na we arababgira, ati Mwebge mwamutse hasi, jeho namutse iyo hejuru; mwebge mur’ab’ iyi si, jeho sind’ uw’ iyi si." 
John8:24 Ico ni co gitumye mbabgira ko muzopfira mu vyaha vyanyu; kuko ni mutizera ko ndi We, muzopfira mu vyaha vyanyu." 
John8:25 Nuko baramubaza, bat’ Uri nde, wewe? Yesu arabishura, ati Nd’ ico nababgiye uhereye ubga mbere." 
John8:26 Mfise ivyo kubabarira vyinshi, no kubacira urubanza. Kand’ uwantumye n’uw’ ukuri; ivyo namwumvanye ni vyo mvuga mw isi." 
John8:27 Ariko bo ntibāmenya yukw ababgiye Se. 
John8:28 Nuko Yesu arababgira, at’ Aho muzomanikira Umwana w’umuntu, ni ho muzomenya ko ndi We, kandi kw ata co nkora nigeneye; uko Data yanyigishije, ni ko mbivuga." 
John8:29 Kand’ uwantumye turi kumwe na we, ntiyansize jenyene, kuko jewe na ntaryo nama nkora ibimuhimbara." 
John8:30 Avuze ivyo, benshi baramwizera." 
John8:31 Nuko Yesu abgira Abayuda bāri bamwemeye, ati Ni mwaguma mw ijambo ryanje, mur’ abigishwa banje vy’ukuri;" 
John8:32 kandi muzomenya ukuri, kand’ ukuri kuzobaha kwidegemvya." 
John8:33 Baramwishura, bati Tur’ uruvyaro rwa Aburahamu, nta ho twigeze kujakarira umuntu n’umwe: non’ uvuga ute ngo tuzohabga kwidegemvya?" 
John8:34 Yesu arabishura, ati N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndababgire: Ūkora icaha wese n’umuja w’icaha." 
John8:35 Umuja ntiyama atsindaje mu nzu, arik’ umwana we yama atsindaje." 
John8:36 Umwana ni yabaha kwidegemvya, muzoba abidegemvya nyakuri." 
John8:37 Ndazi ko mur’ uruvyaro rwa Aburahamu, yamara murondera ingene mwonyica, kukw ijambo ryanje ritagira ikibanza muri mwebge." 
John8:38 Jewe mvuga ivyo nabonye kuri Data; namwe mukora ivyo mwumvise kuri so. 
John8:39 Baramwishura, bati Aburahamu ni we data. Yesu arabishura, at’ Iyo muba mur’ abana ba Aburahamu, muba mukora ibikorwa nk’ivya Aburahamu." 
John8:40 Ariko none murondera ingene mwonyica, umuntu yababariye ivy’ ukuri, ivyo numvise ku Mana; Aburahamu ntiyagize artyo." 
John8:41 Mukora ibikorwa nk’ivya so. Baramubgira, bati Twebge ntitur’ ibivyarwa: dufise Data umwe, n’Imana." 
John8:42 Yesu arababgira, at’ Iy’ Imana iba ari So, muba munkunda, kuko jewe naje mvuye ku Mana; sinaje nitumye, ariko ni yo yantumye." 
John8:43 N’iki gituma mutamenya imvugo yanje? N’uko mudashobora kwumva ijambo ryanje. 
John8:44 Mwebge mur’ aba so wa Murwanizi, kand’ ivyo so yifuza ni vyo mushaka gukora. Uwo yahereye ubga mbere na mbere ar’umwicanyi, kandi ntiyahagaze mu kuri, kukw ata kuri kuri muri we. Iy’ avuga ibinyoma, avuga ivyiwe, kukw ar’ umunyabinyoma, kand’ ari we se wavyo." 
John8:45 Ariko jeho, kuko mvuga ivy’ ukuri, ntimunyemera." 
John8:46 Ni nde muri mwebge yonyagiriza icaha nakoze? Ko mvuga ukuri, n’iki gituma mutanyemera?" 
John8:47 Uw’ Imana yumva amajambo y’Imana; mwebge igituma mutumva, n’uko mutar’ ab’ Imana." 
John8:48 Abayuda baramwishura, bati None se ntitwavuze ukuri k’ur’ Umusamariya, kandi k’urimwo dayimoni?" 
John8:49 Yesu arabishura, ati Jewe sindimwo dayimoni, ariko nubaha Data, namwe ntimunyubaha." 
John8:50 Jewe sinironderera icubahiro, harih’ ūkindonderera, kandi ni we Kamaramagambo." 
John8:51 N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndababgire: Ni hagira uwitondera ijambo ryanje, ntazobona urupfu gushitsa ibihe bidashira." 
John8:52 Abayuda baramubgira, bati Noneho turamenye k’urimwo dayimoni. Aburahamu yarapfuye, n’abāvugishwa n’Imana n’uko, ariko wewe uvuze, uti Ni hagira uwitondera ijambo ryanje, nta ho azokwumviriza ku rupfu." 
John8:53 Mbeg’ uruta sogokuruza wacu Aburahamu? We ko yapfuye, n’abāvugishwa n’Imana na bo bakaba bārapfuye: wiyita nde?" 
John8:54 Yesu arabishura, ati Ni naba niha icubahiro, icubahiro canje kizoba ar’ ic’ ubusa: ūmpa icubahiro ni Data, uwo muvuga ngo n’Imana yanyu," 
John8:55 yamara ntimumuzi, ariko jewe ndamuzi. Kandi ni navuga ngo sindamuzi, nzoba mbaye umunyabinyoma nkamwe: ariko ndamuzi, kandi nitondera ijambo ryiwe." 
John8:56 Aburahamu sogokuruza wanyu yari yarahahamiye kubona umusi wanje, kandi yarawubonye, aranezerwa." 
John8:57 Nuko rer’ Abayuda baramubgira, bat’ Ube utaramara imyaka mirongwitanu, ngo warabonye Aburahamu?" 
John8:58 Yesu arababgira, ati N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndababgire: Aburahamu ataravuka, jewe namye ndiho." 
John8:59 Baca batora amabuye yo kumutera, maze Yesu arihisha, ava mu rusengero." 
John9:1 Arikw arahita, abona umuntu yavutse ar’ impumyi." 
John9:2 Abigishwa biwe baramubaza, bati Mwigisha, ni nde yakoze icaha, n’uyo, canke n’abavyeyi biwe, ko yavutse ar’ impumyi?" 
John9:3 Yesu arabishura, at’ Uyu ntiyakoze icaha, kandi s’abavyeyi biwe, ariko n’ukugira ngw ibikorwa vy’Imana bibonekere kuri we." 
John9:4 Twebge dukwiye gukora ibikorwa vy’uwantumye hakibona; buhava bgira, ata wugishobora gukora." 
John9:5 Nkiri mw isi, nd’ umuco w’isi." 
John9:6 Avuze ivyo, acira amate hasi, avurungisha amate utwondo, araheza amusīga utwo twondo ku maso;" 
John9:7 aramubarira, ati Genda wiyuhagire mu kidengeri Silowamu; (Silowamu risobanurwa ngo Mutumwa). Nukw aragenda ariyuhagira, agaruka abona." 
John9:8 Nukw ababanyi biwe, n’abāhora bamubona kw ar’ umusēzi, barabazanya, bati Mbeg’ uyu si we yahora yicaye asēgerereza?" 
John9:9 Abandi bati Ni we; abandi bat’ Oya, n’uwo basa. Na we arababgira, ati Ni jewe." 
John9:10 Nuko baramubaza, bati Mbega non’ amaso yawe yahumūtse ate?" 
John9:11 Na we arabishura, ati Wa muntu yitwa Yesu yavurunze utwondo, atunsīga ku maso, arambgira, ati Ja kuri Silowamu wiyuhagire; nuko ndagenda, ndiyuhagira, ndahumūka." 
John9:12 Baramubaza, bat’ Ari hehe? Ati Sindahazi." 
John9:13 Umwe yahora ar’impumyi bamujana ku Bafarisayo. 
John9:14 Kand’ uwo musi war’ isabato, Yesu yavurunzek’ utwondo, agahumūra amaso yiwe." 
John9:15 Abafarisayo basubira kumubaza ingene yahumūtse, na we arababgira, ati Yansīze utwondo ku maso, ndiyuhagira, ndahumūka." 
John9:16 Bamwe mu Bafarisayo baravuga, bat’ Uwo muntu ntava ku Mana, kukw ataziririza isabato. Abandi bati Mbeg’ umuntu w’umunyavyaha yoshobora ate gukora ibimenyetso bingana birtyo? Baramupfa." 
John9:17 Basubira kubaza umwe yahora ar’ impumyi, bati Weho uvuga kw ar’ iki, kuko yaguhumūye amaso? Na we ati N’ūvugishwa n’Imana." 
John9:18 Maz’ Abayuda ntibemera ivy’ uwo, yuko yamye ar’impumyi, agaheza agahumūka, kugeza aho bāhamagariye abavyeyi b’uwahumūtse," 
John9:19 barababaza, bati Mbeg’ uyu n’umwana wanyu, mwebge muvuga ko yavutse ar’ impumyi? None yahumūtse ate?" 
John9:20 Abavyeyi biwe barabishura, bat’ Uyu turazi kw ar’ umwana wacu, kandi ko yavutse ar’ impumyi;" 
John9:21 arikw icatumye abona ubu, ntitukizi, kandi n’uwamuhumūye, tweho ntitumuzi. Mumwibarize, n’umugabo, arivugira." 
John9:22 Abavyeyi biwe bāvugiye ivyo, kuko bātinya Abayuda, kukw Abayuda bāri bamaze kuja ingingo, ng’umuntu wese azokwatura Yesu kw ari Kristo acibge mw isinagogi." 
John9:23 Ni co catumye abavyeyi biwe bavuga, bati N’umugabo, ni mumwibarize." 
John9:24 Maze bahamagara ubugira kabiri wa muntu yahora ar’ impumyi, baramubgira, bati Ni wubahe Imana, twebge tuzi yuk’ uwo muntu ar’ umunyavyaha." 
John9:25 Na we arabishura, ati Namb’ ar’ umunyavyaha sindabizi: ico nzi ni kimwe, n’uko nar’ impumyi, none nkaba mbona." 
John9:26 Baramubaza, bati Yakugiriye ate? Yahumūye amaso yawe ate?" 
John9:27 Arabishura, ati Namaze kubibabgira, ko mutavyumvise? Mugombera iki gusubira kuvyumva? Mbega namwe mugomba kuba abigishwa biwe?" 
John9:28 Baramutuka, bati Ni wewe mwigishwa wiwe, natwe tweho tur’ abigishwa ba Mose." 
John9:29 Twebge tuzi yukw Imana yavuganye na Mose, arik’ uwo ntituzi ah’ aturuka." 
John9:30 Wa muntu arabishura, at’ Erega n’igitangaza ko mutazi ah’ aturuka, kand’ ari we yahumūye amaso yanje." 
John9:31 Turazi kw Imana itumviriza abanyavyaha, arik’ ūyubaha, agakora ivyo igomba, uwo ni we yumviriza." 
John9:32 Uhereye kera hose ntihumvikanye ko har’ umuntu yahumūye amaso y’uwavutse ar’ impumyi. 
John9:33 Iyaba uyo atāvuye ku Mana, nta co yoshoboye gukora." 
John9:34 Baramwishura, bati Wewe wavukiye mu vyaha gusa gusa, ni wewe utwigisha? Bamuhindira hanze." 
John9:35 Yesu yumvise ko bamuhindiye hanze, aja kumurāba, aramubaza, ati Mbega wizeye Umwana w’Imana?" 
John9:36 Na we aramwishura, ati Ni nde ga Mugenzi, nkamwizera?" 
John9:37 Yesu aramubgira, ati Wamubonye, kandi ni we muriko muravugana." 
John9:38 Na we ati Ndizeye, Mwami. Araheza aramupfukamira." 
John9:39 Yesu aravuga, ati Naje mur’ iyi si kuba agahinyuza, ngw abatabona babone, n’ababona babe impumyi." 
John9:40 Bamwe mu Bafarisayo bāri kumwe na we bumvise ivyo, bati Mbega natwe tur’ impumyi?" 
John9:41 Yesu arababgira, at’ Iyo muba mwar’ impumyi, nta caha muba mufise, ariko noneho muvuga muti Turabona: icaha canyu camaho." 
John10:1 N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndababgire: Ūdaca mw irembo ry’urugo rw’intama, arikw akūririra ahandi, uwo aba ar’ igisuma n’umwambuzi." 
John10:2 Arik’ ūca mw irembo ni we mwungere w’intama. 
John10:3 Umuteramyi w’irembo aramwugururira, kand’ intama zumva ijwi ryiwe; ahamagara iziwe ntama mu mazina yazo, akaziturutsa." 
John10:4 Kand’ iy’ amaze guturutsa iziwe zose, azija imbere, zikamukurikira kuko zizi ijwi ryiwe." 
John10:5 Arik’ uwo zitazi ntizomukurikira na mba, zomuhunga, kuko zitazi amajwi y’abandi." 
John10:6 Yesu abacira uwo mugani, ariko bo ntibatahura ivyo ababgira ivy’ ari vyo." 
John10:7 Nuko Yesu yongera kubabgira, ati N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndababgire: Ni jewe rembo ry’intama." 
John10:8 Abanyītangiye imbere bose bār’ ibisuma n’abambuzi, arikw intama ntizabumviye." 
John10:9 Ni jewe rembo, kand’ ūshika mu rugo wese aciye muri jewe arakizwa; agataha, agaturuka, akaronka icanya." 
John10:10 Igisuma ntikizanwa n’ikindi, atar’ ukwiba, n’ukwica, n’ugutikiza; nanje jeho nazanywe no kugira ngo zironke ubugingo, kandi ngo ziburonke busāgutse." 
John10:11 Ni jewe mwungere mwiza; umwungere mwiza yigura intama ziwe. 
John10:12 Arik’ umucangero, atar’ umwungere bgite, kand’ intama atar’ iziwe, iy’ abonye ibingira rije, ata intama, agahunga: ibingira rikazisahura, rikazishwiragiza." 
John10:13 Arahunga, kukw ar’ umucangero, atababaye intama." 
John10:14 Ni jewe mwungere mwiza, ndazi izanje, n’izanje ziranzi," 
John10:15 nk’uko Data anzi, nanje nkamumenya; kandi ndigura intama zanje." 
John10:16 Kandi mfise n’izindi ntama zitar’ izo mur’ uru rugo, na zo nyene birankwiye kuzija imbere, zizokwumva ijwi ryanje, hazoba umukuku umwe n’umwungere umwe." 
John10:17 Igituma Data ankunda, n’uko ndekura ubugingo bganje, ngo mpeze nsubire kubgābīra." 
John10:18 Nta n’umwe abunyaka, kuko mburekura kubganje: mfise ububasha bgo kuburekura, mfise n’ububasha bgo gusubira kubgābīra. Ico ni co cagezwe nahawe na Data." 
John10:19 Abayuda bongera kumupfa kubg’ ayo majambo; 
John10:20 benshi muri bo bat’ Arimwo dayimoni, kandi yāsaze: mumwumviririza iki?" 
John10:21 Abandi bat’ Ereg’ ayo majambo si nk’ay’ ūhagazweko na dayimoni: mbega dayimoni arashobora guhumūra amaso y’impumyi? 
John10:22 Maze haza imisi mikuru yo kwibuka uguhumanurwa kw’ urusengero i Yerusalemu: hāri mu rushana. 
John10:23 Yesu agendagenda mu rusengero mw ibaraza rya Salomo. 
John10:24 Abayuda baramukikiza, baramubaza, bat’ Uzogeza ryari gutera imitima yacu kujuragira? Asangw’ uri Kristo bidufoborere." 
John10:25 Yesu arabishura, ati Narababgiye, ariko ntimwizera: ibikorwa nkora mw izina rya Data, ni vyo binshingira intahe." 
John10:26 Ariko ntimwizera, kuko mutar’ abo mu ntama zanje." 
John10:27 Abābaye intama zanje bumva ijwi ryanje, nanje ndabazi, na bo barankurikira," 
John10:28 kandi nanje mbaha ubugingo budashira, nta ho bazokwigera bapfa rubi gushitsa ibihe bidashira, kandi nta wushobora kubanshikura mu kuboko kwanje." 
John10:29 Data yabampaye ni we aruta bose; nta wushobora kubashikura mu kuboko kwa Data. 
John10:30 Jewe na Data tur’ umwe. 
John10:31 Bun’ Abayuda bongera gutora amabuye, ngo bayamutere." 
John10:32 Yesu arababgira, ati Naberetse ibikorwa vyiza vyinshi bivuye kuri Data, ikibanteresha amabuye mur’ ivyo bikorwa n’ikihe?" 
John10:33 Abayuda baramwishura, bati Ntituguterera amabuye kubg’ igikorwa ciza, ariko n’uko warogose; kuko wewe ur’ umuntu ukīgira Imana." 
John10:34 Yesu arabishura, ati Mbega ntihanditswe mu vyagezwe vyanyu, ngo Navuze nti Mur’ imana?" 
John10:35 None ko yabise imana, bamwe ijambo ry’Imana ryashitseko (kand’ ivyanditswe ntibishobora guhinduka)," 
John10:36 mwebge mubgira mute uwo Data yejeje, akamutuma mw isi, ng’ Urarogose, kuko navuze nti Nd’ Umwana w’Imana?" 
John10:37 Asangwa ntakora ibikorwa vya Data, ntimunyemere;" 
John10:38 ariko ni nabikora, naho jewe mutanyemera, mupfe kwemera ibikorwa, kugira ngo mumenye, mutahure, yuko Data ari muri jewe, nanje nkaba muri Data." 
John10:39 Nuko bongera kurondera ingene bomufata, abava mu maboko." 
John10:40 Avayo, yongera kuja hakurya ya Yorodani, ha hantu Yohana yabatiriza ubga mbere, agumayo." 
John10:41 Benshi baza kuri we; baravuga, bati Yohana nta kimenyetso yakoze, arikw ivyo Yohana yavuze vyose kur’ uyu vyar’ ivy’ ukuri." 
John10:42 Kandi benshi bamwizererayo. 
John11:1 Hārih’ uwar’ arwaye, ni Lazaro w’i Betaniya, ni wa musozi Mariya na mwene nyina Marita bābako." 
John11:2 Uwo Mariya ni we yasīze Umwami Yesu amavuta atāmirana ku birenge, amuhanaguza umushatsi wiwe; uyo Lazaro yar’ arwaye ni we musaza we." 
John11:3 Bashiki biwe batuma kuri Yesu, bati Mugenzi, wa wundi ukunda ararwaye." 
John11:4 Yesu avyumvise aravuga, at’ Iyo ndwara s’iyo kumwica, ariko n’iyo gushimagirisha Imana, kugira ngo n’Umwana w’Imana imushimagirishe." 
John11:5 Kandi Yesu yarakunda Marita na mwene nyina na Lazaro. 
John11:6 Nuko yumvise kw arwaye, asībira aho hantu yar’ ari imisi ibiri." 
John11:7 Hanyuma y’ivyo abgira abigishwa biwe, ati Dusubire i Yudaya." 
John11:8 Abigishwa baramubgira, bati Mwigisha, Abayuda baheruka gushaka kugutera amabuye, non’ usubireyo?" 
John11:9 Yesu arabishura, ati Non’ isaha z’umurango s’icumi na zibiri? Ūgenda ku murango ntatsitara, kukw abona umuco w’iyi si." 
John11:10 Arik’ ūgenda mw ijoro aratsitara, kuk’ umuco utari muri we." 
John11:11 Amaze kuvuga ivyo, arababgira, ati Lazaro, umukunzi wacu, arasinziriye, nanje ndagiye kumukangura." 
John11:12 Nukw abigishwa baramubgira, bati Mugenzi, asangw’ asinziriye, azokira." 
John11:13 Yamara Yesu yavuga urupfu rwiwe, ariko bo bagira ngw avuga kuruhuka kwo gusinzira." 
John11:14 Buno Yesu avuga abifoboye, ati Lazaro yahwereye;" 
John11:15 ariko kubganyu ndanezerewe ko ntāriyo, kugira ngo muze mwizere; noneho ni muze tuje iy’ ari." 
John11:16 Toma ari we Hasa abgira abigishwa bagenzi biwe, ati Ngo tugende, dupfane na Yesu." 
John11:17 Nuko Yesu ashitse asanga amaze imisi ine mu mva. 
John11:18 I Betaniya hāri hafi y’i Yerusalemu nka stadiyo cumi na zitanu. 
John11:19 Nukw Abayuda benshi bāri baje kwa Marita na Mariya kubirura kubga musaza wabo. 
John11:20 Nuko Marita yumvise ko Yesu aje, aragenda aramusanganira; ariko Mariya asigara yicaye mu nzu." 
John11:21 Marita abgira Yesu, ati Mugenzi, iy’ uba wari hano, musazanje ntaba yāhwereye." 
John11:22 Kandi n’ubu ndazi kw ivyo wosaba Imana vyose, Imana yobiguha." 
John11:23 Yesu aramubgira, ati Musazawe azozuka." 
John11:24 Marita aramwishura, ati Ndazi kw azozuka mw izuka ryo ku musi w’iherezo." 
John11:25 Yesu aramubgira, ati Ni jewe kuzuka n’ubugingo. Ūnyizera n’iyo yoba yarapfuye, azobaho;" 
John11:26 kand’ ūriho wese anyizera, nta ho azokwigera apfa gushitsa ibihe bidashira. Urizeye ivyo?" 
John11:27 Na we at’ Ego me Mugenzi, nizeye k’uri Kristo, Umwana w’Imana, umwe wo kuza mw isi." 
John11:28 Avuze ivyo, asubira inyuma, yonjorora Mariya, mwene nyina, at’ Umwigisha ari hano, araguhamagaje." 
John11:29 Na we avyumvise, ava hasi n’ingoga, aja ah’ ari." 
John11:30 Yesu ntiyaribgashike mur’ iyo mihana, ariko yar’ akiri ha handi aho Marita yamusanganiriye." 
John11:31 Bun’ Abayuda bāri kumwe na Mariya mu nzu bamwirura, babonye avuye hasi n’ingoga, asohotse, baramukurikira, bagira ngw agiye kuririra ku mva." 
John11:32 Mariya ashitse aho Yesu ari, amubonye, yikubita imbere y’ibirenge vyiwe, ati Mugenzi, iy’ uba wari hano, musazanje ntaba yāhwereye." 
John11:33 Yesu abonye kw arira, n’Abayuda bāri kumwe na we barira, agira ikigumbagumba mu mutima, arawuhagarika," 
John11:34 arababaza, ati Mwamutaye hehe? Bati Mugenzi, ngwino urābe." 
John11:35 Yesu ararira. 
John11:36 Abayuda baravuga, bat’ Eh’ ingene yamukunda." 
John11:37 Ariko bamwe muri bo baravuga, bati Mbeg’ uyo yahumūye amaso y’impumyi, ntiyoshoboye kubuza uyo ngo ntapfe?" 
John11:38 Yesu yongera kugira ikigumbagumba mu mutima, ashika ku mva; kandi yar’ isenga yugajwe ikibuye." 
John11:39 Yesu aravuga, ati Ni mukūreh’ iryo buye. Marita mushiki w’uwapfuye, aramubgira, ati Mugenzi, ereg’ ubu aramaze kunuka, kw amaze imisi ine." 
John11:40 Yesu aramubgira, ati Sinakubgiye nti Ni wizera urabona ubgiza bg’Imana?" 
John11:41 Nuko bakūrah’ ikibuye. Buno Yesu ararangamiza, ati Data, ndagushima ko wanyumvirije." 
John11:42 Jewe nari nsanzwe nzi k’unyumviriza ubudasība, ariko mbivugishijwe n’ishengero rihagaze ngaha, kugira ngo bizere kw ari wewe wantumye." 
John11:43 Amaze kuvuga ivyo, asemerera n’ijwi rirenga, ati Lazaro, ngwino, sohoka." 
John11:44 Uwari yāpfuye arasohoka, azingiriwekw impuzu ku maguru no ku maboko, n’igitambara gipfutse mu maso hiwe. Yesu arababgira, ati Ni mumuhamburure, mumureke, agende." 
John11:45 Nuko benshi mur’ abo Bayuda bari baje kwa Mariya, babonye ico Yesu akoze, baramwizera," 
John11:46 ariko bamwe muri bo baja ku Bafarisayo, bababgira ivyo Yesu akoze." 
John11:47 Nukw abaherezi bakuru n’Abafarisayo bakoranya abanyekombe, barababaza, bati Mbega, tugire dute? K’uyu muntu akora ibimenyetso vyinshi." 
John11:48 Ni twamurekeraho durtyo, bose bazohava bamwizera, kand’ Abaroma bazoza batikize igisagara cacu n’ubgoko bgacu." 
John11:49 Arik’ umwe muri bo, ni Kayafa, yar’ umuherezi mukuru mur’ uwo mwaka, arababgira, ati Mwebge nta co muzi na mba," 
John11:50 kandi nta co mwiyumvira yukw ar’ ibibereye kubganyu k’umuntu umwe apfira abantu, hak’ ubgoko bgose buhona." 
John11:51 Ivyo ntiyabivuze avyigeneye, ariko, kuko yar’ umuherezi mukuru mur’ uwo mwaka, yavugishijwe ko Yesu agira apfire ubgo bgoko;" 
John11:52 kandi s’ubgo bgoko bgonyene, ariko ngw abana b’Imana bose bari basanzaye, abakoranirize hamwe." 
John11:53 Nuko bahēra uwo musi baja inama yo kumwica. 
John11:54 Maze Yesu ntiyaba akigenda yibonekeza mu Bayuda, arikw avayo, aja mu gihugu kiri hafi y’ubugaragwa mu gisagara citwa Efurayimu, agumanayo n’abigishwa." 
John11:55 Maze Pasika y’Abayuda yarikw irashika, benshi bava mu misozi, badūga i Yerusalemu, Pasika itarashika, ngo bihumanure." 
John11:56 Maze barondera Yesu, babazanya bahagaze mu rusengero, bati Mbega, mugira ngw iki? Ubgo ntazoza mur’ iyi misi mikuru?" 
John11:57 Kand’ abaherezi bakuru n’Abafarisayo bāri bashinze ng’ uwomenya ah’ ari aharange, ngo bamufate." 
John12:1 Nuko hasigaye imisi itandatu Pasika igashika, Yesu aja i Betaniya, ni ho Lazaro yaba, umwe Yesu yazuye mu bapfuye." 
John12:2 Barahamuzimanira; Marita yarahereza, kandi na Lazaro yar’ umwe wo mu bicaranye na we basangira." 
John12:3 Maze Mariya yābīra ingero y’amavuta atāmirana y’igiciro kinini cane, y’agati kitwa narada, ayasīga ku birenge vya Yesu, abihanaguza umushatsi wiwe, kand’ inzu yose itāmiranamw’ ayo mavuta." 
John12:4 Ariko Yuda Isikaryota, umwe mu bigishwa biwe, uwagira az’ amugure, aravuga," 
John12:5 ati N’iki catumye ayo mavuta ataguzwe idenariyo amajana atatu, ngo zihabge aboro?" 
John12:6 Arikw ivyo ntiyabivugishijwe no kubabara aboro, n’uko yar’ umwivyi, agendana umupfuko, agasotōra ku bibītswemwo." 
John12:7 Yesu aramubgira, ati N’umureke, kukw ivyo yabibīkiye umusi wo guhambga kwanje." 
John12:8 Aboro murāmana imisi yose, ariko jeho ntituja kwamana imisi yose." 
John12:9 Ishengero ryinshi ry’Abayuda rimenye kw ari ho ari, baraza, mugabo ntihāri kubga Yesu gusa, ariko kwār’ ukugira ngo barābe na Lazaro yazuye mu bapfuye." 
John12:10 Arikw abaherezi bakuru baja inama yo kwica Lazaro na we," 
John12:11 kuko kubgiwe Abayuda benshi bābavako bakizera Yesu. 
John12:12 Bukeye bg’aho, ishengero ryinshi ryari ryaje i Yerusalemu mur’ iyo misi mikuru, bumvise ko Yesu azayo," 
John12:13 bābīra amashami y’ibigazi, baja kumusanganira, barasemerera, bati Hoziyana: hashemezwe ūje mw izina ry’Uhoraho, ni we Mwami w’Abisirayeli." 
John12:14 Kandi Yesu abonye inyana y’indogoba, ayicarako, nk’uko handitswe," 
John12:15 ngo Nta co utinya, mukobga w’i Siyoni, rāba, Umwami wawe araje, ari ku nyana y’indogoba." 
John12:16 Ivyo abigishwa ntibabitahuye ubga mbere, ariko Yesu amaze guhabga ubgiza bgiwe, ni ho bibutse kw ivyo yavyandikiwe, kandi kw ari vyo bāmugiriye." 
John12:17 Nuko rya shengero rimushingira intahe, rimwe ryari kumwe na we hamwe yahamagara Lazaro ngw ave mu mva, akamuzura mu bapfuye." 
John12:18 Kandi ni co catumye ishengero rimusanganira, kuko bumvise ko yakoze ico kimenyetso." 
John12:19 Arikw Abafarisayo bavugana muri bo, bati Murabona kw ata co mumaze: rāba isi yose yamukondoreye inyuma." 
John12:20 Hār’ Abagiriki bamwe, mu bādūze gusenga mu misi mikuru," 
John12:21 bashikīra Filipo w’i Betsayida i Galilaya, baramwinginga, bati Mugenzi, turagomba kurāba Yesu." 
John12:22 Filipo araza abibarira Andereya; Andereya na Filipo baraza babibarira Yesu. 
John12:23 Yesu arabishura, at’ Igihe kirageze c’uk’ Umwana w’umuntu ahabga ubgiza bgiwe." 
John12:24 N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndababgire: Iy’ agatete k’ingano kataguye mw ivu ngo gapfe, kaguma uko kari konyene; arikw iyo gapfuye, gahunda impeke nyinshi." 
John12:25 Ūkunda ubugingo bgiwe azobubura, arik’ uwanka ubugingo bgiwe mur’ iyi si azobuzigama gushitsa ku bugingo budashira." 
John12:26 Ni hagira ūnkorera, n’ankurikire, kand’ aho nzoba ndi, umukozi wanje ni ho azoba: ni hagira ūnkorera, Data azomuha icubahiro." 
John12:27 Umushaha wanje urahagaze: none mvuge iki? Ngire nti Data, n’unkize iki gihe? Yamara ni co canzanye ngo nshike mur’ iki gihe." 
John12:28 Data, shimagiza izina ryawe. Maz’ ijwi riva mw ijuru, riti Ndarishimagije, kandi nzokwongera kurishimagiza." 
John12:29 Ishengero rihagazeho rivyumvise, riti N’umuturagaro. Abandi bati N’umumarayika avuganye na we." 
John12:30 Yesu arabishura, at’ Iryo jwi ntirije kubganje, ariko rije kubganyu." 
John12:31 Non’ ubu iyi si iciriwekw iteka, non’ ubu umutware w’iyi si agira ahindirwe hanze." 
John12:32 Nanje ni namanikwa hejuru y’isi, nzokwikwegerako bose." 
John12:33 Avuga ivyo ar’ukubamenyesha urupfu agira apfe. 
John12:34 Ishengero riramwishura, riti Twebge twumvise mu vyagezwe ko Kristo azohorah’ ibihe bidashira. Non’ uvuze ute ng’ Umwana w’umuntu akwiye kumanikwa? Mbeg’ uwo Mwana w’umuntu ni nde?" 
John12:35 Yesu arababgira, ati Hasigaye igihe gito umuco ukiri muri mwebge: ni mugende mugifise umuco, umwiza woye kubīriranirako. Ūgenda mu mwiza ntamenya iy’ aja." 
John12:36 Mugifise umuco, mwizere umuco, ngo mube abana b’umuco. Yesu amaze kuvuga ivyo, arīgīra, arabīhisha." 
John12:37 Ariko naho yakoreye ibimenyetso bingaho imbere yabo, ntibārushe bamwizera," 
John12:38 ngw ijambo ry’uwavugishwa n’Imana Yesaya rishike, ngo, Mwami, ni nde yizeye ico twumvise? Kand’ ukuboko kw’Uhoraho kwahishuriwe nde?" 
John12:39 Ni co catumye badashobora kwizera, kuko Yesaya yongeye kuvuga," 
John12:40 ati Yabahumye amaso, yabakomantaje imitima, Kugira ngo boye kubonesha amaso, no gutahurisha imitima, No guhindukira, Ngo mbakize." 
John12:41 Ivyo Yesaya yabivuze, kuko yabonye ubgiza bgiwe, kandi ni we yavuzeko." 
John12:42 Yamara no mu bakuru, benshi baramwizeye; ariko kubg’ Abafarisayo ntibāvyatura, kugira ngo boye gucibga mw isinagogi," 
John12:43 kuko bākunda icubahiro c’abantu kukirutisha icubahiro c’Imana. 
John12:44 Yesu arasemerera, at’ Ūnyizera, si jewe yizeye, ariko yizeye uwantumye:" 
John12:45 ūmbonye aba abonye uwantumye. 
John12:46 Naje mw isi nd’ umuco, kugira ng’ ūnyizera wese ntaz’ agume mu mwiza." 
John12:47 Ariko ni hagira uwumva amajambo yanje, ntayazigame, si jewe ndamucirakw iteka; kuko ntāzanywe no gucirakw iteka isi, ariko nazanywe no gukiza isi." 
John12:48 Arik’ ūngaya, ntiyemere amajambo yanje, ari n’ikizomutsindisha: ijambo navuze ni ryo rizomutsindisha ku musi w’umuhero." 
John12:49 Kukw ivyo ntabivuze mvyigeneye, ariko Data yantumye, ni we yangeze ivyo nkwiye kuvuga n’ivyo nkwiye gusigura." 
John12:50 Kandi ndazi yukw ivyo yageze ar’ ubugingo budashira. Nukw ivyo mvuga, mbivuga nk’uko Data yambariye." 
John13:1 Umusi wa Pasika utarashika, Yesu amenye kw igihe ciwe gishitse co kuva mw isi ngw aje kwa Se, uko yakunda abiwe bari mw isi, ni ko yabakunze gushitsa ku muhero." 
John13:2 Bakiriko bararya ku mugoroba, wa Murwanizi amaze kwinjiza ubuguranyi mu mutima wa Yuda Isikaryota, mwene Simoni," 
John13:3 Yesu yar’ azi ko Se yamuhaye vyose yabishize mu maboko yiwe, kandi ko yavuye ku Mana, kandi kw agira asubire ku Mana," 
John13:4 ava hasi mw irīro, akūra umutamana, yābīra icambazo, arakenyera;" 
John13:5 araheza asuka amazi mu mubehe, atangura kwoza ibirenge vy’abigishwa, no kubihanaguza icambazo akenyeje." 
John13:6 Nukw ashika kuri Simoni Petero, na we aramubaza, ati Mugenzi, ni wewe unyoza ibirenge?" 
John13:7 Yesu aramwishura, at’ Ico jewe ndiko ndakora, wewe nturibukimenye ubu: arik’ uzokimenya hanyuma." 
John13:8 Petero aramubgira, ati Nta ho uzokwigera unyoza ibirenge gushitsa ibihe vyose. Yesu aramwishura, ati Ni ntakwoza, nta ho tuzoba duhūriye." 
John13:9 Simoni Petero aramubgira, ati Mugenzi, ntugarukize ku birenge gusa, arik’ ushikane ku maboko no ku mutwe." 
John13:10 Yesu aramubgira, at’ Uwari yiyuhagiye nta kindi agomba, atar’ ukwoga ibirenge, kukw aba akeye umubiri wose: namwe murakeye, ariko si mwese." 
John13:11 Kuko yar’ azi ūzomugura uw’ ari we; ni co catumye avuga, ati Ntimukeye mwese." 
John13:12 Nukw ahejeje kubōza ibirenge, yābīra umutamana wiwe, yongera kwicara; arababaza, ati Mbega muramenye ico mbagiriye?" 
John13:13 Munyita Mwigisha na Shobuja, kandi mubivuga ko, kukw ari ko ndi." 
John13:14 Nuko rero, ko jewe mbogeje ibirenge, ndi Shobuja n’Umwigisha, namwe mukwiye kwozanya ibirenge." 
John13:15 Kuko mbahaye akarorero, kugira ngo nk’uko jewe mbagiriye, abe ari ko namwe mugira." 
John13:16 N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndababgire: Umushumba ntaruta shebuja, kandi n’intumwa ntiruta uwayitumye." 
John13:17 Ni mwamenya ivyo, muzoba muhiriwe ni mwabikora." 
John13:18 Simvuze mwese, kuko nzi abo natoranije, ariko n’ukugira ngw ivyanditswe bishike, ng’ Ūrya ivyo kurya vyanje ni we ambanguriye umugere." 
John13:19 Uhereye ubu ndabibabariye bitaraba, kugira ngw aho bizobera, muze mwizere ko ndi we." 
John13:20 N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndababgire: Uwākīra uwo nzotuma azoba anyakiriye, kand’ ūnyakīra aba yākiriye uwantumye." 
John13:21 Yesu avuze ivyo, ahagarika umutima, abivuga avyataguye, ati N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndababgire: Umwe muri mwebge agira angure." 
John13:22 Abigishwa bararābana, bazazaniwe uwo avuze uw’ ari we." 
John13:23 Hārih’ umwe mu bigishwa biwe yari yegamiye mu gikiriza ca Yesu bariko bararya, umwe Yesu yakunda." 
John13:24 Simoni Petero amuvunira akagohe, ati Tubgire uwo avuze uw’ ari we." 
John13:25 Uyo rero ahengamira inyuma, uko yari hano nyene mu gikiriza ca Yesu, aramubaza, ati Ni nde ga Mugenzi?" 
John13:26 Yesu aramwishura, at’ Uwo nkorezamw’ intore, nkayimuha, azoba ari we. Akojejemw’ intore, arayikūramwo, ayihereza Yuda, mwene Simoni Isikaryota." 
John13:27 Hanyuma y’iyo ntore, Satani aca yinjira muri we. Nuko Yesu aramubarira, at’ Ico ukora, gikore n’ingoga." 
John13:28 Ariko mur’ abo bicaranye nta n’umwe yamenye ico abimubgiriye. 
John13:29 Ariko kuko Yuda ari we yar’ afise umupfuko, bamwe bāgize ngo Yesu yamubgiye, ngo Gura ibizodukwira ku musi mukuru, canke ngw agire ico aha aboro." 
John13:30 Na we amaze kwābīra intore, aca asohoka ako kanya: kandi hāri mw ijoro." 
John13:31 Nukw amaze gusohoka, Yesu aravuga, ati Noneh’ Umwana w’umuntu arashimagijwe, kand’ Imana ishimagirijwe muri we." 
John13:32 Kand’ Imana, kw ishimagirijwe muri we, na yo izomushimagiriza muri yo, kand’ izomushimagiza vuba." 
John13:33 Bana bato, ndacari kumwe namwe akanya gato. Muzondondera, ariko, nk’uko nabgiye Abayuda, nt’ Aho nja ntimushobora gushikayo, ni ko none ndababgira namwe." 
John13:34 Ndabaha icagezwe gisha: ni mukundane; nk’uko nabakunze, abe ari ko namwe mukundana." 
John13:35 Ni mwagiriranira urukundo, ni ho bose bazomenya ko mur’ abigishwa banje." 
John13:36 Simoni Petero aramubaza, ati Mugenzi, uja hehe? Yesu aramwishura, at’ Aho nja ntushobora kunkurikira ubu, arik’ uzonkurikira hanyuma." 
John13:37 Petero aramubaza, ati Mugenzi, n’iki kimbuza kugukurikira n’ubu? Erega nzonakwigura." 
John13:38 Yesu aramwishura, at’ Ugize ng’ uzonyigura? N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndakubgire: Inkoko itarabika, uhava unyihakana gatatu." 
John14:1 Ntimuhagarike imitima yanyu, mwizere Imana, nanje munyizere." 
John14:2 I muhira kwa Data har’ amazu menshi, iy’ aba atariho, mba ndabibabgiye, kuko ngiye kubategurira ahanyu." 
John14:3 Kandi ko ngiye kubategurira ahanyu, nzogaruka kubajana i wanje, ngw aho ndi namwe abe ari ho muba." 
John14:4 Kand’ iyo nja murazi inzira ijayo. 
John14:5 Toma aramubgira, ati Mugenzi, ntituzi iy’ uja, dushobora dute kumenya inzira?" 
John14:6 Yesu aramubgira, ati Ni jewe nzira n’ukuri n’ubugingo: nta wushika kuri Data ntamujanye." 
John14:7 Iyo muba mwarammenye, na Data muba mumuzi. Uhereye ubu muramuzi, kandi mwamubonye." 
John14:8 Filipo aramubgira, ati Mugenzi, twereke So, bizoba bihaye." 
John14:9 Yesu aramubaza, ati Mbega ko nabanye namwe igihe kingana girtyo, nturakaruha ummenya ga Filipo? Ūbonye jewe aba abonye Data: non’ uvuga ute ngo Twereke So?" 
John14:10 Ntiwizeye ko jewe ndi muri Data, na Data ari muri jewe? Amajambo mbabgira s’ayo nigeneye, ariko Data aba muri jewe ni we akora ibikorwa vyiwe." 
John14:11 Ni munyizere ko ndi muri Data, na Data ari muri jewe, bibuze, mupfe kwizera kubg’ ibikorwa ubgavyo." 
John14:12 N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndababgire: Ūnyizera, ibikorwa jewe nkora na we azobikora: kand’ azokora ibibiruta, kuko jewe ngiye kwa Data." 
John14:13 Kand’ ico muzosaba cose mw izina ryanje nzogikora, kugira ngo Se ashimagizwe mu Mwana." 
John14:14 Ni mwagira ico musaba mw izina ryanje, nzogikora." 
John14:15 Ni mwankunda, muzokwitondera ivyagezwe vyanje," 
John14:16 nanje nzosaba Data, na we azobaha uwundi Mwitsa, ngw az’ abane namwe ibihe bidashira," 
John14:17 ni we Mpwemu w’ukuri, uwo ab’ isi badashobora kwākīra, kuko batamubona, kandi batamuzi; mweho muramuzi, kukw abana namwe kand’ azoba muri mwebge." 
John14:18 Sinzobasiga nk’impfuvyi, nzoza kuri mwebge." 
John14:19 Hasigaye igihe gito, ab’ isi ntibabe bakimbona, ariko mweho muzombona; kuko ndiho, namwe muzobaho." 
John14:20 Uwo musi muzomenya ko ndi muri Data, namwe muri muri jewe, nanje ndi muri mwebge." 
John14:21 Ūri n’ivyagezwe vyanje akavyitondera, uwo ni we ankunda, kand’ ūnkunda azokundwa na Data, nanje nzomukunda, kandi nzomwihishurira." 
John14:22 Yuda (atari Isikaryota), aramubaza, ati Mugenzi, bibaye bite, k’ugira wihishurire twebge, ntiwihishurire ab’ isi?" 
John14:23 Yesu aramwishura, ati Ni hagira ūnkunda, azokwitondera ijambo ryanje, kandi Data azomukunda, maze tuzoza kuri we, tubane na we." 
John14:24 Ūtankunda ntiyitondera amajambo yanje, kand’ ijambo mwumva s’iryanje, ariko n’irya Data yantumye." 
John14:25 Ivyo ndabibabariye nkiri kumwe namwe," 
John14:26 arik’ Umwitsa, ari we Mpwemu Yera, uwo Data azorungika mw izina ryanje, ni we azobigisha vyose, kand’ azobibutsa ivyo nababariye vyose." 
John14:27 Amahoro ndayabasigaranye, amahoro yanje ndayabagabiye. Jeho simbagabira nk’ukw ab’ isi bagaba. Imitima yanyu ntihagarare, kandi ntitinye." 
John14:28 Mwumvise ko nababgiye, nti Ndagiye, ariko nzobagarukako. Iyo muba munkunda, muba munezerejwe n’uko ngiye kwa Data, kuko Data ari we anduta." 
John14:29 Nuko none ndabibabgiye bitaraba, ngw aho bizobera muze mwizere." 
John14:30 Sinkivugana namwe vyinshi, kuk’ umwami w’isi ari mu kuza, yamara muri jewe nta kintu ahafise;" 
John14:31 ariko n’ukugira ngw ab’ isi bamenye ko nkunda Data, kand’ uko Data yangeze kw ari ko nkora. Ve hasi, tuve hano tugende." 
John15:1 Jewe nd’umuzabibu w’ukuri, kandi Data ni nyene wo." 
John15:2 Ishami ryose ryo muri jewe ritāma, arikūraho; kand’ iryama ryose araritūtūrira, ngo rirushirize kwama." 
John15:3 N’ubu mwebge mumaze kwezwa kubg’ ijambo nababgiye. 
John15:4 Ni mugume muri jewe, nanje ngume muri mwebge. Nk’ukw ishami ritabasha kwama ubgaryo, ritagumye mu muzabibu, ni ko namwe mutabibasha, mutagumye muri jewe." 
John15:5 Ni jewe muzabibu, namwe mur’ amashami: ūguma muri jewe, nanje nkaguma muri we, uwo ni we yama cane, kukw ata co mubasha gukora mutamfise." 
John15:6 Umuntu n’ataguma muri jewe atabga nk’ukw’ ishami ritererwa inyuma y’uruzabibu, akuma; maze bakayatororokanya, bakayaterera mu muriro, agasha." 
John15:7 Ni mwaguma muri jewe, amajambo yanje akaguma muri mwebge, musabe ico mugomba cose, kizobabera kuno." 
John15:8 Mur’ ivyo Data arashimagizwa, ni mwama cane, kandi mukaba abigishwa banje." 
John15:9 Nk’uko Data yankunze, ni ko nanje nabakunze: ni mugume mu rukundo rwanje." 
John15:10 Ni mwitondera ivyagezwe vyanje, muzoguma mu rukundo rwanje, nk’uko nanje nitondeye ivyagezwe vya Data, nkaguma mu rukundo rwiwe." 
John15:11 Ivyo mbibabgiye, kugira ng’umunezero wanje ube muri mwebge, kandi n’umunezero wanyu wuzuzwe." 
John15:12 Ngiki icagezwe canje: ni mukundane, nk’uko nabakunze." 
John15:13 Nta wogira urukundo ruruta urw’ uk’ umuntu yigura abakunzi biwe. 
John15:14 Mur’ abakunzi banje, ni mwakora ivyo mbagera." 
John15:15 Sinkibita abashumba, kuk’ umushumba atamenya ico shebuja akora; ariko mweho nabise abakunzi, kukw ivyo numvanye Data vyose nabibamenyesheje." 
John15:16 Si mwebge mwantoranije, ariko ni jewe nabatoranije, nabashizeho kugira ngo mugende murāma imbuto, kandi ngw imbuto zanyu zigumeho, kugira ngw ico muzosaba Data cose mw izina ryanje, akibahe." 
John15:17 Ivyo ndabibageze kugira ngo mukundane. 
John15:18 Isi ni yabanka, mumenye ko jewe yabanje kunyanka, itarabanka." 
John15:19 Iyo muba ab’ isi, isi iba ikunze icayo, maze kuko mutar’ ab’ isi, ariko nabatoranije mu b’isi, ni co gituma isi ibanka." 
John15:20 Mwibuke rya jambo nababgiye, nt’ Umushumba ntaruta shebuja; namba bārampamye, namwe bazobahama; namba bāritondeye ijambo ryanje, n’iryanyu bazoryitondera." 
John15:21 Arikw ivyo vyose bazobibagirira babahōra izina ryanje, kuko batazi uwantumye." 
John15:22 Iyo ntaba naraje ngo ngire ico mbabarira, nta caha baba bafise, ariko none ntibari n’ico bireguza icaha cabo." 
John15:23 Ūnyanka aba yanka na Data. 
John15:24 Iyo ntaba narakoreye ibikorwa muri bo bitigeze gukorwa n’uwundi, nta caha baba bafise, ariko noneho twe na Data baratubonye, baraheza baratwanka." 
John15:25 Ariko vyabaye birtyo kugira ngw ijambo ryanditswe mu vyagezwe vyabo rishike, ngo Bānyankiye ubusa." 
John15:26 Arik’ Umwitsa ah’ azozira, uwo nzobarungikira ava kuri Data, ni we Mpwemu w’ukuri akomoka kuri Data, uwo ni we azonshingira intahe," 
John15:27 kandi namwe nyene muranshingira intahe, kuko mwari kumwe nanje uhereye mbere na mbere." 
John16:1 Ico mbabaririye ivyo, n’ukugira ngo ntimuze mutsitazwe." 
John16:2 Bazobaca mu masinagogi, kand’ igihe kigiye kuza, ūzobīca wese azogira ngw agiriye Imana ikimazi." 
John16:3 Kand’ ivyo bazobikora kuko batamenye Data, nanje ntibāmmenye." 
John16:4 Ico mbabaririye ivyo, n’ukugira ngw igihe cavyo ni cashika, muze muvyibuke ko nanje nabibabgiye. Uhereye ubga mbere sinaribgabibabgire, kuko nari nkiri kumwe namwe." 
John16:5 None ngira ngende ku wantumye, kandi nta n’umwe muri mwebge arushe ambaza at’ Uja hehe?" 
John16:6 Ariko kuko mbabariye ivyo, umubabaro waciye wuzura mu mitima yanyu." 
John16:7 Ariko jewe ndababgira ukuri: Ikizogira ico kibamarira, n’uko jewe ngenda; kuko ni ntagenda, Umwitsa ntazoza kuri mwebge: ariko ni nagenda nzomubarungikira." 
John16:8 Uwo ni yaza, azohinyuza ab’ isi, abemeze ivy’ icaha, n’ivy’ ukugororoka, n’ivy’ amateka;" 
John16:9 ivy’ icaha, kuko batānyizeye," 
John16:10 ivy’ ukugororoka, kuko nja kwa Data, kandi namwe muzoba mutakimbona," 
John16:11 ivy’ amateka, kuk’ umwami w’iyi si yaciriwekw iteka." 
John16:12 Nari ngifise vyinshi vyo kubabgira, ariko ntimushobora kuvyihanganira ubu." 
John16:13 Arik’ uwo Mpwemu w’ukuri ni yaza, azobarōngōra abashitse ku kuri kwose, kukw atazovuga ivyo yigeneye, arikw ivy’ azokwumva vyose ni vyo azovuga, kand’ azobamenyesha ibigira bize." 
John16:14 Uwo azoshimagiza jewe, kukw azokwābīra ku vyanje, akabibamenyesha." 
John16:15 Ivyo Data afise vyose n’ivyanje, ni co gitumye mvuga, nti Yābīra ku vyanje, akabibamenyesha." 
John16:16 Hasigaye igihe gito ntimube mukimbona, maze hazoca ikindi gihe gito musubire kumbona."
