John16:17 Bamwe mu bigishwa biwe barabazanya, bati Mbeg’ ivyo atubgiye n’ibiki ngo Hasigaye igihe gito ntimube mukimbona, ngo Maze hazoca ikindi gihe gito musubire kumbona, kandi ngo Kuko nja kwa Data?" 
John16:18 Kandi bat’ Ivyo atubgiye n’ibiki, ngw Igihe gito? Ntitumenye ico avuze ic’ ari co." 
John16:19 Yesu amenya ko bagomba kumubaza, arababaza, ati Mbega mubazanya ic’ ari co, ko mbabariye nti Hasigaye igihe gito ntimube mukimbona, nti Maze hazoca ikindi gihe gito musubire kumbona?" 
John16:20 N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndababgire: Mweho muzorira muboroge, arikw ab’ isi bo bazonezerwa; mweho muzobabara, arik’ umubabaro wanyu uzocika umunezero." 
John16:21 Umugore iy’ aramutswe, aja mu mubabaro, kukw igihe ciwe kigeze, arikw iy’ umwana amaze kuvuka ntaba acibuka kugorwa kwiwe, kukw anezerejwe n’uk’ umuntu avutse mw isi." 
John16:22 Ni ko namwe muri mu mubabaro, ariko nzosubira kubabona, kand’ imitima yanyu izonezerwa, umunezero wanyu nta n’umwe azowubanyaga." 
John16:23 Kur’ uwo musi nta na kimwe muzombaza. N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndababgire: Ni hagira ico musaba Data cose azokibaha mw izina ryanje." 
John16:24 Kugeza ubu nta co mwasavye mw izina ryanje; musabe muzohabga, ng’umunezero wanyu wuzuzwe." 
John16:25 Ivyo mbibabgiriye mu migani, arikw igihe kizoza sinzoba ngisubira kuvuganira namwe mu migani, mugabo nzobabgira ivya Data mbifoboye." 
John16:26 Kur’ uwo musi muzosaba mw izina ryanje, kandi simbabgira ngo nzobasabira Data." 
John16:27 Kuko Data na we ubgiwe abakunda, kuko mwankunze kandi mwizeye ko naturutse ku Mana." 
John16:28 Navuye kwa Data, nza mw isi; ikindi, isi ndiko ndayivamwo, nje kwa Data." 
John16:29 Abigishwa biwe baravuga, bat’ Ubuho urabifoboye, nta mugani uduciriye." 
John16:30 Ubuho tumenye k’uzi vyose, kandi ko kubgawe utarinda ko hogira ūkubaza; ni co gituma twizera ko waturutse ku Mana." 
John16:31 Yesu arabishura, ati Mbega noneho murizeye?" 
John16:32 Igihe kigira kize, mbere kirashitse, aho muhava musābagira, umuntu wese aje mu vyiwe, munte jenyene, ariko sindi jenyene, kuko Data ari kumwe nanje." 
John16:33 Ivyo mbibabgiye, kugira ngo mugire amahoro muri jewe. Mw isi muri n’amarushwa, ariko ni muhūmure, jewe naranesheje isi." 
John17:1 Yesu avuze ivyo, arangamiza mw ijuru, ati Data, igihe kirashitse: shimagiza Umwana wawe, ng’ Umwana agushimagize;" 
John17:2 nk’uko wamuhaye ububasha ku bafise umubiri bose, ngw abo wamuhaye bose abahe ubugingo budashira." 
John17:3 Ubu ni bgo bugingo budashira, ko bamenya wewe, Imana yonyene y’ukuri, n’uwo watumye, Yesu Kristo." 
John17:4 Nagushimagije mw isi, nnonosoye igikorwa wampaye gukora." 
John17:5 Na none Data, unshimagizanye nawe, unshimagirishije bga bgiza nahoranye ndi kumwe nawe, isi itararemwa." 
John17:6 Nahishuriye izina ryawe abantu wampaye mu b’isi; bar’ abawe, urabampa, kandi bitondeye ijambo ryawe." 
John17:7 None bamenye yukw ivyo wampaye vyose biva kuri wewe: 
John17:8 kukw amajambo wampaye nayabahaye, na bo bakayākīra, bakamenya vy’ukuri ko naturutse kuri wewe; bakizera kw ari wewe wantumye." 
John17:9 Ndabasabira; sinsabira ab’ isi, ariko nsabira abo wampaye, kukw ar’ abawe;" 
John17:10 kand’ ivyanje vyose n’ivyawe, n’ivyawe na vyo n’ivyanje, kandi nashimagijwe muri bo." 
John17:11 Sinkiri mw isi, ariko bo bari mw isi, nanje ndaje kuri wewe. Data wera, ubazigamire mw izina ryawe wampaye, ngo babe umwe nk’uko natwe turi." 
John17:12 Nkiri kumwe na bo, nabazigamiye mw izina ryawe wampaye. Narabashibamyeko, kandi nta n’umwe muri bo yapfuye rubi, atari wa mwana wo gupfa rubi, kugira ngw ivyanditswe bishike." 
John17:13 Ariko none ndaje kuri wewe, kand’ ibi mbivuga ndi mw isi, kugira ngo bagire umunezero wanje wuzure muri bo." 
John17:14 Nabahaye ijambo ryawe; kand’ ab’ isi barabanka, kukw atar’ ab’ isi, nk’uko nanje ntar’ uw’ isi." 
John17:15 Singusaba ng’ ubakūre mw isi, ariko ng’ ubarinde wa Mubi." 
John17:16 S’ab’ isi, nk’uko nanje ntar’ uw’ isi." 
John17:17 Ubeze mu kuri: ijambo ryawe ni ryo kuri. 
John17:18 Nk’uko wantumye mw isi, ni ko nanje nabatumye mw isi:" 
John17:19 kandi nanje niyeza kubgabo, kugira ngo na bo babe bejejwe mu kuri." 
John17:20 Sinsabira aba gusa, ariko ndasabira n’abo bazonyizera kubg’ ijambo ry’aba," 
John17:21 kugira ngo bose babe umwe, nk’uko wewe, Data, uri muri jewe, nanje nkaba muri wewe, ngo na bo abe ari ko baba muri twebge, ngw isi yizere kw ari wewe wantumye." 
John17:22 Nanje nabahaye ubgiza wampaye, ngo babe umwe, nk’uko natwe tur’ umwe." 
John17:23 Jewe mbe muri bo, nawe ube muri jewe, ngo bahīngūrwe babe umwe, kugira ngw isi imenye kw ari wewe wantumye, ukabakunda, nk’uko wankunze." 
John17:24 Data, abo wampaye ndagomba kw aho ndi na bo bahabana nanje, ngo barābe ubgiza bganje wampaye, kuko wankunze itanguriro ry’isi ritarashirwaho." 
John17:25 Data ugororotse, isi ntiyakumenye, ariko jewe narakumenye, n’aba na bo bamenye kw ari wewe wantumye." 
John17:26 Nabamenyesheje izina ryawe, kandi nzoribamenyesha, ng’ urukundo wankunze rube muri bo, nanje mbe muri bo." 
John18:1 Yesu avuze ivyo, avanayo n’abigishwa biwe afata hakurya y’umugezi witwa Kidironi; aho hār’ itongo: ashikaho, bo n’abigishwa biwe." 
John18:2 Kandi na Yuda amugura yar’ azi aho hantu, kuko Yesu yahora ajanayo n’abigishwa biwe kenshi." 
John18:3 Nuko Yuda amaze guhabga n’abaherezi bakuru n’Abafarisayo ingabo z’abasoda, bo n’abagendanyi, ajayo, bari n’amatara n’ibimuri n’ibirwanishwa." 
John18:4 Nuko Yesu amenye ibigira bimubeko vyose, arabasanganira, arababaza, ati Murondera nde?" 
John18:5 Na bo baramwishura, bati Yesu Umunyanazareti. Arababgira, ati Ni jewe. Kandi Yuda, amugura, yar’ ahagararanye na bo." 
John18:6 Amaze kubabarira, ati Ni jewe, bagenza imigongo, bagwa hasi." 
John18:7 Na we asubira kubabaza, ati Murondera nde? Na bo bati Yesu Umunyanazareti." 
John18:8 Yesu arabishura, ati Mbabgiye kw ari jewe: asangw’ ari jewe murondera, mureke aba, bīgīre." 
John18:9 Ukwo kwar’ ukugira ngo rya jambo yavuze rishike, ngo Mu bo wampaye nta n’umwe najimije." 
John18:10 Simoni Petero yari n’inkota, arayisokōra, aca ugutwi kw’i buryo kw’umuntu w’umuherezi mukuru: uwo muntu yitwa Malikusi." 
John18:11 Maze Yesu abarira Petero, ati Subiza inkota mu rwubati: mbeg’ igikombe Data yampaye ndeke kukinywa?" 
John18:12 Nukw abasoda n’umukuru w’abagabisha babo n’abagendanyi b’Abayuda bafata Yesu, baramuboha," 
John18:13 babanza kumujana kwa Anasi, kuko yari sebukwe wa Kayafa umuherezi mukuru wo mur’ uwo mwaka." 
John18:14 Kandi Kayafa ni we yari yagīriye inama Abayuda, yukw ar’ ibibereye k’umuntu umwe apfira ubgo bgoko." 
John18:15 Simoni Petero akurikira Yesu, bo n’uwundi mwigishwa. Uwo mwigishwa yar’ azinanyi n’umuherezi mukuru, ashikana na Yesu mu rugo rw’uwo muherezi mukuru," 
John18:16 ariko Petero asigara ahagaze kw irembo. Wa wundi mwigishwa yar’ azinanyi n’umuherezi mukuru, ashika kw irembo, avugana n’umukumirizi, araheza ashikana Petero imbere." 
John18:17 Maz’ iyo ncoreke ikumīra ibaza Petero, iti Mbega nawe uri mu bigishwa b’uyo muntu? Petero at’ Oya, sindimwo." 
John18:18 Abashumba n’abagendanyi bāri bahagaze bacanye umuriro w’amakara, kuko hār’ imbeho, bariko barōta; kandi Petero na we yari kumwe na bo, ahagaze yōta." 
John18:19 Nuk’ umuherezi mukuru asiguza Yesu ivy’ abigishwa biwe n’inyigisho ziwe. 
John18:20 Yesu aramwishura, ati Nabarira ab’ isi mvyeruye, nahora nigishiriza mu masinagogi no mu rusengero ah’ Abayuda bose bakoranira, nta co navugiye mu mpisho." 
John18:21 Umbarije iki? Baza abāhora bavyumva ico nababariye: erega ni bo bazi ivyo navuze. 
John18:22 Avuze artyo, umwe mu bagendanyi ahagazeho akubita Yesu urushi, at’ Uko ni ko wishura umuherezi mukuru?" 
John18:23 Yesu aramubaza, ati Namba mvuze nabi, nyagiriza ico kibi; ariko namb’ ari neza, unkubitiye iki?" 
John18:24 Nuko Anasi amurungika aboshwe kwa Kayafa umuherezi mukuru. 
John18:25 Simoni Petero yar’ ahagaze yōta; nuko baramubaza, bati Mbega nawe uri mu bigishwa biwe? Na we arahakana, at’ Oya, sindimwo." 
John18:26 Umwe mu bashumba b’umuherezi mukuru, yar’ incuti y’umwe Petero yaciye ugutwi, aramubaza, ati Sinakubonye uri kumwe na we muri rya tongo?" 
John18:27 Maze Petero yongera kubihakana, ako kanya inkoko ica irabika." 
John18:28 Bakūra Yesu kwa Kayafa, bamujana mw iboma: hāri mu mutwenzi. Arik’ ubgabo ntibinjira mw iboma, ngo boye kwihumanya, kugira ngo babone ingene barya Pasika." 
John18:29 Kubg’ ivyo Pilato arasohoka aja aho bari, arababaza, at’ Ikirego mufise kur’ uyu muntu n’igiki?" 
John18:30 Baramwishura, bat’ Ugira ng’ uyu, iyaba atākoze ibibi tuba tumukuzaniye?" 
John18:31 Nuko Pilato arababgira, ati Ni mumujane mwebge, mumucire urubanza nk’ukw ivyagezwe vyanyu bivuga. Abayuda baramwishura, bat’ Erega twebge ntitwemererwa kwica umuntu." 
John18:32 Ngw ijambo rya Yesu rishike, iryo yavuze abamenyesha urupfu azopfa urw’ ari rwo." 
John18:33 Nuko Pilato asubira mw iboma, ahamagaza Yesu, aramubaza, ati Ni wewe Mwami w’Abayuda?" 
John18:34 Yesu ati Mbeg’ ivyo ubibajije kubgawe, canke n’abandi bakubariye ivyanje?" 
John18:35 Pilato ati Mbega nanje nd’ Umuyuda? Ab’ ubgoko bganyu n’abaherezi bakuru ni bo bakunzaniye. Wakoze iki? 
John18:36 Yesu aramwishura, at’ Ubgami bganje s’ubgo mur’ iyi si; iyaba ubgami bganje bgar’ ubgo mur’ iyi si, abagendanyi banje baba bārwanye, ngo simpabge Abayuda. Ariko noneh’ ubgami bganje s’ubg’ ino." 
John18:37 Nuko Pilato aramubaza, at’ Ubgo wewe ur’ umwami? Yesu ati Ni wewe uvyivugiye ko nd’ umwami. Iki ni co navukiye, kand’ iki ni co canzanye mw isi, n’ukugira ngo nshingire intahe ukuri. Uw’ ukuri wese yumva ijwi ryanje." 
John18:38 Pilato aramubaza, ati Mbeg’ ukuri n’iki? Amaze kuvuga ivyo, asubira gusohoka, aja ah’ Abayuda bari, arababgira, ati Jewe nta gicumuro mbonye kuri we." 
John18:39 Ariko musanganywe umugenzo ko mbarekurira umwe mu misi ya Pasika: none muragomba ko mbarekurira umwami w’Abayuda? 
John18:40 Nuko basubira gusemerera, bati S’uyo, ariko turekurire Baraba. Yamara Baraba yar’ umwambuzi." 
John19:1 Maze Pilato afata Yesu, aramukubitisha." 
John19:2 Abasoda na bo batsiba igitsibo c’amahwa bakimwambika mu mutwe, baraheza bamwambika impuzu y’inyambarabami." 
John19:3 Baramwēgēra, bati Ndagize bgakeye, Mwami w’Abayuda. Maze baramubīngūra." 
John19:4 Maze Pilato asubira gusohoka, arababgira, at’ Ehe ndamusohokanye aho muri, ngo mumenye kw ata gicumuro mbonye kuri we." 
John19:5 Nuko Yesu asohoka yambaye ico gitsibo c’amahwa na ya mpuzu y’inyambarabami. Pilato arababgira, at’ Ehe rāba uwo muntu!" 
John19:6 Maz’ abaherezi bakuru n’abagendanyi bamubonye, barasemerera, bati Mubambe, mubambe. Pilato arababgira, ati Ni mube ari mwebge mumwishorerera, mumubambe, kuko jewe ata gicumuro mbonye kuri we." 
John19:7 Abayuda baramwishura, bati Twebge dufise icagezwe, kandi kubg’ ico cagezwe akwiye gupfa, kuko yigize Umwana w’Imana." 
John19:8 Nuko Pilato yumvise iryo jambo, arushiriza gutinya;" 
John19:9 asubira kwinjira mw iboma, abaza Yesu, at’ Ur’ uwa hehe? Ariko Yesu ntiyamwishura na rimwe." 
John19:10 Nuko Pilato aramubaza, ati Nta co umbarira? Ntuzi yuko mfise ububasha bgo kukurekura, kandi mfise ububasha bgo kukubamba?" 
John19:11 Yesu aramwishura, ati Nta bubasha war’ ufise kuri jewe, shit’ ubuhawe buvuye hejuru, ni co gituma uwakunshikirije afise icaha kirengeje." 
John19:12 Uhereye aho Pilato arondera uburyo bg’uko yomurekura, arikw Abayuda barasemerera, bati Ni warekura uyo, ntuzoba ucuzura na Kayisari, kuk’ uwīgira umwami wese aba agararije Kayisari." 
John19:13 Nuko Pilato yumvise ayo magambo, asohora Yesu, yicara ku ntebe y’imanza, yar’ ahantu hitwa Musezero w’amabuye, mu Giheburayo hitwa Gabata." 
John19:14 War’ umusi wo kwitegurira Pasika, hari nk’isaha zitandatu. Abgira Abayuda, at’ Ehe rāba umwami wanyu." 
John19:15 Na bo barasemerera, bati Mukūreho, mukūreho, umubambe. Pilato arababaza, ati Mbambe umwami wanyu? Abaherezi bakuru bati Nta mwami dufise, atari Kayisari." 
John19:16 Araheza aramubahereza, ngw abambge. Nuko basūmira Yesu." 
John19:17 Avayo, yiyikorereye umusaraba, ashika ahantu hitwa Nyagihanga, mu Giheburayo hitwa Gologota;" 
John19:18 bamubambaho, hamwe n’abandi babiri, umwe hirya, uwundi hino, Yesu yari hagati." 
John19:19 Pilato yandika icandiko, agishira ku musaraba; canditswe ngo YESU UMUNYANAZARETI UMWAMI W’ABAYUDA." 
John19:20 Benshi mu Bayuda bāsoma ico candiko, kukw aho hantu Yesu yabambge hari hafi y’igisagara; kandi cari canditswe mu Giheburayo no mu Kiroma no mu Kigiriki." 
John19:21 Nukw Abaherezi bakuru b’Abayuda babgira Pilato, bati Nta co wandika ng’ Umwami w’Abayuda, arik’ uti Yivuze ngo Ni jewe Mwami w’Abayuda." 
John19:22 Pilato arabishura, at’ Ico nanditse, nacanditse." 
John19:23 Nukw abasoda, bamaze kubamba Yesu, bābīra impuzu ziwe, bazigaburamw’ imigabane ine, umusoda wese umugabane wiwe; hasigara umwinjiro. Kand’ uwo mwinjiro ntiwar’ ufise umubarīro, war’ ujishwe kumwe, uhereye hejuru kugeza hasi." 
John19:24 Nuko baravugana, bati Twoye kuwutabura, tuwupfindire, ugire ūwegukiye. Kwar’ ukugira ngw ivyanditswe bishike, ngo Bagabuye impuzu zanje, Bapfindira umwambaro wanje. Ivyo ni kw abasoda babikoze." 
John19:25 Arikw i ruhande y’umusaraba wa Yesu hāri hahagaze nyina na nyinabo na Mariya muka Kilopa na Mariya Magadalene. 
John19:26 Yesu abonye nyina na wa mwigishwa yakunda ahagazeho, abarira nyina, ati Nyina wanje, nguyo umwana wawe." 
John19:27 Maz’ abarira wa mwigishwa, ati Nguyo nyoko. Uhereye ako kanya uwo mwigishwa amujana i we." 
John19:28 Hanyuma y’ivyo Yesu amenye yuko noneho vyose birangiye, kugira ngw icanditswe gishike, aravuga, ati Mfise inyota." 
John19:29 Aho hantu hari hateretse inkono yuzuye inkarisha, nuko bashira sipongo yuzuyemw’ inkarisha kw irenga, bayirungika ku munwa wiwe." 
John19:30 Yesu amaze kuyihabga, aravuga, ati Birarangiye. Araheza ajondamika umutwe, umutima uraca." 
John19:31 Uwo musi war’ uwo kwitegurira Pasika; nuko kugira ngw abābambge ntibagume ku misaraba kw isabato, kuk’ uwo musi w’isabato wari mukuru, Abayuda basaba Pilato ngw amaguru yabo avunwe, kandi ngo babambūrwe." 
John19:32 Maz’ abasoda baraza, bavuna amaguru y’uwa mbere n’ay’ uwundi yabambanywe na we." 
John19:33 Ariko bashitse kuri Yesu, babonye amaze gupfa, ntibāba bakimuvuna amaguru," 
John19:34 arik’ umwe mu basoda amucumita icumu mu rubavu; ako kanya hava amaraso n’amazi. 
John19:35 Uwabibonye ni we yabishingiye intahe kand’ intahe yiwe n’iy’ ukuri, kand’ arazi kw avuga ukuri, kugira ngo namwe mwizere." 
John19:36 Kukw ivyo vyabayeho kugira ngw icanditswe gishike, ngo Nta n’igufa ryiwe rizovunwa." 
John19:37 Kandi har’ ikindi canditswe, kivuga ngo Bazobona uwo bācumise." 
John19:38 Hanyuma y’ivyo Yosefu Umunyarimataya, yar’ umwigishwa wa Yesu, ariko mu mpisho, kubgo gutinya Abayuda, yaka Pilato ikiziga ca Yesu ngw akijane: Pilato aremera; nukw araza ajana ikiziga ciwe." 
John19:39 Kandi haza na Nikodemo, umwe yaza kuri Yesu mw ijoro ubga mbere, azana ikivange c’isenga n’imbazi nk’ibilo mirongwitanu." 
John19:40 Nuko bābīra ikiziga ca Yesu, bakizingira mu mpuzu zera derere, hamwe n’ivyo bimota neza, nk’uk’ umugenzo w’Abayuda wo guhamba war’ uri." 
John19:41 Kand’ aho hantu yabambge hār’ itongo; kandi mur’ iryo tongo hār’ imva nsha itarahambgamw’ umuntu; 
John19:42 aho ni ho bāhamvye Yesu, kuko war’ umusi wo kwitegura kw’ Abayuda, kand’ iyo mva ikaba hafi." 
John20:1 Ku wa mbere w’imisi ndwi mu gahuru, hatarabona, Mariya Magadalene aja ku mva, abona ikibuye gikūwe ku mva;" 
John20:2 agenda ariruka ashikīra Simoni Petero na wa mwigishwa wundi Yesu yakunda, arababgira, ati Bākūye Umwami Yesu mu mva, kandi ntituzi aho bāmushize." 
John20:3 Nuko Petero arasohoka, na wa mwigishwa wundi, baja ku mva." 
John20:4 Bompi birukira icarimwe, kandi wa mwigishwa wundi asiga Petero, amutanga ku mva." 
John20:5 Yunamye, arungurutseyo, abona za mpuzu zera derere zirambitseho, ariko ntiyinjira." 
John20:6 Maze Simoni Petero arashika amukurikiye, yinjira mu mva, abona za mpuzu zirambitseho," 
John20:7 n’igitambara cari mu mutwe wiwe, kitarambitse hamwe na za mpuzu, ariko kizinze kir’ ahaco ukwa conyene." 
John20:8 Ni ho hinjiye wa mwigishwa wundi na we, umwe yabanje gushika ku mva, abibonye arizera." 
John20:9 Kuko bataribgamenye ivyanditswe yukw akwiye kuzozuka mu bapfuye. 
John20:10 Maz’ abo bigishwa bavayo basubira i wabo. 
John20:11 Mariya yar’ ahagaze ku mva arira. Akirikw ararira, arunama, arunguruka mu mva," 
John20:12 abona abamarayika babiri bambaye impuzu zera, bicaye umwe ku mutwe, uwundi mu mirambizo y’ah’ ikiziga ca Yesu cari kiryamye." 
John20:13 Baramubaza, bati Mbega nyina wanje, urizwa n’iki? Na we ati N’uko bakūyeh’ Umwami wanje, nanje nkaba ntazi aho bamushize." 
John20:14 Avuze ivyo, arakebuka, abona Yesu ahagaze, ariko ntiyamenya kw ari Yesu." 
John20:15 Yesu aramubaza, ati Mbega nyina wanje, urizwa n’iki? Urondera nde? Na we yiyumvira kw ar’ umurimyi waho, aramubgira, ati Mugenzi, namb’ ari wewe wamukūye hano, ndangira aho wamushize, ndamukūreyo." 
John20:16 Yesu aramuhamagara, ati Mariya. Na we arahindukira, amwitaba mu Giheburayo, ati Rabuni (risobanurwa ngo Mwigisha)." 
John20:17 Yesu aramubgira, ati Ntunkoreko, kuko ntaradūga kwa Data; ariko genda kwa bene Data, ubabarire, ut’ Agira adūge kwa Se ari we So, uti Ku Mana yiwe ari yo Mana yanyu." 
John20:18 Mariya Magadalene aragenda, abarira abigishwa inkuru, ati Nabonye Umwami; abadondera ivyo yamubariye." 
John20:19 Nuko kur’ uwo musi buhwibiriye, ni wo musi wa mbere w’imisi ndwi, inzugi zāri zugaye ah’ abigishwa bari, kubgo gutinya Abayuda, Yesu araza abahagarara hagati, arababgira, at’ Amahoro abe muri mwebge." 
John20:20 Amaze kuvuga artyo, abereka ibiganza vyiwe no mu rubavu. Maz’ abigishwa baranezerwa, babonye Umwami." 
John20:21 Yesu yongera kubabgira, at’ Amahoro abe muri mwebge. Nk’uko Data yantumye ni ko nanje mbatumye." 
John20:22 Avuze ivyo, abahumekerako, ati Ni mwākīre Mpwemu Yera." 
John20:23 Kand’ abo muzoharira ivyaha bose, bazoba babihariwe; arikw abo mutazobiharira bose, ntibazoba babihariwe." 
John20:24 Ariko Toma ari we Hasa, umwe wo muri bamwe cumi na babiri, ntiyari kumwe na bo aho Yesu yaza." 
John20:25 Abandi bigishwa baramubgira, bati Twabonye Umwami. Na we arabishura, ati Ni ntabona inkovu z’imambo mu biganza vyiwe, ngo nkoze urutoke rwanje mu nkovu z’imambo, ngo nshire urushi mu rubavu rwiwe, sinemera." 
John20:26 Maz’ imisi munani ishize abigishwa bāri mu nzu ukundi gusha, na Toma bāri kumwe. Yesu araza, inzugi zari zugaye, abahagarara hagati, at’ Amahoro abe muri mwebge." 
John20:27 Maz’ abgira Toma, ati Zana hano urutoke rwawe, urābe ibiganza vyanje; zana n’urushi, urushire mu rubavu rwanje, nta co uba ūtizera, arik’ ube uwizeye." 
John20:28 Toma aramwishura, ati Mwami wanje, kandi Mana yanje." 
John20:29 Yesu aramubgira, ati Wijejwe n’uk’ umbonye. Hahirwa abatarinze kubona, yamara bakizera." 
John20:30 Hariho n’ibindi bimenyetso vyinshi Yesu yakoreye imbere y’abigishwa, bitanditswe mur’ iki gitabo." 
John20:31 Arikw ibi vyandikiwe kugira ngo mwizere yuko Yesu ari we Kristo, Umwana w’Imana, no kugira ngo mwizeye mugire ubugingo mw izina ryiwe." 
John21:1 Hanyuma y’ivyo Yesu yiyereka abigishwa ukundi gusha, ari ku kiyaga c’i Tiberiya, kand’ uburyo yiyerekanye n’ubu:" 
John21:2 Simoni Petero na Toma ari we Hasa bāri kumwe na Natanayeli w’i Kana i Galilaya, na bene Zebedayo, n’abandi bigishwa babiri." 
John21:3 Simoni Petero arababgira, ati Ndagiye kuroba. Na bo bati Natwe turajana nawe. Barīkora, batambukira mu bgato. Mur’ iryo joro ntibāgira ico bafata." 
John21:4 Umutwenzi ugitambika, Yesu ahagarara ku musenyi, arikw abigishwa ntibāmenya kw ari Yesu." 
John21:5 Nuko Yesu arababaza, ati Bana, har’ ico kurya mufise? Bat’ Oya." 
John21:6 Arababgira, ati Ni muterere urusenga i buryo bg’ubgato, muraronka. Nuko baraterera, ntibāba bakibasha kurukwega, kukw ifi zar’ isinzi." 
John21:7 Wa mwigishwa Yesu yakunda abgira Petero, ati N’Umwami Yesu. Simoni Petero yumvise kw ar’ Umwami, akenyera impuzu, kuko yari gusa, araheza yikubita mu kiyaga." 
John21:8 Arikw abandi bigishwa baza mu bgato, kuko bari hafi y’umusenyi, hāri nk’intambuko ijana, bakwega urusenga rurimw’ ifi." 
John21:9 Bafashe i musozi, babonah’ umuriro w’amakara n’ifi zigeretseko, n’umutsima." 
John21:10 Yesu arababgira, ati Ni muzane ifi ku zo muhejeje kuroba." 
John21:11 Simoni Petero aja mu bgato, akwegera urusenga i musozi rwuzuye ifi nini‐nini ijana na mirongwitanu na zitatu: kandi naho zari zingaho zirtyo, urusenga ntirwacitse." 
John21:12 Yesu arababarira, ati Ni muze murye. Ariko mu bigishwa ntihāgira ūtinyuka kumubaza, at’ Uri nde? Kuko bāri bamenye kw’ ar’ Umwami Yesu." 
John21:13 Yesu araza, yābīra umutsima, arawubaha, n’ifi n’uko." 
John21:14 Ubgo bgar’ ubugira gatatu Yesu yiyereka abigishwa, amaze kuzuka mu bapfuye." 
John21:15 Nuko barangije kurya, Yesu abaza Simoni Petero, ati Simoni, mwene Yohana, mbeg’ urankunda kurusha aba? Na we at’ Ego, Mugenzi, wewe urazi ko nkunogera. Aramubgira, at’ Ahura imyagazi y’intama zanje." 
John21:16 Yongera kumubaza ubugira kabiri, ati Simoni, mwene Yohana, mbeg’ urankunda? Na we at’ Ego, Mugenzi, wewe urazi ko nkunogera. Aramubgira, ati Ragira intama zanje." 
John21:17 Amubaza ubugira gatatu, ati Simoni, mwene Yohana, mbeg’ urannogera? Petero arababara, kuko yamubajije ubugira gatatu ngo Mbeg’ urannogera? Aramwishura, ati Mugenzi, weho urazi vyose, urazi ko nkunogera. Yesu aramubgira, at’ Ahura intama zanje." 
John21:18 N’ukuri, n’ukuri ndakubgire: Ukir’ umusore, warikenyeza, ukaja ah’ ugomba; arikw ah’ uzosāzira, uzoramvura amaboko, uwundi agukenyeze, akujane ah’ utagomba." 
John21:19 Icatumye avuga artyo, kwar’ ukwerekana urupfu azopfa, ashimagirisha Imana. Amaze kuvuga artyo, aramubarira, ati Nkurikira." 
John21:20 Petero arakebuka, abona wa mwigishwa Yesu yakunda abakurikiye, umwe yari yegamiye mu gikiriza ca Yesu hamwe bāsangira, akamubaza, ati Mugenzi, ni nde azokugura?" 
John21:21 Nuko Petero amubonye, abaza Yesu, ati Mugenzi, uyu we bizoba bite?" 
John21:22 Yesu aramwishura, ati Namba ngomba kw azogumaho kugeza aho nzozira, upfa iki? Wewe nkurikira." 
John21:23 Ni co catumye iri jambo rikwira muri bene Data, ng’ uwo mwigishwa ntazopfa. Ariko Yesu ntiyamubgiye kw atazopfa, ariko yavuze, ati Namba ngomba kw agumaho kugeza aho nzozira, upfa iki?" 
John21:24 Uwo ni wa mwigishwa yashingiye intahe ivyo, kandi ni we yavyanditse, kandi natwe tuzi yukw intahe yiwe ar’ iy’ ukuri." 
John21:25 Ariko hariho n’ibindi vyinshi Yesu yakoze, vyokwandikwa bidondowe kimwe‐kimwe, ngira ngo n’isi na yo ntiyokwirwamw’ ibitabo vyokwanditswe." 
Acts1:1 Ca gitabo ca mbere nanditse ga Teyofilo we, kivuga ivyo Yesu yatanguye gukora no kwigisha vyose," 
Acts1:2 gushitsa ku musi yadūgijwe mw ijuru, ahejeje kugerera intumwa muri Mpwemu Yera, zimwe yatoranije." 
Acts1:3 Kand’ amaze kubabazwa, abiyereka ari muzima atanga ibimenyetso vyinshi, ababonekera imisi mirongwine, avuga ivy’ ubgami bg’Imana." 
Acts1:4 Maz’ akoranye na bo, arabihanikiriza ngo ntibave i Yerusalemu, at’ Ariko murorēre isezerano rya Data, iryo mwanyumvanye." 
Acts1:5 Kuko Yohana yabatirisha amazi, ariko mweho, mu misi itari myinshi, muzobatizwa na Mpwemu Yera." 
Acts1:6 Nuko bakoranye, baramubaza, bati Mwami, iki gihe ni co ugira ugarukane ingoma y’Abisirayeli?" 
Acts1:7 Arabishura, ati S’ivyanyu kumenya imisi cank’ ibihe Data yashinze n’ububasha bgiwe wenyene;" 
Acts1:8 ariko muzohabga ubushobozi, Mpwemu Yera ni yabazako, muzoba ivyabona vyo kunshingira intahe i Yerusalemu, n’i Yudaya hose, n’i Samariya, no gushitsa ku mpera y’isi." 
Acts1:9 Amaze kuvuga artyo, adūzwa babona, igicu kimukūra mu maso yabo." 
Acts1:10 Bagihanze amaso mw ijuru akigenda, abagabo babiri bambaye impuzu zera bahagarara i ruhande yabo;" 
Acts1:11 barababaza, bati Yemwe bagabo b’i Galilaya, n’iki gitumye muhagaze murāba mw ijuru? Uyo Yesu, abakūwemwo, akadūzwa mw ijuru, azoza artyo, nk’uko mumubonye aja mw ijuru." 
Acts1:12 Buno basubira i Yerusalemu, bavuye ku musozi witwa Elayono, uri hafi y’i Yerusalemu nk’urugendo rwemewe kugendwa kw’ isabato." 
Acts1:13 Bashitseyo, barūrira baja mu nzu yo hejuru, aho bāri basembereye, ari Petero, na Yohana, na Yakobo, na Andereya, na Filipo, na Toma, na Barutolomayo, na Matayo, na Yakobo mwene Alufayo, na Simoni Zelote, na Yuda mwene Yakobo." 
Acts1:14 Abo bose bāsenga badahumeka n’umutima uhūye, hamwe n’abagore, na Mariya nyina wa Yesu, na bene nyina." 
Acts1:15 Mur’ iyo misi Petero ava hasi ahagarara hagati ya bene Data, (hāri hakoraniye ishengero ry’abantu nk’ijana na mirongwibiri), aravuga," 
Acts1:16 ati Bagabo bene Data, ivyanditswe ntivyobuze gushika, ivyo Mpwemu Yera yari yaravugiye mu kanwa ka Dawidi kuri Yuda, yarōngōye abaja gufata Yesu," 
Acts1:17 kuko yari yaharūwe muri twebge, agahabga umugabane w’iki gikorwa." 
Acts1:18 (Kand’ uwo muntu amaze kugura ubgatsi ku vyo yahawekw ibiguzi vyo kugabitanya kwiwe, agwa yubamye, araturika, amara yiwe yose arasēseka." 
Acts1:19 Bimenyekana mu baba i Yerusalemu bose, ni co catumye ubgo bgatsi mu rurimi rwabo babgita Akeludama, risobanurwa ng’ Ubgatsi bg’amaraso.)" 
Acts1:20 Kuko mu gitabo ca Zaburi handitswe, ngw I we hasigare umusaka, Kandi ntihakagire uwundi ahaba, kandi ng’ Ububgiriza bgiwe busubiremw’ uwundi." 
Acts1:21 Nuko mur’ abo bagabo twahora tugendana igihe cose Umwami Yesu yar’ akiri muri twebge amaja n’amaza," 
Acts1:22 utanguriye ku kubatiza kwa Yohana ukageza ku musi yadukūriwemwo, adūganywe, umwe muri bo akwiye kuba icabona hamwe natwe co gushingira intahe ukuzuka kwiwe." 
Acts1:23 Bahagarika babiri, umwe ni Yosefu ari we Barusaba, irindi ni Yusito, uwundi na we ni Matiya." 
Acts1:24 Barasenga, bati Mwami, ni wewe uzi imitima y’abantu bose, none werekane uwo utoranije mur’ aba bompi" 
Acts1:25 gusubira mu kirenge ca Yuda mur’ iki gikorwa no kuba intumwa, ivyo yataye akaja ahiwe." 
Acts1:26 Barabapfindira, ubupfindo bgerekana Matiya, nukw aharūranwa n’intumwa cumi n’imwe." 
Acts2:1 Umusi wa Pentekote ushitse, bose bāri bakoraniye ahantu hamwe;" 
Acts2:2 haza igihinda kivuye mw ijuru giturumbuka, nk’uguhuhuta kw’umuyaga w’inkomezi, gikwira hose mu nzu bicayemwo." 
Acts2:3 Hababonekera ibirimi vyigabanije, nk’ivy’ umuriro; bibajak’ umwe‐umwe." 
Acts2:4 Bose buzuzwa Mpwemu Yera, batangura kuvuga izindi ndimi, uko Mpwemu abahaye kuzivuga." 
Acts2:5 I Yerusalemu hār’ Abayuda bamyeho, abagabo bubaha Imana, bāri bāravuye mu mahanga yose yo musi y’ijuru." 
Acts2:6 Ico gihinda cumvikanye, hakorana abantu benshi, barajorerwa, kuk’ umuntu wese yumvise ururimi rw’i wabo baruvuga." 
Acts2:7 Barumirwa bose, baratangara, bati Mbeg’ aba bose bavuga s’Abanyagalilaya?" 
Acts2:8 Kandi n’iki gitumye twese tubumva bavuga indimi z’i wacu izo twavukanye? 
Acts2:9 Tur’ Abapariti, n’Abamedi, n’Abelamiti, n’abamye i Mesopotamiya, n’i Yudaya, n’i Kapadokiya, n’i Ponto, no muri Asiya," 
Acts2:10 n’i Furugiya, n’i Pamfiliya, no muri Egiputa, no mu bihugu vy’i Libuwa bihereranye n’i Kureni, n’ab’ i Roma bāgerereye ino, Abayuda, bo n’abātoye idini yabo," 
Acts2:11 Abakirete, n’Abarabo, tukabumva bavuga mu ndimi zacu ibitangaza vy’Imana." 
Acts2:12 Bose barumirwa barazazanirwa, barabazanya, bat’ Ibi n’ibiki?" 
Acts2:13 Arikw abandi barabanegura, bati Baborewe igisāma." 
Acts2:14 Ariko Petero ahagararana na bamwe cumi n’umwe, ababariza ijwi rirenga, ati Yemwe Bayuda n’ababa i Yerusalemu mwese, ibi ni mubimenye, kandi ni mwumvirize amajambo yanje." 
Acts2:15 Aba ntibaborewe nk’uko mwiyumvira, kuk’ ubu ar’ isaha zitatu z’umusi," 
Acts2:16 arikw ivyo n’ivyavuzwe n’uwavugishwa n’Imana Yoweli," 
Acts2:17 ati Bizoba mu misi y’iherezo, ni kw Imana yagize, Nzosuka Mpwemu wanje ku bari n’umubiri bose: Kand’ abahungu n’abakobga banyu bazovugishwa nanje, N’imisore yanyu izobona ivyo yeretswe, N’abatāma banyu bazorota inzozi." 
Acts2:18 Mbere n’abagurano banje b’abahungu n’abakobga mur’ iyo misi Nzobasukako Mpwemu wanje, bavugishwe nanje." 
Acts2:19 Nzoshira utwumiza hejuru mw ijuru, N’ibimenyetso hasi kw isi, Amaraso n’umuriro no gupfūndūka kw’umwotsi." 
Acts2:20 Izuba rizocura umwiza, N’ukwezi guhinduke amaraso, Hataraza uwo musi mukuru rurangiranwa w’Uhoraho:" 
Acts2:21 Kand’ umuntu wese azokwambaza izina ry’Uhoraho azokizwa. 
Acts2:22 Yemwe bagabo b’Abisirayeli, ni mwumve aya majambo: Yesu Umunyanazareti, umuntu Imana yashimagirishije kuri mwebge ibitangaza n’utwumiza n’ibimenyetso, ivyo Imana yamukoresheje hagati yanyu, nk’uko mubizi ubganyu;" 
Acts2:23 uwo muntu amaze gutangwa nk’ukw Imana yabigabiye yikomvomvoye, ibimenye bitaribgabe, mumubambisha amaboko y’abagarariji, muramwica." 
Acts2:24 Arikw Imana yaramuzuye, ibohōye ibise vy’urupfu, kuko bitāshobotse ko rumugumya." 
Acts2:25 Kuko Dawidi yavuze ivy’ uwo, ati Nabonye Uhoraho imbere yanje imisi yose, Kukw ar’ i buryo bganje, ngo sinnyiganyige." 
Acts2:26 Ni co gituma umutima wanje uhimbarwa, ururimi rwanje rukanezerwa, Kandi n’umubiri wanje uzoba nko mu gikāri, wizigiye ibizoba." 
Acts2:27 Kuk’ utazoreka ubugingo bganje ngo buje i kuzimu, Kandi ntuzotanga Uwera wawe ngw az’ abore." 
Acts2:28 Wammenyesheje inzira z’ubugingo, Mu nyonga hawe uzohanyuzurisha akanyamuneza." 
Acts2:29 Bagabo bene Data, s’ikingora kubabarira mvyeruye ivya sogokuruza mukuru Dawidi, yuko yapfuye, agahambga, n’imva yiwe iri ngaha ino muri twebge na bugingo n’ubu." 
Acts2:30 Nuko, kuko yar’ uwavugishwa n’Imana, akamenya kw Imana yamurahiye indahiro, kw izoshira ku ngoma yiwe uwamutse mu bura bgiwe," 
Acts2:31 yavuze ivy’ ukuzuka kwa Kristo abibonye bitaribgabe, yukw atārekewe mu kuzimu, kandi n’umubiri wiwe ata ho wigeze ubora." 
Acts2:32 Uwo Yesu Imana yaramuzuye, natwe twese tur’ ivyabona vyo gushingira intahe ivyo." 
Acts2:33 Nukw amaze gushirwa hejuru n’ukuboko kw’i buryo kw’Imana, kand’ ashikirijwe na Se isezerano, ari ryo Mpwemu Yera, non’ asutse ico muriko murabona kandi mwumva." 
Acts2:34 Kandi Dawidi ntiyadūze mw ijuru, arik’ ubgiwe yaravuze, at’ Uhoraho yabariye Umwami wanje, At’ Icara i buryo bganje," 
Acts2:35 Ushitse aho nzohindurira abansi bawe indava yo musi y’ibirenge vyawe. 
Acts2:36 Nukw abo mu muryango wa Isirayeli bose, ni bamenye badakekeranya yukw Imana yamugize Umwami na Kristo, Yesu umwe mwābamba." 
Acts2:37 Bumvise ivyo, bibacumita mu mitima, babaza Petero n’izindi ntumwa, bati Bagabo bene Data, mbega tugire dute?" 
Acts2:38 Petero arabishura, ati Ni mwihane, umuntu wese muri mwebge abatizwe mw izina rya Yesu Kristo, mubone guharirwa ivyaha vyanyu, kandi muzohabga ingabire, ari yo Mpwemu Yera." 
Acts2:39 Kukw isezerano ar’ iryanyu kand’ ar’ iry’ abana banyu, n’abari kure bose, abazohamagarwa bose n’Umwami Imana yacu." 
Acts2:40 Kand’ ashingisha intahe ayandi majambo menshi, arabahanūra, ati Ni mwikize ab’ iki gihe kigoramye." 
Acts2:41 Nukw abemeye amajambo yiwe barabatizwa: abongewe kur’ uwo musi ku bāri basanzweho bāri nk’ibihumbi bitatu. 
Acts2:42 Bashishikara cane mu vyo intumwa zigisha, no kugira ubumwe, no kumanyagura umutsima no gusenga." 
Acts2:43 Umuntu wese aterwa n’ubgoba: kand’ utwumiza n’ibimenyetso vyinshi vyakorwa n’intumwa. 
Acts2:44 Abizeye bose bāba hamwe, basangira ivyabo vyose:" 
Acts2:45 amatongo yabo n’ibintu vyabo bārabigura, bakabibagabanganya bose, nk’uk’ umuntu wese akennye." 
Acts2:46 Kand’ imisi yose bāshishikara kuja mu rusengero n’umutima uhūye, kand’ i wabo bāmanyagura umutsima, bakarya banezerewe n’imitima itagira akarohe," 
Acts2:47 bahimbaza Imana, kandi na bo bāshimwa n’abantu bose. Umwami Imana akabongera imisi yose abama barakizwa." 
Acts3:1 Petero na Yohana bāriko baradūga baja mu rusengero mu gihe co gusenga, ni co saha cenda." 
Acts3:2 Hār’ umuntu yaremaye ibirenge uhereye kuva mu nda ya nyina, yama aterurwa, bakamushira kw irembo ry’urusengero ryitwa Ryiza uko bukeye, kugira ngw asēge abinjira mu rusengero." 
Acts3:3 Uyo abonye Petero na Yohana bagira binjire mu rusengero, arabasēga ngo bamuhe." 
Acts3:4 Petero amuhanga amaso, bo na Yohana, aramubarira, ati N’uturābe." 
Acts3:5 Abashirak’ umutima agira ngo har’ ico bamuha. 
Acts3:6 Petero aramubarira, at’ Ifeza n’izahabu nta vyo mfise, arikw ico mfise ndakiguha: mw izina rya Yesu Kristo Umunyanazareti, va hasi utambuke." 
Acts3:7 Maz’ amufata ukuboko kw’i buryo, amukūra hasi: ako kanya ibirenge vyiwe n’ingingo zavyo bica birakomera," 
Acts3:8 arabaduka arahagarara, atangura gutambuka, yinjirana na bo mu rusengero, atambuka yitera hejuru, ahimbaza Imana:" 
Acts3:9 abantu bose babona atambuka ahimbaza Imana," 
Acts3:10 bamenya kw ari we yahora yicara kw irembo ry’urusengero ryitwa Ryiza asēgerereza; barumirwa cane, batangazwa n’ibimubayeko." 
Acts3:11 Agifashe Petero na Yohana, abantu bose birukira kuri bo, bakoranira kw ibaraza ryitwa irya Salomo, batangaye cane." 
Acts3:12 Petero abibonye, abaza abo bantu, ati Yemwe bagabo b’Abisirayeli, n’iki gitumye mutangazwa n’ibi, muduhangiye amaso iki, nk’ah’ ubushobozi bgacu cank’ ukwubaha Imana kwacu ari vyo vyaduhaye kumugendesha?" 
Acts3:13 Imana ya Aburahamu na Isaka na Yakobo, ari yo Mana ya ba sogokuruza, yashimagije Umushumba wayo Yesu, umwe mwebge mwatanze mukamwihakanira mu maso ya Pilato, amaze kwahukanya urubanza rwo kumurekura." 
Acts3:14 Ariko mweho mwihakana Uwera kand’ Umugororotsi, musaba ko babarekurira umwicanyi," 
Acts3:15 wa Mukuru w’ubugingo muramwica; arikw Imana muzura mu bapfuye, natwe tur’ ivyabona vyo gushingira intahe ivyo." 
Acts3:16 Kand’ uyu, uwo mubona kandi muzi, kuko yizeye izina ry’uwo, iryo zina ryamuhaye inkomezi: mber’ ukwizera ahawe na we ni kwo kumukirije rwose imbere yanyu mwese." 
Acts3:17 Kandi none, bene Data, ndazi yuko mwabikoze mutabizi, n’ababaganza na bo n’uko." 
Acts3:18 Arikw ivyo Imana yavugiye mu kanwa k’abāvugishwa na yo bose bitaribgabe, yuko Kristo wayo azobabazwa, ivyo yabishikije irtyo." 
Acts3:19 Nuko mwihane, muhindukire, ivyaha vyanyu bihanagurwe, ibihe vyo guhēmbūka bibone ingene biza, bivuye mu nyonga z’Umwami Imana," 
Acts3:20 kugira ngo na yo iz’ itume Kristo yabatoranirijwe kera, ni we Yesu." 
Acts3:21 Arikw ijuru rikwiye kumwākīra, gushitsa ku bihe vyo gusubira guhindura ibintu vyose bisha, nk’ukw Imana yavuze mu kanwa k’abera bayo yavugisha bose, uhereye ubga mbere na mbere." 
Acts3:22 Mose koko yaravuze, at’ Uhoraho Imana azobahagurukiriza ūvugishwa na we mu b’i wanyu ameze nkanje; uwo muze mumwumvire mu vy’ azobabarira vyose." 
Acts3:23 Kand’ umuntu wese atazokwumvira uno avugishwa n’Imana, azorandurwa mu bantu." 
Acts3:24 Mber’ abāvugishwa n’Imana bose, uhereye kuri Samweli n’abāmukurikiye, abāvuze bose bāramenyekanishije ivy’ iyi misi." 
Acts3:25 Namwe mur’ abana b’abāvugishwa n’Imana, kandi mur’ ab’ isezerano Imana yasezeranye na ba sogokuruza banyu, ibarira Aburahamu, iti Mu ruvyaro rwawe ni ho imiryango yose yo mw isi izohērwa umugisha." 
Acts3:26 Ni mwebge Imana yatanguye gutumak’ Umushumba wayo imaze kumuzura, kugira ngw abahe umugisha, abahindure, umuntu wese ave mu bibi vyiwe." 
Acts4:1 Bakivugana n’abantu, abaherezi bazanana aho bari n’umukuru w’abashibamyi b’urusengero, n’Abasadukayo," 
Acts4:2 bababajwe cane n’uko bigisha abantu, bababarira yuk’ ukuzuka kw’abapfuye kwabonetse kuri Yesu." 
Acts4:3 Babashōrerakw amaboko, babashira mw ibohero gushitsa mu gitondo, kuko bgari bugorovye." 
Acts4:4 Ariko benshi mu bumvise iryo jambo barizera, igitigiri c’abagabo gishika nk’ibihumbi bitanu." 
Acts4:5 Bukeye bg’aho, abashingantahe babo bo n’abakuru n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe bakoranira i Yerusalemu," 
Acts4:6 na Anasi umuherezi mukuru, na Kayafa na Yohana na Alekisandero, n’ab’ umuryango bose w’abaherezi bakuru." 
Acts4:7 Babashize hagati, barababaza, bati N’ubushobozi ki, canke n’izina ki, vyabateye gukora ivyo?" 
Acts4:8 Nuko Petero, yuzuye Mpwemu Yera, arababarira, ati Yemwe bashingantahe b’abantu n’abakuru," 
Acts4:9 uyu musi ko ducunaguzwa ivyo twagiriye neza umuntu yanyogomba, kandi n’icamukijije," 
Acts4:10 ni mumenye mwese, n’ubgoko bgose bg’Abisirayeli, yukw ari mw izina rya Yesu Kristo, Umunyanazareti, uwo mwebge mwabamvye, Imana ikamuzura mu bapfuye, kw ari ho hatumye uyu muntu ahagarara imbere yanyu, akomeye." 
Acts4:11 Uwo ni we buye mwebge abubatsi mwātītūye, kandi ryahindutse irigumya imfuruka." 
Acts4:12 Kandi nta wundi agakiza kabonerwamwo, kukw ata rindi zina musi y’ijuru ryāhawe abantu dukwiye gukirizwamwo." 
Acts4:13 Babonye ugushira amanga kwa Petero na Yohana, kandi babona ko batigishijwe, atar’ abanyabgenge, baratangara; maze bamenya ko bābana na Yesu;" 
Acts4:14 kandi babonye uwo muntu yakijijwe ahagararanye na bo, babura ico bavuga." 
Acts4:15 Barabataramura, maze baja inama," 
Acts4:16 bati Mbeg’ aba bantu tubagire dute? Ko vyamenyekanye mu baba i Yerusalemu bose yuko bakoze ikimenyetso kibaye rurangiranwa, natwe ntidushobora kubihakana;" 
Acts4:17 ariko vyoye kurushiriza kwamamara mu bantu, tubahahirize, ntibongere kugira umuntu n’umwe babarira mur’ iryo zina." 
Acts4:18 Babahamagaje, barabihanikiriza ngo ntibazirukanye ngo bavuge canke bigishe mw izina rya Yesu." 
Acts4:19 Petero na Yohana barabishura, bati Namb’ ari vyiza mu nyonga z’Imana kubumvira kubarutisha Imana, ni mubitandukanye:" 
Acts4:20 kuko tweho tudashobora kureka kuvuga ivyo twabonye n’ivyo twumvise. 
Acts4:21 Na bo bongeye kubahahiriza, barabarekura, babuze uko bobahana kubg’ abantu, kuko bose bāhimbaza Imana ku vyābaye." 
Acts4:22 Kuk’ uwo muntu yar’ arengeje imyaka mirongwine avutse, uwakozwekw ico kimenyetso co kumukiza." 
Acts4:23 Nuko barekuwe basubira muri bagenzi babo, babīgānira ivyo abaherezi bakuru n’abakuru bababgiye vyose." 
Acts4:24 Na bo bavyumvise bavuga n’ijwi rirenga, babgira Imana n’umutima uhūye, bati Databuja, ni wewe waremye ijuru n’isi, n’ikiyaga n’ibirimwo vyose," 
Acts4:25 kandi wavugiye mu kanwa ka sogokuruza Dawidi, umusavyi wawe, ubivugisha Mpwemu Yera, ut’ Abanyamahanga n’iki kibateye umuvurungano, N’amoko yagīriye ingingo iki ivy’ ubusa?" 
Acts4:26 Abami bo mw isi batonze urugamba, N’abakuru bakoraniye hamwe, Kurwanya Uhoraho n’Uwo yarobanuje amavuta." 
Acts4:27 Kandi vy’ukuri mur’ iki gisagara, Herode, bo na Pontiyo Pilato hamwe n’abanyamahanga n’imiryango ya Isirayeli, bākoraniye kurwanya Umushumba wawe yera Yesu, uwo warobanuje amavuta," 
Acts4:28 ngo bashitse ivy’ ukuboko kwawe n’inama yawe vyari vyaragabiye vyose ko bizoba. 
Acts4:29 Kandi none, Mwami, rāba agahahirizo kabo, uhe abasavyi bawe kuvuga ijambo ryawe bashize amanga rwose:" 
Acts4:30 ukiramvuye ukuboko kwawe gukiza indwara, ibimenyetso n’ibitangaza bikorwe mw izina ry’Umushumba wawe yera Yesu." 
Acts4:31 Bahejeje gusenga, aho bakoraniye haratigita, bose buzuzwa Mpwemu Yera, bavuga ijambo ry’Imana bashize amanga." 
Acts4:32 Kand’ abizeye b’akavuvu bari bahūje umutima n’inama, kandi nta n’umwe yakīmbūkira ikintu cose atunze ngo n’iciwe, ariko vyose bārabisangira." 
Acts4:33 Kand’ intumwa zāshingira intahe ukuzuka kw’Umwami Yesu ziri n’ubushobozi bginshi, kand’ ubuntu bg’Imana bginshi buba kuri bo bose." 
Acts4:34 Nta mukene yari muri bo, kukw abāri bafise amashamvu bose cank’ amazu bābigura, bakazana ibiguzi vy’ivyo baguze," 
Acts4:35 bakabishira imbere y’ibirenge vy’intumwa; maze bakabigabanganya abantu, umuntu wese ukw akennye." 
Acts4:36 Na Yosefu, uwo intumwa zise Barunaba, risobanurwa ng’Umwana wo guhanūra, Umulewi yavukiye i Kupuro," 
Acts4:37 yar’afise itongo ararigura, azana ibiguzi vyaryo, abishira imbere y’ibirenge vy’intumwa." 
Acts5:1 Kandi hār’ umugabo yitwa Ananiya, agura ishamvu afatanije n’umugore wiwe Safira," 
Acts5:2 yisigariza ku biguzi vyayo, umugore wiwe abizi, azana ikigabane, agishira imbere y’ibirenge vy’intumwa." 
Acts5:3 Petero aramubaza, ati Ananiya, n’iki gitumye Satani yuzuza umutima wawe guhenda Mpwemu Yera, ukīsigariza ku biguzi vy’ishamvu?" 
Acts5:4 Ukiyifise ntiyar’ iyawe? Kand’ umaze kuyigura, ibiguzi vyayo ntuba warabikoze uk’ ugomba? N’iki catumye wīgīra ingingo mu mutima wawe gukora urtyo? S’abantu uhenze, Imana ni yo uhenze." 
Acts5:5 Ananiya yumvise ayo majambo agwa bukumbi: abavyumvise bose baterwa n’ubgoba bginshi. 
Acts5:6 Imisore iva hasi, iramutekera, iramujana, iramuhamba." 
Acts5:7 Hahise nk’isaha zitatu, umugore wiwe arinjira, atazi ivyabaye;" 
Acts5:8 Petero aramubaza, ati Mbarira: mbeg’ ishamvu mwayiguze ayo nyene? Aramwishura, at’ Ego me, n’ayo." 
Acts5:9 Petero aramubaza, ati N’iki gitumye muhūza inama kugerageza Mpwemu w’Umwami Imana? Ehe ibirenge vy’abahejeje guhamba umugabo wawe biri ku rugi, nawe barakujana." 
Acts5:10 Uwo mwanya agwa imbere y’ibirenge vyiwe bukumbi. Ya misore yinjiye isanga amaze guhwera, iramujana, imuhamba i ruhande y’umugabo wiwe." 
Acts5:11 Ishengero ryose n’abavyumvise bose baterwa n’ubgoba bginshi. 
Acts5:12 Ibimenyetso n’ibitangaza vyinshi bikorwa mu bantu n’amaboko y’intumwa: kandi bose bākoranira mw ibaraza rya Salomo n’umutima uhūye: 
Acts5:13 ariko mu bandi nta muntu yatinyuka kwifatanya na bo, yamar’ abantu bose bārabashimagiza," 
Acts5:14 bārushiriza kwongerwakw abizeye Umwami Yesu, ishengero ryinshi ry’abagabo n’abagore;" 
Acts5:15 bituma banaterurira abarwaye ku nzira, babashira mu nderuzo no ku birago, kugira ngo Petero ni yahaca, naho coba igitūtu ciwe gishike kuri bamwe." 
Acts5:16 Hakoranira ishengero rivuye no mu bisagara bihereranye n’i Yerusalemu, bazana abarwaye n’abababazwa n’impwemu zihumanye: bakizwa uko bangana." 
Acts5:17 Maz’ umuherezi mukuru ahagurukana n’abāri kumwe na we bose, ni bo muce witwa uw’ Abasadukayo, buzura ishari," 
Acts5:18 bashōrera amaboko ku ntumwa, bazishira mu nzu y’ibohero rya bose." 
Acts5:19 Maz’ umumarayika w’Umwami Imana ahenga mw ijoro yugurura inzugi z’ibohero, abakūrayo, arababgira," 
Acts5:20 ati Ni mugende, muhagarare mu rusengero, mubarire abantu amajambo yose ya bga Bugingo." 
Acts5:21 Bavyumvise, binjira mu rusengero hāri nko mu mutwenzi, barigisha. Maz’ umuherezi mukuru azanana n’abāri kumwe na we, bahamagaza abanyekombe, n’abakuru bose b’Abisirayeli, maze batuma mu nzu y’abanyororo kubazana." 
Acts5:22 Abagendanyi bagiye ntibabasanga mw ibohero: baragaruka barababgira," 
Acts5:23 bat’ Inzu y’abanyororo dusanze yugaye ata nkomanzi iriho na mba, n’abarinzi bahagaze ku nzugi, maze twuguruye ntitwasangamw’ umuntu." 
Acts5:24 Bumvise ayo majambo umukuru w’abashibamyi b’urusengero n’abaherezi bakuru bazazanirwa n’ivyabo, ikizovamwo." 
Acts5:25 Haza umuntu arababarira, at’ Erega ba bagabo mwashira mw ibohero bari mu rusengero bahagaze bigisha abantu." 
Acts5:26 Maz’ uwo mukuru w’abashibamyi ajana n’abagendanyi, babazana ku neza, kuko bātinya abantu, ngo ntibabatere amabuye." 
Acts5:27 Bamaze kubazana babashira mw ikombe: umuherezi mukuru arababaza," 
Acts5:28 ati Mbega ntitwabīhanije cane kutigisha muri rya zina? None rāba mwujuje Yerusalemu inyigisho zanyu; ico murondera n’ukudushirakw amaraso ya wa muntu. 
Acts5:29 Maze Petero n’intumwa barabishura, bat’ Igikwiye n’ukwumvira Imana kuyirutisha abantu." 
Acts5:30 Imana ya ba sogokuruza yazuye Yesu, uwo mwebge mwishe mumumanitse ku giti." 
Acts5:31 Uyo Imana yaramushize hejuru n’ukuboko kwayo kw’i buryo, ngw abe Umukuru n’Umukiza, ngw ahe Abisirayeli kwihana no guharirwa ivyaha." 
Acts5:32 Natwe tur’ ivyabona vyo gushingira intahe ivyo, na Mpwemu Yera na we n’uko, uwo Imana yahaye abayumvira." 
Acts5:33 Ariko bo bavyumvise baribga mu mitima, bashaka kubica." 
Acts5:34 Maze hahaguruka umwe mw ikombe, w’Umufarisayo yitwa Gamaliyeli, umwigisha w’ivyagezwe, yubahwa n’abantu bose, avuga ko bataramura abo bantu akanya gato." 
Acts5:35 Maz’ arababarira, ati Yemwe bagabo b’Abisirayeli, ni mwirinde mumenye uko mugirira aba bantu:" 
Acts5:36 kuko mu misi ishize Teyuda yādutse yiyita agakomeye, igitigiri c’abantu gishika nk’amajana ane gikondōrera inyuma yiwe: maz’ aricwa, abāmwumvira bose barasābagira, bacika ubusa." 
Acts5:37 Hanyuma yiwe hāduka Yuda Umunyagalilaya, mu misi yo kwandikwa, yikwegera abantu inyuma; na we apfa rubi, n’abāmwumvira bose uko bangana barasābagira." 
Acts5:38 Kandi none ndababgire: Ni muzibukire aba bantu, mubarekure: kukw iyi nama n’iki gikorwa ni vyaba biturutse mu bantu, bizosendwa:" 
Acts5:39 ariko ni vyaba biturutse ku Mana, ntimuzoshobora kubatsinda, mwoye kuzosanga murwanya Imana." 
Acts5:40 Baramwemerera, maze bahamagaje intumwa, barazitonagura, barazīhanikiriza ngo ntizize zigishe mw izina rya Yesu, maze barazirekura." 
Acts5:41 Nuko bava mu maso y’abanyekombe, banezerejwe n’uko bemerewe gutētererezwa iryo zina." 
Acts5:42 Kand’ imisi yose mu rusengero no mu mihana ntibahorereza kwigisha no kuvuga ubutumwa bgiza bga Yesu, kw ari we Kristo." 
Acts6:1 Kandi mur’ iyo misi, abigishwa bāriko baragwira, Abayuda bavuye i Bugiriki bidodombera Abaheburayo b’inyamo, kukw abapfakazi babo bīrengagizwa ku ngaburo y’imisi yose." 
Acts6:2 Bamwe cumi na babiri bakoranya ishengero ry’abigishwa, bati Ntibibereye yuko twebge turekera ijambo ry’Imana kugaburisha ivyo ku meza." 
Acts6:3 Nuko, bene Data, ni murābe muri mwebge abantu ndwi bashimwa, buzuye Mpwemu Yera n’ubgenge, tubashire kur’ iki gikorwa." 
Acts6:4 Ariko tweho tuzoshishikara gusenga no kugabura ijambo ry’Imana. 
Acts6:5 Ayo majambo ishengero ryose rirayashima, batoranya Stefano, umuntu yuzuye ukwizera na Mpwemu Yera, na Filipo, na Purokoro, na Nikanori, na Timoni, na Parumena, na Nikolayo, Umunyantiyokiya yatoye idini y’Abayuda," 
Acts6:6 babashira imbere y’intumwa, kandi bamaze gusenga zibarambikakw ibiganza." 
Acts6:7 Nukw ijambo ry’Imana riragwira; abigishwa barōndōka cane i Yerusalemu, abaherezi b’akavuvu bumvira ukwizera." 
Acts6:8 Stefano yari yuzuye ubuntu bg’Imana n’ubushobozi, yakora mu bantu ibitangaza n’ibimenyetso bikomeye." 
Acts6:9 Ariko hava hasi abantu bamwe bo mw isinagogi y’Abaliberutino, n’iy’ Abanyakurene n’iy’ Abanyalekisanderiya, n’iy’ Abanyakilikiya, n’iy’ Abanyasiya, baja impāri na Stefano," 
Acts6:10 ariko ntibashobora gutsinda ubgenge na Mpwemu bimuvugisha. 
Acts6:11 Nuko bahēra abagabo bo kuvuga, bati Twumvise avuga amagambo y’amarogotano kuri Mose no ku Mana." 
Acts6:12 Bosha abantu n’abakuru n’abanyabgenge b’ivyanditswe baramugīra, baramufata, bamujana mw ikombe." 
Acts6:13 Bahagarika ivyabona vy’ibinyoma, baravuga, bat’ Uyu muntu nta ho ahumeka gutuka aha hantu hēra n’ivyagezwe:" 
Acts6:14 kuko twumvise avuga, ati Yesu Umunyanazareti azokombora aha hantu, kandi ngw azohindura imigenzo twahawe na Mose." 
Acts6:15 Abicaye mw ikombe bose bamuhanze amaso babona mu maso hiwe, hasa n’ah’ umumarayika." 
Acts7:1 Umuherezi mukuru aramubaza, ati Mbeg’ ivyo ni ko biri?" 
Acts7:2 Na we aramwishura, ati Yemwe bene Data kandi ba data, ni mwumve: Imana y’icubahiro yiyeretse sogokuruza Aburahamu, ar’ i Mesopotamiya, ataraja kugerēra i Harani," 
Acts7:3 iramubarira, iti Va mu gihugu canyu no mu muryango wanyu, uje mu gihugu nzokwereka." 
Acts7:4 Maz’ ava mu gihugu c’i Bukaludaya, agerēra i Harani. Se amaze gupfa, iramwimura, imuzana mur’ iki gihugu mubamwo none." 
Acts7:5 Ariko ntiyakimuhayemw’ umwandu, naho hoba aho gushinga ikirenge; isezerana kuzokimuha ngo kibe ishamvu yiwe n’iy’ uruvyaro rwiwe, kand’ ataragira umwana." 
Acts7:6 Kand’ Imana ivuga irtya, it’ Uruvyaro rwawe ruzoba inyambukira mu kindi gihugu, bazobagira abaja, babagirire nabi imyaka amajana ane." 
Acts7:7 Kand’ ihanga rizobagira abaja ni jewe nzoricirakw iteka, Imana ni ko yagize, it’ Arikw amaherezo bazovayo, bansengere aha hantu." 
Acts7:8 Maz’ imuha isezerano ryo gukebga. Nukw avyara Isaka, amukeba ku musi ugira umunani: Isaka avyara Yakobo, Yakobo avyara ba sogokuruza bakuru cumi na babiri." 
Acts7:9 Ba sogokuruza bagirira Yosefu ishari, baramugura ngw ajanwe muri Egiputa. Imana ibana na we," 
Acts7:10 imukiza mu marushwa yiwe yose, imuha ubutoni n’ubgenge kuri Farawo, umwami wo muri Egiputa, amugira icēgēra ciwe ngw aganze muri Egiputa, amuzēza n’urugo rwiwe rwose." 
Acts7:11 Ikigoyi gitera muri Egiputa hose n’i Kanani, hatera n’amarushwa menshi, kandi ba sogokuruza babura ivyo kurya." 
Acts7:12 Maze Yakobo yumvise yuko muri Egiputa har’ amasumo, atuma ba sogokuruza ubga mbere." 
Acts7:13 Kand’ ubugira kabiri Yosefu yibarira bene se, umuryango wa Yosefu umenywa na Farawo." 
Acts7:14 Yosefu atumiza se Yakobo n’abo mu nzu yabo bose, ukw ari mirongwirindwi na batanu." 
Acts7:15 Yakobo aramanuka, aja muri Egiputa; agwayo, bo na ba sogokuruza:" 
Acts7:16 babajana i Shekemu, babahamba mw isenga Aburahamu yaguze igiciro c’ifeza na bene Hamori i Shekemu." 
Acts7:17 Arikw igihe c’isezerano kigira gishike, iry’ Imana yasezeraniye Aburahamu, abantu baragwira, baba benshi muri Egiputa," 
Acts7:18 gushitsa ah’ uwundi mwami yīmiye muri Egiputa atigeze kumenya ivya Yosefu. 
Acts7:19 Uwo mwami agirira ubugunge ubgoko bgacu, agirira ba sogokuruza nabi, abateshereza abana babo b’inzoya kugira ngo ntibabeho." 
Acts7:20 Mur’ ico gihe Mose aravuka, yari mwiza cane, bamurerera mu nzu kwa se amezi atatu;" 
Acts7:21 amaze gutābga, umukobga wa Farawo aramutora, amurerera kuba umwana wiwe." 
Acts7:22 Mose yigishwa ubgenge bgose bg’Abanyegiputa, agira ubushobozi mu majambo yiwe no mu bikorwa vyiwe." 
Acts7:23 Maz’ arikw aramara imyaka mirongwine avutse, haza iciyumviro mu mutima wiwe co kugendera bene wabo b’Abisirayeli." 
Acts7:24 Abonye umuntu agirirwa nabi, aramutabara, ahōra iyo mpahazwa, yica wa Munyegiputa." 
Acts7:25 Yibgira yukw ab’i wabo botahura kw Imana ibakirisha ukuboko kwiwe: ariko ntibabimenya. 
Acts7:26 Bukeye bg’aho, asanga abarwana, ageza kubatātūra, ati Yemwe bagabo, mur’ umuryango umwe, n’iki gitumye mugiriranira nabi?" 
Acts7:27 Arik’ uwagirira mugenzi we nabi aramusunika, aramubaza, ati Ni nde yakugize umukuru cank’ umucamanza wacu?" 
Acts7:28 Mbeg’ ugomba kunyica, nk’ukw ejo wishe wa Munyegiputa?" 
Acts7:29 Mose yumvise iryo jambo, arahunga, aba umwambukīra mu gihugu c’i Midiyani, avyariray’ abahungu babiri." 
Acts7:30 Imyaka mirongwine ishize, umumarayika amubonekerera mu rubeya rw’umuriro waka mu gisaka c’amahwa mu bugaragwa bgo ku musozi Sinayi." 
Acts7:31 Mose abonye ivyo biramutangaza: akivyēgēra ngw avyihweze, havuga ijwi ry’Uhoraho," 
Acts7:32 ati Ni jewe Mana ya ba sogokuruza bawe, Imana ya Aburahamu, Imana ya Isaka, Imana ya Yakobo. Mose ahinda agashitsi, ntiyatinyuka kwihweza." 
Acts7:33 Uhoraho aramubarira, ati Kūra inkweto mu birenge vyawe, kukw aho hantu uhagaze ar’ ahēra." 
Acts7:34 N’ukuri abantu banje bari muri Egiputa nabonye amarushwa barimwo, numvise umuniho wabo, none mmanukanywe no kubarokora: kandi none n’uze ndagutume muri Egiputa." 
Acts7:35 Mose uyo, umwe banka, bati Ni nde yakugize umukuru cank’ umucamanza? ni we Imana yatumye kuba umukuru n’umucunguzi, abihawe n’ukuboko kw’umumarayika yamubonekereye muri ca gisaka." 
Acts7:36 Uwo abakūrayo, amaze gukora ibitangaza n’ibimenyetso mu gihugu ca Egiputa, no ku Kiyaga Gitukura no mu bugaragwa, imyaka mirongwine." 
Acts7:37 Uwo Mose ni we yabgiye Abisirayeli, at’ Imana izobahagurukiriza ūvugishwa na yo mu b’i wanyu, ameze nkanje." 
Acts7:38 Kand’ uwo Mose ni we yari mw ishengero ryo mu bugaragwa, ari kumwe n’umumarayika yavuganiye na we ku musozi Sinayi, kand’ ari kumwe na ba sogokuruza; kandi yaherejwe amajambo y’ubugingo ngw aduhe." 
Acts7:39 Ba sogokuruza banse kumwumvira, baramwikunkumura, basubira muri Egiputa mu mitima yabo," 
Acts7:40 babgira Aroni, bati N’uturonkere imana zo kutuja imbere; kuk’ umwe Mose yaturōngōye adukūra mu gihugu ca Egiputa, tutazi ico yabaye." 
Acts7:41 Bironkera igishushanyo c’imasa mur’ iyo misi, ico kigirwamana bakizanira ibimazi, bahimbarwa n’ibikorwa vy’intoke zabo." 
Acts7:42 Arikw Imana irora irya, irabaheba ngo basenge ingabo zo kw ijuru: nk’uko vyanditswe mu gitabo c’abavugishwa n’Imana, ngo Mbega har’ ibitungwa bibāzwe cank’ ibimazi mwanshikaniye, Ya myaka ukw ari mirongwine yo mu bugaragwa, yemwe ab’ inzu ya Isirayeli?" 
Acts7:43 Mwareruye ihema rya Moloki, N’inyenyeri y’ikigirwamana Refani, Ar’ ibishushanyo mwironkeye ngo mubisenge: Nanje nzobambukana hirya y’i Babuloni." 
Acts7:44 Ba sogokuruza bāri bafise ihema ry’Ibishinga intahe, hamwe bāri mu bugaragwa, nk’ukw iyavuganye na Mose yabigeze, yamubgiye kurigereranya n’ikigereranyo yabonye." 
Acts7:45 Iryo, ba sogokuruza barihawe na ba sekuru babo, barishikana ino, Yosuwa ari kumwe na bo, hamwe bātsinda amahanga, Imana iyirukana imbere ya ba sogokuruza, gushitsa ku gihe ca Dawidi." 
Acts7:46 Kandi Dawidi aronka ubutoni mu nyonga z’Imana, asaba kwubakira Imana ya Yakobo aho kuba." 
Acts7:47 Ariko Salomo ni we yayubakiye ingoro. 
Acts7:48 Yamar’ Īsumba vyose ntiba mu zubakishijwe amaboko: nk’uk’ uwavugishijwe n’Imana yavuze," 
Acts7:49 at’ Ijuru ni ryo ntebe yanje y’ubgami, Isi na yo n’indava y’ibirenge vyanje; Muzonyubakira inzu ki? ni k’Uhoraho abajije, Canke nzoruhukira ahantu ki?" 
Acts7:50 Mbeg’ intoke zanje si zo zaremye ivyo vyose? 
Acts7:51 Yemwe abatagonda izosi, mwa ntakebga mu mitima no mu matwi, na ntaryo murwanya Mpwemu Yera. Uko ba sogokuruza banyu bākora, ni ko namwe mukora." 
Acts7:52 Ni nde mu bavugishijwe n’Imana ba sogokuruza banyu batāhamye? Bishe abābanje kumenyekanisha ivyo kuza kwa wa Mugororotsi, none namwe mwaramuguze muramwica:" 
Acts7:53 ari mwebge mwāhawe ivyagezwe bizanywe n’abamarayika, ntimwavyitondera." 
Acts7:54 Bavyumvise baribga mu mitima, bamuhekenyera imisaya." 
Acts7:55 Ariko Stefano yuzuye Mpwemu Yera, ahanga amaso mw ijuru, abona ubgiza bg’Imana, na Yesu ahagaze i buryo bg’Imana:" 
Acts7:56 aravuga, at’ Ehe mbonye ijuru rikingurutse, n’Umwana w’umuntu ahagaze i buryo bg’Imana." 
Acts7:57 Barayogora n’amajwi arenga, bīziba amatwi, bamugwirakw icarimwe," 
Acts7:58 bamuhindira inyuma y’igisagara, bamwicisha amabuye; kand’ abāmwagirije bāri bafashije hasi imitamana yabo imbere y’ibirenge vy’umusore yitwa Sauli." 
Acts7:59 Maze bakiriko baratera Stefano amabuye, arambaza, aravuga, ati Mwami Yesu, akīra ubugingo bganje." 
Acts7:60 Araheza arapfukama, asemerera n’ijwi rirenga, ati Mwami, ntubaharūrekw iki caha. Amaze kuvuga artyo, aca aracīkāna. Kandi Sauli na we yarabishimye ko yicwa." 
Acts8:1 Bahēra kur’ uwo musi bahama cane ishengero ry’i Yerusalemu: bose basābagirira mu bihugu vy’i Yudaya n’i Samariya, ukūyemw’ intumwa gusa." 
Acts8:2 Abantu bubaha Imana bahamba Stefano, baramuborogera cane." 
Acts8:3 Ariko Sauli yatikiza ishengero; yinjira mu mazu yose, agakūramw’ abagabo n’abagore, akabashira mw ibohero." 
Acts8:4 Arikw abāsābagiye bagendagenda bavuga ijambo ry’Imana. 
Acts8:5 Na Filipo aramanuka, aja mu gisagara c’i Samariya, abamenyesha ivya Kristo." 
Acts8:6 Abantu benshi bashira umutima ku vyo Filipo avuga bashize hamwe, bumvise kandi babonye ibimenyetso akora." 
Acts8:7 Kuko benshi muri bo bāri binjiwemwo n’impwemu zihumanye zābavamwo, ziboroga n’amajwi arenga; kandi n’abāri bamugaye n’abacumbagira benshi barakizwa." 
Acts8:8 Haba umunezero mwinshi mur’ ico gisagara. 
Acts8:9 Kandi hāriy’ umuntu yitwa Simoni, yahora akora ivy’ amarēba mur’ico gisagara, akūmiza ubgoko bg’Abasamariya, akīyita agakomeye." 
Acts8:10 Bama bamushizek’ umutima bose, uhereye ku boroshe ugashitsa ku bahambaye, bat’ Uyu ni we bga bushobozi bg’Imana bgitwa Ubuhambaye." 
Acts8:11 Arikw icatuma bamushirak’ umutima n’uk’ uhereye kera yabūmiza n’amarēba yiwe. 
Acts8:12 Ariko bizeye ubutumwa bgiza Filipo ababgiye bg’ubgami bg’Imana, n’ubg’ izina rya Yesu Kristo, barabatizwa, abagabo n’abagore." 
Acts8:13 Na Simoni na we arizera, kand’ amaze kubatizwa yāmana na Filipo: abonye ibimenyetso n’ibitangaza bihambaye vyakorwa, arūmirwa." 
Acts8:14 Maz’ intumwa zir’i Yerusalemu zumvise yukw Abasamariya bemeye ijambo ry’Imana, zirungikayo Petero na Yohana," 
Acts8:15 na bo bamanutseyo barabasengera ngo bahabge Mpwemu Yera; 
Acts8:16 kuko Mpwemu ataribgamanuke ngw aje no kur’ umwe muri bo, bāri babatijwe gusa mw izina ry’Umwami Yesu." 
Acts8:17 Maze babarambikakw ibiganza, bahabga Mpwemu Yera." 
Acts8:18 Ariko Simoni, abonye yukw abarambitswekw ibiganza vy’intumwa bahabga Mpwemu Yera, azizanira amahera," 
Acts8:19 ati Nanje ni mumpe ubgo bushobozi, kugira ng’uwo nzorambikakw ibiganza az’ ahabge Mpwemu Yera." 
Acts8:20 Petero aramubgira, at’ Ifeza zawe ziragapfana nawe, kuk’ ugira ngw ingabire y’Imana woyironkesha amahera." 
Acts8:21 Nta n’agahimba ufise, nta n’akagabane kavyo, kuk’ umutima wawe udatunganye imbere y’Imana." 
Acts8:22 Nuko wihane ubgo bubi bgawe, usenge Umwami Imana, namba kumbure ivyo wiyumviriye mu mutima wawe wobiharirwa." 
Acts8:23 Kuko mbona yuk’ uri mw ibamba ry’umururazi no mu ngoyi zo kugabitanya. 
Acts8:24 Simoni aramwishura, ati Munsengere Umwami Imana, ivyo muvuze hoye kugira ikimbako." 
Acts8:25 Na bo bamaze gushinga intahe, no kuvuga ijambo ry’Umwami Yesu, basubira i Yerusalemu, bagenda baravuga ubutumwa bgiza mu mihana myinshi y’Abasamariya." 
Acts8:26 Maz’ umumarayika w’Umwami Imana abarira Filipo, ati Va hasi uje i bumanuko, ushike ku nzira imanuka iva i Yerusalemu ikaja i Gaza: imwe yo mu bugaragwa." 
Acts8:27 Ava hasi, aragenda. Haza Umunyetiyopiya, inkone y’ububasha bginshi yakorera Kanidake, umugabekazi w’Abanyetiyopiya, ni yo yazezwa itunga ryiwe ryose, yari yagiye i Yerusalemu gusenga." 
Acts8:28 Yahindukiye yicaye mu mukogote wiwe ukwegwa n’amafarasi, asoma muri Yesaya yavugishwa n’Imana." 
Acts8:29 Mpwemu abarira Filipo, ati Ni wēgēre uriya mukogote, ugendane na wo." 
Acts8:30 Filipo yirukirayo, yumva asoma muri Yesaya yavugishwa n’Imana; aramubaza, at’ Ivyo usoma urabitahuye?" 
Acts8:31 Na we ati Nobishobora nte, ntabonye ūbindōngōramwo? Yinginga Filipo ngo yūrire bicarane." 
Acts8:32 Igihimba co mu vyanditswe yasoma cār’ iki, ngo Yajanywe nk’intama bajana mw ibāgiro, Nk’uk’ umwagazi w’intama utekerereza imbere y’uwukemura Ni kw atākūyek’ umunwa." 
Acts8:33 Hamwe yacishwa bugufi barēngānye urubanza rwiwe, Ab’ urunganwe rwiwe ni nde azoshobora kubadondora? Kuk’ ubugingo bgiwe bukūwe mw isi." 
Acts8:34 Iyo nkone ibaza Filipo, iti Ndakubaza: uwavugishwa n’Imana yavuze ayo majambo kuri nde? Ni we yayīvuzeko, canke yayavuze ku wundi?" 
Acts8:35 Filipo ateranura akanwa, atangurira kur’ ivyo vyanditswe, amubgira ubutumwa bgiza bga Yesu." 
Acts8:36 Bakigenda mu nzira, bashika ah’ ar’ amazi, iyo nkone iramubaza, it’ Ehe amazi: ikimbuza kubatizwa n’iki? [" 
Acts8:37 Filipo arayishura, ati Namba wizeye mu mutima wawe wose birashoboka. Na yo iti Nizeye Yesu Kristo kw ar’ Umwana w’Imana.]" 
Acts8:38 Ivuga ko bahagarika umukogote, baramanukana baja mu mazi bompi, Filipo n’iyo nkone, arayibatiza." 
Acts8:39 Bavuye mu mazi, Mpwemu w’Umwami Imana ajana Filipo, inkone ntiyasubira kumubona, kuko yashishikaye kugenda inezerewe." 
Acts8:40 Ariko Filipo abonekera muri Azoto, ahahita avuga ubutumwa bgiza mu bisagara vyose, kugeza aho yashikiye i Kayisariya." 
Acts9:1 Ariko Sauli, akigenda afuhagira, afitiye abigishwa b’Umwami imihigo n’ubgicanyi, aja ku muherezi mukuru," 
Acts9:2 amusaba ivyete vyo guha ab’ amasinagogi y’i Damasiko, kugira ngo ni yabona abantu bakurikira Inzira ya Yesu, ar’ abagabo cank’ abagore, abajane i Yerusalemu mu ngoyi." 
Acts9:3 Maz’ arikw aragenda, agira ashike i Damasiko, haza umuco giturumbuka, uvuye mw ijuru, umukayanganira irya n’ino." 
Acts9:4 Yikubita hasi, yumva ijwi rimubaza, riti Sauli, Sauli, umpīgira iki?" 
Acts9:5 Aramubaza, at’ Uri nde ga Mwami? Na we ati Ni jewe Yesu, uwo urik’ urahīga;" 
Acts9:6 ariko va hasi, ushike mu gisagara, uzobarirwa ivy’ ukwiye gukora." 
Acts9:7 Abagabo bajanye na we bahagarara badakoma, kuko bumvise ijwi, ata muntu babona." 
Acts9:8 Sauli aravyuka, ava hasi, maz’ akanuye amaso ntiyagira ic’ abona: bamufata ukuboko, bamushikana i Damasiko." 
Acts9:9 Amarayo gatatu, atabona, ata co arya, ata co anywa." 
Acts9:10 I Damasiko hār’ umwigishwa yitwa Ananiya: Umwami Yesu aramwiyereka, aramuhamagara, ati Ananiya. Na we ati Sabge, Mwami." 
Acts9:11 Umwami aramubarira, ati Va hasi, uje mu nzira yitwa Igororotse, ubarizeyo mu rugo kwa Yuda umuntu yitwa Sauli w’i Taruso, kukw arikw arasenga." 
Acts9:12 Kandi yabonye umuntu yitwa Ananiya yinjira ah’ ari, amurambikakw ibiganza, kugira ngw ahumūke." 
Acts9:13 Ananiya aramwishura, ati Mwami, uwo mugabo ko numvise benshi bavuga ivyiwe, vy’inabi nyinshi yagirira abera bawe i Yerusalemu:" 
Acts9:14 kandi n’ino ahafise ububasha abuhāwe n’abaherezi bakuru, bgo kuboha abambaza izina ryawe bose." 
Acts9:15 Umwami aramwishura, ati Pfa kugenda, kuk’ uwo muntu ar’ ikintu nītoranirije, ngw ajane izina ryanje imbere y’abanyamahanga n’abami n’Abisirayeli:" 
Acts9:16 nanje nzomwereka imibabaro ukw ingana azoba akwiye kubabazwa ahōrwa izina ryanje. 
Acts9:17 Ananiya aragenda, yinjira mu nzu, amurambikakw ibiganza, aramubgira, ati Sauli, mwene Data, Umwami arantumye, ni we Yesu yakubonekereye mu nzira wazananye, ng’uhumūke, wuzuzwe Mpwemu Yera." 
Acts9:18 Uwo mwanya ibisa n’ibikaragashi bimuva ku maso, arahumūka, ava hasi, arabatizwa:" 
Acts9:19 maz’ ararya, intege ziragaruka. Amarana imisi n’abigishwa b’i Damasiko;" 
Acts9:20 aca ahērakw avuga mu masinagogi ivya Yesu, yukw ar’ Umwana w’Imana." 
Acts9:21 Abamwumvise bose barūmirwa, bati Mbeg’ uyu si we yatikije abambaza iryo zina i Yerusalemu? Kandi ni co cari kimuzanye n’ino, kugira ngw abashīre abaherezi bakuru bari mu ngoyi." 
Acts9:22 Ariko Sauli arushiriza kugira ubushobozi, atsinda Abayuda baba i Damasiko, abereka yuko Yesu ari we Kristo." 
Acts9:23 Hashize imisi myinshi, Abayuda baja inama yo kumwica:" 
Acts9:24 maze Sauli amenya inama yabo. Bamutegera ku marembo ku murango no mw ijoro kugira ngo bamwice. 
Acts9:25 Maz’ abigishwa biwe bamujana mw ijoro, bamucisha mu ruzitiro rw’amabuye, bamwururukirije mu gisangaza." 
Acts9:26 Ashitse i Yerusalemu, agerageza kwifatanya n’abigishwa: bose baramutinya, ntibemera kw ar’ umwigishwa." 
Acts9:27 Maze Barunaba aramwākīra, amushīra intumwa, azīgānira ingene yaboneye Umwami Yesu mu nzira, n’ingene yavuganye na we, kandi n’ingene yavuze ashize amanga mw izina rya Yesu i Damasiko." 
Acts9:28 Aba kumwe na bo amaja n’amaza i Yerusalemu," 
Acts9:29 avuga ashize amanga mw izina ry’Umwami Yesu; yaravuga ahārīra n’Abayuda bāvuye i Bugiriki: na bo barondera ingene bomwica. 
Acts9:30 Ariko bene Data babimenye, bamumanukana i Kayisariya, bamurungika i Taruso." 
Acts9:31 Nukw ishengero ryose ryari hose i Yudaya n’i Galilaya n’i Samariya rigira amahoro, rirahangama: kandi rigenda ryubaha Umwami Yesu, rihagarikiwe na Mpwemu Yera, riragwira." 
Acts9:32 Nuko Petero agendagenda hose, amanuka no ku bera baba i Luda," 
Acts9:33 asangay’ umuntu yitwa Ayineya, yar’ amaze imyaka munani avunda mu buriri, kuko yari yaramugaye." 
Acts9:34 Petero aramubgira, ati Ayineya, Yesu Kristo aragukijije: vyuka, wizingire ikirago. Aca avyuka ako kanya." 
Acts9:35 Ababa i Luda n’i Saroni bose bamubonye bahindukirira Umwami Yesu. 
Acts9:36 Kand’ i Yopa hār’ umwigishwa yitwa Tabita, risobanurwa ngo Doruka: uwo mugore yari n’ibikorwa vyiza vyinshi, n’ubuntu bginshi yagira." 
Acts9:37 Mur’ iyo misi ararwara, arapfa: bamaze kwuhagira ikiziga, bagishira mu nzu yo hejuru." 
Acts9:38 Kandi kukw i Luda hāri hafi y’i Yopa, abigishwa, bumvise ko Petero ari yo ari, bamutumakw abantu babiri, bamwinginga, bati Ntutebe kudushikīra." 
Acts9:39 Petero arikora, ajana na bo: ashitseyo bamujana muri ya nzu yo hejuru, abapfakazi bose bahagarara i ruhande yiwe barira, berekana amapfundo n’imitamana Doruka yapfunditse akiri muri bo." 
Acts9:40 Petero arabataramura bose, arapfukama, arasenga; maz’ ahindukirira umuvyimba, ati Tabita, vyuka. Arakanura; maz’ abonye Petero, aravyuka, aricara." 
Acts9:41 Amufata ukuboko, aramuhagarika. Maz’ ahamagara abera n’abapfakazi, amubaha ari muzima." 
Acts9:42 Bimenyekana i Yopa hose, benshi bizera Umwami Yesu." 
Acts9:43 Maz’ amara imisi myinshi i Yopa, kwa Simoni umuhazi w’insāto." 
Acts10:1 I Kayisariya hār’ umuntu yitwa Koruneliyo, umugabisha w’abasoda ijana wo mu ngabo zitwa Abanyetaliya." 
Acts10:2 Yar’ umuntu yubaha Imana akayitinyana n’abo mu nzu yiwe bose, yagirira abantu ubuntu bginshi, agasenga Imana ubudasība." 
Acts10:3 Abona yeretswe imbonankubone umumarayika w’Imana yinjiye i we hāri nk’isaha cenda z’umusi: aramuhamagara, ati Koruneliyo." 
Acts10:4 Na we amukanurira amaso, afise ubgoba, aramubaza, ati N’iki ga Mwami? Aramwishura, ati Gusenga kwawe n’ubuntu bgawe vyadūze biba icibutso imbere y’Imana." 
Acts10:5 None rero tuma abantu i Yopa, utumek’ umuntu yitwa Simoni, ari we Petero;" 
Acts10:6 asembereye kwa Simoni umuhazi w’insāto, urugo rwiwe rur’i ruhande y’ikiyaga." 
Acts10:7 Umumarayika yavuganye na we amaze kugenda, ahamagara babiri bo mu basuku biwe, n’umusoda yubaha Imana wo mu bamugendanira:" 
Acts10:8 ahejeje kubīgānira vyose, abatuma i Yopa." 
Acts10:9 Bukeye bg’aho, bakigenda, bari hafi gushika mu gisagara, Petero yūrira hejuru ku nzu gusenga, hāri nk’isaha zitandatu." 
Acts10:10 Yumva arashonje, agomba kurya: bakibirondera, amera nk’ūrota," 
Acts10:11 abona ijuru ryugurutse, maze hamanuka ikintu kimeze nk’uruhuzu runiniya, rufashwe ku mitwe ine, kija hasi," 
Acts10:12 hārimw’ ubgoko bgose bg’ibigenza amaguru ane, n’ibikwega inda hasi vyo kw isi, n’ibiguruka vyo mu kirēre." 
Acts10:13 Haza ijwi, riramubarira, riti Va hasi, Petero, ubāge, urye." 
Acts10:14 Petero at’ Oyaye, Mwami, kuko ntigeze ndya ikizira cank’ igihumanya." 
Acts10:15 Iryo jwi risubira kuza ubugira kabiri, riramubarira, rit’ Ivy’ Imana ihumanuye, reka kuvyita ibizira." 
Acts10:16 Biba birtyo gatatu, ico kintu gica gisubizwa mw ijuru." 
Acts10:17 Petero akizazaniwe mu mutima n’ivyo abonye yeretswe ivy’ ari vyo, abantu batumwe na Koruneliyo, bahejeje kubaza urugo rwa Simoni, bahagarara kw irembo," 
Acts10:18 barahamagara, babaza yuko Simoni ari we Petero ari ho asembereye." 
Acts10:19 Petero aciyumvira ivyo yeretswe, Mpwemu aramubarira, ati Har’ abantu batatu bariko barakurondera." 
Acts10:20 None va hasi, wururuke ujane na bo ata co ukekeranya, kukw ari jewe mbatumye." 
Acts10:21 Petero arururuka, asanga abo bantu aho bari, arababarira, ati Ni jewe uwo murondera: mbega mugenzwa n’iki?" 
Acts10:22 Baramwishura, bati Koruneliyo, umugabisha w’abasoda ijana, umuntu agororoka yubaha Imana, ashimwa n’ubgoko bgose bg’Abayuda, yabariwe n’umumarayika yera kugutumako, ng’ uze i we, yumve amajambo yawe." 
Acts10:23 Maz’ arabinjiza, abaha indāro. Bukeye bg’aho, Petero arīkora, avanayo na bo, na bene Data bamwe b’i Yopa bajana na we." 
Acts10:24 Bukeye bg’aho bashika i Kayisariya, Koruneliyo yar’ abīteze, yākoranije incuti ziwe n’abakunzi bo ku mutima." 
Acts10:25 Petero agira yinjire, Koruneliyo aramusanganira, yikubita imbere y’ibirenge vyiwe, aramupfukamira." 
Acts10:26 Maze Petero amukūra hasi, ati Va hasi, nanje nd’umuntu nkawe." 
Acts10:27 Bakivugana, arinjira asanga abakoraniyeho benshi," 
Acts10:28 arababgira, at’ Ubganyu murazi yuko kizira k’umuntu w’Umuyuda yifatanya n’uw’ ubundi bgoko, canke kw amugendera: ariko jeho, Imana yanyeretse yuko hatogira umuntu nita ikizira cank’ igihumanya." 
Acts10:29 Ni co catumye nza, ntarinze guhakana, ntumweko. None rero ndabaza ico mwantumiyeko ic’ ari co." 
Acts10:30 Koruneliyo ati Hashize imisi ine, nka bugingo ubu, nariko ndasenga ar’ isaha cenda, ndi mu nzu yanje; maz’ umuntu ahagarara imbere yanje, yambaye impuzu ikayangana," 
Acts10:31 arambgira, ati Koruneliyo, ugusenga kwawe kwarumviswe, n’ubuntu bgawe bgibutswe imbere y’Imana." 
Acts10:32 Nuko tuma i Yopa, utumeko Simoni ari we Petero: asembereye mu rugo kwa Simoni umuhazi w’insāto, i ruhande y’ikiyaga." 
Acts10:33 Uwo mwanya nca ndagutumako rero, nawe urayobotse k’uje. None rero twese turi hano imbere y’Imana, kwumva ivy’ Umwami Imana yakugeze kutubgira vyose." 
Acts10:34 Petero yanzika kuvuga, ati N’ukuri ni ho nkimenya yukw Imana itarobanura abantu ku butoni," 
Acts10:35 ariko mu mahanga yose ūyubaha, agakora ivy’ ukugororoka, iramwemera." 
Acts10:36 Ijambo Imana yatumye ku Bisirayeli, ivugisha Yesu Kristo ubutumwa bgiza bg’amahoro, ni we Mwami wa bose;" 
Acts10:37 iryo jambo mwebge murarizi, ryāmāmaye i Yudaya hose, ritanguriye i Galilaya, hanyuma y’umubatizo uwo Yohana yigishije:" 
Acts10:38 rivuga ivya Yesu Umunyanazareti, ingen’ Imana yamusutseko Mpwemu Yera n’ubushobozi, akagenda agirira abantu neza, agakiza abo bose wa Murwanizi atwaza amanyama, kukw Imana yari kumwe na we." 
Acts10:39 Natwe tur’ ivyabona vyo gushingira intahe ivyo yakoze vyose mu gihugu c’Abayuda, bo n’i Yerusalemu, umwe bishe, bamumanitse ku giti." 
Acts10:40 Uyo, Imana iramuzura ku musi ugira gatatu, imuha guserurwa ahibonekeza," 
Acts10:41 s’imbere y’abantu bose, arikw imbere y’ivyabona vyatoranijwe n’Imana ivyo bitarabaho, ni twebge, abāsangira na we, turya kandi tunywa, amaze kuzuka mu bapfuye." 
Acts10:42 Atugera kumenyesha abantu no gushinga intahe kw ari we Imana yashinze kuba Umucamateka w’abariho n’abapfuye. 
Acts10:43 Abāvugishwa n’Imana bose bāmushingiye intahe, bavuga yuk’ ūmwizera wese azoharirwa ivyaha kubg’ izina ryiwe." 
Acts10:44 Petero akivuga ayo majambo, Mpwemu Yera aramanuka, aja ku bariko barumva iryo jambo bose." 
Acts10:45 Abizeye bo mu bākebge barūmirwa, abāzananye na Petero uko bangana, kuko n’abanyamahanga na bo basutswekw ingabire, ari yo Mpwemu Yera." 
Acts10:46 Kuko bumvise bavuga izindi ndimi, bahimbaza Imana. Maze Petero arababaza," 
Acts10:47 ati Mbega har’ uwoshobora kwima amazi abahawe Mpwemu Yera nkatwe, ngo ntibabatizwe?" 
Acts10:48 Avuga ko babatizwa mw izina rya Yesu Kristo. Baca baramwinginga ngw amarey’ imisi. 
Acts11:1 Intumwa na bene Data bar’i Yudaya bumva yukw abanyamahanga na bo bemeye ijambo ry’Imana. 
Acts11:2 Maze Petero adūze i Yerusalemu, abo mu bākebge baramutonganya," 
Acts11:3 bati Ko winjiriye abatākebge, ugasangira na bo!" 
Acts11:4 Maze Petero aratangura, abibasobanurira uko bikurikirana," 
Acts11:5 ati Nari mu gisagara c’i Yopa, ndiko ndasenga, mbona neretswe nko mu nzozi ikintu kimanuka kivuye mw ijuru, kimeze nk’uruhuzu runiniya rufashwe ku mitwe ine, kiza aho ndi." 
Acts11:6 Ngihanga amaso, ndacitegereza, mbonamw’ ibigenza amaguru ane vyo kw isi, n’ibikōko vyo mw ishamba, n’ibikwega inda hasi, n’ibiguruka vyo mu kirēre." 
Acts11:7 Kandi numva ijwi rimbarira, riti Va hasi, Petero, ubāge urye." 
Acts11:8 Nanje nt’ Oyaye, Mwami, kukw ata kizira cank’ igihumanya cigeze kija mu kanwa kanje." 
Acts11:9 Maz’ ijwi rimbarira ubugira kabiri rivuye mw ijuru, rit’ Ivy’ Imana ihumanuye, reka kuvyita ibizira." 
Acts11:10 Biba birtyo gatatu, biradūzwa vyose, bisubizwa mw ijuru." 
Acts11:11 Uwo mwanya abagabo batatu bavuye i Kayisariya, bantumweko, bahagarara imbere y’inzu turimwo." 
Acts11:12 Mpwemu ambarira kujana na bo, ata tandukaniro. Kandi na bene Data aba, ukw ari batandatu, turajana, twinjira mu nzu y’uwo mugabo." 
Acts11:13 Atwīgānira ingene yabonye umumarayika mu nzu yiwe, ahagaze amubarira, ati Tuma i Yopa, utumeko Simoni ari we Petero," 
Acts11:14 azokubarira amajambo yo kugukizanya n’abo mu nzu yawe bose. 
Acts11:15 Ngitanguye kuvuga, Mpwemu Yera arabamanukira, nk’uko yamanukiye kuri twebge ubga mbere." 
Acts11:16 Nibuka rya jambo ry’Umwami Yesu, uko yavuze, ati Yohana yabatirishije amazi, ariko mweho muzobatizwa na Mpwemu Yera." 
Acts11:17 None kw Imana yabahaye ingabire imwe n’iyo natwe twahawe hamwe twizera Umwami Yesu Kristo, jewe nd’ iki gishobora gutāngīra Imana?" 
Acts11:18 Bumvise ivyo barīhorera, bahimbaza Imana, bati Noneho rer’ Imana ihaye n’abanyamahanga kwihana ngo baronke ubugingo." 
Acts11:19 Nukw abāsābagijwe n’amarushwa yabaye kubg’ ivya Stefano baragenda, bashika n’i Foyinike n’i Kupuro no muri Antiyokiya, ata bandi babarira ijambo ry’Imana atar’ Abayuda bonyene." 
Acts11:20 Ariko hāri bamwe muri bo b’abagabo bavuye i Kupuro n’i Kurene bashitse muri Antiyokiya babarira n’Abagiriki na bo, bababgira ubutumwa bgiza bg’Umwami Yesu." 
Acts11:21 Ukuboko kw’Umwami kwari kumwe na bo, abantu benshi barizera, bahindukirira Umwami." 
Acts11:22 Inkuru yabo ishika mu matwi y’ishengero ry’i Yerusalemu, batuma Barunaba ngw ashirwe ashitse muri Antiyokiya." 
Acts11:23 Na we amaze gushikayo, abonye ubuntu bg’Imana, biramunezereza, arabahanūra bose ngo bamaramaze mu mitima kwifatanya akaramata n’Umwami Yesu." 
Acts11:24 Kuko yar’ imico myiza, yuzuye Mpwemu Yera n’ukwizera. Abantu benshi bagwirirana ku Mwami Yesu." 
Acts11:25 Avayo, aja i Taruso kurondera Sauli," 
Acts11:26 amubonye, amujana muri Antiyokiya. Bamaray’ umwaka wose, bakorana n’ishengero, bigisha abantu benshi, kandi muri Antiyokiya ni ho abigishwa bātanguriye kwitwa Abakristo." 
Acts11:27 Mur’ iyo misi, abavugishwa n’Imana bava i Yerusalemu baja muri Antiyokiya." 
Acts11:28 Hava hasi umwe muri bo yitwa Agabo, abamenyesha avugishijwe na Mpwemu yukw ikigoyi cinshi kizotera mw isi yose. Ico yavuga ni kimwe cātera ku ngoma ya Kilawudiyo." 
Acts11:29 Maz’ abigishwa, umuntu wese nk’ukw atunze, bashinga kurungikira bene Data baba i Yudaya ivyo kubatabara." 
Acts11:30 Babigenza bartyo, babirungikira abakuru, bijanye Barunaba na Sauli." 
Acts12:1 Maze nko mur’ ico gihe umwami Herode ata mu maboko bamwe bo mw ishengero ngw abagirire nabi. 
Acts12:2 Yicisha inkota Yakobo mwene nyina wa Yohana. 
Acts12:3 Maz’ abonye ko bihimbaye Abayuda, ariyongeza, afata na Petero. Hāri mu misi y’imitsima itambiwe." 
Acts12:4 Amaze kumufata, amushira mw ibohero, amuha abasoda cumi na batandatu kumurinda ari bane‐bane, agira ngw az’ amushikirize abantu, Pasika ishize." 
Acts12:5 Nuko Petero arindirwa mw ibohero: arikw ab’ishengero baramusengera, batakambira Imana bakobeje." 
Acts12:6 Ku musi Herode bgāca amubashikiriza, mur’ iryo joro Petero yar’ asinziriye hagati y’abasoda babiri, aboheshejwe iminyororo ibiri, abateramyi bāri ku rugi barinda inzu y’ibohero." 
Acts12:7 Maz’ umumarayika w’Umwami Imana amuhagarara i ruhande, umuco ubonesha mu nzu. Akoma Petero mu mbavu, aramukangura, ati Vyuka n’ingoga. Iminyororo imuva ku maboko, irakoroka." 
Acts12:8 Umumarayika aramubarira, ati Kenyera, wambare inkweto zawe. Abigenza artyo. Kand’ aramubarira, at’ Ikubirek’ umutamana wawe, unkurikire." 
Acts12:9 Arasohoka, aramukurikira, yamara ntiyamenya ivyo umumarayika akoze kw ar’ ivy’ ukuri, arikw agira ngw abonye ivyo yeretswe nko mu nzozi." 
Acts12:10 Baciye ku bateramyi ba mbere no ku ba kabiri, bashika kw irembo ryugarije urugi rw’icuma, rija mu gisagara. Rurabīyugururira ubgarwo, barenga irembo baca mu nzira imwe, uwo mwanya umumarayika aca amusiga hano." 
Acts12:11 Akenge kagarutse, Petero aribgira, ati Noneho mmenye vy’ukuri yuk’ Umwami yatumye umumarayika wiwe, akankiza ukuboko kwa Herode, bo n’ivyo ubgoko bg’Abayuda bgāri bushamāje vyose." 
Acts12:12 Amaze kuvyiyumvira, aja kwa Mariya, nyina wa Yohana ari we Mariko, aho bāri bakoraniye benshi, bariko barasenga." 
Acts12:13 Petero akomanga ku rugi rw’irembo, umukobga w’umugurano yitwa Rode aja kwumvīra." 
Acts12:14 Amenye ijwi rya Petero akanyamuneza kamubuza kwugurura, arirukanga arinjira, ababarira yuko Petero ahagaze kw irembo." 
Acts12:15 Baramwishura, bat’ Urasara. Na we avuga ashimitse kw ar’ivy’ ukuri. Bati N’umumarayika wiwe." 
Acts12:16 Ariko Petero ashishikara gukomanga: buguruye baramubona, barūmirwa." 
Acts12:17 Arabamama, abīgānira uk’Umwami Imana yamukūye mw ibohero, arababgira, at’ Ivyo mubibarire Yakobo na bene Data bandi. Arahava, aja ahandi." 
Acts12:18 Ijoro rikeye, havyuka imivurungano itari mike mu basoda, kuko bazazaniwe ukuntu Petero yabaye." 
Acts12:19 Herode amurondeye amubuze, acunaguza abateramyi, avuga ko babajana kubica: maz’ ava i Yudaya amanuka i Kayisariya, agumayo." 
Acts12:20 Maz’ ashāmira abo muri Tiro n’i Sidoni, na bo bahūza inama, baja kuri we, bahongera Bulasito, umukuru w’abagaranzurira umwami, basaba impore, kukw igihugu cabo casuma mu gihugu c’uwo mwami." 
Acts12:21 Nuko ku musi washinzwe, Herode yambara impuzu z’ubgami, avyagira ku ntebe y’icubahiro, abacūrira amajambo." 
Acts12:22 Abantu barasemerera, bati N’ijwi ry’imana, s’iry’ umuntu." 
Acts12:23 Uwo mwanya umumarayika w’Umwami Imana aramukubita, kukw adahaye Imana Rurema icubahiro, aturika inyo, aracīkāna." 
Acts12:24 Arikw ijambo ry’Imana riragwira, riramamara." 
Acts12:25 Kandi Barunaba na Sauli bava i Yerusalemu, basubira inyuma, bashikirije ivyāgabuwe, bajana Yohana, ari we Mariko." 
Acts13:1 Kandi muri Antiyokiya, mw ishengero ryaho, hār’ abavugishwa n’Imana n’abigisha; umwe ni Barunaba na Simeyoni ari we Nigeru, na Lukiyosi Umunyakurene, na Manayeni yarerewe hamwe n’umwami Herode, hāriho na Sauli." 
Acts13:2 Bariko barasenga Umwami Imana bisonzesheje, Mpwemu Yera aravuga, ati Ni mundobanurire Barunaba na Sauli bankorere igikorwa nabahamagariye." 
Acts13:3 Nuko bisonzesheje, basenze, babarambitsekw ibiganza, barabarungika." 
Acts13:4 Nuko bavuyeyo batumwe na Mpwemu Yera bamanuka i Seleyukiya. Bavudukayo bari mu bgato bafata i Kupuro. 
Acts13:5 Maze bashitse i Salamini, bavuga ijambo ry’Imana mu masinagogi y’Abayuda: kandi bāri bafise Yohana agenda arabakorera." 
Acts13:6 Bararamiriza baca mur’ ico kizinga cose, bashika i Pafo, basangay’ umugabo w’umunyamarēba, umuraguzi w’ibinyoma, yar’ Umuyuda, izina ryiwe ni Bari‐Yesu;" 
Acts13:7 yagendanira Serugiyo Paulo, icēgēra ca Kayisari, umuntu w’ubgenge. Uyo ahamagaza Barunaba na Sauli, ashaka kwumva ijambo ry’Imana." 
Acts13:8 Ariko Eluma, uwo munyamarēba (izina ryiwe ni ko risobanurwa), arabahāririza, ashaka guhuvya ico cēgēra ngo nticizere." 
Acts13:9 Ariko Sauli ari we Paulo, yuzuye Mpwemu Yera, amuhanga amaso," 
Acts13:10 ati Wewe wuzuye ubugunge bgose n’ububi bgose, wa mwana w’Umurwanizi we, wa mwansi w’ivyo kugororoka vyose, ntuzoreka kugoreka inzira z’Umwami Imana zigororotse?" 
Acts13:11 Nuko rāba, ukuboko kw’Umwami Imana kuraguhanamiye, ugira uhume, umare imisi utabona izuba. Ako kanya igipfungu n’umwiza bimwubikizako, agenda azimagirika arondera uwo kumufata ukuboko." 
Acts13:12 Ico cēgēra kibonye ibibaye kirizera, gitangajwe n’ivyo cigishijwe vy’Umwami Yesu." 
Acts13:13 Maze Paulo n’abāri kumwe na we bavuduka i Pafo bari mu bgato, bafata i Peruga h’i Pamfiliya: Yohana abasigayo, asubira i Yerusalemu." 
Acts13:14 Ariko bo bavuduka i Peruga, bararamiriza, bashika muri Antiyokiya h’i Pisidiya; ku musi w’isabato binjira mw isinagogi, baricara." 
Acts13:15 Isomwa ry’ivyagezwe n’ivy’ abāvugishwa n’Imana riheze, abakuru b’isinagogi batuma kuri bo, bati Bene Data, ni mwaba mufise ijambo ryo guhanūra abantu, ni murivuge." 
Acts13:16 Paulo ava hasi, arabamama, arababarira, ati Yemwe bagabo b’Abisirayeli, namwe abubaha Imana, ni mwumve." 
Acts13:17 Imana y’ubu bgoko bg’Abisirayeli yatoranije ba sogokuruza, kand’ ishira abantu hejuru hamwe bār’ abambukīra mu gihugu ca Egiputa, ikabakūzay’ ukuboko gukomeye." 
Acts13:18 Yihanganira ingeso zabo nk’imyaka mirongwine mu bugaragwa. 
Acts13:19 Imaze guhonnya amahanga ndwi mu gihugu c’i Kanani, ibēgurira ico gihugu cabo kuba ishamvu yabo. Maze nk’imyaka amajana ane na mirongwitanu ishize," 
Acts13:20 ibaha abacamanza, gushitsa ku wavugishwa n’Imana Samweli." 
Acts13:21 Hanyuma bayisaba umwami, Imana ibaha Sauli mwene Kishi, umugabo wo mu muryango wa Benyamini, amara ku ngoma imyaka mirongwine." 
Acts13:22 Imukūye, ibahagurukiriza Dawidi kuba umwami wabo, imushingira intahe, iti Mbonye Dawidi mwene Isayi umuntu ameze nk’uk’ umutima wanje ugomba, azokora ivyo ngomba vyose." 
Acts13:23 Mu ruvyaro rw’uwo, nk’ukw Imana yasezeranye, yazaniye Abisirayeli Umukiza, ni we Yesu." 
Acts13:24 Ataraza, Yohana yari yigishije ubgoko bgose bg’Abisirayeli ukubatizwa kwo kwihana." 
Acts13:25 Ariko Yohana arikw arasozera urugendo rwiwe, arababaza, ati Mbega mwiyumvira ko ndi nde? Jewe sindi we. Mugabo har’ ūzoza mu nyuma yanje, kandi jewe ntibimbereye no gupfundurura inkweto zo mu birenge vyiwe." 
Acts13:26 Bagabo bene Data, bana bo mu muryango wa Aburahamu, namwe abubaha Imana, ijambo ry’ako gakiza ni twebge ryatumweko." 
Acts13:27 Kukw ababa i Yerusalemu n’abakuru babo batāmumenye, cank’ amajambo y’abavugishwa n’Imana asomwa ukw isabato itashe, ni co catumye bashitsa ivyo bāvugishijwe, hamwe bāmutsindisha:" 
Acts13:28 kandi naho bābuze inyanduruko yo kumwicisha, basaba Pilato kw amwica." 
Acts13:29 Bamaze gushitsa ivyo yandikiwe vyose, bamumanura ku giti, bamushira mu mva." 
Acts13:30 Arikw Imana iramuzura mu bapfuye. 
Acts13:31 Imisi myinshi abonekera abāri baradūganye na we ava i Galilaya aja i Yerusalemu, abo ni bo bamushingira intahe ubu imbere y’abantu." 
Acts13:32 Natwe turababgira ubutumwa bgiza bg’ivyasezeraniwe ba sogokuruza," 
Acts13:33 yukw Imana yabishikije kuri twebge abana babo, hamwe yazura Yesu. Kandi ni ko vyanditswe muri Zaburi ya kabiri, ng’ Ur’ Ubura bganje, uyu musi ndakuvyaye." 
Acts13:34 Kandi kuko yamuzuye mu bapfuye atazosubira mw iborero, yavuze irtya, iti Nzobaha imigisha yera ya Dawidi itazovaho."
