Acts13:35 No muri Zaburi yindi yavuze, ngo Ntuzotanga Uwera wawe ngw az’ abore." 
Acts13:36 Yamara Dawidi mu gihe ciwe amaze gukora ivy’ Imana igomba, arasinzira, ahamvya ba sekuruza, arabora." 
Acts13:37 Arik’ uwo Imana yazuye nta ho yigeze abora. 
Acts13:38 Nuko bagabo bene Data, ni mumenye ko mur’ uwo ari ho mubgirirwa ivy’ uguharirwa ivyaha:" 
Acts13:39 kandi ni we atsindanishiriza ūmwizera wese kuri vyose, ivyo mutāshoboye gutsindanishirizwa n’ivyagezwe vya Mose." 
Acts13:40 Nuko mwiyubare, ivyavuzwe n’abavugishwa n’Imana vyoye kubashikako," 
Acts13:41 ngo Rāba mwa banyagakēngērwe, mutangare, muyongayonge, Kuko ngira nkore igikorwa mu gihe canyu, Igikorwa mutazoruha mwemera, nah’ umuntu yokibasobanurira." 
Acts13:42 Bariko barasohoka, barabinginga ngw ayo majambo az’ avugwe no kw isabato izoza." 
Acts13:43 Abāri mw isinagogi bamaze gusābagira, benshi mu Bayuda bo n’abātoye idini yabo bakubaha Imana, bakurikira Paulo na Barunaba; na bo bayāga na bo, barabahanūra ngo bashishikare kuguma mu buntu bg’Imana." 
Acts13:44 Kw isabato ikurikira iyo, hakorana nk’abo mu gisagara bose kwumva ijambo ry’Imana." 
Acts13:45 Arikw Abayuda babonye ishengero ryinshi, buzura ishari, bahakanya ivyo Paulo avuze, barabicokora." 
Acts13:46 Paulo na Barunaba bavuga bashize amanga, bati Vyari bibereye kw ijambo ry’Imana ribanza kubgirwa mwebge; none ko murishibuye, mukībūra ko mutabereye ubugingo budashira, ehe‐e duhindukiriye abanyamahanga." 
Acts13:47 Kuk’ Umwami Imana ari ko yatubariye, ati Ndagushizeho ng’ ube umuco w’amahanga, Kugira ngo n’abo ku mpera y’isi ubashikirize agakiza." 
Acts13:48 Abanyamahanga bavyumvise baranezerwa, bashimagiza ijambo ry’Imana; abāri baragerewe ubugingo budashira bose barizera." 
Acts13:49 Ijambo ry’Umwami Yesu rikwira mur’ ico gihugu cose. 
Acts13:50 Arikw Abayuda bosha abagore b’icubahiro bubaha Imana, n’abakuru bo mur’ ico gisagara, bavyurira akadenderezo Paulo na Barunaba, babirukana mu ntāra yabo." 
Acts13:51 Na bo babakunkumurira umukungugu wo mu birenge vyabo, baja muri Ikoniyo." 
Acts13:52 Abigishwa buzuzwa umunezero na Mpwemu Yera. 
Acts14:1 Maze bari muri Ikoniyo bompi binjira mw isinagogi y’Abayuda, bavuga amajambo atuma Abayuda n’Abagiriki benshi cane bizera." 
Acts14:2 Arikw Abayuda banse kwumvira ivyo, bavyura urwanko mu mitima y’abanyamahanga ngo bagirire inabi bene Data." 
Acts14:3 Bamara imisi myinshi bavuga batabobotereza kubg’ Umwami Yesu, ashingira intahe ijambo ry’ubuntu bgiwe, abaha gukora ibimenyetso n’ibitangaza n’amaboko yabo." 
Acts14:4 Arikw abantu bo mur’ ico gisagara bīrema ibice, bamwe baherēra ku Bayuda, abandi ku ntumwa." 
Acts14:5 Kand’ abanyamahanga, bo n’Abayuda n’abashingantahe babo baja kubatera ngo babagirire nabi babicishe amabuye;" 
Acts14:6 barabimenya, bahungira i Lusitira n’i Derube, ibisagara vy’i Lukawoniya, no mu gihugu gihereranye na ho:" 
Acts14:7 bagumayo bavuga ubutumwa bgiza. 
Acts14:8 I Lusitira hār’ umugabo yar’ aremaye ibirenge uhereye aho yakaviriye mu nda ya nyina, nta ho yari yarigeze gutambuka." 
Acts14:9 Uwo yumva Paulo avuga, na we amuhanze amaso abona kw afise ukwizera kwo gukizwa." 
Acts14:10 Avuga n’ijwi rirenga, ati Hagarara n’ibirenge vyawe, weme. Arabaduka, aratambuka." 
Acts14:11 Maz’ ishengero ribonye ico Paulo akoze, bavuga n’ijwi rirenga mu Kinyalukawoniya, bat’ Imana zitumanukiyemwo zīshushanije n’abantu." 
Acts14:12 Barunaba bamwita Zeyu, Paulo na we bamwita Herume, kukw ari we yar’ imvuzi." 
Acts14:13 Maz’ umuherezi wa Zeyu, ingoro y’igitabo cayo yar’ imbere y’igisagara, azana amapfizi n’imyīshwa, agira acumite ikimazi, we n’ishengero." 
Acts14:14 Arikw intumwa, Barunaba na Paulo, bavyumvise, bītantamurirakw impuzu zabo, bītera mu bantu, basemerera," 
Acts14:15 bati Yemwe bagabo, n’iki gitumye mugira murtyo? Natwe tur’ abantu buntu, tumeze nkamwe, kandi tubabgira ubutumwa bgiza, ngo mureke ivyo bitagira ikimazi, muhindukirire Imana nzima, yaremye ijuru n’isi n’ikiyaga n’ibirimwo vyose," 
Acts14:16 ni yo yaretse amahanga yose mu bihe vyahise ngo bagendere mu nzira zabo. 
Acts14:17 Ariko ntiyabirekeye ngaho, itagira ico kuyishingira intahe, kuko yama ibagirira neza, ibaha imvura iva mw ijuru, n’ibihe vy’ivyimburo vyiza, ibahāza ivyo kurya, yuzuza imitima yanyu umunezero." 
Acts14:18 Aho bāvuga ayo majambo, hāri hasigaye gatoya ntibabe bakibuza ishengero kubacumitira ikimazi." 
Acts14:19 Maze haza Abayuda bavuye muri Antiyokiya no muri Ikoniyo; bamaze kwosha ishengero, batera Paulo amabuye, bamukwegera inyuma y’igisagara, bagira ngo yāpfuye." 
Acts14:20 Arikw abigishwa bahagaze bamukikije, aravyuka, aja mu gisagara; bukeye bg’aho avanayo na Barunaba, aja i Derube." 
Acts14:21 Bamaze kuvuga ubutumwa bgiza mur’ ico gisagara no guhindura benshi abigishwa, basubira i Lusitira no muri Ikoniyo no muri Antiyokiya," 
Acts14:22 baremesha imitima y’abigishwa, babahanūra ngo bagume mu kwizera: kandi yuko dukwiye guca mu marushwa menshi mu kwinjira mu bgami bg’Imana." 
Acts14:23 Kandi bamaze kubatorera abakuru mu mashengero yose, no gusenga bisonzesha, babaragiza Umwami Yesu, uwo bizeye." 
Acts14:24 Baca i Pisidiya, bashika i Pamfiliya." 
Acts14:25 Bamaze kuvuga ijambo ry’Imana i Peruga baramanuka baja muri Ataliya; 
Acts14:26 bavudukayo bari mu bgato bafata muri Antiyokiya, aho bāri barazigamishirijwe ubuntu bg’Imana ubga mbere ku gikorwa baheraheje." 
Acts14:27 Bashitseyo bakoranya ishengero, babīgānira ivy’ Imana yakoranye na bo vyose, n’ingene yugururiye abanyamahanga urugi rwo kwizera." 
Acts14:28 Bamarana n’abigishwa igihe kitari gito. 
Acts15:1 Maze haza abantu bamwe bavuye i Yudaya bigisha bene Data, bati Ni mutākebga, nk’uk’ umugenzo wa Mose uri, ntimuzoruha mukizwa." 
Acts15:2 Maze Paulo na Barunaba bamaze kugira ibihāri n’imibūrano itari mike n’abo bantu, abaho bahūza inama gutuma Paulo na Barunaba n’abandi bamwe bo muri bo, ngo baje i Yerusalemu ku ntumwa n’abakuru kubg’ iyo mibūrano." 
Acts15:3 Nukw abo, ishengero rimaze kubaherekeza, baca i Foyinike bo n’i Samariya, babamenyesha ingen’ abanyamahanga bāhindukiriye Imana, batera bene Data bose akanyamuneza kenshi." 
Acts15:4 Bashitse i Yerusalemu, ishengero n’intumwa n’abakuru barabākīra, na bo babīgānira ivy’ Imana yakoranye na bo vyose." 
Acts15:5 Maze hava hasi bamwe bo mu muce w’Abafarisayo bizeye, baravuga, bat’ Abanyamahanga birakwiye ko bakebga, no kubabgiriza kwitondera ivyagezwe vya Mose." 
Acts15:6 Nukw intumwa n’abakuru bakoranira hamwe kuja inama y’iryo jambo. 
Acts15:7 Habaye imibūrano myinshi, Petero ava hasi, arababgira, ati Bagabo bene Data, murazi yuko kera Imana yantoranije muri mwebge kugira ngo mu kanwa kanje abe ari ho abanyamahanga bumva ijambo ry’ubutumwa bgiza, bizere." 
Acts15:8 Kand’ Imana izi imitima, yarabashingiye intahe, hamwe yabaha Mpwemu Yera, nk’uko yamuduhaye natwe;" 
Acts15:9 ntiyashirah’ itandukaniro hagati yacu na bo, yogesheje imitima yabo ukwizera." 
Acts15:10 None rero n’iki gitumye mugerageza Imana, mwikoreza abigishwa imitwaro ba sogokuruza batāshoboye kwikorera canke twebge?" 
Acts15:11 Ariko twizeye yuko tuzokizwa n’ubuntu bg’Umwami Yesu nka bo. 
Acts15:12 Maz’ ishengero ryose riracereza, bumviriza Barunaba na Paulo babīgānira ibimenyetso n’ibitangaza vyose Imana yabahaye gukora mu banyamahanga." 
Acts15:13 Barangije kuvuga, Yakobo aravuga, ati Bagabo bene Data, ni munyumvirize." 
Acts15:14 Simoni yabīgāniye ingen’ Imana yatanguye kugendera abanyamahanga ngw ibarobanuremw’ ubgoko bg’izina ryayo. 
Acts15:15 Amajambo y’abavugishwa na yo ahūye n’ivyo, nk’uko handitswe," 
Acts15:16 ngo Hanyuma y’ivyo nzogaruka, Nongere nubake urusago rwa Dawidi rwatemvye, Nongere nsanasane ahāshize harwo, ndaruhagarike," 
Acts15:17 Kugira ngw amasigarira y’abantu baronderane Uhoraho N’amahanga yose yitirirwa izina ryanje," 
Acts15:18 Ni k’Uhoraho agize, akora ivyo vyose, yabimenye uhereye ku kuremwa kw’isi." 
Acts15:19 Nuko rer’ inama yanje n’uko tureka kugora abo mu banyamahanga bahindukirira Imana," 
Acts15:20 ariko tubandikire ngo bareke ibihumanya vy’ibigirwamana, no gusambana, no kurya ibinizwe, bo n’amaraso." 
Acts15:21 Kuk’ uhereye kera hose Mose afise mu bisagara vyose abigisha ivyiwe, bisomwa mu masinagogi ukw isabato itashe." 
Acts15:22 Maz’ intumwa n’abakuru, bo n’ishengero ryose, bashima gutoranya abagabo muri bo, ni Yuda ari we Barusaba, na Sila, abantu bakuru muri bene Data, no kubatumana muri Antiyokiya na Paulo na Barunaba:" 
Acts15:23 bandika icete, barakibarungikana, canditswe girtya, ngw Intumwa na bene Data bakuru turabatasha mwebge bene Data bo mu banyamahanga bari muri Antiyokiya n’i Siriya n’i Kilikiya." 
Acts15:24 Kuko twumvise yuko bamwe bāvuye muri twebge bābahagarikishije imitima amajambo, bakayisangangura, kandi tutābibageze;" 
Acts15:25 duhūje inama dushimye gutoranya abo bantu no kubatumana kuri mwebge n’abo dukunda Barunaba na Paulo," 
Acts15:26 abantu bāhevye amagara yabo kubg’ izina ry’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo. 
Acts15:27 Nukw abo dutumye ni Yuda na Sila, na bo ubgabo bazobabarira mu rurimi bimwe n’ibi." 
Acts15:28 Kuko Mpwemu Yera bimubereye vyiza, natwe n’uko, kutabīkoreza uwundi mutwaro urenze ibi bikwiye:" 
Acts15:29 mureke kurya ivyaterekerejwe ibigirwamana, n’amaraso, n’ibinizwe, mureke no gusambana; ivyo ni mwavyirinda, muzomera neza. Nuko muganūke." 
Acts15:30 Nukw abo basezewe bamanuka muri Antiyokiya; bamaze gukoraniriza hamwe ishengero, babashikiriza kino cete." 
Acts15:31 Bamaze kugisoma banezererwa iyo mpanūro. 
Acts15:32 Na Yuda na Sila, kuko na bo bār’ abavugishwa n’Imana, bahanūra bene Data mu majambo menshi, barabaremesha." 
Acts15:33 Bahamaze imisi, bene Data babasezera amahoro, ngo basubire ku bābatumye. [" 
Acts15:34 Mugabo Sila bimubera vyiza kugumayo.] 
Acts15:35 Kandi Paulo na Barunaba baguma muri Antiyokiya bigisha abantu, bababgira ijambo ry’Umwami Yesu, bafatanije n’abandi benshi." 
Acts15:36 Hashize imisi, Paulo abgira Barunaba, at’ Ingo dusubire ha handi tugendere bene Data mu gisagara cose aho twāvuze ijambo ry’Umwami Yesu, tumenye uko bameze." 
Acts15:37 Barunaba agomba ko bajana na Yohana na we, ari we Mariko." 
Acts15:38 Ariko Paulo ntivyamubera vyiza kujana uwabataye i Pamfiliya, ntajane na bo mur’ ico gikorwa." 
Acts15:39 Havyuka imitongano ibatera gutandukana, Barunaba ajana Mariko, avudukayo ari mu bgato, afata i Kupuro;" 
Acts15:40 Paulo na we atoranya Sila, avayo, bene Data bamaze kumuragiza ubuntu bg’Umwami Yesu." 
Acts15:41 Aca i Siriya n’i Kilikiya, aremesha amashengero." 
Acts16:1 Nukw ashika i Derube n’i Lusitira; hāriy’ umwigishwa yitwa Timoteyo, umwana w’Umuyudakazi umugore yizeye, ariko se yar’ Umugiriki:" 
Acts16:2 yashimwa na bene Data b’i Lusitira no muri Ikoniyo. 
Acts16:3 Uyo, Paulo agomba ko bajana, aramwābīra aramukeba, kubg’ Abayuda bo mur’ izo ntāra, kuko bose bāri bazi yuko se yar’ Umugiriki." 
Acts16:4 Bariko baraca mu bisagara, bagenda bababgira ivyo intumwa n’abakuru b’i Yerusalemu bāshinze, ngo bavyitondere." 
Acts16:5 Nukw amashengero akomerezwa mu kwizera, agenda yunguka ibitigiri imisi yose." 
Acts16:6 Baca mu gihugu c’i Furugiya n’i Galatiya, babuzwa na Mpwemu Yera kuvuga ijambo ry’Imana muri Asiya." 
Acts16:7 Bashitse ahabangikanye n’i Musiya, bagerageza kuja i Bituniya, Mpwemu wa Yesu ntiyabakundira:" 
Acts16:8 baca i Musiya baramanuka, bashika i Tirowa." 
Acts16:9 Maze Paulo mw ijoro arota inzozi, abona umugabo w’i Makedoniya ahagaze amwinginga, ati Jabuka uze i Makedoniya, udutabare." 
Acts16:10 Amaze kurota izo nzozi, duca turondera ingene tuja i Makedoniya, kuko tumenye yukw Imana iduhamagariye kubabgira ubutumwa bgiza." 
Acts16:11 Nuko tuvuduka i Tirowa mu bgato, turaramiriza tuja i Samotirake, bukeye bg’aho dushika i Neyapoli," 
Acts16:12 tuvuyeyo dushika i Filipi, igisagara c’i Makedoniya gikuru mur’ iyo ntāra, cubatswe n’Abaroma. Tumara imisi mur’ ico gisagara." 
Acts16:13 Ku musi w’isabato turenga irembo ry’igisagara, tuja ku ruzi, dukēka ko hobay’ ahahora hasengerwa. Turicara, tuyāga n’abagore bahakoraniye." 
Acts16:14 Umugore umwe yitwa Ludiya, umudandaza w’impuzu z’inyambarabami, wo mu gisagara citwa Tuwatira, yubaha Imana, aratwumviriza. Umwami Yesu amwugurura umutima, kugira ngw awushire ku vyo Paulo yavuga." 
Acts16:15 Amaze kubatizanywa n’abo mu nzu yiwe, aratwinginga, at’ Asangwa mubonye nd’uwizeye Umwami Yesu, ni muze i wanje, musembereho. Aratugōbēra." 
Acts16:16 Bukeye tugiye aho basengera, duhūra n’umwigeme arimwo dayimoni aragura, yar’ atungishije ba shebuja cane kubg’ iyo ndagu." 
Acts16:17 Uyo aradukurikira twebge na Paulo, asemerera, at’ Aba bantu n’abasavyi b’Imana isumba vyose, kandi bababarira inzira y’agakiza." 
Acts16:18 Amara imisi myinshi agenza artyo. Ariko Paulo adundumiwe, arahindukira, abarira dayimoni, ati Ndakubariye mw izina rya Yesu Kristo, muvemwo. Amuvamwo mur’ ako kanya." 
Acts16:19 Maze ba shebuja babonye yukw ico bazigakw inyungu kivuyeho, bafata Paulo na Sila, barabakwega babajana mu kaguriro imbere y’abashingantahe," 
Acts16:20 babashīra abacamanza, bat’ Aba bantu bahagarika imitima y’abo mu gisagara cacu, kand’ ar’ Abayuda;" 
Acts16:21 batuzanira imigenzo tuzira kwemera canke kuyikora, twebge tur’ Abaroma." 
Acts16:22 Ishengero ribahagurukira icarimwe, abacamanza babakākagurirakw impuzu, bagera ko babakubita." 
Acts16:23 Bamaze kubakubita inkoni nyinshi, babashira mw ibohero, babarira umurinzi kubarinda cane." 
Acts16:24 Na we abariwe artyo abashira mu nzu yo hagati, arobeza amaguru yabo mu mpatane z’ibiti." 
Acts16:25 Maze nko mu gicugu Paulo na Sila bariko barasenga baririmbira Imana, izindi mbohe zibumva," 
Acts16:26 isi ica inyiganyiga cane giturumbuka, bituma amatanguriro y’inzu y’ibohero anyiganyiga, ako kanya inzugi zose ziruguruka, iminyororo ya bose iradohoka." 
Acts16:27 Uwo murinzi yikanguye, abonye inzugi z’ibohero zuguruye, asokora inkota agira yiyahure, kuko yagira ngw imbohe zācitse." 
Acts16:28 Ariko Paulo asemerera n’ijwi rirenga, ati Ntiwigirire nabi, twese turi hano." 
Acts16:29 Ahamagaza imuri, yitera mu nzu, ari mu gatengo k’ubgoba, yikubita imbere ya Paulo na Sila," 
Acts16:30 arabasohokana, arababaza, ati Bagenzi, nkwiye gukora iki ngo nkire?" 
Acts16:31 Baramwishura, bat’ Izere Umwami Yesu, urakira, mwe n’abo mu nzu yawe." 
Acts16:32 Bamubarira ijambo ry’Umwami Yesu, n’abo mu nzu yiwe bose." 
Acts16:33 Mur’ ico gihe nyene c’ijoro arabajana, abuhagira inguma z’inkoni, aca arabatizwa, bo n’abiwe bose." 
Acts16:34 Arabadūgana, abajana i we, arabagaburira, anezeranwa cane n’abo mu nzu yiwe bose, kuko yizeye Imana." 
Acts16:35 Ijoro rikeye, abacamanza batuma abagendanyi, bati Rekura abo bantu." 
Acts16:36 Umurinzi w’imbohe abarira Paulo ayo majambo, at’ Abacamanza baratumye ngo murekurwe, nuko rero ni musohoke, mwīgīre amahoro." 
Acts16:37 Ariko Paulo arabishura, ati Ko bādukubitiye imbere y’ishengero, ata kidutsinze, kandi tur’ Abaroma, bakadushira mw ibohero: none bagomba kuduhinda mu mpisho? Ekaye, ni babe ari bo biyizira ubgabo badusohore." 
Acts16:38 Abo bagendanyi babarira abacamanza ayo majambo: na bo baratinya, bumvise kw ar’ Abaroma," 
Acts16:39 baraza, babakomera ibōbo, barabasohora, babinginga kuva mur’ ico gisagara." 
Acts16:40 Bavuye mw ibohero, baja kwa Ludiya, barinjira; bamaze kubona bene Data, barabahanūra, bavayo." 
Acts17:1 Bamaze guca muri Amfipoli no muri Apoloniya, bashika i Tesalonike, hārih’ isinagogi y’Abayuda." 
Acts17:2 Nuko Paulo, nk’uko yamenyereye, yinjira muri bo, amara amasabato atatu avugana na bo ivyo mu vyanditswe," 
Acts17:3 abibasobanurira, amenyekanisha yuko Kristo yar’ uwo kubabazwa, no kuzuka mu bāpfuye: kand’ ati Yesu, uwo mbabgira, ni we Kristo." 
Acts17:4 Bamwe muri bo birabemeza, bīfatanya na Paulo na Sila, n’ishengero ryinshi ryo mu Bagiriki bubaha Imana n’uko, no mu bagore b’icubahiro batari bake." 
Acts17:5 Arikw Abayuda bagize ishari, bajana abagabo b’imburakimazi bo mu bigaramangira, bakoranya abantu benshi, bavyura imigūmūko mu gisagara, batera inzu ya Yasona, bashaka gukūramwo Paulo na Sila, ngo babashikirize abantu." 
Acts17:6 Bababuze, bakwegera Yasona na bene Data bamwe imbere y’abaganza igisagara, barasemerera, bat’ Abāteye isi yose umugūmūko bashitse n’ino," 
Acts17:7 kandi Yasona yabashembereje: abo bose barenze ivyagezwe vya Kayisari, bavuga yuko harih’ uwundi mwami, ngo ni Yesu." 
Acts17:8 Bahagarika imitima y’ishengero rihakoraniye n’iy’ abaganza igisagara, bumvise ivyo," 
Acts17:9 nuko bāka Yasona n’abandi ingwati, barabarekura." 
Acts17:10 Nuko bene Data baca banyuruza Paulo na Sila mw ijoro baja i Beroya; maze bashitseyo binjira mw isinagogi y’Abayuda. 
Acts17:11 Arikw abo bo bār’ imico myiza kuruta ab’i Tesalonike, kuko bākiriye ijambo ry’Imana n’umutima ukunze, basesa mu vyanditswe uko bukeye, ngo bamenye yukw ivyo ar’ivy’ ukuri." 
Acts17:12 Nuko benshi muri bo barizera, n’abagore b’icubahiro b’Abagirikikazi n’abagabo batari bake." 
Acts17:13 Arikw Abayuda b’i Tesalonike bamenye yukw ijambo ry’Imana rivugwa na Paulo i Beroya kandi, bajayo na ho, bavyura imivurungano mu bantu, babahagarika imitima." 
Acts17:14 Uwo mwanya bene Data banyuruza Paulo ngw ahave, aje ku kiyaga; ariko Sila na Timoteyo basigarayo." 
Acts17:15 Kand’ abaherekeje Paulo bamugeza muri Atenayi; maze babariwe kubgira Sila na Timoteyo ngo bamusangeyo n’ingoga, basubira inyuma." 
Acts17:16 Ariko Paulo akibarindīriye muri Atenayi, umutima wiwe utunturira muri we abonye ingen’ ico gisagara cuzuye ibigirwamana." 
Acts17:17 Nukw ahārīrira n’Abayuda n’abubaha Imana mw isinagogi, no mu kaguriro imisi yose ahārīra n’abāmusangaho." 
Acts17:18 Maze bamwe mu banyabgenge bitwa Abepikureyo, n’abandi bitwa Abasitoyiko bahūra na we. Bamwe muri bo barabazanya, bati Mbeg’ uyu adedemba agomba kuvuga ibiki? Abandi bat’ Umenga n’ūzanye imana z’ivyaduka: kuko yavuga ubutumwa bgiza bga Yesu n’ubg’ ukuzuka." 
Acts17:19 Baramufata bamujana ahitwa Areyopago, baramubaza, bati Mbeg’ ubona twoshobora kumenya ukwo kwigisha gusha uvuga ukw ari kwo?" 
Acts17:20 Kuk’ utuzanye mu matwi ibintu vy’ivyaduka: none rero turagomba kumenya ivy’ ari vyo. 
Acts17:21 Kukw Abanyatenayi bose n’ab’ akavantara bāriho, batāgira ikindi bakora, atar’ ukwumva canke kudonda amakuru mashāsha." 
Acts17:22 Paulo ahagarara hagati muri Areyopago, aravuga, ati Bagabo bo muri Atenayi, mbonye muri vyose ko mukabije kwubaha imana zanyu." 
Acts17:23 Kukw aho nagendagenda nitegereza ivyo musenga, nasanze hari n’igicaniro canditsweko, ngw IC’ IMANA ITAZWI. Nukw iyo musenga mutayizi, ni yo mbabarira." 
Acts17:24 Imana Rurema, yaremye isi n’ibirimwo vyose, iyo, kukw ari yo Mwami w’ijuru n’isi, ntiba mu nsengero zubatswe n’amaboko," 
Acts17:25 kandi ntikorerwa n’amaboko y’abantu, nk’ūri n’ic’ akennye: kukw ari yo yahaye bose ubugingo, no guhumeka, n’ibindi vyose." 
Acts17:26 Kandi yaremye amahanga yose y’abantu, ibakūye mu muntu umwe, ngo basagaze mw isi yose, yashinze ibihe vy’imyaka ko bikūranwa uko yageze, icira abantu imbibe z’aho baba," 
Acts17:27 kugira ngo barondere Imana, ngo namba kumbure bakabakavye boyibona, nah’ itari kure y’umuntu n’umwe muri twebge." 
Acts17:28 Kuko muri yo ari ho tubeshejweho, tugenda, turi n’ubugingo; nk’uko na bamwe bo mu bigeneye indirimbo banyu bāvuze, bati Kuko natwe, tur’ uruvyaro rwayo." 
Acts17:29 Nuko rero, ko tur’ uruvyaro rw’Imana, ntidukwiye kwiyumvira yukw Imana isa n’izahabu, cank’ ifeza, cank’ amabuye, ivyābājwe n’ubuhinga n’ubgenge bg’abantu." 
Acts17:30 Nukw iyo misi y’ubutamenya, Imana yarayīrengagije, ariko noneho, igera kw abantu bose bari hose bihana," 
Acts17:31 kuko yashinze umusi wo gucirakw isi yose amateka y’ukuri, izoyacisha umuntu yatoranije, kandi yahaye bose ikimenyamenya c’ivyo, mu kumuzura imukūye mu bapfuye." 
Acts17:32 Maze bumvise ivy’ ukuzuka mu bapfuye, bamwe barishinyira, abandi bati Tuzoba turumva ukundi ivy’ utubarira kur’ ivyo." 
Acts17:33 Nuko Paulo ava muri bo. 
Acts17:34 Arikw abagabo bamwe bīfatanya na we barizera; muri bo umwe ni Diyonisiyo wo mu Bareyopago, kandi n’umugore yitwa Damari, n’abandi hamwe na bo." 
Acts18:1 Hanyuma y’ivyo Paulo ava muri Atenayi, aja i Korinto." 
Acts18:2 Abonye Umuyuda yitwa Akwila, amamo yiwe n’i Ponto, yar’ avuye muri Italiya mur’ iyo misi, bo n’umugore wiwe Purisikila, kuko Kilawudiyo yari yageze kw Abayuda bose bava i Roma, aja aho bari." 
Acts18:3 Kandi kuko bāri bahūje ubuhinga, abana na bo, barabungirana, kuk’ ubuhinga bgabo bgar’ ubgo kujisha amahema." 
Acts18:4 Ahārīrira n’abaho mw isinagogi amasabato yose, ngo yemeze Abayuda n’Abagiriki." 
Acts18:5 Maze Sila na Timoteyo bamanutse, bavuye i Makedoniya, Paulo agōbērwa n’ijambo ry’Imana, ashingira intahe Abayuda yuko Yesu ari we Kristo." 
Acts18:6 Na bo babihāririje barogose, akunkumura impuzu ziwe, arababarira, at’ Amaraso yanyu araba ari mwebge akora! Jeho ndacuna; guhēra ubu ndaja ku banyamahanga." 
Acts18:7 Avaho, yinjira mu nzu y’umuntu yitwa Tito Yusito, yubaha Imana, inzu yiwe yar’ ihereranye n’isinagogi." 
Acts18:8 Ariko Krisipo, umukuru w’isinagogi, yizerana Umwami Yesu n’abo mu nzu yiwe bose; n’Abakorinto benshi bumvise barizera, barabatizwa." 
Acts18:9 Maz’ Umwami Yesu abarira Paulo mw ijoro nko mu nzozi, ati Ntutinye, arik’ uvuge, woye gucereza," 
Acts18:10 kuko ndi kumwe nawe, kandi nta muntu azogutera ngw akugirire nabi, kuko mfise abantu benshi mur’ iki gisagara." 
Acts18:11 Amaray’ umwaka n’amezi atandatu, yigisha ijambo ry’Imana muri bo." 
Acts18:12 Maze Galiyo abaye icēgēra ca Kayisari muri Akaya, Abayuda bahūza inama bakūrira hasi Paulo, bamujana imbere y’intebe y’imanza," 
Acts18:13 bat’ Uyu muntu yemeza abantu gusenga Imana uburyo bunyuranye n’ivyagezwe. 
Acts18:14 Paulo arikw arahaga amatama, Galiyo abgira Abayuda, at’ Iyo haba hāri habonetse ibirego vy’icaha, cank’ igicumuro kigoye, yemwe Bayuda, hari kuboneka inyanduruko yuko mbihanganira kubumva:" 
Acts18:15 ariko kw ar’ibihāri vy’amajambo n’ivy’ amazina n’ivy’ ivyagezwe vyanyu ubganyu, ni mubimare ubganyu: jeho singomba guca urubanza rwa ben’ ivyo." 
Acts18:16 Abirukana imbere y’intebe y’imanza. 
Acts18:17 Abagiriki bose basūmira Sositene, umukuru w’isinagogi, bamukubitira imbere y’intebe y’imanza. Ariko Galiyo, ivyo vyose ntiyabibabara." 
Acts18:18 Paulo amaray’ iyindi misi myinshi hanyuma y’ivyo, maz’ asezera bene Data, avudukayo ari mu bgato ngw aje i Siriya, Purisikila na Akwila bajana na we, amaze kwikemuriza i Kenkireya: kuko yari mw isezerano." 
Acts18:19 Bashitse muri Efeso, abasiga ngaho; ariko we aragenda yinjira mw isinagogi, ahārīra n’Abayuda." 
Acts18:20 Bamwinginze ngw amarey’ iyindi misi ntiyabakundira. 
Acts18:21 Arikw asezerana na bo, ati Nzogaruka ikindi gihe, Imana ni yabigomba. Avuduka muri Efeso ari mu bgato." 
Acts18:22 Afashe i Kayisariya, aradūga aja i Yerusalemu, aramutsa ishengero, aramanuka, aja muri Antiyokiya." 
Acts18:23 Amazey’ imisi avayo, aca mu gihugu c’i Galatiya n’i Furugiya, aja mu bisagara uko bikurikirana, aremesha abigishwa bose." 
Acts18:24 Maz’ Umuyuda yitwa Apolo, amamo yiwe ni muri Alekisanderiya, yar’ umuntu w’ubgenge, ashika muri Efeso; yar’ umunyabushobozi mu vyanditswe." 
Acts18:25 Uwo yari yigishijwe inzira y’Umwami wacu, acānīrwa mu mutima n’umwete, yavuga yigisha ivya Yesu avyitondeye, yar’ azi umubatizo wa Yohana gusa." 
Acts18:26 Atangura kuvugira mw isinagogi ashize amanga. Maze Purisikila na Akwila bamwumvise, bamujana i wabo, barushiriza kumutahuza inzira y’Imana." 
Acts18:27 Agomvye kujabuka ngw aje muri Akaya, bene Data baramuremesha, bandikira abigishwa ngo bamwākīre. Na we ashitseyo, ubuntu bg’Imana bumutera gufasha cane abizeye:" 
Acts18:28 kuko yatururuza Abayuda abatsindira imbere y’abantu, yerekana mu vyanditswe yuko Yesu ari we Kristo." 
Acts19:1 Maze Apolo akir’ i Korinto, Paulo aca mu bihugu vyo haruguru, ashika muri Efeso, asangay’ abigishwa bamwe." 
Acts19:2 Arababaza, ati Mbega mwarahawe Mpwemu Yera igihe mwizera? Baramwishura, bati Ntitwaribganavyumve yuko Mpwemu Yera yatanzwe." 
Acts19:3 Arababaza, ati None mwabatijwe umubatizo ki? Bat’ Umubatizo wa Yohana." 
Acts19:4 Paulo ati Yohana yabatije umubatizo wo kwihana, abarira abantu ko bakwiye kwizera ūzoza hanyuma yiwe, ni Yesu." 
Acts19:5 Bavyumvise babatizwa mw izina ry’Umwami Yesu. 
Acts19:6 Paulo amaze kubarambikakw ibiganza, Mpwemu Yera abazako, bavuga izindi ndimi, bavugishwa n’Imana." 
Acts19:7 Abo bose bār’ abagabo nk’icumi na babiri. 
Acts19:8 Yinjira mw isinagogi, amara amezi atatu avuga ashize amanga: akīranira ivy’ ubgami bg’Imana abibemeza." 
Acts19:9 Ariko bamwe bikomantaje imitima, b’intumva, batukira Inzira ya Yesu imbere y’abantu, ava muri bo, arobanura abigishwa, uko bukeye ahārīrira mu nzu yo kwigishirizamwo ya Turano." 
Acts19:10 Bimara imyaka ibiri bimeze birtyo: nukw ababa muri Asiya bose bumva ijambo ry’Umwami wacu, Abayuda n’Abagiriki." 
Acts19:11 Kand’ Imana ikoresha amaboko ya Paulo ibitangaza vy’agaheta: 
Acts19:12 vyatuma bashīra abarwaye ibitambara n’ivyambazo bivuye ku mubiri wiwe, bagakira indwara zabo, impwemu zihumanye zikabavamwo." 
Acts19:13 Arikw inyererezi zimwe zo mu Bayuda zāsenda impwemu zihumanye zīgerera kuvugira izina ry’Umwami Yesu hejuru y’abatewe n’impwemu zihumanye, ziti Tubarahiye Yesu, uwo Paulo avuga." 
Acts19:14 Kandi hārih’ abahungu ndwi b’Umuyuda yitwa Sikewa, umwe mu baherezi bakuru, bāgenza bartyo." 
Acts19:15 Impwemu ihumanye irabishura, iti Yesu ndamuzi, na Paulo ndamuzi, ariko mweho muri ba nde?" 
Acts19:16 Umuntu arimw’ impwemu ihumanye abagurukirako bompi, arabanesha, arababirika, bahunga mur’ iyo nzu bambaye ubusa bakomeretse." 
Acts19:17 Ivyo bimenyekana mu Bayuda no mu Bagiriki bose baba muri Efeso, bose baterwa n’ubgoba, izina ry’Umwami Yesu rishirwa hejuru." 
Acts19:18 Kandi benshi mu bari barizeye baraza, bātura ivyo bākoze, barabiserura." 
Acts19:19 Benshi no mu bakora ivy’ ubupfumu bakoranya ibitabo vyabo vy’ubupfumu, babituririra mu maso ya bose: baharūra igiciro cavyo, basanga gishitse ku ntete z’ifeza ibihumbi mirongwitanu." 
Acts19:20 Uko ni kw ijambo ry’Umwami Yesu ryagwiriye cane, rigira ububasha." 
Acts19:21 Ivyo bishize Paulo agabira mu mutima wiwe guca i Makedoniya no muri Akaya aja i Yerusalemu, ati Ni namara gushikayo, nkwiye kuja kurāba n’i Roma na ho." 
Acts19:22 Atuma abāgenda bamukorera babiri, Timoteyo na Erasito, ngo baje i Makedoniya; ariko we, atebera muri Asiya imisi." 
Acts19:23 Nko mur’ ico gihe havyuka imivurungano itari mike kubg’ Inzira ya Yesu. 
Acts19:24 Hār’ umuntu yitwa Demetiriyo, umucuzi w’ifeza, yacura utunyabugoro twa Arutemi mw ifeza, akaronkesha abacuzi biwe inyungu nyinshi." 
Acts19:25 Nukw abakoraniriza hamwe n’abandi bākora ibikorwa ben’ ivyo, arababgira, ati Yemwe bagabo, murazi yuk’ ubutunzi bgacu buva mur’ iki gikorwa." 
Acts19:26 Murabona kandi murumva yukw atari muri Efeso honyene, ariko nko muri Asiya hose, umwe Paulo yoheje abantu benshi akabahindura, at’ Imana zākozwe n’intoke si zo mana." 
Acts19:27 S’ukw igikorwa cacu kiri mw irinde kigiye gukēngērwa gusa, ariko kandi n’ingoro y’igitabo c’imanakazi ihambaye Arutemi yotītūrwa, mbere yonakūrwakw icubahiro cayo gikomeye, ari yo abo muri Asiya bose n’isi yose basenga." 
Acts19:28 Bavyumvise barasugurirwa, barasemerera, bati Arutemi y’Abanyefeso irahambaye." 
Acts19:29 Maz’ igisagara cose kiravurungana, bashwabadukira icarimwe baja ku kibuga c’ibirori, bashika Gayo na Arisitariko Abanyamakedoniya, bāgendana na Paulo." 
Acts19:30 Maze Paulo agomvye kuja mur’ iryo gugu ry’abantu, abigishwa baramutesha." 
Acts19:31 Kandi bamwe mu bakuru bo muri Asiya, kuko bār’ abagenzi, bamutumako bamwinginga ngo yoye kwiroha mu kibuga c’ibirori." 
Acts19:32 Nuko barayogora, bamwe ukwabo abandi ukwabo, kukw iryo shengero ryavurunganye, abenshi batāri bazi icatumye bakorana." 
Acts19:33 Maze basokorora Alekisandero mu bantu, Abayuda bamwīgiza imbere. Maze Alekisandero arabamama, agira yiregure ku bantu." 
Acts19:34 Ariko bamumenye kw ar’ Umuyuda, bose basemererera icarimwe, bamara nk’amasaha abiri, bati Arutemi y’Abanyefeso irahambaye." 
Acts19:35 Umwanditsi (ari we mukuru w’igisagara) amaze guhoza ishengero, arababarira, ati Bagabo b’Abanyefeso, mbega harih’ umuntu atazi yukw igisagara c’Abanyefeso ari co kizigama ingoro y’igitabo c’imanakazi ihambaye Arutemi, ari co gishushanyo cākorotse kiva mw ijuru?" 
Acts19:36 None kw ata woshobora guhakana ivyo, mukwiye guhora, no kutagira ico mukora mutitonze." 
Acts19:37 Kuko muzanye aba bagabo, bativye ivyo mu ngoro z’imana kandi batārogose ku manakazi yacu." 
Acts19:38 Nuko Demetiriyo n’abacuzi bari kumwe na we, namba bafise uwo barega, imisi y’imanza iriho, kandi hariho n’ivyēgēra vya Kayisari, ni baregane." 
Acts19:39 Ariko ni mwaba mufise ibindi murondera, bizomarirwa mu rukinja rusanzweho." 
Acts19:40 Mbere turi mw irinde, kumbure ibibaye uyu musi vyotuma turegwa ubugarariji, kukw ata nyanduruko; kandi ntituzoshobora gusobanura icakoranije iri shengero rivurunganye." 
Acts19:41 Avuze ivyo, acūra ikoraniro." 
Acts20:1 Umugūmūko umaze gushira, Paulo atumakw abigishwa, arabahanūra, arabasezera, avayo ngw aje i Makedoniya." 
Acts20:2 Amaze guca mur’ ivyo bihugu, abahanūra mu majambo menshi, aja i Bugiriki." 
Acts20:3 Amaray’ amezi atatu; maz’ Abayuda bamugīriye inama yo kumutega agira atambukire mu bgato aja i Siriya, agabira gusubira inyuma aciye i Makedoniya." 
Acts20:4 Abājana na we bashikana no muri Asiya ni Sopatero mwene Puro w’i Beroya, n’ab’i Tesalonike ni Arisitariko na Sekondo, bo na Gayo w’i Derube, na Timoteyo, n’abo muri Asiya ni Tukiko na Tirofimo." 
Acts20:5 Abo bāri bitangiye imbere, baturorērera i Tirowa." 
Acts20:6 Natwe tuvuduka i Filipi turi mu bgato hanyuma y’imisi y’imitsima itambiwe, tubasanga i Tirowa ku musi ugira gatanu, tumaray’ imisi ndwi." 
Acts20:7 Ku wa mbere w’imisi ndwi, dukoranira kumanyagura imitsima, Paulo ayāga na bo, agira ngo buce agenda, atevya mu majambo ashitsa mu gicugu." 
Acts20:8 Maze hār’ amatara menshi mu cumba co mu nzu yo hejuru aho twari dukoraniye. 
Acts20:9 Kandi mw idirisha hari hicaye umusore yitwa Eyutuko, aremērwa n’itiro ryinshi; maze Paulo arushirije gutevya mu majambo, itiro riramuremēra, arakoroka avuye mu nzu yo hejuru ya gatatu, bamuyora ahwereye." 
Acts20:10 Paulo arururuka, amwubama hejuru, aramugumbira, ati Mureke gukoma induru, kuk’ ubugingo bgiwe bukiri muri we." 
Acts20:11 Asubira kwūrira, amanyagura umutsima, ararya, ayāga na bo igihe kirekire, ashitsa no mu macaca, maz’ aragenda." 
Acts20:12 Bazana uwo muhungu ari muzima, imitima yabo iraruhuka." 
Acts20:13 Ariko tweho tumwitangira imbere dutambukira mu bgato, turajabuka dufata muri Aso, aho twari tugabiye guhitana Paulo: kuko yari yabishinze artyo, kugira ngo we ace i musozi." 
Acts20:14 Adusanze muri Aso turamujana, turajabuka dufata i Mitulene." 
Acts20:15 Tuvuyeyo, bukeye bg’aho dushika imbere y’i Kiyo, ku musi ugira gatatu dufata i Samo, bukeye dufata i Mileto." 
Acts20:16 Kuko Paulo yari yagabiye guca i ruhande ya Efeso, kugira ngo ntatebe muri Asiya: kuko yihuta, ngo ni vyashoboka umusi wa Pentekote uz’ ushike ar’i Yerusalemu." 
Acts20:17 Ar’i Mileto atuma muri Efeso, atumakw abakuru b’ishengero." 
Acts20:18 Na bo bashitse ah’ ari, arababgira, at’ Ubganyu murazi ingene nabana namwe na ntaryo, uhereye umusi natanguriye gushika muri Asiya," 
Acts20:19 nkorera Umwami wacu n’umutima wicishije bugufi, kandi ndira, nterwa n’ibingerageza kubg’ inama z’Abayuda." 
Acts20:20 Kandi murazi yukw ata jambo ribereye nacishije i ruhande kubabgira canke kubigishiriza imbere y’abantu mu nzu no mu yindi. 
Acts20:21 Nashinze intahe mu Bayuda no mu Bagiriki y’ukwihana mu nyonga z’Imana, n’ukwizera Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo." 
Acts20:22 None rāba, ngiye i Yerusalemu mboshwe mu mutima, ntazi ibizombako nshitseyo;" 
Acts20:23 atar’ uko Mpwemu Yera anshingira intahe mu gisagara cose yukw ingoyi n’ivyago bintegeyeyo. 
Acts20:24 Ariko simbabaye ubugingo bganje nk’ah’ ar’ubg’ igiciro, kugira ngo ndangize urugendo rwanje, n’igikorwa nahawe n’Umwami Yesu, co gushingira intahe ubutumwa bgiza bg’ubuntu bg’Imana." 
Acts20:25 Kandi none rāba, ndazi yuko mutazosubira kubona mu maso hanje, abo naciyemwo mwese mbabgira ivy’ ubgami bg’Imana." 
Acts20:26 Ni co gituma mbashingira intahe uyu musi ncuna, yukw amaraso ya bose atazonkora," 
Acts20:27 kuko ntacishije i ruhande mbabgira ivy’ Imana yagabiye vyose. 
Acts20:28 Mwirinde ubganyu, muzigame n’ubusho bgose Mpwemu Yera yabashizemwo, ngo mube abo kubuzēzwa, kugira ngo muragire ishengero ry’Imana, iryo yaguze amaraso yayo." 
Acts20:29 Ndazi yuko ni namara kuhava, amabingira y’inkazi azobinjiramwo atababaye umukuku." 
Acts20:30 Kandi no muri mwebge ubganyu hazokwadukamw’ abantu bavuga ibigoramye kugira ngo bakwegere abigishwa inyuma yabo. 
Acts20:31 Nuko mwame mugavye, mwibuke yuko namaze imyaka itatu ntasība guhanūra umuntu wese ndira, ku murango no mw ijoro." 
Acts20:32 Kandi none mbaragije Imana n’ijambo ry’ubuntu bgayo, rishobora kububaka no kubahēra ibiragwa hamwe n’abejejwe bose." 
Acts20:33 Nta co nifuje, ar’ ifeza ar’ izahabu ar’ ivyambarwa vy’umuntu n’umwe." 
Acts20:34 Ubganyu murazi kw aya maboko yanje yankenurana ivyo nkennye n’abo turi kumwe. 
Acts20:35 Nabahaye akarorero muri vyose, yuko mu butame nk’ubgo, ari ko mukwiye gufasha abadakomeye, no kwibuka amajambo y’Umwami Yesu, ingen’ ubgiwe yavuze, ati Gutanga kuzana umugisha, kuruta guhabga." 
Acts20:36 Amaze kuvuga artyo, arapfukama, asengera hamwe na bo bose." 
Acts20:37 Bose bararira cane, bagwa Paulo mw izosi, baramugumbira:" 
Acts20:38 cane‐cane bababajwe n’ijambo yababgiye ngo ntibazosubira kumubona mu maso. Maze baramuherekeza, bamugeza ku bgato." 
Acts21:1 Tumaze gutandukana na bo, no gutambukira mu bgato, turaramiriza tuja i Kosi: bukeye bg’aho dufata i Rodo, tuvayo dufata i Patara." 
Acts21:2 Dusanze ubgato bugira bujabuke buja i Foyinike, tubutambukiramwo turagenda." 
Acts21:3 Tubonye i Kupuro tuhasiga i bumoso, tuja i Siriya, dufata muri Tiro: kukw ari ho bari bagabiye gukūrira ibintu mu bgato." 
Acts21:4 Tuhasanze abigishwa, dusībiray’ imisi ndwi: na bo bavugishijwe na Mpwemu babarira Paulo ngo yoye kuja i Yerusalemu." 
Acts21:5 Turangije iyo misi, tuvayo turagenda, bose baduherekezanya n’abagore n’abana, baturenza igisagara, dupfukama ku musenyi, turasenga." 
Acts21:6 Tumaze gusezerana dutambukira mu bgato, na bo basubira i wabo." 
Acts21:7 Natwe turangije urugendo rwo kuva muri Tiro, dufata i Putolemayi, turamutsa bene Data, tumarana na bo umusi umwe." 
Acts21:8 Bukeye bg’aho tuvayo, dushika i Kayisariya, twinjira mu nzu ya Filipo umuvuzi w’ubutumwa bgiza, n’umwe muri ba bandi ndwi, twaka indāro i we." 
Acts21:9 Uwo yar’ afise abakobga bane b’inkumi, bāvugishwa n’Imana." 
Acts21:10 Tugitevyey’ imisi myinshi, haza ūvugishwa n’Imana yitwa Agabo, yar’ amanutse avuye i Yudaya." 
Acts21:11 Aza aho turi, yābīra umukanda wa Paulo, awibohesha amaguru n’amaboko, aravuga, at’ Uku ni ko Mpwemu Yera agize: Nyen’ uyu mukanda, uku ni kw Abayuda bazomubohera i Yerusalemu, bazomushira mu maboko y’abanyamahanga." 
Acts21:12 Maze twumvise ivyo, twebge n’abantu baho turamwinginga ngo ntadūge i Yerusalemu." 
Acts21:13 Maze Paulo aratubaza, ati Mukora ibiki, kurira mundandura umutima? Siniteguye kuboherwa gusa i Yerusalemu, ariko no gupfirayo, kubg’ izina ry’Umwami Yesu." 
Acts21:14 Yanse kubicungūrako, turīhorera, tut’ Ivyo Umwami agomba ni bibeho!" 
Acts21:15 Hanyuma y’iyo misi dutekera ibintu vyacu, turadūga tuja i Yerusalemu." 
Acts21:16 Bamwe mu bigishwa bavuye i Kayisariya turajana, bazana Umunyakupuro yitwa Munasona, yar’ umwigishwa wa kera, tuba ari we dusemberako." 
Acts21:17 Dushitse i Yerusalemu bene Data batwākīrana umunezero. 
Acts21:18 Bukeye bg’aho Paulo yinjirana natwe kwa Yakobo, abakuru bose ni ho bāri bari." 
Acts21:19 Amaze kubaramutsa, ababarira ivy’ Imana yakoze mu banyamahanga imukoresheje, abidonze kimwe‐kimwe." 
Acts21:20 Na bo bavyumvise bahimbaza Imana; maze baramubgira, bat’ Urabona, mwene Data, ingen’ Abayuda bizeye ar’ ibihumbi vyinshi; kandi bose bagira ishaka ry’ivyagezwe." 
Acts21:21 Kandi bābariwe ivyawe, yuko wigisha Abayuda bose bari mu banyamahanga guheba ivya Mose, ukavuga ngo ntibakwiye gukeba abana babo canke kugendera mu migenzo yacu." 
Acts21:22 Non’ icobimara n’iki? Ntibazobura kwumva ko waje. 
Acts21:23 Nuko genza urtya, uko tukubgira. Dufise abagabo bane bari n’ico bāsezeranye." 
Acts21:24 Ubajane, wihumanurane na bo, ubatērēre, ngo babone kwimosha. Maze bose bazomenya yukw ivyo bāguteranije kuri bo ata kuri kurimwo, kandi ko nawe ubgawe ugenda witonze, witondera n’ivyagezwe." 
Acts21:25 Yamar’ ivy’ abizeye bo mu banyamahanga, twanditse dushinze ko birinda kurya ivyaterekerejwe ibigirwamana, bo n’amaraso, bo n’ibinizwe, birinde no gusambana." 
Acts21:26 Nuko Paulo ajana abo bagabo, bukeye bg’aho yihumanurana na bo, yinjirana na bo mu rusengero, avuga igihe imisi yo guhumanurwa izoshirira, agenza artyo gushitsa ah’ ikimazi c’umuntu wese muri bo catangiwe." 
Acts21:27 Nukw iyo misi ndwi igira ishire, Abayuda bāvuye muri Asiya bamubonye mu rusengero, bavurunga ishengero ryose, bamushōrerakw amaboko," 
Acts21:28 baratabaza, bati Bagabo b’Abisirayeli, mudutabare! Nguyu wa muntu yigisha hose abantu bose, akēngereza ubu bgoko n’ivyagezwe n’aha hantu: ikigeretseko yazanye n’Abagiriki mu rusengero, yahumanije aha hantu hēra." 
Acts21:29 Kuko bāri babonye Tirofimo w’Umunyefeso ari kumwe na we mu gisagara, bagira ngo Paulo yamujanye mu rusengero." 
Acts21:30 Igisagara cose kiravurungana, abantu barashwabaduka: basūmira Paulo, baramukwega bamukūra mu rusengero; ako kanya bugara inzugi." 
Acts21:31 Bakirondera ingene bamwica, inkuru ishika ku mukuru w’abagabisha b’abasoda yukw abo muri Yerusalemu bose bavurunganye." 
Acts21:32 Aca ajana abasoda n’abagabisha babo, abamanukira yiruka. Na bo babonye uwo mukuru w’abagabisha n’abasoda, basigaho gukubita Paulo." 
Acts21:33 Maz’ uwo mukuru w’abagabisha arabashikīra, aramufata, avuga ko bamufatisha iminyororo ibiri, abaza uw’ ari we, n’ic’ akoze ic’ ari co." 
Acts21:34 Abo mw ishengero barayogora, bamwe ukwabo abandi ukwabo: abujijwe n’uruyogoyogo kumenya ukuri, avuga ko bamujana mw iboma." 
Acts21:35 Ashitse ku ngazi y’amabuye abasoda baramuterura kubg’ ubusugurirwe bg’abantu," 
Acts21:36 kukw ishengero ry’abantu ryābaja inyuma, basemerera, bati Kūrah’ uyo." 
Acts21:37 Bagira bamushikane mw iboma, Paulo abaza uwo mukuru w’abagabisha, ati Wonkundira ijambo nkubarira? Na we aramubaza, at’ Urazi Ikigiriki?" 
Acts21:38 Si wewe wa Munyegiputa yateye umugararizo mu gihe gishize, akajana mu bugaragwa abantu b’abicanyi ibihumbi bine?" 
Acts21:39 Paulo aramwishura, ati Nd’ Umuyuda, umuntu w’i Taruso, igisagara c’i Kilikiya kitayoberanye: none ndakwinginze unkundire ico mbarira abantu." 
Acts21:40 Amukundiye, Paulo ahagarara ku ngazi y’amabuye, amama abantu: hamaze kuba agacerere rwose, ababarira mu Giheburayo," 
Acts22:1 Ati Yemwe bagabo bene Data kandi ba data, ni mwumvirize ivyo nireguza muri mwebge." 
Acts22:2 Bumvise ababariye mu Giheburayo, barushiriza gucereza. Aravuga," 
Acts22:3 ati Nd’ Umuyuda, navukiye i Taruso h’i Kilikiya, ariko nakuriye mur’ iki gisagara, nigishirizwa imbere y’ibirenge vya Gamaliyeli nk’uk’ uruhande rugoye rw’ivyagezwe vya ba sogokuruza ruri, ngira ishaka ry’Imana, nk’uko namwe mwese murifise uyu musi." 
Acts22:4 Kandi nahama abakurikira Inzira ya Yesu gushitsa bapfuye, nkababoha nkabashira mu mabohero abagabo n’abagore." 
Acts22:5 Kandi n’umuherezi mukuru na we aranshingira intahe y’ivyo, bo n’abanyekombe bose. Ni bo bāmpaye ivyete vyandikiwe bene Data b’i Damasiko, ikinjanyeyo ar’ ukuzana i Yerusalemu abaho na bo bari mu ngoyi, ngo bishure." 
Acts22:6 Nuko nkigenda, nshitse hafi y’i Damasiko, hāri nko mu mashōka, umuco uhambaye uza giturumbuka uvuye mw ijuru, unkayanganira irya n’ino." 
Acts22:7 Nikubita hasi numva ijwi rimbaza, riti Sauli, Sauli, umpīgira iki?" 
Acts22:8 Nanje ndabaza, nt’ Uri nde ga Mwami? Aranyishura, ati Ndi Yesu Umunyanazareti, uwo urik’ urahīga." 
Acts22:9 Kandi n’abo twāri kumwe umuco bārawubonye, ariko ntibumva ijwi ry’uwo tuvugana." 
Acts22:10 Ndamubaza, nti Ngire nte ga Mwami? Umwami aranyishura, ati Va hasi, ushike i Damasiko, ni ho uzobaririrwa ivyashinzwe k’uzokora." 
Acts22:11 Maz’ ubgiza bg’uwo muco bumpumishije, abo twāri kumwe bamfata ukuboko, nshika i Damasiko." 
Acts22:12 Umugabo yitwa Ananiya, yubaha Imana mu kwumvira ivyagezwe, yashimwa n’Abayuda bose babayo," 
Acts22:13 aza aho ndi, ampagarara hejuru, arambarira, ati Sauli, mwene Data, humūka. Ako kanya ndahumūka, ndamurāba." 
Acts22:14 Aravuga, at’ Imana ya ba sogokuruza yagutoranirije kumenya ivy’ igomba, no kubona wa Mugororotsi, no kwumva ijwi riva mu kanwa kiwe:" 
Acts22:15 kuk’ uzomubera icabona ku bantu bose ku vyo wabonye kandi wumvise. 
Acts22:16 Non’ ikigutevya n’iki? Va hasi, ubatizwe, wiyuhagire ivyaha vyawe, wambaze izina ryiwe." 
Acts22:17 Maze ngarutse i Yerusalemu, nariko ndasenga mu rusengero, mmera nk’ūrota," 
Acts22:18 ndamubona ambgira, ati Tebuka, uve i Yerusalemu vuba, kuko batazokwemera ivy’ unshingira intahe." 
Acts22:19 Nanje nti Mwami, na bo ubgabo barazi yuko nashira abakwizeye mw ibohero, nkabatonagurira mu masinagogi yose." 
Acts22:20 Kandi hamwe amaraso y’uwagushingira intahe Stefano yava, nanje ni ho nari mpagaze, mbishimye, nsanze impuzu z’abāmwica." 
Acts22:21 Aranyishura, ati Genda, kuko nzogutuma kure ku banyamahanga." 
Acts22:22 Baramwumviriza gushitsa kur’ iryo jambo: maze basemerera n’ijwi rirenga, bati Kūra ūmeze artyo mw isi, na kare ntiyar’ abereye kubaho." 
Acts22:23 Bakiyogora, bata impuzu zabo, basūrira umukungugu hejuru," 
Acts22:24 umukuru w’abagabisha b’abasoda avuga ko bamwinjiza mw iboma, ababarira kumucacisha ibimoko, kugira ngw amenye icatumye bamuvugiriza uruhōgo bartyo." 
Acts22:25 Bamaze kumubohesha imigozi, Paulo abaza umugabisha w’abasoda ijana ahagaze aho, ati Mbega biremerwa ko mukubita umuntu w’Umuroma, kand’ ata rubanza rwamutsinze?" 
Acts22:26 Uwo mugabisha avyumvise, aja ku mukuru w’abagabisha, arabimumenyesha, at’ Ugira ukore iki? Erega wa muntu n’Umuroma." 
Acts22:27 Uwo mukuru w’abagabisha araza, aramubaza, ati Mbarira: mbeg’ ur’ Umuroma? Na we at’ Ego me." 
Acts22:28 Uwo mukuru aramubarira, ati Jewe naguze ubgo buroma amahera menshi. Paulo at’ Ariko jeho nabuvukiyemwo." 
Acts22:29 Nukw abāri bagiye kumucaca baca baramureka; umukuru w’abagabisha na we aratinya, amenye kw ar’ Umuroma, kandi yamuboshe." 
Acts22:30 Ariko bukeye bg’aho, agomvye kumenya neza ic’ Abayuda bamurega ic’ ari co, aramubohora, agera kw abaherezi bakuru bakorana n’abanyekombe bose, amanukana Paulo, amuhagarika imbere yabo." 
Acts23:1 Paulo ahanga amaso abanyekombe, arababgira, ati Bagabo bene Data, nāmanye umutima utarimw’ ijwi rinyagiriza ikibi na kimwe imbere y’Imana gushitsa kur’ uyu musi." 
Acts23:2 Ananiya umuherezi mukuru abarira abamuhagaze i ruhande kumukubita ku munwa. 
Acts23:3 Maze Paulo aramubgira, at’ Imana izogukubita, wa rusika rukuyengejekw ingwa: mbega wewe ko wicaritswe no kuncira urubanza nk’ukw ivyagezwe biri, ugatako ukavuga ko bankubita ukanyuranya n’ivyagezwe?" 
Acts23:4 Abāri bahagazeho, bati Mbeg’ uratuka umuherezi mukuru w’Imana?" 
Acts23:5 Paulo, ati Sinari ndamuzi, bene Data, kw ar’ umuherezi mukuru; kuko handitswe ngo Ntukavuge nabi umukuru wo mu bgoko bganyu." 
Acts23:6 Maze Paulo amenye yuk’ umuce umwe ar’uw’ Abasadukayo, uwundi ar’uw’ Abafarisayo, ashira ijwi hejuru mu banyekombe, ati Bagabo bene Data, nd’ Umufarisayo, nd’ umwana w’Abafarisayo: ivy’ ivyizigiro vy’ibizoba n’ukuzuka kw’abapfuye ni vyo bimpagaritse mur’ izi manza." 
Acts23:7 Avuze artyo, havyuka ibihāri mu Bafarisayo n’Abasadukayo, abanyarukinja birema ibice." 
Acts23:8 Kukw Abasadukayo bāhakana yukw ata kuzuka kuriho, cank’ umumarayika n’impwemu; arikw Abafarisayo bāvyemera vyompi." 
Acts23:9 Habah’ urwamo rwinshi; bamwe mu banyabgenge b’ivyanditswe bo mu muce w’Abafarisayo bava hasi barahārīra, bati Nta kibi twabonye kur’ uyu muntu. Kumbure impwemu cank’ umumarayika yoba yavuganye na we." 
Acts23:10 Habah’ ibihāri vyinshi, umukuru w’abagabisha b’abasoda atinye ko bogabangana Paulo, abarira ingabo ngo zimanuke zimubashikure, zimujane mw iboma." 
Acts23:11 Ijoro ry’uwo musi, Umwami Yesu amuhagarara hejuru, ati Hūmura; nk’uko wanshingiye intahe i Yerusalemu, ni k’ukwiye kuzonshingira intahe i Roma." 
Acts23:12 Iryo joro rikeye, Abayuda barakorana, barahira bīsiba yuko batazorya ntibanywe batarica Paulo." 
Acts23:13 Abāhize bartyo bāsāga mirongwine. 
Acts23:14 Baja ku baherezi bakuru n’abakuru, bati Twarahiye twisivye bikomeye yukw ata co tuzotamira tutarica Paulo." 
Acts23:15 Nuko rero mwebge n’abanyekombe, ni mubgire umukuru w’abagabisha b’abasoda amubamanukanire, nk’abarondera kurushiriza gutahura ivyiwe neza. Natwe, atarabashikīra, twiteguye kumwica." 
Acts23:16 Mwishwa wa Paulo yumva uwo mutego, araza ashika mw iboma, abibarira Paulo." 
Acts23:17 Paulo ahamagara umwe mu bagabisha b’abasoda ijana, ati Jana uyu muhungu ku mukuru w’abagabisha b’abasoda; afise ijambo amubarira." 
Acts23:18 Na we aramujana amushīra uwo mukuru w’abagabisha, ati Ya mbohe Paulo yampamagaye aranyinginga, ngo nkuzanire uyu muhungu, afise ic’ akubarira." 
Acts23:19 Uwo mukuru amufata ukuboko, aramwikebanya aramubaza biherereye, at’ Ic’ ufise kumbarira n’iki?" 
Acts23:20 Aramwishura, at’ Abayuda bahūje inama yo kukwinginga ngw ejo uz’ umanukane Paulo mw ikombe, nk’ūgomba kubaza ivyiwe ng’ urushirize kubimenya neza." 
Acts23:21 None rero ntuje kubumvira, kukw abantu babo basāga mirongwine bamuryamiye, barahiye bīsivye ko batazorya ntibanywe bataramwica; kandi none bariteguye, barorereye ic’ uribubemerere." 
Acts23:22 Uwo mukuru arungika uwo muhungu, amaze kumwihanikiriza, ati Ntugire umuntu ubarira yuk’ ummenyesheje ivyo." 
Acts23:23 Ahamagara babiri bo mu bagabisha b’abasoda ijana, arababarira, ati Ni mwitegure abasoda amajana abiri bo kuja i Kayisariya, n’abagendera ku mafarasi mirongwirindwi, n’ab’ amacumu amajana abiri, bahenge mw ijoro isaha zitatu bagende." 
Acts23:24 Kandi bazane n’amafarasi kugira ngo bayashireko Paulo, bamushikane kwa Feliki icēgēra ca Kayisari akiri muzima." 
Acts23:25 Yandika icete nka ben’ iki: 
Acts23:26 ati Jewe Kilawudiyo Lusiya ndakuganūtsa wewe Feliki umwubahwa, icēgēra ca Kayisari." 
Acts23:27 Non’ uyo mugabo Abayuda bāri bamaze kumuta mu maboko bagira bamwice, nanje mmenye kw ar’ Umuroma nzanana n’ingabo ndamubakiza." 
Acts23:28 Kandi nshatse kumenya ico bamurega, ndamumanukana mw ikombe ryabo." 
Acts23:29 Mbona yuko bamurega amajambo y’ivyagezwe vyabo, ariko kw ata co yarezwe gikwiye kumwicisha canke kumubohesha." 
Acts23:30 Maze mbariwe yuko bahigiye uwo mugabo, nca ndamukurungikira, mbarira abarezi ko bamuregera imbere yawe. Ndakwikebanuye." 
Acts23:31 Nukw abasoda bābīra Paulo uko babariwe, bahenga mw ijoro bamujana muri Antipatiri." 
Acts23:32 Bumaze guca basigay’ abagendera ku mafarasi, ngw abe ari bo bajana na we, na bo basubira iyo bavuye kw iboma." 
Acts23:33 Abo bashitse i Kayisariya bashīra icēgēra ca Kayisari ca cete, bamushikiriza na Paulo." 
Acts23:34 Amaze kugisoma abaza intāra y’i wabo iy’ ari yo; amenye kw ar’uw’ i Kilikiya," 
Acts23:35 aravuga, ati Nzokwumva ivyawe abarezi bawe ni bamara kuza. Agera ko bamurindira mw iboma ya Herode." 
Acts24:1 Imisi itanu ishize, umuherezi mukuru Ananiya amanukana n’abakuru bamwe n’uwo kubavuganira yitwa Teritulo, barega Paulo ku cēgēra ca Kayisari." 
Acts24:2 Amaze guhamagazwa, Teritulo atangura kumurega, ati Ni kubgawe igituma tugazagaza mu mahoro menshi, n’ibindi vyaroranirijwe ubu bgoko kubg’ imigabo yawe:" 
Acts24:3 nuko turavyemera uburyo bgose ahantu hose, Feliki umwubahwa, tugukengurukiye cane." 
Acts24:4 Reka noye guhava nkurambira, ndakwinginze zirikana tuvuge amajambo make, kubg’ ubugwaneza bgawe." 
Acts24:5 Twabonye uyu muntu ar’ ikīza, atera umugararizo Abayuda bose bari mu bihugu vyose; ni we remezo ry’igice c’Abanazareti." 
Acts24:6 Kandi yagejeje no guhumanya urusengero, turamufata, [twāri tugomvye kumucira urubanza nk’ukw ivyagezwe vyacu bivuga." 
Acts24:7 Arik’ umukuru w’abagabisha b’abasoda Lusiya araza, amudushikura mu maboko," 
Acts24:8 abarira abarezi biwe kuza imbere yawe.] Nawe ni wamwibariza ubgawe urashobora kumenya ivyo tumureze vyose. 
Acts24:9 Abayuda na bo bafatanya na we mur’ ico kirego, bavuga kw ivyo ari ko biri." 
Acts24:10 Icēgēra ca Kayisari kimaze kumukebura ngw avuge, Paulo aramwishura, ati Ndazi k’umaze imyaka myinshi ur’ umucamanza w’ubu bgoko, ni co gitumye niregura ivyanje ndemye;" 
Acts24:11 kuk’ ushobora kumenya yukw imisi itarasāga icumi n’ibiri, uhereye aho nadūgiye i Yerusalemu gusengerayo." 
Acts24:12 Kandi ntibāsanze mpārīra n’umuntu n’umwe, canke nkoraniriza abantu kubakikiza, naho hoba mu rusengero canke mu masinagogi canke mu gisagara." 
Acts24:13 Kandi ku vyo bandeze ubu, ntibashobora kuronka ikinyagiriza imbere yawe." 
Acts24:14 Arikw iki ni co nkwemerera: n’uk’ ukw iyo Nzira iri, iyo abo bita igice, ari ko nkorera Imana ya ba sogokuruza bacu, nemera vyose bifatanije n’ivyagezwe kandi vyanditswe mu vy’abāvugishwa n’Imana;" 
Acts24:15 mfise ivyizigiro ku Mana bimwe n’ivyo aba na bo biteze, yuko hazoba ukuzuka kw’abagororotsi n’abagabitanya." 
Acts24:16 Ni co gituma na ntaryo nkobereza kugira umutima utanyagiriza ikibi ku Mana canke ku bantu. 
Acts24:17 Maz’ imyaka myinshi ishize, njanwayo no gushīra ubgoko bgacu ivy’ubuntu, no gutanga ibimazi." 
Acts24:18 Nkiri muri vyo bansanga mu rusengero nihumanuye, ata bantu nkoranije, ata n’uruhōgo ruriho. Ariko hār’ Abayuda bamwe bavuye muri Asiya," 
Acts24:19 ni bo bāri bakwiye kuza hano imbere yawe no kundega, iyaba bafise ico bangaya." 
Acts24:20 Canke na bano na bo ni bavuge icaha bambonyeko, aho nari mpagaze imbere y’abanyekombe," 
Acts24:21 shiti ryoba rya jambo rimwe navuze n’ijwi rirenga mpagaze muri bo, nt’ Ukuzuka kw’ abapfuye ni kwo kumpagaritse mur’ izi manza imbere yanyu uyu musi." 
Acts24:22 Ariko Feliki, kuko yar’ azi neza ivy’ Iyo Nzira ivy’ ari vyo, arabibīka, ati Lusiya umukuru w’abagabisha b’abasoda ni yaza, nzoca urubanza rw’amajambo yanyu." 
Acts24:23 Abarira umugabisha w’abasoda ijana kumurinda urw’ amaso, no kutabuza n’umwe mu bagenzi kumukorera." 
Acts24:24 Imisi mike ishize, Feliki azanana n’umugore wiwe Durusila w’Umuyudakazi, ahamagaza Paulo, yumviriza ivyo avuga ku vy’ukwizera Kristo Yesu." 
Acts24:25 Akirikw aravuga ivy’ ukugororoka n’ivy’ ukwirinda n’ivy’ amateka azocibga, Feliki aranduka umutima, aramubarira, at’ Ubu ni wīgīre, ni naronka uburyo bgiza nzogutumako." 
Acts24:26 Kandi yanaziga ko Paulo yomuhēra amahera; ico ni co camutera kwama amuhamagaza ngo bayāge. 
Acts24:27 Imyaka ibiri ishize, Porukiyo Fesito akūra Feliki. Maze Feliki agomvye kwikundisha Abayuda asiga Paulo akiboshwe." 
Acts25:1 Nuko Fesito ashikiriye intāra amara gatatu, araheza ava i Kayisariya adūga i Yerusalemu." 
Acts25:2 Abaherezi bakuru n’abahambaye bo mu Bayuda bamuregako Paulo, baramwinginga," 
Acts25:3 bamusaba kubagirira neza kur’ uyo, ngw amutumeko, aze i Yerusalemu, na bo baze bamuryamire bamutsinde mu nzira." 
Acts25:4 Ariko Fesito abishura yuko Paulo arindirwa i Kayisariya, kand’ ubgiwe kw agiye kujayo vuba." 
Acts25:5 Arababgira, ati Nukw abakuru bo muri mwebge ni bamanuke tujane, maze namba kur’ uyo mugabo har’ ikidakwiye, bakimurege." 
Acts25:6 Amaze muri bo imisi itarenga umunani cank’ icumi, aramanuka aja i Kayisariya; bukeye bg’aho yicara ku ntebe y’imanza avuga ko bazana Paulo." 
Acts25:7 Na we ashitse, Abayuda bamanutse bavuye i Yerusalemu baramukikiza, bamurega ibirego vyinshi bikomeye, ivyo badashobora kuronkera icagiriza." 
Acts25:8 Paulo ariregura, ati Nta caha nakoze, ari ku vyagezwe vy’Abayuda, canke ku rusengero, canke kuri Kayisari." 
Acts25:9 Fesito agomvye kwikundiriza Abayuda, abaza Paulo, ati Wokwemera kudūga i Yerusalemu gucirirway’ urubanza rw’ivyo mu maso yanje?" 
Acts25:10 Ariko Paulo aramwishura, ati Mpagaze aha imbere y’intebe y’imanza ishinzwe na Kayisari, ni ho nkwiye gucirwa urubanza. Nta kibi nagiriye Abayuda, kandi nawe urabizi neza." 
Acts25:11 Nuko namba naragabitanije, canke narakoze ibikwiye kunyicisha, sinanka gupfa: ariko namb’ ivyo aba bandega atari ko biri, nta muntu ashobora kubampa. Nzokwitwara kuri Kayisari." 
Acts25:12 Fesito amaze kuja inama n’abanyekombe, aramwishura, ati K’ugomvye kwitwara kuri Kayisari, imbere ya Kayisari ni ho uzoja." 
Acts25:13 Hashize imisi, umwami Agiripa na Berenike bashika i Kayisariya, baja kuramutsa Fesito." 
Acts25:14 Bamazey’ imisi myinshi, Fesito ashira imbere y’umwami ivya Paulo, ati Harih’ umuntu Feliki yasize ar’ imbohe." 
Acts25:15 Aho nar’i Yerusalemu abaherezi bakuru n’abakuru b’Abayuda bambariye ivyiwe, basaba ko ndamucira urubanza." 
Acts25:16 Ndabishura, nti S’umugenzo w’Abaroma gutanga umuntu uw’ ari we wese, umuregwa atabanje kuba kumwe n’abāmureze imbonankubone, no kubona uburyo bgo kwiregura ibirego bāmureze." 
Acts25:17 Nuko bakoraniye hano, sinarinze guteba, ariko bukeye bg’aho nicara ku ntebe y’imanza, mpamagaza uwo muntu." 
Acts25:18 Abarezi bavuye hasi, ntibāmurega ikirego na kimwe co mu bibi nakēka;" 
Acts25:19 ariko bāmurega ibihāri vyo mw idini yabo, n’ivy’ umuntu yitwa Yesu, yapfuye, uwo Paulo yavuga ashimitse kw ari muzima." 
Acts25:20 Nanje nzazaniwe ingene nobaza ivy’ ivyo, ndamubaza yukw agomba kuja i Yerusalemu, gucirirway’ urubanza rw’ivyo." 
Acts25:21 Ariko Paulo asavye kurindwa kugira ngw az’ acirwe urubanza na Augusito, mvuga kw arindwa gushitsa aho nzomurungikira Kayisari." 
Acts25:22 Agiripa yishura Fesito, ati Nanje nagomba kwumva uwo muntu. Na we at’ Ejo uzomwumva." 
Acts25:23 Bukeye bg’aho, Agiripa na Berenike bazanana icubahiro cinshi, binjirana mw ikombe n’abakuru b’abagabisha b’abasoda n’abahambaye bo mur’ ico gisagara; maze Fesito avuga ko bazana Paulo." 
Acts25:24 Nuko Fesito aravuga, ati Mwami Agiripa, namwe mwese abo turi kumwe hano, murabona uyu, uwo ishengero ry’Abayuda bose bānsabira i Yerusalemu bo n’ino, basemerera ngo ntagikwiye kubaho." 
Acts25:25 Ariko nsanga ntiyakoze igikwiye kumwicisha, kand’ ubgiwe agomvye kwitwara kuri Augusito, ngabira kumumurungikira." 
Acts25:26 None mbuze ijambo rimenyekanisha ivyiwe ryo kwandikira umwami wanje, ni co gitumye ndamuzana imbere yanyu, kandi cane‐cane imbere yawe, mwami Agiripa, kugira ngo ni twamara kumusiguza, mbone ico kwandika." 
Acts25:27 Kuko ngira ngo n’ic’ ubgenge buke kurungika imbohe, sinerekane ibirego vyayo." 
Acts26:1 Agiripa abarira Paulo, at’ Uremerewe kwiregura. Maze Paulo aramvura ukuboko, ariregura," 
Acts26:2 at’ Ivyo narezwe n’Abayuda vyose, mwami Agiripa, numva nnezerewe kw ari wewe ngira mvyiregureko uyu musi:" 
Acts26:3 kandi cane‐cane kuk’ uzi imigenzo n’impāri vyo mu Bayuda vyose: ni co gitumye nkwinginga ngo wihangane, unyumvirize." 
Acts26:4 Ingeso zanje, uhereye mu buto bganje, izo nārukanye mu bgoko bgacu n’i Yerusalemu, Abayuda bose barazizi." 
Acts26:5 Kandi bokwemera kubishingira intahe, baranzi, uhereye mbere na mbere, yuko nar’ Umufarisayo wo mu muce urusha iyindi yo mw idini yacu gushimikira imigenzo." 
Acts26:6 None mpagaze ngo ncirwe urubanza, kuko nizigira kuzobona ivy’ Imana yasezeraniye ba sogokuruza:" 
Acts26:7 ivyo imiryango yacu cumi n’ibiri yizigira kuzobona, ikorera Imana ishizek’ umwete mwinshi ku murango no mw ijoro. Kandi ni kubg’ ivyo vyizigiro ndezwe n’Abayuda, mugenzi!" 
Acts26:8 N’iki gituma mugira ngo n’ikintu kitoruha cemerwa kw Imana izura abapfuye? 
Acts26:9 Nanje ubganje nahora niyumvira muri jewe yuko nkwiye gukora vyinshi birwanya izina rya Yesu Umunyanazareti. 
Acts26:10 Kand’ ivyo narabikora nyene nd’i Yerusalemu, ngashira abera benshi mu mabohero, mpawe ubushobozi n’abaherezi bakuru, kand’ aho bābica, nanje nishira mu bemera ko bicwa." 
Acts26:11 No mu masinagogi yose nābahana kenshi, nkagerageza cane kubatukisha Yesu; kandi kuko nasazwa cane mbazira, narabatuza no gushitsa mu bisagara vy’abanyamahanga." 
Acts26:12 Ngikora ivyo, nja i Damasiko mpawe ubushobozi ndungitswe n’abaherezi bakuru." 
Acts26:13 Nuko mugenzi, nkigenda mu mashōka, mbona umuco uvuye mw ijuru, urusha ukw izuba rica ibibatsi, unkayanganira irya n’ino, twe n’abo tugendanye." 
Acts26:14 Twese twikubise hasi, numva ijwi rimbgira mu rurimi rw’Igiheburayo, riti Sauli, Sauli, umpīgira iki? Erega birakugoye gutera imigere ku mihunda." 
Acts26:15 Nanje ndabaza, nt’ Uri nde ga Mwami? Umwami aranyishura, ati Ndi Yesu, uwo urik’ urahīga." 
Acts26:16 Ariko va hasi, hagarara n’ibirenge vyawe: kukw igitumye nkwiyereka, ar’ukugira ngo ngutoranye nkugire umukozi wanje n’icabona co gushingira intahe ivy’ umbonanye, n’ivyo nzokwiyerekeramwo;" 
Acts26:17 ndagukize abo mur’ ubu bgoko bo n’abanyamahanga, ni bo ngutumyeko," 
Acts26:18 kubahumūra amaso kugira ngo bahindukire bave mu mwiza baje mu muco, bave no mu bubasha bga Satani baje ku Mana, bateko baharirwe ivyaha vyabo, baraganwe n’abejejwe n’ukunyizera." 
Acts26:19 Nuko, mwami Agiripa, sinanka kwumvira ivyo neretswe vyavuye mw ijuru." 
Acts26:20 Ariko nabanje kubgira ab’i Damasiko hanyuma ab’i Yerusalemu, n’abo mu gihugu cose c’i Yudaya, n’abanyamahanga na bo, yuko bakwiye kwihana, no guhindukirira Imana, bakore ibikorwa bikwiranye n’ukwihana." 
Acts26:21 Ni co catumye Abayuda bamfatira mu rusengero, bakageza kunyica." 
Acts26:22 None nabonye gutabarwa kwavuye ku Mana, ndacahagaze kugeza n’ubu, nshingira intahe aboroshe n’abahambaye, nta kindi mvuga atar’ ivy’ abāvugishwa n’Imana na Mose bāvuze ko bizoba," 
Acts26:23 yuko Kristo atazobura kubabazwa, kandi kw ari we azobanza kuzuka mu bapfuye, no kubgira ubgoko bgacu n’abanyamahanga ubutumwa bg’umuco." 
Acts26:24 Aciregura artyo, Fesito avuga n’ijwi rirenga, at’ Erega Paulo urasaze; ubgenge bgawe bginshi buragushajije." 
Acts26:25 Paulo aramwishura, ati Sinsaze, Fesito umwubahwa, ariko mvuga amajambo y’ukuri kand’ aroranye." 
Acts26:26 Umwami arazi ivyo neza, kandi ndamubarira nshize amanga; kuko nzi yukw ata na kimwe mur’ ivyo ahishijwe, kukw ivyo bitākorewe mu mfuruka." 
Acts26:27 Mwami Agiripa, uremeye ivy’ abāvugishwa n’Imana? Ndazi yuk’ uvyemeye." 
Acts26:28 Agiripa yishura Paulo, at’ Unkwegesha ivyo bike ng’ umpindure Umukristo?" 
Acts26:29 Paulo, ati Ndasaba Imana ari bike ari vyinshi, yukw atoba wewe wenyene, ariko n’abanyumva uyu musi mwese, ko vyobahindura nkanje, ukūye iyi minyororo." 
Acts26:30 Umwami ahagurukana n’icēgēra ca Kayisari na Berenike, n’abāri bicaranye na we;" 
Acts26:31 maze basohotse baravugana, bati Nta co uyu muntu yakoze gikwiye kumwicisha canke kumubohesha." 
Acts26:32 Agiripa abarira Fesito, at’ Uyu muntu aba arekuwe, iy’ ataba yar’ agomvye kuzokwitwara kuri Kayisari." 
Acts27:1 Bamaze gushinga ngo tujabuke tuje muri Italiya, Paulo n’izindi mbohe babaha umugabisha w’abasoda ijana yitwa Yuliyo, wo mu ngabo za Augusito." 
Acts27:2 Dutambukira mu bgato bgāvuye muri Aduramutiyo, bugira bugende bujabukiranya ahantu ho muri Asiya haherereye ku kiyaga, tuvudukayo turi kumwe na Arisitariko Umunyamakedoniya w’i Tesalonike." 
Acts27:3 Bukeye bg’aho dufata i Sidoni, Yuliyo agirira Paulo neza, amukundira kugendera abagenzi ngo bamuzimane." 
Acts27:4 Tuvudukayo, duca musi y’i Kupuro ngo tuhīkinge umuyaga, kuko war’ uduturutse imbere." 
Acts27:5 Tujabutse ikiyaga gihereranye n’i Kilikiya n’i Pamfiliya, dufata mu gisagara c’i Lukiya citwa Mura." 
Acts27:6 Uwo mugabisha w’abasoda ijana ahasanga ubgato buvuye muri Alekisanderiya buja muri Italiya, adushiramwo." 
Acts27:7 Tumaze imisi myinshi tugenda buhoro, dushika hafi y’i Kinido bitugoye cane, maz’ umuyaga utubujije duca musi y’i Kirete, imbere y’i Salumone, ngo tuhikinge umuyaga." 
Acts27:8 Tuhakikira bitugoye cane, dushika ahantu hitwa Vyambuvyiza, hafi y’igisagara citwa Laseya." 
Acts27:9 Hashize igihe kirekire, kandi kujabuka kubaye irinde, kukw igihe co kwisonzesha cari gishize, Paulo arabahanūra," 
Acts27:10 arababarira, ati Yemwe bagabo, mbonye yuk’ uru rugendo rugira rubemw’ ivyago n’ubuhombe bginshi, s’ivy’ ubgato n’ibirimwo gusa, ariko n’ivy’ amagara yacu na yo." 
Acts27:11 Ariko, umugabisha w’abasoda yumvira ūtumbereza ubgato na nyene bgo kurusha ivyo Paulo avuze." 
Acts27:12 Kandi kukw icambu atari ciza co kugumamwo kuhamara urushana, abenshi babagīra inama yo kuvayo, ngo bishobotse bashike i Foyinike, kuba ari ho bamara urushana, hār’ icambu c’i Kirete, cerekeye hagati y’i burārūko n’i burasirazuba, kandi hagati y’i burasirazuba n’i bumanuko." 
Acts27:13 Maz’ umuyaga uturutse i bumanuko uheheye buhoro, bibgiye ko baronse ico bāgomba, bazitura ubgato, bagenda bakikira hafi cane y’i Kirete." 
Acts27:14 Arikw igihe kitari kinini gishize, hatera umuyaga w’igihuhuta citwa Ewurakulo, uturutse kur’ ico kizinga." 
Acts27:15 Ubgato bumaze guhehwa, butagishobora gutumbera umuyaga, turabureka burakubebga." 
Acts27:16 Duca musi y’akazinga kitwa Kilawuda, tuhīkinga umuyaga, tubona uko tuboha akāto k’inyuma bitugoye cane;" 
Acts27:17 bamaze kugaterura, bābīra ibitsibo vy’integakiba, babicisha musi y’ubgato, barabuboha: kandi kuko batinya gusukwa ku musenyi ushaya witwa Suriti, bamanura igihuzu kigendesha ubgato, bagenda bartyo bakubebga." 
Acts27:18 Tuzungagizwa cane n’igihuhuta, bukeye bg’aho bata imitwaro mu kiyaga." 
Acts27:19 Ku musi ugira gatatu batesha amaboko yabo ibikoreshwa mu bgato. 
Acts27:20 Kand’ izuba n’inyenyeri bimaze imisi myinshi bitaboneka, turi mu gihuhuta cinshi girtyo, twihebura rwose kw ata wuzokira." 
Acts27:21 Bamaze igihe kirekire batakirya, Paulo ahagarara hagati muri bo, arababarira, ati Yemwe bagabo, mwāri mukwiye kunyumvira, ntimuve i Kirete, ngo mugire ibi vyago n’ubuhombe." 
Acts27:22 Kandi none ndabaremesha, ni muhūmure, kuko muri mwebge hatazopfa n’umwe, atar’ ubgato." 
Acts27:23 Kuko mur’ iri joro umumarayika w’Imana, nd’ uwayo, kandi ni yo nkorera, yahagaze i ruhande yanje," 
Acts27:24 arambgira, ati Nta co utinya, Paulo; ukwiye guhagarara imbere ya Kayisari, kand’ ehe Imana ikwemereye n’abo mugendanye bose." 
Acts27:25 Nuko ni muhūmure, yemwe bagabo, kuko nizeye Imana, yuko bizoba nk’uko nabariwe." 
Acts27:26 Ariko har’ ikizinga dukwiye gusukwako. 
Acts27:27 Ijoro ry’icumi na kane rishitse, dukūbēbga irya n’ino mu kiyaga ca Adiriya; maze nko mu gicugu abagendesha ubgato bakēka ko har’ igihugu bēgereye." 
Acts27:28 Bagera uburebure bg’amazi yo hasi, babona ingero mirongwibiri; hashize umwanya muto bongera kugera, babona ingero cumi na zitanu." 
Acts27:29 Kandi kuko batinya gusukwa ahantu h’amabuye baterera mu mazi ivyuma bine vyo kuzirika ubgato babicishije mu mutwe w’inyuma; bifuza ko buca. 
Acts27:30 Maz’ abagendesha ubgato barondeye ingene bobuhungamwo, bururukiriza ka kāto mu kiyaga, biyenzereza nk’abagomba kuzirikisha ivyuma umutwe w’imbere." 
Acts27:31 Paulo abarira wa mugabisha w’abasoda ijana, hamwe n’abasoda na bo, at’ Aba ni bataguma mu bgato ntimushobora gukira." 
Acts27:32 Maz’ abasoda baca imigozi ifashe akāto, ngo bakareke gakoroke." 
Acts27:33 Bugira buce Paulo arabinginga bose ngo barye, ati Non’ uyu musi n’ūgira icumi na kane mukirorereye mutarya, ata co mutamira." 
Acts27:34 Nuko ndabinginze, ni murābe utwo murya: kukw ari vyo vyobakiza, kandi ntihazohara agashatsi na kamwe ko ku mitwe yanyu." 
Acts27:35 Amaze kuvuga ivyo, yābīra umutsima, ashimira Imana imbere yabo bose, arawumanyagura, atangura kurya." 
Acts27:36 Bose basubiza umutima mu nda, na bo bararya." 
Acts27:37 Kandi twese abāri mu bgato twar’ abantu amajana abiri na mirongwirindwi na batandatu. 
Acts27:38 Bamaze guhāga, baremurura ubgato, bata ingano mu kiyaga." 
Acts27:39 Ijoro rikeye, ntibāmenya ico gihugu, ariko babonye ikigobe kirimw’ umusenyi, baja inama yuko boshobora gushikanah’ ubgato." 
Acts27:40 Bazitura imigozi ifashe ivyuma biziritse ubgato, babirekera i bgina; bariko barabikora, batenzūra imigozi yar’ igumije ingafe zihindukiza ubgato, badūza igihuzu c’imbere kibugendesha ngo gihēhwe n’umuyaga, batumbereza ku musenyi." 
Acts27:41 Ariko bashitse mw ihūriro ry’amazi, basekura ubgato ku gataka, maz’ umutwe wabgo w’imbere winjiramwo, urahamangira, uw’ inyuma na wo utangura kumenagurwa n’inkomezi z’imipfunda." 
Acts27:42 Inama y’abasoda kwar’ uko bokwica imbohe, kugira ngo ntihagire uwo muri zo yokwoga agacika." 
Acts27:43 Ariko wa mugabisha w’abasoda, agomvye gukiza Paulo, ababuza iyo nama yabo, avuga yukw abazi kwoga bokwisuka mu mazi, kugira ngo babanze gushika ku nkombe:" 
Acts27:44 abandi na bo, bamwe bagende ku mbaho, abandi ku bindi bivuye mu bgato. Nuko bagenza bartyo, bashika ku nkombe bose, barakira." 
Acts28:1 Tumaze gukira, tumenya ico kizinga yuko citwa Melita." 
Acts28:2 Abanyamahanga badebagura baratubukabuka bitangaje, baducanira umuriro, batwākīra twese, kubg’ imvura n’imbeho vyāriho." 
Acts28:3 Ariko Paulo amaze gusenya umuganda w’inkwi, arazikomānya, inzoka iva mu muriro, imukomora ku kuboko." 
Acts28:4 Abo badebaguzi babonye ico gikōko cenena ku kuboko kwiwe, baravugana, bat’ Uyu muntu ntabuze kuba umwicanyi; kandi naho yakize ikiyaga, Īdaca urwa nkunzi ntimukundiye kw abaho." 
Acts28:5 Arikw akunkumurira ico gikōko mu muriro, ntiyagira ic’ aba." 
Acts28:6 Ba bandi barereka kw avyimba, canke kw agwa bukumbi: ariko bamara umwanya munini babireretse, babonye ata co abaye, barahindura, bati N’imana." 
Acts28:7 Hafi y’aho hantu hār’ amatongo y’umukuru w’ico kizinga, yitwa Pubiliyo, aratwākīra, atuzimāna neza imisi itatu." 
Acts28:8 Se wa Pubiliyo yar’ arwaye inyonko kand’ agacibgamw’ amaraso, maze Paulo yinjira i we, arasenga, amurambikakw ibiganza, aramukiza." 
Acts28:9 Ivyo bibaye, abandi bari n’indwara bo mur’ ico kizinga baraza, arazibakiza." 
Acts28:10 Baduha icubahiro mu buryo bginshi; maze mu gihe co kujabuka kwacu bashira mu bgato ivyo dukennye. 
Acts28:11 Tuhamaze amezi atatu, tuvudukayo mu bgato bgari bgavuye muri Alekisanderiya, bgari bumaze iyo misi y’urushana ku kizinga, ikimenyetso cabgo car’ Imana z’Amahasa." 
Acts28:12 Dufata i Surakusa, tuhamara imisi itatu." 
Acts28:13 Turahava, turazinguka, dufata i Regiyo. Hashize umusi umwe umuyaga uturutse i bumanuko urahehera, tugenda imisi ibiri, dufata i Puteyoli." 
Acts28:14 Tuhasanga bene Data bamwe, baratwinginga ngo tumarane na bo imisi ndwi: uko ni ko twashitse i Roma." 
Acts28:15 Bene Data b’i Roma bumvise inkuru yacu, baza kudusanganirira ahitwa Akaguriro ka Apiyo, n’ahitwa Amaduka Atatu: Paulo ababonye ashima Imana, umutima urarema." 
Acts28:16 Tumaze gushika Roma, umugabisha w’abasoda ijana ashikiriza imbohe umugabisha w’abasoda bahora bashibama kwa Kayisari: ariko bakundira Paulo kuba ukwiwe, ari kumwe n’umusoda amurinda." 
Acts28:17 Imisi itatu ishize ahamagara abakuru bo mu Bayuda abakoraniriza hamwe; bamaze gukorana, arababarira, ati Bagabo bene Data, naho ntāgize ikibi nakoze ku bgoko bgacu canke ku migenzo ya ba sogokuruza, bāmpaye Abaroma nd’imbohe, bamvanye i Yerusalemu." 
Acts28:18 Na bo bamaze kuncunaguza, bashaka kundekura, kukw ata nyanduruko yambonetseko yo kunyicisha." 
Acts28:19 Arikw Abayuda batagaye, numva nkwiye kwitwara kuri Kayisari; ariko s’uko mfise ico ndega ubgoko bgacu." 
Acts28:20 Ivyo ni vyo nabatumiyeko ngo tuvugane tubonāna: kukw ivyo Abisirayeli bizigira kuzobona ari vyo vyatumye mboheshwa uyu munyororo. 
Acts28:21 Na bo baramwishura, bati Nta vyete twāronse bivuye i Yudaya bivuga ivyawe, kandi bene Data baje nta watubariye inkuru mbi yawe, canke ngw akuvuge nabi." 
Acts28:22 Ariko turagomba kwumva ivyo wiyumvira, kukw ico gice tuzi yuko bakivuga nabi hose." 
Acts28:23 Basezerana na we umusi, baza iy’ ari ari benshi, mu nzu bamuhaye, arabibasobanurira, ashingira intahe ivy’ ubgami bg’Imana, abemeza ivya Yesu, abikuye mu vyagezwe vya Mose no mu vy’ abāvugishwa n’Imana, ahēra mu gitondo ashitsa ku mugoroba." 
Acts28:24 Maze bamwe bemera ivyo avuze, abandi ntibāvyemera." 
Acts28:25 Batemeranije ubgabo barataha, Paulo asubiye kuvuga ijambo rimwe, at’ Ivyo Mpwemu Yera yabaririye ba sogokuruza banyu mu kanwa k’uwavugishwa n’Imana Yesaya, yabivuze neza," 
Acts28:26 ati Ja kur’ ubgo bgoko, Uti Kwumva muzokwumva, ariko ntimuzoruha mubitahura; Kurāba muzorāba, ariko ntimuzoruha muvyihweza." 
Acts28:27 Kuk’ umutima w’ubu bgoko ucuramye, Amatwi yabo akaba ari bihurugutwi, Amaso yabo bakayahumiriza: Ngo ntibarābishe amaso, Ntibumvishe amatwi, Ntibatahurishe imitima, Ngo bahindukire, Mbakize." 
Acts28:28 Nuko mumenye yukw ako gakiza k’Imana kārungitswe ku banyamahanga: kand’ abo bazokwumva. [ 
Acts28:29 Amaze kuvuga artyo, Abayuda bagenda bahāririzanya bikomeye.]" 
Acts28:30 Amara mu nzu yiwe yatangiye ikibuguro imyaka ibiri yiramvuriye: yama yākīra abaje kumugendera bose," 
Acts28:31 akabahanūra mu vy’ubgami bg’Imana, akigisha ivy’ Umwami Yesu Kristo, ashize amanga rwose, ata wumubuza." 
Romans1:1 Paulo, umugurano wa Yesu Kristo, nahamagariwe kuba intumwa, narobanuriwe ubutumwa bgiza bg’Imana," 
Romans1:2 ubgo yasezeraniye kera mu kanwa k’abo yavugisha mu vyanditswe vyera," 
Romans1:3 buvuga ivy’ Umwana wayo, yavutse mu ruvyaro rwa Dawidi mu buryo bg’umubiri," 
Romans1:4 yerekanywe kw ar’ Umwana w’Imana mu buryo bga Mpwemu Yera, ukuzuka kwiwe kwavyerekanishije ubushobozi, ni we Yesu Kristo Umwami wacu." 
Romans1:5 Ni we yaduhesheje ubuntu no kuba intumwa kubg’ izina ryiwe, kugira ngo mu mahanga yose habemw’ abumvira Imana, babiheshwa no kwizera:" 
Romans1:6 kandi namwe muri muri bo, mwahamagariwe kuba aba Yesu Kristo:" 
Romans1:7 ndabandikiye mwese mur’ i Roma mukundwa n’Imana, mwahamagariwe kuba abera. Ubuntu bube muri mwebge n’amahoro, biva ku Mana, Data wa twese, no ku Mwami Yesu Kristo." 
Romans1:8 Irya mbere, mwese mbashimiye Imana yanje muri Yesu Kristo, kukw inkuru y’ukwizera kwanyu ikwiye mw isi yose." 
Romans1:9 Imana, nkorera mu mutima wanje mvuga ubutumwa bgiza bg’Umwana wayo, ni yo ntanzekw icabona yuko mbahoza mu kanwa ubudasība," 
Romans1:10 imisi yose uko nsenze nsaba ngo noneho bishobotse Imana yemere kungendesha amahoro no kunzana i wanyu. 
Romans1:11 Kuko nifuza kubabona, kugira ngo mbahe ingabire y’impwemu, ibaremeshe;" 
Romans1:12 ni kwo guhūmurizanya namwe, mpūmurizwe n’ukwizera kwanyu, namwe muhūmurizwe n’ukwanje." 
Romans1:13 Kandi bene Data, singomba ko mutamenya yuko kenshi nari mfise imigabo yo kuza i wanyu, ngo mbone imbuto muri mwebge namwe, nk’uko nazibonye mu yandi mahanga, ariko ngira ikimbuza kugeza n’ubu." 
Romans1:14 Abagiriki bo n’abanyamahanga badebagura, abanyabgenge bo n’ibipfu, ndi n’umwenda wabo;" 
Romans1:15 ni co gituma jeho kubganje niteguye kubabgira ubutumwa bgiza namwe mur’ i Roma. 
Romans1:16 Kuk’ ubutumwa bgiza butantera isoni, ar’ ubushobozi bg’Imana, buzanira uwizera wese agakiza, uhereye ku Muyuda ukageza ku Mugiriki." 
Romans1:17 Kuko muri bgo ari ho ukugororoka kuva ku Mana guhishurwa, guheshwa n’ukwizera kukagwiza ukwizera, nk’uko vyanditswe, ng’ Umugororotsi azobeshwaho n’ukwizera." 
Romans1:18 Uburake bg’Imana bgarahishuwe, buvuye mw ijuru, ubgo irakira ukutayubaha kw’abantu kwose n’ukugabitanya, banyikirisha ukuri ukugabitanya kwabo." 
Romans1:19 Kukw ivyo umuntu yomenya vy’Imana vyerekanwa muri bo, Imana ari yo yabiberetse." 
Romans1:20 Kukw ibitaboneka vyayo, ni vyo bushobozi bgayo budashira n’ubumana bgayo, bibonwa neza, uhereye ku kuremwa kw’isi, bimenyekanishwa n’ivyo yaremye, kugira ngo ntibagire ico bireguza," 
Romans1:21 kuko bāmenye Imana ntibayubahe nk’Imana, ntibayishime; ariko bācitse abiyumvira ivy’ ubusa, imitima yabo y’imburabgenge icura umwiza." 
Romans1:22 Biyise abanyabgenge bacika ibipfu," 
Romans1:23 icubahiro c’Imana idapfa baragikāba ngo basenge ibishushanyo bisa n’umuntu apfa, n’ivy’ ibiguruka n’ivy’ ibigenza amaguru ane n’ivy’ ibikwega inda hasi." 
Romans1:24 Ni co catumye Imana ibaheba ngo bakore ibiteye isoni, bumvire ivy’ imitima yabo yifuza, bonone imibiri yabo," 
Romans1:25 kuk’ ukuri kw’Imana bāgukāvye ibinyoma, bagasenga bagakorera icaremwe, bakakirutisha Iyakiremye, ni yo ikwiye gushimwa ibihe bidashira: Amen." 
Romans1:26 Ni co catumye Imana ibaheba ngo bifuze ivyonona: kukw abagore babo ic’ imibiri yabo yaremewe bāgihinduye ukundi, itāremewe." 
Romans1:27 Kandi n’abagabo n’uko, bāretse kugirira abagore ivy’ imibiri yabo yaremewe, bashuha babengukana, abagabo bagirira abandi bagabo ibiteye isoni, kandi mu mibiri yabo bahabga ingero zikwiranye n’ubuzimire bgabo." 
Romans1:28 Kandi nk’uko banse kumenya Imana mu mitima yabo, ni kw Imana yabahevye ngo bagire imitima y’akāhebge, bakore ibitabereye;" 
Romans1:29 buzuye ukugabitanya kwose, no kugira nabi, no kwifuza, n’urwanko rw’ubusa: buzuye n’igono, n’ubgicanyi, no gutongana, n’ubugunge, no kwitamba ku muvyimba; n’abaneguranira mu vyongorerano," 
Romans1:30 n’abavuga abandi nabi, n’abanka Imana, n’abatukana, n’abībona, n’abīrārīra, n’abīgenera ibibi, n’abatumvira abavyeyi," 
Romans1:31 n’ibipfu, n’abava mw isezerano, n’abadakunda n’ababo, n’imburakigongwe." 
Romans1:32 Abo, naho bāmenye urubanza Imana ica, yukw abakora ibisa birtyo bakwiye gupfa, ntibabikora gusa, ariko batako bagashima n’ababikora." 
Romans2:1 Ni co gituma utagira ico wireguza, wewe muntu wese uhinyura uwundi. K’uhinyura uwundi, uba witsindishije; kuko wewe umuhinyura ukora bimwe n’ivy’ akora." 
Romans2:2 Ariko turazi yuk’ urubanza rw’Imana ar’ urw’ ukuri, urwo icira abakora ibisa birtyo." 
Romans2:3 Wewe ga muntu, uhinyura abakora ibisa birtyo, nawe ubikora, mbega wiyumvira yuk’ uzokira urubanza Imana ica?" 
Romans2:4 Cank’ ukēngēra itunga ryo kugira neza kwayo n’iry’ imbabazi zayo n’iry’ ukwihangana kwayo? Ntuzi yuko kugira neza kw’Imana kugushikana ku kwihana? 
Romans2:5 Ariko kuk’ ufise umutima ukomantaye utihana, wirindiriza uburake buzoba ku musi wo kuraka, ah’ amateka abereye y’Imana azohishurirwa," 
Romans2:6 izokwishura umuntu wese ibikwiranye n’ivyo yakoze. 
Romans2:7 Abarondera ubgiza n’icubahiro no kudapfa, bahora bakora ivyiza bihanganye, izobishura ubugingo budashira." 
Romans2:8 Ariko ku bakēbana ntibumvire ivy’ ukuri, ariko bakumvira ukugabitanya, hazoba uburake no guhambarirwa" 
Romans2:9 n’amarushwa n’ivyago ku bugingo bg’umuntu wese akora ibibi, uhereye ku Muyuda, ukageza ku Mugiriki." 
Romans2:10 Arik’ ubgiza n’icubahiro n’amahoro bizoba ku muntu wese akora ivyiza, uhereye ku Muyuda, ukageza ku Mugiriki," 
Romans2:11 kukw Imana itarobanura abantu ku cubahiro. 
Romans2:12 Abākoze ivyaha bose, batazi ivyagezwe, bazohona ivyagezwe bitarinze kwiyumvirwa; kand’ abākoze ivyaha bose bazi ivyagezwe bazotsindishwa n’ivyagezwe:" 
Romans2:13 kukw abumvise ivyagezwe atari bo bagororoka imbere y’Imana, abāvyumviye ni bo bazotsindanishirizwa." 
Romans2:14 Abanyamahanga badafise ivyagezwe n’Imana iyo bakoze ibibgirizwa na vyo kubgabo, baba bihindukiye ivyagezwe naho batabifise:" 
Romans2:15 kuko berekana igikorwa kibgirijwe n’ivyagezwe canditswe mu mitima yabo, ijwi ryo mu mitima yabo ribgiririkanya na co, ar’ icabona cavyo, kand’ ivyo biyumvira bifatanya kubarega canke kubaregura." 
Romans2:16 Ni ko bizoba ku musi Imana izocira amabanga y’abantu amateka muri Yesu Kristo, nk’uk’ ubutumwa bgiza nahawe buvuga." 
Romans2:17 Ko witwa Umuyuda, ukishimira ivyagezwe, ukirata Imana," 
Romans2:18 ukamenya ivy’ igomba, ukarobanura ibidahwana, kuko wigishijwe ivy’ ivyagezwe," 
Romans2:19 ukishima yuk’ ushobora kujana impumyi, kandi k’ur’ umuco w’abari mu mwiza," 
Romans2:20 n’umuhanūzi w’abanyabgenge buke, n’umwigisha w’utwana, kuko mu vyagezwe ufise icerekana ubgenge n’ukuri:" 
Romans2:21 nuko wewe wigisha abandi, mbega ntiwiyigisha? Wewe wihaniza abība, weho ntiwiba?" 
Romans2:22 Wewe ubabuza gusambana, weho ntusambana? Wewe wanka ibishushanyo vy’ibigirwamana, weho ntiwiba ivyo mu nsengero zavyo?" 
Romans2:23 Wewe wirata ivyagezwe, mbega ntugayisha Imana kuk’ ubicumurako?" 
Romans2:24 Izina ry’Imana muritukisha mu mahanga, nk’uko vyanditswe." 
Romans2:25 Kuko gukebga kugira ico kukumarira, iyo witondeye ivyagezwe: arikw iy’ ucumuye ku vyagezwe, ugukebga kwawe kuba gucitse ukudakebga." 
Romans2:26 Non’ ūtākebge ni yitondera ibibgirijwe n’ivyagezwe, mbega kudakebga kwiwe ntikuzomuharūrwako nko gukebga?" 
Romans2:27 Kand’ ūtākebge umubiri ni yitondera ivyagezwe, azogutsindisha, wewe ucumura ku vyagezwe, ufise inyuguti zavyo no gukebga." 
Romans2:28 Kuk’ Umuyuda wo ku rukoba atari we Muyuda; kand’ ugukebga kwo ku rukoba kwo ku mubiri atari kwo gukebga. 
Romans2:29 Arik’ Umuyuda wo mu mutima ni we Muyuda, kandi gukebga n’ukw’ umutima, n’ukwo mu buryo bg’impwemu, atar’ ukwo mu buryo bg’inyuguti: ūmeze artyo ntashimwa n’abantu, arikw ashimwa n’Imana." 
Romans3:1 Non’ Umuyuda aruta abandi ate? Canke gukebga kumara iki? 
Romans3:2 Arabibarusha vyose. Ica mbere, n’ukw Abayuda bābikijwe ivyavuzwe n’Imana." 
Romans3:3 Tuvuge iki? Naho bamwe batizeye, mbega kutizera kwabo kuzohindura ubusa ivy’ Imana yizigiweko?" 
Romans3:4 Biragahera: arikw Imana iboneke kw ar’ inyakuri, n’iy’umuntu wese yoba ar’ umubeshi: nk’uko handitswe, ngo Kugira ngo mu majambo yawe uboneke k’ugororotse, Kand’ utsinde ni washika mu rukinja." 
Romans3:5 Ariko namb’ ukugabitanya kwacu kwāshimagije ukugororoka kw’Imana, tuvuge iki? Mbeg’ Imana iragabitanya, kukw iduhanisha uburake bgayo? Mbivuze nk’imvugo y’abantu." 
Romans3:6 Eka na mba! Iyo biba birtyo, Imana yociriye abari mw isi urubanza ite?" 
Romans3:7 Ariko namb’ ibinyoma vyanje vyatumye ukuri kw’Imana kurushiriza kwerekanwa, bikayitera icubahiro, n’iki gituma nanje ncirwa urubanza nk’umunyavyaha?" 
Romans3:8 Kandi n’iki kitubuza gukora ibibi kugira ngw ivyiza bibeho? (nk’uko batubeshera, kandi bamwe bavuga ko twigisha). Abakora bartyo bazocirwa urubanza bakwiranye." 
Romans3:9 Nuko tuvuge iki? Mbega turuta abandi? Oya, ntitubaruta na gatoya, kuko tumaze kwagiriza Abayuda n’Abagiriki bose ko baganzwa n’icaha:" 
Romans3:10 nk’uko handitswe, ngo Nta wugororoka, nta n’umwe," 
Romans3:11 Nta wutahura, Nta wurondera Imana." 
Romans3:12 Bārazimiye iyo bava bakagera, bose bācitse imburakimazi, Nta wukora ivyiza, eka nta n’umwe." 
Romans3:13 Imihogo yabo n’imva zirangāye, Bāhendahendanishije indimi zabo; Ubumara bg’inzoka buri mu binyigishi vyabo." 
Romans3:14 Akanwa kabo kuzuye ukuvuma no kujingitwa," 
Romans3:15 Ibirenge vyabo vyihutira kuvisha amaraso. 
Romans3:16 Guhonnya no kubabaza biri mu nzira zabo," 
Romans3:17 Inzira y’amahoro ntibāyimenye; 
Romans3:18 Nta gutinya Imana kuri mu maso yabo. 
Romans3:19 Ariko turazi yukw ivy’ ivyagezwe bivuga vyose bibibgira abaganzwa na vyo, kugira ngw akanwa kose kazibge, kand’ abari mw isi bose babe abo gutsindwa n’urubanza imbere y’Imana:" 
Romans3:20 kukw imbere yayo ata muntu azotsindanishirizwa n’ibikorwa bibgirijwe n’ivyagezwe, kukw ivyagezwe ari vyo bimenyekanisha icaha." 
Romans3:21 Ariko noneh’ ivyagezwe bitariho, ukugororoka kuva ku Mana kurahishuwe, gushingirwa intahe n’ivyagezwe n’ivy’ abāvugishwa n’Imana," 
Romans3:22 n’ukugororoka kuva ku Mana, kuzanwa no kwizera Yesu Kristo, kugira ngw abizeye bose baguhabge. Kukw ata tandukaniro;" 
Romans3:23 bose bākoze ivyaha, ntibashikīra ubgiza bg’Imana;" 
Romans3:24 batsindanishirizwa n’ubuntu bgayo, ibibahereye ubusa, kubgo gucungurwa kubonerwa muri Kristo Yesu:" 
Romans3:25 uwo Imana yashizeho kuba impongano y’uwizera, ayigirwa n’amaraso yiwe, kugira ngw Imana yerekane ukugororoka kwayo, kuko yirengagije ivyaha vyakozwe kera kubg’ imbabazi zayo;" 
Romans3:26 no kugira ngo yerekane ukugororoka kwayo mur’ iki gihe, ngw ibe Īgororoka n’Ītsindanishiriza uwizeye Yesu." 
Romans3:27 None rer’ ukwihaya kuri hehe? Kwarabujijwe. Kwabujijwe n’ivyagezwe ki? Mbega n’ivy’ ibikorwa? Haba na mba: kwabujijwe n’ivy’ ukwizera. 
Romans3:28 Ni co gituma twiyumvira yuk’ umuntu atsindanishirizwa n’ukwizera, ibikorwa bibgirijwe n’ivyagezwe bitarinze kwiyumvirwa." 
Romans3:29 Cank’ Imana n’iy’ Abayuda bonyene? Mbega s’iy’ abanyamahanga na bo? Ego me, n’iy’ abanyamahanga na bo:" 
Romans3:30 kw Imana ar’ imwe, izotsindanishiriza abākebge kubg’ ukwizera, kand’ izotsindanishiriza abatākebge babiheshwa n’ukwizera." 
Romans3:31 Mbega non’ ivyagezwe tubihinduza ubusa ukwizera? Eka na mba: ushime turabigumisha. 
Romans4:1 None rero, ico twovuga yuko Aburahamu sogokuruza ku mubiri yaronse n’igiki?" 
Romans4:2 Iyo Aburahamu atsindanishirizwa n’ibikorwa, aba afise ico yihaya. Arikw imbere y’Imana nta co afise." 
Romans4:3 Ivyanditswe bivuga iki? Bivuga ngo Aburahamu yizeye Imana, ibimuharūrako nk’ukugororoka." 
Romans4:4 Yamar’ ūkora, ingero yiwe ntiharūrwa nk’ubuntu, arikw iharūrwa nk’inyishu." 
Romans4:5 Arik’ ūdakora, akizera Ītsindanishiriza abatāyubashe, ukwizera kwiwe guharūrwa nk’ukugororoka:"
