Romans4:6 nk’uko Dawidi na we yavuze ubuhīrwe bg’umuntu uwo Imana iharūra nk’ūgororotse, atari kubg’ ibikorwa," 
Romans4:7 ati Hahirwa abāhariwe ibigabitanyo vyabo, Kand’ ivyaha vyabo bigatwikīrwa," 
Romans4:8 Hahirwa umuntu Uhoraho atazoharūrakw icaha. 
Romans4:9 Mbeg’ ubgo buhirwe buvugwa ku bākebge bonyene, canke ku batākebge na bo? Kuko tuvuga, tut’ Ukwizera kwaharūwe kuri Aburahamu nk’ukugororoka." 
Romans4:10 Kwāharūwe ryari? Yari yarakebge, canke ntiyaribgakebge? Ico gihe s’uko yar’ amaze gukebga, ariko ntiyaribgakebge." 
Romans4:11 Kand’ ahabga ikimenyetso, ni kwo gukebga, kuba ikimenyetso c’ukugororoka kwavuye kuri kwa kwizera yar’ afise atarakebga, kugira ngw abe sekuruza w’abizera bose batākebge, ngo bibaharūrweko nk’ukugororoka;" 
Romans4:12 kand’ abe na sekuruza w’abākebge, batākebge gusa, ariko bagera ikirenge mu c’ukwo kwizera kwa sogokuruza Aburahamu, ukwo yar’ afise, atarakebga." 
Romans4:13 Kukw atari kubg’ ivyagezwe Aburahamu yasezeraniwe cank’ uruvyaro rwiwe, yukw azoragwa isi yose, ariko ni kubg’ ukugororoka kuva ku kwizera." 
Romans4:14 Abizigira ivyagezwe iyo baba ari bo baragwa, ukwizera kuba kwarahindutse ubusa, ivyasezeranywe bikaba bititutse." 
Romans4:15 Kukw ivyagezwe bizana uburake, arikw ah’ ivyagezwe bitari, nta gicumuro kiba kiriho." 
Romans4:16 Ni co gituma ivyo vyavuye ku kwizera, ngo bibe ivy’ ubuntu; kugira ngo ku ruvyaro rwa Aburahamu rwose, ivyasezeranywe bize vyame bihamye, atar’ ab’ ivyagezwe gusa, ariko n’ab’ ukwizera kwa Aburahamu, ni we sogokuruza wa twese," 
Romans4:17 mu nyonga z’Iyo yizeye (nk’uko vyanditswe, ngo Nkugize sekuruza w’amahanga menshi) ni yo Mana, izura abāpfuye, kandi yita ibitariho nk’ibiriho." 
Romans4:18 Aburahamu yizera yizigiye ibitokwizigiwe, ngw abe sekuruza w’amahanga menshi, nk’uko vyavuzwe, ng’ Uruvyaro rwawe ni ko ruzongana." 
Romans4:19 Kandi ntiyagabanukak’ ukwizera, yitegereje umubiri wiwe umaze kuba akāheze, kuko yar’ amaze imyaka nk’ijana y’amavuka yiwe, na Sara yari yaraciye." 
Romans4:20 Ariko yiyumviriye ic’ Imana yamusezeraniye, ntiyakekeranishwa no kutizera, arikw aremeshwa cane no kwizera, ahesha Imana icubahiro," 
Romans4:21 amenya neza adakekeranya yukw ico yasezeranye ishobora no kugikora. 
Romans4:22 Ni co catumye bimuharūrwako nk’ukugororoka. 
Romans4:23 Ariko ntivyandikiwe we wenyene yuko vyamuharūweko nk’ukugororoka," 
Romans4:24 ariko no kubgacu, bizoduharūrwako nka kwo, kuko twizeye Iyazuye Yesu Umwami wacu imukūye mu bāpfuye," 
Romans4:25 yatangiwe ibicumuro vyacu, akazurwa kugira ngo dutsindanishirizwe." 
Romans5:1 None rero, ko twatsindanishirijwe no kwizera, dufise amahoro ku Mana kubg’ Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo," 
Romans5:2 yadushikanishije ukwizera mur’ ubu buntu duhagazemwo, kandi tunezerezwa no kwizigira kuzobona ubgiza bg’Imana." 
Romans5:3 Kandi si vyo vyonyene, ariko kandi tunezererwe n’amarushwa yacu, kuko tuzi yukw amarushwa atera ukwihangana;" 
Romans5:4 kand’ ukwihangana kugatera kudatsindwa no kugeragezwa; kudatsindwa no kugeragezwa kugatera kwizigira ibitaraba; 
Romans5:5 ukwo kwizigira ntigutētereza, kuk’ urukundo rw’Imana rwasutswe hose mu mitima yacu na Mpwemu Yera twāhawe." 
Romans5:6 Tugifise intege nke, mu gihe gikwiye Kristo yapfiriye abatubaha Imana." 
Romans5:7 Kw ar’ ibigoye k’umuntu apfira umugororotsi, umunyangeso nziza kumbure umuntu yotinyuka kumupfira:" 
Romans5:8 arikw Imana yatweretse urukundo rwayo idukunda, kuko Kristo yadupfiriye tukir’ abanyavyaha." 
Romans5:9 Nuko none tumaze gutsindanishirizwa n’amaraso yiwe, tuzorushiriza guheshwa na we gukizwa uburake bg’Imana." 
Romans5:10 Ko twujujwe n’Imana n’urupfu rw’Umwana wayo, tukir’ abansi bayo, none tumaze kwuzura na yo, ubugingo bgiwe buzorushiriza kudukiza." 
Romans5:11 Kandi si vyo vyonyene, arikw ikindi, tunezererwa Imana kubg’ Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, yaduhesheje kwuzura na yo." 
Romans5:12 None rero ko bimeze birtyo, nk’ukw icaha cazanywe mw isi n’umuntu umwe, urupfu rukazanwa n’icaha, ni k’urupfu rushika ku bantu bose, kuko bose bākoze ivyaha:" 
Romans5:13 ivyagezwe bitarabaho, icaha cari mw isi, arikw abantu ntibāharūrwakw icaha, ivyagezwe bitariho." 
Romans5:14 Arik’ uhereye kuri Adamu, ukageza kuri Mose, urupfu rwaganza n’abatākoze icaha gisa n’igicumuro ca Adamu, yar’ igishushanyo c’uwagira az’ aze." 
Romans5:15 Arikw ingabire y’Imana ntimera nka ca gicumuro. Kw igicumuro c’umwe catumye abenshi bapfa, ubuntu bg’Imana n’ingabire y’ubuntu bg’umuntu umwe Yesu Kristo vyarushirije gusāguka kuri benshi." 
Romans5:16 Kand’ iyo ngabire ntiyaje nk’icazanywe n’igicumuro c’umuntu umwe: kuko gucirwa urubanza kwavuye ku muntu umwe, kugatera gutsindwa, ariko ya ngabire yavuye mu bicumuro vyinshi, izana gutsindanishirizwa." 
Romans5:17 Kw igicumuro c’umwe catumye urupfu rushirwa ku ngoma n’umwe, abākīra ubuntu n’ingabire yo kugororoka bisēsekaye bazorushiriza gushirwa ku ngoma mu bugingo n’umwe, Yesu Kristo." 
Romans5:18 None rero nk’uko gucirwa urubanza kwazanywe n’igicumuro kimwe ku bantu bose, ngo batsindwe, ni ko ya ngabire yazanywe n’igikorwa kigororotse kimwe ku bantu bose, ngo batsindanishirizwe baronke ubugingo." 
Romans5:19 Kandi nk’uko kutumvira Imana kw’umuntu umwe kwatumye benshi bacika abanyavyaha, ni ko kuyumvira kw’ umwe kuzotuma benshi bacika abagororotsi." 
Romans5:20 Arikw ivyagezwe vyaje na vyo, kugira ngo gucumura kugwīre: yamara, ah’ icaha cagwiriye ni ho ubuntu bg’Imana bgarushirije kugwira," 
Romans5:21 kugira ngo, nk’ukw icaha cashizwe ku ngoma n’urupfu, abe ari ko n’ubuntu bg’Imana bushirwa ku ngoma n’ukugororoka, buheshe ubugingo budashira, kubga Yesu Kristo Umwami wacu." 
Romans6:1 Nuko tuvuge iki? Mbega twame dukora ivyaha kugira ng’ubuntu bg’Imana bugwire? 
Romans6:2 Biragahera. Twebge twapfuye ku caha, twoba tukikibamwo dute?" 
Romans6:3 Canke ntimuzi yuko twese abābatirijwe kuba muri Kristo Yesu, twabatirijwe kuba mu rupfu rwiwe?" 
Romans6:4 None rero kubatizwa kwatumye duhambanwa na we tuba mu rupfu rwiwe, kugira ngo, nk’uko Kristo yazuwe mu bapfuye n’ubgiza bga Data wa twese, abe ari ko natwe tugendana ubugingo busha." 
Romans6:5 Ko twakoranijwe na we n’igishushanyo c’urupfu rwiwe, tuzokoranywa na we n’ic’ ukuzuka kwiwe na co." 
Romans6:6 Kandi tumenye iki, yuk’ umuntu wacu wa kera yabambanywe na we, kugira ng’umubiri w’icaha uhindurwe ubusa, ntitwame tujakariye icaha:" 
Romans6:7 kuk’ uwapfuye aba atsindanishirijwe icaha. 
Romans6:8 Ariko bisanzwe twapfanye na Kristo, twizera yuko tuzobanaho na we;" 
Romans6:9 kuko tuzi yuko Kristo, amaze kuzuka mu bapfuye, atagipfa, urupfu rutakimuganza." 
Romans6:10 Ukwo gupfa yapfuye, ni ho yapfuye rimwe ku caha; ariko kw ariho, ariho ar’ uw’ Imana." 
Romans6:11 Abe ari ko namwe mwiyumvira ko mwāpfuye ku caha, ariko ko muriho mur’ ab’ Imana, muri muri Kristo Yesu." 
Romans6:12 None rer’ icaha ntikikabe ku ngoma mu mibiri yanyu izopfa, ngo mwumvire ivyo yifuza." 
Romans6:13 Kandi ntimugahe icaha imibiri yanyu ngw ikoreshwe n’ukugabitanya; ariko mwishikanire Imana nk’abazuke bavuye mu bapfuye, n’imibiri yanyu muyihe Imana kugira ngw ikoreshwe no kugororoka." 
Romans6:14 Icaha ntikizobaganza, kuko mutaganzwa n’ivyagezwe, ariko muganzwa n’ubuntu." 
Romans6:15 Nuko tugire dute? Mbega dukore ivyaha, kuko tutaganzwa n’ivyagezwe, ariko tuganzwa n’ubuntu? Biragahera." 
Romans6:16 Ntimuzi yuko shobuja mwihaye kuba abagurano bo kumwumvira, mur’ abagurano b’uwo mwumvira uwo? Namba mur’ abagurano b’icaha kizana urupfu, cank’ abo kwumvira Imana kuzana ukugororoka." 
Romans6:17 Arikw Imana ishimwe yuko naho mwar’ abagurano b’icaha, mwumviye mu mitima uburyo bgo kwigishwa mwahawe:" 
Romans6:18 kandi mwacunguwe ngo ntimuganzwe n’icaha, mujakarira ukugororoka." 
Romans6:19 Mbivuze nk’imvugo y’abantu, kubg’ intege nke z’imibiri yanyu. Nk’uko mwaha imibiri yanyu ibiteye isoni n’umugararizo, kuba abagurano bavyo, bigatuma muba abagarariji, abe ari ko na none muha ukugororoka imibiri yanyu, kuba abagurano bakwo, kugira ngo mwezwe." 
Romans6:20 Mukir’ abagurano b’icaha, ntimwaganzwa n’ukugororoka." 
Romans6:21 None rer’ ico gihe mwari n’imbuto ki mu bibamāramāza ubu? Kukw amaherezo yavyo ar’ urupfu. 
Romans6:22 Ariko noneho, ko mwacunguwe ngo ntimuganzwe n’icaha, mukajakarira Imana, mufise imbuto zanyu zizana ukwezwa, kand’ amaherezo n’ubugingo budashira." 
Romans6:23 Ingero y’icaha n’urupfu; arikw ingabire y’Imana n’ubugingo budashira, bubonerwa muri Kristo Yesu Umwami wacu." 
Romans7:1 Canke ga bene Data, ntimuzi yukw ivyagezwe biganza umuntu akiriho? mbgiye abazi ivyagezwe." 
Romans7:2 Kukw ivyagezwe bihambirira umugore ku mugabo wiwe, akiriho: arik’ umugabo wiwe iy’ apfuye, umugore aba ahamburuwe ngo ntaganzwe na we." 
Romans7:3 None rero, umugabo wiwe akiriho, yokwābīrwa n’uwundi mugabo, yokwitwa umusambanyikazi: arik’ umugabo wiwe iy’ apfuye, ntaba akiganzwa n’ivyagezwe, bituma atoba umusambanyikazi, naho yokwābīrwa n’uwundi mugabo." 
Romans7:4 None rero namwe, bene Data, gukoranywa n’umubiri wa Kristo kwatumye mucika abapfuye ku vyagezwe, kugira ngo mwābīrwe n’uwundi, ni we yazutse mu bapfuye, twamire Imana imbuto." 
Romans7:5 Tukiganzwa n’akameremere kacu, ukwifuza kw’ivyaha kw’uburyo bginshi kwazanywe n’ivyagezwe kwakorera mu mibiri yacu, kugira ngo twamire urupfu imbuto." 
Romans7:6 Ariko noneho ntitukiganzwa n’ivyagezwe, kuko twapfuye ku camye kidufashe, ni co gituma tuba abagurano, dukorera Mpwemu adukoresha uburyo busha, tudakoreshwa bga buryo bga kera bg’inyuguti." 
Romans7:7 Nuko tuvuge iki? Mbeg’ ivyagezwe n’icaha? Eka na mba. Ariko simba naramenye icaha, iyo ntakimenyeshwa n’ivyagezwe; kuko ntaba naramenye ukwifuza, iy’ ivyagezwe bitavuga ngo Ntukifuze." 
Romans7:8 Arikw icaha kibonye urwitwazo mu vyagezwe, gikorera muri jewe ukwifuza kw’uburyo bgose: kukw icaha kiba gipfuye, ivyagezwe bitariho." 
Romans7:9 Nanje kera nariho, ntafise ivyagezwe: maz’ icagezwe kije, icaha kirarabūka, nanje ndapfa;" 
Romans7:10 kand’ ico cagezwe co kuzana ubugingo nakibona kinzanira urupfu. 
Romans7:11 Kukw icaha campendahenze, kibonye urwitwazo mu cagezwe, kandi kigitera kunyica." 
Romans7:12 None rer’ ivyagezwe n’ivyera, kand’ ibgirizwa n’iryera, rigororotse, ryiza." 
Romans7:13 Mbeg’ iciza cambereye urupfu? Eka na mba! Arikw icaha ni co cārubaye, ngo kimenyekane kw ar’ icaha, kuko canyicishije iciza, ngw icagezwe gitume icaha kirushiriza kuba kibi." 
Romans7:14 Kuko tuzi yukw ivyagezwe ar’ ivy’ impwemu; ariko jewe nganzwa n’akameremere kanje, naguriwe kuba umugurano w’icaha." 
Romans7:15 Sinzi ico nkora; kukw ico ngomba atari co nkora, arikw ico nanka akaba ari co nkora." 
Romans7:16 Ariko ko nkora ico ntagomba, mba nemeye ivyagezwe kw ari vyiza." 
Romans7:17 None rero si jewe nkibikora, ariko n’icaha kimbamwo." 
Romans7:18 Ndazi yuko muri jewe, mu kameremere kanje, ata ciza kimbamwo: kuko kugomba gukora iciza kubana nanje, ariko kugikora nta kwo." 
Romans7:19 Kukw iciza ngomba atari co nkora, arikw ikibi ntagomba akaba ari co nkora." 
Romans7:20 Ariko ko nkora ico ntagomba, si jewe nkigikora, ariko n’icaha kimbamwo." 
Romans7:21 Ni ko mbona ikingera, yuko naho ngomba gukora iciza, ikibi kibana nanje." 
Romans7:22 Nnezererwa ivyagezwe n’Imana mu mutima wanje," 
Romans7:23 ariko mbona ikindi kingera kiri mu mubiri wanje kirwanya ikingera co mu mutima wanje, kikamfatira mpiri kuganzwa n’ikingera kiri mu mubiri wanje, ikingera c’icaha." 
Romans7:24 Ewe jewe ndagowe! Ni nde yonkiza umubiri untera uru rupfu? 
Romans7:25 Imana ishimwe, kubga Yesu Kristo Umwami wacu. Nuko jewe mu mutima wanje njakariye ivyagezwe n’Imana, ariko mu kameremere njakariye ikingera c’icaha." 
Romans8:1 Nuko rero noneh’ abari muri Kristo Yesu nta rubanza ruzobatsinda. 
Romans8:2 Kukw ikingera ca Mpwemu w’ubugingo bgo muri Kristo Yesu cancunguye ngo singanzwe n’icangera c’icaha n’ic’ urupfu. 
Romans8:3 Ic’ ivyagezwe bitāshoboye gukora kuko bifise intege nke kubg’ akameremere kacu, Imana yatumye Umwana wayo, afise ishusho y’umubiri w’icaha, kuba ikimazi c’icaha, itsindisha icaha kiri mu mubiri," 
Romans8:4 kugira ngw ivy’ ivyagezwe bibgiriza bishikanwe muri twebge, tutagenda mu buryo bg’akameremere kacu, ariko tugenda mu bg’ impwemu." 
Romans8:5 Kukw abaganzwa n’akameremere k’umubiri bitwaririka ivy’ umubiri, kand’ abaganzwa n’impwemu bitwaririka ivy’ impwemu." 
Romans8:6 Kwitwaririka ivy’ umubiri kuzana urupfu, ariko kwitwaririka ivy’ impwemu kuzana ubugingo n’amahoro." 
Romans8:7 Kuko kwitwaririka ivy’ umubiri gutera kwanka Imana, kuko kutumvira ivyagezwe n’Imana, kandi kudashobora kuvyumvira." 
Romans8:8 Kand’ abaganzwa n’akameremere k’umubiri ntibashobora guhimbara Imana. 
Romans8:9 Ariko mweho ntimuganzwa n’akameremere k’umubiri, ariko muganzwa n’impwemu, bisanzwe Mpwemu w’Imana aba muri mwebge. Arikw iy’ umuntu adafise Mpwemu wa Kristo ntaba ar’ uwiwe." 
Romans8:10 Bisanzwe Kristo ari muri mwebge, umubiri uba upfuye kubg’ icaha, arikw impwemu ni nzima kubgo kugororoka." 
Romans8:11 Ariko bisanzwe Mpwemu w’Iyazuye Yesu imukūye mu bapfuye aba muri mwebge, Iyazuye Kristo Yesu imukūye mu bapfuye izozura n’imibiri yanyu ipfa, kubga Mpwemu wayo aba muri mwebge." 
Romans8:12 None rero, bene Data, turi n’umwenda, atar’ uw’ akameremere kacu, ngo twitondere ivyako." 
Romans8:13 Kuko namba mwitondera ivy’ akameremere kanyu, ntimuzobura gupfa: ariko ni mwica ivy’ umubiri ukora, muvyicisha impwemu, muzobaho." 
Romans8:14 Abarōngōrwa na Mpwemu w’Imana bose ni bo bana b’Imana. 
Romans8:15 Kuko mutāhawe impwemu y’ubuja ngo mwongere gutinya; ariko mwāhawe impwemu yo kubahindura abana b’Imana, idutakisha ngo Abba, Data." 
Romans8:16 Mpwemu ubgiwe abgiririkanya n’impwemu yacu, ar’ icabona, yuko tur’ abana b’Imana." 
Romans8:17 Ariko ko tur’ abana bayo, tur’ abaragwa; tur’ abaragwa b’Imana, tur’ abaraganwa na Kristo, namba tubabazanywa na we, ngo tubone guhānwa ubgiza na we." 
Romans8:18 Niyumvira yukw imibabaro y’iki gihe idakwiye kugereranywa n’ubgiza tuzohishurirwa. 
Romans8:19 Kukw ivyaremwe vyiteze uguhishurwa kw’abana b’Imana biguhahamiye cane. 
Romans8:20 Kukw ivyaremwe vyagezwe kuganzwa n’ibitagira ikimazi, kandi si vyo vyavyigombeye, ariko vyagizwe n’Iyageze ko biganzwa birtyo," 
Romans8:21 kugira ngo vyizigire yuko na vyo bizocungurwa ngo ntibibe ibija vyo kubora, bizohabga ukwidegemvya, gufatana n’ubgiza bg’abana b’Imana." 
Romans8:22 Kuko tuzi yukw ivyaremwe vyose binihira hamwe bikaramukirwa hamwe kugeza n’ubu: 
Romans8:23 kandi si co gusa, ariko natwe abafise umushuzo wa Mpwemu, natwe nyene tunihira mu mitima yacu, twiteze gucika abana b’Imana, ni kwo gucungurwa kw’ imibiri yacu." 
Romans8:24 Kuko twakijijwe mu buryo bgo kugira ico twiteze: arikw icari citezwe iyo kibonetse ntikiba kicitegwa. Ic’ umuntu abonye, yoba akicitega ate?" 
Romans8:25 Yamara ko twiteze ico tutarabona, nuko tukirorēra twihangana." 
Romans8:26 Ni ko na Mpwemu adufasha mu ntege nke zacu: kuko tutazi uko dukwiye gusenga, ariko Mpwemu ubgiwe aradusengera, aniha iminiho itovugwa;" 
Romans8:27 arikw Īsesa imitima irazi ivyo Mpwemu yiyumvira, kuk’ ukw Imana igomba ari ko Mpwemu asengera abera." 
Romans8:28 Kandi turazi yuko ku bakunda Imana vyose bifataniriza hamwe kubazanira ivyiza, abāhamagawe nk’uko yabigabiye." 
Romans8:29 Kukw abo yamenye kera yabatoranirije kera gushushanywa n’ishusho y’Umwana wayo, kugira ngw abe imfura muri bene Se benshi:" 
Romans8:30 abo yatoranije kera, yarabahamagaye; abo yahamagaye, yarabatsindanishirije; abo yatsindanishirije, yabahaye ubgiza." 
Romans8:31 Ko bimeze birtyo, tuvuge iki? Bisanzwe Imana iri mu ruhande rwacu, uwoturwanya ni nde?" 
Romans8:32 Ītimanye Umwana wayo, ikamutanga kubgacu twese, izobura ite kutugabirira vyose kuri we?" 
Romans8:33 Ni nde azorega abo Imana yatoranije? Mbega n’Imana, kand’ ari yo ibatsindanishiriza?" 
Romans8:34 Ni nde azobatsindisha? Mbega ni Kristo Yesu, kand’ ari we yapfuye? Ibibiruta yarazutse, ar’i buryo bg’Imana, bitayekw aradusengera." 
Romans8:35 Ni nde azodutandukanya n’urukundo rwa Kristo? Mbega n’amarushwa, canke n’ivyago, canke n’uguhamwa, canke n’inzara, canke n’ukwambara ubusa, canke n’ukuba mw irinde, canke n’inkota?" 
Romans8:36 Nk’uko handitswe, ngo Twirirwa twicwa, bakuduhōra, Twagereranijwe n’intama z’imbagwa." 
Romans8:37 Ariko mur’ ivyo vyose turushishwaho kunesha n’uwadukunze. 
Romans8:38 Kuko mmenye neza ntabikekeranya yuko naho rwoba urupfu, cank’ ubugingo, cank’ abamarayika, cank’ abaganza, cank’ ibiriho, cank’ ibizoba, cank’ abafise ubushobozi," 
Romans8:39 cank’ uburebure bg’igihagararo, cank’ uburebure bg’amajepfo, cank’ ikindi caremwe cose, ata kizoshobora kudutandukanya n’urukundo rw’Imana ruri muri Kristo Yesu Umwami wacu." 
Romans9:1 Ndavuga ukuri muri Kristo, simbesha, ijwi ryo mu mutima wanje ribgiririkanya nanje muri Mpwemu Yera," 
Romans9:2 yuko mfise intuntu nyinshi n’umubabaro udahengeshanya mu mutima. 
Romans9:3 Iyaba vyashoboka, noshimye kuvumwa no kuba igicibga kuri Kristo kubga bene wacu, abo tuvukana ku mubiri," 
Romans9:4 ni bo Bisirayeli, ivyabo n’ugucika abana b’Imana, n’ubgiza, n’amasezerano, no guhabga ivyagezwe, no gusenga Imana, n’ivyasezeranywe:" 
Romans9:5 bafise ba sogokuruza ba bandi, kandi ku mubiri Kristo yamutse kuri bo, ni we ari hejuru ya vyose, ni we Mana ikwiye gushimwa ibihe bidashira. Amen." 
Romans9:6 Ariko s’ukugira ngw ijambo ry’Imana ntiryashitse: kukw abamutse kuri Isirayeli atari bo Bisirayeli bose. 
Romans9:7 Kandi kukw ar’ uruvyaro rwa Aburahamu, si co kibagira abana biwe bose: ariko, Kuri Isaka ni ho uruvyaro rwawe ruzokwītīrirwa." 
Romans9:8 Ni kwo kuvuga kw abana b’umubiri atari bo bana b’Imana, arikw abana b’isezerano ni bo baharūrwa nk’uruvyaro." 
Romans9:9 Kukw ijambo ry’isezerano ar’ iri, ngw Ikindi gihe nk’iki nzoza, Sara yavyaye umuhungu." 
Romans9:10 Kandi si co gusa, ariko na Rebeka, igihe yar’ amaze gusama inda y’umugabo umwe, Isaka sogokuruza," 
Romans9:11 kand’ abana bataravuka, batarakora iciza cank’ ikibi, ngw ivy’ Imana yagabiye itoranya bibeho, bitavuye ku vy’abantu bakora, ariko vyavuye kw Ībahamagara," 
Romans9:12 ico gihe yabgiwe, ngo Bukuru azoshumbira Butoyi;" 
Romans9:13 nk’uko handitswe, ngo Yakobo naramukunze, Esau na we naramwanse." 
Romans9:14 Nuko tuvuge iki? Mbeg’ Imana iragabitanya? Eka na mba! 
Romans9:15 Kuko yabgiye Mose, iti Nzogirira ikigongwe uwo nzokigirira, ngirire n’imbabazi uwo nzozigirira." 
Romans9:16 Ni co gituma bitava ku kugomba kw’umuntu, canke ku gushimika kwiwe, ariko biva ku Mana igira ikigongwe." 
Romans9:17 Kukw ivyanditswe vyabgiye Farawo, ngw Icatumye nguhagarika n’ukugira ngo nkwerekanirek’ ubushobozi bganje, kandi ngw izina ryanje rivugwe hose mw isi yose." 
Romans9:18 Nukw igirira ikigongwe uw’ igomba, kand’ ikomantaza umutima w’uw’ igomba." 
Romans9:19 Nuko wombaza, uti N’iki gituma ikigaya umuntu? Ni nde yankiye ivy’ igomba?" 
Romans9:20 Ariko ga wa muntu, uri nde, uhārīra n’Imana? Mbeg’ icābūmbge cobaza uwakibumvye, kiti N’iki catumye umbumba urtya?" 
Romans9:21 cank’ umubumvyi ntagera ibumba, mu mugoma umwe kubumbamw’ urwavya rumwe rwo gukoresha ivy’ icubahiro, n’urundi rwo gukoresha ibiteye isoni?" 
Romans9:22 Mbega har’ ico biriko, nah’ Imana yagomvye kwerekana uburake bgayo, no kumenyesha ubushobozi bgayo, namba yihangananiye imbabazi nyinshi inzavya z’ukuraka, ziteguriwe guhona;" 
Romans9:23 kugira ngo yerekanire ubutunzi bg’ubgiza bgayo ku nzavya z’ikigongwe, izo yiteguriye guha ubgiza kera," 
Romans9:24 kuri twebge, abo yahamagaye, si mu Bayuda bonyene ariko no mu banyamahanga?" 
Romans9:25 Nk’uko yavugiye mu kanwa ka Hoseya, it’ Abatār’ abantu banje nzobita abantu banje, Kand’ ūtār’ inkundwakazi nzomwita inkundwakazi." 
Romans9:26 Kand’ aho hantu bābgiriwe, ngo Ntimur’ abantu banje, Ni ho bazokwitirwa abana b’Imana nzima." 
Romans9:27 Kandi Yesaya asemerera ivy’ Abisirayeli, at’ Igitigiri c’Abisirayeli n’iyo coba nk’umusenyi wo ku kiyaga, amasigarira ni yo azokira:" 
Romans9:28 kuk’ Uhoraho azoshitsa ijambo ryiwe mw isi, ariringanize kand’ arihimbure." 
Romans9:29 Kandi nk’uko Yesaya yavuze kera, at’ Iyaba Uhoraho Nyen’ ingabo atādushigarije uruvyaro, Tuba twarabaye nk’i Sodomu, tukagirwa nk’i Gomora." 
Romans9:30 None tuvuge iki? Enda tuvuge yukw abanyamahanga batākurikiye ivy’ ukugororoka bāshitse ku kugororoka, ni kwo kugororoka kuva ku kwizera:" 
Romans9:31 arikw Abisirayeli bākurikiye ivy’ ivyagezwe vy’ukugororoka, ntibābishikako." 
Romans9:32 Ni ku ki? N’uko batābironderesheje ukwizera, yamara bābironderesheje ibikorwa nk’ivyobibahesha, batsitara kuri rya buye ritsitaza," 
Romans9:33 nk’uko handitswe, ngw Ehe ndashira i Siyoni ibuye ritsitaza, urutare rugwisha, Kand’ uwizera uyo ntazoterwa n’isoni." 
Romans10:1 Bene Data, ivyohimbara umutima wanje n’ivyo nsengera Abisirayeli ku Mana, n’ukugira ngo bakizwe." 
Romans10:2 Ndabashingira intahe yuko bafise ishaka ry’Imana, ariko si mu buryo bg’ubgenge." 
Romans10:3 Ko batari bazi ukugororoka kuva ku Mana bakarondera kwishingira ukugororoka kwabo ubgabo, ntibāganjwe n’ukuva ku Mana." 
Romans10:4 Kuko Kristo ari we ivyagezwe bishikirako, kugira ngw aheshe uwizera wese ukugororoka." 
Romans10:5 Mose yanditse, at’ Ūshishikara ukugororoka kuva ku vyagezwe ni kwo kuzomubeshaho." 
Romans10:6 Arik’ ukugororoka kuva ku kwizera kuvuga gurtya, ngo Ntiwibaze, uti Ni nde azodūga, ngw aje mw ijuru? (risobanurwa ngo kumanukana Kristo)," 
Romans10:7 cank’ uti Ni nde azomanuka i kuzimu? (risobanurwa ngo kudūgana Kristo, amukūye mu bāpfuye)." 
Romans10:8 Ariko kwavuze gute? Kwavuze kut’ Ijambo riri hafi yawe, riri mu kanwa kawe no mu mutima wawe; ni ryo jambo ryo kwizera, iryo tubigisha." 
Romans10:9 Kuko ni wāturisha akanwa yuko Yesu ar’ Umwami, ukizera mu mutima yukw Imana yamuzuye imukūye mu bapfuye, uzokizwa." 
Romans10:10 Kuk’ umutima ari wo umuntu yizeresha, akaronka ukugororoka: kand’ akanwa akaba ari ko yāturisha, akaronka agakiza." 
Romans10:11 Kukw ivyanditswe bivuga, ng’ Ūmwizera wese ntazoterwa n’isoni." 
Romans10:12 Nta tandukaniro ry’Umuyuda n’Umugiriki: kuk’ Umwami umwe ar’ Umwami wa bose, ni we afise ubutunzi bukwiye abamwambaza bose;" 
Romans10:13 kuko, Umuntu wese azokwambaza izina ry’Uhoraho azokizwa." 
Romans10:14 None bazokwambaza bate uwo batarizera? Kandi bazokwizera bate uwo batarumva? Kandi bazokwumva bate, ata wabasiguriye ivyiwe?" 
Romans10:15 Kandi bazosigura ivyiwe bate, batātumwe? Nk’uko handitswe, ngw Ewe kuntu ibirenge vy’abazanye ubutumwa bg’ivyiza ari vyiza!" 
Romans10:16 Arikw abumviye ubutumwa bgiza si bose. Kuko Yesaya yavuze, ati Mwami, ni nde yemeye ivyo twumvise?" 
Romans10:17 Nuk’ ukwemera kuva ku kwumva, n’ukwumva kuzanwa n’ijambo rya Kristo." 
Romans10:18 Ariko ndabaza: Mbega ntibumvise? Ego, bārumvise. Ijwi ryavyo ryumvikanye mw isi yose, Bo n’amajambo yavyo ku mpera y’isi." 
Romans10:19 Ariko ndabaza: Mbeg’ Abisirayeli ntibābimenye? Mose ni we yabanje kuvuga, ati Nzobateza ishari abatar’ ihanga ry’ukuri, Nzobarakisha ihanga ry’imburabgenge." 
Romans10:20 Kandi Yesaya ashira amanga cane, aravuga, ati Nabonywe n’abatāndondeye, Neretswe abatāmbaririkije." 
Romans10:21 Ariko ku Bisirayeli aravuga, ati Nirirwa ntegeye amaboko ubgoko butumva butongana." 
Romans11:1 Nuko ndabaza: Mbeg’ Imana yaciye abantu bayo? Eka na mba! Kuko nanje nd’ Umwisirayeli, wo mu ruvyaro rwa Aburahamu, wo mu muryango wa Benyamini." 
Romans11:2 Imana ntiyataye abantu bayo yamenye kera. Canke ntimuzi ukw ivyanditswe bivuga kuri Eliya? Ko yareze Abisirayeli ku Mana," 
Romans11:3 ati Mwami, bishe abavugishwa nawe, bāsambuye ibicaniro vyawe, nanje nsigaye jenyene, kandi barangenza ngo banyice." 
Romans11:4 Arikw Imana yamwishuye ngw iki? Iti Nishigarije abantu ibihumbi ndwi batāpfukamiye Bayali. 
Romans11:5 Nuko ni ko biri no mur’ iki gihe, harih’ amasigarira nk’uko yatoranijwe n’ubuntu bg’Imana." 
Romans11:6 Ariko ni vyaba bivuye ku buntu, ntibikiva ku bikorwa: namb’ atari ko biri, ubuntu si bgo buntu." 
Romans11:7 None vyabaye bite se? Ic’ Abisirayeli bārondeye, ntibākibonye; ariko, abātoranijwe bārakironse, abandi bakomantazwa imitima." 
Romans11:8 Nk’uko handitswe, ngw Imana yabahaye umutima wo guhunyiza, n’amaso atabona, n’amatwi atumva, gushitsa kur’ uyu musi." 
Romans11:9 Kandi Dawidi yaravuze, at’ Ameza yabo abe nk’ururiba, n’umutego, N’ikigwisha, n’inyishu yabo:" 
Romans11:10 Amaso yabo n’ahumwe, ntibabone, Kandi wame ubahetamitse umugongo imisi yose." 
Romans11:11 Nuko ndabaza: Mbega bātsitariye kugwa mahera? Eka na mba! Yamar’ ukugwa kwabo kwāzaniye abanyamahanga agakiza, ngo bitere Abisirayeli ishari." 
Romans11:12 Ariko, k’ukugwa kwabo ar’ ubutunzi bg’abari mw isi, n’ukugabanuka kwabo ar’ ubutunzi bg’abanyamahanga, ukugwira kwabo ntikuzorushiriza cane?" 
Romans11:13 Ariko ndababarira mwebge, abanyamahanga. Ndashimisha igikorwa canje, kuko nd’ intumwa ku banyamahanga," 
Romans11:14 kugira ngo kumbure ntere ishari ab’i wacu, nkize bamwe muri bo." 
Romans11:15 Ko gutabga kwabo kwazaniye abari mw isi kwuzura n’Imana, ukugarukanwa kwabo kuzoba gute? Mbega ntikuzoba ubugingo buzutse mu bapfuye?" 
Romans11:16 Kandi kw ifu y’umushuzo ar’ iyera, n’irobe ni ko rimeze; kandi kw igishitsi ar’ icera, n’amashami ni kw ameze." 
Romans11:17 Ariko namb’ amashami amwe yarahanyuwe, nawe ur’ ikija ca elayo watewe nk’ingurukizi hagati mu mashami, usangira na yo ubukame bg’igishitsi ca elayo bgite," 
Romans11:18 ntiwihayagize kur’ ayo mashami. Namb’ uyihayagizako s’igishitsi kimeze kuri wewe, ariko ni wewe umeze ku gishitsi." 
Romans11:19 Wovuga rero, ut’ Amashami yahanyuwe kugira ngo nterweko." 
Romans11:20 Ni ko: ukutizera ni kwo kwayahanyuje, nawe ukwizera ni kwo kuguhagaritse. Ntiwibone, ariko wiyubare." 
Romans11:21 Kukw Imana, kw itāgiriye ikigongwe amashami bgite, nawe ntizokikugirira." 
Romans11:22 Rāba rer’ ukugira neza kw’Imana, n’ubuhambazi bgayo: ku bāguye n’ubuhambazi, ariko kuri wewe n’ukugira neza kw’Imana, ni waguma mur’ ukwo kugira neza kwayo: kuko n’utagira urtyo, nawe uzohanyurwa." 
Romans11:23 Kandi ba bandi na bo, ni batāguma mu kutizera, bazosubizwako nk’ingurukizi: Imana ishobora kubasubizako." 
Romans11:24 Kuko, ko wahanyuwe ku giti cameze ar’ ikija ca elayo, ugaterwa nk’ingurukizi muri elayo nziza, mudasangiye ubgoko, ba bandi babusangiye ntibazorushiriza cane guterwa muri elayo yabo?" 
Romans11:25 Bene Data, singomba ko mutamenya iri banga, mwoye kwiyita abanyabgenge, n’iry’ uko habaye gukomantaza imitima y’Abisirayeli, ariko si bose, gushitsa ah’ igitigiri gikwiye c’abanyamahanga kizokwinjirira mw ishengero." 
Romans11:26 Ni vyaba birtyo, Abisirayeli bose bazokizwa, nk’uko handitswe, ngw I Siyoni hazova Umurokozi, Azokūra muri Yakobo ukutubaha Imana;" 
Romans11:27 Kandi ni ryo sezerano, nsezeranye na bo, Aho nzobakūrakw ivyaha." 
Romans11:28 Ku vy’ubutumwa bgiza, n’abansi kubganyu: ariko ku vy’ugutoranya kw’Imana, n’abakundwa kubga ba sekuruza." 
Romans11:29 Kukw ingabire z’Imana no guhamagara kwayo itavyicuza. 
Romans11:30 Nk’uko mwebge kera mwagarariza Imana, ariko non’ umugararizo wabo wazaniye mwebge kugirirwa imbabazi:" 
Romans11:31 ni ko na bo none bāgararije, kugira ngw imbabazi mwagiriwe zibazanire na bo kuzigirirwa." 
Romans11:32 Kukw Imana yugaraniye abantu bose mu mugararizo, kugira ngw ibagirire imbabazi bose." 
Romans11:33 Yō, uburebure bg’amajepfo bg’ubutunzi bg’ubgenge no kumenya vy’Imana! Imigabo yayo ntishoboka kubariritswa, n’inzira zayo ntizigira akehe!" 
Romans11:34 Ni nde yamenye umutima w’Uhoraho? Canke ni nde yabaye umujanama wiwe? 
Romans11:35 Canke ni nde yabanje kumuha kand’ akazokwishurwa? 
Romans11:36 Kuko vyose biva muri we, kandi bizanwa na we, kandi vyamuremewe: icubahiro kibe iciwe ibihe bidashira. Amen." 
Romans12:1 Nuko bene Data, ndabahanūra kubg’ imbabazi z’Imana, ngo mutange imibiri yanyu ibe ibimazi bizima vyera, bihimbara Imana, ni kwo kuyikorera kwanyu kwogira ikimazi." 
Romans12:2 Ntimushushanywe n’ivy’ iki gihe, yamara muhinduke rwose, mugize imitima misha, kugira ngo mumenye neza ivy’ Imana igomba, ni vyo vyiza bishimwa, bitunganye rwose." 
Romans12:3 Ndabgira umuntu wese muri mwebge, mbgirijwe n’ubuntu nahawe, yoye kwifata ukw atari, yamara yiyumvire yitonze nk’ukw Imana yagereye umuntu wese ukwizera." 
Romans12:4 Nk’uko mu mubiri umwe dufise ingingo nyinshi, kand’ ingingo zose zitagira igikorwa kimwe," 
Romans12:5 natwe ni ko turi; turi benshi, kandi tur’ umubiri umwe muri Kristo, umuntu wese n’urugingo rwa mugenzi we." 
Romans12:6 Nuko dufise ingabire zitandukana, nk’uk’ ubuntu twāhawe butandukana: namba twarahawe kuvugishwa n’Imana, tuvugishwe na yo uk’ ukwizera kwacu kungana;" 
Romans12:7 canke namba twarahawe igikorwa co mw ishengero, tugishishikare; cank’ uwigisha ashishikarire kwigisha;" 
Romans12:8 cank’ ūhanūra ashishikarire guhanūra; ūgira ubuntu, abugire ata kinubge; ūganza aganzanye umwete; ūgira imbabazi, azigire anezerewe." 
Romans12:9 Urukundo rwanyu rwoye kuba uruheyiheyi. Mwanke ibibi, mumatane n’ivyiza;" 
Romans12:10 ku vyo gukunda bene Data, mukundane rwose; ku vy’icubahiro, umuntu wese ashire imbere mugenzi we;" 
Romans12:11 ku vy’ ugushishikara, ntimugire urwangara; mukovye mu mitima gukorera Umwami wacu." 
Romans12:12 Munezererwe kwizigira ibizoba; mwihanganire amagorwa; mushishikare gusenga; 
Romans12:13 mugabanirize abera, uko bakennye; mushishikare gutanga indāro." 
Romans12:14 Ababahama mubahezagire; mubahezagire, ntimubavume;" 
Romans12:15 munezeranwe n’abanezerewe, murirane n’abarira." 
Romans12:16 Muhūze umutima; ntimushire umutima ku bikomeye, ariko mugendane n’ivyiyoroheje. Ntimwiyite abanyabgenge." 
Romans12:17 Ntimusubirize umuntu mu nkōko ikibi yabagiriye; mubabare gukora ivyiza imbere y’abantu bose. 
Romans12:18 Namba bishoboka, mu ruhande rwanyu, mwuzure n’abantu bose." 
Romans12:19 Abo nkunda, ntimwīhōrane, ariko muhe uburyo uburake bg’Imana: kuko handitswe, ng’ Uguhōra n’ukwanje, ni jewe nzobasubiriza mu nkōko, ni k’Uhoraho agize." 
Romans12:20 Ariko, Umwansi wawe ni yasonza, umugaburire; ni yagira inyota, umuhe ic’ anywa: kuko ni wagira urtyo, uzoba umurunzekw amakara yaka ku mutwe." 
Romans12:21 Ikibi coye kukunesha, yamara ikibi ukinesheshe iciza." 
Romans13:1 Umuntu wese n’agamburukire abamuganza: kukw ata kuganza kutava ku Mana, ukuriho kwagezwe n’Imana." 
Romans13:2 Ni co gituma, ūgābagābiye ūganza aba agābagābiye icagezwe n’Imana: kand’ abakigābagābiye bazoba bihamagariye gutsindwa n’urubanza." 
Romans13:3 Kukw abaganza atar’ abateye ubgoba k’ūkora iciza, shit’ ūkora ikibi. Uragomba kutagirira ubgoba ūganza? Kora neza, azogushima." 
Romans13:4 Kukw ar’ umukozi w’Imana kubgawe, ngw akuzanire ivyiza. Ariko ni wakora nabi, ugire ubgoba, kukw atambarira inkota ubusa, kukw ar’ umukozi w’Imana, umuhōzi ashitsa uburake k’ūkora nabi." 
Romans13:5 Ni co gituma ukwiye kugamburuka, atari kubgo kurakirwa gusa, ariko no kubg’ ijwi ryo mu mutima." 
Romans13:6 Ni co gituma kandi mutanga ikori; kukw abaganza ar’ abakozi b’Imana, bashishikarira ico gikorwa nyene." 
Romans13:7 Muhe bose ivyo bakwiye: abahabga ikori mubahe ikori; ababuguza mubabugurire; abo gutinywa mubatinye; abo kwubahwa mububahe. 
Romans13:8 Ntihagire uwo mugirira umwenda, atar’ ugukundana: kuk’ ūkunda uwundi aba ashikije ivyagezwe." 
Romans13:9 Kukw ibi, ngo Ntugasambane, ntukice, ntukibe, ntukifuze, n’ikindi cagezwe cose, bipoperanirijwe mur’ iri jambo, ng’ Ukunde mugenzawe nk’uko wikunda." 
Romans13:10 Ūfise urukundo ntagirira mugenzi we nabi: ni co gituma urukundo ari rwo rushitsa ivyagezwe. 
Romans13:11 Nuko mwame mugenza murtyo, kuko muzi imisi, yukw igihe gishitse co kwikangura. Non’ agakiza kacu karatwēgereye, kurusha igihe twizereye." 
Romans13:12 Ijoro rirakuze, bugira buce. Nuko twiyambure ibikorwa vy’umwiza, twambare ibirwanishwa vy’umuco." 
Romans13:13 Tugendane ingeso nziza, nk’abagenda ku murango, tutadandahirwa, tutaborerwa, tudasambana, tudakora ivy’ isoni nke, tudatongana, tutagira ishari." 
Romans13:14 Ariko mwambare Umwami Yesu Kristo, kandi ntimubabare ivy’ umubiri, ngo mukore ivyo wifuza." 
Romans14:1 Ūdakomeye mu vyizerwa, mumwemere, ariko s’ukumuhāririza ku vy’ akekeranya." 
Romans14:2 Umuntu umwe afise ukwizera kwo kumurisha vyose, arik’ ūdakomeye arya ibirimwa gusa." 
Romans14:3 Ūrya inyama yoye gukēngēra ūtazirya; kand’ ūtazirya yoye guhinyura ūzirya, kukw Imana yamwemeye." 
Romans14:4 Wewe uri nde uhinyura umushumba w’abandi? Kukw imbere ya shebuja ari ho ahagarara cank’ agatemba; mber’ ushime azohagarara, kuk’ Umwami wacu ashobora kumuhagarika." 
Romans14:5 Umuntu umwe ashima umusi umwe kuwurutisha iyindi; uwundi agashima imisi yose. Umuntu wese n’ashirwe mu mutima wiwe. 
Romans14:6 Uwiyumvira umusi awiyumvira kubg’ Umwami wacu; ūrya inyama azirya kubg’ Umwami, kukw ashima Imana; kand’ ūtazirya, yanka kuzirya kubg’ Umwami, na we ashima Imana." 
Romans14:7 Kukw ata muntu muri twebge ariho kubgiwe, cank’ apfa kubgiwe:" 
Romans14:8 namba turiho, turiho kuba ab’ Umwami; kandi namba dupfa, dupfira kuba ab’ Umwami. Nuko namba turiho, canke namba dupfa, tur’ ab’ Umwami." 
Romans14:9 Kukw icatumye Kristo apfa, akazuka, ar’ ukugira ngw abe Umwami w’abāpfuye kandi n’uw’ abariho." 
Romans14:10 Ariko weho, n’iki gituma uhinyura mwene So? Kandi nawe, n’iki gituma ukēngēra mwene So? Kuko twese tuzohagarara imbere y’intebe y’imanza y’Imana." 
Romans14:11 Kuko handitswe, ngo Nk’uko ndiho, ni k’Uhoraho agize, amavi yose azompfukamira, N’indimi zose zizovuga ishimwe ry’Imana." 
Romans14:12 Nuko rero, umuntu wese muri twebge azobazwa n’Imana ivyo yakoze." 
Romans14:13 Uhereye none rero, twoye guhinyurana; yamara tugire iyi migabo: ngo hoye kugira ūshira igitsitaza cank’ ikigwisha imbere ya mwene Se." 
Romans14:14 Ndabizi, kandi nemejwe neza n’Umwami Yesu, yukw ata gihumanya ubgaco; shit’ uwiyumvira kw ikintu gihumanya, ni we cohumanya." 
Romans14:15 Iyo mwene So ababajwe n’ivy’ urya, ntuba ukigendera mu rukundo. Uwo Kristo yapfiriye ntumuranduze ivyo kurya vyawe." 
Romans14:16 Iciza canyu coye gutukwa. 
Romans14:17 Kuk’ ubgami bg’Imana atar’ ukurya n’ukunywa, ariko n’ukugororoka, n’amahoro, n’umunezero vyo muri Mpwemu Yera." 
Romans14:18 Ūkorera Kristo artyo, ahimbara Imana, kandi n’abantu baramwemera." 
Romans14:19 Nuko dukurikire ivy’ amahoro n’ivyo gukomezanya: 
Romans14:20 ntimusenyure igikorwa c’Imana kubg’ ivyo kurya. Vyose ntibihumanya koko, ariko, uwo muntu arya ibimutsitaza, azobona ibara." 
Romans14:21 Ni ciza kutarya inyama, canke kutanywa vino, canke kudakora ikindi cose gitsitaza mwene So, canke kimugwisha, canke kimutera intege nke." 
Romans14:22 Ukwizera ufise, ukugumane mu mutima wawe imbere y’Imana. Hahirwa ūtihinyura ku vyo yemeye." 
Romans14:23 Ariko, ūkekeranya wese iy’ ariye aba atsinzwe, kuko bitaba bivuye ku kwizera: ikitava ku kwizera cose n’icaha." 
Romans15:1 Twebge abakomeye dukwiye kwihanganira intege nke z’abadakomeye, no kutinezereza." 
Romans15:2 Umuntu wese muri twebge anezereze mugenzi we, kugira ngw abone ivyiza, akomezwe." 
Romans15:3 Kuko na Kristo atinejereje, nk’uko handitswe, ngw Ibitutsi vy’abāgutuka vyaguye kuri jewe." 
Romans15:4 Kukw ivyanditswe kera vyose vyandikiwe kutwigisha, kugira ngo kwihangana no guhumurizwa guheshwa n’ivyanditswe biduhe kwizigira ibizoba." 
Romans15:5 Arikw Imana itanga ukwihangana n’uguhumurizwa ibahe guhūza imitima yanyu, nk’uko Kristo Yesu agomba," 
Romans15:6 kugira ngo muhimbaze n’umutima umwe n’akanwa kamwe Imana y’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, ni yo Se." 
Romans15:7 Nuko mwemerane, nk’uko Kristo na we yabemeye, kugira ngw Imana ishimishwe." 
Romans15:8 Ico mvuga n’uko Kristo yacitse umukozi w’abākebge wo kubagaburira ivy’ Imana, kubg’ ukuri kwayo, kugira ngw ashitse ivyo ba sogokuruza bāsezeraniwe," 
Romans15:9 kandi ngw abanyamahanga bahimbarize Imana imbabazi zayo, nk’uko handitswe, ngo Ni co gituma nzogutazira mu mahanga, Ndirimbe izina ryawe." 
Romans15:10 Kandi yongera kuvuga, ati Yemwe banyamahanga ni munezeranwe n’abantu bayo." 
Romans15:11 Kand’ arongera, ati Yemwe banyamahanga mwese, ni mushime Uhoraho, Kand’ amoko yose amuhimbaze." 
Romans15:12 Kandi Yesaya na we yaravuze, ati Hazobah’ igishitsi ca Isayi, Ni we azohaguruka kuganza amahanga, Ni we abanyamahanga bazokwizigira." 
Romans15:13 Imana itanga ivyizigiro ibuzuze umunezero wose n’amahoro biva ku kwizera, kugira ngo murushirize kwizigira ibizoba, mubihawe n’ubushobozi bga Mpwemu Yera." 
Romans15:14 Bene Data, nanje nyene ndazi ivyanyu ntakekeranya, yuko mwuzuye ineza, mwuzuye ubgenge bgose, mushobora no guhanūrana." 
Romans15:15 Ariko mbandikiye hamwe-hamwe ndushirije gushira amanga, nk’ūbibutsa, kubg’ ubuntu nahawe n’Imana," 
Romans15:16 ngo mbe umusuku wa Kristo Yesu ku banyamahanga, nsukūrira ubutumwa bgiza bg’Imana nk’umuherezi, kugira ngw abanyamahanga babe ikimazi gishimwa, cejejwe na Mpwemu Yera." 
Romans15:17 Nuko mfise ukwirata mu vy’Imana muri Kristo Yesu. 
Romans15:18 Sinzotinyuka kuvuga ikintu na kimwe atar’ ico nakoreshejwe na Kristo, kugira ngw abanyamahanga baganduke, ampaye amajambo n’ibikorwa," 
Romans15:19 n’ubushobozi bg’ibimenyetso bikomeye, n’ibitangaza, n’ubushobozi bga Mpwemu Yera. Ivyo vyatumye nshitsa ubutumwa bga Kristo, utanguriye i Yerusalemu, ugakikuza, ugashika no muri Iluriko," 
Romans15:20 namanye imigabo yo kuvuga ubutumwa bgiza, ah’ izina rya Kristo ritaribgamenyekane, ngo sinubake kw itanguriro ryubatswe n’uwundi:" 
Romans15:21 yamara ngo bimere nk’uko handitswe, ngw Abatīgāniwe ivyiwe bazobibona, Kand’ abataravyumva bazovyitegereza." 
Romans15:22 Ni co gituma ngira igisīvya kenshi co kuza i wanyu: 
Romans15:23 ariko none ntihakinyagukiye mur’ ibi bihugu, kand’ uhereye mu myaka myinshi nifuza kuza i wanyu," 
Romans15:24 aho nzogīra i Sipaniya. Kuko nizigira kuzobarāba nciye iyo, mukamperekeza, mukansezera neza njayo, ni namara kubashira inkumbu buhoro." 
Romans15:25 Arik’ ubu ndiko ndaja i Yerusalemu kugaburira abera. 
Romans15:26 Kukw ab’i Makedoniya no muri Akaya bahimbawe no gusorōranya ivyo gutabara aboro bo mu bera b’i Yerusalemu. 
Romans15:27 Vyarabahimbaye, kandi babafitiye umwenda: kuko namb’ abanyamahanga bāsangiye ivy’ impwemu vyabo, bafise umwenda wo kubafasha ku vy’umubiri." 
Romans15:28 Ni naheraheza ivyo, mmaze kubashikiriza neza izo mbuto z’ubuntu, nzovayo, nce i wanyu, nje i Sipaniya." 
Romans15:29 Kandi ndazi yukw aho nzozira i wanyu, nzoza nzanye umugisha wa Kristo wuzuye." 
Romans15:30 Nuko ndabinginga, bene Data, kubg’ Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, no kubg’ urukundo ruva kuri Mpwemu, murwanane nanje munsabire Imana," 
Romans15:31 nkire ab’i Yudaya batayumvira, kand’ ingaburo yanje ngiye kugabura i Yerusalemu ishimwe n’abera;" 
Romans15:32 mbone uko nza i wanyu nnezerewe, Imana ni yabikunda, nduhukane namwe." 
Romans15:33 Imana Nyen’ amahoro ibane namwe mwese. Amen. 
Romans16:1 Mbashimiye Foyibe mwene Data, ni we mukozi w’ishengero ry’i Kenkireya," 
Romans16:2 ngo mumwākīre kubg’ Umwami wacu, nk’uko bibereye abera, kandi mumufashe ku c’azogomba cose, kuko na we yafashije benshi, barimwo jewe." 
Romans16:3 Muntahirize Purisikila na Akwila abākoranye nanje muri Kristo Yesu," 
Romans16:4 kandi bāhevye iyabo mitwe ko yocibga kugira ngo bakize amagara yanje. Si jewe jenyene mbashima, ariko n’amashengero yose yo mu banyamahanga arabashima." 
Romans16:5 Kandi muntahirize ishengero ryo mu nzu yabo. Muntahirize Epayineto, uwo nkunda, ni we yashurije abo muri Asiya bābaye aba Kristo." 
Romans16:6 Muntahirize Mariya yakoreye mwebge cane. 
Romans16:7 Muntahirize Andironiko na Yuniya, dusangiye umuryango, abābohanywe nanje, ni ba rurangiranwa mu ntumwa, ni bo bantanze kuba muri Kristo." 
Romans16:8 Muntahirize Ampuliyato, uwo nkunda mu Mwami wacu." 
Romans16:9 Muntahirize Urubano, akorana natwe muri Kristo, na Sitaku, uwo nkunda." 
Romans16:10 Muntahirize Apele yagejejwe akarama muri Kristo. Muntahirize abo mu bo kwa Arisitobulo. 
Romans16:11 Muntahirize Herodiyoni dusangiye umuryango. Muntahirize abo mu bo kwa Narukiso, abari mu Mwami wacu." 
Romans16:12 Muntahirize Tirufayina na Tirufosa, bakorera mu Mwami wacu. Muntahirize Perusi akundwa, yakoreye mu Mwami cane." 
Romans16:13 Muntahirize Rufo, yatoranijwe n’Umwami, na nyina ni nka mama." 
Romans16:14 Muntahirize Asunkirito, na Fulegoni, na Herume, na Patiroba, na Heruma, na bene Data bari kumwe na bo." 
Romans16:15 Muntahirize Filologo na Yuliya, na Nereyu na mushiki we, na Olumpa n’abera bose bari kumwe na bo." 
Romans16:16 Muramukanishe kugumbirana kwera. Amashengero ya Kristo yose arabaganūtsa. 
Romans16:17 Ariko bene Data, ndabinginga kwitegereza abazana ivyo gutandukanya n’ibitsitaza, bidahūra n’ivyo mwize, mubazibukire." 
Romans16:18 Kukw abameze bartyo Umwami wacu Kristo atari we bajakariye, ariko n’inda zabo, kandi bōhesha imitima y’aberanda amajambo meza n’ivyo kubanezereza." 
Romans16:19 Igitumye mbabgira ivyo, n’uko kwumvira Imana kwanyu kwamamaye mu bantu bose: ni co gitumye mbanezererwa, ariko ndagomba ko muba abanyabgenge ku vyiza, mukaba abatungu ku bibi." 
Romans16:20 Imana Nyen’ amahoro izofyonyorera Satani vuba musi y’ibirenge vyanyu. Ubuntu bg’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo bubane namwe. 
Romans16:21 Timoteyo, dukorana, arabaganūtsa, bo na Lukiyosi na Yasona na Sosipatiro, dusangiye umuryango." 
Romans16:22 Nanje Terutiyo, nanditse iki cete, ndabaganūtsa mu Mwami wacu." 
Romans16:23 Gayo arabaganūtsa, uwansembereje, kand’ akākīra n’abo mw ishengero bose. Erasito, aganza ivy’ ikori ry’iki gisagara, na Kwaruto mwene Data, barabaganūtsa. [" 
Romans16:24 Ubuntu bg’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo bubane namwe mwese. Amen.] 
Romans16:25 Imana ishobora kubakomeza, nk’uk’ ubutumwa bgiza nahawe n’ukwigisha ivya Yesu Kristo bivuga, bihūra no guhishurwa kw’ ibanga ryahozwe uhereye kera hose," 
Romans16:26 ariko mur’ iki gihe riraserutse, kand’ ivyanditswe n’abavugishwa n’Imana birimenyesheje amahanga yose, nk’ukw Imana ihoraho yageze, kugira ngo bumvire Imana babiheshwa no kwizera," 
Romans16:27 Imana ifise ubgenge yonyene, icubahiro kibe icayo kubga Yesu Kristo, ibihe bitazoshira. Amen." 
1Corinthians1:1 Jewe Paulo, nahamagariwe kuba intumwa ya Yesu Kristo, nk’ukw Imana yagomvye, na Sositene mwene Data," 
1Corinthians1:2 turabandikiye mwebge abo mw ishengero ry’Imana ry’i Korinto, bejejwe muri Kristo Yesu, bāhamagariwe kuba abera, hamwe na bose bambariza ahantu hose izina ry’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, ni we Mwami wabo n’uwacu." 
1Corinthians1:3 Ubuntu n’amahoro bibe muri mwebge, biva ku Mana Data wa twese no ku Mwami Yesu Kristo." 
1Corinthians1:4 Ndashima Imana yanje na ntaryo kubganyu, kubg’ ubuntu bg’Imana mwahērewe muri Kristo Yesu:" 
1Corinthians1:5 kuko muri vyose mwatungiye muri we, mu vyo muvuga vyose, no mu bgenge bgose," 
1Corinthians1:6 kuk’ ugushingira intahe Kristo kwakomejwe muri mwebge. 
1Corinthians1:7 Bituma mutagira ingabire n’imwe muhaza, mwiteze guhishurwa kw’ Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo." 
1Corinthians1:8 Ni we azobakomeza gushitsa kw iherezo, kugira ngo ntimuze mugawe kuri wa musi w’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo." 
1Corinthians1:9 Imana n’iyo kwizerwa, yabahamagariye kugirirana ubumwe n’Umwana wayo Yesu Kristo Umwami wacu." 
1Corinthians1:10 Ariko ndabinginga, bene Data, mw izina ry’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, mwese mube imvugarimwe, kandi n’ibice ntibiremwe muri mwebge, ariko mutunganywe rwose hamwe, muhūje umutima n’inama." 
1Corinthians1:11 Kuko nabariwe ivyanyu, bene Data, n’abo kwa Kilowe, yuko har’ imitongano muri mwebge." 
1Corinthians1:12 Ico mvuze n’iki, yuk’ umuntu wese muri mwebge avuga, ati Jeho nd’uwa Paulo; uwundi ati Jeho nd’uwa Apolo; uwundi ati Jeho nd’uwa Kefa; uwundi ati Jeho nd’uwa Kristo." 
1Corinthians1:13 Mbega Kristo aragabanijwemw’ ibice? Paulo yarababambiwe? Canke mwabatijwe mw izina rya Paulo? 
1Corinthians1:14 Nshimira Imana yukw ata n’umwe nabatije muri mwebge, atari Kirisipo na Gayo;" 
1Corinthians1:15 kugira ngo ntihagire umuntu avuga yuko mwabatijwe mw izina ryanje. 
1Corinthians1:16 Kandi nabatije n’abo kwa Stefana: atar’ abo, sinzi ko har’ uwundi nabatije." 
1Corinthians1:17 Kuko Kristo atāntumye kubatiza, ariko yantumye kuvuga ubutumwa bgiza, ntavugishije ubgenge bg’amajambo, kugira ng’ umusaraba wa Kristo ntucīke ubusa." 
1Corinthians1:18 Kukw ijambo ry’umusaraba ku bahona ar’ ubupfu, ariko kuri twebge abakizwa n’ubushobozi bg’Imana." 
1Corinthians1:19 Kuko handitswe, ngo Nzohonnya ubgenge bg’abanyabgenge, N’ubuhanga bg’abahanga nzobuhindura ubusa." 
1Corinthians1:20 Umunyabgenge ari hehe? Umwanditsi ari hehe? Umunyabihāri wo mur’ iki gihe ari hehe? Mbeg’ Imana ntiyahinduye ubupfu ubgenge bg’iyi si? 
1Corinthians1:21 Kuko nah’ ubgenge bg’Imana bgageze yukw ab’ isi batazohabga n’ubgenge bg’isi kumenya Imana, Imana yahimbawe gukirisha abayizera ubupfu bg’ivyigishwa." 
1Corinthians1:22 Kukw Abayuda basaba ibimenyetso, Abagiriki barondera ubgenge," 
1Corinthians1:23 ariko tweho tubabarira ivya Kristo yabambge: uyo ku Bayuda n’ikigwisha, ku banyamahanga n’ubupfu:" 
1Corinthians1:24 ariko ku bahamagarwa, b’Abayuda n’Abagiriki, ni Kristo, ubushobozi bg’Imana, kandi n’ubgenge bg’Imana." 
1Corinthians1:25 Kuk’ ubupfu bg’Imana burusha abantu ubgenge; kandi n’intege nke z’Imana zirusha abantu inkomezi. 
1Corinthians1:26 Muzirikane ihamagarwa ryanyu, bene Data, yukw ab’ ubgenge bg’abantu bāhamagawe atari benshi, abakomeye bāhamagawe atari benshi, abapfasoni bāhamagawe atari benshi." 
1Corinthians1:27 Arikw Imana yatoranije ibipfu vyo mw isi, ngw imāramāze abanyabgenge: kandi yatoranije ibinyantege nke vyo mw isi ngw imāramāze ibikomeye," 
1Corinthians1:28 kandi n’ivyoroshe vyo mw isi, n’ibikēngērwa, mbere n’ibitariho, Imana yarabitoranije ngw itītūre ibiriho:" 
1Corinthians1:29 kugira ngo ntihagire umuntu yirata imbere y’Imana. 
1Corinthians1:30 Ni yo ibaha kuba muri Kristo Yesu, yaduhindukiye ubgenge buva ku Mana, n’ukugororoka n’ukwezwa n’ugucungurwa:" 
1Corinthians1:31 kugira ngo bibe nk’uko handitswe, ng’ Uwirata, yirate Uhoraho." 
1Corinthians2:1 Nanje, bene Data, hamwe nabasanga i wanyu, sinaje nd’agakūra mu majambo canke mu bgenge, mu kubamenyesha ibanga ry’Imana." 
1Corinthians2:2 Kuko nagabiye kutagira ico mmenya muri mwebge, atari Yesu Kristo, we yabambge." 
1Corinthians2:3 Ariko nabana namwe mfise intege nke, ndi n’ubgoba, mpinda agashitsi kenshi," 
1Corinthians2:4 imvugo yanje n’ukwigisha kwanje ntivyarimw’ amajambo y’ubgenge yo kwemeza abantu, ariko vyaserukamwo Mpwemu n’ubushobozi," 
1Corinthians2:5 kugira ng’ukwizera kwanyu ntiguhagarare mu bgenge bg’abantu ariko guhagarare mu bushobozi bg’Imana. 
1Corinthians2:6 Yamara, tuvugana ubgenge hagati mu bātunganijwe rwose, arik’ ubgo bgenge s’ubg’ iki gihe, cank’ ubg’ abaganza b’iki gihe bagenda bayōka." 
1Corinthians2:7 Ariko tuvugishwa n’ubgenge bg’Imana bgari bgaragizwe ibanga, bgari bgaranyegejwe, ubgo Imana yagabiye kera, ibihe vyose bitarabaho ko buzoba icubahiro cacu." 
1Corinthians2:8 Kandi mu baganza b’iki gihe nta wabumenye: iyo baba bārabumenye ntibaba bārabamvye Umwami w’icubahiro. 
1Corinthians2:9 Ariko nk’uko handitswe, ngw Ivy’ ijisho ritigeze kubona, n’ivy’ ugutwi kutigeze kwumva, Ibitigeze kwinjira mu mutima w’umuntu, Vyose Imana yavyiteguriye abayikunda." 
1Corinthians2:10 Arikw Imana yabiduhishuriye muri Mpwemu wayo: Mpwemu asesa vyose, n’ibihishijwe vy’Imana." 
1Corinthians2:11 Ni nde mu bantu azi ibiri mu muntu, atar’ impwemu yiwe, iri muri we? Ni ko n’ivy’ Imana biri, nta wubizi, atari Mpwemu w’Imana." 
1Corinthians2:12 Ariko tweho ntitwāhawe impwemu y’iyi si, ariko twāhawe Mpwemu ava ku Mana, kugira ngo tumenye ivy’ Imana yatugabiye." 
1Corinthians2:13 Na vyo nyene turabivuga, ariko ntitubivuga mu majambo yigishwa n’ubgenge bg’abantu, ariko tubivuga mu yigishwa na Mpwemu, tugereranya ivy’ impwemu n’ivy’ impwemu bindi." 
1Corinthians2:14 Arik’ umuntu afise umubiri n’ubgenge gusa ntiyemera ivya Mpwemu w’Imana: kukw ar’ ubupfu kuri we, kandi ntashobora kubimenya, kuko vyitegerezwa mu buryo bg’impwemu." 
1Corinthians2:15 Arik’ umuntu w’impwemu asesa vyose, kand’ ubgiwe nta wumusesa." 
1Corinthians2:16 Ni nde yigeze kumenya ivyiyumviro vy’Uhoraho ngo yigishe Uhoraho? Ariko twebge dufise ivyiyumviro vya Kristo. 
1Corinthians3:1 Kubganje, bene Data, sinashoboye kubabgira nk’ab’ impwemu, ariko nababgiye nk’abaganzwa n’akameremere k’imibiri yabo, nk’abana b’inzoya bo muri Kristo." 
1Corinthians3:2 Nabaramije amata, sinabagaburiye ivyo kurya bigumye: kuko mutaribgabishobore. Kandi na none ntimurabishobora," 
1Corinthians3:3 kuko mukiganzwa n’ivy’ akameremere kanyu. Ko muri mwebge har’ ishari n’ugutongana, ntimuganzwa na vyo? Ntimugenda nk’abantu?" 
1Corinthians3:4 Umuntu umwe kw avuga, ati Jeho nd’uwa Paulo, uwundi ati Jeho nd’uwa Apolo, ntimur’ abantu se?" 
1Corinthians3:5 None Apolo n’iki? Kandi Paulo n’iki? Mbega s’abakozi batumye mwizera Imana, nk’ukw Imana yahaye umuntu wese?" 
1Corinthians3:6 Ni jewe nateye imbuto, Apolo arazivomera, arikw Imana ni yo yazikujije." 
1Corinthians3:7 Nuk’ ūzitera nta co amaze, cank’ ūzivomera, atar’ Imana ikuza." 
1Corinthians3:8 Ūzitera n’ūzivomera ni bamwe: arik’ umuntu wese azogererwa nk’uko yakoze igikorwa ciwe. 
1Corinthians3:9 Kukw Imana ari yo dukorana, namwe mur’ indimiro y’Imana, mur’ inzu yubakwa n’Imana." 
1Corinthians3:10 Nk’uko nahawe ubuntu n’Imana, nashizeh’ itanguriro, nk’umwubakisha mukuru w’ubgenge, uwundi yubakako. Arik’ umuntu wese ni yiyubare uko yubakako." 
1Corinthians3:11 Kukw irindi tanguriro ata muntu ashobora kurishiraho, atar’ iryashizweho, ni ryo Yesu Kristo." 
1Corinthians3:12 Arikw iryo tanguriro, umuntu ni yaryubakishakw izahabu, cank’ ifeza, cank’ amabuye y’igiciro kinini, cank’ ibiti, cank’ ubgatsi, cank’ ibishakashaka," 
1Corinthians3:13 igikorwa c’umuntu wese kizoseruka. Wa musi uzogiserura, kuk’ uzohishuranwa n’umuriro, kand’ igikorwa c’umuntu wese uwo muriro uzokigeza ico kirimwo." 
1Corinthians3:14 Igikorwa c’umuntu, ico yubatse kur’ iryo tanguriro, ni carama, azohabga ingero;" 
1Corinthians3:15 igikorwa c’umuntu ni casha, azobura ingero, yamara ubgiwe azokira, ariko nk’uwokowe mu muriro." 
1Corinthians3:16 Mbega ntimuzi yuko mur’ urusengero rw’Imana, kandi ko Mpwemu w’Imana aba muri mwebge?" 
1Corinthians3:17 Umuntu ni yonona urusengero rw’Imana, Imana izomurandura; kuk’ urusengero rw’Imana ar’ urwera, kand’ urwo rusengero ni mwebge." 
1Corinthians3:18 Ntihakagire umuntu yihenda; umuntu wo muri mwebge ni yiyumvira kw ar’ umunyabgenge ku vy’iki gihe, abe igipfu, kugira ngw abone kuba umunyabgenge." 
1Corinthians3:19 Kuk’ ubgenge bg’iyi si ar’ ubupfu ku Mana. Kuko handitswe, ngw Itegesha abanyabgenge ubugunge bgabo." 
1Corinthians3:20 Kandi ng’Uhoraho arazi ivyiyumviro vy’abanyabgenge, kandi ko bitagira ikimazi." 
1Corinthians3:21 Nuko ntihakagire umuntu yirata abantu. Kuko vyose ar’ ivyanyu: 
1Corinthians3:22 ari Paulo, canke Apolo, canke Kefa, cank’ isi, cank’ ubugingo, cank’ urupfu, cank’ ibiriho, cank’ ibizoba, vyose n’ivyanyu," 
1Corinthians3:23 namwe mur’ aba Kristo, Kristo n’uw’ Imana." 
1Corinthians4:1 Umuntu n’atwiyumvire yuko tur’ abasuku ba Kristo, n’ababgiriza b’amabanga y’Imana." 
1Corinthians4:2 Kand’ ababgiriza babagomba ko baboneka ar’ abizigirwa. 
1Corinthians4:3 Ariko kubganje ni nk’ubusa rwose gucirwa urubanza namwe, canke n’urukinja rw’abantu; kandi nanje nyene sinicira urubanza." 
1Corinthians4:4 Kukw ata co niyiziko, ariko si co kintsindishiriza; arik’ ūncira urubanza n’Umwami wacu." 
1Corinthians4:5 Ni co gituma mudakwiye guca urubanza rw’ikintu na kimwe igihe carwo kitarashika, ni co kuza kw’Umwami wacu, azomurika ivyari vyanyegejwe mu mwiza, kand’ azogaragaza inama zo mu mitima: ni ho umuntu wese azohabga n’Imana ishimwe rimukwiye." 
1Corinthians4:6 Ariko, bene Data, ivyo mvyigereranijeko, jewe na Apolo, kubganyu, nk’igishushanyo: kugira ngw ivyo mvuze kuri twebge bibigishe kutarenga ivyanditswe; ntihagire umuntu yikakisha arwana ishaka ry’umwe akagaya uwundi." 
1Corinthians4:7 Ni nde aguteye kwitandukanya n’abandi? Kand’ ic’ ufise utāhawe n’igiki? Ariko namba waragihawe, n’iki gituma wirata, nk’ūtāgihawe?" 
1Corinthians4:8 Mumaze guhāga; mumaze gutunga; mwimye nk’abami, tutarimwo: ereg’ icompa mukaba mwārīmye, kugira ngo natwe twimane namwe." 
1Corinthians4:9 Kuko niyumvira yuko twebge intumwa, Imana yatwerekanye nk’abari hasi inyuma ya bose, nk’abagerewe kwicwa, kuko twacitse akābarore mw isi, mu bamarayika no mu bantu." 
1Corinthians4:10 Twebge tur’ ibipfu kubga Kristo; mweho mur’ abanyabgenge muri Kristo: tur’ abanyantege nke, mur’ abanyabushobozi: mur’ abanyacubahiro, tur’ inkēngērwa." 
1Corinthians4:11 Gushitsa n’ubu twishwe n’inzara n’inyota, twambaye ubusa, dukubitwa ibipfunsi, tubura uburagamo," 
1Corinthians4:12 dukoresha amaboko yacu tugatama: iyo badutuka turabahezagira, iyo baduhama turihangana," 
1Corinthians4:13 iyo batwambika ibara turabahōyahōya. Twahindutse umwavu w’isi, n’udukokorwa kuri bose gushitsa n’ubu." 
1Corinthians4:14 Ivyo simvyandikiye kubatetereza, ariko ni nko kubahanūra, nk’abana banje nkunda." 
1Corinthians4:15 Kuko naho mufise muri Kristo ababarera ibihumbi cumi, ntimufise ba so benshi, kukw ari jewe nabavyaje ubutumwa bgiza muri Kristo Yesu." 
1Corinthians4:16 Nuko ndabinginga, munyigāne." 
1Corinthians4:17 Ni co gituma mbatumyeko Timoteyo, umwana wanje nkunda, ayobokera Umwami wacu; azobībutsa inzira zanje zo muri Kristo, nk’uko nigisha hose mu mashengero yose." 
1Corinthians4:18 Ariko bamwe bīkakīsha, biyumvira yuko ntazoza i wanyu." 
1Corinthians4:19 Ariko nzoza vuba, Umwami wacu ni yabigomba; kandi s’amajambo y’abīkakīsha nzomenya, ariko n’ubushobozi bgabo." 
1Corinthians4:20 Kuk’ ubgami bg’Imana atar’ ubg’ amajambo, ariko n’ubg’ ubushobozi." 
1Corinthians4:21 Mugomba iki? Ko nza i wanyu nzanye inkoni, canke ko nzana urukundo n’umutima w’ubugwaneza?" 
1Corinthians5:1 Inkuru yāmamaye hose yuko muri mwebge harih’ ubusambanyi: kand’ ubgo busambanyi butoba no mu banyamahanga, umuntu gucīkiza muka se ngw amwābīre." 
1Corinthians5:2 Namwe mukīkakīsha, ntimubabare, nk’uko mwari mukwiye, kugira ng’uwakoze ico caha akūrwe muri mwebge." 
1Corinthians5:3 Kubganje naho ntariho ku mubiri, ariko ndiho mu mpwemu, nahejeje gutsindisha uwakoze ibimeze birtyo nk’aho ndiho," 
1Corinthians5:4 mw izina ry’Umwami Yesu mwebge n’impwemu yanje dukoranye dufise ubushobozi bg’Umwami wacu Yesu," 
1Corinthians5:5 guha Satani ūmeze artyo, kugira ng’umubiri wiwe uranduke, ubugingo bgiwe buze burokoke ku musi w’Umwami Yesu." 
1Corinthians5:6 Kwirata kwanyu si kwiza. Ntimuzi yuk’ umwambiro muke wambira irobe ryose? 
1Corinthians5:7 Nuko ni mukūreh’ umwambiro wa kera, kugira ngo mube irobe risha, nk’uko mutarimw’ umwambiro. Kuk’ umwagazi w’intama wa Pasika wacu watanzwe kw ikimazi, ari we Kristo." 
1Corinthians5:8 Nuko tuziririze imisi mikuru, tudafise umwambiro wa kera, cank’ umwambiro w’urwanko n’ikibi, ariko tugire imitsima itambiwe y’imitima ikeye n’ukuri." 
1Corinthians5:9 Nabandikiye muri ca cete ko mutivanga n’abasambanyi. 
1Corinthians5:10 Ariko sinavuga abasambanyi bo mu b’iyi si, cank’ abifuza, cank’ abanyazi, cank’ abasenga ibigirwamana, kukw iyo biba birtyo mwari mukwiye kuva mw isi." 
1Corinthians5:11 Ariko burya nabandikiye ko mutivanga n’uwitwa mwene Data, namb’ ar’ umusambanyi, cank’ uwifuza, cank’ ūsenga ibigirwamana, cank’ ūtukana, cank’ ūborerwa, cank’ umunyazi: ūmeze artyo, no gusangira ntimugasangire na we." 
1Corinthians5:12 Mpūriye hehe no gucira urubanza abo hanze? Mbega si mwebge mucira urubanza abo muri mwebge? 
1Corinthians5:13 Arikw abo hanze Imana ni yo izobacira urubanza. Ni mukūre umunyakibi muri mwebge. 
1Corinthians6:1 Mbega har’ uwo muri mwebge yogira ic’ apfa na mugenzi we, akūbahuka kubūranira ku bagabitanya, ntābūranire ku bera?" 
1Corinthians6:2 Ntimuzi yukw abera ari bo bazocira ab’ isi urubanza? Kandi kw ari mwebge muzocira ab’ isi urubanza, none ntimubereye guca imanza nto‐nto?" 
1Corinthians6:3 Ntimuzi yuko tuzocira abamarayika urubanza? None ntiturushiriza kuba abo guca imanza z’ivy’ ubu bugingo? 
1Corinthians6:4 Nuko, iyo mufise imanza zo gucibga z’ivy’ ubu bugingo, mbega mushirah’ abatagira ico bamariye ishengero ngw abe ari bo bazica?" 
1Corinthians6:5 Mbivugiye kubatētereza. Mbega vyoshoboka yuko muri mwebge hatagira umunyabgenge n’umwe yoshobora gucira urubanza bene Se? 
1Corinthians6:6 Ariko mwene Data akabūrana na mwene Data wundi, kandi bakabūranira no ku batizera!" 
1Corinthians6:7 Mbere n’ubu har’ ico muhomvye rwose, kuko musubiranamwo mukabūrana. Ntimwopfuma mugirirwa nabi? Ntimwopfuma mwemera kugungwa?" 
1Corinthians6:8 Ariko ni mwebge mugiriranira nabi, mugungana, kand’ abo mugirira murtyo ni bene So." 
1Corinthians6:9 Ntimuzi yukw abagabitanya batazoragwa ubgami bg’Imana? Ntimuzimire: abashakanyi, cank’ abasenga ibigirwamana, cank’ abasambanyi, cank’ abagabo bendwa, cank’ abagabo bendana," 
1Corinthians6:10 cank’ ibisuma, cank’ abifuza, cank’ imborerwa, cank’ abatukana, cank’ abanyazi, ntibazoragwa ubgami bg’Imana." 
1Corinthians6:11 Kandi bamwe muri mwebge ni ko mwari muri: ariko mwaruhagiwe, ariko mwarejejwe, ariko mwatsindanishirijwe mw izina ry’Umwami Yesu Kristo no muri Mpwemu w’Imana yacu." 
1Corinthians6:12 Vyose ndavyemererwa, ariko si vyose bingirira ikimazi. Vyose ndavyemererwa, ariko sinzoganzwa n’ikintu na kimwe." 
1Corinthians6:13 Ivyo kurya n’ivy’ inda, n’inda n’iy’ ivyo kurya; yamar’ Imana izobikūraho vyompi. Ariko, imibiri yacu s’iyo gushakana, mugabo n’iy’ Umwami wacu, kand’ Umwami n’uw’ imibiri yacu." 
1Corinthians6:14 Kand’ Imana yazuye Umwami, natwe nyene izotuzurisha ubushobozi bgayo." 
1Corinthians6:15 Ntimuzi yukw imibiri yanyu ar’ ingingo za Kristo? None ntore ingingo za Kristo, ndazihindure ingingo z’umusambanyikazi? Biragahera." 
1Corinthians6:16 Ntimuzi yuk’ uwimatanya n’umusambanyikazi aba ar’ umubiri umwe na we? Kuko yavuze, iti Bompi bazoba umubiri umwe." 
1Corinthians6:17 Arik’ uwimatanije n’Umwami wacu aba abaye impwemu imwe na we. 
1Corinthians6:18 Muhunge ubushakanyi. Icaha cose umuntu akora s’ic’ umubiri, arik’ ūshakana aba acumuye ku mubiri wiwe." 
1Corinthians6:19 Ntimuzi yukw imibiri yanyu ar’ insengero za Mpwemu Yera ari muri mwebge, uwo mufise, avuye ku Mana? Kandi si mwe mwiganza," 
1Corinthians6:20 kuko mwaguzwe igiciro. Nuko rero, mushimishe Imana mu mibiri yanyu." 
1Corinthians7:1 Ariko ku vyo mwanyandikiye, iciza n’ukw izinamuhungu atohūye n’icitwa umukobga." 
1Corinthians7:2 Ariko kubgo kwirinda gushakana, umugabo wese agire uwiwe mugore, n’umugore wese agire uwiwe mugabo." 
1Corinthians7:3 Umugabo ahe umugore wiwe ivy’ akwiye, kand’ umugore na we abigenze artyo ku mugabo wiwe." 
1Corinthians7:4 Kuk’ umugore ataganza umubiri wiwe, arik’ uganzwa n’umugabo; kand’ umugabo na we ntaganza umubiri wiwe, arik’ uganzwa n’umugore." 
1Corinthians7:5 Ntimukīmane, shiti kumbure musezeranye igihe, kugira ngo mubone uburyo bgo gusenga, kandi mwongere mubane, Satani ntabageragereshe kutirinda kwanyu." 
1Corinthians7:6 Ariko mvuze ivyo ar’ ukwemerana, s’ivyagezwe mbagerera." 
1Corinthians7:7 Nagomba kw abantu bose bomera nkanje: arik’ umuntu wese afise ingabire yiwe ahawe n’Imana, umwe ukwiwe, uwundi ukwiwe." 
1Corinthians7:8 Abatararongorana, bo n’abapfakazi, ndababgira yukw iciza kuri bo ar’ uko bogumya kumera nkanje." 
1Corinthians7:9 Ariko namba badashobora kwirinda bābīrane: kuko kwābīrana ari kwiza, kuruta gushuha." 
1Corinthians7:10 Abamaze kurongorana, ndabagera, ariko si jewe, n’Umwami wacu, umugore yoye kuvana n’umugabo wiwe;" 
1Corinthians7:11 arikw aramutse avanye na we, abe igisubiramuhira, canke yisubize hamwe n’umugabo wiwe. Kand’ umugabo yoye guta umugore wiwe." 
1Corinthians7:12 Arikw abandi ni jewe mbabgira, s’Umwami wacu. Mwene Data asanzwe afise umugore atizera, kand’ uwo mugore agakunda kubana na we, yoye kumuta." 
1Corinthians7:13 Kand’ umugore afise umugabo atizera, na we agakunda kubana na we, yoye kuvana n’umugabo wiwe." 
1Corinthians7:14 Kuk’ umugabo atizera yezwa kubg’ umugore wiwe, kand’ umugore atizera yezwa kubga mwene Data uyo. Iyo bitamera birtyo, abana banyu baba ar’ ibihumane, ariko noneho n’abera." 
1Corinthians7:15 Arik’ ūtizera, namb’ agomba kwahukana, ni yahukane. Mwene Data w’umugabo canke w’umugore ntahambirwa, iyo bimeze birtyo. Imana yaduhamagariye amahoro." 
1Corinthians7:16 Yewe mugore, ubgirwa n’iki yuk’ uzokiza umugabo wawe? Yewe mugabo, ubgirwa n’iki yuk’ uzokiza umugore wawe?" 
1Corinthians7:17 Ariko gusa, uk’ Umwami wacu yagabiye umuntu wese, kand’ ukw Imana yamuhamagaye, abe ari kw amera. Ni ko ngera mu mashengero yose." 
1Corinthians7:18 Mbega harih’ umuntu yahamagawe yarakebge? Ntagacike nk’ūtakebge. Harih’ umuntu yahamagawe atākebge? Ntagakebge. 
1Corinthians7:19 Gukebga nta co kumaze, no kudakebga nta co kumaze, arikw ikigira ico kimaze n’ukwitondera ivyagezwe n’Imana." 
1Corinthians7:20 Umuntu wese, uko yar’ ari mw ihamagarwa ryiwe, abigumemwo." 
1Corinthians7:21 Wahamagawe ur’ umugurano? Ntibikubabaze. Ariko, namba bishoboka k’ucika uwidegemvya, ubihitemwo." 
1Corinthians7:22 Uwahamagawe n’Umwami wacu ar’ umugurano, aba acitse uwidegemvya acunguwe n’Umwami. Ni ko, uwahamagawe n’Umwami ar’ uwidegemvya, aba acitse umugurano wa Kristo." 
1Corinthians7:23 Mwaguzwe igiciro, ntimukabe abagurano b’abantu." 
1Corinthians7:24 Bene Data, umuntu wese uko yar’ ari aho yahamagarwa, akugumanemwo n’Imana." 
1Corinthians7:25 Ku vy’ inkumi, simfise icagezwe n’Umwami wacu; ariko ndababgira ivyo niyumvira, nk’umuntu yagiriwe ikigongwe n’Umwami, ngo mbe umwizigirwa." 
1Corinthians7:26 Nuko ndiyumvira yukw ari vyiza kubg’ igihe kigoye ca none, yukw ari vyiza k’umuntu aguma ukw ari." 
1Corinthians7:27 Wahambiriwe ku mugore? Nturondere kubohorwa. Wabohowe ku mugore? Nturondere umugore. 
1Corinthians7:28 Arikw iy’ urongoye, nta caha uba ukoze. N’inkumi, iy’ irongowe nta caha iba ikoze. Mugabo, abameze bartyo bazogira amagorwa mu mubiri, ariko jewe nagomba kuyabakingira." 
1Corinthians7:29 Ariko, bene Data, ibi ni vyo mvuga, yukw igihe cāgiriye: uhereye none abari n’abagore bamere nk’abatabagira;" 
1Corinthians7:30 kand’ abarira bamere nk’abatarira, n’abanezerewe bamere nk’abatanezerewe, n’abagura bamere nk’abatagira ico bafise," 
1Corinthians7:31 n’abakoresha ivy’ isi, bamere nk’abatabishishikaye: kuk’ ukw isi imeze uku, kugenda gushira." 
1Corinthians7:32 Ariko ndagomba ko mutiganyira. Ūtagira umugore yitwaririka ivy’ Umwami wacu, uko yonezereza Umwami:" 
1Corinthians7:33 arik’ ūmufise yitwaririka ivy’ isi, uko yonezereza umugore." 
1Corinthians7:34 Kandi harih’ itandukaniro ku mugore n’inkumi. Ūtābiriwe yitwaririka ivy’ Umwami wacu, kugira ngw abe uwera ku mubiri no mu mutima: arik’ uwābiriwe yitwaririka ivy’ isi, uko yonezereza umugabo." 
1Corinthians7:35 Ivyo mbivugiye kubafasha, s’ukubashira mu mpururu, ariko n’ukubiroranya, no kugira ngo mukorere Umwami wacu, mudafise imitima ibiri." 
1Corinthians7:36 Arik’ umuntu ni yiyumvira kw atagirira umukobga wiwe neza, namb’ arenze ubukumi, kandi namba bikwiye rwose, n’agenze ukw agomba: nta caha azoba akoze, abareke barongorane." 
1Corinthians7:37 Arik’ ūkomeye mu mutima wiwe, adafise ikimuhambira, arikw ashobora gukora ivy’ agomba ubgiwe, yagabiye mu mutima kuzigama umukobga wiwe ngo ntarongorwe, azoba agize neza." 
1Corinthians7:38 Nuk’ ūtanga umukobga wiwe ngw arongorwe aba agize neza; kand’ ūtamutanga aba arushirije kugira neza. 
1Corinthians7:39 Umugore ahambīrirwa ku mugabo wiwe akiriho; arikw iy’ umugabo apfuye, nta kimubuza gucūrwa n’uw’ agomba, mugabo rero, ar’ ūri mu Mwami wacu." 
1Corinthians7:40 Arikw iy’ agumye ukw ari, ni ho arushiriza guhirwa, uko niyumvira kubganje: kandi ngira ngo nanje mfise Mpwemu w’Imana." 
1Corinthians8:1 Ku vy’ ivyaterekerejwe ibishushanyo vy’ibigirwamana, turazi yuko twese turi n’ubgenge. Ubgenge burakakīsha, arik’ urukundo rurubaka." 
1Corinthians8:2 Ni hagira umuntu yiyumvira yuko har’ ic’ azi, azoba ataramenya nk’ukw akwiye kumenya." 
1Corinthians8:3 Arik’ ūkunda Imana ni we amenywa na yo. 
1Corinthians8:4 Nuko, ku vyo kurya ivyaterekerejwe ibigirwamana, turazi yukw igishushanyo atar’ ikintu mw isi, kandi yukw ata mana yindi iriho, atar’ Imwe." 
1Corinthians8:5 Naho har’ ivyitwa imana mw ijuru canke mw isi, nk’uko har’ imana nyinshi n’abami benshi," 
1Corinthians8:6 ariko kuri twebge har’ Imana imwe, Data wa twese, yandurukwamwo na vyose, natwe twabesherejweho kuba abayo: kandi har’ Umwami umwe, ni Yesu Kristo, abeshaho vyose, natwe akatubeshaho." 
1Corinthians8:7 Arik’ ubgo bgenge ntibufiswe na bose: kuko bamwe bāremariye mu bigirwamana gushitsa n’ubu, barya ikintu bibgira ko caterekerejwe ikigirwamana, kand’ umutima ugahumanywa no kudakomera." 
1Corinthians8:8 Arikw ivyo kurya si vyo bidushikiriza Imana: iyo tutabiriye, nta co duhōmba; cank’ iyo tubiriye, nta co duhōmbōka." 
1Corinthians8:9 Mwiyubare, kugira ng’ ubgo bushobozi bganyu bgoye kuba igitsitaza c’abadakomeye na gato." 
1Corinthians8:10 Kuk’ umuntu iy’ akubonye, wewe wahawe gutahura, wicaye urīra mu rusengero rw’ikigirwamana, umutima w’uwo, iy’ adakomeye, mbega ntuzorinduka, akarya ivyaterekerejwe ibigirwamana?" 
1Corinthians8:11 Nuk’ ūdakomeye aba aranduwe no gutahura kwawe, kand’ ari we mwene Data Kristo yapfiriye." 
1Corinthians8:12 Nukw iyo mukoreye icaha bene Data murtyo, mugakomeretsa imitima yabo idakomeye, muba mukoreye icaha Kristo." 
1Corinthians8:13 Ni co gituma namb’ ivyo kurya bigwisha mwene Data, sinzopfa nongeye kurya inyama kugira ngo singwishe mwene Data." 
1Corinthians9:1 Mbega sind’ uwidegemvya? Sind’ intumwa? Sinabonye Yesu Umwami wacu? Namwe ntimur’ igikorwa canje mu Mwami? 
1Corinthians9:2 Namba ku bandi ntar’ intumwa, ariko kuri mwebge ndi yo: kuko mur’ ikimenyetso mu Mwami c’uko nd’intumwa." 
1Corinthians9:3 Ibi ni vyo nireguza ku bampinyura: 
1Corinthians9:4 mbega ntitwemererwa kurya no kunywa? 
1Corinthians9:5 Ntitwokwemerewe kujana abagore bacu ari bene Data nk’ukw izindi ntumwa zikora, na bene nyina w’Umwami wacu, na Kefa?" 
1Corinthians9:6 Canke jewe na Barunaba ni twebge twenyene tutemererwa kureka gukora? 
1Corinthians9:7 Ni nde yigeze kwitunga, ar’ umusoda? Ni nde yotera uruzabibu ntarye inzabibu zarwo? Canke ni nde yoragira ubusho, ntabunywe?" 
1Corinthians9:8 Mbeg’ ivyo mbivuze mu buryo bg’abantu, cank’ ivyagezwe vyo ntibivuga birtyo?" 
1Corinthians9:9 Kuko handitswe mu vyagezwe vya Mose, ngo Ntimuze murumye umunwa w’inka irikw irasekura ingano. Mbeg’ inka ni zo Imana ibabaye?" 
1Corinthians9:10 Canke se yabivuze kubgacu? Ego me, vyanditswe kubgacu; kuk’ umurimyi akwiye kurima afise ivyizigiro, kand’ umusekuzi akwiye gusekura yizigiye kw azohabgako." 
1Corinthians9:11 Mbega ko twababivyemw’ ivy’ impwemu, none n’ibikomeye ko twokwimbura ivyanyu vy’umubiri?" 
1Corinthians9:12 Abandi namba bāravyemerewe kuri mwebge, mbega ntitubarusha cane? Ariko ntitwarwaniye ivyo twemerewe, yamara twihanganira vyose, kugira ngo ntituzane ikidehesha ubutumwa bgiza bga Kristo." 
1Corinthians9:13 Ntimuzi yukw abakora ibikorwa vy’ivyera barya ivy’ urusengero, kand’ abakora ivy’ igicaniro basangira n’igicaniro?" 
1Corinthians9:14 Kandi n’Umwami wacu ni ko yageze kw abavuga ubutumwa bgiza batungwa n’ubutumwa. 
1Corinthians9:15 Ariko jewe ubganje nta co narwaniye mur’ ivyo: kandi sinandikiye ivyo kugira ngo nkorerwe ntyo. Ivyoba vyiza n’uko nopfuma mpfa, hak’ umuntu ahindura ubusa ivyo vyirato vyanje." 
1Corinthians9:16 Iyo mvuga ubutumwa, singira ico nirata; kuko mfise ikingōbēra: ntavuze ubutumwa nobona ibara." 
1Corinthians9:17 Ngenjeje ntyo mbikunze, ndagererwa; ariko ngenjeje ntyo ntabikunze na ho nyene ngōbērwa n’ububgiriza nizigiweko." 
1Corinthians9:18 Non’ ingero yanje n’inki? N’uk’ ubutumwa, uko mbuvuze, mbuvuga ku buntu, kugira ngo sindwanire ivyo nemerewe mu butumwa." 
1Corinthians9:19 Naho kuri bose nd’uwidegemvya, nihinduye umugurano wa bose, kugira ngo ndushirize kuronka benshi." 
1Corinthians9:20 Ku Bayuda nabaye nk’Umuyuda, kugira ngo ndonke Abayuda: ku baganzwa n’ivyagezwe nabaye nk’ūganzwa na vyo, nah’ ubganje ntaganzwa na vyo, kugira ngo ndonke abaganzwa n’ivyagezwe." 
1Corinthians9:21 Ku bataganzwa n’ivyagezwe, nabaye nk’ūtaganzwa na vyo, kugira ngo ndonke abataganzwa n’ivyagezwe, yamara ku Mana ho sind’ ūtaganzwa n’ivyagezwe, kuko kuri Kristo nganzwa na vyo." 
1Corinthians9:22 Ku badakomeye nabaye nk’ūdakomeye, kugira ngo ndonke abadakomeye. Kuri bose nabaye vyose kugira ngo nkirishe bamwe‐bamwe uburyo bgose." 
1Corinthians9:23 Kand’ ivyo vyose mbikora kubg’ ubutumwa bgiza, kugira ngo mfatanye n’abandi muri bgo." 
1Corinthians9:24 Ntimuzi yuko mu birori abasiganwa biruka bose, arik’ ūhērwa akaba umwe? Namwe abe ari ko mwiruka, kugira ngo muronke impēra." 
1Corinthians9:25 Kuk’ umuntu wese azorushanywa yitegura muri vyose: abo bagenza bartyo, kugira ngo bahabge igitsibo gishira, ariko twebge tugenza durtyo kugira ngo duhabge ikitazoshira." 
1Corinthians9:26 Nuko nanje ndiruka, ariko si nk’ūtazi iy’ aja: nkubitana ibipfunsi, ariko si nk’ūhusha;" 
1Corinthians9:27 kandi ndwanya umubiri wanje, nkawuhindura umuja, kugira ngo kumbure mmaze kwigisha abandi, nanje ubganje sinze mboneke ko ntemewe." 
1Corinthians10:1 Bene Data, singomba ko mutamenya yuko ba sogokuruza bose bāri musi ya ca gicu, kandi yuko bose bāciye hagati ya ca kiyaga cigabanije," 
1Corinthians10:2 bose bakabatirizwa kuba aba Mose mur’ ico gicu no mur’ ico kiyaga," 
1Corinthians10:3 bose bagasangira vya vyo kurya vy’impwemu," 
1Corinthians10:4 bose bagasangira vya vyo kunywa vy’ impwemu. Kuko bānywa ku gitandara c’impwemu cabakurikira, ico gitandara cāri Kristo." 
1Corinthians10:5 Arikw abenshi muri bo, Imana ntiyabashimye, kuko bahonerejwe mu bugaragwa." 
1Corinthians10:6 Arikw ivyo vyatubereye akarorero kugira ngo ntitwifuze ibibi, nk’uko ba bandi bāvyifuje." 
1Corinthians10:7 Kandi ntimugasenge ibishushanyo vy’ibigirwamana, nk’uko bamwe bo muri ba bandi bābisenga: nk’uko handitswe, ngw Abantu bicaritswe no kurya no kunywa, bava hasi baravyina." 
1Corinthians10:8 Kandi ntitugashakane, nk’uko bamwe bo muri ba bandi bāshakanye, maze hagapfamw’ abantu ibihumbi mirongwibiri na bitatu ku musi umwe." 
1Corinthians10:9 Kandi ntitukagerageze Umwami wacu, nk’uko bamwe bo muri ba bandi bāmugerageje, bakamarwa n’inzoka." 
1Corinthians10:10 Kandi ntimukidodombe, nk’uko bamwe bo muri ba bandi bidodomvye, bakamarwa n’umuranduzi." 
1Corinthians10:11 Arikw ivyo vyababayeko kugira ngo bitubere akarorero, kandi vyandikiwe kuduhanūra twebge, abashikwako n’amaherezo y’ibihe." 
1Corinthians10:12 Nuko rer’ uwiyumvira kw ahagaze ni yiyubare ntagwe. 
1Corinthians10:13 Nta cabagerageje kitar’ ic’ umuntu yoshobora kwihanganira: arikw Imana n’iyo kwizigirwa ntizobakundira ko mugeragezwa n’ibiruta ivyo mushobora, ariko hamwe n’ikibagerageza izobacira icanzo, kugira ngo mubone ingene mushobora kucihanganira." 
1Corinthians10:14 Nuko, abo nkunda, ni muhunge gusenga ibigirwamana." 
1Corinthians10:15 Ndababgira nk’abanyabgenge; mwiyumvire ivyo mvuga, yukw ari ko biri." 
1Corinthians10:16 Igikombe c’umuhezagiro, ico duhezagira, mbega si kwo gusangira amaraso ya Kristo? Umutsima tumanyagura, si kwo gusangira umubiri wa Kristo?" 
1Corinthians10:17 Nk’uk’ uwo mutsima ar’ umwe, twebge, naho turi benshi, tur’ umubiri umwe: kuko twese dusangira umutsima umwe." 
1Corinthians10:18 Murābe Abisirayeli ku rukoba: abarya ikimazi, mbega ntibasangira n’igicaniro?" 
1Corinthians10:19 Nukw ico mvuga n’igiki? Mbega mvuga yukw icaterekerejwe ikigirwamana ar’ ikintu, canke yukw ikigirwamana ar’ ikintu?" 
1Corinthians10:20 Ariko mvuga yukw ibimazi abanyamahanga batanga, babiha abadayimoni, babiterekereza abadayimoni, ntibabiha Imana: nanje singomba yuko musangira n’abadayimoni." 
1Corinthians10:21 Ntimushobora kunywera ku gikombe c’Umwami wacu, no ku gikombe c’abadayimoni: ntimushobora gusangira ivyo ku meza y’Umwami wacu n’ivyo ku meza y’abadayimoni." 
1Corinthians10:22 Cank’ Umwami tumutere ishari? Mbega tumurusha inkomezi? 
1Corinthians10:23 Vyose turavyemererwa, arikw ibitugirira ikimazi si vyose. Vyose turavyemererwa, arikw ivyubaka si vyose." 
1Corinthians10:24 Ntihagire umuntu ababara ivyiwe, arikw ababare ivya mugenzi we." 
1Corinthians10:25 Izo zigurwa mw ibāgiro, mube muzirya ata co mubajije kubg’ ijwi ryo mu mutima:" 
1Corinthians10:26 kukw isi ar’iy’ Uhoraho, n’ibiyuzuye." 
1Corinthians10:27 Umuntu wo mu batizera ni yabahamagara, mukagomba kugenda, ico bazoshira imbere yanyu cose, mube mukirya, ata co mubajije, kubg’ ijwi ryo mu mutima." 
1Corinthians10:28 Ariko ni hagira umuntu ababgira, at’ Ico n’icāterekerejwe: ntimukakirye, kubg’ uyo abiseruye, no kubg’ ijwi ryo mu mutima." 
1Corinthians10:29 Arik’ umutima mvuze s’uwawe, n’uwa wa wundi. N’iki gituma ukwidegemvya kwanje guhinyurwa n’umutima w’uwundi?" 
1Corinthians10:30 Ko ndya mbishimiye, n’iki gituma ntukirwa ivyo nshimiye?" 
1Corinthians10:31 Nukw iyo murya, canke munywa, canke mukora ikindi kintu cose, mube mukorera vyose gushimisha Imana." 
1Corinthians10:32 Ntimubere Abayuda igitsitaza, cank’ Abagiriki, cank’ ishengero ry’Imana:" 
1Corinthians10:33 nk’uko nanje nnezereza bose muri vyose, ntarondera ikigira ico kimmarira ubganje, ariko nkarondera ikigira ico kimarira abenshi, kugira ngo bakire." 
1Corinthians11:1 Munyigāne, nk’uko nanje nīgāna Kristo." 
1Corinthians11:2 Ndabashima, kuko munyibuka muri vyose, mukagumya ivyo nabashikirije, nk’uko nabibahaye." 
1Corinthians11:3 Ariko ndagomba ko mumenya k’umutwe w’umugabo wese ari Kristo, kandi k’umutwe w’umugore ar’ umugabo, kandi k’umutwe wa Kristo ar’ Imana." 
1Corinthians11:4 Umugabo wese iy’ asenga cank’ avugishwa n’Imana umutwe wiwe utwikiriye, aba awuteye isoni." 
1Corinthians11:5 Arik’ umugore wese iy’ asenga cank’ avugishwa n’Imana, adatwikiriye umutwe, aba awuteye isoni: kukw ari bimwe rwose no kumobga." 
1Corinthians11:6 Ni hagira umugore atitwikira mu mutwe, bamukerere n’umushatsi: namb’ ar’ ibiteye isoni k’umugore akererwa umushatsi canke kw amobga ni yitwikire mu mutwe." 
1Corinthians11:7 Umugabo ntakwiye kwitwikira mu mutwe, kukw ar’ ishusho y’Imana n’ubgiza bgayo: arik’ umugore n’ubgiza bg’umugabo." 
1Corinthians11:8 Kuk’ umugabo atamutse ku mugore, arik’ umugore ni we yamutse ku mugabo." 
1Corinthians11:9 Kand’ umugabo ntiyaremwe kubg’ umugore, arik’ umugore ni we yaremwe kubg’ umugabo." 
1Corinthians11:10 Ni co gituma umugore akwiye kwambara mu mutwe ikimenyetso co kugabga, kubg’ abamarayika." 
1Corinthians11:11 Ariko mu Mwami wacu, umugore agenda ku mugabo, ni ko n’umugabo agenda ku mugore." 
1Corinthians11:12 Nk’uk’ umugore yamutse ku mugabo, ni k’umugabo avyarwa n’umugore: ariko vyose vyamuka ku Mana." 
1Corinthians11:13 Ni mwiyumvire ubganyu uko biri. Mbega birakwiye k’umugore asenga Imana atitwikiriye mu mutwe? 
1Corinthians11:14 Akameremere kacu mbega ntikabigisha yuk’ umugabo yotega umushatsi, womutera isoni," 
1Corinthians11:15 kandi k’umugore, iy’ ateze umushatsi, uba ar’ ubgiza bgiwe? Kuko yahawe umushatsi ng’ube umwambaro wo mu mutwe." 
1Corinthians11:16 Ariko namba har’ umuntu agomba kuvyura ibihāri, twebge ntidufise umugenzo nk’uwo, kandi n’amashengero y’Imana ntawufise." 
1Corinthians11:17 Arik’ uko mbabarira ibi, simbashima, kuko mudakoranira iciza, ariko mukoranira ikibi." 
1Corinthians11:18 Ica mbere, iyo mukoraniye mw ikoraniro, numva yuko mwitandukanya, kandi ngira ngo muri bimwe‐bimwe vyoba ari ko biri." 
1Corinthians11:19 Kuko n’ibice bitobura kuba muri mwebge, ngw abemewe muri mwebge baseruke." 
1Corinthians11:20 Nukw iyo mukoranye, burya ntikuba ar’ukurya ingaburo y’Umwami wacu." 
1Corinthians11:21 Kuko mu kurya, umuntu wese yisangiza ivyiwe agacura abandi: maz’ umwe agasonza, uwundi akaborerwa." 
1Corinthians11:22 Mbega yemwe: ntimufise ingo zo kurīramwo no kunyweramwo? Canke mukēngēra ishengero ry’Imana, mugatētereza abadafise? Ndababgire iki? Ndabashime? Kur’ ivyo simbashima." 
1Corinthians11:23 Kukw ico nahawe n’Umwami wacu ari co nabashikirije namwe, yuk’ Umwami Yesu mw ijoro yaguzwemwo yābiriye umutsima," 
1Corinthians11:24 akawushimira Imana, akawumanyagura, akavuga, at’ Uyu n’umubiri wanje ubatangiwe, murahora mugira murtya kugira ngo kibe icibutso canje." 
1Corinthians11:25 N’igikombe akigenza artyo, bahejeje kurya, arababgira, at’ Iki gikombe n’isezerano risha ryo mu maraso yanje; murahora mugira murtya uko muzonywako, kugira ngo kibe icibutso canje." 
1Corinthians11:26 Uko murya uwo mutsima kand’ uko munywera kur’ ico gikombe, muba mumenyekanisha urupfu rw’Umwami wacu, kugeza ah’ azozira." 
1Corinthians11:27 Ni co gituma, umuntu wese azorya umutsima w’Umwami wacu, cank’ azonywera ku gikombe ciwe, uko bidakwiye, azotsindwa n’urubanza rw’uko yakēngereye umubiri n’amaraso vy’Umwami." 
1Corinthians11:28 Arik’ umuntu yibaze ukw ameze, abone kurya kur’ uwo mutsima, no kunywera kur’ ico gikombe." 
1Corinthians11:29 Kuk’ ūrya cank’ ūnywa, atamenye umubiri w’Umwami wacu, arya kand’ anywa ibimuzanira gutsindwa n’urubanza." 
1Corinthians11:30 Ni co gituma muri mwebge benshi bagira intege nke, abandi bakarwaragurika, kand’ abatari bake bakaba bārapfuye." 
1Corinthians11:31 Arikw iyo twimenye uko turi, ntidutsindwa n’urubanza." 
1Corinthians11:32 Arikw iyo dutsinzwe n’urubanza duhanwa n’Umwami, kugira ngo ntituze dutsindwe n’urubanza rudashira hamwe n’ab’ isi." 
1Corinthians11:33 Nuko, bene Data, uko mukoraniye kurya, murorērane." 
1Corinthians11:34 Umuntu ni yasonza, ararya i we, kugira ngo ntimukoranire gutsindwa n’urubanza. Ibisigaye nzobiroranya aho nzozira." 
1Corinthians12:1 Bene Data, ivy’ ingabire za Mpwemu, singomba ko mutabimenya." 
1Corinthians12:2 Murazi yuko mukir’ injabuka mwakwegwa, mukaja ku bigirwamana bitazi kuvuga, nk’uko mwabikwegeweko." 
1Corinthians12:3 Ni co gituma mbamenyesha yukw ata muntu avugishwa na Mpwemu w’Imana, avuga ati Yesu n’ikivume: kand’ ata muntu ashobora kuvuga, ati Yesu n’Uhoraho, atabivugishijwe na Mpwemu Yera." 
1Corinthians12:4 Yamara harih’ ingabire z’uburyo bginshi, ariko Mpwemu n’umwe." 
1Corinthians12:5 Kandi har’ amabango menshi, arik’ Umwami n’umwe." 
1Corinthians12:6 Kandi harih’ uburyo bginshi bgo gukora, arikw Imana n’imwe, ikorera vyose muri bose." 
1Corinthians12:7 Yamara, umuntu wese ahabga ikimwerekanako Mpwemu, kugira ngo bigire ikimazi." 
1Corinthians12:8 Kuk’ umwe aheshwa na Mpwemu ijambo ry’ubgenge, uwundi agaheshwa n’uwo Mpwemu ijambo ryo kumenya," 
1Corinthians12:9 uwundi agaheshwa n’uwo Mpwemu ukwizera, uwundi agaheshwa n’uwo Mpwemu umwe ingabire zo gukiza indwara," 
1Corinthians12:10 uwundi agahābga gukora ibitangaza, uwundi agahabga kuvugishwa n’Imana, uwundi agahabga kurobanura impwemu, uwundi agahabga kuvuga indimi nyinshi, uwundi agahabga gusobanura indimi:" 
1Corinthians12:11 arikw ivyo vyose uwo Mpwemu umwe ni we abikorera muri bo, agabira umuntu wese ukw agomba." 
1Corinthians12:12 Nk’uk’ umubiri ar’ umwe, ukagira ingingo nyinshi, kand’ ingingo z’umubiri zose nah’ ari nyinshi ar’ umubiri umwe, ni ko na Kristo ari." 
1Corinthians12:13 Kuko muri Mpwemu umwe, twese ari ho twabatijwe ngo tube umubiri umwe, naho boba Abayuda cank’ Abagiriki, naho boba abagurano cank’ abidegemvya. Kandi twese twanyweshejwe Mpwemu umwe." 
1Corinthians12:14 Umubiri s’urugingo rumwe, ariko ni nyinshi." 
1Corinthians12:15 Ikirenge covuga, kiti Ko ntar’ ikiganza sind’ uwo ku mubiri; ivyo ntivyotuma kitaba ico ku mubiri." 
1Corinthians12:16 Kand’ ugutwi kwovuga, kuti Ko ntar’ ijisho, sind’ uwo ku mubiri; ivyo ntivyotuma kutaba ukwo ku mubiri." 
1Corinthians12:17 Iy’ umubiri wose uba ijisho, kwumva kwobaye hehe? Iyo wose uba kwumva, kumoterwa kwobaye hehe?" 
1Corinthians12:18 Ariko noneh’ Imana yashizeh’ ingingo z’umubiri, urugingo rwose aho yagomvye." 
1Corinthians12:19 Kand’ iyo zose ziba urugingo rumwe, umubiri wobaye hehe?" 
1Corinthians12:20 Ariko noneho, ingingo ni nyinshi, umubiri ukaba umwe." 
1Corinthians12:21 Ijisho ntiryoshobora kubarira ikiganza, ngo Nta co ummariye; cank’ umutwe kubarira ibirenge, ngo Nta co mummariye." 
1Corinthians12:22 Ariko bir’ ukundi rwose: ingingo z’umubiri ziyumvirwa kw ar’ iz’ intege nke inyuma y’izindi, ni zo zitōhara;" 
1Corinthians12:23 kand’ izo ku mubiri twiyumvira ko zidafise icubahiro, ni zo zirushiriza kuronka icubahiro: kand’ ingingo zacu ziteye isoni ni zo zirushiriza gusharizwa." 
1Corinthians12:24 Yamar’ izidateye isoni ntizirinda kwambikwa: arikw Imana yafatanije umubiri hamwe, urugingo rukennye icubahiro iruha icubahiro kirushiriza," 
1Corinthians12:25 kugira ng’umubiri ntiwireme ibice, arikw ingingo zibabarane kumwe." 
1Corinthians12:26 Kand’ urugingo rumwe iyo rubabaye, ingingo zose zirababazanywa na rwo: cank’ iy’ urugingo rumwe ruhawe icubahiro, ingingo zose zihimbaranwa na rwo." 
1Corinthians12:27 Namwe mur’ umubiri wa Kristo, kand’ umuntu wese wo muri mwebge n’urugingo rwawo."
