1Corinthians12:28 Kand’ Imana yabanje gushira mw ishengero bamwe kuba intumwa, maz’ aba kabiri ibashiraho kuba abavugishwa na yo, maz’ aba gatatu, ibashiraho kuba abigisha, maz’ ishirah’ abakora ibitangaza, maz’ ishirah’ abāhawe ingabire zo gukiza indwara, n’abāhawe gufasha abandi, n’abāhawe kurōngōra, n’abāhawe kuvuga indimi nyinshi." 
1Corinthians12:29 Mbega bose n’intumwa? Bose n’abavugishwa n’Imana? Bose n’abigisha? Bose bakora ibitangaza? 
1Corinthians12:30 Bose bafise ingabire zo gukiza indwara? Bose bavuga izindi ndimi? Bose basobanura indimi? 
1Corinthians12:31 Ariko mwifuze cane ingabire ziruta izindi. Kandi ndabereka inzira irushiriza kuba nziza. 
1Corinthians13:1 Naho novuga indimi z’abantu n’iz’ abamarayika, ariko ntagira urukundo, noba ncitse umuringa uvuga, cank’ icuma kivuzwa kigasāma." 
1Corinthians13:2 Kandi naho nogira ingabire yo kuvugishwa n’Imana, nkamenya amabanga yose, n’ubgenge bgose, kandi naho nogira ukwizera kwose, ngashobora gukūrah’ imisozi, ariko ntagira urukundo, noba nd’ ubusa." 
1Corinthians13:3 Kandi naho notanga ivyanje vyose, ngo ngaburire aboro, kandi naho notanga umubiri wanje ngo nturirwe, ariko ntagira urukundo, nta co vyommarira." 
1Corinthians13:4 Urukundo rurihangana, rugira neza, urukundo ntirugira ishari, urukundo ntirwihayagiza, ntirwihimbaza," 
1Corinthians13:5 ntirukora ibiteye isoni, ntirurondera ivyarwo, ntirwiciraho, ntirwiyumvira ikibi ku bantu," 
1Corinthians13:6 ntirunezererwa ukugabitanya kw’abandi, ariko runezeranwa n’ukuri:" 
1Corinthians13:7 rurenzako muri vyose, rwizera vyose, rwizigira vyose, rwihanganira vyose." 
1Corinthians13:8 Urukundo nta ho rushira. Ukuvugishwa n’Imana kuzokūrwaho, ukuvuga izindi ndimi kuzogira iherezo, ubgenge buzokūrwaho." 
1Corinthians13:9 Kuko tuzi agace, kandi tuvugishwa n’Imana agace," 
1Corinthians13:10 ariko, ah’ igihingūye kizoshikira, ivy’ agace bizokūrwaho." 
1Corinthians13:11 Nkir’u mwana mutoya, navuga rwana, niyumvira rwana, nibgira rwana. Mmaze gukura, mva mu vy’ ubgana." 
1Corinthians13:12 Kuk’ ubu turābira mu cirore ivyijiji, arikw ico gihe tuzorāba nk’abarābana imbonankubone. Ubu nzi agace, arikw ico gihe nzomenya rwose nk’uko namenywe rwose." 
1Corinthians13:13 None rero hagumyeh’ ukwizera, n’ivyizigiro, n’urukundo, ivyo ukw ari bitatu: arikw ikibiruta n’urukundo." 
1Corinthians14:1 Mwirukire urukundo: yamara mwifuze cane ingabire za Mpwemu, cane‐cane kuvugishwa n’Imana." 
1Corinthians14:2 Ūvuga ururimi rutamenyekana s’abantu abarira, arikw abarira Imana, kukw ata wuvyumva, ariko mu mpwemu avuga amabanga." 
1Corinthians14:3 Arik’ ūvugishwa n’Imana, abarira abantu ivyo kubakomeza n’ivyo kubahanūra n’ivyo kubirura." 
1Corinthians14:4 Ūvuga ururimi rutamenyekana ariyubaka, arik’ ūvugishwa n’Imana yubaka ishengero." 
1Corinthians14:5 Nagomba ko mwese muvuga indimi zitamenyekana, arikw ikirushiriza, ko muvugishwa n’Imana. Ūvugishwa na yo aruta ūvuga indimi zitamenyekana, shiti yobisobanura, kugira ngw ishengero ryubakwe." 
1Corinthians14:6 Ariko none, bene Data, ni naza i wanyu mvuga indimi zitamenyekana, nzobamarira iki, ni ntababarira ivyo mpishuriwe, cank’ ivyo mpawe kumenya, canke kuvugishwa n’Imana, canke kwigisha?" 
1Corinthians14:7 Kandi n’ibidafise ubugingo biri n’amajwi: umwironge iy’ udatandukanije ijwi, cank’ inanga, bomenya bate irivuzwa cank’ iricurarangwa?" 
1Corinthians14:8 Kandi n’inzamba yovuga ijwi ritamenyekana, ni nde yokwitegura gutabara?" 
1Corinthians14:9 Namwe n’uko, ururimi rwanyu ni rutavuga ibimenyekana, bazomenya bate ivyo muvuga? Kuko muzoba muvuga ibitwarwa n’umuyaga." 
1Corinthians14:10 Amajwi yo mw isi, nah’ ari menshi ate, nta ridafise uko risobanurwa:" 
1Corinthians14:11 nukw iyo ntamenye ukw ijwi risobanurwa, uno avuga mba ndamubereye ūdebagura, kandi nanje, uno avuga aba ambereye ūdebagura." 
1Corinthians14:12 Namwe n’uko, kuko mwifuza ivya Mpwemu, kuremesha ishengero kube ari kwo gutuma mugomba kurushiriza." 
1Corinthians14:13 Nuk’ ūvuga ururimi rutamenyekana asenge, kugira ngw ahabge kubisobanura." 
1Corinthians14:14 Iyo nsenga mu rurimi rutamenyekana, impwemu yanje irasenga, arik’ ubgenge bganje buragumbaha." 
1Corinthians14:15 Nuko ngire nte? Nzosengesha impwemu yanje, ariko kandi nzosengesha n’ubgenge: nzoririmbisha impwemu yanje, ariko kandi nzoririmbisha n’ubgenge." 
1Corinthians14:16 Iy’ ushimye Imana, ushimishije impwemu yawe yonyene, mbeg’ ūri ku ruhande rw’abatungu yoshobora ate kuvuga, ati Amen, ni waheza gushima, kand’ atamenye ic’ uvuze?" 
1Corinthians14:17 N’ukuri kubgawe ushima neza, ariko wa wundi ntakomezwa." 
1Corinthians14:18 Nshimira Imana yuko mbarusha mwese kuvuga indimi zitamenyekana: 
1Corinthians14:19 ariko mw ishengero nopfuma mvugisha ubgenge bganje amajambo atanu, kugira ngo nigishe n’abandi, hako mvuga amajambo ibihumbi cumi mu rurimi rutamenyekana." 
1Corinthians14:20 Bene Data, ntimube abana mu bgenge, ariko mube ibitazi mu bibi; ariko mu bgenge mube abagabo." 
1Corinthians14:21 Mu vyagezwe handitswe, ngo Nzovuganira n’ubu bgoko mu kanwa k’abavuga izindi ndimi no mu kanwa k’abanyamahanga, ariko naho nzovuga ntyo, ntibazonyumvira, ni k’Uhoraho agize." 
1Corinthians14:22 Ni co gituma indimi zitamenyekana zitabera abizera ikimenyetso, ariko zikibera abatizera: ariko kuvugishwa n’Imana kwo, ntikubera abatizera ikimenyetso ariko kukibera abizera." 
1Corinthians14:23 Nukw ishengero ryose, iyo rikoraniye hamwe, bose bakavuga indimi zitamenyekana, hakinjiramw’ abatungu cank’ abatizera, ntibovuga yuko mwasaze?" 
1Corinthians14:24 Ariko bose iyo bavugishwa n’Imana, hakinjiramw’ ūtizera cank’ umutungu, yomenyeshwa ivyaha vyiwe na bose, agahinyuzwa na bose," 
1Corinthians14:25 ibihishijwe mu mutima wiwe bigaseruka; nukw akubika inda, agasenga Imana, akātura yukw Imana iri muri mwebge vy’ukuri." 
1Corinthians14:26 Ni bite ga bene Data? Iyo mukoranye, umuntu wese aba afise indirimbo, cank’ amajambo yo kwigisha, cank’ amajambo ahishuriwe, cank’ ururimi rutamenyekana, cank’ amajambo yo kurusobanura. Vyose bikorwe kugira ngw abantu bakomezwe." 
1Corinthians14:27 Ni haba harih’ abavuga ururimi rutamenyekana, havuge babiri canke batatu, badasāga, kandi bavuge bakurikirana, hagire ūbisobanura." 
1Corinthians14:28 Ariko ni haba hatarih’ ūbisobanura, ūvuga urutamenyekana acereze mw ishengero, yibgire, kand’ abgire Imana." 
1Corinthians14:29 Kandi n’abavugishwa n’Imana bavuge ari babiri canke batatu, abandi babigenzure." 
1Corinthians14:30 Arik’ uwundi yicaye ni yagira ic’ ahishūrirwa, uwabanje ahore." 
1Corinthians14:31 Kuko mwese mushobora kuvugishwa n’Imana umwe‐umwe, ngo bose bige, bose bahanūrwe." 
1Corinthians14:32 Impwemu z’abavugishwa n’Imana ziganzwa na bo: 
1Corinthians14:33 kukw Imana atar’ iy’ umuvurungano, ariko n’iy’ amahoro. Nk’uko bimeze mu mashengero yose y’abera," 
1Corinthians14:34 abagore bacereze mw ishengero, kuko batemererwa kuvuga. Ariko baganzwe, nk’ukw ivyagezwe na vyo bivuga." 
1Corinthians14:35 Kandi ni hagira ico bagomba kwiga, babarize abagabo babo i muhira, kuko biteye isoni k’umugore avuga mw ishengero." 
1Corinthians14:36 Mbega kuri mwebge ni ho ijambo ry’Imana ryandurutse? Canke ryashitse kuri mwebge mwenyene? 
1Corinthians14:37 Ni hagira umuntu yiyumvira kw ar’ ūvugishwa n’Imana, canke kw ar’ uw’ impwemu, amenye ivyo mbandikiye yukw ar’ icagezwe c’Umwami wacu." 
1Corinthians14:38 Ariko, namba har’ umuntu atabimenye, ntakabimenye." 
1Corinthians14:39 Nuko, bene Data, mwifuze cane kuvugishwa n’Imana, kandi ntimubuze kuvuga indimi zitamenyekana." 
1Corinthians14:40 Ariko vyose bitungane neza, birorane." 
1Corinthians15:1 Bene Data, ndabamenyesha ubutumwa bgiza, ubgo nababariye, namwe mukabgākīra, kandi mukabuhagararamwo," 
1Corinthians15:2 kandi mugakizwa na bgo, asangwa mukibufashe nk’uko nabubabgiye, shiti mwoba mwizereye ubusa." 
1Corinthians15:3 Kuko nabanje kubashikiriza ico nanje nahawe, yuko Kristo yapfiriye ivyaha vyacu, nk’ukw ivyanditswe bivuga," 
1Corinthians15:4 agahambga, akazuka ku musi ugira gatatu, nk’ukw ivyanditswe bivuga;" 
1Corinthians15:5 akiyereka Kefa, maz’ akiyereka bamwe cumi na babiri," 
1Corinthians15:6 akongera akiyerekera hamwe bene Data basāga amajana atanu, mur’ abo abenshi baracariho n’ubu, ariko bamwe bārasinziriye:" 
1Corinthians15:7 maze yiyereka Yakobo, hanyuma yiyereka intumwa zose." 
1Corinthians15:8 Maze hanyuma ya bose nanje aranyiyereka ndi nk’umwana w’icenda. 
1Corinthians15:9 Mbere jewe nd’ inyuma y’izindi ntumwa zose, sinkwiye no kwitwa intumwa, kuko nahama ishengero ry’Imana." 
1Corinthians15:10 Arik’ ubuntu bg’Imana ni bgo bgatumye mba uko ndi, kand’ ubuntu bgayo nagiriwe ntibgabaye ubg’ ubusa, ariko natamye kurusha bose; ariko si jewe yamara n’ubuntu bg’Imana bgari kumwe nanje." 
1Corinthians15:11 Nukw ari jewe ar’ abo, ivyo ni vyo tubabarira, namwe ni vyo mwizeye." 
1Corinthians15:12 Ariko, ko Kristo avugwa ko yazutse mu bapfuye, bamwe muri mwebge bavuga bate yukw ata wuzuka?" 
1Corinthians15:13 Asangw’ ata wuzuka, na Kristo ntarakazuka:" 
1Corinthians15:14 kand’ asangwa Kristo atāzutse, ivyo twigisha n’ivy’ ubusa, n’ukwizera kwanyu n’ukw’ ubusa." 
1Corinthians15:15 Natwe twoba tubonetse ko tur’ abashingira Imana intahe y’ikinyoma, kuko twayishingiye intahe yuko yazuye Kristo, uwo itāzuye, namb’ abapfuye batazuka." 
1Corinthians15:16 Asangw’ abapfuye batazuka na Kristo ntarakazuka: 
1Corinthians15:17 arikw asangwa Kristo atāzutse, ukwizera kwanyu n’ukw’ ubusa, muracari mu vyaha vyanyu." 
1Corinthians15:18 Kand’ asangwa bimeze birtyo, n’abāsinziririye muri Kristo barayogeye." 
1Corinthians15:19 Asangwa mur’ ubu bugingo bgonyene ari ho twizigirira Kristo, turusha abandi bantu bose kuba abagowe." 
1Corinthians15:20 Ariko noneho Kristo yarazutse mu bapfuye, ni we yashurije abāsinziriye." 
1Corinthians15:21 Kuko nk’uk’ urupfu rwazanywe n’umuntu, n’ukuzuka kw’abapfuye kwazanywe n’umuntu." 
1Corinthians15:22 Nk’uko Adamu yandukije bose gupfa, ni ko muri Kristo bose bazohindurwa bazima." 
1Corinthians15:23 Arik’ umuntu wese mu mwanya wiwe: Kristo ni we mushuzo, maz’ aba Kristo bazobonerwa bazuke, ah’ azozira;" 
1Corinthians15:24 iherezo rizoca rishika, ah’ azoshikiriza Imana ubgami, ni yo Data wa twese, ni yamara gukūrah’ ubukuru bgose, n’ububasha bgose, n’ubushobozi bgose." 
1Corinthians15:25 Kuko guhangama azokwama ahangamye gushitsa ah’ azoshirira abansi biwe bose musi y’ibirenge vyiwe. 
1Corinthians15:26 Urupfu ni we mumenja w’imperēra azorandurwa. 
1Corinthians15:27 Kuko handitswe, ngo Yamuhaye kuganza vyose, ibishira musi y’ibirenge vyiwe. Ariko kw ivuga, it’ Ahawe kuganza vyose; biraboneka yukw Iyamuhaye kuganza vyose itabiharūrwamwo." 
1Corinthians15:28 Ariko ni yamara gushikirizwa inganji ya vyose, ni ho n’Umwana ubgiwe azoganzwa n’Iyamuhaye inganji ya vyose, ngw Imana ibe vyose muri vyose." 
1Corinthians15:29 Cank’ ababatizwa mu gishingo c’abapfuye bazobamarira iki? Asangw’ abapfuye batazurwa na mba, n’iki gituma bababatirizwa?" 
1Corinthians15:30 Natwe n’iki gituma twama turi mw irinde? 
1Corinthians15:31 Uko bukeye ndapfa, indahiro ndahiye ni mwebge vyirato vyanje, ivyo mfise muri Kristo Yesu Umwami wacu." 
1Corinthians15:32 Asangwa narwaniye n’ibikōko muri Efeso, ndi mu buryo bg’abantu gusa, bimmarira iki? Namb’ abapfuye batazurwa, ni twīrīre, twinywere, kukw ejo tuzopfa." 
1Corinthians15:33 Ntimuzimire: kubana n’ababi kwonona ingeso nziza. 
1Corinthians15:34 Mushire ibirāre, mugororoke, ntimukore ivyaha: kuko bamwe batazi Imana. Mbivugiye kubatētereza." 
1Corinthians15:35 Arik’ umuntu yobaza, at’ Abapfuye bazurwa bate, kandi baza bafise umubiri ki?" 
1Corinthians15:36 Wa gipfu we, ic’ ubiba ntikimera kitabanje gupfa." 
1Corinthians15:37 Kand’ ic’ ubiba, ntubiba umutumba uzohaba, arik’ ubiba akabuto uko kari, ari nk’ak’ ingano, cank’ akandi kose." 
1Corinthians15:38 Arikw Imana igaha umutumba, nk’uko yagomvye, kand’ akabuto kose igaha umutumba wako ukwako." 
1Corinthians15:39 Inyama zose si zimwe; iz’ abantu zir’ ukwazo, n’iz ibikōko zir’ ukwazo, n’iz’ inyoni n’ibisīga zir’ ukwazo, n’iz’ ifi zir’ ukwazo." 
1Corinthians15:40 Kandi har’ imitumba yo kw ijuru n’imitumba yo kw isi: arik’ ubgiza bg’iyo kw ijuru bur’ ukwabgo; n’ubg’ iyo kw isi bur’ ukwabgo. 
1Corinthians15:41 Ubgiza bg’izuba bur’ ukwabgo, n’ubgiza bg’ukwezi bur’ ukwabgo, n’ubgiza bg’inyenyeri bur’ ukwabgo: kand’ inyenyeri ntinganya ubgiza na mugenzi wayo." 
1Corinthians15:42 N’ukuzuka kw’abapfuye ni nk’uko: habibga ikibora, hazurwa ikitabora;" 
1Corinthians15:43 habibga igikēngērwa, hazurwa ic’ icubahiro; habibga ikinyantege nke hazurwa ic’ inkomezi;" 
1Corinthians15:44 habibga umubiri w’inyama, hazurwa umubiri w’impwemu. Asangwa harih’ umubiri w’inyama hariho kandi n’uw’ impwemu." 
1Corinthians15:45 Kand’ uko ni ko handitswe, ng’ Umuntu wa mbere Adamu yabaye ūfise ubugingo; Adamu wo hanyuma yabaye impwemu itanga ubugingo." 
1Corinthians15:46 Arikw ic’ impwemu si co kibanza, yamar’ ic’ inyama ni co kibanza, kigaherukirwa n’ic’ impwemu." 
1Corinthians15:47 Umuntu wa mbere yandurutse mw ivu, n’uw’ umukungugu: umuntu wa kabiri yandurutse mw ijuru." 
1Corinthians15:48 Nk’uk’ uw’ umukungugu ari, ni ko n’ab’ umukungugu bandi bari: kandi nk’uk’ uw’ ijuru ari, ni ko n’ab’ ijuru bandi bari." 
1Corinthians15:49 Kandi nk’uko twambaye ishusho y’uw’ umukungugu, ni ko tuzokwambara n’ishusho y’uw’ ijuru." 
1Corinthians15:50 Ariko bene Data, ico mvuga n’iki, yukw ab’inyama n’amaraso badashobora kuragwa ubgami bg’Imana, kand’ ibibora bitaragwa ibitabora." 
1Corinthians15:51 Ehe, ndababarira akabanga: ntituzosinzira twese, ariko twese tuzohindurwa," 
1Corinthians15:52 mu kanya gato, mu kanya nk’ako gukubita ingohe, ah’ inzamba y’iherezo izovugira. Kukw inzamba izovuga, abapfuye bakazurwa batagishobora kubora, natwe tuzohindurwa." 
1Corinthians15:53 Kuk’ uyu mubiri ubora ukwiye kuzokwambara ukutabora, kand’ uyu mubiri upfa ukwiye kuzokwambara ukudapfa." 
1Corinthians15:54 Ariko, uyu ubora ni wamara kwambara ukutabora, n’uyu upfa ni wamara kwambara ukudapfa, ni ho hazoshika rya jambo ryanditswe, ng’Urupfu rumizwe n’intsinzi." 
1Corinthians15:55 Wa rupfu we, intsinzi yawe iri hehe? Wa rupfu we, uruboyi rwawe ruri hehe?" 
1Corinthians15:56 Ivyaha ni vyo ruboyi rw’urupfu, kand’ ubushobozi bg’ivyaha n’ivyagezwe." 
1Corinthians15:57 Arikw Imana ishimwe, iduha gutsinda kubg’ Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo." 
1Corinthians15:58 Nuko bene Data nkunda, mukomere ntimunyiganyige, murushirize imisi yose gukora ibikorwa vy’Umwami wacu, kuko muzi yuk’ ubutame bganyu atar’ ubg’ ubusa mu Mwami." 
1Corinthians16:1 Nuko ku vyo gukoranya ibitabara abera, nk’uko nageze amashengero y’i Galatiya, abe ari ko namwe mukora." 
1Corinthians16:2 Ku wa mbere wose w’imisi ndwi, umuntu wese muri mwebge abīke i we ibimuhaye uburyo, nk’ukw atunze, kugira ngw aho nzozira ntihabe ari ho amashikanwa azokoranirizwa." 
1Corinthians16:3 Kand’ aho nzoshikira, abo muzoshima, nzobatuma mbahaye ivyete, kugira ngo bajane ivy’ ubuntu bganyu i Yerusalemu." 
1Corinthians16:4 Kandi namba nzoba nkwiye kugenda nanje, tuzojana." 
1Corinthians16:5 Ariko nzoza i wanyu, ni namara guca i Makedoniya; kuko nzorinda gucayo." 
1Corinthians16:6 Ariko kumbure nzomarana namwe imisi, canke nzomara n’urushana, kugira ngo mumperekeze, munsezere neza aho nzoja hose." 
1Corinthians16:7 Singomba ko tubonana none mbakubise rurabge, ariko nizigira kuzomarana namwe imisi, Umwami wacu ni yankundira." 
1Corinthians16:8 Ariko nzotebera muri Efeso gushitsa kuri Pentekote: 
1Corinthians16:9 kuko nugururiwe urugi runini ruja mu bikorwa bikomeye, kand’ abarwanizi bakaba benshi." 
1Corinthians16:10 Timoteyo ni yaramuka aje i wanyu, muze mumubabare kugira ngw abane namwe ata bgoba; kukw akora igikorwa c’Umwami wacu nkanje." 
1Corinthians16:11 Nuko ntihaze hagire ūmukēngēra, ariko muze mumuherekeze mumusezere amahoro, az’ ansange ino, kuko niteze kw azozanana na bene Data." 
1Corinthians16:12 Arikw ivya Apolo mwene Data, naramwinginze cane ngw aze i wanyu, az’ azanane na bene Data abo; ntiyakunda na gatoya kuza none, arikw azoza, ni yabona uburyo." 
1Corinthians16:13 Mwame mugavye, mushikame mu kwizera, mube abagabo, mugire inkomezi." 
1Corinthians16:14 Ivyo mukora vyose mubikorane urukundo. 
1Corinthians16:15 Nuko ndabinginze, bene Data, murazi abo kwa Stefana, kw ari bo bāshuje mu Banyakaya, kandi kw ari bo bītangiye gukorera abera." 
1Corinthians16:16 Nuko namwe mugāmburukire abameze bartyo, n’uwundi wese afatanije n’abandi mur’ ico gikorwa, agatama." 
1Corinthians16:17 Birannezereye ko Stefana na Forutunato na Akayiko baje; bāmmaze inkumbu nari mbafitiye," 
1Corinthians16:18 kuko bāhēmbūye umutima wanje, bo n’uwanyu: mwame mwibuka abameze bartyo." 
1Corinthians16:19 Abo mu mashengero yo muri Asiya barabaganūtsa. Akwila na Purisikila barabaganutsa cane mu Mwami wacu, bo n’ishengero ryo mu nzu yabo." 
1Corinthians16:20 Bene Data bose barabaganūtsa. Muramukanishe kugumbirana kwera. 
1Corinthians16:21 Uku ni kwo gutasha kwanje Paulo, kwanditswe n’ukwanje kuboko." 
1Corinthians16:22 Ni hagira umuntu adakunda Umwami wacu, arakavumwa. Maran ata." 
1Corinthians16:23 Ubuntu bg’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo bubane namwe. 
1Corinthians16:24 Urukundo rwanje rubane namwe mwese muri Kristo Yesu. Amen. 
2Corinthians1:1 Paulo, intumwa ya Kristo Yesu, nk’ukw Imana yagomvye, na Timoteyo mwene Data, turabandikiye abo mw ishengero ry’Imana ry’i Korinto, n’abera bose bari muri Akaya hose:" 
2Corinthians1:2 ubuntu bube muri mwebge n’amahoro, biva ku Mana Data wa twese no ku Mwami Yesu Kristo." 
2Corinthians1:3 Imana y’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, ari yo Se, iragahezagirwa, Data wa twese w’imbabazi, kand’ Imana yirura imibabaro yose," 
2Corinthians1:4 itwirura mu marushwa yacu yose, kugira ngo natwe tubone uko twirura imibabaro abari mu marushwa yose, tuyibiruza uko natwe twiruwe n’Imana." 
2Corinthians1:5 Nk’ukw ivyo Kristo yababajwe vyarushirije kutuzako, ni ko n’ukwirurwa kwacu kwarushirije kugwizwa na Kristo." 
2Corinthians1:6 Iyo tubabazwa, kuba ar’ ukugira ngo bibazanire ukwirurwa, bo n’agakiza: kand’ iyo twirurwa, kuba ar’ ukugira ngo bibazanire ukwirurwa nyene, guserukira mu kwihanganira imibabaro imwe n’iyo natwe tubabazwa." 
2Corinthians1:7 Kand’ ivyo tubazigako birashikamye, kuko tuzi yuko, ko musangiye natwe iyo mibabaro, dusangiye n’ukuyirurwa." 
2Corinthians1:8 Kuko bene Data, tutagomba yuko mutamenya amarushwa yatubayeko muri Asiya, ko twaremerewe cane, biruta uko dushobora, bigatuma twihebura ko tutagikiza amagara yacu:" 
2Corinthians1:9 kandi tumenyeshwa mu mitima yuko duciriwekw iteka ryo gupfa, kugira ngo ntitwiyizigire ubgacu, ariko twizigire Imana izura abapfuye:" 
2Corinthians1:10 yadukijije urupfu rukomeye rurtyo, kand’ izodukiza; ni yo twizigira yukw izokwama irudukiza," 
2Corinthians1:11 namwe muhūje imitima yo kudufasha mudusengera, ngw ingabire twaheshejwe na benshi, benshi bayishimire Imana kubgacu." 
2Corinthians1:12 Kuk’ ukwirata kwacu ar’ uku, kand’ ijwi ryo mu mitima yacu rirabishingira intahe: ingeso twagirira mw isi, kandi cane‐cane muri mwebge, zar’ ukwera, n’imitima itagira ubugunge iva ku Mana, atari mu bgenge bg’abantu, ariko mu buntu bg’Imana." 
2Corinthians1:13 Kukw ata bindi tubandikira, atar’ ivyo nyene musoma kandi mwemera, kandi nishimiye ko muzovyemera gushitsa kw iherezo," 
2Corinthians1:14 nk’uko mwatwemeye agace, yuko tur’ ivyirato vyanyu, nk’uko namwe muzoba ivyacu ku musi w’Umwami wacu Yesu." 
2Corinthians1:15 Kandi nk’uko nizigiye ivyo, nagira ngo nzobanza kuza i wanyu, ngo muhabge ubuntu ubugira kabiri," 
2Corinthians1:16 no kubacako nja i Makedoniya, nkagaruka i wanyu mvuye i Makedoniya, ngo mumperekeze, munsezere neza nja i Yudaya." 
2Corinthians1:17 Nukw aho nagomba gukora ntyo, mbega narahindagurika? Cank’ ivyo ngabira, mbigabira mbgirijwe n’akameremere kanje, ngo nībūranye, nt’ Ego, ego, maze nt’ Oya, oya?" 
2Corinthians1:18 Ariko nk’ukw Imana ar’ iyo kwizerwa, ijambo tubabarira ntituvuga ngw Ego, maze ng’ Oya." 
2Corinthians1:19 Umwana w’Imana Yesu Kristo, umwe twabigisha ivyiwe, twe na Siluwano na Timoteyo, ntiyar’ Ego, kandi ngw abe Oya; ariko muri we harimw’ Ego me." 
2Corinthians1:20 Ivy’ Imana yasezeranye uko bingana, muri we ni ho Ego me riri: ni co gituma ari we adutera kuvuga ngo Amen, ngw Imana ishimishwe natwe." 
2Corinthians1:21 Imana ni yo idukomezanya namwe muri Kristo, kandi ni yo yaturobanuje amavuta." 
2Corinthians1:22 Kandi ni yo yadushizekw ikimenyetso, itugwatiriza Mpwemu wayo mu mitima yacu." 
2Corinthians1:23 Arikw Imana ni yo ntanzekw icabona ku bugingo bganje, icatumye ntongera kuza i Korinto, kwar’ ukwanka kubababaza." 
2Corinthians1:24 S’uko tuganza ukwizera kwanyu, ariko dukorana namwe mu bibungura umunezero: kuk’ ukwizera ari kwo muhagazemwo." 
2Corinthians2:1 Ariko nagabiye mu mutima kutazogaruka i wanyu nzanye umubabaro. 
2Corinthians2:2 Ni nabatera umubabaro, ūzonnezereza ni nde? S’uwo nteye umubabaro nyene?" 
2Corinthians2:3 Kandi nandikiye ivyo, kugira ngw aho nzozira noye guterwa umubabaro n’abari bakwiye kunnezereza: kuko mbizigira mwese yuk’ umunezero wanje ari wo wanyu mwese." 
2Corinthians2:4 Nabandikiye mfise intuntu nyinshi, umutima wamvuyemwo, ndira amarira menshi; ntikwar’ ukugira ngo muterwe umubabaro mwebge, ariko kwar’ ukugira ngo mumenye urukundo ndushiriza kubagirira." 
2Corinthians2:5 Ariko namba har’ umuntu ateye umubabaro, si jewe awuteye, ariko ni mwebge awuteye mwese — singomba kubababaza cane, ariko bamwe n’agace." 
2Corinthians2:6 Ico gihano abenshi bāmuhannye, kiramaze k’ūmeze artyo," 
2Corinthians2:7 none ni co gituma mukwiye cane‐cane kumuharira, no kumwirura, ng’ūmeze artyo ntarengerwe n’umubabaro usāgutse." 
2Corinthians2:8 Nuko ndabinginga mukomeze urukundo kuri we. 
2Corinthians2:9 Kukw icanteye kubandikira ar’ iki: kwar’ ukugira ngo mbageze, mmenye uko muri, ko munyumvira muri vyose." 
2Corinthians2:10 Arik’ uwo muribuharire wese, nanje ndamuharira: kuko nanje ico mpariye, namba har’ ico mparira, ngihariye kubganyu, mu nyonga za Kristo," 
2Corinthians2:11 kugira ngo Satani ntaronke ic’ adutsindisha, kuko tutayobewe imigabo yiwe." 
2Corinthians2:12 Arikw aho naja i Tirowa, njanywe n’ubutumwa bgiza bga Kristo, ngasanga nugururiwe urugi mu Mwami wacu," 
2Corinthians2:13 nabuze uko nduhuka mu mutima wanje, kuko ntasanzeyo Tito mwene Data; nuko narabasezeye, nja i Makedoniya." 
2Corinthians2:14 Arikw Imana ishimwe, yama itujana nk’abafashwe mpiri muri Kristo, idutera kwerekana ubumote bgo kumumenyekanisha ahantu hose." 
2Corinthians2:15 Kuko tur’ ubumote bgiza bga Kristo ku Mana, hagati y’abariko barakira n’abariko barahona." 
2Corinthians2:16 Kur’ abo tur’ agacūku k’urupfu kazana urupfu, kuri ba bandi tur’ ubumote bg’ubugingo buzana ubugingo. Kand’ ivyo ni nde abishobora?" 
2Corinthians2:17 Kuko tutari nka bamwe benshi, bacurūrīsha ijambo ry’Imana, ariko tuvuga nk’abatagira ubugunge, bavuga ibiva ku Mana, ni ko tuvuga muri Kristo, imbere y’Imana." 
2Corinthians3:1 Mbega dutanguye kwongera kwishimagiza? Canke turinda ivyete vyo kudushimagiza, mwandikiwe canke mwanditse, nk’uko bamwe bandi bagomba?" 
2Corinthians3:2 Ni mwebge cete cacu, canditswe ku mitima yacu, ico abantu bose bamenya bagasoma." 
2Corinthians3:3 Kuko muboneka ko mur’ icete Kristo yatwandikishije, nk’ukw igikorwa cacu kiri; kitandikishijwe wino, ariko candikishijwe Mpwemu w’Imana nzima; kitanditswe ku bisate vy’amabuye, ariko canditswe ku bisate ni vyo mitima y’inyama." 
2Corinthians3:4 Uko ni ko twizigira Imana kubga Kristo," 
2Corinthians3:5 s’uko dushobora ubgacu kwiyumvira ikintu cose nk’ah’ ari twebge candurutseko, ariko dushobozwa n’Imana;" 
2Corinthians3:6 ni yo yadushoboje kuba abakozi b’isezerano risha, yamara s’abakozi b’ivyandikishijwe inyuguti, ariko n’ab’ impwemu: kukw ivyandikishijwe inyuguti vyicisha, arikw impwemu ihesha ubugingo." 
2Corinthians3:7 Yamar’ ubgo bugabuzi bgandikishijwe inyuguti zikorogoshowe mu mabuye bgaganzwa n’urupfu, naho bgari bgazananye n’ubgiza. Arik’ ubgo bgiza, naho bgagenda bushira, bgatumye Abisirayeli badashobora gutumbera mu maso ha Mose." 
2Corinthians3:8 None ko vyabaye birtyo, ubugabuzi buganzwa na Mpwemu ntiburushiriza cane kuzanana n’ubgiza?" 
2Corinthians3:9 Ubugabuzi bgo gutsindwa kw ar’ ubgiza, ubugabuzi bgo kugororoka burushiriza kugira ubgiza bg’akaburarugero." 
2Corinthians3:10 Mber’ icari gisanganywe ubgiza nta bgiza kigifise, kuko haje ubgiza bukirengeye." 
2Corinthians3:11 Igishira ko cari n’ubgiza, igihoraho kirushiriza cane kugira ubgiza." 
2Corinthians3:12 Nuko ko dufise icizigiro kingana girtyo, tuvuga tutabobotereza na gatoya," 
2Corinthians3:13 ntidusa na Mose, yitwikira mu maso, kugira ngw Abisirayeli ntibahange amaso iherezo ry’ubgariko buraherengetera." 
2Corinthians3:14 Arikw imitima yabo irakomantara. Kuko gushitsa na bugingo n’ubu, ca citwikiro kikiriho mw isomwa ry’isezerano rya kera, ntikirakūrwaho, kuko muri Kristo ari ho giherera." 
2Corinthians3:15 Ariko gushitsa n’ubu, ivya Mose iyo bisomwa ico citwikiro kiba ku mitima yabo:" 
2Corinthians3:16 yamara, iy’ umuntu ahindukiriye Umwami, ico citwikiro gica gikūrwaho." 
2Corinthians3:17 Arik’ uwo Mwami ni we Mpwemu: kand’ aho Mpwemu w’Umwami ari, ni ho haba umwidegemvyo." 
2Corinthians3:18 Tweho twese, ko tutitwikiriye mu maso, tukerekana nk’icirore ubgiza bg’Umwami, turahinduka, tugashushanywa n’iyo shusho, tukava mu bgiza tukaja mu bundi, nk’abahindurwa n’Umwami, ari we Mpwemu." 
2Corinthians4:1 Ni co gituma tutihebura, kuko dufise ubgo busuku, nk’uko twagiriwe ikigongwe." 
2Corinthians4:2 Twanse ibiteye isoni bikorerwa mu mpisho, ntitugenda mu bugunge, ntidufudika ijambo ry’Imana, ariko kwerekana ukuri ni kwo twishimagirisha mu nyonga z’Imana ku mutima w’umuntu wese." 
2Corinthians4:3 Ariko namb’ ubutumwa bgiza twahawe butwikirwa, butwikirirwa abahona," 
2Corinthians4:4 ni bo batizera, bamwe imana y’iki gihe yahumye imitima, ng’umuco ntubākire w’ubutumwa bg’ubgiza bga Kristo, ni we shusho y’Imana." 
2Corinthians4:5 Kuko tutigisha abantu ivyacu, ariko tubigisha ivya Kristo Yesu kw ari we Mwami, natwe yuko tur’ abashumba banyu kubga Yesu." 
2Corinthians4:6 Imana, imwe yavuze ng’ Umuco wāke, uvuye mu mwiza, ni yo yākiye mu mitima yacu, kwerekana umuco, ni wo kumenya ubgiza bg’Imana buri mu nyonga ha Yesu Kristo." 
2Corinthians4:7 Ariko dufise ubgo butunzi mu nzavya z’ibumba, ng’ ubushobozi buhebuje bube ubg’ Imana, butavuye kuri twebge." 
2Corinthians4:8 Dusugerezwa impande zose, ariko ntidushika mu mbombane; turazazanirwa, ariko ntituranduka umutima;" 
2Corinthians4:9 turahamwa, ariko ntiduhebga; dukubitwa hasi, ariko ntitugwaho:" 
2Corinthians4:10 imisi yose tugendana mu mubiri urupfu rwa Yesu, ng’ubugingo bga Yesu na bgo buserukire mu mubiri wacu." 
2Corinthians4:11 Kuko twebge abariho, na ntaryo dutangwa ngo dupfe baduhōra Yesu, ng’ubugingo bga Yesu na bgo buserukire mu mubiri wacu uzopfa." 
2Corinthians4:12 Nuko rer’ urupfu rukorera muri twebge, arik’ ubugingo bukorera muri mwebge." 
2Corinthians4:13 Ariko ko dufise uwo mutima wizera, uboneka mu vyanditswe, ngo Nizeye, ni co catumye mvuga; natwe nyene turizera, ni co gituma tuvuga." 
2Corinthians4:14 Kuko tuzi yukw iyazuye Umwami Yesu, natwe izotuzurana na Yesu, kand’ izomudushīra, twe namwe." 
2Corinthians4:15 Kukw ivyo vyose biba kubganyu, kugira ng’ubuntu bg’Imana bgongeranishwe n’ukugwira kw’ abantu, bugwize ishimwe, ngo ritere Imana icubahiro." 
2Corinthians4:16 Ni co gituma tutihebura; ariko, nah’ umuntu wacu wo ku rukoba arikw arabora, umuntu wacu w’imbere yama ahinduka musha uko bukeye." 
2Corinthians4:17 Kukw amarushwa yacu ahwahutse y’akanya ka none yiyongeranije cane kudushikiriza ubgiza buremereye bg’ibihe bidashira. 
2Corinthians4:18 Natwe ntiturāba ku biboneka, ariko turāba ku bitaboneka: kukw ibiboneka ar’ ivy’ igihe gito, arikw ibitaboneka bikaba ivy’ ibihe bidashira." 
2Corinthians5:1 Turazi yukw inzu y’urusago yacu yo kw isi ni yaramuka isambuwe, dufise inyubako iva ku Mana, inzu itubatswe n’amaboko, itazoshira yo mw ijuru." 
2Corinthians5:2 Kuko tunihira mur’ uru rusago, twifuza kurwambikirwakw inzu yacu izova mw ijuru," 
2Corinthians5:3 namba tuyambaye tutazosangwa twambaye ubusa. 
2Corinthians5:4 Kuko twebge abari mur’ uru rusago tuniha turemerewe, s’uko tugomba kwamburwa, ariko tugomba kwambikirwa kuri rwo, ngw igipfa kimirwe n’ubugingo." 
2Corinthians5:5 Kand’ iyaturoranije kubg’ ico nyene n’Imana, iyatugwatirije Mpwemu." 
2Corinthians5:6 Ni co gituma na ntaryo turinda mu mutima, kandi tumenya yukw iyo tur’ i wacu mu mubiri tuba tugerereye kure y’Umwami wacu —" 
2Corinthians5:7 kuko tugenda turōngōrwa n’ukwizera, ntiturōngōrwa n’ivyo tubona —" 
2Corinthians5:8 ego me turinda mu mutima, kand’ ico turushiriza gukunda ngiki: n’ukugerēra kure y’umubiri, tukaba i wacu ku Mwami wacu." 
2Corinthians5:9 Kandi ni co gituma tugira umwete wo kumunezereza, iyo tur’ i wacu mu mubiri, cank’ iyo tugerereye kure y’umubiri." 
2Corinthians5:10 Kuko twese tutazobura kugaragarizwa imbere y’intebe y’amateka ya Kristo, kugira ng’umuntu wese ahabge ibihwanye n’ico yakoze akiri mu mubiri, ari ciza ari kibi." 
2Corinthians5:11 Nuko kuko tuzi ingen’ ugutinya Umwami wacu kumeze, twemeza abantu, arikw Imana turayigaragarira: kandi rero nizigiye yuko tugaragarira n’imitima yanyu." 
2Corinthians5:12 Ntitwongera kwishimagiza kuri mwebge, ariko tubaha inyanduruko y’ingene mwokwirata kubgacu, kugira ngo mubone ivyo mwokwishura abirata ivyo ku rukoba, batirata ivyo mu mutima." 
2Corinthians5:13 Namba dusaze, dusaze ivy’ Imana; namba dufise ubgenge, ni mwebge dukorera." 
2Corinthians5:14 Kuk’ urukundo rwa Kristo rutugōbēra, kand’ ico tuzi tudakekeranya n’uk’ umwe yapfiriye bose, nuko rero bose bārapfuye." 
2Corinthians5:15 Kand’ icatumye apfira bose kwar’ ukugira ngw abariho babeho batacinezereza, ariko babeho banezereza uwabapfiriye, akabazukira." 
2Corinthians5:16 Ni co gituma uhereye none tutakigira uwo tumenya ku vyo ku rukoba; naho twari tuzi Kristo mu vy’ umubiri, ariko none ntitukimumenya durtyo." 
2Corinthians5:17 Nuko rer’ umuntu wese iy’ ari muri Kristo, aba ar’ icaremwe gisha: ivya kera biba bihise, vyose biba bicitse bisha." 
2Corinthians5:18 Arikw ivyo vyose biva ku Mana, yatwiyujujeko kubga Kristo, ikaduha igikorwa co kugabura umwuzuzo," 
2Corinthians5:19 ni kwo kuvuga yukw Imana yari muri Kristo yiyuzuza n’abari mw isi, ntiyabaharūrakw ibicumuro vyabo, kandi yatubīkije ijambo ry’umwuzuzo." 
2Corinthians5:20 Ni co gituma tur’ intumwa mu gishingo ca Kristo, Imana isa n’ībingingira muri twebge. Turabinginga mu gishingo ca Kristo, mwuzure n’Imana." 
2Corinthians5:21 Umwe atigeze kumenya icaha, Imana yamuhinduye icaha kubgacu, kugira ngo muri we duhinduke ukugororoka kw’Imana." 
2Corinthians6:1 Kandi ko dukorana na yo, turabinginga, ntimuhērwe ubuntu bg’Imana gupfa ubusa:" 
2Corinthians6:2 kuko yavuze, iti Mu gihe co kwemererwamwo ndakwumvise, No ku musi wo gukirizwako ndagutabaye. Ehe none n’igihe co kwemererwamwo, ehe none n’umusi wo gukirizwako." 
2Corinthians6:3 Kandi ntitugira ico tuzana gitsitaza mu kintu na kimwe, kugira ngo kugabura ivy’ Imana kwacu ntikugawe." 
2Corinthians6:4 Ariko twishimagiza muri vyose nk’abakozi b’Imana, twihangana cane mu marushwa, mu mibabaro, mu vyago," 
2Corinthians6:5 mu bimoko, mu mabohero, mu migūmūko, mu butame, mu kurāra maso, mu kwirirwa ubusa," 
2Corinthians6:6 mu kugira umutima utanduye, mu kugira ubgenge, mu kutarambirwa, mu kuba inda nziza, muri Mpwemu Yera, mu rukundo rutar’ uruheyiheyi," 
2Corinthians6:7 mw ijambo ry’ukuri, mu bushobozi bg’Imana, dufise ibirwanishwa vy’ukugororoka vyo mu kuryo n’ivyo mu kubamfu;" 
2Corinthians6:8 mu cubahiro no mu gakēngērwe, mu mugayo no mw ishimwe; twiyumvirwa nk’abanyabinyoma, ariko tur’ abanyakuri;" 
2Corinthians6:9 twiyumvirwa nk’abatamenyekana, ariko turi ba rurangiranwa; tuboneka nk’abagira bapfe, ariko rāba, turi bazima; tuboneka nk’abahanwa, ariko ntitwicwa;" 
2Corinthians6:10 tuboneka nk’abababara, ariko tunezerwa imisi yose; tuboneka nk’aboro, ariko dutungisha benshi; tuboneka nk’abatagira ico batunze, yamara dutunze vyose." 
2Corinthians6:11 Akanwa kacu karabasēsekariye, yemwe Bakorinto, umutima wacu urāgutse;" 
2Corinthians6:12 ntimwāgiwe muri twebge, yamara mwāgiwe mu mitima yanyu." 
2Corinthians6:13 Nuko ndababgira nk’abana banje, namwe ni mwāguke, mwishure nk’uko mwagiriwe." 
2Corinthians6:14 Ntimwifatanye n’abatizera, kand’ ata co musangiye: ukugororoka n’ukugabitanya bifatana bite? Cank’ umuco n’umwiza bifatanya bite?" 
2Corinthians6:15 Kandi Kristo ahūriye hehe na Beliyari? Cank’ uwizera n’ūtizera basangiye iki? 
2Corinthians6:16 Kand’ urusengero rw’Imana ruhūza rute n’ibigirwamana? Kuko twebge tur’ urusengero rw’Imana nzima: nk’ukw Imana yavuze, iti Nzogerēra muri bo, nzogendera muri bo, Mbe Imana yabo, na bo babe abantu banje." 
2Corinthians6:17 Nuko muve hagati ya ba bandi, Mubītandukanyeko, ni k’Uhoraho agize, Kandi ntimugakore ku kintu gihumanya na kimwe; Nanje nzobākira," 
2Corinthians6:18 Kandi nzobabera So, Namwe muzombera abahungu n’abakobga, Ni k’Uhoraho ashobora vyose agize." 
2Corinthians7:1 Nuko bakundwa, ko dufise ivyo vyasezeranywe, twiyuhagire ubuhumane bgose bg’umubiri n’ubg’ umutima, kuba abera tugushikishe kwubaha Imana." 
2Corinthians7:2 Muduhe ikibanza mu mitima yanyu; nta we twagiriye nabi, nta we twononye, nta we twagunze." 
2Corinthians7:3 Simbivugiye kubagaya; kuko mmaze kuvuga yuko muri mu mitima yacu, ngo dupfane kandi ngo tubaneho." 
2Corinthians7:4 Mvuga ntababembeteranyako na mba, ndabirata cane. Nuzuye ihūmure, ndushiriza kunezerwa mu marushwa yacu yose." 
2Corinthians7:5 Hamwe twaja i Makedoniya umubiri wacu ntiwaribgatenzukirwe na gatoya, kuko twababajwe uburyo bgose; inyuma hār’ intambara, imbere hār’ ubgoba." 
2Corinthians7:6 Arikw Imana ihūmuriza abicisha bugufi yaduhūmurishije ukuza kwa Tito. 
2Corinthians7:7 Kandi s’ukuza kwiwe kwonyene, ariko kandi n’uguhūmurizwa yahūmurijwe namwe, n’uko yatwīgāniye inkumbu zanyu mwangiriye, n’amarira yanyu, n’ishaka mwandwanira, ni co catumye ndushiriza kunezerwa." 
2Corinthians7:8 Naho nabateje umubabaro ca cete canje, sinicuza, naho nari naricujije; kuko mbonye yukw ico cete cabateye umubabaro, naho mwawugize igihe gito gusa;" 
2Corinthians7:9 noneho ndanezerewe; sinnejerejwe n’uko mwagize umubabaro, ariko n’uk’ uwo mubabaro wabateye kwihana. Kuko mwagize umubabaro mu buryo bg’Imana, kugira ngo ntihagire ico mubura kubgacu." 
2Corinthians7:10 Umubabaro wo mu buryo bg’Imana utera ukwihana kuticuzwa, kuzana agakiza: arik’ umubabaro wo mu buryo bg’isi utera urupfu." 
2Corinthians7:11 Ntimubona uwo mubabaro wo mu buryo bg’Imana, ukuntu wabateye umwete mwinshi urtyo? Kandi ko wabateye no kwiregura, no guhigimanga, no gutinya, n’inkumbu, n’ishaka, no guhana? Muri vyose mwiyerekanye ko mwejejwe mur’ ivyo." 
2Corinthians7:12 Nuko naho nabandikiye, ivyanyandikishije s’ivy’ uwagize nabi, kandi s’ivy’ uwagiriwe nabi, ariko n’ukugira ng’umwete mutugirira werekanirwe hagati yanyu mu nyonga z’Imana." 
2Corinthians7:13 Ni co catumye duhūmurizwa. Kandi mur’ ukwo guhūmurizwa turushiriza guterwa umunezero n’umunezero wa Tito, kuk’ umutima wiwe waruhuwe namwe mwese." 
2Corinthians7:14 Namba har’ icanteye ko mbirata mbarātira Tito, ntivyantētereje: ariko nk’uko twababgiye vyose ukuri, ni ko n’ukwirata kwacu, twarātiye Tito, kwabonetse kw ar’ ukw’ ukuri." 
2Corinthians7:15 Kand’ umutima wiwe urushiriza kubagirira igishika, uko yibutse ingene mwanyumviye mwese, n’ingene mwamwākiriye mutinya, muhinda agashitsi." 
2Corinthians7:16 Nnezerewe yuko mfise umutima uremye kubg’ ivyanyu vyose. 
2Corinthians8:1 Bene Data, turabamenyesha ubuntu bg’Imana amashengero y’i Makedoniya yagiriwe." 
2Corinthians8:2 Bakigeragezwa n’amarushwa menshi, umunezero wabo w’akaburarugero, n’ubgoro bgabo butagira iyo buhērwa, vyarushirije kuzana ubutunzi bg’ivy’ ubuntu bgabo." 
2Corinthians8:3 Kubgabo bāratanze nk’uko bashoboye, ndabibashingira intahe, kandi n’ukurusha ivyo bashoboye," 
2Corinthians8:4 badusaba binginga cane kubatera iteka kugira ngo bafatanye n’abagaburira abera. 
2Corinthians8:5 Kandi si nk’uko twābiziga gusa, ariko bābanje kwitanga bīha Umwami wacu, natwe nyene baratwiha, nk’ukw Imana yagomvye." 
2Corinthians8:6 Ni co catumye twinginga Tito, ngw asozere ico gikorwa c’ubuntu no muri mwebge, nk’uko yagitanguye kera." 
2Corinthians8:7 Ariko nk’uko murushiriza kugira vyose — ukwizera, n’amajambo, n’ubgenge, n’umwete mwinshi, n’urukundo mudukunda — ni murushirize no kugira ubgo buntu na bgo." 
2Corinthians8:8 Simbivugiye kubagera, ariko mbivugiye kugeza urukundo rwanyu kw ar’urw’ ukuri, ndarugeragereshe umwete w’abandi." 
2Corinthians8:9 Kuko muzi ubuntu bg’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, yuko naho yar’ umutunzi, yahindutse umworo kubganyu, kugira ng’ubgoro bgiwe bubatungishe." 
2Corinthians8:10 Kand’ ivyo mbabgiye kur’ ivyo n’ukubagisha inama; kuko bibabereye, abātanguriye abandi uhereye ku mwaka ushize, s’ukubikora gusa, ariko no kubikunda." 
2Corinthians8:11 Nuko none mushitse no kubikora, kugira ngo nk’uko mwakunze kuvyemera, abe ari ko mubishitsa ku vyo mufise." 
2Corinthians8:12 Kukw iyo har’ umutima ukunze, wemerwa ku vy’umuntu afise, si ku vy’ adafise." 
2Corinthians8:13 Simvuze ntyo kugira ngw abandi boroherwe, namwe ngo mugorwe." 
2Corinthians8:14 Ariko n’ukugira ngo munganye, ngw ibisāgutse kuri mwebge mur’ iki gihe bimare ubukene bgabo, kandi ngw ibizobasāguka na bo bize bimare ubukene bganyu, munganye." 
2Corinthians8:15 Nk’uko handitswe, ng’Uwegeranije vyinshi asanga nta co asāguye; uwegeranije bike asanga nta co akehaniwe." 
2Corinthians8:16 Arikw Imana ishimwe, ishize mu mutima wa Tito kubagirira umwete nk’uwo mbagirira." 
2Corinthians8:17 Kuko yemeye inama yacu, kandi kukw agize umwete mwinshi, aje i wanyu bivuye ku mutima." 
2Corinthians8:18 Kandi hamwe n’uwo turungitse na mwene Data ngo bazanane, ishimwe ryiwe ryo ku vy’ ubutumwa bgiza ryamamaye mu mashengero yose." 
2Corinthians8:19 Kandi si co gusa, ariko na kare uwo ni we yatoranijwe n’amashengero kwama ajana natwe kubg’ ico gikorwa c’ubuntu, ubgo tugabura ng’ Umwami wacu ashimishwe, kandi ngo twerekane umutima wacu k’ubikunze." 
2Corinthians8:20 Kukw ico twirinda ar’ iki, ar’ ic’ umuntu yotugaya kubg’ izi ngabire nyinshi tugabura." 
2Corinthians8:21 Tubabaye gukora ivyiza, si mu nyonga z’Umwami wacu gusa, ariko no mu maso y’abantu." 
2Corinthians8:22 Kand’ abo tubarungikanye na mwene Data, uwo twagejeje kenshi, akaboneka kw ar’ umunyamwete muri vyinshi, ariko non’ arushiriza kugira umwete, kukw abizigira cane." 
2Corinthians8:23 Ivya Tito, ni we dufatanije igikorwa, kandi ni mugenzanje dukorana ivyanyu; kand’ ivya bene Data abo, n’intumwa z’amashengero, kandi n’icubahiro ca Kristo." 
2Corinthians8:24 Nuko mubereke ivyerekana urukundo rwanyu mu maso y’amashengero, kandi yuko twari dufise inyanduruko yo kwirata mwebge." 
2Corinthians9:1 Ivy’ ukugaburira abera sindinda kubibandikira. 
2Corinthians9:2 Kuko nzi umutima ukunze wanyu, ni wo nirata mu Banyamakedoniya yuko muwufise, mvuga yukw Abanyakaya bāri basanzwe biteguye, uhereye mu mwaka ushize, kandi gushishikara kwanyu kwateye abenshi umwete." 
2Corinthians9:3 Kandi ndungitse abo bene Data kugira ng’ ukwirata mwebge kwacu ntikuze gupfe ubusa mur’ ivyo; kugira ngo muze mube mwiteguye nk’uko nababgiye," 
2Corinthians9:4 twebge (sinovuga mwebge) ntituze tumāramāzwe n’ivyo twari twizigiye, namb’ Abanyamakedoniya bamwe bazozanana nanje bagasanga mutiteguye." 
2Corinthians9:5 Ni co gitumye niyumviriye yuko nkwiye kwinginga abo bene Data kunyitangira imbere mu kuza i wanyu, ngo babanze gutunganya ivy’ ubuntu mwasezeranye kera, bibe vyiteguwe nk’ivy’ ubuntu, ata kinubge." 
2Corinthians9:6 Arikw ico mvuga ngiki, ng’ Ūbiba nke, azokwimbura bike, ūbiba nyinshi azokwimbura vyinshi." 
2Corinthians9:7 Umuntu wese atange nk’ukw abigabiye mu mutima wiwe, atababaye cank’ atagōberewe, kukw Imana ikunda ūtanga anezerewe." 
2Corinthians9:8 Kand’ Imana ishobora kubasāzako ubuntu bgose, kugira ngo murushirize gukora ivyiza vyose, mufise ibibahāgije muri vyose." 
2Corinthians9:9 Nk’uko handitswe, ngo Yatanze isābagire, yahaye abakene, Ukugororoka kwiwe kwamah’ ibihe bidashira." 
2Corinthians9:10 Kand’ Īha umubivyi imbuto n’imitsima yo kurya, ni yo izobaha, ibongeranirize imbuto zanyu zo kubiba, kand’ izogwiza imbuto z’ukugororoka kwanyu." 
2Corinthians9:11 Namwe muzotungishwa muri vyose, ngo mugire ubuntu bgose, butuma dushimisha Imana." 
2Corinthians9:12 Kukw igikorwa c’ukwo kugabura kitamara ubgoro bg’abera gusa, ariko kandi kirushiriza gushimisha Imana muri benshi." 
2Corinthians9:13 Kuk’ uburyo mwageragejwe n’ukwo kugabura bgatumye abo bahimbaza Imana yuko muyumvira, mwātura ubutumwa bgiza bga Kristo, kandi yuko mwagize ubuntu bginshi bgo kubafasha no gufasha abandi bose." 
2Corinthians9:14 Kandi mu kubasengera babagirira inkumbu, kuk’ ubuntu bg’ Imana burushiriza kuba muri mwebge." 
2Corinthians9:15 Imana ishimirwe ingabire yayo nziza itovugwa. 
2Corinthians10:1 Jewe Paulo ubganje ndabinginga kubg’ ubugwaneza n’ineza vya Kristo, jewe umuntu aciye bugufi muri mwebge imbere yanyu, arikw iyo tutari kumwe ndabubahuka;" 
2Corinthians10:2 nuko ndabinginga kugira ngo ni twaba kumwe sinze ndinde kububahuka, nk’uko ngabiye kuzokwubahuka bamwe nshize ubgoba, batwiyumvira ko tugenda dukurikira ivy’ akameremere kacu." 
2Corinthians10:3 Naho turi n’umubiri ntiturwana mu buryo bg’umubiri," 
2Corinthians10:4 kukw ibirwanishwa vy’intambara yacu atar’ ivyo mu buryo bg’umubiri, arikw imbere y’Imana bifise ubushobozi bgo gushingūra akarimbi," 
2Corinthians10:5 dushingūra impāri n’igishizwe hejuru cose, kihashiriwe kurwanya ukumenya Imana, dufata mpiri ivyiyumvirwa mu mitima vyose, ngo tubigomōrere Kristo." 
2Corinthians10:6 Kandi twiteguye guhana ubutumva bgose, aho mwebge muzogirira ukwumva gushitse." 
2Corinthians10:7 Mbega murāba ibibonwa n’amaso? Namba har’ umuntu yizigiye kw ar’ uwa Kristo, yibgire n’ibi, yuk’ ukw ar’uwa Kristo, natwe ari ko turi." 
2Corinthians10:8 Kuk’ ububasha bgacu Umwami wacu yaduhaye kugira ngo tububake, ntitubasambure, naho norushiriza kubgirata, sinzomāramāzwa;" 
2Corinthians10:9 sinze niyumvirwe nk’ūbateza ubgoba ivyete vyanje. 
2Corinthians10:10 Kuko bavuga, bat’ Ivyete vyiwe birahambaye, birasogōta, arikw iy’ ar’ ino, arakēngēretse, kand’ amajambo yiwe nta co amaze." 
2Corinthians10:11 Ūvuga ibisa birtyo ni yibgire n’ibi, yuk’ uko tumeze ku majambo yo mu vyete atari ho turi, ari ko tumeze no ku vyo dukora ari ho turi." 
2Corinthians10:12 Kuko tutubahuka kwishira mu gitigiri ca bamwe bishimagiza, canke kwigereranya na bo: arikw abo, ko bīrēhēsha ubgabo kandi bīgereranya ubgabo, nta bgenge bagira." 
2Corinthians10:13 Tweho ntituzokwirata ibirenze urugero, ariko tuzokwiyumvira urugero rwacu ko ruhwanye n’urugezo rw’ah’ Imana yatugereye, ngo dushike no kuri mwebge." 
2Corinthians10:14 Ntidushingīra ngo turenge urugezo rwacu, nk’abatāshitse kuri mwebge, kuko twāshitse no kuri mwebge koko, tuzanye ubutumwa bgiza bga Kristo." 
2Corinthians10:15 Ntitwirata ibirenze urugero, ntitwirata ivy’ abandi bakoze. Ariko twizigiye yuk’ ukwizera kwanyu ni kwakura, tuzoshirwa hejuru kubganyu, ku vyo twagerewe, ngo twāgukirwe," 
2Corinthians10:16 tuvuge ubutumwa bgiza mu bihugu biri hirya yanyu, kugira ngo twoye kwirata ivyo dusanze bīteguye, ahāgerewe uwundi." 
2Corinthians10:17 Arik’ uwirata yirate Uhoraho. 
2Corinthians10:18 Kuk’ uwishimagiza atari we yemerwa, ariko hemerwa uw’ Umwami wacu ashimagiza." 
2Corinthians11:1 Icompa mukanyihanganira ku bupfu buciyemwo, kandi n’ubgo muranyihanganira." 
2Corinthians11:2 Mbafuhira ifuhe ryo kubg’ Imana, kuko nabahaye umugabo umwe, ni we Kristo, ngo ndabamushingire mumeze nk’inkumi itunganye." 
2Corinthians11:3 Ariko ndiyubara yuko, nk’uko ya nzoka yahendesheje Eva ukwiyorobeka kwayo, kumbure ivyiyumviro vyanyu vyokwoshwa, mugaca mureka ukugororoka n’ukwera mu vya Kristo." 
2Corinthians11:4 Kukw iyo hagize ūza i wanyu akababarira Yesu wundi, tutābabariye, cank’ iyo mwākiriye iyindi mpwemu mutākiriye, cank’ ubundi butumwa mutemeye, we muramwihanganira neza!" 
2Corinthians11:5 Kuko nibgira yukw izo ntumwa zihambaye cane ata co zindusha na gatoya. 
2Corinthians11:6 Naho nd’umutungu mu majambo, sind’ umutungu mu bgenge, kand’ ivyo twarabiberetse muri vyose no mu maso ya bose." 
2Corinthians11:7 Canke mbega naracumuye kuko nicishije bugufi ngo mushirwe hejuru, mbabgiye ubutumwa bgiza bg’Imana ku busa?" 
2Corinthians11:8 Nasahuye ayandi mashengero ndayāka ingero, kugira ngo nkorere mwebge," 
2Corinthians11:9 kand’ aho nari kumwe namwe ngakena, sinagize uwo ngōra: kuko bene Data bavuye i Makedoniya bāmmaze ubukene. Muri vyose nirinda kubagora, kandi nzoshishikara kuvyirinda." 
2Corinthians11:10 Uk’ ukuri kwa Kristo kuri muri jewe, nta wuzombuza kwirata ntyo mu ntāra zo muri Akaya." 
2Corinthians11:11 Ni ku ki? N’uko ntabakunda? Bizi Imana. 
2Corinthians11:12 Arikw ivyo nkora nzoshishikara kubikora, kugira ngo mbuze inyanduruko abagomba inyanduruko yo kuboneka nkatwe mu vyo birata." 
2Corinthians11:13 Abameze bartyo n’intumwa z’ibinyoma, n’abakozi bagunga, bīgira intumwa za Kristo." 
2Corinthians11:14 Kand’ ivyo ntibitangaza, kuko na Satani yīgira umumarayika w’umuco." 
2Corinthians11:15 Nuko s’ikigoye kw abakozi biwe na bo bīgira nk’abakozi b’ukugororoka: iherezo ryabo rizohwana n’ibikorwa vyabo. 
2Corinthians11:16 Kandi nongere kubivuga: Ntihagire ūnyiyumvira ko nd’ igipfu. Ariko ni mwaramuka munyiyumviriye murtyo, munyemere nk’igipfu, kugira ngo nanje nirate gatoya." 
2Corinthians11:17 Ivyo mvuga simbivuga nk’ijambo ry’Umwami wacu, ariko ndabivuga nk’ūvugishwa n’ubupfu, nizigiye yuko mfise inyanduruko yo kwirata." 
2Corinthians11:18 Ko benshi birata ivy’ umubiri, reka nanje nyene ndavyirate." 
2Corinthians11:19 Mwihanganira ibipfu munezerewe, kuko mwibereye abanyabgenge." 
2Corinthians11:20 Murihangana, iy’ umuntu abagize abaja, iy’ abariye, iy’ abafashe, iyo yishize hejuru, iy’ abakubise urushi." 
2Corinthians11:21 Mbivuganye isoni: bisa n’aho tweho twabagizemw’ intege nke. Arikw ikintu cose gitera umuntu gushira amanga (mbivugishijwe n’ubupfu) nanje kirabintera. 
2Corinthians11:22 Mbeg’ abo n’Abaheburayo? Nanje ndi we. N’Abisirayeli? Nanje ndi we. N’uruvyaro rwa Aburahamu? Nanje ndi rwo. 
2Corinthians11:23 N’abakozi ba Kristo? (Mvuga nk’umusazi) ndabarusha. Ndabarusha mu butame, ndabarusha gushirwa mu mabohero, ndabarusha mu gukubitwa kurenze urugero: kenshi nari mw irinde ry’urupfu." 
2Corinthians11:24 Abayuda ibihe bitanu bankubise ibimoko mirongwitatu n’icenda. 
2Corinthians11:25 Ibihe bitatu nakubiswe ingāge; igihe kimwe natewe amabuye; ibihe bitatu ubgato bgarammenekanye, naraye mw idamba nirirwaho;" 
2Corinthians11:26 nari mu ngendo kenshi, mw irinde ry’inzūzi, mw irinde ry’abambuzi, mw irinde ry’ubgoko bgacu, mw irinde ry’abanyamahanga, mw irinde ryo mu bisagara, mw irinde ryo mu bugaragwa, mw irinde ryo mu kiyaga, mw irinde ryo mu bīgira bene Data;" 
2Corinthians11:27 mu butame no mu bucumukure, ndāra maso kenshi, ngira inzara n’inyota, mmara ubusa kenshi, nicwa n’imbeho, nambara ubusa." 
2Corinthians11:28 Kandi ntarinze kuvuga ibindi, har’ ikinzako uko bukeye, n’umwitwaririko w’amashengero yose." 
2Corinthians11:29 Ni nde adakomera, nanje simbe ūdakomeye? Ni nde agira ikimugwisha, nanje isoni ntizinyice?" 
2Corinthians11:30 Namba nkwiye kwirata, nirata ivy’ intege nke zanje." 
2Corinthians11:31 Imana y’Umwami Yesu, ni yo Se, ishimwa ibihe bidashira, irazi ko ntabesha." 
2Corinthians11:32 I Damasiko icēgēra c’umwami Areta carindishije igisagara c’Abanyadamasiko ngo bamfate. 
2Corinthians11:33 Bancisha mu kadirisha k’uruzitiro rw’amabuye, ndi mu gisāngāza, ndahunga ndamuva mu maboko." 
2Corinthians12:1 Numva mpambīrwa kwirata, naho bitagira ikimazi. Ariko ngira mvuge ivyo kwerekwa no guhishurirwa n’Umwami wacu." 
2Corinthians12:2 Ndazi umuntu wo muri Kristo, yadūganywe akajanwa mw ijuru rya gatatu, ubu hashize imyaka cumi n’ine — namba yari mu mubiri simbizi; canke namb’ atāri mu mubiri simbizi, bizi Imana." 
2Corinthians12:3 Kandi nzi yuk’ ūmeze artyo — namba yari mu mubiri, canke namb’ atāri mu mubiri, simbizi, bizi Imana —" 
2Corinthians12:4 yadūganywe, akajanwa muri Paradiso, akumva ibitovugwa, ivy’ umuntu atemererwa kuvuga." 
2Corinthians12:5 Kubg’ umuntu ameze artyo ndirata, ariko kubganje sinokwirata, atar’ intege nke zanje." 
2Corinthians12:6 Kandi nogomvye kwirata sinobaye nd’ igipfu, kuko noba mvuga ukuri. Ariko nsizeho kugira ngo ntihagire ūnyiyumvira ibiruta ivy’ ambonako cank’ ivy’ anyumvako." 
2Corinthians12:7 Kandi kugira ngo noye guterwa kwishira hejuru birenze urugero, mbitewe n’uko nahishuriwe ibirushiriza kuba ibihambaye, ni co catumye mpabga igisata mu mubiri, intumwa ya Satani yo kunkubita ibipfunsi, ngo noye guterwa kwishira hejuru birenze urugero." 
2Corinthians12:8 Kandi kur’ ivyo natakambiye Umwami wacu gatatu ngo kimvemwo. 
2Corinthians12:9 Arambarira, at’ Ubuntu bganje buraguhāgije; kuk’ ubushobozi bganje buhīngūrirwa mu ntege nke. Nuko cane‐cane nzonezererwa kwirata intege nke zanje, ng’ubushobozi bga Kristo bunzeko." 
2Corinthians12:10 Ni co gituma kubga Kristo nzonezererwa intege nke zanje, no gukubagurwa, n’imibabaro, no guhīgwa, n’ivyago: kukw iyo mbaye umunyantege nke ari ho ndushiriza kugira ubushobozi." 
2Corinthians12:11 Mbaye igipfu, ni mwebge mwabinteye, kukw ivyari bikwiye ar’ uko mba narashimagijwe namwe. Za ntumwa zihambaye cane nta co zindushije, naho nd’ ubusa." 
2Corinthians12:12 N’ukuri ivyerekana intumwa vyakorewe hagati yanyu mu kwihangana kwose, ni vyo bimenyetso n’ibitangaza n’ibikorwa bikomeye." 
2Corinthians12:13 Ayandi mashengero yabarushije iki, atar’ uko jewe ubganje ntābabereye ikirusha? Mumparire ico caha!" 
2Corinthians12:14 Ehe niteguye kuza i wanyu ubugira gatatu: sinzobabera ikirusha. Kukw atar’ ivyanyu ndondera ariko ni mwebge ubganyu ndondera: kukw abana badakwiye kuziganiriza abavyeyi, arikw abavyeyi ni bo bakwiye kuziganiriza abana." 
2Corinthians12:15 Kubganje nzonezererwa cane gutanga ivyanje, no kwitanga rwose, nitangira ubugingo bganyu. Mbega ko ndushiriza kubagirira urukundo, non’ urwo nkundwa rugabanuke?" 
2Corinthians12:16 Ivyo vyo birahaye: ubganje sinabaremereye; ariko, ko naciye mu kandi kenge, nabafatishije ubugunge." 
2Corinthians12:17 Mbega mu bo nabatumyeko har’ umuntu natumye kubāka inyungu? 
2Corinthians12:18 Nagishije inama Tito, ndamurungikana na mwene Data wa wundi. Har’ inyungu Tito yabātse? Ntitwagendeye muri Mpwemu umwe? Ntiyageze ikirenge mu canje?" 
2Corinthians12:19 Uhereye kera mwiyumvira yuko tubiregurako. Imbere y’Imana no muri Kristo ni ho tuvugira. Ariko yemwe abo nkunda, vyose tubivugiye kubakomeza." 
2Corinthians12:20 Kuko binteye akōba yuko, aho nzozira, kumbure nzosanga mumeze uko ntagomba, nanje muzosanga mmeze uko mutagomba; kandi yuko kumbure hazoba imitongano, n’ishari, n’uburake, n’ikēba, n’ukuvuga abandi nabi, n’insaku, n’ukwihimbariza ubusa, n’imivurungano;" 
2Corinthians12:21 kandi yuko, aho nzozira, Imana yanje izosubira kuncisha bugufi muri mwebge, nanje nkazoririra benshi bācumuye kera, ntibihane ivyonona, n’ubushakanyi, n’ivy’ isoni nke bākoze." 
2Corinthians13:1 Ubu bugira bube ubga gatatu nza i wanyu. Ijambo ryose rizoringanizwa bivuye mu kanwa k’ivyabona bibiri canke bitatu. 
2Corinthians13:2 Nabivuze nkiri kumwe namwe ubugira kabiri kera, na none ntar’ iyo ni ko mbivuga bitaraba, mbarira abācumuye kera n’abandi bose, yuko ni nagaruka ntazogira akagongwe:" 
2Corinthians13:3 kuko murondera ikimenyetso co kwerekana yuko Kristo ari we amvugisha, umwe atar’ umunyantege nke kuri mwebge, arikw agira ubushobozi hagati yanyu." 
2Corinthians13:4 Kukw intege nke zāteye kw abambga, ariko non’ ariho kubg’ ubushobozi bg’Imana. Natwe tur’ abanyantege nke muri we, ariko tuzobanaho na we, kubg’ ubushobozi bg’Imana tubereyeho mwebge." 
2Corinthians13:5 Ba ari mwebge mwisuzuma, mumenye yuko muhagaze mu kwizera; ba ari mwebge mwirāba. Mbega ntimwiyizi, ntimuzi yuko Yesu Kristo ari muri mwebge? — shiti kumbure mur’ abāhinyuwe!" 
2Corinthians13:6 Ariko nizigiye yuko muzomenya ko tweho tutar’ abāhinyuwe. 
2Corinthians13:7 Kandi turasaba Imana ngo ntimugire ikibi mukora, s’ukugira ngo tuboneke ko tur’ abemewe, ariko n’ukugira ngo mukore iciza, natwe tuboneke nk’abahinyuwe." 
2Corinthians13:8 Kuko tudashobora kurwanya ukuri, ariko duherereye mu ruhande rw’ukuri." 
2Corinthians13:9 Turanezerwa iyo tugize intege nke, namwe mukagira inkomezi: kand’ ico dusaba ngiki, n’uko mutunganywa rwose." 
2Corinthians13:10 Ni co gitumye mbandikira ivyo tutari kumwe, kugira ngo ni twaba kumwe noye kuzohambara, nk’uko nahawe ububasha n’Umwami wacu bgo kwubaka, ariko s’ubgo gusambura." 
2Corinthians13:11 Ibisigaye bene Data, muganūke; mutungane rwose, mwemere guhanūrwa, muhuze imitima, mubane amahoro. Ni ho Imana Nyen’ urukundo n’amahoro izobana namwe." 
2Corinthians13:12 Muramukanishe kugumbirana kwera. 
2Corinthians13:13 Abera bose barabaganūtsa. 
2Corinthians13:14 Ubuntu bg’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, n’urukundo rw’Imana, n’ubumwe buva kuri Mpwemu Yera, bibane namwe mwese." 
Galatians1:1 Paulo, intumwa itātumwe n’abantu, kandi nta muntu yabariwe kuntuma, ariko natumwe na Yesu Kristo, n’Imana Data wa twese yamuzuye mu bapfuye," 
Galatians1:2 mfatanije na bene Data turi kumwe bose kubandikira, abo mu mashengero y’i Galatiya." 
Galatians1:3 Ubuntu bube muri mwebge n’amahoro biva ku Mana Data wa twese, no ku Mwami wacu Yesu Kristo," 
Galatians1:4 yitangiye ivyaha vyacu, ngw aturokore mur’ iki gihe kibi ca none, nk’ukw Imana yacu yagomvye, ni yo Data we twese." 
Galatians1:5 Icubahiro kibe icayo ibihe bitazoshira. Amen. 
Galatians1:6 Ndatangaye yuko muriko murareka vuba murtyo Iyabahamagaye kubg’ ubuntu bga Kristo, mukemera ubutumwa bunyuranye n’ubgo," 
Galatians1:7 kand’ ata bundi buriho; ariko harih’ abantu babahagarika imitima, bakagomba guhindura ukundi ubutumwa bga Kristo." 
Galatians1:8 Ariko naho yoba ari twebge cank’ umumarayika avuye mw ijuru, ababarira ubutumwa bunyuranye n’ubgo twababariye, arakavumwa." 
Galatians1:9 Nk’uko twāvuze ubga mbere, na none nongeye kubivuga, nti Ni hagira umuntu ababarira ubutumwa bunyuranye n’ubgo mwemeye, arakavumwa." 
Galatians1:10 Mbeg’ ubu n’ishimwe ry’abantu ngomba, canke n’iry’ Imana? Canke se ndondera kunezereza abantu? Iyo mba nkinezereza abantu, simba nd’umugurano wa Kristo." 
Galatians1:11 Ku vy’ ubutumwa navuze, ndabamenyesha bene Data, yukw atar’ ubg’ abantu:" 
Galatians1:12 kuko nanje ntābuhawe n’umuntu, kandi sinabgigishijwe, ariko ni Yesu Kristo yabumpishuriye." 
Galatians1:13 Mwumvise ingeso zanje nari mfise kera, nkiri mw idini y’Abayuda, ingene nahīga ishengero ry’Imana birengereje, nkaritikiza." 
Galatians1:14 Kandi mu bgoko bgacu narushije benshi bo mu bo twārukanye kuja imbere mw idini y’Abayuda, kuko nabarusha kugira ishaka ry’imigenzo twārazwe na ba sogokuruza." 
Galatians1:15 Arikw aho bihimbariye Imana yandobanuye nkiri mu nda ya mama, ikampamagara kubg’ ubuntu bgayo," 
Galatians1:16 guhishurira umutima wanje Umwana wayo, ngo mvuge ubutumwa bgiwe bgiza mu banyamahanga, ako kanya sinagishije inama abafise inyama n’amaraso," 
Galatians1:17 kandi sinadūze i Yerusalemu ku bantanguriye kuba intumwa, ariko nagiye muri Arabiya, kandi hanyuma nsubira i Damasiko." 
Galatians1:18 Maz’ imyaka itatu ishize ndūga i Yerusalemu kwibonanira na Kefa, mmara i we imisi cumi n’itanu." 
Galatians1:19 Ariko mu zindi ntumwa nta wundi nabonye, atari Yakobo, mwene nyina w’Umwami Yesu." 
Galatians1:20 Ku vyo mbandikiye, ehe nd’imbere y’Imana, simbesha." 
Galatians1:21 Maze nja mu ntāra z’i Siriya n’i Kilikiya. 
Galatians1:22 Abo mu mashengero y’i Yudaya yo muri Kristo ntibāribgankubite ijisho," 
Galatians1:23 ariko bumva gusa abamvuga, bat’ Umwe yahora aduhīga mbere, ubu asigaye yamamaza ivyizerwa yatikiza kera;" 
Galatians1:24 nuko bahimbaza Imana kubganje. 
Galatians2:1 Maze hahise imyaka cumi n’ine, nongera kudūgana na Barunaba, kandi na Tito ndamujana." 
Galatians2:2 Kandi nadūzeyo kubgo guhishurirwa, mbashira imbere ubutumwa bgiza mvuga mu banyamahanga, ariko mbushira imbere y’abashimwa twiherereye, ngo sinirukire ubusa, canke simbe narirukiye ubusa." 
Galatians2:3 Ariko na Tito twari kumwe ntiyagōberewe ngw akebge, naho yar’ Umugiriki," 
Galatians2:4 kand’ ari co coshimishije abīgira bene Data bānyegetejwe mw ishengero, binjiye mu mpisho ngo batate ukwidegemvya kwacu dufise muri Kristo Yesu, kugira ngo badushire mu buja." 
Galatians2:5 Abo ntitwabumviye na gatoya ngo tuganzwe na bo; kugira ng’ ukuri kw’ubutumwa bgiza kugume muri mwebge. 
Galatians2:6 Arikw abashimwa kw ari bakuru — uko bari bameze ubga mbere simbibabaye, kubganje vyose ni bimwe, Imana ntirobanura abantu ku cubahiro — abo bashimwa nta co bānyongerereje." 
Galatians2:7 Ariko babonye yuko najejwe ubutumwa bgo kwigisha abatākebge, nk’uko Petero yajejwe ubgo kwigisha abākebge." 
Galatians2:8 Kukw Iyashoboje Petero gutumwa ku bākebge, ari yo yanshoboje nanje gutumwa ku banyamahanga." 
Galatians2:9 Kandi bamaze kumenya ubuntu nahāwe, Yakobo na Kefa na Yohana, abashimwa kw ar’inkingi, badukora mu minwe, twe na Barunaba, ngo dufatanye na bo, ngo twebge tuje ku banyamahanga, na bo baje ku bākebge." 
Galatians2:10 Arikw ico bāgomvye gusa n’uko twibuka aboro, ari co nyene nanje nari nsanzwe mfitiye umwete." 
Galatians2:11 Ariko Kefa aje muri Antiyokiya, mmugisha impāri imbonankubone, kuko yari n’ibimutsindishije." 
Galatians2:12 Kukw abāvuye kwa Yakobo batarashikayo yasangira n’abanyamahanga; ariko bashitseyo, ariyonjorora, arabanēna, kukw atinye abo mu bākebge." 
Galatians2:13 Kandi n’abandi Bayuda bahumbana na we, bitayeko na Barunaba atwarwa n’ubgo buhumvyi bgabo." 
Galatians2:14 Ariko mbonye badaca mu nzira igororotse, nk’uk’ ukuri kw’ubutumwa bgiza kuri, mbaririra Kefa imbere ya bose, nti Ko wewe witondera ingeso z’abanyamahanga, zitar’ iz’ Abayuda, kand’ ur’ Umuyuda, ugōbēra ute abanyamahanga kuba nk’Abayuda?" 
Galatians2:15 Twebge mu kameremere kacu tur’ Abayuda, ntitur’ abanyavyaha bo mu banyamahanga." 
Galatians2:16 Ariko tuzi yuk’ umuntu adatsindanishirizwa n’ibikorwa bishinzwe n’ivyagezwe, arikw atsindanishirizwa no kwizera Yesu Kristo. Natwe twizeye Kristo Yesu, ngo kwizera Kristo kube ari kwo kudutsindanishiriza, atar’ ibikorwa bishinzwe n’ivyagezwe; kukw ata muntu atsindanishirizwa n’ibikorwa bishinzwe n’ivyagezwe." 
Galatians2:17 Ariko namba twabonetse ko tur’ abanyavyaha, hamwe twarondera gutsindanishirizwa no kuba muri Kristo, mbega Kristo n’umukozi agabura icaha? Eka na mba!" 
Galatians2:18 Nokwongera kwubaka ivyo nasambuye noba niseruye ko nd’umuntu acumura. 
Galatians2:19 Ivyagezwe vyanteye gupfa ku vyagezwe, ngo mbeho ku Mana." 
Galatians2:20 Nabambanywe na Kristo, ariko ndiho; yamara si jewe nkiriho, ni Kristo ariho muri jewe. Ivyo nkora vyose nkiriho mu mubiri mbikoreshwa no kwizera Umwana w’Imana yankunze, akanyigura." 
Galatians2:21 Simpindura ubusa ubuntu bg’Imana, kukw asangw’ ukugororoka kuzanwa n’ivyagezwe, Kristo azoba yapfiriye ubusa." 
Galatians3:1 Yemwe Bagalatiya b’ibijuju, ni nde yabaroze, kand’ ari mwebge mweretswe Yesu Kristo abambge, mu maso yanyu?" 
Galatians3:2 Iki conyene ni co ngomba ko mumbgira: mbega Mpwemu mwamuronkeshejwe n’ibikorwa vy’ivyagezwe, canke n’ukwumva gufatanije n’ukwizera?" 
Galatians3:3 Mbega mwakabaye mur’ ibijuju murtyo? Mwatanguye mu vya Mpwemu, mbega none musozereye mu vy’umubiri?" 
Galatians3:4 Mbeg’ ayo yose mwayaboneye ubusa? Namba yar’ ay’ ubusa koko! 
Galatians3:5 Ībaha Mpwemu, igakorera ibitangaza muri mwebge, mbeg’ ibikoreshwa n’uko mukora ibikorwa vy’ivyagezwe, canke n’uko mwumvise mukizera?" 
Galatians3:6 Nk’uko Aburahamu yizeye Imana, akabiharūrwako nk’ukugororoka." 
Galatians3:7 Mumenye rero yukw abīshimiye ukwizera ari bo bana ba Aburahamu. 
Galatians3:8 Kand’ ivyanditswe vyabimenye bitaraba yukw Imana izotsindanishiriza abanyamahanga kubg’ ukwizera, bibarira Aburahamu ubutumwa bgiza bg’ibitaraba, biti Muri wewe ni ho amahanga yose azohērwa umugisha." 
Galatians3:9 Nukw abīshimira ukwizera bahabga umugisha hamwe na Aburahamu yizera. 
Galatians3:10 Abishimira ibikorwa vy’ivyagezwe bose bari n’umuvumo: kuko handitswe ngw Azoba avumwe umuntu wese adashishikarira ivyanditswe vyose mu gitabo c’ivyagezwe, ngw avyitondere." 
Galatians3:11 Biraseruka yukw ata muntu atsindanishirizwa n’ivyagezwe imbere y’Imana, kuko handitswe ng’ Umugororotsi azobeshwaho n’ukwizera." 
Galatians3:12 Arikw ivyagezwe ntibiva ku kwizera, yamara ng’Ūzovyitondera ni vyo bizomubeshaho." 
Galatians3:13 Kristo yaducunguye umuvumo w’ivyagezwe, yacitse ikivume kubgacu; kuko handitswe ngw Azoba avumwe umuntu wese amanitswe ku giti:" 
Galatians3:14 kugira ng’umugisha wa Aburahamu ushike ku banyamahanga, bawuheshejwe na Yesu Kristo, kugira ng’ukwizera kuturonkeshe Mpwemu twasezeraniwe." 
Galatians3:15 Bene Data, ibi ndabivuga nk’imvugo y’abantu. Isezerano, naho ryoba iry’ umuntu gusa, iyo rishinzwe nta muntu arikūraho cank’ aryongerako." 
Galatians3:16 Nuko Aburahamu ni we yasezeraniwe amasezerano, bo n’uruvyaro rwiwe. Ntiyavuze, it’ Imvyaro; nk’ūvuga benshi: yamara yavuze nk’ūvuga umwe, iti N’uruvyaro rwawe; ni rwo Kristo." 
Galatians3:17 Arikw ico mvuze n’iki: isezerano ryabanje gushingwa n’Imana, ivyagezwe vyaje hashize imyaka amajana ane na mirongwitatu, ntivyorikūraho ngo bihindure ubusa iryo sezerano." 
Galatians3:18 Kukw iy’ umwandu uzanwa n’ivyagezwe, woba utazanywe n’isezerano: arikw Imana yawuhaye Aburahamu, iwumusezeraniye." 
Galatians3:19 Nukw ivyagezwe n’ibiki? Vyageretsweko kubg’ ibicumuro, ngo bigumeho kugeza ah’ uruvyaro ruzozira rwasezeranywe ivy’ isezerano: kandi vyahawe abamarayika kubigera, na bo babiha umushikirwa w’amajambo." 
Galatians3:20 Arik’ umushikirwa ntaba uw’ umwe, yamar’ Imana n’imwe." 
Galatians3:21 Mbeg’ ivyagezwe birwanya amasezerano y’Imana? Eka na mba! Iyo haba harih’ ivyagezwe vyashinzwe bishobora kubeshah’ abantu, n’ukuri ukugororoka kuba kwarazanywe n’ivyagezwe." 
Galatians3:22 Arikw ivyanditswe bivuga yuko vyose vyugaranywe ngo biganzwe n’icaha, kugira ngw abizera bahabge ivyasezeranywe biheshwa no kwizera Yesu Kristo." 
Galatians3:23 Arik’ ukwizera kutaraza, twarindwa n’ivyagezwe, twugaranywe turindiriye ukwizera kwagira kuze guhishurwe." 
Galatians3:24 Uko ni kw ivyagezwe vyatubereye umurezi aturera akadushikiriza Kristo, ngo dutsindanishirizwe n’ukwizera." 
Galatians3:25 Arik’ ukwizera ko kwaje, ntitukirerwa n’umurezi." 
Galatians3:26 Mwese mur’ abana b’Imana kubgo kwizera Kristo Yesu: 
Galatians3:27 kuko mwese ababatirijwe kuba aba Kristo mwanbaye Kristo. 
Galatians3:28 Ntihashobora kuba Umuyuda cank’ Umugiriki, ntihashobora kuba umugurano cank’ uwidegemvya, ntihashobora kuba umugabo cank’ umugore; kuko mwese mur’ umwe muri Kristo Yesu." 
Galatians3:29 Ko mur’ aba Kristo, mur’ uruvyaro rwa Aburahamu, mur’ abaragwa nk’uko vyasezeranywe." 
Galatians4:1 Ariko mvuga yuko samuragwa, iy’ akir’ umwana, ata co atandukanako n’umugurano, nah’ ari we nyen’ ibintu vyose." 
Galatians4:2 Arikw aganzwa n’abamuzigama n’ababgiriza kugeza mu kibariro cashinzwe na se. 
Galatians4:3 Natwe n’uko: tukir’ abana twari tujakariye ivya mbere vyo mw isi. 
Galatians4:4 Maz’ igihe gikwiye gishitse, Imana ituma Umwana wayo, yavyawe n’umugore, kandi yavutse aganzwa n’ivyagezwe," 
Galatians4:5 ngw acungure abaganzwa n’ivyagezwe, biduheshe gucika abana bayo." 
Galatians4:6 Kandi kuko mur’ abana bayo, Imana yatumye Mpwemu w’Umwana wayo mu mitima yacu, ataka, ati Abba, Data." 
Galatians4:7 Ni co gituma utakir’ umugurano, arik’ ur’ umwana wayo; kandi k’ur’ umwana wayo, ur’ umuragwa, ubihawe n’Imana." 
Galatians4:8 Arikw ico gihe, kuko mutāri muzi Imana, mwari mujakariye imana zitari zo uhereye mu kameremere kazo:" 
Galatians4:9 ariko none, ko mwamenye Imana, cane‐cane ko mwamenywe na yo, n’iki catumye musubira inyuma mugahindukirira ivya mbere vya goyi‐goyi, bitagira ikimazi, mukagomba kubijakarira ukundi gusha?" 
Galatians4:10 Muziririza imisi n’amezi n’ibihe n’imyaka. 
Galatians4:11 Munteye akōba, yuko kumbure ivyo nabakoreye natamijwe n’ubusa." 
Galatians4:12 Ndabinginze, bene Data, mumere nkanje, kuko nanje mmeze nkamwe. Nta nabi mwangiriye," 
Galatians4:13 ariko murazi yukw amagara make y’umubiri ari yo yatumye mbabarira ubutumwa bgiza ubga mbere: 
Galatians4:14 kand’ ivyābagerageza kubg’ umubiri wanje ntimwabitītūye, ntimwāciriye inyeri, ariko mwānyakiriye nk’umumarayika w’Imana, canke nka Kristo Yesu." 
Galatians4:15 None kwa kwishima kwanyu kuri hehe? Nd’ icabona canyu yukw iyo biba vyarashobotse, muba mwaremeye kwinogora amaso, mukayampa." 
Galatians4:16 Mbega mpinduwe umwansi wanyu no kubabgira ukuri? 
Galatians4:17 Ba bandi babagirira ishaka mu buryo butari bgiza; arikw ico bagomba n’ukubazigira hanze, kugira ngo namwe mubagirire ishaka." 
Galatians4:18 Mugabo, ni vyiza kugirira ivyiza ishaka ibihe vyose, atar’ igihe turi kumwe gusa," 
Galatians4:19 bana banje bato, abo nongera kuramukwa, gushitsa ah’ ishusho ya Kristo izoremerwa muri mwebge." 
Galatians4:20 Kandi nagomba gushikīrana namwe aka kanya, no kworosha ijwi, kukw ivyanyu binzazaniye." 
Galatians4:21 Mwebge abagomba kuganzwa n’ivyagezwe, ni mumbarire: mbega ntimwumva ivyagezwe?" 
Galatians4:22 Kuko vyanditswe yuko Aburahamu yar’ afise abahungu babiri, umwe ar’ uwo ku ncoreke, uwundi ar’ uwo ku mugore bgite." 
Galatians4:23 Uwo ku ncoreke yavyawe mu buryo bg’umubiri; uwo ku mugore bgite yavyawe kubg’ isezerano. 
Galatians4:24 Ivyo ni nk’umugani. Kukw abo bagore ari nk’amasezerano abiri, rimwe ryavuye ku musozi Sinayi, rivyara abo kuguma mu buja, iryo ni Hagari." 
Galatians4:25 Nuko Hagari n’umusozi Sinayi wo muri Arabiya, usobanurwa ngo Yerusalemu wa none, kuk’ usangiye ubuja n’abana bawo." 
Galatians4:26 Ariko Yerusalemu wo hejuru ni wo mugore bgite, ni wo mama wa twese." 
Galatians4:27 Kuko handitswe, ngo Nezerwa, yewe mugore w’ingumba utavyara, Turika, usemerere, wewe utaramukwa, Kukw abana b’intābga ari benshi, baruta ab’ ūfise umugabo." 
Galatians4:28 Namwe bene Data, mur’ abana b’isezerano, nk’uko Isaka yar’ ari." 
Galatians4:29 Ariko nk’ukw ico gihe uwavyawe mu buryo bg’umubiri yahama uwavyawe mu buryo bga Mpwemu, na none ni ko biri." 
Galatians4:30 Ivyanditswe bivuga iki? Bit’ Irukana incoreke n’umwana wayo, kuk’ umwana w’incoreke atazoraganwa n’umwana w’umugore bgite." 
Galatians4:31 Nuko bene Data, ntitur’ abana b’incoreke, tur’ aba wa mugore bgite." 
Galatians5:1 Kristo yatugobotoye ngo tube mu mwidegemvyo: nuko muhagarare mushikamye, ntimukongere kuzīngīrwa n’ugutwazwa ituntu n’ubuja." 
Galatians5:2 Umve, jewe Paulo ndababgira yuko ni mwakebga, Kristo ata co azobamarira." 
Galatians5:3 Kandi ndabarira umuntu wese akebga, mbishingiye intahe, yukw ari n’umwenda wo kwitondera ivyagezwe vyose." 
Galatians5:4 Yemwe abagomba gutsindanishirizwa n’ivyagezwe, erega muhinduye ubusa gufatana na Kristo kwanyu, muratemvye muretse ubuntu bg’Imana." 
Galatians5:5 Kuko twebge, mu buryo bga Mpwemu, twiteze ivyizigiro vy’ukugororoka, kubg’ ukwizera." 
Galatians5:6 Kuko muri Kristo Yesu, ar’ ugukebga, ar’ ukudakebga, bitagira ikimazi; ikigira ikimazi n’ukwizera gukoreshwa n’urukundo." 
Galatians5:7 Ko mwagenda neza; ni nde yabateye gutenzekanya ngo ntimwumvire ukuri? 
Galatians5:8 Iyo nyosha ntiyavuye kur’ uwo abahamagara. 
Galatians5:9 Umwambiro muke ututumbisha irobe ryose. 
Galatians5:10 Ndabizigiye kubg’ Umwami wacu yuko mutazogira uwundi mutima; arik’ ūbahagarika imitima, uw’ ari we wese, urubanza ruzomusubirako." 
Galatians5:11 Ariko jewe, bene Data, namba nkibarira abantu gukebga, n’iki gituma ngihamwa? Igitsitaza c’umusaraba kiba carahindutse ubusa." 
Galatians5:12 Icompa ababavurunga bakīkona rwose. 
Galatians5:13 Bene Data, mwahamagariwe umwidegemvyo; mugabo rero, uwo mwidegemvyo ntimuwugire urwitwazo rw’akameremere kanyu, arik’ urukundo rubatere gukorerana." 
Galatians5:14 Kukw ivyagezwe vyose bihūrira mur’ iri jambo, ngo Mukunde bagenzi banyu nk’uko mwikunda." 
Galatians5:15 Ariko ni mwashikurana, mugatsontsomerana, mwirinde ntimuhezanye." 
Galatians5:16 Ndavuga nti Mugendeshwe na Mpwemu, ni ho mutazoshitsa ivy’ akameremere kanyu kifuza." 
Galatians5:17 Kukw akameremere kifuza ivyo Mpwemu yanka, kandi Mpwemu yifuza ivy’ akameremere kanka: kukw ivyo bihiganwa, ngo ntimukore ivyo mugomba." 
Galatians5:18 Ariko namba murōngōrwa na Mpwemu, ntimuganzwa n’ivyagezwe." 
Galatians5:19 Kand’ ibikorwa vy’akameremere kacu biramenyekana, n’ibi: ubushakanyi, ibihumanya, ivy’ isoni nke," 
Galatians5:20 gusenga ibigirwamana, uburozi, ubgansi, intonganya, ishari, uburake, ikēba, kwitandukanya, ibice," 
Galatians5:21 igono, kuborerwa, kudandahirwa, n’ibindi ben’ ivyo. Ivyo ndabibabūriye, nk’uko nabibabūriye kera, yukw abakora ibisa birtyo batazoragwa ubgami bg’Imana." 
Galatians5:22 Arikw ivyo Mpwemu yama n’urukundo, umunezero, amahoro, ukwihangana, kugira neza, ingeso nziza, kuba umwizigirwa," 
Galatians5:23 ubugwaneza, ukwirinda: ibimeze birtyo nta vyagezwe bibibuza." 
Galatians5:24 Kand’ aba Kristo Yesu bābambanye akameremere kabo n’ivyo gahahamiye n’ivyo kifuza. 
Galatians5:25 Namba tubeshwaho na Mpwemu, tuyoborwe na Mpwemu." 
Galatians5:26 Ntitwifate uko tutari, ngo twandurutsanye, tugiriranire ishari." 
Galatians6:1 Bene Data, umuntu n’iyo yobonekakw icaha, mwebge ab’ impwemu mutunganye ūmeze artyo, mumuhanūrishe umutima w’ubugwaneza; kandi wiyubare ubgawe, nawe nyene woye kwoshwa nabi." 
Galatians6:2 Mwākīrane imitwaro, mushikane murtyo ivyagezwe na Kristo." 
Galatians6:3 Umuntu ni yiyumvira kw ar’ agakomeye, kand’ ata co amaze, arībesha." 
Galatians6:4 Arik’ umuntu wese asuzume igikorwa ciwe, ni ho azobona ico yirata ku mutumba wiwe bgite, atari kubga mugenzi we." 
Galatians6:5 Kuk’ umuntu wese azokwiyikorerera uwiwe mutwaro. 
Galatians6:6 Arik’ uwigishwa ijambo ry’Imana ahe umwigisha mu vyiza vyose. 
Galatians6:7 Ntimuzimire: Imana yo nticokorwa; kukw ic’ umuntu abiba cose ari co azokwimbura. 
Galatians6:8 Ūbiba mu buryo bg’umubiri azokwimbura ukubora mu mubiri; arik’ ūbiba muri Mpwemu azokwimbura muri Mpwemu ubugingo budashira. 
Galatians6:9 Twame dukora ivyiza, ntiducobogore, kukw igihe ni cashika tuzokwimbura, ni tutarambirwa." 
Galatians6:10 Nuko rero, iyo turonse uburyo, tugirire bose neza, cane‐cane ab’ inzu y’abizera." 
Galatians6:11 Murābe ingene mbandikishirije ukwanje kuboko inyuguti nini‐nini. 
Galatians6:12 Abagomba bose kwiha igikundiro ku vy’ umubiri ni bo babagōbēra gukebga; nta yindi nyanduruko, n’ukugira ngo ntibahamwe bahōrwa umusaraba wa Kristo." 
Galatians6:13 Kukw abākebge na bo nyene batitondera ivyagezwe, ariko bashaka ko mukebga, ngo birate imibiri yanyu." 
Galatians6:14 Ariko jeho sinkirate ikindi, atar’ umusaraba w’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, watumye isi imbera ikibambge, nanje isi nkayibera ikibambge." 
Galatians6:15 Kuko gukebga ata kimazi, no kudakebga nta kimazi, ikigira ikimazi n’icaremwe gisha." 
Galatians6:16 Abazogendera kur’ urwo rugezo, amahoro abe muri bo n’ikigongwe, no mu Bisirayeli b’Imana." 
Galatians6:17 Uhereye none ntihakagire umuntu angora, kuko mfise ku mubiri inkovu za Yesu." 
Galatians6:18 Bene Data, ubuntu bg’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo bubane n’imitima yanyu. Amen." 
Ephesians1:1 Paulo, nagizwe intumwa ya Kristo Yesu n’ukw Imana yabigomvye, ndabandikiye abera bari muri Efeso, b’abizigirwa bo muri Kristo Yesu." 
Ephesians1:2 Ubuntu bube muri mwebge n’amahoro, biva ku Mana Data wa twese no ku Mwami Yesu Kristo." 
Ephesians1:3 Imana y’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, ari yo Se, iragahezagirwa, yaduhezagiriye imihezagiro yose y’impwemu ahantu ho mw ijuru muri Kristo:" 
Ephesians1:4 nk’uko yadutoranirije muri we, itanguriro ry’isi ritarashirwaho, kugira ngo tube abera tutagira agasembga imbere yayo, turi mu rukundo." 
Ephesians1:5 Kuko yagabiye kera ko duheshwa na Yesu Kristo gucika abana bayo kubgayo, nk’uko yabigomvye bikayihimbara:" 
Ephesians1:6 kugira ng’ubgiza bg’ubuntu bgayo bushimwe, ubgo yatugabiriye mu wo ikunda." 
Ephesians1:7 Muri we ni ho duhērwa gucungurwa n’amaraso yiwe, ni kwo guharirwa ibicumuro vyacu, nk’ukw itunga ry’ubuntu bgayo riri," 
Ephesians1:8 ubgo yadusēsekarije mu bgenge bgose no kumenya: 
Ephesians1:9 itwātiye ibanga ry’ivy’ igomba, nk’uko vyayihimbaye, ibigabiye kera muri we," 
Ephesians1:10 vy’ingene izogenza vyose, igihe gikwiye gishitse, gukoraniriza vyose muri Kristo, ibiri mw ijuru n’ibiri mw isi." 
Ephesians1:11 Kuba mur’ uwo kwaduhesheje gucika ishamvu yayo, twashiriweho kera nk’ukw Iyo yabigabiye, ikora vyose nk’ukw imigabo yo mu mutima wayo iri," 
Ephesians1:12 kuzoba abo guhesha icubahiro ubgiza bgayo, twebge abizigiye Kristo kera." 
Ephesians1:13 Muri we namwe mumaze kwumva ijambo ry’ukuri, ni ryo butumwa bgiza bg’agakiza kanyu, mumaze no kumwizera, ni ho mwashiriwekw ikimenyetso, ni co Mpwemu Yera yasezeranywe," 
Ephesians1:14 ni we ngwati y’umwandu tuzohabga, kugira ngw abo Imana yaronse ibacungure, ng’ubgiza bgayo bushimwe." 
Ephesians1:15 Ni co gituma nanje, numvise ukwizera Umwami Yesu kuri muri mwebge, n’urukundo mukunda abera bose," 
Ephesians1:16 ntahengeshanya kubashimira Imana, mbahoza mu kanwa uko nsenze," 
Ephesians1:17 ngw Imana y’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, Data wa twese w’ubgiza, ibahe umutima w’ubgenge no guhishurirwa mu kuyimenya;" 
Ephesians1:18 ngw amaso y’imitima yanyu yihweze, kugira ngo mumenye ivyo mwizigizwa n’uguhamagara kwayo ivy’ ari vyo, mumenye n’itunga ry’ubgiza bg’ishamvu ifise mu bera," 
Ephesians1:19 mumenye n’ubginshi buhebuje bg’ubushobozi bgayo ikoreshereza muri twebge abizera, nk’uko kwa gukora kw’ububasha bg’ubushobozi bgayo kungana," 
Ephesians1:20 ukwo yakoreye muri Kristo, hamwe yamuzura mu bapfuye, ikamuvyagiza i buryo bgayo ahantu ho mw ijuru," 
Ephesians1:21 imushize hejuru cane y’ubukuru bgose n’ububasha bgose n’ubushobozi bgose n’ubgami bgose n’izina ryose rivugwa, si mur’ iki gihe gusa, ariko no mu kizoza." 
Ephesians1:22 Kandi yamushikirije vyose, ibishira musi y’ibirenge vyiwe, kand’ imuha ishengero ngw abe umutwe waryo wo gusumba vyose," 
Ephesians1:23 ni ryo mubiri wiwe, unengesereye ūnengesera vyose hose." 
Ephesians2:1 Namwe yarabagize bazima, hamwe mwari mupfuye mwishwe n’ibicumuro n’ivyaha vyanyu," 
Ephesians2:2 ivyo mwagenderamwo kera, nk’ukw ivy’ iyi si bigenda, mwumvira umwami w’abaganza ikirēre, ni we mpwemu ikorera mu bantu b’intabarirwa." 
Ephesians2:3 Kandi natwe twese twahora muri bo kera mu kwifuza kw’ imibiri yacu, tugakora ivy’ imibiri n’imitima vyacu bigomba, kandi mu kameremere kacu twar’ abo kurakirwa, nk’abandi bose." 
Ephesians2:4 Arikw Imana, kukw ar’ umutunzi w’ikigongwe, kubg’ urukundo rwayo rwinshi yadukunze," 
Ephesians2:5 hamwe twari tugipfuye, twishwe n’ibicumuro vyacu, yatugiranye bazima na Kristo — ubuntu ni bgo bgabakijije —" 
Ephesians2:6 yatuzuranye na we, itwicarikana na we ahantu ho mw ijuru, turi muri Kristo Yesu," 
Ephesians2:7 kugira ngo mu bihe bizoza ize yerekane itunga rihebuje ry’ubuntu bgayo mu kutugirira neza muri Kristo Yesu. 
Ephesians2:8 Ubuntu ni bgo bgabakijije kubg’ ukwizera: na vyo nyene ntivyavuye kuri mwebge, n’ingabire y’Imana;" 
Ephesians2:9 ntivyavuye ku bikorwa, kugira ngo hoye kugira uwirarira." 
Ephesians2:10 Kuko tur’ ibiremwa vyayo, twaremewe muri Kristo Yesu ngo dukore ibikorwa vyiza, ivyo Imana yateguye kera ngo tubigenderemwo." 
Ephesians2:11 Nuko mwibuke yuk’ ubga mbere, mwebge abanyamahanga ku rukoba, mwebge mucitwa abatākebge n’abo bitwa abākebge n’intoke ku mubiri," 
Ephesians2:12 kw ico gihe mwari mutandukanye na Kristo, muri n’itandukaniro n’ihanga rya Isirayeli, mur’ injabuka ku masezerano y’ivyasezeranywe, ata co mwizigiye ku bizoba, mwari mw isi mutagira Imana Rurema." 
Ephesians2:13 Ariko noneho, kuko muri muri Kristo Yesu, mwebge abāri kure kera mwigijwe hafi n’amaraso ya Kristo" 
Ephesians2:14 Ni we mahoro yacu, kuko yahinduye ya macakubiri kuba kimwe, ahomvoye ca gisika co hagati cadutandukanya," 
Ephesians2:15 ubgansi amaze kubuhinduza ubusa umubiri wiwe, ni bgo vya vyagezwe birimw’ amabgirizwa ava mu vyashinzwe; kugira ngo muri we ya macakubiri ayarememw’ umuntu umwe musha, ngw azane amahoro artyo;" 
Ephesians2:16 kandi ngw ayo macakubiri, amaze kuyagira umubiri umwe, ayuzurishe n’Imana umusaraba, awicishije bga bgansi." 
Ephesians2:17 Yaraje, ababgira ubutumwa bgiza bg’amahoro, mwebge abāri kure; kand’ abāri hafi na bo ababgira amahoro:" 
Ephesians2:18 kuko, uko tur’ amacakubiri, ari we adushikiriza Data wa twese, turi muri Mpwemu umwe." 
Ephesians2:19 Nuko ntimukir’ abashitsi n’akavantara, ariko musangiye ubgoko n’abera, mur’ abo mu ngoro y’Imana;" 
Ephesians2:20 kuko mwubatswe ku mabuye y’itanguriro, ari yo ntumwa n’abāvugishwa n’Imana, Kristo Yesu ari we buye rigumya imfuruka." 
Ephesians2:21 Muri we ingoro yose, yubatswe neza, irakura, ngw ibe urusengero rwera mu Mwami wacu." 
Ephesians2:22 Muri we namwe murubakanwa, kugira ngo muheshwe na Mpwemu kuba ingoro Imana ibamwo." 
Ephesians3:1 Ni co gituma jewe Paulo, imbohe ya Kristo Yesu, mbohewe mwebge abanyamahanga —" 
Ephesians3:2 namba mwarumvise ububgiriza bga bga buntu bg’Imana nahawe kubagaburira: 
Ephesians3:3 yuko mu guhishurirwa nātiwe ibanga, nk’uko nabanje kwandika mu majambo make," 
Ephesians3:4 namwe, ni mwayasoma, muzoshobora kubona ingene nzi ibanga rya Kristo." 
Ephesians3:5 Ivyo, abana b’abantu ntibābimenyeshejwe mu bindi bihe, nk’uko mur’ iki gihe intumwa ziwe zera n’abavugishwa na we bābihishuriwe na Mpwemu:" 
Ephesians3:6 yukw abanyamahanga basangiye natwe ibiragwa, basangiye natwe umubiri umwe, basangiye natwe ivyasezeranywe muri Kristo Yesu kubg’ ubutumwa bgiza." 
Ephesians3:7 Nacitse umukozi wabgo, nk’ukw ingabire y’ubuntu bg’Imana iri, ubgo nahawe, nk’uk’ ubushobozi bgayo bukora." 
Ephesians3:8 Jewe, uwuri mu nyuma y’uwo mu nyuma y’abera bose, naherewe ubgo buntu kubgira abanyamahanga ubutumwa bgiza bg’itunga rya Kristo ritagira aho riherera," 
Ephesians3:9 no guserurira bose ububgiriza bg’ibanga ubg’ ari bgo, ryari rihishijwe, uhereye kera hose, mu Mana Umuremyi wa vyose;" 
Ephesians3:10 kugira ngo noneh’ abakuru n’abafise ububasha b’ahantu ho mw ijuru bamenyere kw ishengero ubgenge bg’Imana bg’uburyo bginshi," 
Ephesians3:11 nk’ukw imigabo yayo iri, iyo yagabiye uhereye kera hose muri Kristo Yesu Umwami wacu" 
Ephesians3:12 Muri we ni ho duhērwa ubushizi bg’ubgoba no gushikīra Imana tuyizigiye, kubgo kumwizera." 
Ephesians3:13 Ni co gituma mbinginga ngo mwoye kwihebuzwa n’amarushwa yanje yo kubganyu, kukw ari yo cubahiro canyu." 
Ephesians3:14 Ni co gituma mpfukamira Data wa twese," 
Ephesians3:15 uwo imiryango yose yo mw ijuru n’iyo mw isi yītirirwa," 
Ephesians3:16 ngw abahe, nk’ukw itunga ry’ubgiza bgiwe riri, kuremeshwa n’ubushobozi imbere mu mitima mubihawe na Mpwemu wiwe:" 
Ephesians3:17 Kristo abe mu mitima yanyu kubg’ ukwizera; kugira ngo mugize imizi ishinzwe mu rukundo, n’amabuye y’itanguriro arwubatswemwo," 
Ephesians3:18 mugire inkomezi zibashoboza gutahurira hamwe n’abera bose uburebure bg’ubgaguke n’ubg’ amakika n’ubg’ igihagararo n’ubg’ amajepfo ubg’ ari bgo," 
Ephesians3:19 mumenye urukundo rwa Kristo ruruta uko rwomenywa; ngo mubone kunengeserezwa mushitse ku kunengesera kw’Imana kwose. 
Ephesians3:20 Nukw Īshobora gukora ibirengeye cane ivyo dusaba n’ivyo twiyumvira vyose, nk’uk’ ubushobozi bgayo budukoreramwo buri," 
Ephesians3:21 icubahiro kibe icayo mw ishengero no muri Kristo Yesu, kugeza ku buzukuruza bose b’ibihe bitazoshira. Amen." 
Ephesians4:1 Ni co gitumye mbinginga, jewe imbohe y’Umwami wacu, ngo mugende uko bibereye ihamagarwa mwahamagawe," 
Ephesians4:2 mwiyoroheje rwose, mufise ubugwaneza, mwihangana, mubabariranira muri mu rukundo," 
Ephesians4:3 mushishikaye kuzigamisha ubumwe buva kuri Mpwemu umugozi w’amahoro. 
Ephesians4:4 Harih’ umubiri umwe, na Mpwemu umwe, nk’uko kandi mwahamagariwe icizigiro kimwe c’ihamagarwa ryanyu." 
Ephesians4:5 Harih’ Umwami umwe, n’ukwizera kumwe, no kubatizwa kumwe;" 
Ephesians4:6 n’Imana imwe, ni yo Data wa twese, asumba bose, akoresha bose, ari muri bose." 
Ephesians4:7 Arik’ umuntu wese muri twebge yahawe ubuntu, nk’uko tugererwa ingabire ya Kristo." 
Ephesians4:8 Ni co gituma ivuga, iti Yaradūze, aja iyo hejuru, ajanye iminyago, Agabira abantu ingabire." 
Ephesians4:9 Arikw iryo jambo ngo Yaradūze, n’iki? Mbega ntiryerekana yuko yabanje kumanuka i kuzimu?" 
Ephesians4:10 Uwo yamanutse ni we yadūze, aja hejuru y’amajuru yose, kugira ngw anengesere vyose."
