Ephesians4:11 Kandi yahaye bamwe kuba intumwa, abandi kuba abavugishwa na we, abandi kuvuga ubutumwa bgiza, abandi kuba abungere n’abigisha:" 
Ephesians4:12 kugira ngw abera babone gutungana, baheze bakore igikorwa co kugabura ivy’ Imana, bubake umubiri wa Kristo:" 
Ephesians4:13 kugeza aho twese tuzoshikira ku kugiriranira ubumwe buva ku kwizera n’ukumenya Umwana w’Imana, kandi kugeza aho tuzoshikira kuba abantu bakuze, no ku rugezo rw’ubginshi bg’ukunengesera kwa Kristo:" 
Ephesians4:14 kugira ngo dushire ubgana, ntituzungazungishwe n’imipfunda, ngo tujanwe irya n’ino n’imiyaga yose y’inyigisho n’amangetengete y’abantu, n’ubugunge bgabo, n’uburyo bginshi bgo kutuzimiza." 
Ephesians4:15 Ariko tube imvugakuri turi mu rukundo, dukurire muri we muri vyose, ari we mutwe, ni wo Kristo;" 
Ephesians4:16 umubiri wiwe wose, uteranijwe neza, ufatanijwe n’ibifashisho vy’ingingo zawo zose, nk’ukw igihimba cose gikora ibango cagerewe, kuri we ni ho uronka gukura kwawo, ukubakwa mu rukundo." 
Ephesians4:17 Ni co gituma mvuga ibi, nkabishingira intahe mu Mwami wacu, ngo ntimube mukigenda nk’ukw abanyamahanga bagenda, bagendera mu bitagira ikimazi vyo mu bgenge bgabo," 
Ephesians4:18 ivyiyumviro vyabo biri mu mwiza, batandukanijwe n’ubugingo buva ku Mana kubg’ ukutamenya kuri muri bo, n’ugukomantara kw’ imitima yabo." 
Ephesians4:19 Kandi bābaye ibiti, bīshira mu ngeso z’isoni nke, gukora ibihumanya vy’uburyo bgose bifatanije n’ukwifuza." 
Ephesians4:20 Ariko mweho ntimwize Kristo murtyo," 
Ephesians4:21 namba mwaramwumvise, mukigishirizwa muri we nk’uk’ ukuri kwo muri Yesu kuri," 
Ephesians4:22 kubabgira ku vy’ingeso zanyu za kera ngo mwiyambure wa muntu wa kera, abozwa n’ukwifuza kw’uruhendo;" 
Ephesians4:23 mugahinduka basha mu mpwemu y’ubgenge bganyu," 
Ephesians4:24 mukambara wa muntu musha, yaremwe mw ishusho y’Imana mu kugororoka no mu kwera kw’ukuri." 
Ephesians4:25 Maze mwiyambuye ibinyoma, umuntu wese avugane ivy’ ukuri na mugenzi we, kuko tur’ ingingo za bagenzi bacu." 
Ephesians4:26 Ni mwaraka ntibibakoreshe icaha: izuba ntirirenge mukiratse," 
Ephesians4:27 kandi ntimuhe wa Murwanizi icicaro. 
Ephesians4:28 Uwiba ntakongere kwiba, arikw apfume acumukura, akoreshe ayiwe maboko ivyiza, kugira ngw aronke ivyo gufasha ūkennye." 
Ephesians4:29 Ntihaze hagire ibiyāgo bibi biva mu kanwa kanyu, ariko muvuge ijambo ryiza ryose ryo gukuza ūkwiye kuribgirwa, kugira ngo riheshe abaryumvise ubuntu bg’Imana." 
Ephesians4:30 Kandi ntimukababaze Mpwemu Yera w’Imana, yabashiriweko kuba ikimenyetso, gushitsa ku musi wo gucungurwa." 
Ephesians4:31 Umururazi wose no kujingitwa n’uburake no gutongana no gutukana bibavemwo, hamwe n’inzigo yose." 
Ephesians4:32 Mugiriranire neza, mugiriranire imbabazi, muharirane, nk’ukw Imana na yo yabahaririye muri Kristo" 
Ephesians5:1 Nuko mwīgāne Imana, nk’abana ikunda." 
Ephesians5:2 Kandi mugendere mu rukundo, nk’uko Kristo na we yabakunze, akatwigura, akatubera ishikanwa n’ikimazi bihabga Imana, umubabge umota neza." 
Ephesians5:3 Arik’ ubushakanyi n’ibihumanya vyose cank’ ukwifuza ntimukabishire no mu kanwa, mube nk’uko bibereye abera:" 
Ephesians5:4 cank’ ibiteye isoni, cank’ amagambo y’ubupfu, cank’ ibitwenza bibi, kukw ivyo bitabereye; ikibereye n’ugushima Imana." 
Ephesians5:5 Kukw ibi mubizi neza, yukw ata mushakanyi, cank’ igihumane, cank’ uwifuza (ni we asenga ibigirwamana), azogira ico aragwa mu bgami bga Kristo n’Imana." 
Ephesians5:6 Ntihakagire umuntu abahendesha amagambo y’ubusa: kukw ivyo ari vyo bizanira uburake bg’Imana abantu b’intabarirwa. 
Ephesians5:7 Nuko ntimugafatanye na bo; 
Ephesians5:8 kuko kera mwar’ umwiza, none mukaba mur’ umuco mu Mwami wacu: mugende nk’abana b’umuco," 
Ephesians5:9 kukw imbuto y’umuco iboneka mu ngeso nziza zose no mu kugororoka no mu kuri. 
Ephesians5:10 Mumenye neza ibihimbara Umwami wacu," 
Ephesians5:11 kandi ntimugafatanye n’ibikorwa birumvye vy’umwiza, ariko cane‐cane mubiserure," 
Ephesians5:12 kukw ibikorwa na bo mu mpisho biteye isoni no kubivuga. 
Ephesians5:13 Ariko vyose, iyo bishizwe ahabona, bigaragazwa n’umuco, kukw ikigaragazwa cose ar’ umuco." 
Ephesians5:14 Ni co gituma bivugwa, ngw Ikangure, wewe usinziriye, uzuke uve mu bapfuye, Kristo arakumurikira." 
Ephesians5:15 Nuko mwirinde cane uburyo mugenda, mwoye kugenda nk’imburabgenge, ariko mugende nk’abanyabgenge," 
Ephesians5:16 mugura uburyo mubugwiza, kukw imisi ari mibi." 
Ephesians5:17 Nuko ntimube ibipfu, ariko mutahure ivy’ Umwami wacu agomba ivy’ari vyo." 
Ephesians5:18 Kandi ntimukaborerwe vino, irimw’ ubuhumbu; ariko mwuzure Mpwemu." 
Ephesians5:19 Mubgirane zaburi n’indirimbo n’amatazirano y’ivya Mpwemu, muririmba, mucurarangira Umwami wacu mu mitima yanyu;" 
Ephesians5:20 Imana, Data wa twese, muyishimire vyose imisi yose, mw izina ry’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo." 
Ephesians5:21 Mugamburukanire, kuko mwubashe Kristo." 
Ephesians5:22 Bagore, mugamburukire abagabo banyu, nk’uko mugamburukira Umwami wacu." 
Ephesians5:23 Kuk’ umugabo ari we mutwe w’umugore wiwe, nk’uko Kristo na we ar’ umutwe w’ishengero, akaba Umukiza waryo, ari wo mubiri wiwe." 
Ephesians5:24 Ariko nk’ukw ishengero rigamburukira Kristo, abe ari kw abagore bagamburukira abagabo babo muri vyose." 
Ephesians5:25 Bagabo, mukunde abagore banyu, nk’uko Kristo na we yakunze ishengero, akaryigura," 
Ephesians5:26 ngw aryeze, aryogesheje amazi n’ijambo," 
Ephesians5:27 ngw aryīshīre, ar’ ishengero rifise ubgiza, ridafise amarabaga cank’ injebejebe cank’ ikintu cose gisa girtyo, ariko ngo ribe iryera ridafise agasembga." 
Ephesians5:28 Ni kw abagabo na bo bakwiye gukunda abagore babo nk’imibiri yabo bgite. Ūkunda umugore wiwe, aba yīkunda:" 
Ephesians5:29 kukw ata muntu yigeze kwanka umubiri wiwe, arikw arawugaburira, akawubungabunga, nk’uko Kristo na we agirira ishengero:" 
Ephesians5:30 kuko tur’ ingingo z’umubiri wiwe. 
Ephesians5:31 Ni co gituma umuntu azosiga se na nyina, akabana n’umugore wiwe akaramata, bompi bakaba umubiri umwe." 
Ephesians5:32 Iryo banga rirahambaye, ariko mbivuze kuri Kristo n’ishengero." 
Ephesians5:33 Ariko namwe nyene, umuntu wese akunde umugore wiwe nk’uko yīkunda; umugore na we ni yubahe umugabo wiwe." 
Ephesians6:1 Bana, mwumvire abavyeyi banyu mu Mwami wacu: kukw ivyo ari vyo bigororotse." 
Ephesians6:2 Wubahe so na nyoko: ico ni co cagezwe ca mbere kirimw’ isezerano," 
Ephesians6:3 kugira ng’uronke amahoro, urambire kw isi." 
Ephesians6:4 Namwe ba se, ntimukaratse abana banyu, ariko mubarere, mubahana mubahanūra, uk’ Umwami wacu agomba." 
Ephesians6:5 Bagurano, mwumvire ba shobuja bo ku mubiri, nk’uko mwumvira Kristo, mububashe muhinda agashitsi, mutagira ubupfunya mu mitima yanyu." 
Ephesians6:6 Ntimubakorere bakibahagarikiye, nk’abanezereza abantu, ariko mubakorere nk’abagurano ba Kristo, mukora ivy’ Imana igomba bivuye ku mutima." 
Ephesians6:7 Mubakorere mushize icira, nk’abakorera Shobuja mukuru, ntimube nk’abakorera abantu." 
Ephesians6:8 Kuko muzi yuk’ umuntu wese iy’ akoze iciza, azocishurwa na Shebuja mukuru, n’iyo yoba umugurano cank’ uwidegemvya." 
Ephesians6:9 Namwe ba shebuja, mubagirire murtyo nyene, mwirinde kubakangisha, kuko muzi yuko Shobuja musangiye ari mw ijuru, kandi ntarobanura abantu ku butoni." 
Ephesians6:10 Ibisigaye, muremesherezwe mu Mwami wacu, no mu bushobozi bgiwe bginshi." 
Ephesians6:11 Mwambare ibirwanishwa vyose vy’Imana, kugira ngo mushobore guhagarara mudatsinzwe n’ubugunge bga wa Murwanizi." 
Ephesians6:12 Kukw abo tunigana atar’ ab’ inyama n’amaraso, ariko tunigana n’abakuru n’abafise ububasha n’abaganza iyi si y’umwiza, n’impwemu mbi z’ahantu ho mw ijuru." 
Ephesians6:13 Kubg’ ivyo mwābīre ibirwanishwa vyose vy’Imana, kugira ngo mushobore kudatsindwa ku musi mubi, kandi ni mwaheza vyose mugahagarara mushikamye." 
Ephesians6:14 Nuko rero mushikame, mukenyeje ukuri, mwambaye ukugororoka nk’icuma gikīngīra igikiriza," 
Ephesians6:15 mwambaye inkweto z’ivyo ubutumwa bgiza bg’amahoro bibīteguza; 
Ephesians6:16 kandi hamwe n’ivyo vyose mwābīre inkinzo y’ukwizera, ni yo muzoshoboza kuzimisha imyampi ya wa Mubi yose yaka umuriro." 
Ephesians6:17 Mwābīre inkofero y’agakiza, bo n’inkota ya Mpwemu, ni yo jambo ry’Imana:" 
Ephesians6:18 musengere muri Mpwemu ibihe vyose, mu buryo bgose bgo gusenga no kwinginga, kand’ ivyo mubibere maso, mukobeje rwose, musengera abera bose." 
Ephesians6:19 Kandi nanje nyene munsengere, kugira ngo mpabge insiguro uko mvuze kwose, mmenyekanishe nshize amanga ibanga ry’ubutumwa bgiza," 
Ephesians6:20 kuko nd’ intumwa yabgo iboheshejwe umunyororo, nsigure ivyabgo nshize amanga, nk’uko bimbereye kuvuga." 
Ephesians6:21 Kandi Tukiko, mwene Data nkunda, umukozi w’umwizigirwa mu vy’Umwami wacu, azobīgānira vyose, kugira ngo mumenye ivyanje, uko mmeze." 
Ephesians6:22 Ni we mbatumyeko kubg’ ivyo nyene, ngo mumenye ivyacu, kandi ngw aremeshe imitima yanyu." 
Ephesians6:23 Amahoro abe muri bene Data, n’urukundo rufatanije n’ukwizera, biva ku Mana Data wa twese no ku Mwami Yesu Kristo." 
Ephesians6:24 Ubuntu bg’Imana bubane n’abakunda Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo bose ata bupfunya. 
Philippians1:1 Paulo na Timoteyo, abagurano ba Kristo Yesu, turabandikiye abera bose bo muri Kristo Yesu b’i Filipi, hamwe n’abazezwashengero n’abakozi baryo." 
Philippians1:2 Ubuntu bube muri mwebge n’amahoro, biva ku Mana Data wa twese no ku Mwami Yesu Kristo." 
Philippians1:3 Nshima Imana yanje, uko mbibutse kwose," 
Philippians1:4 kand’ uko nsenze kwose mbasengera mwese nnezerewe," 
Philippians1:5 kuko mwafatanije nanje gukwiza ubutumwa bgiza, muhereye ku musi wa mbere, mugashitsa n’ubu." 
Philippians1:6 Kand’ ico nizigiye ntakekeranya, n’uk’ uwatanguye igikorwa ciza muri mwebge azogiheraheza gushitsa ku musi wa Yesu Kristo." 
Philippians1:7 Nanje birambereye kubiyumvirako ntyo mwese, kuko mbafise mu mutima, kuko mu ngoyi zanje, no mu gukiranira ubutumwa bgiza no kubucimbataza, mwese musangiye nanje ubuntu bg’Imana." 
Philippians1:8 Imana ni yo ntanzekw icabona c’ingene mbagirira igishika mwese, mfise imbabazi za Kristo Yesu." 
Philippians1:9 Kand’ ico nsengera, n’ukugira ng’urukundo rwanyu rugwire rwongerekane mu bgenge no mu kumenya kwose," 
Philippians1:10 murobanure ibidahwana, muhore mutagira ubupfunya cank’ ibigwisha gushitsa ku musi wa Kristo," 
Philippians1:11 mwuzuye imbuto zo kugororoka ziheshwa na Yesu Kristo, ngo muheshe Imana icubahiro n’ishimwe." 
Philippians1:12 Bene Data, ndagomba ko mumenya yukw ivyambāyeko cane‐cane vyashize imbere ubutumwa bgiza:" 
Philippians1:13 bituma ingoyi zanje zo kubga Kristo zimenyekana mu basoda bahora bashibama kwa Kayisari bose, no mu bandi bose." 
Philippians1:14 Kand’ abenshi bo muri bene Data bari mu Mwami wacu, bāremeshejwe n’ingoyi zanje, barushiriza gutinyuka kuvuga ijambo ry’Imana bashize amanga." 
Philippians1:15 Mugabo bamwe ishari n’amahane ni vyo bibatera kuvuga ivya Kristo; abandi babivugishwa n’ugushira icīra. 
Philippians1:16 Abo babivugishwa n’urukundo, kuko bazi ko nashiriweho gukīranira ubutumwa bgiza:" 
Philippians1:17 ba bandi ikēba ni ryo ribatera kuvuga ivya Kristo atar’ uko bivuye ku mutima, biyumvira kw ar’ ukwongera kuntoneka mu ngoyi zanje." 
Philippians1:18 Har’ ico biriko? Kizima mu buryo bgose, ari mu buryarya ari mu kuri, Kristo avugwa, kand’ ivyo ndabinezererewe, kandi nzokwama mbinezererwa;" 
Philippians1:19 kuko nzi yukw ivyo bizomviramw’ agakiza, munsengeye kandi ndonkejwe Mpwemu wa Yesu Kristo;" 
Philippians1:20 nk’uko niteze cane nkizigira yuko hatazogira ikintu kimmāramāza, ariko ko mu bushizi bg’amanga bganje bgose Kristo aheshwe icubahiro n’umubiri wanje, nk’uko bihora biba, na none kw ari ko bizoba, naho noba ndiho canke naho noba mpfuye." 
Philippians1:21 Kuko kubganje kubaho ari Kristo, kandi gupfa ar’ inyungu." 
Philippians1:22 Ariko namb’ ari kubaho mu mubiri, ico kizonyamira imbuto z’igikorwa, kandi sinzi ico mpitamwo." 
Philippians1:23 Ndazazaniwe mur’ ivyo bibiri, kuko nifuza gutaha ngo mbane na Kristo, kukw ari co kirushirije cane:" 
Philippians1:24 yamara kuguma mu mubiri ni co corushiriza kubagirira ikimazi. 
Philippians1:25 Kandi ko nizigiye ivyo, ndazi neza yuko nzogumaho, nkabana namwe mwese, kugira ngo muje imbere, munezererwe ukwizera;" 
Philippians1:26 ngo muze murushirize kunyirata muri Kristo Yesu nsubiye kugaruka i wanyu. 
Philippians1:27 Ariko kimwe gusa, ingeso zanyu zimere nk’uko bibereye ubutumwa bgiza bga Kristo, kugira ngo nje kubagendera canke ntaje, numve ivyanyu ko muhagaze mushikamye mufise impwemu imwe, muhuje umutima mu kurwanira ukwizera ubutumwa bgiza," 
Philippians1:28 ko mudakangwa n’abarwanizi ku kintu na kimwe; ico kizobera abo ikimenyetso co guhona, ariko mwebge ic’ agakiza, kandi kivuye ku Mana." 
Philippians1:29 Kukw ico mwagabiwe kubga Kristo, atar’ ukumwizera gusa, ariko mwagabiwe no kubabazwa kubgiwe;" 
Philippians1:30 muri muri ya ntambara mwambonanye kand’ iyo munyumvana n’ubu. 
Philippians2:1 Nuko namba har’ ukuremeshwa muri Kristo, namba har’ ukwirurwa kuva mu rukundo, namba har’ ugusangira Mpwemu, namba har’ imbabazi n’ikigongwe," 
Philippians2:2 mwuzuze umunezero wanje muhwanije imitima, musangiye urukundo rumwe, muhūje umutima n’inama." 
Philippians2:3 Ntimugire ico mukora kubgo gukēbana cank’ ukwifata uko mutari, ariko mwicishije bugufi, umuntu wese yiyumvire yuko mugenzi we amuruta," 
Philippians2:4 kand’ umuntu wese ntiyiyumvire ivyiwe gusa, ariko yiyumvire n’ivy’ abandi." 
Philippians2:5 Mugire wa mutima muri mwebge wari muri Kristo Yesu. 
Philippians2:6 Uwo, naho yar’ asanganywe ishusho y’Imana, ntiyiyumviriye yuko kuringanira n’Imana ar’ ikintu co kwumirako:" 
Philippians2:7 ariko yīsiga ubusa, yābīra ishusho y’umugurano, acika ūsa n’abantu." 
Philippians2:8 Kand’ abonetse afise ishusho nk’iy’ umuntu, yicisha bugufi, araganduka no gushitsa ku rupfu, kand’ urupfu rwo ku musaraba." 
Philippians2:9 Ni co catumye Imana imushira hejuru cane, ikamuha rya zina rirengeye ayandi mazina yose:" 
Philippians2:10 kugira ngw amavi yose az’ apfukame mw izina rya Yesu, ay’ ivyo mw ijuru n’ay’ ivyo kw isi n’ay’ ivy’ i kuzimu," 
Philippians2:11 kand’ indimi zose zize zature yuko Yesu Kristo ar’ Uhoraho, ngo biheshe Imana Data wa twese icubahiro." 
Philippians2:12 Nuko rer’ abo nkunda, nk’uko mwamye muganduka abe ari ko mushitsa agakiza kanyu, mutinya muhinda agashitsi, yamara s’iyo ndiho gusa, ariko n’ubu nyene naho ntar’ iyo ni murushirize." 
Philippians2:13 Kukw Imana ari yo ikorera mu mitima yanyu, ikabaha gukunda no gukora ibiyihimbara." 
Philippians2:14 Mukore vyose ata kwidodomba, ata guhārīra," 
Philippians2:15 kugira ngo ntimugire umugayo cank’ akarohe, mube abana b’Imana batagira agasembga, hagati y’ab’ iki gihe bagoramye b’ibidambidambi, abo mubonekeramwo nk’amatara mw isi," 
Philippians2:16 mwerekana ijambo ry’ubugingo; kugira ngo mbone ico nzokwirata ku musi wa Kristo, yuko ntirukiye ubusa kandi ntātamijwe n’ubusa." 
Philippians2:17 Arikw asangwa nkwiye gusukwa ku kimazi c’ukwizera kwanyu no kw ibango ryakwo, ndanezerwa, nnezeranwa namwe mwese:" 
Philippians2:18 abe ari ko namwe munezerwa, munezeranwe nanje." 
Philippians2:19 Ariko nizigijwe n’Umwami Yesu yuko nzobatumako Timoteyo vuba, kugira ngo nanje nze nshire umutima hamwe, ni namenya ivyanyu." 
Philippians2:20 Simfise uwundi ari n’umutima nk’uw’ uwo, yobabara ivyanyu vy’ukuri." 
Philippians2:21 Kuko bose barondera ivyabo, batarondera ivya Yesu Kristo." 
Philippians2:22 Ariko murazi ingen’ uwo yagejejwe akarama, kandi yuko, nk’uk’ umwana amereranira na se, ari ko yakoranye nanje igikorwa co gukwiza ubutumwa bgiza." 
Philippians2:23 Nuk’ uwo ni we nizigiye yukw ari we nzoca mbatumako, aho nzomenyera ibizombako." 
Philippians2:24 Ariko nizigijwe cane n’Umwami wacu yuko nanje nyene nzoza vuba. 
Philippians2:25 Kandi mbonye yukw ar’ igikwiye kubatumako Epafurodito, mwene Data dufatanije igikorwa n’intambara, ari we ntumwa yanyu inkorera ivyo nkennye;" 
Philippians2:26 kukw abagirira igishika mwese, akarandurwa umutima n’uko mwumvise yuko yar’ arwaye." 
Philippians2:27 Kandi koko yari yararwaye ahakwa guhwera: arikw Imana imugirira imbabazi, kandi si we wenyene, ni jewe yazigiriye, kugira ng’umubabaro wanje ntiwongerekane." 
Philippians2:28 Ni co gitumye ngira umwete wo kumurungika, kugira ngo ni mwongera kumubona muze munezerwe, nanje ngabanuke umubabaro." 
Philippians2:29 Nuko mumwākīrane umunezero mwinshi kubg’ Umwami wacu; kand’ abameze nk’uwo mwame mububaha; 
Philippians2:30 kuko yagarukiye hafi yo gupfa kubg’ igikorwa ca Kristo, yahevye amagara yiwe, ngw ashikane ivyasigaye vyo kumfasha kwanyu." 
Philippians3:1 Ibisigaye bene Data, munezererwe mu Mwami wacu. Kubandikira ben’ ivyo ntikundambira, kandi namwe kurabaremesha." 
Philippians3:2 Mwirinde za mbga, mwirinde za nkozi z’ibibi, mwirinde bamwe bīkebagura." 
Philippians3:3 Kuko tweho tur’ abākebge, dusenga Imana mu buryo bga Mpwemu, tukirata Kristo Yesu, ntitwishimire ivy’ umubiri;" 
Philippians3:4 naho jewe nokwishimiye ivy’ umubiri. Hogira uwundi wese yokwiyumvira kwishimira ivy’ umubiri, nomurusha." 
Philippians3:5 Nakebge ku musi ugira umunani, nd’ uwo mu bgoko bga Isirayeli, nd’ uwo mu muryango wa Benyamini, mu Baheburayo nd’ Umuheburayo, ku vyo gushimikira ivyagezwe, nd’ Umufarisayo;" 
Philippians3:6 ku vy’ ishaka nahama ishengero; ku vy’ ukugororoka kuzanwa n’ivyagezwe nta wobonye ic’ angaya. 
Philippians3:7 Arikw ivyahora bimbera inyungu ndavyiyumvira kw ar’ ubuhombe kubga Kristo 
Philippians3:8 Eka mbere n’ibintu vyose ndavyiyumvira kw ar’ ubuhombe, kubg’ ikibirengeye, ni co kumenya Kristo Yesu Umwami wanje. Kubg’ uwo nahomvye ibintu vyose, ndavyiyumvira kw ar’ ishano, kugira ngo ndonke Kristo," 
Philippians3:9 kandi mboneke ko ndi muri we, ntafise ukwanje kugororoka, kumwe kuva mu vyagezwe, ariko mfise kumwe kuzanwa no kwizera Kristo, ni kwo kugororoka kuva ku Mana, guhabga uwizeye," 
Philippians3:10 ngo ndamumenye, mmenye n’ubushobozi bg’ukuzuka kwiwe, n’ugufatanya na we imibabaro yiwe, nshushanywe n’urupfu rwiwe," 
Philippians3:11 ngo kumbure nshike ku kuzuka kw’abapfuye. 
Philippians3:12 S’ukugira ngo mpejeje kubihabga, canke ngo mpejeje gutunganywa rwose, ariko ndabandanya kugira ngo mbone gufata kimwe catumye nanje ubganje mfatwa na Kristo Yesu." 
Philippians3:13 Bene Data, jeho kubganje sinibgira yuko mmaze kugifata, arikw ico nkora n’iki kimwe gusa, nibagira ibir’ inyuma, kandi nshingīra ibir’ imbere," 
Philippians3:14 mbandaniriza gushika aho dutanguranirwa, ku mpēra y’umuhamagaro w’Imana muri Kristo Yesu wo kuja mw ijuru." 
Philippians3:15 Nukw abatunganijwe uko tungana twiyumvire durtyo; kandi namba har’ ico mwiyumvira ukundi, Imana izokibahishurira na co." 
Philippians3:16 Mugabo rero, ukuri dushitsemwo, abe ari kwo tugenderamwo." 
Philippians3:17 Bene Data, munyigāne, mwitegereze abagenda batwīgāna, nk’uko mudufisekw icitegererezo." 
Philippians3:18 Kuko benshi bagenda ukundi, abo nababgiye kenshi, na none ndabababgira ndira, yukw ar’ abansi b’umusaraba wa Kristo," 
Philippians3:19 iherezo ryabo n’uguhona, imana yabo n’inda, biratana ibiteye isoni vyabo, ivy’ isi ni vyo bababaye." 
Philippians3:20 Tweho i wacu ni mw ijuru, ni ho twiteze Umukiza kw azova, ni we Mwami Yesu Kristo," 
Philippians3:21 azohindura imibiri y’ubufafara bgacu, ishushanywe n’umubiri w’ubgiza bgiwe, nk’ukw afise ubushobozi bumubashisha kwigandurira vyose." 
Philippians4:1 Nuko rero, bene Data, abo nkunda mporanira igishika, mur’ umunezero wanje n’igitsibo nambaye, muhagarare mushikamye murtyo muri mu Mwami wacu, abo nkunda." 
Philippians4:2 Ndahanūra Ewodiya, ndahanūra na Sintike, ngo bahūrize imitima mu Mwami wacu." 
Philippians4:3 Kandi nawe, ndakwinginga, uwo dufatanije igikorwa vy’ukuri, wame ufasha abo bagore, kuko bārwananye nanje mu kurwanira ubutumwa bgiza, bo na Kilementi n’abandi bāfatanya nanje, amazina yabo yanditswe mu gitabo c’ubugingo." 
Philippians4:4 Mwame munezererwa mu Mwami wacu imisi yose; ndabivuze ubugira kabiri: ni munezerwe. 
Philippians4:5 Ubugwaneza bganyu bumenywe n’abantu bose; Umwami wacu ari hafi. 
Philippians4:6 Ntimugire ico mwiganyira, ariko muri vyose ivyo mugomba bimenyeshwe Imana, mu gusenga no mu kwinginga bifatanije no gukenguruka." 
Philippians4:7 Maz’ amahoro y’Imana aruta uko yomenywa n’umuntu wese, azoshibamira imitima yanyu n’ivyiyumviro vyanyu muri Kristo Yesu" 
Philippians4:8 Ibisigaye bene Data, ivy’ ukuri vyose, ivyo kwubahwa vyose, ibigororotse vyose, ibitānduye vyose, ivy’ igikundiro vyose, ibishimwa vyose, ni haba harih’ ingeso nziza, ni haba hariho gushimwa, abe ari vyo mwiyumvira." 
Philippians4:9 Ivyo mwize, ivyo mwākiriye, ivyo mwumvise, ivyo mwambonanye, abe ari vyo mukora: ni ho Imana Nyen’ amahoro izobana namwe." 
Philippians4:10 Ariko ndanezererewe cane mu Mwami wacu kuk’ ubu mwahavuye mukongera kubabara ivyanje: kandi mwaranabibabara, ariko mukabura uburyo." 
Philippians4:11 Simbivuze kubg’ ubukene, kuko nize kubumbga n’ivyo mfise uko ndi kose." 
Philippians4:12 Nzi gucishwa bugufi, nzi no kugira umurengera; muri cose no muri vyose nātiwe ibanga ryo mu vyo guhāga no mu vyo gusonza, ryo mu vyo kugira umurengera no mu vyo gukena." 
Philippians4:13 Nshobozwa vyose n’ūmpa inkomezi. 
Philippians4:14 Ariko mwagize neza, kuko mwafatanije nanje amarushwa." 
Philippians4:15 Kandi yemwe Bafilipi, namwe n’ico muzi yuko mw itanguriro ry’ubutumwa bgiza, hamwe nava i Makedoniya, ata rindi shengero rya Kristo ryafatanije nanje mu vyo gutanga no guhabga, atari mwebge mwenyene." 
Philippians4:16 Kuko n’i Tesalonike na ho mwandungikiyeyo ivyo kummara ubukene si rimwe ni kabiri kose. 
Philippians4:17 S’uko ndondera ingabire, ariko ndondera imbuto zigwiririkanya amaronko yanyu." 
Philippians4:18 Ariko mfise ibinkwiye vyose, mfise umurengera: ndahāze, kuko mpāwe na Epafurodito ivyo mwarungitse, ar’ umubabge umota neza, ikimazi cemewe gihimbara Imana." 
Philippians4:19 Kand’ Imana yanje izobamara ubukene bganyu bgose, nk’ukw itunga ry’ubgiza ryayo riri ryo muri Kristo Yesu." 
Philippians4:20 Nukw icubahiro kibe ic’ Imana yacu, ni yo Data wa twese, ibihe bitazoshira. Amen." 
Philippians4:21 Muntahirize abera bose bo muri Kristo Yesu. Bene Data turi kumwe barabatasha. 
Philippians4:22 Abera bose barabatasha, cane‐cane abo mu rugo kwa Kayisari." 
Philippians4:23 Ubuntu bg’Umwami Yesu Kristo bubane n’imitima yanyu. 
Colossians1:1 Paulo, nagizwe intumwa ya Kristo Yesu n’ukw Imana yabigomvye, na Timoteyo mwene Data," 
Colossians1:2 turabandikiye bene Data bo muri Kristo bera b’abizigirwa, mur’ i Kolosayi. Ubuntu n’amahoro bibe muri mwebge biva ku Mana Data wa twese." 
Colossians1:3 Dushima Imana Se w’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, twama tubasengera ubudasība," 
Colossians1:4 kuko twumvise ukwizera Kristo Yesu kwanyu, n’urukundo mufitiye abera bose," 
Colossians1:5 kubg’ ivyizigirwa mwabīkiwe mw ijuru, ivyo mwumvise kera, mw ijambo ry’ukuri kw’ ubutumwa bgiza," 
Colossians1:6 bgābashitseko, nk’uko buri mw isi yose bgama imbuto bugwira: kandi no muri mwebge bugenza burtyo, uhereye wa musi mwumviye mukamenya ubuntu bg’Imana vy’ukuri:" 
Colossians1:7 nk’uko mwigishijwe na Epafura uwo dukunda, umugurano mugenzi wacu, ni we mukozi wa Kristo wo kwizigirwa abagaburira ivya Kristo mu gishingo cacu," 
Colossians1:8 kandi ni we yatumenyesheje urukundo rwanyu muhabga na Mpwemu. 
Colossians1:9 Ni co gituma natwe, uhereye igihe twavyumviye, tudahengeshanya kubasengera, no kubasabira ngo mwuzuzwe ukumenya ivy’ igomba n’ubgenge bgose no kumenya ivy’ impwemu," 
Colossians1:10 kugira ngo mugende nk’uko bibereye ab’ Umwami wacu, mumunezereza muri vyose, mwama imbuto mu bikorwa vyiza vyose, mugwizwa no kumenya Imana," 
Colossians1:11 mushobozwa n’ubushobozi bgose, nk’ukw inkomezi z’ubgiza bgayo ziri, ngo mwihangane rwose, ntimurambirwe, mubigiranye umunezero." 
Colossians1:12 Mushime Data wa twese yabashoboje kuraganwa n’abera umwandu wo mu muco; 
Colossians1:13 yadukijije ububasha bg’umwiza, atwimurira mu bgami bg’Umwana wiwe akunda." 
Colossians1:14 Mur’ uwo ni ho dufise ugucungurwa, ni kwo guharirwa ivyaha vyacu." 
Colossians1:15 Ni we shusho y’Imana itaboneka, ni we mfura mu vyaremwe vyose:" 
Colossians1:16 kuko muri we ari ho vyose vyaremewe, ivyo mw ijuru n’ivyo mw isi, ibiboneka n’ibitaboneka, ur’ intebe z’icubahiro, ur’ ubgami, ur’ ubukuru, ur’ ububasha: vyose vyaremwe na we, biremerwa kuba ivyiwe." 
Colossians1:17 We yabayeho vyose bitarabaho, kandi muri we vyose ni ho bifataniye." 
Colossians1:18 Ni we mutwe w’umubiri, ni wo shengero: kandi ni we tanguriro, ni we mfura mu kuva mu bapfuye, kugira ngw abe agaheta muri vyose." 
Colossians1:19 Kukw Imana yahimbawe n’uk’ ukunengesera kwayo kwose kuba muri we: 
Colossians1:20 kandi yahimbawe no kumuha kwuzuza vyose na yo, ar’ ivyo mw isi, ar’ ivyo mw ijuru, izanishije impore amaraso yo ku musaraba wiwe." 
Colossians1:21 Namwe abāri bāratandukanijwe n’Imana kera, mugahindurwa abansi bayo mu mitima yanyu n’ivyo mwakoze bibi," 
Colossians1:22 none yabuzurije na yo mu mubiri wiwe w’umuntu kubg’ urupfu yapfuye, ngw abashikane imbere yayo mur’ abera, mudafise agasembga, mutagira ico mwogawa;" 
Colossians1:23 asangwa muhora mwizeye, mushinzwe neza mutanyiganyiga, mudatirimuka mu vyizigiro biheshwa n’ubutumwa mwumvise, bgavuzwe mu bāremwe bose bo musi y’ijuru, ubgo jewe Paulo nacikiye umukozi wabgo." 
Colossians1:24 None nnezererewe amagorwa yanje yo kubganyu, kand’ ivyasigaye ku marushwa ya Kristo nanje ndabishitsa mu mubiri wanje, kubg’ umubiri wiwe, ni wo shengero," 
Colossians1:25 iryo nacikiye umukozi, nk’uko nahawe n’Imana ububgiriza bgo kugaburira mwebge, kugira ngo nkwize ijambo ry’Imana rishitse," 
Colossians1:26 ni ryo banga ryari ryarahishijwe uhereye kera hose n’ibihe vyose, ariko noneho ryahishuriwe abera bayo," 
Colossians1:27 abo Imana yakunze kumenyesha itunga ry’ubgiza bg’iri banga, rivugwa mu banyamahanga, ni ryo Kristo ari muri mwebge, ivyizigiro vyo kuzoronka ubgiza." 
Colossians1:28 Natwe ni we twamamaza, duhanūra umuntu wese, twigishisha umuntu wese ubgenge bgose, ngo dushikirize Imana umuntu wese ahīngūriwe muri Kristo:" 
Colossians1:29 ico ni co kintamisha, mbirwanira nk’uk’ ubushobozi bgiwe buri, bunkoreramwo bishimitse." 
Colossians2:1 Ndagomba ko mumenya ukuntu mbarwanira intambara, mwe n’ab’i Lawodikiya n’abatarankubita ijisho bose uko bangana," 
Colossians2:2 kugira ngw imitima yabo ireme, kuko bamatanirijwe mu rukundo ngo bahabge itunga ryose ry’ugutahura ata mazinda, babone kumenya ibanga ry’Imana, ni ryo Kristo," 
Colossians2:3 muri we ni ho itunga ryose ry’ubgenge n’ukumenya ryahishijwe. 
Colossians2:4 Mvuze ivyo kugira ngo ntihagire ūbahendagirisha amagambo y’inyosha. 
Colossians2:5 Kuko naho ntari kumwe namwe ku mubiri, ndi kumwe namwe ku mutima, nnezerewe kandi mbona ugushira hamwe kwanyu kwiza, n’ugushikama mu kwizera Kristo kwanyu." 
Colossians2:6 Nuko nk’uko mwākiriye Kristo Yesu Umwami wacu, abe ari ko mugendera muri we," 
Colossians2:7 mushinze imizi muri we, mwubakwa muri we, mushikamishijwe n’ukwizera nk’uko mwigishijwe, murushiriza gushima." 
Colossians2:8 Mwirinde, ntihakagire ūbagira inyagano, abanyagishije ubgenge bg’abantu ar’ ibihendo vy’ubusa, bikurikira akaronda k’imigenzo y’abantu, bikurikira ivya mbere vyo mw isi, bidakurikira Kristo." 
Colossians2:9 Kuko muri we ari ho haba ukunengesera kwose kw’Ubumana mu buryo bg’umubiri. 
Colossians2:10 Kandi munengeserezwa no kumubamwo, ni we mutwe w’ubukuru bgose n’ububasha bgose." 
Colossians2:11 Kandi muri we mwākebge ugukebga kutar’ ukw’ intoke, hamwe mwiyambura akameremere k’umubiri, ni kwo gukebga kwo muri Kristo;" 
Colossians2:12 kuko mwahambanywe na we mw ibatizwa, ni ho kandi mwazuranywe na we, kubgo kwizera ubushobozi bg’Imana yamuzuye mu bapfuye." 
Colossians2:13 Kandi hamwe mwari mugipfuye mwishwe n’ibicumuro vyanyu n’ukudakebga kw’imibiri yanyu, yabagiranye bazima na we, imaze kuduharira ibicumuro vyacu vyose," 
Colossians2:14 ihanaguye n’icete kitwagiriza, kirimw’ amabgirizwa cāduhama, igikūra hagati yacu na yo, ikibamba ku musaraba." 
Colossians2:15 Kandi yambuye abakuru n’abafise ububasha, ibateterereza mu maso ya bose, ibashorera bafashwe mpiri kubg’ uwo musaraba." 
Colossians2:16 Nuko ntihakagire ūbahinyura ku biribga canke ku binyobga, canke mu vy’ imisi mikuru canke mu vy’ ukwezi kubonetse canke mu vy’ isabato:" 
Colossians2:17 ivyo vyar’ igitūtu c’ivyari birāriye kuzoza, arik’ umutumba ubgawo n’uwa Kristo." 
Colossians2:18 Ntihakagire umuntu abagunga impēra yanyu, nk’uko yigombera ubgiwe, ayibagungishije kwicisha bugufi no gusenga abamarayika, aguma mu vyo yabonye gusa, atewe kwihimbariza ubusa n’ubgenge bg’akameremere kiwe," 
Colossians2:19 kand’ atifatanya na wa Mutwe, kuri wo umubiri wawo wose, ufashijwe n’ingingo n’imitsi, ugateranywa neza na vyo, ni ho uronka gukura kwawo gutangwa n’Imana." 
Colossians2:20 Asangwa mwarapfanye na Kristo, mukareka ivya mbere vy’isi, n’iki gituma mwemera kuganzwa na ya mabgirizwa, nk’abazokwama bari kw isi —" 
Colossians2:21 ngo, Ntugafateko, ntugatamireko, ntugakoreko;" 
Colossians2:22 kand’ ivyo vyose biba biheze iyo birīwe — mukumvira ivyagezwe n’abantu n’inyigisho zabo? 
Colossians2:23 Ayo mabgirizwa koko afise ishusho y’ubgenge, kukw abgiriza gusenga nk’ukw abantu bīrāritse, no kwicisha bugufi, no kwibabaza umubiri, ariko ntagira ikimazi co kubuza ukwifuza kw’akameremere k’umuntu." 
Colossians3:1 None rer’ asangwa mwarazuranywe na Kristo, murondere ibiri hejuru, iyo Kristo ari, avyagiye i buryo bg’Imana." 
Colossians3:2 Mushire imitima ku biri hejuru, ntimuyishire ku biri mw isi." 
Colossians3:3 Kuko mwapfuye, kand’ ubugingo bganyu bukaba buhishanijwe na Kristo mu Mana." 
Colossians3:4 Kristo, ni we bugingo bgacu, ni yerekanwa, namwe muzoca mwerekananwa na we muri mu bgiza." 
Colossians3:5 Nuko mwice ingingo zanyu ziri mw isi, ubushakanyi, ibihumanya, ukwifuza kw’umubiri, ukwifuza kubi kwose, no kwifuza ivy’ abandi, ni kwo gusenga ibigirwamana;" 
Colossians3:6 ivyo ni vyo bizanira uburake bg’Imana abantu b’intabarirwa. 
Colossians3:7 Namwe mwabigenderamwo kera, hamwe mwāba muri vyo." 
Colossians3:8 Ariko noneho mwiyambure n’ibi vyose: uburake, kujingitwa, urwanko rw’ubusa, gucokorana, kandi ntihakagire amagambo ateye isoni ava mu kanwa kanyu." 
Colossians3:9 Ntimukabeshane, kuko mwiyambuye umuntu wa kera n’ibikorwa vyiwe," 
Colossians3:10 mukambara umuntu musha, ahindurwa musha ngw agire ubgenge, amere nk’ishusho y’Iyamuremye:" 
Colossians3:11 aho ntihaba Umugiriki cank’ Umuyuda, uwakebge cank’ ūtākebge, ūdebagura cank’ Umusikiti, umugurano cank’ uwidegemvya; ariko Kristo ni vyose, kand’ ari muri bose." 
Colossians3:12 Nuko rero, nk’uko bibereye abātoranijwe n’Imana bera bakundwa na yo, mwambare umutima w’ikigongwe, n’ineza, n’ukwicisha bugufi, n’ugutekereza, n’ukwihangana," 
Colossians3:13 mwihanganirana, muharirana, iy’ umuntu agize ico apfa n’uwundi. Nk’uk’ Umwami wacu yabahariye, namwe abe ari ko muharirana." 
Colossians3:14 Ikigeretse kur’ ivyo vyose mwambare urukundo, ni rwo mugozi uzana gutungana." 
Colossians3:15 Kand’ amahoro ya Kristo aganze mu mitima yanyu, ayo mwahamagariwe ngo mube umubiri umwe: kandi mube abama bakenguruka." 
Colossians3:16 Ijambo rya Kristo ribe muri mwebge rigwiriye, ririmw’ ubgenge bgose: mwigishanye, muhanūrane, muririmba zaburi n’indirimbo n’amatazirano y’ivya Mpwemu, muririmbire Imana mu mitima yanyu mubiheshwa n’ubuntu bgayo." 
Colossians3:17 Kand’ ivyo muzokora vyose, mu majambo no mu bikorwa, muhore mubikora vyose mw izina ry’Umwami Yesu, mushima Imana Data wa twese kubg’ uwo." 
Colossians3:18 Bagore, mugamburukire abagabo banyu, nk’uko bibereye abari mu Mwami wacu." 
Colossians3:19 Bagabo, mukunde abagore banyu, ntimubabere umururazi." 
Colossians3:20 Bana, mwumvire abavyeyi banyu muri vyose, kukw ivyo ari vyo bishimwa mu Mwami wacu." 
Colossians3:21 Ba se, ntimukaratse abana banyu, ngo ntibaranduke imitima." 
Colossians3:22 Bagurano, mwumvire ba shobuja bo ku mubiri muri vyose, atar’ iyo babahagarikiye gusa, nk’abanezereza abantu, ariko mubakorere mutagira ubupfunya mu mitima yanyu, mwubaha Shobuja mukuru." 
Colossians3:23 Ivyo mukora vyose, mubikore bivuye mu mutima, nk’abakorera Shobuja mukuru, ntimube nk’abakorera abantu," 
Colossians3:24 muzi yuko muzohabga impēra na Shobuja mukuru, ni yo wa mwandu. Shobuja uwo Kristo ni we mukorera." 
Colossians3:25 Kuk’ ūgabitanya azokwihōrwa nk’uko yagabitanije: kandi nta kurobanura ku butoni. 
Colossians4:1 Ba shebuja, namwe ni mugirire abagurano banyu ibigororotse n’ibibereye, kuko muzi yuko namwe mufise Shobuja mw ijuru." 
Colossians4:2 Mukovye mu gusenga, mukubemwo maso, mushima;" 
Colossians4:3 kandi natwe nyene mudusengere, kugira ngw Imana itwugururire urugi rwo kuvuga ijambo ryayo, tuvuge ibanga rya Kristo, iryo mbohewe," 
Colossians4:4 kugira ngo ndariserure nk’uko nkwiye kuvuga. 
Colossians4:5 Mugendane ubgenge ku bo hanze, mugura uburyo mubugwiza." 
Colossians4:6 Imvugo zanyu zamane ubuntu bg’Imana, zirunzwe umunyu, kugira ngo mumenye ingene mukwiye kwishura umuntu wese." 
Colossians4:7 Tukiko mwene Data dukunda, umukozi w’umwizigirwa, umugenzi dukorana mu Mwami wacu, azobīgānira ivyanje vyose." 
Colossians4:8 Ni we mbatumyeko kubg’ ivyo nyene, ngo mumenye ivyacu, kandi ngw aremeshe imitima yanyu," 
Colossians4:9 ndamutumanye na Onesimo mwene Data w’umwizigirwa, uwo dukunda, yavuye i wanyu; bazobīgānira ivy’ ino vyose." 
Colossians4:10 Arisitariko, uwo dusangiye umunyororo, arabatasha; na Mariko, mwene se wabo wa Barunaba, arabatasha, umwe mwabgirizwa ivyiwe: ni yaramuka aje i wanyu muze mumwākīre." 
Colossians4:11 Na Yesu, ari we Yusito, arabatasha: abo bonyene bo mu bākebge ni bo bakorana nanje kubg’ ubgami bg’Imana, kandi bāmmaze umubabaro." 
Colossians4:12 Epafura w’i wanyu, umugurano wa Kristo Yesu, arabatasha, yama abarwanira mu gusenga kwiwe kugira ngo mushikame, mutunganye rwose, mumenya neza mudakekeranya ivy’ Imana igomba vyose." 
Colossians4:13 Ndamushingira intahe yukw abagirira umwete mwinshi, mwebge n’ab’i Lawodikiya n’ab’i Hiyerapoli." 
Colossians4:14 Luka, umuganga akundwa, na Dema, barabatasha." 
Colossians4:15 Muntahirize bene Data b’i Lawodikiya, na Numfa, n’ishengero ryo mu nzu yiwe." 
Colossians4:16 Kand’ iki cete ni mwaheza kugisomerwa, muze mwitwaririke ko gisomerwa ishengero ry’i Lawodikiya; kandi namwe muze musome ikizova i Lawodikiya nyene." 
Colossians4:17 Kandi muze mubarire Arukipo, mut’ Urābe igikorwa c’ubusuku wahawe mu Mwami wacu, ucuzuze." 
Colossians4:18 Uku ni kwo gutasha kwanje Paulo, kwanditswe n’ukwanje kuboko. Mwibuke iminyororo yanje. Ubuntu bubane namwe." 
1Thessalonians1:1 Paulo na Siluwano na Timoteyo turabandikiye abo mw ishengero ry’i Tesalonike, bari mu Mana Data wa twese no mu Mwami Yesu Kristo: ubuntu bube muri mwebge n’amahoro." 
1Thessalonians1:2 Mwese tubashimira Imana imisi yose, tubahoza mu kanwa uko dusenze," 
1Thessalonians1:3 twibuka ubudasība ibikorwa vyanyu biva ku kwizera, n’ubutame buva mu rukundo, n’ukwihangana kuva ku kwizigira Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, imbere y’Imana yacu, ni yo Data wa twese." 
1Thessalonians1:4 Bene Data bakundwa n’Imana, tuzi yuko mwatoranijwe na yo:" 
1Thessalonians1:5 kuk’ ubutumwa bgacu butābashitseko ar’ amajambo yonyene ariko bgarimwo n’ubushobozi na Mpwemu Yera, no kumara amazinda rwose; namwe murazi ubugene twari tumeze hagati muri mwebge kubganyu." 
1Thessalonians1:6 Namwe mwaratwīgānye, mwīgāna n’Umwami wacu, mumaze kwakīrira ijambo ry’Imana mu marushwa menshi, munezerejwe na Mpwemu Yera," 
1Thessalonians1:7 bituma muba icitegererezo c’abizera bose bar’ i Makedoniya no muri Akaya. 
1Thessalonians1:8 Kuko muri mwebge humvikanye ijambo ry’Umwami wacu, kandi ntiryumvikanye i Makedoniya no muri Akaya honyene, arik’ ukwizera Imana kwanyu kwaramamaye hose; bituma tutarinda kugira ico tuvuga mur’ ivyo." 
1Thessalonians1:9 Kuko bose bīvugira ubgabo inkuru z’ingene twaje muri mwebge, kand’ ingene mwahindukiriye Imana, mugaheba ibigirwamana, ngo mukorere Imana nyakuri kandi nzima," 
1Thessalonians1:10 kandi ngo mwitege Umwana wayo kw ava mw ijuru, umwe yazura imukuye mu bapfuye, ni Yesu, adukiza uburake bugira buze." 
1Thessalonians2:1 Bene Data, ubganyu murazi yuk’ ugushika muri mwebge kwacu kutābaye ukw’ ubusa:" 
1Thessalonians2:2 ariko tumaze kubabarizwa i Filipi no kuhatētererezwa, nk’uko muzi, dushira amanga mu Mana yacu kubgira mwebge ubutumwa bgiza bg’Imana turi mu ntambara nyinshi." 
1Thessalonians2:3 Kuk’ uguhanūra kwacu kutava mu buzimire, canke mu buhumane, kand’ atar’ ukw’ ubugunge:" 
1Thessalonians2:4 ariko nk’ukw Imana yatwemeye ko tur’ abo kuzezwa ubutumwa, ni ko tuvuga. Ntituvuga nk’abagomba kunezereza abantu, ariko nk’abagomba kunezereza Imana igerageza imitima yacu." 
1Thessalonians2:5 Kukw ata na rimwe twigeze kuvuga ijambo dushashe akarimi, murabizi, cank’ ijambo ryo guhisha ukwifuza, Imana ni yo cabona c’ivyo." 
1Thessalonians2:6 Kandi ntitwarondera icubahiro co ku bantu, ari kuri mwebge canke ku bandi: naho tuba twarashoboye kubaremēra, kuko tur’ intumwa za Kristo." 
1Thessalonians2:7 Ariko twaritonda hagati muri mwebge, nk’uk’ umurezi abungabunga abana biwe." 
1Thessalonians2:8 Ni ko twabagirira igishika, ni co catumye duhimbarwa no kubaha, s’ubutumwa bgiza bg’Imana gusa, ariko n’ubgacu bugingo na bgo, kuko mwabaye abo dukunda rwose." 
1Thessalonians2:9 Bene Data, muribuka ubutame bgacu n’ubucumukure; twābabgira ubutumwa bgiza bg’Imana twikenurira umurango n’ijoro, kugira ngo ntihagire uwo muri mwebge turemēra." 
1Thessalonians2:10 Mwebge mur’ ivyabona hamwe n’Imana vy’ingene twamerera mwebge abizera, tur’ abera, tugororoka, tutarik’ umugayo:" 
1Thessalonians2:11 nk’uko muzi ingene twari tumeze ku muntu wese muri mwebge, nk’uko se amera ku bana biwe, tubahanūra, tubaremesha, dushinga intahe," 
1Thessalonians2:12 kugira ngo mugende nk’uko bibereye ab’ Imana, ibahamagarira kuja mu bgami bgayo no mu bgiza bgayo." 
1Thessalonians2:13 Natwe igituma dushima Imana ubudasība, n’uko hamwe mwākīra ijambo ry’ubutumwa mwatwumvanye, ni ryo ry’Imana, mutāryemeye nk’ijambo ry’abantu, ariko nk’ijambo ry’Imana, nk’uko riri koko, rikorera muri mwebge abizera." 
1Thessalonians2:14 Namwe bene Data, mwīgānye amashengero y’Imana y’i Yudaya, ari muri Kristo Yesu, kukw ivyo mwābabajwe n’ubgoko bganyu ari bimwe n’ivy’ abo bābabajwe n’Abayuda," 
1Thessalonians2:15 bishe Umwami Yesu n’abāvugishwa n’Imana, kandi natwe bāratwirukanye, ntibānezereje Imana, barwanya abantu bose;" 
1Thessalonians2:16 batubuza kubarira abanyamahanga ngo bakire; na ntaryo buzuza ingero y’ivyaha vyabo. Arik’ uburake bububiriye kubamara rwose. 
1Thessalonians2:17 Ariko twebge, bene Data, hamwe twatandukanywa namwe igihe gito ubg’ amaso, ariko si mu mutima, twarushirije kugira umwete wo kubonana namwe imbonankubone, tubafitiye inkumbu nyinshi:" 
1Thessalonians2:18 kuko twagomba kuza i wanyu, mbere jewe Paulo kubigomba si rimwe ni kabiri kose, Satani akatubuza." 
1Thessalonians2:19 Non’ ivyizigiro vyacu n’iki, cank’ umunezero, cank’ igitsibo co mu mutwe twirata? Mbega si mwebge, imbere y’Umwami wacu Yesu ah’ azozira?" 
1Thessalonians2:20 Kukw ari mwebge cubahiro cacu n’umunezero wacu. 
1Thessalonians3:1 Nuko tutagishoboye kwihangana, dushima gusigara twenyene muri Atenayi," 
1Thessalonians3:2 dutuma Timoteyo, mwene Data, umukozi w’Imana agabura ubutumwa bgiza bga Kristo, ngw abakomeze abaremeshe ku vy’ ukwizera kwanyu," 
1Thessalonians3:3 kugira ngo ntihagire uwo muri mwebge anyiganyizwa n’ayo marushwa: kuk’ ubganyu muzi yukw ar’ ico twashiriweho nyene. 
1Thessalonians3:4 Kandi hamwe twari kumwe namwe, twababūriye yuko tutazobura kubabazwa; kandi ni ko vyābaye, murabizi." 
1Thessalonians3:5 Nanje ni co catumye ntuma iyo, bitakinkundiye kwihangana, kugira ngo mmenye ukwizera kwanyu, nikenga ko wa musukanyi yoba yarabasutse, natwe tukaba twaratamijwe n’ubusa." 
1Thessalonians3:6 Ariko none Timoteyo arashitse, avuye i wanyu, atuzaniye inkuru nziza y’ukwizera kwanyu n’urukundo rwanyu, kandi yuko mutwibuka neza imisi yose, mudukumbura mugomba kubonana natwe, nk’uko natwe tubakumbura." 
1Thessalonians3:7 Ni co catumye bene Data, turemeshwa kubganyu n’ukwizera kwanyu, mu mubabaro wacu wose no mu marushwa." 
1Thessalonians3:8 Kuko none turiho, asangwa muhagaze mu Mwami." 
1Thessalonians3:9 N’ishimwe ki twoshobora kwishura Imana kubganyu, kubg’ umunezero wose tubanezererwa imbere y’Imana yacu?" 
1Thessalonians3:10 Dusenga cane ijoro n’umurango kugira ngo twibonanire namwe imbonankubone, tunonosore ivyasigaye ku kwizera kwanyu." 
1Thessalonians3:11 Non’ Imana yacu ubgayo, ni yo Data wa twese, n’Umwami wacu Yesu, agorore inzira yacu yo kuza iyo." 
1Thessalonians3:12 Namwe Umwami wacu abagwirize, abasagirize urukundo mukundana, no gukunda abandi bose, nk’uko natwe tumeze kuri mwebge:" 
1Thessalonians3:13 kugira ngw aremeshe imitima yanyu, ntigire umugayo, ibe iyera imbere y’Imana yacu ni yo Data wa twese, iz’ isangwe irtyo ah’ Umwami wacu Yesu azozananira n’abera biwe bose." 
1Thessalonians4:1 Nuko bene Data, ibisigaye, turabinginga tubahanūra mu Mwami Yesu, nk’uko mwize kuri twebge ingene mukwiye kugenda no kunezereza Imana (kandi ni ko mugenda), murushirize cane kugenza murtyo." 
1Thessalonians4:2 Murazi ivyagezwe twahawe n’Umwami Yesu kubabarira ivy’ ari vyo. 
1Thessalonians4:3 Ico Imana igomba, n’ukwezwa kwanyu, ko mwirinda ubushakanyi;" 
1Thessalonians4:4 kugira ng’ umuntu wese muri mwebge amenye kuganziriza uwiwe mubiri mu kwezwa no mu kuwubaha," 
1Thessalonians4:5 atari mu buryo bgo kwāngāza umutima mu vyifuzo, nk’ukw abanyamahanga batazi Imana bagira;" 
1Thessalonians4:6 ng’umuntu wese ntarenge ibikwiye, kandi ntagunge mwene Data wundi kur’ ivyo, kuk’ Umwami wacu ar’ umuhōzi kur’ ivyo vyose, nk’uko twababūriye tubishimikiye." 
1Thessalonians4:7 Kukw Imana itāduhamagariye guhumana, ariko yaduhamagariye kwezwa." 
1Thessalonians4:8 Ni co gituma ūvyanka ataba yanse umuntu arikw aba yanse Imana, kand’ ari yo ibaha Mpwemu wayo Yera." 
1Thessalonians4:9 Arikw ivyo gukunda bene Data ntimurinda kuvyandikirwa, kuk’ ubganyu mwigishijwe n’Imana gukundana;" 
1Thessalonians4:10 kandi ni ko nyene mugiriranira na bene Data bose b’i Makedoniya hose. Ariko bene Data turabahanūra ngo murushirize kugira rwinshi. 
1Thessalonians4:11 Kandi mushishikare kwiyorosha, no gukora ivyanyu, no gukoresha amaboko yanyu, nk’uko twababariye," 
1Thessalonians4:12 kugira ngo mugendane ingeso nziza ku bo hanze, kandi mutagira ico mukennye." 
1Thessalonians4:13 Ariko bene Data, ntitugomba ko muyoberwa ivy’ abasinzira itiro ry’urupfu, ngo ntimubabare nka ba bandi badafise ivyizigiro." 
1Thessalonians4:14 Uko twizera yuko Yesu yapfuye akazuka, abe ari ko twizera yukw abāsinziririye muri Yesu, Imana izobazanana na we." 
1Thessalonians4:15 Iki ni co tubabgira, n’ijambo ry’Umwami twashikirijwe, yuko twebge abazoba bakiriho, dusigaye gushitsa ku kuza kw’Umwami wacu, tutazokwitangira imbere y’abasinziriye na gatoya." 
1Thessalonians4:16 Kuk’ Umwami wacu ubgiwe azoza, amanutse avuye mw ijuru, aranguruye ijwi rirenga, hamwe n’akāmo k’umumarayika mukuru, n’inzamba y’Imana. Maz’ abapfiriye muri Kristo ni bo bazobanza kuzuka;" 
1Thessalonians4:17 maze natwe abazoba bakiriho, dusigaye, tuzoca duteruranwa na bo mu bicu, dusanganirire Umwami mu kirēre. Ni ho tuzokwama tubana n’Umwami." 
1Thessalonians4:18 Nuko mwiruranishe ayo majambo. 
1Thessalonians5:1 Ariko bene Data, ivy’ ibihe n’imisi ntimurinda kuvyandikirwa." 
1Thessalonians5:2 Kuk’ ubganyu muzi neza yuk’ umusi w’Umwami wacu uzoza nk’ukw igisuma kiza mw ijoro. 
1Thessalonians5:3 Aho bazoba bavuga, bati Har’ amahoro, nta nkomanzi; ni ho uguhona kuzobazako giturumbuka, nk’ukw ibise biza ku mugore akuriwe, kandi ntibazokwikiza na gatoya." 
1Thessalonians5:4 Ariko mweho, bene Data, ntimuri mu mwiza, ng’uwo musi ubūbīre nk’igisuma:" 
1Thessalonians5:5 kuko mwese mur’ abana b’umuco n’abana b’umurango. Ntitur’ ab’ ijoro cank’ ab’ umwiza. 
1Thessalonians5:6 Nuko rero ntidusinzire nka ba bandi, ariko twame tugavye, twirinde ibiboreza." 
1Thessalonians5:7 Kukw abasinzira basinzira mw ijoro, n’ababorerwa baborerwa mw ijoro." 
1Thessalonians5:8 Ariko tweho, ko tur’ ab’ umurango, twirinde ibiboreza, twambaye icuma gikīngīra igikiriza c’ukwizera n’urukundo, kandi twambaye nk’inkofero ukwizigira agakiza." 
1Thessalonians5:9 Kukw Imana itādushiriyeho kuturakira, ariko yadushiriyeho guheshwa agakiza n’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo," 
1Thessalonians5:10 ni we yadupfiriye kugira ngo tubaneho na we, ar’ iyo turi maso canke dusinziriye itiro ry’urupfu." 
1Thessalonians5:11 Nuko muhanūrane, mukomezanye, nk’uko mubikora nyene." 
1Thessalonians5:12 Ariko bene Data, turabinginga, mumenye abakora muri mwebge bagatama, babaganza mu Mwami wacu, bakabahanūra," 
1Thessalonians5:13 mububahe rwose mu rukundo kubg’ igikorwa cabo. Mubane amahoro. 
1Thessalonians5:14 Kandi turabahanūra, bene Data, muhubūre abasaragurika, muremeshe abarandutse imitima, muramire abanyantege nke, mwihanganire bose." 
1Thessalonians5:15 Mwirinde, ntihagire umuntu yīhōra uwundi ikibi yamugiriye, ariko mwame mukurikira iciza mu vyo mugiriranira no mu vyo mugirira abandi bose." 
1Thessalonians5:16 Munezerwe imisi yose; 
1Thessalonians5:17 musenge ubudasība; 
1Thessalonians5:18 mwame mukenguruka muri vyose, kukw ico ari co Imana ibagombako muri Kristo Yesu." 
1Thessalonians5:19 Ntimukazimye Mpwemu; 
1Thessalonians5:20 ntimugakengere ivy’ abavugishwa n’Imana; 
1Thessalonians5:21 mugerageze vyose, mugumye ivyiza," 
1Thessalonians5:22 mwirinde icitwa ikibi cose. 
1Thessalonians5:23 Kand’ Imana Nyen’ amahoro ibe ari yo ibeza rwose: kand’ impwemu yanyu n’ubugingo n’umubiri vyose hamwe bizigamwe, ngo bize bisangwe bitagira umugayo, ah’ Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo azozira." 
1Thessalonians5:24 Ībahamagara n’iyo kwizigirwa; no kubikora izobikora. 
1Thessalonians5:25 Bene Data, mudusengere." 
1Thessalonians5:26 Muramukishe bene Data kugumbirana kwera. 
1Thessalonians5:27 Ndabarahiye Umwami wacu, iki cete ntikize kibure gusomerwa bene Data bose." 
1Thessalonians5:28 Ubuntu bg’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo bubane namwe. 
2Thessalonians1:1 Paulo na Siluwano na Timoteyo turabandikiye abo mw ishengero ry’i Tesalonike, bari mu Mana Data wa twese no mu Mwami Yesu Kristo:" 
2Thessalonians1:2 ubuntu n’amahoro bibe muri mwebge, biva ku Mana Data wa twese no ku Mwami Yesu Kristo." 
2Thessalonians1:3 Biradukwiye kwama tubashimira Imana, bene Data, nk’uko bikwiye, kuk’ ukwizera kwanyu gukura cane, n’urukundo rw’ umuntu wese muri mwebge mukundana rugwira." 
2Thessalonians1:4 Ni co gituma ubgacu tubirata mu mashengero y’Imana, kubg’ ukwihangana kwanyu n’ukwizera mu guhamwa kwanyu kwose n’amagorwa mushinyiriza." 
2Thessalonians1:5 Ico n’ikimenyetso co guca amateka kw’ Imana kugororotse, ngo muze mwemererwe gushika mu bgami bg’Imana, ubgo namwe mubabarizwa." 
2Thessalonians1:6 Kukw ar’ ibigororotse ku Mana kwishura amarushwa abayabatera," 
2Thessalonians1:7 no kwishura mwebge abayaterwa kuruhukana natwe, ah’ Umwami Yesu azohishurirwa, ava mw ijuru, azananye n’abamarayika b’ubushobozi bgiwe," 
2Thessalonians1:8 hagati mu muriro waka, yishure guhōrwa abatāmenye Imana n’abatumvira ubutumwa bgiza bg’Umwami wacu Yesu." 
2Thessalonians1:9 Bazohanwa, ni kwo guhona kw’ibihe bidashira, kuva mu nyonga h’Umwami no mu bgiza bg’ubushobozi bgiwe," 
2Thessalonians1:10 ah’ azozira gushimirwa abera biwe kuri wa musi, no gutangarirwa kubg’ abāmwizeye bose, kukw intahe twashinze muri mwebge yemewe." 
2Thessalonians1:11 Ni co gituma tubasengera imisi yose, ngw Imana yacu ibemere ko mumeze nk’uko bibereye ihamagarwa ryanyu, kand’ ishikishe ubushobozi ico munezererwa ciza cose n’igikorwa canyu cose kiva ku kwizera:" 
2Thessalonians1:12 kugira ngw izina ry’Umwami wacu Yesu rishimagizwe muri mwebge, namwe mushimagizwe muri we, nk’uk’ ubuntu bg’Imana yacu n’ubg’ Umwami Yesu Kristo buri." 
2Thessalonians2:1 Turabinginga, bene Data, kubgo kuzoza kw’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo no kuzokoranirizwa kuri we kwacu," 
2Thessalonians2:2 ntimushōke munyiganyiga ngo mugwe igihūmura, canke ngo muhagarike imitima, naho mwoba mubitewe n’impwemu canke n’ijambo canke n’icete kimeze nk’ikivuye kuri twebge, kivuga yuk’ umusi w’Umwami wacu uhejeje gushika." 
2Thessalonians2:3 Ntihakagire umuntu abahenda mu buryo na bumwe, kuk’ utazoza, kwa kureka Imana kutabanje kuboneka, kandi wa muntu w’umugarariji atarahishurwa, ni we mwana wo kuranduka," 
2Thessalonians2:4 umurwanizi yishira hejuru y’icitwa Imana cose cank’ igisengwa; nukw azokwicara mu rusengero rw’ Imana, yiyerekana ngo n’Imana." 
2Thessalonians2:5 Ntimwibuka yuko nababgiye ivyo nkiri kumwe namwe? 
2Thessalonians2:6 Kandi none murazi ikibuza, kugira ngw az’ ahishurwe mu gihe ciwe." 
2Thessalonians2:7 Kukw ibanga ry’umugararizo n’ubu ririko rirakora, mugabo har’ ūbibuza none, gushitsa igihe azokūrirwaho." 
2Thessalonians2:8 Ni ho wa mugarariji azohishurirwa, umwe Umwami Yesu azokwicisha impwemu ziva mu kanwa kiwe, azomutītūza uguseruka kw’ukuza kwiwe." 
2Thessalonians2:9 Ukuza kw’uwo mugarariji kuri mu buryo bg’inkomezi za Satani, kuri n’ubushobozi bgose n’ibimenyetso n’ibitangaza vy’ibinyoma," 
2Thessalonians2:10 n’ubugunge bgose bgo kugabitanya ku bahona, kuko batemeye gukunda ivy’ ukuri ngo bakizwe." 
2Thessalonians2:11 Ni co gituma Imana ibarungikira ubuzimire bubakoreramwo, ngo bizere ibinyoma:" 
2Thessalonians2:12 kugira ngw abatizeye ukuri bose, bagahimbarirwa ukugabitanya, bacirwekw iteka." 
2Thessalonians2:13 Ariko bene Data bakundwa n’Umwami wacu, biradukwiye kwama tubashimira Imana, kuk’ uhereye mbere na mbere Imana yabatoranije ngo muronkere agakiza mu kwezwa na Mpwemu no mu kwizera ukuri." 
2Thessalonians2:14 Ni vyo yabahamagariye, ibahamagarishije ubutumwa bgiza twajejwe, kugira ngo muhabge ubgiza bg’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo." 
2Thessalonians2:15 Nuko bene Data, mushikame, mugumye ivyo mwashikirijwe, mwigishijwe, ar’ ivyo mwigishirijwe mu majambo canke mu cete cacu." 
2Thessalonians2:16 Ariko, Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo ubgiwe, n’Imana Data wa twese, yadukunze, ikaduha kwirurwa imibabaro guhoraho, bo n’ivyizigiro vyiza biheshwa n’ubuntu bgayo," 
2Thessalonians2:17 ibirure mu mitima yanyu, iyikomeze mu gikorwa cose ciza, n’ijambo ryose ryiza." 
2Thessalonians3:1 Ibisigaye bene Data mudusengere, ijambo ry’Umwami wacu ryamamare rishimagizwe, nk’uko biri no muri mwebge," 
2Thessalonians3:2 kandi turokoke abantu babi badadika; kuk’ ukwizera kudafiswe na bose. 
2Thessalonians3:3 Ariko, Umwami n’uwo kwizigirwa, ni we azobashinga neza abarinde wa Mubi." 
2Thessalonians3:4 Kandi twizigiye Umwami ku vyanyu, yukw ivyo tugeze mubikora kandi muzokwama mubikora." 
2Thessalonians3:5 Umwami arōngōre imitima yanyu, ayerekeze ku rukundo rw’Imana no ku kwihangana kwa Kristo." 
2Thessalonians3:6 Ariko bene Data, turabagera mw izina ry’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, kuzibukīra mwene Data wese agenda asaragurika, cank’ adakurikira ivyo mwashikirijwe natwe." 
2Thessalonians3:7 Ubganyu murazi ingene mukwiye kutwīgāna, kuko tutāsaragurika muri mwebge," 
2Thessalonians3:8 ntitwarya ivyo kurya vy’ umuntu n’umwe ku busa, ariko twagira ubutame n’ubucumukure, dukora ku murango no mw ijoro, kugira ngo ntitugire umuntu muri mwebge tugora." 
2Thessalonians3:9 S’uko tutāvyemerewe, ariko n’ukugira ngo tubabere icitegererezo ngo mutwīgāne." 
2Thessalonians3:10 Kuko tukiri kumwe namwe twābageze iki, ng’umuntu wese ni yanka gukora ntākarye." 
2Thessalonians3:11 Kuko twumvise yuko hariho bamwe bo muri mwebge bagenda basaragurika, bama bīneganegera bakīta mu bitabakwiye." 
2Thessalonians3:12 Arikw abameze bartyo turabagera tubahanūra kubg’ Umwami Yesu Kristo, gukora ibikorwa batekereje, babone kurya ivyo bīronkeye ubgabo." 
2Thessalonians3:13 Ariko mweho bene Data, ntimurambirwe no gukora iciza." 
2Thessalonians3:14 Ni hagira umuntu atumvira ijambo ryacu ryo mur’ iki cete, mumwitegereze, ntimufatanye na we, kugira ngw amāramāre." 
2Thessalonians3:15 Ariko ntimumwiyumvire kw ar’ umwansi wanyu, ariko mumuhanūre nka mwene So." 
2Thessalonians3:16 Kand’ Umwami Nyen’ amahoro ubgiwe, yame abaha amahoro ibihe vyose uburyo bgose. Umwami abane namwe mwese." 
2Thessalonians3:17 Uku ni kwo gutasha kwanje Paulo, kwanditswe n’ukwanje kuboko, ni co kimenyetso mu cete canje cose: ni ko nandika." 
2Thessalonians3:18 Ubuntu bg’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo bubane namwe mwese. 
1Timothy1:1 Paulo, intumwa ya Kristo Yesu, nk’uko vyagezwe n’Imana Umukiza wacu na Kristo Yesu ivyizigiro vyacu," 
1Timothy1:2 ndakwandikiye Timoteyo, umwana wanje nyakuri mu kwizera. Ubuntu n’imbabazi n’amahoro bibe kuri wewe, biva ku Mana Data wa twese no kuri Kristo Yesu Umwami wacu." 
1Timothy1:3 Nuko guma muri Efeso, nk’uko nakugīriye inama hamwe naja i Makedoniya, kugira ng’ uteshe ba bandi ntibigishe ibiciye ukundi," 
1Timothy1:4 ntibababare ivy’ imigani y’ibinyoma n’ivyo kuzīrōra ivy’ akārōnda katagira iherezo, bidafasha igikorwa c’Imana gikorera mu kwizera, ariko bizana impāri." 
1Timothy1:5 Arikw inyanduruko y’ukwigisha kwacu n’ukugira ngo bagire urukundo ruva mu mutima utanduye, utarimw’ ijwi ribāgiriza ikibi, no ku kwizera kutar’ ukw’ uburyarya." 
1Timothy1:6 Ivyo bamwe bārabihushije, bata inzira, baja mu bitagira ikimazi kuba ari vyo bavuga," 
1Timothy1:7 bagomba kuba abigisha b’ivyagezwe, ariko ntibatahura ivyo bavuga n’ivyo bashingira intahe babishimikiye." 
1Timothy1:8 Ariko turazi yukw ivyagezwe ari vyiza, iy’ umuntu abigenjeje nk’uko bikwiye ivyagezwe," 
1Timothy1:9 azi yukw ivyagezwe bitāshiriweh’ umugororotsi, ariko vyāshiriweh’ abagarariji n’ibigāba, abatubaha Imana n’abanyavyaha, abanegura ivyayo n’abakora ibizira, abica ba se na ba nyina, abicanyi," 
1Timothy1:10 abashakanyi, abagabo bendana, abanyaga abantu bakabashōra, ababeshi, abarahira nabi, n’ibindi vyose birwanya ukwigisha kuzima," 
1Timothy1:11 gukurikira ubutumwa bg’ubgiza bg’Imana ishemagizwa, ubgo najejwe." 
1Timothy1:12 Ndashimira Kristo Yesu Umwami wacu yabinshoboje, kuko yanyiyumviriye ko nd’uwo kwizigirwa, akampa ubusuku:" 
1Timothy1:13 naho nabanje kumurogotako no kumuhīga no kumwambika ibara. Ariko naragiriwe ikigongwe kuko nabikoze ntabizi ntarizera; 
1Timothy1:14 kand’ ubuntu bg’Umwami wacu bgiyongeranya kuri jewe, bo n’ukwizera n’urukundo rubonerwa muri Kristo Yesu." 
1Timothy1:15 Iri jambo n’iryo kwizerwa, rikwiye kwemerwa rwose, yuko Kristo Yesu yazanywe mw isi no gukiza abanyavyaha: muri bo jewe nd’agahebuza." 
1Timothy1:16 Ariko, icatumye ngirirwa ikigongwe n’ukugira ngo Yesu Kristo yerekanire muri jewe gahebuza, ukwihangana kwiwe kwose, mbe icitegererezo c’abazomwizera bakaronka ubugingo budashira." 
1Timothy1:17 Umwami ahoraho, adapfa, ataboneka, ari we Mana imwe yonyene, igitinyiro n’icubahiro bibe ivyayo, ibihe bitazoshira. Amen." 
1Timothy1:18 Iri bgirizwa ndariguhaye, mwana wanje Timoteyo, nk’ukw abavugishwa n’Imana bākuvuzeko ubga mbere, ng’ ufashwe na vyo kurwana intambara nziza," 
1Timothy1:19 ugumye ukwizera, ufise umutima utarimw’ ijwi rikwagiriza ikibi; iryo bamwe bāshibuye bakamera nk’ubgato busāvye mu vy’ ukwizera." 
1Timothy1:20 Mur’ abo, umwe ni Humenayo na Alekisandero, abo nahaye Satani, kugira ngo bibigishe kutarogota." 
1Timothy2:1 Irya mbere y’ibindi vyose, ndabahanūra kwingingira abantu bose no kubasengera no kubasabira no kubashimira Imana:" 
1Timothy2:2 kandi cane‐cane abami n’abashizwe hejuru bose, kugira ngo twame mu mahoro dutekereje, twubaha Imana tur’ inyankamugayo rwose." 
1Timothy2:3 Ivyo ni vyo vyiza vyemerwa mu nyonga z’Imana Umukiza wacu," 
1Timothy2:4 igomba kw abantu bose bakizwa bagashika ku kumenya ivy’ ukuri. 
1Timothy2:5 Kuko har’ Imana imwe, kandi har’ Umuhūza umwe w’Imana n’abantu, na we nyene n’umuntu, ni Kristo Yesu," 
1Timothy2:6 yitanze kw incungu ya bose. Kand’ ivyo bishingirwe intahe mu bihe vyavyo," 
1Timothy2:7 ni co nashiriweho kuba umusiguzi n’intumwa (mvuze ukuri, simbeshe) n’umwigisha wo kwigisha abanyamahanga ukwizera n’ivy’ ukuri." 
1Timothy2:8 Nuko ndagomba kw abagabo basenga hose, batarika amaboko yera, bataratse, batagira ibihāri." 
1Timothy2:9 Kandi n’abagore nyene, ndagomba ko bambara imyambaro biberanye, bagendane isoni badahugumba kandi badashazisha gutsiba umushatsi, cank’ izahabu, cank’ imaragarita, cank’ impuzu z’igiciro kinini," 
1Timothy2:10 ariko bashazishe ibikorwa vy’ingeso nziza, nk’uko bikwiye abagore bavuga yuko bubaha Imana." 
1Timothy2:11 Umugore yige atekereje agamburuka rwose. 
1Timothy2:12 Ariko sinkundira umugore ko yigisha canke kw aganza umugabo, arikw atekereze." 
1Timothy2:13 Kuko Adamu ari we yabanje kuremwa, hanyuma Eva." 
1Timothy2:14 Kandi Adamu si we yahenzwe, arik’ umugore ni we yahenzwe, agwa mu bicumuro." 
1Timothy2:15 Yamar’ azokizwa kubg’ ukuvyara, ni bashishikara kwizera no kugira urukundo no kwezwa, bifatanye no kudahugumba." 
1Timothy3:1 Iri jambo n’iryo kwizerwa: umuntu ni yagomba kuzezwa ishengero, aba yifuje igikorwa ciza." 
1Timothy3:2 Nuk’ umuzezwashengero akwiye kutabak’ umugayo, kand’ akwiye kuba umugabo afise umugore umwe gusa; abe ūtarenza urugero, adahugumba, aganza ingeso ziwe, akunda gutanga indāro, afise ubgenge bgo kwigisha," 
1Timothy3:3 atar’ umunoho wa vino, cank’ umusinzi, arikw abe umugwaneza, atitoraguza, atar’ inkunzi y’amahera," 
1Timothy3:4 aganza neza abo mu rugo rwiwe, abana biwe bamwumvira, yanka umugayo wose." 
1Timothy3:5 (Ūtazi kuganza abo mu rugo rwiwe yoshobora ate kuzigama ishengero ry’Imana?) 
1Timothy3:6 Kandi ntakwiye kuba muto mu kwizera, kugira ngo ntiyikakishe, ngw atembe, agacirwakw iteka wa Murwanizi yaciriweko." 
1Timothy3:7 Kand’ akwiye gushingirwa intahe neza n’abo hanze, kugira ngo ntatembere mu mugayo no mu mutego wa wa Murwanizi." 
1Timothy3:8 Kandi n’abakozi b’ishengero na bo nyene, bakwiye kuba inyankamugayo batavuga indimi zibiri, kandi ntibabe abatwawe na vino nyinshi, cank’ abifuza inyungu mbi." 
1Timothy3:9 Ariko bagumye ibanga ry’ukwizera, bafise imitima itarimw’ ijwi ribāgiriza ikibi." 
1Timothy3:10 Kand’ abo babanze kugezwa, maze ni batābonekak’ umugayo babone gukora igikorwa c’ibango ryabo." 
1Timothy3:11 N’abagore nyene babe inyankamugayo, batarementaniriza abandi, batarenza urugero, bizigirwa muri vyose." 
1Timothy3:12 Umukozi w’ishengero wese abe umugabo afise umugore umwe gusa, aganza neza abana biwe n’abo mu rugo rwiwe." 
1Timothy3:13 Kukw abākoze neza ico gikorwa c’ibango ryabo bīronkera igishingo ciza n’ubushizi bg’amanga bginshi mu kwizera Kristo Yesu. 
1Timothy3:14 Nkwandikiye ivyo, nizigiye ko nzoza i wawe vuba:" 
1Timothy3:15 ariko ni naba ngitevye n’ukugira ng’uz’ umenye uko bikwiye kugenzwa mu ngoro y’Imana, ni yo shengero ry’Imana nzima, vyongeye ni yo nkingi ishigikiye ukuri." 
1Timothy3:16 Nta wuhakana yukw ibanga ryo kwubaha Imana ridahambaye cane, n’iri: umwe yerekanywe afise umubiri, akaboneka kw ar’ umugororotsi mu mpwemu, akabonwa n’abamarayika, akamenyekanishwa mu banyamahanga, akizererwa mw isi, akadūzwa agahabga ubgiza." 
1Timothy4:1 Ariko Mpwemu avuga avyeruye yuko mu bihe bizoza bamwe bazota ivyizerwa, bagashira umutima ku vy’ impwemu zizimiza no ku vy’ inyigisho z’abadayimoni," 
1Timothy4:2 bavugisha uburyarya bg’abanyabinyoma, bokejwe icapa mu mitima yabo ibāgiriza ikibi," 
1Timothy4:3 baziza kwābīrana, baziza n’ivyo kurya, kand’ ari vyo Imana yaremye kugira ngw abizera, bakamenya ivy’ ukuri, babirye bashima." 
1Timothy4:4 Ico Imana yaremye cose ni ciza, ntiharimw’ ico gutabga, iyo cakiriwe n’ūshima:" 
1Timothy4:5 kuko kiba gihezagiwe n’ijambo ry’Imana no gusenga. 
1Timothy4:6 Ni wibutsa bene Data ivyo, uzoba ur’ umukozi mwiza wa Kristo Yesu, yarerewe mu majambo y’ukwizera n’ay’ inyigisho nziza wakurikiye." 
1Timothy4:7 Arikw imigani ihumanya n’iy’ abakecuru ntuyemere. Wimenyereze kwubaha Imana; 
1Timothy4:8 kuko kwimenyereza kw’umubiri kugira ikimazi kuri bike, ariko kwubaha Imana kugira ikimazi kuri vyose, kuko kuzana isezerano ry’ubugingo bga none n’ubuzoza." 
1Timothy4:9 Iryo jambo n’iryo kwizerwa rikwiye kwemerwa rwose. 
1Timothy4:10 Kukw igituma dutama tukāma mu ntambara ar’ uko twizigiye Imana nzima, ni yo Mukiza w’abantu bose, cane‐cane w’abizera." 
1Timothy4:11 Wame ubgiriza ivyo kand’ uvyigisha. 
1Timothy4:12 Ntihakagire ūkugayira ubusore, arik’ ubere abizera icitegererezo mu vy’uvuga, no mu ngeso zawe, no mu rukundo, no mu kwizera, no ku mutima utanduye." 
1Timothy4:13 Gushitsa aho nzozira wame ugira umwete wo gusomera abantu no kubahanūra no kubigisha. 
1Timothy4:14 Ntiwanjanjwe ku ngabire iri muri wewe, imwe waheshwa n’ivy’ abavugishwa n’Imana mu kurambikwakw ibiganza vy’abakuru." 
1Timothy4:15 Ivyo ubishirek’ umwete, uvyamemwo, kugira ngo kuja imbere kwawe kubonekere bose." 
1Timothy4:16 Wirinde ubgawe no ku vyo wigisha. Wame ushishikara ivyo, kuko ni wagira urtyo uzokwikizanya n’abakwumva." 
1Timothy5:1 Ntuhambarire umutāma, arik’ umuhanūre nka so, n’abakiri bato n’imisore ubahanūre nka bene nyoko," 
1Timothy5:2 n’abatamakazi nyene nka ba nyoko, n’abakiri bato n’abigeme nka bashiki bawe, uri n’umutima utanduye na gatoya." 
1Timothy5:3 Wubahe abapfakazi b’inyakamwe vy’ukuri. 
1Timothy5:4 Ariko, umupfakazi wese, namb’ afise abana cank’ abuzukuru, ni babanze kwiga kwubaha Imana ku vyo bagirira ababo, no kwishura ivyiza abavyeyi babo: kukw ivyo ari vyo bishimwa mu nyonga z’Imana." 
1Timothy5:5 Umupfakazi w’inyakamwe asigaye ar’ umwe, yizigira Imana, agashishikara kwinginga no gusenga ku murango no mw ijoro." 
1Timothy5:6 Ariko, uwihaye ukwifuza aba apfuye ahagaze." 
1Timothy5:7 Ubabgirize ivyo, kugira ngo ntibabek’ umugayo." 
1Timothy5:8 Arik’ umuntu n’atātunga abo mu nzu y’i wabo, cane‐cane abiwe, azoba yihakanye ukwizera, kand’ azoba abaye hanyuma y’ūtizera." 
1Timothy5:9 Ntihakagire umupfakazi yandikirwa gufashwa ataramara imyaka mirongwitandatu y’amavuka, kandi handikwe uwar’ afiswe n’umugabo umwe gusa," 
1Timothy5:10 handikwe ūshimirwa ibikorwa vyiza, namba yararera abana, namba yaratanga indāro, yarōza ibirenge vy’abera, yarafasha abababaye, yarashishikara gukurikira ibikorwa vyiza vyose." 
1Timothy5:11 Arikw abapfakazi bakiri bato ntubemerere, kuko kwifuza kw’umubiri ni kwamara kubatera kugarariza Kristo bazogomba kwābīrwa," 
1Timothy5:12 bagatsindwa n’urubanza kuko bavuye mw isezerano ryabo rya mbere. 
1Timothy5:13 Kand’ ikindi, biga kugira ubunebge, bagenda imihana; ariko rero s’ubunebge gusa, ikigeretseko bararegeteranya bīta mu bitar’ ivyabo, bavuga ivyo badakwiye." 
1Timothy5:14 Ni co gituma ngomba kw abapfakazi bakiri bato bābīrwa, bakavyara abana, bakubaka ingo zabo, ntibahe umurwanizi urwitwazo rw’ibitutsi." 
1Timothy5:15 Kuko n’ubu bamwe bamaze guta inzira, ngo bakurikire Satani." 
1Timothy5:16 Umugore wese yizera namb’ afise incuti z’abapfakazi, abafashe, ishengero ntiriremērwe, ribone gufasha abapfakazi b’inyakamwe." 
1Timothy5:17 Abakuru b’ishengero baganza neza ni babiyumvire ko bakwiye guhabga icubahiro kirushiriza, kandi cane‐cane abacumukura mu kuvuga ijambo ry’Imana no mu kwigisha." 
1Timothy5:18 Kukw icanditswe kivuga, ngo Ntimuze murumye umunwa w’inka irikw irasekura ingano; kandi ng’ Umukozi akwiye ingero yiwe." 
1Timothy5:19 Umukuru ntukemere ico bazomukuregako hatabonetse ivyabona bibiri canke bitatu. 
1Timothy5:20 Abakora ivyaha ubahanire mu maso ya bose, kugira ngw abandi na bo batinye." 
1Timothy5:21 Ndakwihanikiririza mu nyonga z’Imana na Yesu Kristo n’imbere y’abamarayika bātoranijwe, witondere ivyo, ntuce urw’ umwe, ntukore ivyo guca urwa nkunzi." 
1Timothy5:22 Ntukagire umuntu wihutira kurambikakw ibiganza, kandi ntugafatanye n’abandi mu vyaha vyabo. Uze wame wirinda ubuhumane." 
1Timothy5:23 Uhereye none ntunywe amazi gusa, arik’ unywe n’utuvino duke kubgo mu nda hawe, kuk’ urwaragurika." 
1Timothy5:24 Har’ abantu ivyaha vyabo biboneka bikabītangira imbere mu kuja mu rubanza; hari n’abandi bibāza inyuma. 
1Timothy5:25 Kand’ ibikorwa vyiza na vyo n’uko, har’ ibiboneka; kandi n’ibitameze birtyo ntibishobora kunyegezwa." 
1Timothy6:1 Abagurano bose bari mu buja ni biyumvire ba shebuja ko bakwiye kwubahwa rwose, ngw izina ry’Imana n’ukwigisha ntibitukwe." 
1Timothy6:2 Kand’ abafise ba shebuja bizera, boye kubagayishwa n’ukw ari bene Data, ariko barushirize kubakorera, kukw abagirirwa ico kimazi ar’ abizera n’abakundwa. Uze wigishe ivyo, ubibahanūre." 
1Timothy6:3 Umuntu ni yigisha ukundi, ntiyemere amajambo mazima, ari yo majambo y’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, n’inyigisho zihūra n’ukwubaha Imana;" 
1Timothy6:4 azoba yikakishije, ata co azi, arwaye ibihāri, n’intambara z’amagambo, zivamw’ igono, no gutongana, n’ibitutsi, n’ikēkwe ribi," 
1Timothy6:5 n’ibihāri bidashira vy’abantu bononekaye ubgenge, bakūwekw ivy’ ukuri, bibgira yuko kwubaha Imana ar’ ukwironkera inyungu." 
1Timothy6:6 Ariko kwubaha Imana gufatanije no kubūmbga n’ivy’ ufise kuvamw’ inyungu nyinshi koko: 
1Timothy6:7 kukw ata co twazanye mw isi kand’ ata co dushobora kuyivanamwo. 
1Timothy6:8 Arikw iyo dufise ivyo turya n’ivyo twambaye biba bitubūmvye. 
1Timothy6:9 Arikw abagomba kuba abatunzi bagwa mu nyosha no mu mutego no mu kwifuza kwinshi kw’ubupfu gusinzikaza, kudobeza abantu mu bibonona bikabarandura." 
1Timothy6:10 Kuko gukunda amahera ar’imizi y’ibibi vyose; ayo bamwe bifuje, bakazimira, bagata ukwizera, bītobekeranisha imibabaro myinshi." 
1Timothy6:11 Ariko weho, muntu w’Imana, wame uhunga ivyo, arik’ ukurikire ukugororoka, n’ukwubaha Imana, n’ukwizera, n’urukundo, n’ukwihangana, n’ubugwaneza," 
1Timothy6:12 wame urwana intambara nziza yo kwizera, ucakire ubugingo budashira, ubgo wahamagariwe, ukabgaturira ukwatura kwiza mu maso y’ivyabona vyinshi." 
1Timothy6:13 Ndakubgiririza mu nyonga z’Imana ibeshaho vyose, no mu za Kristo Yesu yashingishije intahe ukwatura kwiza imbere ya Pontiyo Pilato," 
1Timothy6:14 witondere icagezwe, ntugire agasembga, ntubek’ umugayo, gushitsa ku guseruka kw’ Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo," 
1Timothy6:15 kuzokwerekanwa mu gihe cakwo n’Inyabushobozi yonyene, ishemagizwa, ni yo Mwami w’abami, ūganza abaganza;" 
1Timothy6:16 ni yo yonyene ifise ukudapfa, iba mu muco utēgērwa, ata muntu yigeze ayibona, ata wushobora kuyibona. Icubahiro n’ubushobozi bidashira bibe ivyayo. Amen." 
1Timothy6:17 Wihanize abatunzi bo mu vy’ iki gihe, boye kwibona, canke kwishimira ubutunzi butar’ ubgo kwishimirwa, ariko bishimire Imana, iduha vyose bisēsekaye, ngo tubinezererwe;" 
1Timothy6:18 kandi bakore iciza, babe abatunzi ku bikorwa vyiza, babe abanyabuntu bakunda gutanga," 
1Timothy6:19 bībīkire ubutunzi buzoba itanguriro ryiza mu gihe kizoza, kugira ngo bacakire ubugingo nyakuri." 
1Timothy6:20 Ewe Timoteyo, wame uzigama ico wabikijwe, utere ibitugu ibizira vy’amagambo ahumanya n’ukurwana kw’ivyitwa ubgenge atari bgo," 
1Timothy6:21 ubgo bamwe bīvuga ko babufise bakazimira, bagata ukwizera. Ubuntu bubane namwe." 
2Timothy1:1 Paulo, intumwa ya Kristo Yesu, nk’ukw Imana yagomvye, intumwa yo kuvuga isezerano ry’ubugingo bubonerwa muri Kristo Yesu," 
2Timothy1:2 ndakwandikiye Timoteyo, umwana wanje nkunda: ubuntu n’imbabazi n’amahoro bibe kuri wewe, biva ku Mana Data wa twese no kuri Kristo Yesu Umwami wacu." 
2Timothy1:3 Imana, nkorera nkurikiye ba sogokuruza, mfise umutima utanduye, utarimw’ ijwi rinyagiriza ikibi, ndayishimira yuko nkwibuka ubudasība, uko nsenze, ijoro n’umurango." 
2Timothy1:4 Nibuka amosozi yawe, ngakumbura kukubona, ngo nuzure umunezero:" 
2Timothy1:5 kuko nibutse ukwizera kutar’ ukw’ uburyarya kuri muri wewe, kwabanje kuba muri nyogokuru Lowisi no muri nyoko Ewunike: kandi ndazi ntakekeranya yuko kuri muri wewe nawe." 
2Timothy1:6 Ni co gituma nkwibutsa gufurūra ingabire y’Imana iri muri wewe ngo yake, yagushizwemwo no kurambikwakw ibiganza vyanje." 
2Timothy1:7 Kukw Imana itaduhaye umutima w’ubujora: ariko yaduhaye uw’ ubushobozi n’urukundo n’ukwirinda. 
2Timothy1:8 Nuko ntugire isoni zo gushingira intahe Umwami wacu, cank’ izanje imbohe yiwe. Arik’ ufatanye nanje kwihanganira imibabaro kubg’ ubutumwa bgiza, nk’uk’ ubushobozi bg’Imana bugushoboza," 
2Timothy1:9 yadukijije, ikaduhamagarisha umuhamagaro wera, udatewe n’ibikorwa vyacu, arik’ utewe n’uko yabigabiye ubgayo, kand’ utewe n’ubuntu bgayo, twaherewe muri Kristo Yesu ibihe vyose bitaraba," 
2Timothy1:10 ariko none bgaseruwe n’ukuboneka kw’Umukiza wacu Kristo Yesu, yahinduye urupfu ubusa, ubugingo no kutagipfa akabiserurisha ubutumwa bgiza." 
2Timothy1:11 Ubgo butumwa nabushiriweho kuba umuvuzi wabgo n’intumwa n’umwigisha. 
2Timothy1:12 Ni co gituma kandi mbabazwa ntya, yamara ntibintera isoni, kuko nzi uwo nizeye, kandi nzi ntakekeranya yukw ashobora kuzigama ikibītsanyo namubīkije gushitsa kuri wa musi." 
2Timothy1:13 Gumya icitegererezo c’amajambo mazima wanyumvanye, ukigumishe ukwizera n’urukundo rubonerwa muri Kristo Yesu." 
2Timothy1:14 Ikibītsanyo ciza wabīkijwe, ukizigamishe Mpwemu Yera aba muri twebge." 
2Timothy1:15 Urazi yukw abo muri Asiya bose banteye ibitugu, mur’ abo umwe ni Fugelo na Herumogene." 
2Timothy1:16 Umwami agirire abo kwa Onesiforo ikigongwe, kuko yanduhura kenshi, kandi ntiyatewe n’isoni n’umunyororo wanje," 
2Timothy1:17 ariko, ashitse i Roma, agira umwete wo kundondera, arambona." 
2Timothy1:18 Umwami amuhe kuzoronka imbabazi ziva ku Mwami kuri wa musi. Kand’ ivyo yankoreye muri Efeso uko bingana, nta wukurusha kubimenya." 
2Timothy2:1 Weho mwana wanje, ugirire ubushobozi mu buntu buri muri Kristo Yesu," 
2Timothy2:2 kand’ ivyo wanyumvanye mu maso y’ivyabona vyinshi, ubishikirize abantu bo kwizigirwa, bazoshobora kuvyigisha n’abandi." 
2Timothy2:3 Ufatanye nanje kwihanganira imibabaro, nk’uko bikwiye umusoda mwiza wa Kristo Yesu." 
2Timothy2:4 Nta musoda yikwegera mu vy’ubu bugingo, ngw az’ ahimbare uwamwandikiye ubusoda." 
2Timothy2:5 Kand’ iy’ umuntu arushanywa, ntahabga igitsibo, shiti arushanijwe nk’uko vyagezwe." 
2Timothy2:6 Umurimyi kukw ari we yacumukuye ni we akwiye kubanza gusoroma ku vyeze. 
2Timothy2:7 Umenye ivyo mvuze, kuk’ Umwami wacu azoguha ubgenge muri vyose." 
2Timothy2:8 Wame wibuka Yesu Kristo, yazutse mu bapfuye, yakomotse mu ruvyaro rwa Dawidi, nk’uk’ ubutumwa nahawe buvuga:" 
2Timothy2:9 ubgo mbabarizwamwo, no kubohwa nkabohwa, nk’inkozi y’ikibi; arikw ijambo ry’Imana ntiriboshwe." 
2Timothy2:10 Ni co gituma nihanganira vyose kubg’ abatoranijwe, kugira ngo na bo baronke agakiza kari muri Kristo Yesu, gafatanije n’ubgiza budashira." 
2Timothy2:11 Iri jambo n’iryo kwizerwa, ngo Namba twarapfanye na we, tuzobanaho na we;" 
2Timothy2:12 namba twihangana, tuzokwimana na we; namba tuzomwihakana, na we azotwihakana;" 
2Timothy2:13 naho tutoba abizigirwa, we ahora ar’ umwizigirwa, kukw adashobora guhindagurika." 
2Timothy2:14 Wame ubibutsa ivyo, ubihanikiririza mu nyonga z’Imana ntibarwanire amajambo kuko bitagira ikimazi, bigwisha abumva." 
2Timothy2:15 Wame ugira umwete wo kwiha Imana nk’uwamaze kurama, umukozi atarinda gutētērwa, aramiriza neza mw ijambo ry’ukuri." 
2Timothy2:16 Ariko, ibihumanya vy’amagambo y’ubusa ubizibukīre, kukw ababivuga bazoshishikara inzira yo kutubaha Imana," 
2Timothy2:17 kand’ ijambo ryabo rizorandagurana nk’igisebe c’igitema. Mur’ abo umwe ni Humenayo na Fileto," 
2Timothy2:18 kuko bāzimiye bakava mu vy’ ukuri, bavuga ng’ ukuzuka kwarahejeje kubaho, bagahenura ukwizera kwa bamwe." 
2Timothy2:19 Arikw itanguriro ry’Imana ryo kwubakako rirakomeye, ryanditswekw iki kimenyetso, ng’ Uhoraho arazi abiwe; kandi ng’ Umuntu wese avuga izina ry’Uhoraho ave mu kugabitanya." 
2Timothy2:20 Mu nzu nini y’umutunzi ntihabamw’ imbombovu z’ivyacuzwe mw izahabu no mw ifeza gusa, ariko habamwo n’iz’ ivy’ ibiti n’iz’ ivy’ ibumba, kandi bimwe babikoresha ivy’ icubahiro, ibindi babikoresha ibiteye isoni." 
2Timothy2:21 Umuntu ni yiyeza, akitandukanya n’ivyo, azoba igikoreshwa c’icubahiro, cejejwe, kigirira nyene co ikimazi, catunganirijwe igikorwa ciza cose." 
2Timothy2:22 Ariko kwifuza kw’ubusore uguhunge, maz’ ukurikire ukugororoka n’ukwizera n’urukundo n’amahoro, ufatanya n’abambaza Umwami wacu n’imitima itanduye." 
2Timothy2:23 Arikw ibihāri vy’ubupfu n’ivy’ ubutungu ntukavyemere, uzi yuko bivyara intonganya." 
2Timothy2:24 Kand’ umushumba w’Umwami wacu ntakwiye gutongana, arikw akwiye kugira ineza kuri bose, no kuba uburyo bgo kwigisha, no kwihangana," 
2Timothy2:25 no guhanūrisha ubugwaneza abamuhāririza, ngo kumbure, bishobotse, Imana ibahe kwihana ngo bamenye ivy’ ukuri," 
2Timothy2:26 bashire ibirāre, bave mu mutego wa wa Murwanizi yabafashe ngo bakore ivy’ agomba." 
2Timothy3:1 Arik’ umenye yuko mu misi y’iherezo hazoza ibihe bigoye. 
2Timothy3:2 Kukw abantu bazoba bikunda gusa, bakunda amahera, bīrārīra, bībona, batukana, batumvira abavyeyi, intashima, abanegura ivy’ Imana," 
2Timothy3:3 badakunda n’ababo, banka kwuzura, barementanya, batigarura, inkazi, badakunda ivyiza," 
2Timothy3:4 abaguranyi, ibirandamuke, abikakisha, bakunda ibibahimbara bakabirutisha Imana," 
2Timothy3:5 bafise ishusho yo kwubaha Imana, ariko bahakana ubushobozi bgakwo: abameze bartyo wame ubatera ibitugu." 
2Timothy3:6 Kuko muri bo harimw’ abagabo banyegetera mu mazu, bagatwara abagore batagira imitima, baremerewe n’ivyaha, batwarwa n’ukwifuza kw’ uburyo bginshi," 
2Timothy3:7 bama biga, ariko nta ho bashobora gushitsa ku kumenya ukuri." 
2Timothy3:8 Nk’uko Yane na Yambure bārwanije Mose, ni ko n’abo bagabo barwanya ukuri, abo n’abononekaye ubgenge, babaye ibihombe ku kwizera." 
2Timothy3:9 Mugabo ntibazoshobora kurengaho: kuk’ ubusazi bgabo buzogaragarira abantu bose, nk’uk’ ubga ba bandi bgagaragaye." 
2Timothy3:10 Ariko weho wakurikiye neza ukwigisha kwanje, n’ingeso, n’imigabo, n’ukwizera, n’ukutarambirwa, n’urukundo, n’ukwihangana," 
2Timothy3:11 no guhamwa, n’imibabaro, nk’ivyambereyeko muri Antiyokiya no muri Ikoniyo n’i Lusitira; ivyo nihanganiye vyose mpamwa, kandi vyose Umwami wacu arabinkiza." 
2Timothy3:12 Mber’ abagomba bose kugenda bubaha Imana bari muri Kristo Yesu, bazohamwa." 
2Timothy3:13 Arikw abantu babi, bo n’abahūmbūzi, bazorushiriza kuba babi, bazimiza bakazimizwa." 
2Timothy3:14 Ariko weho ugume mu vyo wize, ukavyizezwa, kuk’ uzi abākwigishije:" 
2Timothy3:15 kand’ uzi yuk’ uhereye mu buto bgawe wamye uzi ivyanditswe vyera bishobora kukumenyesha ubgenge bgo kukuzanira agakiza gaheshwa no kwizera Kristo Yesu. 
2Timothy3:16 Ivyanditswe vyose vyahumetswe n’Imana, kandi bigira ikimazi co kwigisha umuntu, no kumuhana, no kumutunganya, no kumutoza indero nziza mu kugororoka:" 
2Timothy3:17 kugira ng’ umuntu w’Imana abe ūshitse, afise ibimukwiye vyose, ngw akore igikorwa ciza cose." 
2Timothy4:1 Ndakwihanikiririza mu nyonga z’Imana no mu za Kristo Yesu azocirakw iteka abazoba bariho n’abazoba bapfuye, kandi no kubgo kuzoboneka kwiwe n’ubgami bgiwe:" 
2Timothy4:2 uvuge ijambo ry’Imana, uhore ugavye mu gihe gikwiye no mu kidakwiye, uhane, wihanize, uhanūre, mu kwihangana kwose no mu kwigisha." 
2Timothy4:3 Kukw igihe kizoza, batazokwemera kwumva ukwigisha kuzima; ariko kukw amatwi abarya yifuza kwumva ibibanezereza, bazokwirundaniriza abigisha bahūje n’ukwifuza kwabo," 
2Timothy4:4 kandi bazokwiziba amatwi, ngo ntibumve ukuri, bazozimira bakurikire imigani y’ibinyoma." 
2Timothy4:5 Ariko weho, wirinde muri vyose, wihanganire imibabaro, ukore igikorwa c’umuvuzi w’ubutumwa bgiza, ushitse igikorwa c’ibango ryawe." 
2Timothy4:6 Kuko jeho n’ubu ndiko ndasukwa nk’ibisukwa ku gicaniro, igihe co gutāmbūra kwanje kirashitse;" 
2Timothy4:7 narwanye intambara nziza, narangije urugendo, nazigamye ukwizera." 
2Timothy4:8 Ibisigaye, mbīkiwe igitsibo c’ukugororoka, ico Umwami wacu, umucamanza agororotse, azompa kuri wa musi, kandi si jewe jenyene nzogihabga, ariko kandi n’abakunze kuzoseruka kwiwe bose bazogihabga." 
2Timothy4:9 Gira umwete wo kuza aho ndi vuba. 
2Timothy4:10 Dema yarantaye, kukw akunze iyi si ya none, yīgīra i Tesalonike: Keresikenti yagiye i Galatiya: Tito yagiye i Dalumatiya." 
2Timothy4:11 Luka gusa ni we twasigaranye. Hitana Mariko, umuzane, kukw angirira ikimazi mu gikorwa c’ibango ryanje." 
2Timothy4:12 Ariko Tukiko namurungitse muri Efeso. 
2Timothy4:13 Ah’ uzozira uranzanira impuzu yo kwipfuka nasize i Tirowa kwa Karupo, n’ibitabo, kandi cane‐cane uz’ uzane ivy’ insāto." 
2Timothy4:14 Alekisandero umucuzi yangiriye inabi nyinshi. Umwami wacu azomwishura ibikwiranye n’ivyo yakoze. 
2Timothy4:15 Nawe umwiyubare kuko yarwanije amajambo yacu cane. 
2Timothy4:16 Mw ibūrana ryanje rya mbere nta wanyikije, ariko bose barantaye: icompa ntibabiharūrweko." 
2Timothy4:17 Arik’ Umwami wacu ni we yampagarikiye, arandemesha, kugira ng’ ubutumwa buvugwe nanje butagabanije, abanyamahanga bose babgumve. Nuko mva mu menyo y’intambge." 
2Timothy4:18 Umwami wacu azonkiza ibibi vyose bangirira, azondokora kugira ngw anjane mu bgami bgiwe bgo mw ijuru. Icubahiro kibe iciwe, ibihe bitazoshira. Amen." 
2Timothy4:19 Untahirize Purisikila na Akwila n’abo kwa Onesiforo. 
2Timothy4:20 Erasito yagumye i Korinto, ariko Tirofimo namusize i Mileto arwaye." 
2Timothy4:21 Gira umwete wo kuza urushana rutarajobanya. Ewubulo arakuganutsa, na Pudenti na Lino na Kilawudiya na bene Data bose." 
2Timothy4:22 Umwami abane n’umutima wawe. Ubuntu bg’Imana bubane namwe. 
Titus1:1 Paulo, umugurano w’Imana, intumwa ya Yesu Kristo, mbihērewe kwizeza abo Imana yatoranije no kwigisha kumenya ivy’ ukuri gufatanije n’ukwubaha Imana;" 
Titus1:2 nkora nizigiye kuzoronka ubugingo budashira, ubgo Imana itazi kubesha yasezeranye kera, ibihe vyose bitarabaho." 
Titus1:3 Ariko mu bihe yitoranirije yerekanishije ijambo ryayo ubutumwa najejwe, nk’ukw Imana Umukiza wacu yageze." 
Titus1:4 Ndakwandikiye Tito, umwana wanje nyakuri kubg’ ukwizera dusangiye. Ubuntu n’amahoro bibe kuri wewe biva ku Mana Data wa twese no kuri Kristo Yesu Umukiza wacu." 
Titus1:5 Icatumye ngusiga i Kirete kwar’ ukugira ng’ utunganye ivyasigaye, kandi mu gisagara caho cose ng’ uhashinge abakuru b’ishengero, nk’uko nabikubariye:" 
Titus1:6 ar’ umuntu atabonekak’ umugayo, afise umugore umwe gusa, afise abana bizera, bataregwa kw ar’ ibihumbu cank’ ibiganda." 
Titus1:7 Kuk’ umuzezwashengero akwiye kutabak’ umugayo, nk’umubgiriza w’Imana nyene; kandi ntakwiye kuba ūdakūrwa kw ijambo, cank’ ūsugurirwa, cank’ umunywi wa vino, cank’ umusinzi, cank’ uwifuza inyungu mbi;" 
Titus1:8 arikw abe ūkunda gutanga indāro, akunda ivyiza, adahugumba, agororoka, yera, yirinda," 
Titus1:9 agumya ijambo ryo kwizerwa rihūra n’ukwigisha kwacu, kugira ngw abone guhanūra abantu mu kwigisha kuzima no gutsinda abamuhāririza." 
Titus1:10 Kuko hariho benshi b’ibiganda, cane‐cane n’abo mu bākebge, bavuga ibitagira ikimazi, n’inyosha mbi," 
Titus1:11 bakwiye kuzibga iminwa, kuko har’ imiryango bagwisha igahenebera, bigisha ibidakwiye kubg’ inyungu mbi." 
Titus1:12 Umwe muri bo w’umumenyi wabo yaravuze, ati Na ntaryo Abanyakirete n’ababeshi, n’ibikōko bibi, n’abanebge b’abakunzi b’inda." 
Titus1:13 Iyo ntahe yashinze n’iy’ ukuri. Ni co gituma ukwiye kubahana cane, kugira ngo babe abahangaye mu kwizera," 
Titus1:14 ntibashire imitima ku migani y’ibinyoma y’Abayuda no ku vyagezwe vy’abantu batera ibitugu ukuri. 
Titus1:15 Ku badahumanye nta gihumanye, ariko ku banduye, batizera, nta kidahumanye, arik’ ubgenge bgabo n’imitima ibāgiriza vyaranduye." 
Titus1:16 Bavuga yuko bazi Imana, ariko bayihakanisha ivyo bakora; n’abo kwankwa urunuka, n’abatumvira Imana, no mu bikorwa vyiza vyose nta co bamaze." 
Titus2:1 Ariko weho uvuge ibihwanye na kwa kwigisha kuzima. 
Titus2:2 Bgira abatāma boye kurenza urugero, babe inyankamugayo, badahugumba, babe abahangaye mu kwizera no mu rukundo no mu kwihangana." 
Titus2:3 N’abatāmakazi nyene, ubabgire bagende nk’uko bibereye abera, batarementaniriza abandi, batanohorwa imitima na vino nyinshi, bigisha ivyiza," 
Titus2:4 kugira ngo batoze abagore bakiri bato ubgenge bgo gukunda abagabo babo n’abana babo," 
Titus2:5 no kudahugumba, no kwirinda ubgēruzi, no kwubaka ingo zabo, no kuba inda nziza, bagororokere abagabo babo, kugira ngw ijambo ry’Imana ntiritukwe." 
Titus2:6 N’imisore n’uko ubahanūre ntibahugumbe; 
Titus2:7 nawe ubgawe wiyerekane muri vyose nk’icitegererezo c’ibikorwa vyiza, ugire ukwigisha kudatosekaye, ube inyankamugayo," 
Titus2:8 ugire n’ijambo rizima ritogawa, kugira ng’ umuntu ari mu ruhande rw’abansi amāramāre, abuze ikibi yotuvuga." 
Titus2:9 Hanūra abagurano bagororokere ba shebuja, babahimbare muri vyose, ata guhārīra," 
Titus2:10 badakorakora, ariko berekane ukuyoboka kwiza kwose, kugira ngo muri vyose basharize ivyigishwa vy’Imana, Umukiza wacu." 
Titus2:11 Kuk’ ubuntu bg’Imana bgaserutse, buzanira abantu bose agakiza,"
