Titus2:12 butwigisha kwikunkumura ukutubaha Imana n’ukwifuza ivy’ isi, bukatwigisha kwama tudahugumba, tugororoka, twubaha Imana, mu gihe ca none," 
Titus2:13 twitega ivyizigiro vy’amahirwe no kuzoseruka kw’ubgiza bga Yesu Kristo, ni we Mana yacu ihambaye n’Umukiza," 
Titus2:14 yatwiguze kugira ngw aducungure, adukūrekw ivyo twagabitanije vyose, kandi yihumanurire ubgoko ngo babe icibare ciwe, barwane ishaka ry’ibikorwa vyiza." 
Titus2:15 Wame uvuga ivyo, ubahanūra, ubahana, nk’ūfise ububasha rwose. Ntihakagire ūgukēngēra." 
Titus3:1 Ubibutse kugamburukira abakuru n’abafise ubushobozi, no kubumvira, no kwitegurira igikorwa ciza cose," 
Titus3:2 no kutagira uwo bambika ibara, no kutitoraguza, no kwengenga, berekana ubugwaneza bgose ku bantu bose." 
Titus3:3 Kuko natwe nyene kera twar’ ibipfu, tur’ intabarirwa, tuzimizwa, tujakariye ukwifuza n’ukwinezereza vy’uburyo bginshi, twama tugira urwanko n’igono, tur’ abo kwankwa natwe twankana." 
Titus3:4 Arikw ineza y’Imana Umukiza wacu n’urukundo ikunda abantu, bimaze kuboneka," 
Titus3:5 iradukiza, itadukirishije ibikorwa vyo kugororoka twakoze, ariko, nk’ukw imbabazi zayo ziri, idukirisha ukwozwa kuzana ukuvyarwa ubga kabiri, ikadukirisha uguhindurwa basha na Mpwemu Yera," 
Titus3:6 uwo yaducuncuburiyeko kubga Yesu Kristo Umukiza wacu," 
Titus3:7 kugira ngo dutsindanishirizwe n’ubuntu bgayo, duce tuba abaragwa b’ubugingo budashira, nk’ukw ivyizigiro vyacu biri." 
Titus3:8 Iryo jambo n’iryo kwizerwa, ndagomba yuk’ utsindagira ivyo, ubikobereje, kugira ngw abizeye Imana bagire umwete wo kugumya gukora ibikorwa vyiza. Ivyo ni vyiza, bigira ico bimarira abantu." 
Titus3:9 Ariko, impāri z’ubupfu no kuzirora ivy’ akaronda n’imitongano no guhārīra ivyo mu vyagezwe, wame ubizibukīra, kuko bitagira ikimazi kand’ ar’ ivy’ ubusa." 
Titus3:10 Ūzana ibice ni wamara kumuhanūra ubga mbere n’ubga kabiri akanka, ntukamwemere," 
Titus3:11 kuk’ uzi yuk’ ūmeze artyo agoramye kand’ akora ivyaha, yitsindisha." 
Titus3:12 Ni nagutumako Arutema canke Tukiko, uz’ ugire umwete wo kunsanga i Nikopoli; kukw ari ho nagabiye kuzomara urushana." 
Titus3:13 Witwaririke guherekeza no gusezera neza Zena umunyabgenge w’ivyagezwe, na Apolo, kugira ngo ntibaze bagire ico babura." 
Titus3:14 Kand’ abacu na bo ni bige kugumya gukora ibikorwa vyiza ngo babone kumara ubukene ababikwiye rwose, kugira ngw abacu ntibabe ibirumbirane." 
Titus3:15 Abo turi kumwe bose baragutasha. Untahirize abadukunda dusangiye ukwizera. Ubuntu bubane namwe mwese. 
Philemon1:1 Paulo, imbohe ya Kristo Yesu, na Timoteyo mwene Data, turakwandikiye Filemoni uwo dukunda, dusangiye igikorwa," 
Philemon1:2 na Apiya mushiki wacu, na Arukipo turwanana, n’ishengero ryo mu nzu yawe:" 
Philemon1:3 ubuntu bube muri mwebge n’amahoro biva ku Mana, Data wa twese, no ku Mwami Yesu Kristo." 
Philemon1:4 Nshima Imana yanje ubudasība, nguhoza mu kanwa uko nsenze," 
Philemon1:5 kuko numvise urukundo rwawe n’ukwizera Umwami Yesu kwawe, ukwo wereka abera bose:" 
Philemon1:6 kugira ng’ ugufataniriza mu kwizera kwawe gushobore vyinshi kubga Kristo, mu kumenyekanisha ivyiza vyose vyo muri twebge." 
Philemon1:7 Kuk’ urukundo rwawe rwanteye umunezero mwinshi rukandemesha, kand’ imitima y’abera warayiruhuye, mwene Data." 
Philemon1:8 Kubg’ ivyo, naho mfise ubushizi bg’amanga bgose muri Kristo bgo kukugerakw ibikwiye," 
Philemon1:9 mpisemwo kukwinginga kubg’ urukundo, uko ndi kose Paulo umutāma, kandi none nd’imbohe ya Kristo Yesu." 
Philemon1:10 Ndakwitwayeko ku mwana wanje Onesimo uwo navyariye mu minyororo yanje," 
Philemon1:11 atākugirira ikimazi kera, ariko noneh’ atugirira ikimazi twempi." 
Philemon1:12 Ni we nyene nkurungikiye, ni we mutima wanje." 
Philemon1:13 Mba ndamugumije kugira ngw ankorere mu gishingo cawe, mboshwe n’iminyororo y’ubutumwa bgiza." 
Philemon1:14 Ariko nta co ngomba gukora ntakugishije inama, kugira ngw iciza ukora ntikibe ic’ ugōberewe, arik’ ugikore ubikunze." 
Philemon1:15 Kumbure icatumye atandukanywa nawe igihe gito kwar’ ukugira ng’ uz’ umwamane imisi yose: 
Philemon1:16 atakir’ umugurano wawe, arikw aruta umugurano, ari mwene So, akundwa: akundwa nanje cane, arikw arushiriza gukundwa nawe, mu vy’umubiri no mu Mwami wacu." 
Philemon1:17 Nuko namb’ unyiyumvira ko dusangiye igikorwa, umwākīre nk’uko nanje wonyakiriye." 
Philemon1:18 Arikw asangwa har’ ico yaguhemukiyeko, canke har’ umwenda agufitiye, ubimparūreko." 
Philemon1:19 Ni jewe Paulo nandikishije ukwanje kuboko yuko nzovyishura: reka noye kukubgira yuk’ uri n’umwenda wanje, uwo mwenda ni wewe ubgawe." 
Philemon1:20 Ego, mwene Data, nkubonemw’ ikimazi mu Mwami wacu: unduhure umutima muri Kristo." 
Philemon1:21 Nkwandikiye nizigiye k’uzonyumvira, nzi yuk’ uzokora n’ibiruta ivyo mvuze." 
Philemon1:22 Kandi n’ikindi, untegurire indāro; kuko nizigiye yuko muzompabga kubg’ amasengesho yanyu." 
Philemon1:23 Epafura, mugenzanje tubohanywe muri Kristo, aragutasha," 
Philemon1:24 na Mariko, na Arisitariko, na Dema, na Luka, abo dusangiye igikorwa, baragutasha." 
Philemon1:25 Ubuntu bg’Umwami Yesu Kristo bubane n’imitima yanyu. Amen. 
Hebrews1:1 Kera Imana yabaririye ba sogokuruza mu kanwa k’abavugishwa na yo mu bihe vyinshi no mu buryo bginshi," 
Hebrews1:2 mur’ iyi misi y’iherezo yabaririye twebge mu kanwa k’Umwana wayo, uwo yashiriyeho kuba samuragwa wa vyose, ni we yahaye kurema isi." 
Hebrews1:3 Uwo, kukw ar’ ugukayangana kw’ubgiza bgayo, n’ishusho y’akameremere kayo, kand’ ashigikiza vyose ijambo ry’ubushobozi bgiwe, ahejeje gushirah’ umwuhagiro w’ivyaha, avyagira i buryo bg’icubahiro c’ubgami bgo mw ijuru:" 
Hebrews1:4 amaze kuba ūhambaye kurusha abamarayika, nk’ukw izina yarazwe rirengeye ayabo." 
Hebrews1:5 Ni nde wo mu bamarayika yigeze kubarira, it’ Ur’ Ubura bganje, Uyu musi ndakuvyaye? Kandi iti Nzoba Se, Na we azoba Umwana wanje?" 
Hebrews1:6 Kand’ ah’ izokwongera kuzana imfura yayo mw isi, it’ Abamarayika b’Imana bose bamusenge." 
Hebrews1:7 Kand’ ivy’ abamarayika yarabivuze, it’ Ihindura abamarayika bayo imiyaga, Abasavyi bayo ibahindura imbeya z’umuriro." 
Hebrews1:8 Ariko, ivy’ Umwana wayo yabivuze, it’ Ingoma yawe, Mana, ihangamye ibihe bidashira, Icumu ry’ubugabe bgawe n’icumu ry’ūganza atunganye." 
Hebrews1:9 Wakunze ukugororoka, wanka ubugarariji, Ni co catumye Imana, ni yo Mana yawe, ikurobanuza amavuta y’umunezero, ikakurutisha bagenzi bawe." 
Hebrews1:10 Kandi iti Ni wewe, Uhoraho, mbere na mbere washizeh’ itanguriro ry’isi, Kand’ amajuru n’igikorwa c’intoke zawe." 
Hebrews1:11 Ivyo bizoshira, ariko weho uzokwamaho; Ivyo vyose bizosāza nk’impuzu," 
Hebrews1:12 Kand’ uzobizinga nk’umutamana, Bikūranwe n’ibindi nk’ukw impuzu zikūranywa. Ariko weho ur’ uko wamye, Imyaka y’ukubaho kwawe ntizoshira." 
Hebrews1:13 Ariko ni nde wo mu bamarayika yigeze kubarira, it’ Icara i buryo bganje, Ushitse aho nzohindurira abansi bawe indava yo musi y’ibirenge vyawe?" 
Hebrews1:14 Mbeg’ abamarayika bose s’impwemu ziyikorera, zitumwa gukora igikorwa kubg’ abazoragwa agakiza?" 
Hebrews2:1 Ni co gituma dukwiye kurushiriza kwitwaririka ivyo twumvise, kugira ngo ntidutwarwe akayombekere tukabivako." 
Hebrews2:2 Kw ijambo ryavugiwe mu kanwa k’abamarayika ryagumyeho, kand’ ibicumuro vyose no kutaryumvira bikagererwa ingero bikwiranye," 
Hebrews2:3 tweho tuzokwikiza dute, ni twanjanjwa ku gakiza kangana gartyo? Kabanje kuvugwa n’Umwami wacu, kagakomezwa kuri twebge n’abakumvise," 
Hebrews2:4 Imana ifatanije na bo kugashingira intahe, iyishingisha ibimenyetso n’ibitangaza n’ibikomeye vy’uburyo bginshi n’ingabire za Mpwemu Yera zagabanganijwe nk’uko yagomvye." 
Hebrews2:5 Kukw atar’ abamarayika Imana yahaye gutwara isi izobaho, iyo tuvuga." 
Hebrews2:6 Ariko har’ ah’ umuntu yashinze intahe, at’ Umuntu n’iki ah’ umwibuka, Cank’ umwana w’umuntu ah’ umugendera?" 
Hebrews2:7 Wamucishije bugufi, aba musi y’abamarayika gato. Wamwambitse ubgiza n’icubahiro nk’igitsibo, Wamuhaye kugaba ibikorwa vy’amaboko yawe." 
Hebrews2:8 Wamuhaye kuganza ibintu vyose, ubishira musi y’ibirenge vyiwe. Kw Imana yamuhaye kuganza ibintu vyose nta co yishigarije itamuhaye kugiganza. Ariko none ntiturabona ibintu vyose biganzwa na we." 
Hebrews2:9 Ariko, uwacishijwe bugufi, akaba musi y’abamarayika gato, ni we Yesu, tumubona yambitswe ubgiza n’icubahiro nk’igitsibo, kubg’ imibabaro y’urupfu, kugira ng’ ubuntu bg’Imana butume arogorera umuntu wese urupfu." 
Hebrews2:10 Kukw iyo, (ni yo yaremewe vyose kandi ni yo ibeshejeho vyose), mu kurōngōra abana benshi ngw ibazane mu bgiza, vyari biyikwiye gutunganisha rwose indōngōzi y’agakiza kabo kubabazwa." 
Hebrews2:11 Kuk’ uweza n’abezwa bose bākomotse kur’ Imwe: ni co gituma atagira isoni zo kubīta bene Se," 
Hebrews2:12 ati Nzobarira bene Data izina ryawe, Nzoririmba ngutazira hagati y’ishengero." 
Hebrews2:13 Kand’ ati Nzokwama ndayizigira. Kand’ at’ Ehe twe n’abana Imana yampaye. 
Hebrews2:14 Nuko rero, kukw abana bahūje inyama n’amaraso, na we ubgiwe yahūje ivyo na bo, kugira ngw abone ukw apfa, kand’ urupfu rwiwe aruhindurishe ubusa ūfise ubushobozi bg’urupfu, ni we wa Murwanizi," 
Hebrews2:15 kandi ngw arokore abājakariye ubgoba bg’urupfu bose, imisi yose y’ukubaho kwabo." 
Hebrews2:16 Kuko tuzi neza kw abamarayika atari bo yatoye, ariko yatoye uruvyaro rwa Aburahamu." 
Hebrews2:17 Ni co catumye vyaramubereye gushushanywa na bene Se kuri vyose, ngw abe umuherezi mukuru wo mu vy’Imana, w’imbabazi kand’ agororoka, abe impongano y’ivyaha vy’abantu." 
Hebrews2:18 Kuk’ ubgiwe ko yababajwe no kugeragezwa, ashobora no gutabara abageragezwa." 
Hebrews3:1 Nuko rero, bene Data bera, abasangiye ihamagarwa riva mw ijuru, ni mwitegereze Yesu, intumwa n’umuherezi mukuru w’ivyo twizeye tukavyatura," 
Hebrews3:2 ayobokera iyamutoranije, nk’uko Mose yayoboka mu rugo rwayo hose." 
Hebrews3:3 Kuk’ uyo yiyumviriwe kw akwiye guhabga icubahiro kiruta ica Mose, nk’ukw ishimwe ry’uwubatse urugo riruta iry’ urugo." 
Hebrews3:4 Kuk’ urugo rwose rugira ūrwubaka, arikw Imana ni yo yubatse ibintu vyose." 
Hebrews3:5 Kandi Mose yayoboka mu rugo rwayo hose nk’umushumba, kugira ngw abe icabona co gushingira intahe ibizovugwa hanyuma." 
Hebrews3:6 Ariko Kristo ayoboka nk’Umwana, atwara urugo rwayo. Kand’ urugo rwayo ni twebge, namba tubangirije ubushizi bg’amanga n’ukwirata ivyizigiro vyacu rwose, gushitsa kw iherezo." 
Hebrews3:7 Nuko, nk’uko Mpwemu Yera avuga, at’ Uyu musi aho mwumvira ijwi ryayo," 
Hebrews3:8 Ntimukomantaze imitima yanyu, nk’uko mwayikomantaje mu gihe co kuratsa, Kuri wa musi wo kugerageza mu bugaragwa," 
Hebrews3:9 Aho ba sogokuruza banyu bangeragereje bancaca, Bakabona ibikorwa vyanje imyaka mirongwine." 
Hebrews3:10 Ni co catumye ngirira umwikomo ab’ ico gihe, Nkavuga, nti Bama bazimira mu mitima yabo, Kandi ntibamenya inzira zanje;" 
Hebrews3:11 Nk’uko narahiranye uburake bganje, Nti Ntibazoshika mu buruhukiro bganje." 
Hebrews3:12 Bene Data, ni mwirinde, ntihagire uwo muri mwebge agira umutima mubi utizera, umutera kureka Imana nzima." 
Hebrews3:13 Ariko muhanūrane uko bukeye bicitwa uyu musi, ntihagire uwo muri mwebge akomantazwa umutima n’uruhendo rw’icaha." 
Hebrews3:14 Kuko twacitse abasangiye Kristo, namba tubangirije rwose ivyizigiro vyacu twatanguranye gushitsa kw iherezo:" 
Hebrews3:15 bikivugwa, ng’ Uyu musi aho mwumvira ijwi ryayo, Ntimukomantaze imitima yanyu, nk’uko mwayikomantaje mu gihe co kuratsa." 
Hebrews3:16 Ni ba nde bamaze kwumva bakayiratsa? Mbega s’abāvuye muri Egiputa bose, barōngōwe na Mose?" 
Hebrews3:17 Kandi ni ba nde yagiriye umwikomo imyaka mirongwine? S’abācumuye, imivyimba yabo igahindikirana mu bugaragwa?" 
Hebrews3:18 Ni ba nde yarahiye ko batazoshika mu buruhukiro bgayo? S’abatāyumviye? 
Hebrews3:19 Kandi tubona ko batāshoboye kubushikamwo, kuko batizeye." 
Hebrews4:1 Nuko, kukw isezerano ryo gushika mu buruhukiro bgayo rikiriho, twiyubare kugira ngo kumbure ntihagire uwo muri mwebge yiyumvirwa kw akērerewe." 
Hebrews4:2 Kuko natwe twabgiwe ubutumwa bgiza nka bo, ariko, ijambo bumvise ntiryābagiriye ikimazi, kuko ritāvanzwe n’ukwizera mu mitima y’abāryumvise." 
Hebrews4:3 Kuko twebge abizeye dushika mur’ ubgo buruhukiro, nk’uko yavuze, iti Nk’uko narahiranye uburake bganje, Nti Ntibazoshika mu buruhukiro bganje: naho yari yarahejeje ibikorwa vyayo, uhereye ku kuremwa kw’ isi." 
Hebrews4:4 Kuko har’ aho yavuze ku vy’ umusi w’indwi nk’ibi, it’ Imana yaruhutse ku musi ugira indwi ibikorwa vyayo vyose." 
Hebrews4:5 Kandi na hano, ngo Ntibazoshika mu buruhukiro bganje." 
Hebrews4:6 Nuko rero, kuko bukibīkiwe bamwe ngo babushikemwo, arikw abābanje kubgirwa ubutumwa bgiza bābujijwe kubushikamwo no kutumvira Imana," 
Hebrews4:7 yongera gutoranya umusi, ni wo uyu musi; ivugira mu kanwa ka Dawidi, igihe kirekire cane gihise, nk’uko tumaze kuvuga, it’ Uyu musi aho mwumvira ijwi ryayo Ntimukomantaze imitima yanyu." 
Hebrews4:8 Kukw iyaba Yosuwa yarabaruhuye, ntiba yaravuze ubga nyuma ivy’ uwundi musi." 
Hebrews4:9 Nuko rero haracarih’ uburuhukiro bg’isabato bubīkiwe abantu b’Imana. 
Hebrews4:10 Kuk’ ūshitse mu buruhukiro bgayo, na we aba aruhutse ibikorwa vyiwe, nk’ukw Imana yaruhutse ivyayo." 
Hebrews4:11 Nuko tugire umwete wo gushika mur’ ubgo buruhukiro, hoye kugira umuntu agwa, akurikiye icitegererezo ca ba bandi co kutumvira Imana." 
Hebrews4:12 Kukw ijambo ry’Imana ari rizima, rifise ubukuba, rifise ubugi buruta ubg’ inkota zose, rikinjira n’aho ritanya ubugingo n’impwemu, rigatanya ingingo n’umusokōro, risuzuma ivyo umutima wiyumvira, ukagabira." 
Hebrews4:13 Kand’ imbere yayo nta caremwe gihishijwe, ariko vyose vyambaye ubusa, biragaragara, imbere y’inyonga z’Iyizotubaza ivyo twakoze." 
Hebrews4:14 Nuko, ko dufise umuherezi mukuru akomeye, yaciye mw ijuru, ni Yesu Umwana w’Imana, tubangirize ivyo twizera tukavyatura." 
Hebrews4:15 Kuk’ umuherezi mukuru dufise, atar’ ūdashobora kubabarana natwe mu ntege nke zacu, ariko n’uwageragejwe uburyo bgose nkatwe, yamara we nta caha yakoze." 
Hebrews4:16 Nuko ni twēgēre intebe y’ubuntu dushize ubgoba, kugira ngo turonke ikigongwe, tubone ubuntu bgo kudutabara mu gihe gikwiye." 
Hebrews5:1 Umuherezi wese mukuru, kuko yarobanuwe mu bantu, ashirirwaho gukorera Imana kubg’ abantu, kugira ngw ashikane amashikanwa, atange ibimazi, vyompi vy’ivyaha;" 
Hebrews5:2 kand’ ashobora kwihanganira inyoberwa n’abazimiye, kuko na we nyene har’ ah’ agira intege nke." 
Hebrews5:3 Ni co gituma akwiye no kwitangira ibimazi vy’ivyiwe vyaha, nk’ukw abitangira abandi bantu." 
Hebrews5:4 Nta muntu yiha ico cubahiro, shit’ ahamagawe n’Imana, nk’uko Aroni yahamagawe." 
Hebrews5:5 Ni ko biri, na Kristo si we yihaye ico cubahiro co kuba umuherezi mukuru, ariko yagihawe n’iyamubariye, it’ Ur’ Ubura bganje, Uyu musi ndakuvyaye." 
Hebrews5:6 Nk’uko yavuze ahandi, it’ Ur’ umuherezi ibihe bidashira, Mu buryo bga Melekisedeki." 
Hebrews5:7 Kristo mu misi yabaye mu mubiri, amaze kwinginga no gusenga cane iyashoboye kumukiza urupfu, atakamba cane arira, kand’ amaze kwumvirwa kubgo kuyubaha kwiwe," 
Hebrews5:8 naho yar’ Umwana, yigishwa kwumvira Imana n’ivyo yababajwe," 
Hebrews5:9 kand’ amaze guhīngūrwa rwose, abera abamwumvira bose inyanduruko y’agakiza kadashira:" 
Hebrews5:10 Imana imaze kumwita umuherezi mukuru mu buryo bga Melekisedeki. 
Hebrews5:11 Tumufiseko vyinshi vyo kuvuga, kandi bigoye isobanura, kuko mwabaye ibitumva." 
Hebrews5:12 Naho mwari mugeze kuba abigisha, kuko mumaze igihe kirekire mwiga, mukwiye kwongera kwigishwa namwe nyene ivya mbere vy’itanguriro ry’ivyavuzwe n’Imana: kandi mwahindutse abakwiye gutungwa n’amata, s’ukugaburirwa ivyo kurya bigumye." 
Hebrews5:13 Nuk’ ūtunzwe n’amata aba ataramenya ijambo ry’ukugororoka, kukw aba ar’ uruhinja." 
Hebrews5:14 Ariko, ivyo kurya bigumye n’ivy’ abakuze, bafise ubgenge, maze kubgo kwama babukoresha, bumogorera gutandukanya ikibi n’iciza." 
Hebrews6:1 Nuko rero turēngāne ivya mbere vya Kristo, twīgire imbere, dushike ku vyo gutunganywa rwose, twoye gusubira gushirah’ itanguriro ryo kwihana ibikorwa vy’impfagusa, no kwizera Imana," 
Hebrews6:2 no kwigisha ivyo kubatizwa n’ivyo kurambikwakw ibiganza, n’ivyo kuzuka kw’abapfuye, n’ivyo gucirwakw iteka kw’ibihe bidashira." 
Hebrews6:3 Imana ni yabikunda turagenza durtyo. 
Hebrews6:4 Kukw abamaze kwākirwa n’umuco, bagatamira ingabire iva mw ijuru, bagasangira Mpwemu Yera," 
Hebrews6:5 bagatamira ijambo ryiza ry’Imana, n’ububasha bgo mu gihe kizoza," 
Hebrews6:6 maze bakagwa bakabivamwo, ntibishoboka gusubira kubahindura basha ngo bihane: kuko bongera kwibambira Umwana w’Imana, bakamutēterereza ahibonekeza." 
Hebrews6:7 Indimiro zinyoye imvura yaziguyeko kenshi, iyo zimezemw’ ibirimwa bikwiye abazirimiwe, zironka umugisha w’Imana." 
Hebrews6:8 Arikw iyo zimezemw’ imikere n’ibitovu, ziba zisivye, ziba zishigaje gatoya zikavumwa, iherezo ryazo n’uguturirwa." 
Hebrews6:9 Ariko, abo nkunda, naho tuvuze durtyo, turazi ivyanyu tudakekeranya yuko birusha ivyo kuba vyiza, kandi bizanana n’agakiza." 
Hebrews6:10 Imana ntigabitanya ngo yibagire ibikorwa vyanyu n’urukundo mwerekanye ko mukunze izina ryayo, kuko mwātunga abera, na none mukibatunze." 
Hebrews6:11 Kandi turagomba cane yuk’ umuntu wese wo muri mwebge yerekana uwo mwete nyene w’ivyizigiro vyuzuye gushitsa kw iherezo: 
Hebrews6:12 kugira ngo ntimube ibinebge, ariko mwīgāne abaheshwa n’ukwizera n’ukwihangana kuragwa ivyasezeranywe." 
Hebrews6:13 Hamwe Imana yasezeranira Aburahamu isezerano, kukw ata we yogira indahiro ayiruta, yarīrahiye," 
Hebrews6:14 it’ Eka no kuguha umugisha nzowuguha, kandi no kukugwiza nzokugwiza." 
Hebrews6:15 Ni ko vyamubereye: amaze kwihangana ahabga ivyasezeranywe. 
Hebrews6:16 Kukw abantu bagira indahiro ūbaruta, no mu mpāri zabo zose indahiro irengeje ikaba ari yo iziheraheza." 
Hebrews6:17 Ni co catumye Imana, kukw igomba kurushiriza kwereka abaragwa b’ivyasezeranywe ingen’ imigabo yayo idahinduka, ishira hagati indahiro kuba umuhūza;" 
Hebrews6:18 kugira ngo bibiri bidahinduka, ivyo Imana itabasha kubesheramwo, biduheshe kurema cane, twebge abashitse mu buhungiro, ni bgo kubangiriza ivyizigiro vyashizwe imbere yacu." 
Hebrews6:19 Ivyo vyizigiro tubifise nk’ikizirika umutima kigumye, gikomeye, cinjira hirya y’igihūzu gikīngiriye ahēra cane," 
Hebrews6:20 aho Yesu yatwinjiriye, atwitangiye imbere, amaze guhinduka umuherezi mukuru w’ibihe bidashira mu buryo bga Melekisedeki." 
Hebrews7:1 Melekisedeki uyo, umwami w’i Salemu, umuherezi w’Imana isumba vyose, ni we yasanganiye Aburahamu, aramuhezagira, hamwe Aburahamu yatabaruka, avuye kunesha abami," 
Hebrews7:2 kandi ni we Aburahamu yagabanirije ikigiracumi muri vyose, irya mbere asobanurwa, ng’ Umwami agororoka, kand’ irya kabiri yitwa Umwami w’i Salemu, risobanurwa, ng’ Umwami w’amahoro." 
Hebrews7:3 Nta se, nta nyina, nta karonda, nta tanguriro ry’imisi cank’ iherezo ry’ubugingo, arikw agereranywa n’Umwana w’Imana, kandi na ntaryo ahora ar’ umuherezi." 
Hebrews7:4 Nuko mwiyumvire uwo muntu ingen’ ahambaye, uwo Aburahamu sogokuruza mukuru yahaye ikigiracumi co mu minyago iruta iyindi." 
Hebrews7:5 Kandi mu bana ba Lewi, ivyagezwe bigera yukw abahawe ubuherezi batangisha abantu ikigiracumi, ni bo bene wabo, nah’ abo bandurutse mu rura rwa Aburahamu." 
Hebrews7:6 Ariko wa wundi adaharūrwa mu muryango wabo yatangishije Aburahamu ikigiracumi, kand’ ahezagira nyene gusezeranywa." 
Hebrews7:7 Ariko nta wohakana k’uworoshe adahezagirwa n’ūmurengeye. 
Hebrews7:8 Kandi muri twebge, abantu bapfa ni bo bahabga ikigiracumi, ariko muri ya majambo yandi cahawe ūshingirwa intahe kw ariho." 
Hebrews7:9 Kandi twoshobora kuvuga yuko Lewi, umwe ahabga ikigiracumi, na we yari yaragitanze muri Aburahamu," 
Hebrews7:10 kuko yar’ akiri mu rura rwa sekuruza, hamwe Melekisedeki yamusanganira." 
Hebrews7:11 Non’ iyaba gutunganywa rwose kwāzanywe n’ubuherezi bg’Abalewi — kuko ku ngoma yabgo ari ho ubgo bgoko bgāhawe ivyagezwe — n’iki catumye bigikwiye ko haboneka uwundi muherezi wo mu buryo bga Melekisedeki, atavugwa mu buryo bga Aroni?" 
Hebrews7:12 Iy’ ubuherezi buhindutse, ivyagezwe ntibibura guhinduka na vyo." 
Hebrews7:13 Kuk’ uwavuzwekw ivyo, ar’ uwo mu wundi muryango, utigeze kuvamw’ uwakoze igikorwa co ku gicaniro." 
Hebrews7:14 Birazwi yuk’ Umwami wacu yakomotse kuri Yuda, kand’ uwo muryango Mose nta co yawuvuzeko c’ubuherezi." 
Hebrews7:15 Ivyo birushiriza guseruka rwose, ko haboneka uwundi muherezi, ahwanye na Melekisedeki," 
Hebrews7:16 atāhawe ubuherezi n’uko vyashinzweho n’ivyagezwe vyo mu buryo bg’abantu, ariko yahawe ubushinzwe n’ubushobozi bg’ubugingo budashobora gukūrwaho." 
Hebrews7:17 Kukw ashingirwa intahe, ng’ Ur’ umuherezi ibihe bidashira, Mu buryo bga Melekisedeki." 
Hebrews7:18 Nuko rer’ icagezwe ca mbere cakūweho kubg’ inkomezi nke zaco n’ikimazi gike," 
Hebrews7:19 (kukw ivyagezwe bitigeze kugira ico bihīngūra rwose) hasubizwah’ ivyizigiro bikiruta, biduhesha kwegera Imana." 
Hebrews7:20 Kand’ ivyo ntivyabaye hatarih’ indahiro. 
Hebrews7:21 Abalewi bo bāhawe ubuherezi ata ndahiro; arikw iyabuhaye uyo yararahiye, imubgiye, it’ Uhoraho ararahiye, ntazokwicuza, At’ Ur’ umuherezi ibihe bidashira." 
Hebrews7:22 Uko ni ko Yesu yabaye umwishinzi w’isezerano riruta rya rindi. 
Hebrews7:23 Kandi ba bandi bābaye abaherezi benshi, kuk’ urupfu rubabuza kwamaho;" 
Hebrews7:24 arik’ uyo we, kuko yamah’ ibihe bidashira, afise ubuherezi budakūrwaho." 
Hebrews7:25 Ni co gituma ashobora gukiza rwose abashikīra Imana kubgiwe, kuko na ntaryo yamaho ngw abasabire." 
Hebrews7:26 Vyari bitubereye kugira umuherezi mukuru ameze artyo, yera, atagira ubugunge, atanduye, yatandukanijwe n’abanyavyaha, yashizwe hejuru y’amajuru," 
Hebrews7:27 atarinda kubanza gutanga ibimazi vy’ivyiwe vyaha uko bukeye, nka ba baherezi bakuru bandi, hanyuma agatanga ivy’ abandi bantu. Kukw ivyo yabikoze rimwe, hamwe yitanga." 
Hebrews7:28 Ivyagezwe bishirah’ abanyantege nke kuba abaherezi bakuru, arikw ijambo ry’indahiro yaherukiye ivyagezwe rishirah’ Umwana w’Imana yahīngūwe rwose gushitsa ibihe bidashira." 
Hebrews8:1 Mu yo tuvuga, yose arutwa na rimwe, n’iri: dufise umuherezi mukuru ameze artyo, avyagiye i buryo bg’intebe y’Īhambaye cane yo mw ijuru," 
Hebrews8:2 akorera ahēra, no mw ihema nyakuri, ryashinzwe n’Uhoraho atar’ abantu." 
Hebrews8:3 Kuk’ umuherezi mukuru wese ashirirwaho gushikana amashikanwa no gucumita ibimazi. Ni co gituma wa wundi na we akwiye kugira ic’ ashikana. 
Hebrews8:4 Iyaba ari mw isi ntiyobaye umuherezi, kuko har’ abandi bashikana amashikanwa nk’ukw ivyagezwe bibgiriza." 
Hebrews8:5 Kand’ abo bakorera igishushanyo n’igitūtu c’ivyo mw ijuru, nk’uko Mose yabgiwe n’Imana, agira akoreshe rya hema, it’ Ugire umwete wo gukoresha vyose, ubigereranye n’ikigereranyo werekewe kuri wa musozi." 
Hebrews8:6 Ariko none, igikorwa yahawe kirusha icabo kuba ciza, nk’ukw ar’ umuhūza w’isezerano riruta iryabo, kuko ryashizweho n’ivyasezeranywe biruta ivy’ iryabo." 
Hebrews8:7 Iyo rya rindi rya mbere ritabakw agasembga, ntihari hakwiye kuronderwa irindi." 
Hebrews8:8 Kuko yavuze ibagaya, it’ Eh’ imisi igira ize, ni jewe Uhoraho mbivuze, Aho nzosezerana isezerano risha n’umuryango w’Abisirayeli n’umuryango wa Yuda," 
Hebrews8:9 Ridahwanye n’isezerano nasezeranye na ba sekuruza, Ku musi nabafata ukuboko nkabakūra mu gihugu ca Egiputa, Kuko batāgumye mw isezerano ryanje, Nanje sinabababara, ni jewe Uhoraho mbivuze." 
Hebrews8:10 Kukw iri ari ryo sezerano nzosezerana n’umuryango w’Abisirayeli Hanyuma y’iyo misi, ni jewe Uhoraho mbivuze: Nzoshira ivyagezwe vyanje mu bgenge bgabo, No ku mitima yabo kandi ni ho nzovyandika, Nanje nzobabera Imana, Na bo bazoba abantu banje." 
Hebrews8:11 Kandi ntibazokwigishanya, ng’ umuntu wese yigishe mugenzi we, Canke ngo yigishe uwo bavukana, ati Menya Uhoraho, Kuko bose bazonyimenyera, Uhereye kuri nyarucari ugashitsa k’ūhambaye muri bo." 
Hebrews8:12 Kuko nzobagirira ikigongwe ku kugabitanya kwabo, Kand’ ivyaha vyabo sinzovyibuka ukundi." 
Hebrews8:13 Kw avuga, at’ Isezerano risha, rer’ irya mbere yarishājishije; arikw igisāza kikaba akāheze kiba kigira gikamangane." 
Hebrews9:1 Nukw isezerano rya mbere na ryo ryarimw’ ibirōngōra ivy’ ubuherezi, rifise n’ahēra, ariko ho mur’ iyi si." 
Hebrews9:2 Kuko hār’ ihema ryiteguwe, mu ryo hino hārimw’ igiterekwakw amatara, n’ameza, n’imitsima y’ibiterekerwa yama kuri yo: iryo ryitwa Ahēra." 
Hebrews9:3 Kandi hirya y’igihuzu ca kabiri gikinze, hār’ ihema ryitwa Ahēra Cane:" 
Hebrews9:4 hārimw’ igicaniro co kwoserezakw imibavu cakozwe mw izahabu, hārimwo n’isandugu y’isezerano yometswekw izahabu impande zose, irimw’ urwavya rw’izahabu rurimwo manu, irimwo na ya nkoni ya Aroni yashurika, na vya bisate vy’amabuye vyanditswekw isezerano." 
Hebrews9:5 Kandi hejuru yayo hār’ abakerubi b’ubgiza bateye igitūtu umutemere wo guhongerako: ivyo ntidushobora kubidonda kimwe‐kimwe nonaha. 
Hebrews9:6 Nukw ivyo vyateguwe birtyo, abaherezi na ntaryo bama binjira mw ihema ryo hino, kugira ngo bashitse ivy’ ubuherezi:" 
Hebrews9:7 ariko mu rya kabiri hinjiramw’ umuherezi mukuru wenyene, rimwe gusa uk’ umwaka utashe, ariko ntiyinjiramwo atajanye amaraso yo kwitangirira no gutangirira ubuzimuzimu bg’abantu." 
Hebrews9:8 Mpwemu Yera amenyekanisha artyo yukw inzira ija ahēra cane itaribgerekanwe, ihema rya mbere rikiriho:" 
Hebrews9:9 ni ryo kigereranyo c’igihe ca none, abakurikira ivyagezwe vyaryo bashikana amashikanwa bagatanga ibimazi, ariko ku ruhande rw’ijwi ryo mu mutima ntibishobora gutunganya ūsenga," 
Hebrews9:10 kukw ivyo, hamwe n’ivy’ ivyo kurya n’ivyo kunywa n’ivyo kwiyuhagira bo n’ukwoza vy’uburyo bginshi, ar’ amabgirizwa yo mu buryo bg’abantu gusa, yashinzwe gushitsa igihe co gutunganywa." 
Hebrews9:11 Ariko Kristo amaze kuza, umuherezi mukuru w’ivyiza bizoza, aca mw ihema rirusha rya rindi kuba irihambaye n’iritunganye rwose, ritākozwe n’intoke, bisobanurwa ngo ritar’ iryo mu vyaremwe vy’ubu." 
Hebrews9:12 Kand’ amaraso y’impene cank’ ay’ amashūri, si yo yamushikanye ahēra cane, ariko yahashikanywe n’ayiwe maraso rimwe gusa, yironkeye ugucungura kw’ibihe bidashira." 
Hebrews9:13 Non’ amaraso y’impene n’ay’ amapfizi bo n’umunyota w’inka y’iriza ucucagiwe abahumanye, ko vyeza imibiri igahumanuka," 
Hebrews9:14 mbeg’ amaraso ya Kristo, uwo yitanze ku Mana atagira agasembga, abitewe na Mpwemu ahoraho, ntazorushiriza guhumanura imitima yanyu ngw ibikorwa vy’impfagusa biyivemwo, kugira ngo mubone ingene mukorera Imana nzima?" 
Hebrews9:15 Ni co gituma aba umuhūza, ahesha isezerano risha, kugira ngw abāhamagawe bahabge umwandu udashira w’isezerano, bitewe n’uko habayeh’ urupfu rucungura abacumuye bakiganzwa n’isezerano rya mbere." 
Hebrews9:16 Kukw ah’ icete c’iragi kiri hakwiye rwose yuk’ urupfu rw’uwaraze ruseruka. 
Hebrews9:17 Icete c’iragi kibeshwaho n’urupfu rwonyene, kuko kitagira ikimazi uwaraze akiriho." 
Hebrews9:18 Ni co gituma isezerano rya mbere ritāsezeranywe ata maraso. 
Hebrews9:19 Mose amaze kubgira abantu bose amabgirizwa yose nk’uko vyagezwe, yābīra amaraso y’amashūri n’ay’ impene n’amazi n’ubgoya bg’intama buzigishijwe agahama, yābīra na ezobu, acucagira igitabo c’ivyagezwe, bo n’abantu bose," 
Hebrews9:20 arababgira, at’ Aya ni yo maraso y’isezerano Imana yabagereye." 
Hebrews9:21 Kand’ ihema n’imbombovu zose z’ivy’ ubuherezi, na vyo n’uko abicucagira amaraso." 
Hebrews9:22 Nk’ukw ivyagezwe biri, ibintu ni nka vyose vyozwa n’amaraso, kandi hatavuye amaraso ntihaba guharirwa ivyaha." 
Hebrews9:23 Nuko vyari bibereye kw ibigereranyo vy’ivyo mw ijuru vyozwa n’ivyo bimazi, ariko, ivyo mw ijuru ubgavyo bikozwa n’ibimazi biruta ivyo." 
Hebrews9:24 Kuko Kristo atinjiye ahēra cane hākozwe n’intoke, h’ikigereranyo c’ah’ ukuri, ariko yinjiye mw ijuru ubgaho, kugira ngo non’ aduserukire imbere y’inyonga z’Imana." 
Hebrews9:25 Kandi ntiyashikanyweyo no kwitanga kenshi, nk’uk’ umuherezi mukuru yinjira ahēra cane uk’ umwaka utashe, ajanye amaraso atar’ ayiwe;" 
Hebrews9:26 kukw iyo biba birtyo, aba yar’ akwiye kubabazwa kenshi uhereye ku kuremwa kw’ isi. Yamar’ ubu yabonetse rimwe kw iherezo ry’ibihe, kugira ngw akūzeh’ icaha ukwitanga." 
Hebrews9:27 Kandi nk’ukw abantu bābīkiwe gupfa rimwe, hanyuma yaho hakaza amateka," 
Hebrews9:28 na Kristo n’uko, yamaze gutangwa rimwe ngo yishirekw ivyaha vya benshi, azoboneka ubga kabiri, atazanywe n’ivyaha, abonekere gukiza abamwiteze." 
Hebrews10:1 Ivyagezwe ko bifise igitūtu c’ivyiza bizoza, bidafise ishusho bgite y’ivyo vyiza, nta ho vyoshobora guhīngūra abēgēra igicaniro, bibahīngūrisha ivyo bimazi nyene bahora batanga imyaka n’imyaka." 
Hebrews10:2 Iyo bibishobora, mbega ntibaba barasizeho kubitanga? Kukw abavyitangirira bamaze guhumanurwa rwose rimwe, bataba bakigira imitima irimw’ ijwi ribāgiriza ivyaha." 
Hebrews10:3 Ariko mur’ ivyo bimazi har’ icibukiriza ivyaha uk’ umwaka utashe. 
Hebrews10:4 Kuko bidashoboka kw amaraso y’amapfizi n’ay’ impene akūrah’ ivyaha. 
Hebrews10:5 Ni co catumye, hamwe yaza mw isi, avuga, At’ Ibimazi n’amashikanwa ntiwabigomvye, Ariko wanteguriye umubiri." 
Hebrews10:6 Ibimazi vyoshejwe bidasonōye, n’ibimazi vy’ivyaha, ntivyaguhimbaye:" 
Hebrews10:7 Mperako ndavuga, nt’ Ehe ndaje, (Mu muzingo w’igitabo ni ko vyanditswe kuri jewe) Nzanywe no gukora ivy’ ugomba, Mana." 
Hebrews10:8 Ahejeje kuvuga haruguru, at’ Ibimazi n’amashikanwa, n’ibimazi vyoshejwe bidasonōye n’ibimazi vy’ivyaha, ntiwabigomvye kandi ntivyaguhimbaye (ni vyo bitangwa nk’uko bibgirijwe n’ivyagezwe)," 
Hebrews10:9 aherakw aravuga, at’ Ehe nzanywe no gukora ivy’ ugomba. Akūrah’ ivya mbere ngw ashinge ivya kabiri." 
Hebrews10:10 Ukwo kugomba kwayo ni kwo kwatumye twezwa, tubiheshwa n’uk’ umubiri wa Yesu Kristo watanzwe rimwe gusa." 
Hebrews10:11 Kand’ umuherezi wese ahagarara uko bukeye akora ivy’ ubuherezi, atanga kenshi ivyo bimazi nyene, ata ho vyoshobora gukūrah’ ivyaha na mba." 
Hebrews10:12 Arik’ uwo we, amaze gutanga ikimazi kimwe c’ivyaha c’intahava, avyagira i buryo bg’Imana," 
Hebrews10:13 ahēraho, arorēra igihe abansi biwe bazohindurirwa indava yo musi y’ibirenge vyiwe." 
Hebrews10:14 Kukw ikimazi kimwe ari co yatunganishije rwose abezwa, ukazoshitsa ibihe bidashira." 
Hebrews10:15 Kandi na Mpwemu Yera ni we cabona kidushingira intahe y’ivyo. Amaze kuvuga," 
Hebrews10:16 at’ Iri ni ryo sezerano nzosezerana na bo Hanyuma y’iyo misi, ni jewe Uhoraho mbivuze; Nzoshira ivyagezwe vyanje mu mitima yabo, No mu bgenge bgabo kandi ni ho nzovyandika: arongera" 
Hebrews10:17 ati Kand’ ivyaha vyabo n’ukugabitanya kwabo sinzovyibuka ukundi. 
Hebrews10:18 Ariko, ah’ ivyo bihariwe, ntihaba hakiriho gutanga ikimazi c’ivyaha." 
Hebrews10:19 Nuko bene Data, ko turi n’ubushizi bg’ubgoba bgo gushikanwa ahēra cane n’amaraso ya Yesu," 
Hebrews10:20 duciye mu nzira yadutoboreye nsha iri n’ubugingo, ica mu gihuzu gikinze, bisobanurwa ngo mu mubiri wiwe;" 
Hebrews10:21 kandi ko dufise umuherezi akomeye aganza urugo rw’Imana," 
Hebrews10:22 twegereze dufise imitima y’ukuri, twizeye ata mazinda, imitima yacu icucagiwe ngw ivanwemw’ ibitwagiriza bibi, imibiri yacu yuhagijwe amazi meza." 
Hebrews10:23 Tugumye ukwatura ivyizigiro vyacu ntikunyiganyige, kuk’ uwasezeranye ar’ uwo kwizerwa," 
Hebrews10:24 kandi twiyumviraneko, kugira ngo turwane ishaka ryo gukundana n’iry’ ibikorwa vyiza," 
Hebrews10:25 twoye guheba gukoranira hamwe, nk’uko bamwe bagira, ariko duhanūrane, kand’ uko mubonye wa musi wegereza, murushirize kugenza murtyo." 
Hebrews10:26 Kuko namba dukora ivyaha ibigirankana, kandi tumaze guhabga kumenya ivy’ ukuri, ntihaba hagisigaye ikimazi c’ivyaha," 
Hebrews10:27 ariko haba hasigaye kwitegana ubgoba gucirwakw iteka, no kwitega umuriro w’inkazi, uzorigata abansi b’Imana." 
Hebrews10:28 Ūkēngereye ivyagezwe vya Mose, ivyabona bibiri canke bitatu biramwicisha, ata kagongwe." 
Hebrews10:29 Mugira ng’umuntu ntazoba akwiye guhanwa ibirushirije cane, asiribanze Umwana w’Imana, akiyumvira amaraso y’isezerano yamwejeje kw ar’ igihumane, agacokora Mpwemu w’ubuntu?" 
Hebrews10:30 Kuko tuzi uwavuze, at’ Uguhōra n’ukwanje, ni jewe nzobasubiriza mu nkōko. Kand’ at’ Uhoraho azocira urubanza abantu biwe." 
Hebrews10:31 Erega birateye ubgoba gukorokera mu maboko y’Imana nzima. 
Hebrews10:32 Ariko mwibuke imisi ya mbere, hamwe mwari mumaze kwākirwa n’umuco, mwihanganira ibisinzikaza vy’indwano nyinshi:" 
Hebrews10:33 kimwe, mwacitse akābarore mutukwa mubabazwa; ikindi, mwafatanije n’abagirirwa bartyo." 
Hebrews10:34 Kuko mwababaranye n’ababoshwe, kandi mwemeye munezerewe kunyagwa ivyo mutunze, mumenya yuko mufise itunga riruta ivyo kuba ryiza, rikamaho." 
Hebrews10:35 Nuko ntimute ubushizi bg’ubgoba bganyu, buri n’impēra ikomeye." 
Hebrews10:36 Kuko mukwiye kwihangana, kugira ngo ni mwamara gukora ivy’ Imana igomba mubone guhabga ivyasezeranywe." 
Hebrews10:37 Kuko hasigaye igihe gito cane, Kand’ ūgira aze, azoza, ntazoteba." 
Hebrews10:38 Ariko, umugororotsi wanje azobeshwaho n’ukwizera, Na ho ni yiyonjorora ntazohimbara umutima wanje." 
Hebrews10:39 Ariko tweho ntitur’ abo mu biyonjorora bagahona, ariko tur’ abo mu bizera, ubugingo bgabo bugakizwa." 
Hebrews11:1 Ukwizera n’ukumenya rwose ivyizigirwa, udakekeranya ngo ntibizoba, kand’ ibitabonwa ni kwo kubitumenyesha kw ar’ ivy’ ukuri." 
Hebrews11:2 Icatumye aba kera bashingirwa intahe n’uko bari bagufise. 
Hebrews11:3 Ukwizera ni kwo kutumenyesha yukw isi yaremwe n’ijambo ry’Imana, ni co catumye ibiboneka bitāremwe mu biseruka." 
Hebrews11:4 Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye Abeli aha Imana ikimazi kiruta ica Kayini, ni kwo kwamuhesheje gushingirwa intahe kw ar’ umugororotsi, hamwe Imana yashingira intahe amashikanwa yiwe yukw ari meza, kandi ni kwo kwatumye na none akivuga, naho yapfuye." 
Hebrews11:5 Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye Henoki ajanwa mw ijuru, ngo ntabone urupfu, kandi ntiyaboneka, kukw Imana yamujanye. Kuko yashingiwe intahe atarajanwa yuko yahimbaye Imana," 
Hebrews11:6 kand’ ūtizera ntibishoboka kw ayihimbara; kuk’ uwēgēra Imana akwiye kwizera yukw iriho, igaha impēra abayirondera." 
Hebrews11:7 Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye Nowa yubaha, amaze kubūrirwa n’Imana ibitaribgaboneke, akabāza ubgato bgo kurokora abo mu nzu yiwe, kandi ni kwo kwamuhaye gutsindisha abari mw isi, no kuragwa ukugororoka kuzanwa n’ukwizera." 
Hebrews11:8 Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye Aburahamu yumvira Imana imuhamagaye, akaja ahantu yar’ abīkiwe kuragwa: nukw agenda, atazi iy’ aja." 
Hebrews11:9 Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye aba inyambukīra mu gihugu yasezeraniwe, nk’ikitar’ iciwe, akabana mu mahema na Isaka na Yakobo, abāraganywe na we ivyo vyasezeranywe." 
Hebrews11:10 Kuko yar’ arorereye ca gisagara cubatswe kw itanguriro, umugezi n’umwubatsi waco n’Imana." 
Hebrews11:11 Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye na Sara ashobozwa gusama inda, naho yari yaraciye, kuko yiyumviriye yukw iyasezeranye ar’ iyo kwizerwa." 
Hebrews11:12 Ni co catumye umuntu umwe — kand’ uwo yar’ akāheze — yāmukwako n’isinzi nk’inyenyeri zo kw ijuru, kandi n’abangana n’umusenyi uri kw isēsero ry’ikiyaga utoharūrika." 
Hebrews11:13 Abo bose bāpfuye bacizeye, batarahabga ivyasezeranywe, ariko bārabibona biri kure bakabisāsirira, bakemera kw ar’ akavantara n’ingenzi kw isi." 
Hebrews11:14 Abavuga bartyo baba berekana yuko barondera igihugu cabo bgite. 
Hebrews11:15 Iyo baba barakumbuye ico bavuyemwo, baba barabonye uburyo bgo gusubirayo." 
Hebrews11:16 Ariko noneho barifuza igihugu kirushije ico kuba ciza, n’ico mw ijuru. Ni co gituma Imana itamāramāzwa no kwitwa Imana yabo, kuko yabateguriye igisagara." 
Hebrews11:17 Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye Aburahamu atanga Isaka kw ikimazi, hamwe yagezwa: mber’ uwari yarākīranye igishika amasezerano, yarikw aratanga kw ikimazi umwana wiwe w’ikinege," 
Hebrews11:18 uwo yari yarabariwe ivyiwe, ngo Kuri Isaka ni ho uruvyaro rwawe ruzokwītīrirwa:" 
Hebrews11:19 kuko yishimiye yukw Imana ishobora no kuzura abapfuye, ni co catumye amugarurirwa nk’ūzutse." 
Hebrews11:20 Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye Isaka ahezagira Yakobo na Esau abahesha imigisha y’ibizoba. 
Hebrews11:21 Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye Yakobo, aho yagira acīkāne, ahezagira abana ba Yosefu bompi, agasenga yishimikije ipfundo ry’inkoni yiwe." 
Hebrews11:22 Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye Yosefu, aho yagira apfe, avuga ivyo kuvayo kw’ Abisirayeli, akagera ivy’ amagufa yiwe." 
Hebrews11:23 Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye Mose, amaze kuvuka, anyegezwa n’abavyeyi biwe amezi atatu, kuko babonye kw ar’ akana keza, ntibatinya ibgirizwa ry’umwami." 
Hebrews11:24 Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye Mose, amaze gukura, yanka kwitwa umwana w’umukobga wa Farawo," 
Hebrews11:25 agahitamwo kugiriranwa nabi n’abantu b’Imana, abirutisha kumara igihe mu bihimbaro vy’ivyaha;" 
Hebrews11:26 kuko yiyumviriye yuko gucokoranwa na Kristo ar’ ubutunzi burengeye itunga ryo muri Egiputa, kuko yatumbera ingero azogererwa." 
Hebrews11:27 Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye ava muri Egiputa, ntiyatinya uburake bg’umwami, kuko yashikamye nk’ah’ abona Ītaboneka." 
Hebrews11:28 Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye ashinga Pasika, no kumijagira amaraso, kugira ng’ ūhonnya imfura ntabakoreko." 
Hebrews11:29 Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye baca mu Kiyaga Gitukura, nk’abaca ku musozi, arikw Abanyegiputa babigejeje, bararengerwa." 
Hebrews11:30 Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye inzitiro z’amabuye z’i Yeriko zisenyuka, bamaze kuzikikuza imisi ndwi." 
Hebrews11:31 Ukwizera ni kwo kwatumye Rahabu, maraya, ataranduranwa n’abatumviye Imana, kuko yākīranye amahoro abaje gutata." 
Hebrews11:32 Mvuge ikindi ki? Kukw igihe condengana ndondoye ivya Gideyoni n’ivya Baraki n’ivya Samusoni n’ivya Yefuta n’ivya Dawidi n’ivya Samweli n’ivy’ abāvugishwa n’Imana," 
Hebrews11:33 bāheshejwe n’ukwizera gutsinda abami, no gukora ibigororotse, no kuronka ivyasezeranywe, no kuziba iminwa y’intambge," 
Hebrews11:34 no kuzimya ubukare bg’umuriro, no gukira ubugi bg’inkota, no guhindurwa mu ntege nke ngo zicike inkomezi, no kuba agahebuza mu ntambara, no kunesha ingabo z’abanyamahanga." 
Hebrews11:35 Abagore bāgaruriwe abo bābuze bazutse, abandi bicishwa amahiri ntibemera gucungurwa, kugira ngo baze bahabge ukuzuka kurushiriza kuba kwiza." 
Hebrews11:36 Abandi bāgeragereshwa gushinyagurirwa no gukubitwa ibimoko, mbere bāshirwa mu ngoyi no mu mabohero:" 
Hebrews11:37 bicishijwe amabuye, bākerewemwo kubiri, bārageragejwe, bicishijwe inkota, bāyerera bambaye insāto z’intama n’iz’ impene, bāri baburaniwe, bababazwa, bagirirwa nabi," 
Hebrews11:38 (isi ntiyar’ ibabereye ko bayibamwo), bāyerera mu bugaragwa no mu bisozi no mu masenga no mu vyobo." 
Hebrews11:39 Abo bose bamaze gushingirwa intahe kubg’ ukwizera kwabo, ntibahabga ivyasezeranywe," 
Hebrews11:40 kukw Imana yatuboneye kera ikirushiriza kuba ciza, kugira ngw abo ntibatunganywe rwose tutari kumwe." 
Hebrews12:1 Nuko natwe, ko dukikijwe n’igipfungu c’ivyabona kingana girtyo, twiyambure ibituremēra vyose, n’icaha gikunda kutwizingirako vuba, dusiganirwe ivyo twashizwe imbere twihanganye," 
Hebrews12:2 dutumbereye Yesu wenyene, ni we nyanduruko yo kwizera kandi ni we yagusozereye; uwo, kubg’ umunezero yashizwe imbere, yihanganiye umusaraba, ntiyagira ikindi isoni zawo, avyagira i buryo bg’intebe y’Imana." 
Hebrews12:3 Nuko mushire imitima kur’ uyo yihanganiye ibihāri bihambaye birtyo abanyavyaha bāmuhāririje, ntimucobogore, ntimudendebukirwe mu mitima yanyu." 
Hebrews12:4 Ntimuragera ku kuvishwa amaraso murwanya icaha," 
Hebrews12:5 kandi mwibagiye rya jambo ribahubūra ribahanūra nk’abana, ngo Mwana wanje, ntugaye igikāngīro c’Uhoraho, Kandi ntudendebukirwe ni yaguhana." 
Hebrews12:6 Kuk’ uwo Uhoraho akunda ari we akāngīra, Kand’ aramagura uwo yemera wese kw ar’ umwana wiwe." 
Hebrews12:7 Ico mukwiye kwihanganira n’ugutozwa indero nziza. Imana ibagirira nk’abana bayo. N’umwana ki, adakāngīrwa na se?" 
Hebrews12:8 Ariko namba mudakāngīrwa nk’ico abandi bose bakorerwa, mur’ ibivyarwa, ntimur’ ubura bgayo." 
Hebrews12:9 Kandi twari dufise ba data b’imibiri, bāradukāngīra, natwe tukabubaha: none ntituzorushiriza cane kugororokera Se w’impwemu tugahoraho?" 
Hebrews12:10 Kuko ba bandi bādukāngīra imisi mike nk’uko bāgomba, ariko we adukāngīrira ikigira ikimazi, kugira ngo dusangire na we ukwera kwiwe." 
Hebrews12:11 Nta gikāngīro kiboneka ko giteye umunezero ako kanya, atar’ umubabaro, ariko hanyuma abamenyerejwe na co kibāmira imbuto zizana amahoro zo kugororoka." 
Hebrews12:12 Nuko mugorore amaboko acitse urudendevu, n’amavi aregarega:" 
Hebrews12:13 kandi muharurire ibirenge vyanyu inzira zigororotse, kugira ngw igihinyiza ntigikondoke, ariko gikire." 
Hebrews12:14 Mukurikire kugiriranira amahoro n’abantu bose, n’ukwezwa, kuk’ ūtejejwe atazorāba Umwami;" 
Hebrews12:15 mwizigame, ntihagire umuntu adashikīra ubuntu bg’Imana, kandi ntihagire umuzi wo kurura umera, ukabahagarika imitima, abenshi bakāndura," 
Hebrews12:16 ntihabeh’ umushakanyi, cank’ igihumane nka Esau, yagurānye ivyo kuba samuragwa kwiwe ingaburo imwe." 
Hebrews12:17 Kuko muzi yuko hanyuma, hamwe yagomba kuragwa umugisha, atemerewe, kukw atābonye uburyo bgo kwihana, naho yawurondera cane arira." 
Hebrews12:18 Ntimwegereye umusozi wokorwako, waka umuriro, kandi ntimwegereye umwiza w’umuzimagiza n’uw’ umuzitanya, n’igihuhuta," 
Hebrews12:19 n’inzamba ivuga, n’ijwi ry’amajambo; abāryumvise binginga kutabgirwa irindi jambo:" 
Hebrews12:20 kuko batābashije ivyagezwe, ngo Naho coba igitungwa gikoze kur’ uwo musozi bacicishe amabuye." 
Hebrews12:21 Kand’ ivyabonetse vyar’ ibiteye ubgoba, vyatumye Mose avuga, ati Mfise ubgoba cane, ndahinda agashitsi." 
Hebrews12:22 Ariko mwegereye umusozi Siyoni, n’umurwa w’Imana nzima, Yeru salemu ho mw ijuru, n’ikoraniro rikuru ry’isinzi ry’abamarayika," 
Hebrews12:23 n’ishengero ry’abana b’imfura banditswe mw ijuru, mwegereye n’Imana umucamanza wa bose, n’impwemu z’abagororotsi batunganijwe rwose," 
Hebrews12:24 mwegereye na Yesu, umuhūza ahesha isezerano risha, mwegereye n’amaraso acucagirwa, avuga ivyiza kurusha aya Abeli." 
Hebrews12:25 Mwirinde ntimwanke kwumva Iyirikw iravuga. Ba bandi ko batākize, hamwe banka uwababūririye mw isi, tweho tuzorushiriza cane kudakira, namba dutera ibitugu Iyitubūrira iri mw ijuru." 
Hebrews12:26 Ijwi ryayo ryanyiganyigije isi ico gihe: ariko noneh’ irasezeranye, iti Hasigaye rimwe, ngatigitisha, s’isi gusa, ariko n’ijuru na ryo." 
Hebrews12:27 Iryo jambo, ngo Hasigaye rimwe, ryerekana gukūrwaho kw’ibinyiganyizwa, kukw ar’ ivyaremwe, kugira ngw ibitoshobora kunyiganyizwa bigumeho." 
Hebrews12:28 Ni co gituma, kuko twākīra ubgami budashobora kunyiganyizwa, dukwiye gukenguruka, kugira ngo tubone ingene dukorera Imana tuyihimbaye, tuyubaha tuyitinya:" 
Hebrews12:29 kukw Imana yacu ar’ umuriro utōngōra. 
Hebrews13:1 Ugukunda bene Data ni kugumeho. 
Hebrews13:2 Ntimwibagire kugirira neza abashitsi: kuko bamwe bāgize bartyo bāhaye indāro abamarayika batabizi. 
Hebrews13:3 Mwibuke ababoshwe nk’ababohanywe na bo: mwibuke n’abagirirwa nabi, kuko namwe muri mu mubiri." 
Hebrews13:4 Umubano w’abābīranye ni wubahwe na bose, kand’ uburiri bgabo bgoye guhumanywa: kukw abashakanyi n’abasambanyi Imana izobacirakw iteka." 
Hebrews13:5 Gukunda amahera ntikube mu ngeso zanyu; ivyo mufise bibabumbe; kuk’ ubgayo yavuze, iti Nta ho nzoguhemukira, nta ho nzoguta." 
Hebrews13:6 Ni co gituma tuvuga dushize ubgoba, tut’ Uhoraho n’umutabazi wanje, sinzotinya: Non’ umuntu yoshobora kungira iki?" 
Hebrews13:7 Mwibuke abābaganza, bakababgira ijambo ry’Imana; mwitegereje iherezo ry’ingeso zabo, mwīgāne ukwizera kwabo." 
Hebrews13:8 Yesu Kristo uko yar’ ar’ ejo, n’uyu musi ni kw akiri, ni kw azokwama ibihe bidashira." 
Hebrews13:9 Ntimutwarwe n’inyigisho z’uburyo bginshi zādutse; kukw iciza ar’ uk’ umutima ushikamizwa n’ubuntu bg’Imana, ntushikamizwe n’ivyo kurya, kukw abishize muri vyo bitābagiriye ikimazi." 
Hebrews13:10 Dufise igicaniro, ico abakorera muri rya hema batemererwa kurīrako." 
Hebrews13:11 Kukw imivyimba ya vya bitungwa, ivyo umuherezi mukuru ajana amaraso yavyo ahēra kuba impongano y’ivyaha, ituririrwa inyuma y’insago." 
Hebrews13:12 Ni co catumye na Yesu ababarizwa inyuma y’irembo, kugira ngo yezeshe abantu ayiwe maraso." 
Hebrews13:13 Nuko tuve mur’ izo nsago, tumusange inyuma yazo, twiremētse ugucokorwa kwiwe." 
Hebrews13:14 Kuko hano tutahafise igisagara kizokwamaho, ariko turondera ikizoza." 
Hebrews13:15 Nuko na ntaryo twame duha Imana ikimazi co gukenguruka tubiheshwa n’uyo, ni co mbuto z’iminwa ishima izina ryayo." 
Hebrews13:16 Kugira neza no kugira ubuntu ntimukavyibagire, kukw ibimazi bimeze birtyo ari vyo bihimbara Imana." 
Hebrews13:17 Mwumvire ababaganza, mubagamburukire: kukw ari bo bama bagavye bazigama imitima yanyu, nk’abazobibazwa; mugenze murtyo kugira ngo babikore banezerewe, batitsa umutima, kuko bimeze birtyo ata co vyomarira mwebge." 
Hebrews13:18 Mudusengere, kuko tuzi tudakekeranya ko turi n’imitima itarimw’ ijwi ritwagiriza ikibi, tugomba kugira ingeso nziza muri vyose." 
Hebrews13:19 Kandi ndabinginga nshimitse ngo mudusengere, kugira ngo ntebutswe kubagarukanirwa vuba." 
Hebrews13:20 Imana Nyen’ amahoro, imwe yakūra Umwami wacu Yesu mu bapfuye, ari we Mwungere mukuru w’intama, imukūjey’ amaraso y’isezerano ry’ibihe bidashira," 
Hebrews13:21 ibe ari yo ibatunganya rwose mu ciza cose, kugira ngo mukore ivy’ igomba, ikorera muri twebge ibishimwa mu nyonga zayo, kubga Yesu Kristo: icubahiro kibe icayo ibihe bitazoshira. Amen." 
Hebrews13:22 Ariko bene Data, ndabahanūra, mwihanganire iri jambo ribahanūra, kuko mbandikiye amajambo make." 
Hebrews13:23 Mumenye yuko mwene Data Timoteyo yarekuwe: ni yaza vuba tuzobonana namwe. 
Hebrews13:24 Muntahirize ababaganza bose, bo n’abera bose. Abo muri Italiya barabatasha." 
Hebrews13:25 Ubuntu bubane namwe mwese. Amen. 
James1:1 Yakobo, umugurano w’Imana n’uw’ Umwami Yesu Kristo, ndabandikiye abo mu miryango cumi n’ibiri y’abāsābagiye: muganuke." 
James1:2 Mwiyumvire kw ar’ ivyo kunezererwa rwose, bene Data, ni mwagwa mu bibagerageza bitari bimwe," 
James1:3 mumenye yukw ibigeza ukwizera kwanyu bitera ukwihangana. 
James1:4 Arik’ ukwihangana gukwiye guhīngūra igikorwa cakwo, ngo mubone gutungana rwose muhīngūwe, mudahajije na kamwe." 
James1:5 Arikw asangwa har’ uwo muri mwebge akennye ubgenge, n’abusabe Imana, igabira bose ata kinūbge, idaterana imirarwe, azobuhabga." 
James1:6 Arikw asabe yizeye, ata co akekeranya, kuk’ ūkekeranya ameze nk’umupfunda wo mu kiyaga, utwarwa n’umuyaga, usimbaguritswa." 
James1:7 Uyo muntu yoye kwiyumvira kw ari n’ic’ azohabga n’Umwami Imana," 
James1:8 kukw ar’ umuntu w’imitima ibiri, adāguza mu nzira ziwe zose." 
James1:9 Ariko, mwene Data w’umufafara ni yirate kw ashizwe hejuru," 
James1:10 umutunzi na we, ni yirate kw acishijwe bugufi, kukw azoyoka nk’amashurwe y’ivyatsi." 
James1:11 Kukw izuba rirasa, rizanye indugumba, rikūmisha ivyatsi, amashurwe yavyo agahunguruka, ubgiza bg’ishusho yayo bugashira. Uko ni k’umutunzi azoyonga mu ngendo ziwe." 
James1:12 Hahirwa umuntu yihanganira ibimugerageza, kuko ni yamara kurama azohabga igitsibo c’ubugingo, ico Imana yasezeraniye abayikunda." 
James1:13 Umuntu ni yageragezwa gukora ibibi, yoye kuvuga ngw Imana ni yo ingerageje. Kukw Imana itageragezwa n’ibibi, kandi na yo nta we ibigerageresha." 
James1:14 Arik’ umuntu wese ageragezwa, iy’ akwezwe n’ivyo yifuza bikamusuka." 
James1:15 Maz’ ukwo kwifuza gutwara inda, kukavyara icaha, icaha kimaze gukura kikavyara urupfu." 
James1:16 Ntimuzimire, bene Data nkunda." 
James1:17 Gutanga kwose kwiza, n’ingabire yose itunganye rwose biva mw ijuru, vyururuka biva kuri Se w’imico, adashobora guhinduka canke kugira igitūtu gitewe n’uguhindagurika." 
James1:18 Nk’uko yabigabiye ubgayo, yatuvyarishije ijambo ry’ukuri, kugira ngo tube nk’umushuzo w’ibiremwa vyayo." 
James1:19 Ivyo murabizi, bene Data nkunda. Yamar’ umuntu wese ni yihutire kwumva, atebe kuvuga, atebe kuraka:" 
James1:20 kuk’ uburake bg’umuntu budakora ivy’ ukugororoka kw’Imana. 
James1:21 Nuko rero, mwiyambure imyanda yose n’ububi busigaye, mwākīrane ubugwaneza ijambo ritewe muri mwebge, rishobora gukiza ubugingo bganyu." 
James1:22 Kandi mube abakora ivy’ iryo jambo, ntimube abaryumva gusa, mwibesha." 
James1:23 Kuk’ uwumva iryo jambo ntarikore, ameze nk’umuntu yirābiye mu cirore mu maso hiwe yavukanye." 
James1:24 Amaze kwirāba, akagenda, uwo mwanya agaca yiyibagira ukw asa." 
James1:25 Ariko, uwitegereza ivyagezwe bitunganye rwose, ari vyo vy’umwidegemvyo, akabishishikara, atar’ uwumva akavyibagira, arikw ar’ ūbikora, ni we azohabga umugisha mu vy’ akora." 
James1:26 Umuntu ni yigira ngo n’umunyedini, ntafate ururimi, arikw agahenda umutima wiwe, idini y’uyo izoba ar’ iy’ ubusa." 
James1:27 Idini itunganye itagira agasembga imbere y’Imana Data wa twese, n’ukurāba impfuvyi n’abapfakazi mu marushwa yabo, no kwirinda ngo ntiwanduzwe n’ivy’ isi." 
James2:1 Bene Data, kwizera Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo w’ubgiza ntikubemwo kurobanura abantu ku cubahiro." 
James2:2 Mw isinagogi yanyu ni hinjiramw’ umuntu yambaye impeta y’izahabu n’impuzu zishajije, hakinjira n’umworo yambaye impuzu mbi y’ubuhoma," 
James2:3 namwe mukitegereza uwambaye impuzu zishajije, mukamubarira, muti Ni wicare hano heza; kandi mukabarira nya mworo, muti Weho hagarara hariya, cank’ icara hambavu y’ibirenge vyanje;" 
James2:4 none se ntimuba mwisobanuye, mukaba abacamanza biyumvira ibibi?" 
James2:5 Ni mwumve, bene Data nkunda. Mbeg’ Imana ntiyatoranirije aboro b’ivy’ isi kuba abatunzi mu kwizera, no kuragwa ubgami yasezeraniye abayikunda?" 
James2:6 Ariko mweho mwatētereje umworo. Non’ abatunzi si bo babatwaza amanyama, bakaba ari bo babakwega babajana mu manza?" 
James2:7 Si bo barogota kw izina ryiza mwitirirwa? 
James2:8 Mugabo namba mushitsa icagezwe c’i bgami nk’uko canditswe, ngo Mukunde bagenzi banyu nk’uko mwikunda, muba mugize neza." 
James2:9 Arikw iyo murobanuye abantu ku cubahiro, muba mukoze icaha, mutsinzwe n’ivyagezwe ko mubaye abanyabicumuro." 
James2:10 Kuk’ umuntu wese azokwitondera ivyagezwe vyose, agatsitara kuri kimwe, azoba acumuye kuri vyose." 
James2:11 Uwavuze, ati Ntugasambane, ni we yavuze, ati Ntukice. Nuko rero n’utasambana arik’ ukica, uzoba ucumuye ku vyagezwe." 
James2:12 Muvuge kandi mukore nk’abagira bacirwe urubanza n’ivyagezwe bizana umwidegemvyo. 
James2:13 Kuk’ urubanza rutagirira akagongwe ūtāgize akagongwe. Ariko mu rubanza ikigongwe kiratsinda. 
James2:14 Vyomara iki ga bene Data, namb’ umuntu avuga yukw afise ukwizera, ata bikorwa akora? Mbeg’ ukwo kwizera kwoshobora kumukiza?" 
James2:15 Ni haba hariho mwene Data uw’ ari we wese yoba yambaye ubusa, agenda aburanirwa ku vyo kurya," 
James2:16 maz’ umwe muri mwebge akamubgira, ati Genda amahoro, ususuruke, uhāge; ariko ntimumuhe ivy’ umubiri ukena, vyomara iki?" 
James2:17 Ni ko bimeze, n’ukwizera kutari n’ibikorwa, kuri kwonyene, kuba gupfuye." 
James2:18 Nk’umuntu yovuga, ati Weho ufise ukwizera, jeho mfise ibikorwa: nyereka ukwizera kwawe kutagira ibikorwa, nanje ndakwereka ukwizera kwanje guserurwa n’ibikorwa vyanje." 
James2:19 Wemera yukw Imana ar’ imwe. Ugize neza; abadayimoni na bo nyene baravyemera, bagahinda agashitsi." 
James2:20 Ariko wa muntu w’imburakimazi we, mbeg’ ugomba kumenya ingen’ ukwizera kutagira ibikorwa ar’ ukw’ ubusa?" 
James2:21 Aburahamu sogokuruza, mbega ntiyatsindanishirijwe n’ibikorwa, hamwe yar’ atanze kw ikimazi umwana wiwe Isaka ku gicaniro?" 
James2:22 Ntubona yuk’ ukwizera kwafatanije n’ibikorwa vyiwe, kandi k’ukwizera kwahīngūwe rwose n’ibikorwa?" 
James2:23 Kand’ icanditswe kirashika, kivuga ngo Aburahamu yizeye Imana, ibimuharūrako nk’ukugororoka; kandi yitwa umukunzi w’Imana." 
James2:24 Murabona yukw ibikorwa ari vyo bitsindanishiriza umuntu, atar’ ukwizera kwonyene." 
James2:25 Kandi na Rahabu maraya ni ko vyabaye: mbega ntiyatsindanishirijwe n’ibikorwa kuko yahaye za ntumwa indāro, akazirangira iyindi nzira?" 
James2:26 Nk’uk’ umubiri utarimw’ impwemu uba upfuye, ni k’ukwizera kutagira ibikorwa kumera, kuba gupfuye." 
James3:1 Bene Data, muri mwebge ntihakabe benshi barondera kuba abigisha: murazi ko tuzocirwa urubanza ruruta iz’ abandi." 
James3:2 Kuko twese dutsitara muri vyinshi. Umuntu wese adatsitara mu vy’avuga, aba ar’ umuntu atunganye rwose, ashobora no kuganza umubiri wiwe wose." 
James3:3 Iyo tujiginyitse amafarasi mu kanwa kayo, kugira ngw adukundire, duhindukiza n’imibiri yayo yose." 
James3:4 Kandi rāba, n’amāto naho yoba maninimanini ate, agakubebga n’umuyaga uhuhuta cane, ingafe nah’ ari nto‐nto cane ni zo ziyerekeza, ah’ abayatumbereza bagomba." 
James3:5 N’ururimi ni ko ruri: n’urugingo rutoya, rukirarira ibikomeye. Rāba ishamba, naho ryoba rinini rite, ridomekwa n’akariro gake." 
James3:6 Ururimi n’umuriro, n’ikibi kingana n’isi: ururimi rwashizwe mu ngingo zacu, ruhumanya umubiri wose, rudomeka ukubaho kwacu kwose, na rwo ruba rwadometswe na Gehinomu." 
James3:7 Kukw amoko yose y’ibikōko n’ibiguruka n’ivyikwega n’ivyo mu kiyaga bigundwa n’abantu, kandi bārabigunze;" 
James3:8 ariko, ururimi nta muntu yoshobora kurugunda: n’ububi bucambagirana, rwuzuye ubumara bgica." 
James3:9 Urwo ni rwo dushimisha Umwami Data wa twese, kandi ni rwo tuvumisha abantu, bāremwe mw ishusho y’Imana:" 
James3:10 mu kanwa kamwe havamw’ umuhezagiro n’umuvumo. Bene Data, ivyo ntibikwiye kumera birtyo." 
James3:11 Mbeg’ iriba ryodudubiza amazi aryoshe n’ay’ umururazi mu mbizi imwe? 
James3:12 Bene Data, mbeg’ umusukoni woshobora kwama elayo, cank’ umuzabibu wokwama insukoni? Ni kw amazi y’umunyu adashobora kuvamw’ ayaryoshe." 
James3:13 Ni nde muri mwebge w’umunyabgenge kandi w’umuhanga? Ni yerekanishe ibikorwa vyiwe ingeso nziza mu bugwaneza bufatanije n’ubgenge. 
James3:14 Ariko namba mugira ishari ry’inkazi mu mitima yanyu, mugakunda kwirema ibice, mwoye kwirata, mubesha, mucumura ku kuri." 
James3:15 Ubgo bgenge si bgo bgururuka buvuye mw ijuru, ariko n’ubg’ isi, n’ubg’ abantu, n’ubg’ abadayimoni." 
James3:16 Kukw ah’ ishari riri, bo no kwirema ibice, ari ho umuvurungano uri, n’igikorwa kibi cose." 
James3:17 Arik’ ubgenge buva mw ijuru, irya mbere buratunganye, kandi n’ubg’ amahoro, burengenga, bukunda kugīrwa inama, bguzuye imbabazi n’imbuto nziza, ntibukekeranya, ntibugira uburyarya." 
James3:18 Kand’ imbuto zo kugororoka zibibga mu mahoro n’ababanguranya. 
James4:1 Muri mwebge intambara ziva hehe, n’imitongano iva hehe? Mbega ntibiva mu bibahimbara birwanira mu ngingo zanyu?" 
James4:2 Murifuza, ariko ntimuhabga: murica, mugira ishari, ariko ntimushobora kuronka; murarwana muratabara. Ntimuhabga kuko mudasaba:" 
James4:3 murasaba ntimuhabge, kuko musaba nabi, kugira ngo muvyononere mu bibahimbara." 
James4:4 Yemwe basambanyi, ntimuzi yuko gucudika n’isi ar’ ukwankana n’Imana? Nuk’ umuntu wese agomba kuba incuti y’isi aba yīgize umwansi w’Imana." 
James4:5 Canke mwiyumvira yukw ivyanditswe bivugira ubusa, ng’ Uwo Mpwemu yagererewe muri twebge atwikundiriza afuha?" 
James4:6 Arikw itanga ubuntu burushirije. Ni co gituma ivuga, it’ Imana irwanya abibona, arikw abicisha bugufi ibaha ubuntu." 
James4:7 Nuko mugamburukire Imana, ariko murwanye wa Murwanizi, na we azobahunga." 
James4:8 Mwiyegereze Imana, na yo izobēgēra. Yemwe banyavyaha, ni mukarabe: yemwe ab’ imitima ibiri, ni mwiyeze imitima." 
James4:9 Mubabare, muboroge, murire; ibitwengo vyanyu bihinduke amaborogo, umunezero uhinduke umubabaro." 
James4:10 Mwicishe bugufi imbere y’Umwami Imana, na yo izobashira hejuru." 
James4:11 Bene Data, ntimuvuganane nabi. Ūvuga nabi mwene Se, cank’ ūhinyurira mwene Se ku mutima, aba avuze nabi ivyagezwe, ni vyo aba ahinyuye. Arikw iy’ uhinyura ivyagezwe, ntuba uvyitondera, uba ubaye umucamanza wavyo." 
James4:12 Ūshinga ivyagezwe, ari we mucamanza, n’Imwe gusa; ni yo ishobora kurokora no guhonnya: ariko wewe ur’ iki, uhinyura mugenzawe?" 
James4:13 Umve rero, yemwe abavuga ng’ Uyu musi cank’ ejo tuzoja mu gisagara c’i naka, tuzomaray’ umwaka, tudandaze, turonke inyungu:" 
James4:14 ariko mutazi ibizoba ejo. Ubugingo bganyu ni nk’iki? Mur’ umwuka uboneka umwanya muto, ugahava uyongayonga." 
James4:15 Ariko mwari mukwiye kuvuga, mut’ Umwami wacu ni yabikunda, tuzoramba, kandi tuzokora durtya canke durtya." 
James4:16 Yamara none mwirata ukwihayagiza kwanyu: ukwirata kwose ben’ ukwo ni kubi. 
James4:17 Nuk’ ūzi gukora neza ntabikore, bimubera icaha." 
James5:1 Enda rero, yemwe batunzi, ni murire muboroge kuko mugira mufutane." 
James5:2 Ubutunzi bganyu buraboze, impuzu zanyu zirīwe n’inyenzi;" 
James5:3 izahabu n’ifeza vyanyu binyengeterewe n’ingese: ingese zavyo zizoba icabona co kubāgiriza, zizonyengetera imibiri yanyu nk’umuriro. Mwārundanije mu misi y’umuhero." 
James5:4 Eh’ ingero z’abashwabuzi bābashwaburiye imirima, izo mwabagunze, zirataka: amaborogo y’abābashwaburiye yinjiye mu matwi y’Uhoraho Nyen’ ingabo." 
James5:5 Mwidibamiye mw isi, mwihaye ibibahimbara: mwifunereje mu mitima ku musi wo gukekagurwa." 
James5:6 Umugororotsi mwamuciriyekw iteka, muramwica, ntiyabarwanya." 
James5:7 Nuko bene Data, mwihangane mushitse ah’ Umwami Yesu azozira. Eh’ umurimyi arorēra imirima myiza, ayirīndīra yihanganye, gushitsa ah’ izoronkera imvura y’agatāsi n’iy’ urushana." 
James5:8 Nuko namwe mwihangane, mureme mu mitima, kuk’ ukuza kw’Umwami kuri hafi." 
James5:9 Ntimwidodomberanire, bene Data, kugira ngo ntimucirwekw iteka: eh’ Umucamanza ahagaze ku rugi." 
James5:10 Abāvugishijwe mw izina ry’Umwami Imana bababere icitegererezo bene Data, co kubabazwa no kwihangana." 
James5:11 Eh’ abihanganye tubita abahirwe: mwarumvise ukwihangana kwa Yobu, mwabonye ivy’ Umwami Imana yaherutse kumugirira, ingene yuzuye imbabazi no kugira ikigongwe." 
James5:12 Ariko bene Data, ikiruta vyose, ntimukarahire: ntimurahire ijuru, cank’ isi, cank’ iyindi ndahiro yose; arikw ijambo ryanyu ribe Ego, ego; Oya, oya; kugira ngo ntimucirwekw iteka." 
James5:13 Muri mwebge ni haba harih’ ūbabaye, n’asenge; namba harih’ ūroraniwe, n’aririmbe ishimwe;" 
James5:14 muri mwebge namba harih’ ūrwaye, n’atumekw abashingantahe b’ishengero, baze kumusengera, bamusīge amavuta ya elayo mw izina ry’Umwami wacu." 
James5:15 Kand’ ugusenga gufatanije n’ukwizera kuzokiza umurwayi, Umwami azomuvyura: kand’ asanzwe yarakoze ivyaha azobiharirwa." 
James5:16 Mwaturanire ivyaha vyanyu, musengeranire, kugira ngo mukire indwara. Ugusaba kw’umugororotsi kugira ikimazi kuri vyinshi mu gikorwa cakwo." 
James5:17 Eliya yar’ umuntu ameze nkatwe, asaba yinginga ngw imvura ntigwe, imvura imara imyaka itatu n’amezi atandatu itagwa mu gihugu;" 
James5:18 yongera gusaba, ijuru rirekura imvura, isi imeza imirima yayo." 
James5:19 Bene Data, ni hagira umuntu muri mwebge azimira, akava ku vy’ ukuri, uwundi akamuzimurura," 
James5:20 mumenye yuk’ ūzimuruye umunyavyaha, akamukūra mu nzira yiwe yazimiriyemwo, aba amukirije ubugingo urupfu, kand’ aba apfutse ivyaha vyinshi." 
1Peter1:1 Petero, intumwa ya Yesu Kristo, ndabandikiye abātoranijwe b’inyambukīra zo mu bāsanzariye i Ponto n’i Galatiya n’i Kapadokiya no muri Asiya n’i Bituniya," 
1Peter1:2 mwatoranirijwe mu kweza kwa Mpwemu nk’ukw Imana Data wa twese yabamenye uhereye kera, kugira ngo mwumvire Imana, mucucagirwe amaraso ya Yesu Kristo. Ubuntu n’amahoro bigwire muri mwebge." 
1Peter1:3 Imana y’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, ari yo Se, iragahezagirwa, yatuvyaye ubga kabiri nk’ukw imbabazi zayo nyinshi ziri, kugira ngo tugire ivyizigiro bizima, ituvyaza ukuzuka mu bapfuye kwa Yesu Kristo," 
1Peter1:4 ngo tuze twegukire umwandu utazobora, utanduye, udakabirana, mwabīkiwe mw ijuru," 
1Peter1:5 mwebge abazigamwa n’ubushobozi bg’Imana kubg’ ukwizera, muzigamirwa agakiza kāteguwe kuzohishurwa mu gihe c’iherezo." 
1Peter1:6 Ivyo murabinezererwa cane, nah’ ubu ar’ igihe gito mubabazwa n’ibibagerageza vyinshi, kuko bitobura kuza:" 
1Peter1:7 kugira ngo kuramura kw’ukwizera kwanyu (kand’ ukwo kwizera kurusha igiciro izahabu ishira, nah’ ivugutirwa mu muriro ikaramura) kuze kuboneke kuri n’ishimwe n’ubgiza n’icubahiro mu guhishurwa kwa Yesu Kristo." 
1Peter1:8 Uwo muramukunda naho mutigeze kumubona; kandi n’ubu, naho mutaramubona, muramwizera, bibatera kunezerwa akanyamuneza k’ubgiza katovugwa," 
1Peter1:9 mugahabga ikizanwa n’ukwizera kwanyu, ni co gakiza k’ubugingo bganyu." 
1Peter1:10 Ivy’ ako gakiza, abāvugishwa n’Imana, ari bo bāvuze ubuntu mwāgira muze muhabge, bārabirondera, bārabisesa," 
1Peter1:11 basesa igihe ic’ ari co n’ibimenyetso vyaco, cerekanwa na Mpwemu wa Kristo yari muri bo, yavuga yātagura ivy’ imibabaro ya Kristo bitaribgabe, n’ivy’ ubgiza bg’uburyo bginshi bgagira buze buyiherukire." 
1Peter1:12 Kandi bāhishurirwa yukw atari bo bavyikorera, ariko kw ari mwebge babikorera; ni vyo none mumaze kubarirwa n’abābabgiye ubutumwa bgiza, bāvugishijwe na Mpwemu Yera yatumwe ava mw ijuru: kand’ ivyo abamarayika bifuza kubirunguruka." 
1Peter1:13 Nuko rero mukenyere mu mitima yanyu, mwirinde ibiboreza, mwizigire rwose ubuntu muzozanirwa mu kuzohishurwa kwa Yesu Kristo." 
1Peter1:14 Mumere nk’abana bagamburuka, ntimwishushanye n’ukwifuza kwanyu kwa kera kwo mu gihe c’ukutamenya kwanyu." 
1Peter1:15 Ariko nk’ukw Iyabahamagaye ar’ iyera, namwe abe ari ko muba abera mu ngeso zanyu zose." 
1Peter1:16 Kuko vyanditswe, ngo Mube abera, kuko nanje nd’uwera." 
1Peter1:17 Kandi kw Iyo mwambaza muyita So ari yo icira umuntu wese urubanza rukwiranye n’ivyo yakoze itarobanuye ku cubahiro, mumare igihe co kuba inyambukīra mutinya." 
1Peter1:18 Muzi yukw ivyo mwacungujwe ngo muve mu ngeso zanyu z’imburakimazi mwatojwe na ba sogokuruza atar’ ibishira, nk’ifeza cank’ izahabu," 
1Peter1:19 ariko mwacungujwe amaraso y’igiciro kinini, nk’ay’ umwagazi w’intama utagira agasembga cank’ ibara, ni yo ya Kristo." 
1Peter1:20 Uwo yamenywe n’Imana kera, itanguriro ry’isi ritarashirwaho, ariko yerekanywe kw iherezo ry’ibihe kubganyu," 
1Peter1:21 mwebge abo yahaye kwizera Imana, ni yo yamuzuye mu bapfuye ikamuha ubgiza: ni co gituma ukwizera kwanyu n’ivyizigiro vyanyu biba ku Mana." 
1Peter1:22 Nuko rero, ko mwejesheje imitima kwumvira ukuri, kugira ngo mukunde bene Data bitar’ uruheyiheyi, mukovye mu gukundana bivuye mu mitima." 
1Peter1:23 Kuko mwavyawe ubga kabiri, mutavyawe n’imbuto ibora, ariko mwavyawe n’imbuto itabora, mubiheshejwe n’ijambo ry’Imana ririho rigahoraho." 
1Peter1:24 Kuko, Abafise umubiri bose basa n’ivyatsi, Ubgiza bgabo bgose bumeze nk’amashurwe y’ivyatsi; Ivyatsi birūma, amashurwe agahunguruka," 
1Peter1:25 Arikw ijambo ry’Uhoraho ryamah’ ibihe bidashira. Kand’ iryo ni ryo jambo ry’ubutumwa bgiza mwabgiwe. 
1Peter2:1 Nuko rero mwiyambure inzigo yose n’ubugunge bgose n’uburyarya n’ishari no kuvuga abandi nabi kwose," 
1Peter2:2 mumere nk’inzoya zivutse vuba, mwifuze amata y’umutima adafunguye, kugira ngw abakuze abashitse ku gakiza;" 
1Peter2:3 asangwa mwarayumvirije mukumva yuk’ Umwami wacu agira neza. 
1Peter2:4 Nuko mumwēgēre, ari we buye rifise ubugingo, ryagawe n’abantu, ariko ku Mana ryaratoranijwe, riri n’igiciro," 
1Peter2:5 mwubakwe nk’amabuye afise ubugingo, kugira ngo mube inzu yo mu buryo bg’impwemu, mugire ibango ry’ubuherezi ryera, ngo mutange ibimazi mu buryo bg’impwemu, bishimwa n’Imana kubga Yesu Kristo." 
1Peter2:6 Kuko mu vyanditswe harimw’ aya majambo, ngo Rāba, ndashira i Siyoni ibuye rigumya imfuruka, ryatoranijwe, riri n’igiciro, Kand’ ūryizera ntazomāramāzwa." 
1Peter2:7 Nuko mwebge abizera ni mwebge mwagerewe ico giciro, ariko ku banka kwizera, ngw Ibuye abubatsi bāgaye, Ni ryo ryahindutse irigumya imfuruka," 
1Peter2:8 N’ibuye ritsitaza n’urutare rugwisha; kuko batsitara kw ijambo ry’Imana, bataryumvira: kandi ni co bāshiriweho." 
1Peter2:9 Ariko mweho mur’ ubgoko bgātoranijwe, mukoranije kuba abami n’abaherezi, mur’ ihanga ryera, abantu bāshiriweho kuba inyegu yiharije, kugira ngo mukwize ishimwe ry’Iyabahamagaye, ikabakūra mu mwiza, ikabashitsa mu muco wayo utangaje:" 
1Peter2:10 kera nta bantu mwarimwo, ariko noneho mur’ abantu b’Imana; kera ntimwaribgagirirwe imbabazi, ariko noneho mwarazigiriwe." 
1Peter2:11 Abo nkunda, ndabinginga, ko mur’ inyambukīra n’ingenzi mwirinde ivyifuzo vy’umubiri birwanya ubugingo;" 
1Peter2:12 mugire ingeso nziza mu mahanga, kugira ngo, no ku vyo babavuga nabi nk’inkozi z’ibibi, ibikorwa vyanyu vyiza babona bize bitume bahimbaza Imana ku musi ibagendeye." 
1Peter2:13 Kubg’ Umwami wacu, ubukuru bgose bgashizweho n’abantu mubugamburukire: ar’ umwami, kukw ari we gaheta;" 
1Peter2:14 cank’ abakuru, kukw ari bo atuma guhana inkozi z’ibibi no gushima inkozi z’ivyiza." 
1Peter2:15 Kukw ivy’ Imana igomba ar’ uk’ ugukora neza kwanyu kuba agahomerabunwa ku bantu b’imburabgenge batagira ico bazi: 
1Peter2:16 ngo mube nk’abidegemvya, arikw atar’ ukugira umwidegemvyo wanyu igitwikirizo c’inzigo, ariko mube nk’abagurano b’Imana." 
1Peter2:17 Mwubahe abantu bose; mukunde bene Data; mutinye Imana; mwubahe umwami. 
1Peter2:18 Bashumba, mugamburukire ba shobuja, mububashe rwose, atar’ ababagirira neza n’ababihanganira gusa, ariko n’abadadika." 
1Peter2:19 Kukw igishimwa ar’ uk’ umuntu, namb’ ahanūwe n’ijwi ryo mu mutima gukora ivy’ Imana igomba, yokwihanganira imibabaro ahōwe ubusa." 
1Peter2:20 Mwokwihanganira gukubitwa ibipfunsi muhōwe icaha, mwokwihaya iki? Ariko mwokwihanganira kubabazwa muhōwe gukora neza, ivyo ni vyo bishimwa ku Mana." 
1Peter2:21 Ivyo ni vyo mwahamagariwe, kuko na Kristo yabababarijwe, akabasigarana icitegererezo, kugira ngo mugere ikirenge mu ciwe." 
1Peter2:22 We nta caha yakoze, kandi nta bugunge bgabonetse mu kanwa kiwe;" 
1Peter2:23 yaratutswe, ntiyabasubiza; yarababajwe, ntiyabahigira; ariko yiha Īdaca urwa nkunzi." 
1Peter2:24 Ubgiwe yikoreye ivyaha vyacu mu mubiri wiwe, abambge ku giti, kugira ngo dupfuye ku vyaha tubeho ku kugororoka; inguma ziwe ni zo zabakijije." 
1Peter2:25 Kuko mwari muzimiye nk’intama, ariko noneho mugarutse ku Mwungere w’ubugingo bganyu, ari we nyene abujējwe." 
1Peter3:1 Namwe bagore n’uko, mugamburukire abagabo banyu, kugira ngo, naho bamwe batumvira ijambo ry’Imana, bareshwe n’ingeso nziza z’abagore babo, batagize ijambo bavuze," 
1Peter3:2 ni bābona ingeso zanyu zitunganye zifatanije n’ugutinya. 
1Peter3:3 Ugushaza kwanyu ntikube ukwo ku rukoba kwo gutsiba umushatsi, cank’ ukwo kwambara izahabu cank’ ukwo kwambara impuzu nziza;" 
1Peter3:4 ariko kube ukw’ umuntu ahishijwe wo mu mutima, ugushaza kudashira, ni kwo mutima w’ubugwaneza utekereje, ni kwo kw’ igiciro kinini imbere y’Imana." 
1Peter3:5 Ni kw abagore bera bizigira Imana bāshaza kera, bagamburukira abagabo babo," 
1Peter3:6 nk’uko Sara yumvira Aburahamu, akamwita umwami wiwe; namwe mur’ abana b’uwo, ni mwahora mukora neza, mudaterwa ubgoba n’icobaca ivutu." 
1Peter3:7 Namwe bagabo n’uko, mubane n’abagore banyu nk’abazi ibibereye, kukw ari nk’imbombovu zidahwanije namwe inkomezi: kandi mubahe icubahiro, kuko na bo ar’ abaraganwa namwe ubuntu bg’ubugingo, kugira ng’ugusenga kwanyu ntikugire ikigutesha." 
1Peter3:8 Ibisigaye, mwese muhūze umutima, mubabarane, mukundane nk’abavukana, mugiriranire imbabazi, mwicishe bugufi mu mutima;" 
1Peter3:9 ntimugere ikibi ku kindi, cank’ igitutsi ku kindi; ariko mubigerāne n’umuhezagiro, kukw ico ari co mwahamagariwe, kugira ngo namwe muragwe umugisha." 
1Peter3:10 Kuko handitswe, ng’ Ūgomba gukunda ubugingo, No kubona imisi myiza, N’abuze ururimi rwiwe, rwoye kuvuga ikibi, N’iminwa yiwe yoye kuvuga ivy’ uguhendana:" 
1Peter3:11 Kand’ azibukīre ibibi, akore ivyiza; Arondere amahoro, ayakurikire, kugira ngw ayashikīre." 
1Peter3:12 Kukw inyonga z’Uhoraho ziri ku bagororotsi, N’amatwi yiwe ari ku vyo basenga, Arikw igitsure c’Uhoraho kiri ku bakora ibibi." 
1Peter3:13 Kandi ni nde yobagirira nabi, ni mwagira ishaka ry’ivyiza?" 
1Peter3:14 Yamara naho mwobabazwa muhōwe ukugororoka, mwoba muhiriwe. Ntimuze mutinye ivyo babakangisha, ntimuhagarike imitima," 
1Peter3:15 ariko mwubahe Kristo mu mitima yanyu kw ari we Mwami, muhore mwiteguye kwishura umuntu wese ababajije inyanduruko y’ivyizigiro biri muri mwebge, ariko muri n’ubugwaneza, mutinya," 
1Peter3:16 mufise imitima itarimw’ ijwi ribāgiriza ikibi, kugira ngo no ku vyo muvugwa nabi, abatuka ingeso zanyu nziza zo muri Kristo bamāramāre." 
1Peter3:17 Ivyoba vyiza n’uko mwobabazwa muhōwe gukora ivyiza, ari co Imana igomvye, hako muhōrwa gukora ibibi." 
1Peter3:18 Kuko na Kristo yababajwe rimwe ahōrwa ivyaha, umugororotsi yababarijwe abagabitanya, kugira ngw adushikirize Imana; yishwe umubiri, ariko yahinduwe muzima mu buryo bg’impwemu:" 
1Peter3:19 ni bgo yagiyemwo abarira impwemu ziri mw ibohero ijambo ry’Imana," 
1Peter3:20 ni zo z’abatumviye Imana kera, hamwe ukwihangana kwayo kwari kukirorereye mu misi ya Nowa, bga bgato bukibāzwa; muri bgo hārokokeye abantu bakeya, bashika umunani, bākirijwe mu mazi." 
1Peter3:21 Ayo ni yo abakiza namwe ubu, mu buryo bg’ikigereranyo c’ukubatizwa, s’ugukūrah’ imvyiro zo ku mubiri, ariko n’isezerano ry’umutima utāgiriza ikibi usezeranye ku Mana, abakirisha ukuzuka kwa Yesu Kristo," 
1Peter3:22 ar’i buryo bg’Imana, kuko yagiye mw ijuru, amaze guhabga gutwara abamarayika n’abanyabubasha n’abanyabushobozi." 
1Peter4:1 Nuko kuko Kristo yababarijwe mu mubiri, mwitwaze nk’ibirwanishwa ben’ uyo mutima: kuk’ ūbabarijwe mu mubiri aba amaze kureka icaha," 
1Peter4:2 kugira ngw amare imisi isigaye akiri mu mubiri atagikorera ivyifuzo vy’abantu, arikw akora ivy’ Imana igomba." 
1Peter4:3 Kukw igihe cashize gihāgije gukora ivy’ abanyamahanga bakunda gukora, no kugendera mu ngeso z’isoni nke, n’izo kwifuza, no kunohorwa na vino, no kudandahirwa, no kurundāna aho bateretse, n’ibizira vyo gusenga ibigirwamana." 
1Peter4:4 Birabatangaza yuko mudafatanya na bo kwirukira mu birenze urugero vy’ubuhumbu, bakabarementaniriza;" 
1Peter4:5 mugabo ni bo bazobazwa ivyo n’uwiteguye kuzoca imanza z’abakiriho n’abapfuye. 
1Peter4:6 Kukw icatumye abapfuye na bo bābariwe ubutumwa bgiza kwar’ ukugira ngo bacirirwe imanza mu mubiri mu buryo bg’abantu, ariko babeho mu mpwemu mu buryo bg’Imana." 
1Peter4:7 Arik’ umuhero wa vyose uri hafi: nuko ntimuhugumbe, mwirinde, kugira ngo mubone uko mushishikara gusenga." 
1Peter4:8 Ikiruta vyose, mukovye mu gukundana, kuk’ urukundo rupfuka ivyaha vyinshi." 
1Peter4:9 Muhāne indāro mutidodomba. 
1Peter4:10 Nk’uk’ umuntu wese yagabiwe ingabire muzigaburirane, nk’uko bibereye ababgiriza beza b’ubuntu bg’Imana bg’uburyo bginshi." 
1Peter4:11 Umuntu iy’ avuze, avuge nk’ūbivugishijwe n’Imana: umuntu iy’ agabuye, agabure nk’ūfise ubushobozi Imana itanga; kugira ngw Imana iterwe icubahiro muri vyose, kubga Yesu Kristo, afise icubahiro n’ububasha ibihe bitazoshira. Amen." 
1Peter4:12 Abo nkunda, umuriro uri hagati yanyu wo kubagerageza ntukabatangaze, nk’aho mubonye akatābonetse." 
1Peter4:13 Ariko munezerezwe n’uko mufatanije n’imibabaro ya Kristo, kugira ngo no mu gihe co guhishurwa kw’ubgiza bgiwe muze munezerwe muhimbarwe." 
1Peter4:14 Iyo mututswe muhōwe izina rya Kristo, muba muhiriwe: kuko Mpwemu w’ubgiza, ari we Mpwemu w’Imana, aba kuri mwebge." 
1Peter4:15 Ntihakagire umuntu wo muri mwebge ahōrwa kuba umwicanyi canke kuba igisuma canke kuba inkozi y’ikibi canke kwita mu vyo atagezwemwo. 
1Peter4:16 Ariko ni hāgira ūhōrwa kuba Umukristo, yoye kumāramāra, arikw aheshe Imana icubahiro kubg’ iryo zina." 
1Peter4:17 Kukw igihe gishitse c’uk’ urubanza rutangurira mu b’inzu y’Imana: none ko rutanguriye kuri twebge, iherezo ry’abatumvira ubutumwa bgiza bg’Imana rizomera rite?" 
1Peter4:18 Kandi k’umugororotsi akizwa agarukiye ku manga, ūtubaha Imana n’umunyavyaha bazoboneka hehe?" 
1Peter4:19 Nuko rer’ abababazwa nk’ukw Imana igomba ni babītse ubugingo bgabo uwo Muremyi wo kwizigirwa, bakore ivyiza." 
1Peter5:1 Abashingantahe b’ishengero bo muri mwebge ndabahanūra, kuko nanje nd’ umushingantahe mugenzi wanyu, kandi nd’ icabona c’imibabaro Kristo yababajwe, kandi mfatanije namwe ubgiza buzohishurwa." 
1Peter5:2 Muragire ubusho bg’Imana bgo muri mwebge, mutaburagira nk’abagōberewe, ariko mubikunze, nk’ukw Imana igomba: ntimuburagirishwe no kurondera inyungu mbi, ariko muburagire mushize igikonyo." 
1Peter5:3 Kandi ntimuragire nk’abatwaza amanyama amasho mwagabanganirijwe, ariko mube ivyitegererezo vy’ubusho." 
1Peter5:4 Nuk’ Umwungere mukuru ni yerekanwa, muzokwambikwa mu mitwe igitsibo c’ubgiza kitazoshira." 
1Peter5:5 Namwe bukungu, mugamburukire abashingantahe. Mwese mukenyere ukwicisha bugufi kugira ngo mukorerane: kukw Imana irwanya abībona, arikw abicisha bugufi ikabaha ubuntu." 
1Peter5:6 Nuko mwicishe bugufi muri musi y’ukuboko kw’Imana kw’ubushobozi, kugira ngw iz’ ibashire hejuru mu gihe gikwiye." 
1Peter5:7 Muyikorere amaganya yanyu yose, kukw ibababara." 
1Peter5:8 Mwirinde ibiboreza, mwame mugavye: umurezi wanyu, ari we wa Murwanizi, agendagenda nk’intambge yivuga, arondera uwo arotsa." 
1Peter5:9 Mumurwanye mufise ukwizera gushikamye, muzi yukw imibabaro ihwanye n’iyanyu ishitswa kuri bene Data bari mw isi." 
1Peter5:10 Kand’ Imana igira ubuntu bgose, yabahamagariye ubgiza bgayo budashira muri muri Kristo, ni mwaheza kubabazwa akanya gato, izobahīngūra rwose ubgayo, izobaremesha, ibahe inkomezi." 
1Peter5:11 Ububasha bube ubgayo ibihe bitazoshira. Amen. 
1Peter5:12 Mbandikiye icete c’amajambo make, canditswe na Siluwano, mwene Data w’umwizigirwa uko niyumvira; mbahanūra nshinga intahe yuk’ ubgo ari bgo buntu bg’Imana bg’ukuri: mubuhagararemwo mushikamye." 
1Peter5:13 Ishengero ry’i Babuloni ry’abātoranijwe nkamwe rirabatasha, bo na Mariko, umwana wanje." 
1Peter5:14 Muramukanishe kugumbirana kw’urukundo. Amahoro abe muri mwebge mwese muri muri Kristo. 
2Peter1:1 Simoni Petero, umugurano wa Yesu Kristo kand’ intumwa yiwe, ndabandikiye mwebge abāhawe ukwizera kw’akaburarugero kungana n’ukwacu, muguheshejwe n’ukugororoka kwa Yesu Kristo, ni we Mana yacu n’Umukiza." 
2Peter1:2 Ubuntu n’amahoro bigwire muri mwebge, mubiheshwa no kumenya Imana neza na Yesu Umwami wacu." 
2Peter1:3 Kuk’ ubushobozi bg’ubumana bgayo bgaduhaye ivy’ ubugingo no kwubaha Imana vyose, tubiheshwa no kumenya neza uwaduhamagarishije ubgiza bgiwe n’ingeso ziwe nziza." 
2Peter1:4 Ivyo vyatumye aduha ivyo yasezeranye vy’akaburarugero, bihambaye cane, kugira ngo bibatere gusangira n’Imana akameremere kayo, mumaze gucika muva mw iborero ryazanywe mw isi no kwifuza." 
2Peter1:5 Mbere kubg’ iyo nyanduruko nyene, ubganyu mushiruke umwete wose; ukwizera kwanyu mukwongerekw ingeso nziza; ingeso nziza muzongerek’ ubgenge;" 
2Peter1:6 ubgenge mubgongereko kwirinda; ukwirinda mukwongereko kwihangana; ukwihangana mukwongereko kwubaha Imana; 
2Peter1:7 ukwubaha Imana mukwongereko gukunda bene Data; ugukunda bene Data mukwongerek’ urukundo. 
2Peter1:8 Kuko namba mugira ivyo, bikagwira, bituma mutaba abanyabute cank’ ingumba ku vyo kumenya neza Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo." 
2Peter1:9 Kuk’ ūtagira ivyo ar’ impumyi, abona ibiri hafi gusa, yibagiye umwuhagiro w’ivyaha vyiwe vya kera." 
2Peter1:10 Ni co gituma, bene Data, mukwiye kurushiriza kugira umwete wo gukomeza ihamagarwa ryanyu, bo n’ugutoranywa. Ni mwakora ivyo, ntimuzotsitara na gatoya." 
2Peter1:11 Kuko ni vyaba birtyo, muzohabga rwose kwinjira mu bgami budashira bga Yesu Kristo, ni we Mwami n’Umukiza wacu." 
2Peter1:12 Ni co gituma imisi yose ntazotenzura kubibutsa ivyo, naho mubizi mukaba mushikamye mu kuri kuri muri mwebge." 
2Peter1:13 Ndiyumvira yuko nkwiye kubakangura mbibutsa, nkiri mur’ uru rusago." 
2Peter1:14 Kuko nzi yukw igihe co kwamburwa urusago rwanje kiza kuza gitebutse, nk’uk’ Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo yammenyesheje." 
2Peter1:15 Ariko nzogira umwete, kugira ngo ni namara gutaha muze mushobore kwama mwibuka ivyo." 
2Peter1:16 Kuko tutākurikiye imigani yaremwe n’akenge, hamwe twabamenyesha ubushobozi bg’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo no kuzoza kwiwe; ariko n’uko twiboneye n’amaso yacu icubahiro ciwe gihambaye." 
2Peter1:17 Kuko yahawe n’Imana Data wa twese ishimwe n’ubgiza, ah’ ijwi rivuzwe n’ubgiza bukomeye cane ryamushikako, rikavuga, ngo Nguyu Umwana wanje nkunda akampimbara." 
2Peter1:18 Iryo jw i twaryumvise rivuye mw ijuru, aho twari kumwe na we kuri wa musozi wera." 
2Peter1:19 Ariko turafise ijambo ryavugishijwe, ryarakomejwe kurushiriza. Mugira neza ko murishirak’ umutima, ni nk’itara ryākira ahacuze umwiza, rigakesha ijoro, rikageza ah’ ikinyenyeri co mu gaturuturu kizobandurira mu mitima yanyu:" 
2Peter1:20 irya mbere mukwiye kumenya, n’ukw ata jambo ry’abāvugishwa n’Imana ryo mu vyanditswe rishobora gusobanurwa nk’uk’ umuntu avyigombera," 
2Peter1:21 kukw ata jambo ry’abāvugishwa n’Imana ryazanywe no kugomba kw’umuntu, arikw abantu bāvuga ivyava ku Mana, barōngōwe na Mpwemu Yera." 
2Peter2:1 Ariko hār’ abigira abavugishwa n’Imana kandi, mu bgoko bg’Abisirayeli, nk’uko no muri mwebge hazobah’ abigisha b’ibinyoma, bazozana inyigisho mu mpisho zirema ibice, zitera guhona: bazokwihakana na Shebuja yabaguze, bīhamagarire uguhona gutebutse." 
2Peter2:2 Kand’ ingeso zabo z’isoni nke benshi bazozikurikira; kubg’ ivyo inzira y’ukuri bazoyitukisha. 
2Peter2:3 Kand’ ukwifuza inyungu kwabo kuzobatera kwunguka kuri mwebge, bababgiye amagambo y’amaremano: gucirwakw iteka kwabo uhereye kera ntiguteba, no guhona kwabo ntiguhunyiza."
