Jude1:1 Yuda, umugurano wa Yesu Kristo, kandi mwene nyina wa Yakobo, ndabandikiye abahamagawe, bakundwa kuko muri mu Mana Data wa twese, mukazigamirwa Yesu Kristo." 
Jude1:2 Imbabazi n’amahoro n’urukundo bigwire muri mwebge. 
Jude1:3 Bakundwa, hamwe nashiruka umwete wo kubandikira ivy’ agakiza dusangiye, nari numvise ikingōbēra kubandikira ivyo kubahanūra kurwanira cane ukwizera abera bahawe rimwe gusa." 
Jude1:4 Kuko hariho bamwe bābājemwo binyegeteza, bandikiwe kera gucirwakw iryo teka, batubaha Imana, bahindura ubuntu bg’Imana yacu isoni nke, bakīhakana Yesu Kristo, ni we wenyene Databuja n’Umwami wacu." 
Jude1:5 Ndagomba kubibutsa, naho vyose musanzwe mubizi, yuk’ Umwami Imana, imaze gukirisha bga bgoko kubakūra mu gihugu ca Egiputa, hanyuma yahoneje abatizeye." 
Jude1:6 N’abamarayika batāgumye mu bukuru bgabo, ariko bātaye ahantu habo, ibarindira kuzocirwakw iteka ryo ku musi uhambaye, bari mu minyororo idashira no mu mwiza." 
Jude1:7 Kandi n’abantu b’i Sodomu n’i Gomora bo n’ibisagara vyari bihereranye na ho, kuko bitanze bakīha ubusambanyi nka ba bandi, n’ukwendana, ukw imibiri itaremewe, ivyo bisagara vyashiriweho kuba akabarore, bibabazwa n’igihano c’umuriro utazima." 
Jude1:8 Ariko na barya nyene bahwanye na bo, inzozi zabo zibatera kwōnōna imibiri yabo, no gukēngēra ukuganzwa no gutuka abanyacubahiro." 
Jude1:9 Ariko na Mikayeli, umumarayika mukuru, hamwe yatongana na wa Murwanizi, ahārīra na we bapfa umuvyimba wa Mose, ntiyubahutse kumuhinyura ngw amucokore, ariko yamubgiye, at’ Uhoraho aguhane." 
Jude1:10 Arikw abo bantu batuka ivyo batazi: kandi n’ivyo bamenyeshwa n’akameremere kabo, nk’ukw ibikōko bimeze bitagira ubgenge, na vyo nyene baravyiyonōnesha." 
Jude1:11 Bazobona ibara, kuko bajanye inzira ya Kayini, bakiroha mu buzimire bga Balamu kubg’ amaronko, bagahonera mu mugararizo wa Kora." 
Jude1:12 Abo n’ivyubirizi mw isangira ryanyu ry’urukundo, iyo basangira namwe ivyiza; n’abungere bīragira ubgabo ata dusoni: n’ibicu bitagira amazi, bikubebga hose n’umuyaga; n’ibiti birumvye bitāma, vyapfuye kabiri, vyaranduranywe n’imizi;" 
Jude1:13 n’imipfunda yo mu kiyaga isūriranya, babimba ifuro ry’ibiteye isoni vyabo; n’inyenyeri ziyerera zibīkiwe umwiza w’umuzitanya ibihe bidashira." 
Jude1:14 Kandi Henoki, ni we yagira indwi uhereye kuri Adamu, yavugishijwe n’Imana ivyabo, at’ Eh’ Uhoraho yazananye n’amasinzi y’abera biwe," 
Jude1:15 kugira ngw acire bose amateka, no kwemeza abatubaha Imana bose ko batsinzwe ku bikorwa vyose vyo kutubaha Imana bakoze batayubaha, n’amagambo yose akomeye abanyavyaha batubaha Imana bavuze bayirwanya." 
Jude1:16 Abo n’abidodomba n’abanyamwikomo bagenda bakurikira ukwifuza kwabo, akanwa kabo kavuga amagambo atumbaganyemw’ ukwirarira, bubahira abantu kubakūramw’ amaronko." 
Jude1:17 Ariko mweho, bakundwa, mwibuke amajambo yavuzwe kera n’intumwa z’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo;" 
Jude1:18 ko bābabgiye, bati Mu gihe c’iherezo hazoboneka abacokoranyi bagenda bakurikira ukwifuza kwabo kwo kutubaha Imana." 
Jude1:19 Abo ni bo bazana kwirema ibice; n’abantu gusa, ntibafise Mpwemu." 
Jude1:20 Ariko mweho, bakundwa, mwiyubake ku kwizera kwanyu kwera cane, musengere muri Mpwemu Yera," 
Jude1:21 mwizigamire mu rukundo rw’Imana, mwiteze imbabazi z’Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo zibashitsa ku bugingo budashira." 
Jude1:22 Ababahāririza mubahanūre: 
Jude1:23 abandi mubakize, mubokore mu muriro: abandi mubagirire ikigongwe mutinya, mwanke n’impuzu itewe amarabaga n’umubiri." 
Jude1:24 Ariko, Īshobora kubazigama ngo ntimutsitare, no kubahagarika imbere y’ubgiza bgayo mudafise agasembga munezerewe cane," 
Jude1:25 ni yo Mana imwe yonyene, Umukiza wacu yadukirishije Yesu Kristo Umwami wacu, ubgiza n’icubahiro n’inganji n’ububasha bibe ivyayo, uhereye kera hose, na bugingo n’ubu, ugashitsa ibihe bidashira. Amen." 
Revelation1:1 Uguhishura kwa Yesu Kristo, ukwo yahawe n’Imana ngo yereke abagurano biwe ibigira bibeho vuba, agatuma umumarayika wiwe akabimenyesha umugurano wiwe Yohana," 
Revelation1:2 yashingiye intahe ivyo yabonye vyose, ni vyo jambo ry’Imana, no gushinga intahe kwa Yesu Kristo." 
Revelation1:3 Hahirwa ūsoma, hahirwa n’abumva amajambo y’uku kuvugishwa n’Imana, bakitondera ivyanditswe muri yo: kukw igihe kiri hafi." 
Revelation1:4 Jewe Yohana ndabandikiye mwebge abo mu mashengero ndwi yo muri Asiya. Ubuntu bube muri mwebge n’amahoro biva kur’ Iyo, iriho, kandi yamyeho, kand’ igira ize, biva no ku Mpwemu ndwi zir’ imbere y’intebe yayo," 
Revelation1:5 no kuri Yesu Kristo, icabona co kwizigirwa, imfura y’abari barapfuye, ūganza abami bo mw isi. Umwe adukunda, yatubohoje ivyaha vyacu amaraso yiwe," 
Revelation1:6 akaduhindura ubgami, no kuba abaherezi b’Imana yiwe, ni yo Se: icubahiro n’inganji bibe ivyiwe ibihe bitazoshira. Amen." 
Revelation1:7 Eh’ arazanana n’ibicu, kand’ ijisho ryose rizomwibonera, n’abāmucumise bazomubona: kand’ amoko yose yo mw isi azoborogeshwa na we. Ni ko biri. Amen." 
Revelation1:8 Jewe ndi Alufa na Omega, ni k’Umwami Imana igize, iriho, kandi yamyeho, kand’ igira ize, ni yo ishobora vyose." 
Revelation1:9 Jewe Yohana, mwene So, musangiye amarushwa n’ubgami n’ukwihangana biri muri Yesu, nari ku kizinga Patimo co mu kiyaga, bampōra ijambo ry’Imana no gushingira intahe Yesu." 
Revelation1:10 Ku musi w’Imana nari muri Mpwemu, numva inyuma yanje ijwi rirenga nk’iry’ inzamba," 
Revelation1:11 rivuga, rit’ Ic’ ubona ucandike mu gitabo, ukirungikire amashengero ndwi, ukirungike muri Efeso n’i Simuruna n’i Perugamo n’i Tuwatira n’i Sarudi n’i Filadelufiya n’i Lawodikiya." 
Revelation1:12 Mpindukira kurāba ijwi rivuganye nanje: mpindukiye mbona ibiterekwakw amatara ndwi vy’izahabu," 
Revelation1:13 kandi hagati y’ivyo biterekwakw amatara mbona uwusa n’Umwana w’umuntu, yambaye imyambaro ishika ku birenge, yambaye mu gikiriza umukanda w’izahabu." 
Revelation1:14 Kand’ umutwe wiwe n’umushatsi vyari vyera nk’ubgoya bg’intama y’umwero, canke nka shelegi; n’inyonga ziwe zasa n’imbeya z’umuriro;" 
Revelation1:15 ibirenge vyiwe vyasa n’umuringa w’umwakaka, utukujwe n’umuriro; n’ijwi ryiwe ryari rimeze nk’iry’ amazi menshi asūma," 
Revelation1:16 kandi mu kuboko kwiwe kw’i buryo yar’ afise inyenyeri ndwi, mu kanwa kiwe hāvamw’ inkota ikarishe, mu nyonga hiwe hari hameze nk’izuba iyo ryatse umutari." 
Revelation1:17 Ndamubonye, nikubita imbere y’inyundo ziwe nk’ūpfuye; maz’ anshirak’ ukuboko kw’i buryo, ati Ntutinye; jewe nd’ uwa mbere kandi nd’ uw’ iherezo," 
Revelation1:18 kandi ndi muzima; nari narapfuye, kandi rāba mpora ndi muzima ibihe bitazoshira, mfise impfunguzo z’urupfu n’iz’ i kuzimu." 
Revelation1:19 Nuko wandike ivy’ ubonye n’ibiriho n’ibizoba hanyuma y’ivyo," 
Revelation1:20 ibanga ry’inyenyeri ndwi izo umbonanye mu kuboko kwanje kw’i buryo, n’ivy’ ibiterekwakw amatara ndwi vy’izahabu. Inyenyeri ndwi ni zo bamarayika b’ayo mashengero ndwi, ibiterekwakw amatara ndwi na vyo ni vyo mashengero ndwi." 
Revelation2:1 Andikira umumarayika w’ishengero ryo muri Efeso, ut’ Ūfashe inyenyeri indwi mu kuboko kw’i buryo, akagendera hagati y’ibiterekwakw amatara indwi vy’izahabu, aravuga ibi," 
Revelation2:2 ngo Ndazi i bikorwa vyawe n’ubutame bgawe n’ukwihangana, kandi yuk’ udashobora kwirengagiza ababi, ariko wagenzuye abiyita intumwa kand’ atari zo, usanga n’abanyabinyoma." 
Revelation2:3 Kand’ ugira ukwihangana, wirengagije ivy’ ugirirwa kw izina ryanje, ntiwacobogora." 
Revelation2:4 Ariko mfise ico nkugayako, yuko waretse urukundo rwawe rwa mbere." 
Revelation2:5 Nuko ni wibuke aho wavuye ukagwa; wihane, ukore ibikorwa nk’ivya mbere. N’utagira urtyo, nzoza kuri wewe nkūre igiterekwakw itara cawe ahantu haco, shiti wihannye." 
Revelation2:6 Arikw ic’ ufise n’uko wanka ibikorwa vy’Abanikolayiti, ivyo nanje nanka." 
Revelation2:7 Ūri n’ugutwi ni yumve ico Mpwemu abgira amashengero. Ūnesha, nzomuha kurya ku vyamye ku giti c’ubugingo kiri muri Paradiso y’Imana." 
Revelation2:8 Kandi wandikire umumarayika w’ishengero ry’i Simuruna, ut’ Uwa mbere kand’ uw’ iherezo, uwari yarapfuye kand’ akaba muzima, aravuga ibi," 
Revelation2:9 ngo Ndazi amarushwa yawe n’ubgoro bgawe (yamar’ ur’ umutunzi), n’ibitutsi vy’abiyita Abayuda, atari bo, arikw ar’ isinagogi ya Satani." 
Revelation2:10 Ntutinye ivy’ ugira ubabazwe. Eh’ uwo Murwanizi agira ashire bamwe muri mwebge mw ibohero kugira ngo mugeragezwe, kandi muzogira amarushwa imisi cumi. Wame uyoboka gushitsa ku gupfa, nanje nzoguha igitsibo c’ubugingo." 
Revelation2:11 Ūri n’ugutwi ni yumve ico Mpwemu abgira amashengero. Ūnesha nta co urupfu rwa kabiri ruzomugira. 
Revelation2:12 Kandi wandikire umumarayika w’ishengero ry’i Perugamo, ut’ Ūfise inkota ikarishe aravuga ibi," 
Revelation2:13 ngo Ndazi ah’ uba, kw ari ho umurwa wa Satani uri; kandi wumiye kw izina ryanje, ntiwihakanye kunyizera no mu misi ya Antipa, icabona canje, n’umugororotsi wanje, yiciwe i wanyu, aho Satani aba." 
Revelation2:14 Ariko mfise i vyo nkugayako bike, kukw i wanyu uhafise abakomeza inyigisho za Balamu, yigishije Balaki gushira igitsitaza imbere y’Abisirayeli, kugira ngo barye ivyaterekerejwe ibigirwamana, bashakane." 
Revelation2:15 Ni ko nawe, ufise abakomeza inyigisho z’Abanikolayiti nk’uko nyene." 
Revelation2:16 Nuko rero ni wihane: n’utihana nzoza kuri wewe vuba, kand’ abo nzobarwanya, mbakubite inkota yo mu kanwa kanje." 
Revelation2:17 Ūri n’ugutwi ni yumve ico Mpwemu abgira amashengero. Ūnesha nzomuha kuri manu yanyegejwe, kandi nzomuha ibuye ryera, kur’ iryo buye handitswekw izina risha, nta muntu arizi, atar’ ūzorihabga." 
Revelation2:18 Kandi wandikire umumarayika w’ishengero ry’i Tuwatira, ut’ Umwana w’Imana, afise inyonga zisa n’imbeya z’umuriro, ibirenge vyiwe bisa n’umuringa w’umwakaka, aravuga ibi," 
Revelation2:19 ngo Ndazi ibikorwa vyawe, n’urukundo rwawe, n’ukwizera kwawe, n’ingen’ ushitsa ibango ryawe, n’ukwihangana kwawe, kandi kw ibikorwa vyawe vyo hanyuma biruta ivya mbere kuba vyinshi." 
Revelation2:20 Ariko mfise ico nkugayako, yuk’ ukundira urya mugore Yezebeli, yiyita ūvugishwa n’Imana, akigisha akazimiza abagurano banje, kugira ngo bashakane barye ivyaterekerejwe ibigirwamana." 
Revelation2:21 Kandi namuhaye uburyo bgo kwihana, ntiyakunda kwihana ngw areke ubushakanyi bgiwe." 
Revelation2:22 Ehe ndamutsinda ku buriri, ndarungikira abasambana na we amarushwa menshi, ni batihana ibikorwa vyiwe." 
Revelation2:23 Kandi n’abana biwe nzobicisha urupfu, kand’ amashengero yose azomenya yukw ari jewe nsesa mu mishaha no mu mitima, kandi nzokwishura umuntu wese wo muri mwebge ibihwanye n’ivyo mwakoze." 
Revelation2:24 Ariko mweho abasigaye mu b’i Tuwatira, abadafise iyo nyigisho mwese, batāmenye ivyo ba bandi bita ivy’i bgina vya Satani, ndababgira, nti Nta wundi mutwaro mbikoreza atar’ uyu," 
Revelation2:25 ko mwumira ku co mufise mugashitsa aho nzozira. 
Revelation2:26 Ūnesha akitondera ibikorwa vyanje agashitsa kw iherezo, nzomuha ububasha bgo kuganza amahanga:" 
Revelation2:27 azoyaragiza inkoni y’icuma, nk’uko bamenagura inzavya z’ibumba; nk’uko nanje nahawe na Data." 
Revelation2:28 Kandi nzomuha ikinyenyeri co mu gaturuturu. 
Revelation2:29 Ūri n’ugutwi, ni yumve ico Mpwemu abgira amashengero." 
Revelation3:1 Kandi wandikire umumarayika w’ishengero ry’i Sarudi, ut’ Ūfise Impwemu ndwi z’Imana n’inyenyeri ndwi, aravuga ibi, ngo Ndazi ibikorwa vyawe, k’uvugwa k’uri muzima, arik’ ur’ uwapfuye." 
Revelation3:2 Gira ube maso, ukomeze ibisigaye bigira bipfe: kukw ata bikorwa vyawe nabonye bisozerewe imbere y’Imana yanje." 
Revelation3:3 Ni wibuke rero ingene wākiriye kandi wumvise: uvyitondere, wihane. Nuko rero n’utaba maso, nzoza nk’igisuma, nawe ntuzomenya igihe nzokwūbīra." 
Revelation3:4 Arik’ ufise amazina makeya y’ab’ i Sarudi batanduje impuzu zabo; ni bo bazogendana nanje bambaye impuzu zera, kuko bibabereye." 
Revelation3:5 Ūnesha azokwambikwa artyo impuzu zera, kandi sinzosibanganya izina ryiwe mu gitabo c’ubugingo na mba, kandi nzokwatura izina ryiwe imbere ya Data, n’imbere y’abamarayika biwe." 
Revelation3:6 Ūri n’ugutwi, ni yumve ico Mpwemu abgira amashengero." 
Revelation3:7 Wandikire umumarayika w’ishengero ry’i Filadelufiya, ut’ Uwera, uw’ ukuri, ūfise urupfunguzo rwa Dawidi, uwugurura ntihagire uwugara, kand’ uwugara ntihagire uwugurura, aravuga ibi," 
Revelation3:8 ngo Ndazi ibikorwa vyawe (ehe nashize imbere yawe urugi rwuguruye, nta wushobora kurwugara) yuk’ ufise ubushobozi buke, witondeye ijambo ryanje, ntiwihakanye izina ryanje." 
Revelation3:9 Ehe nguhaye bamwe bo mw isinagogi ya Satani, biyita Abayuda, atari bo, ariko babesha; ehe nzobagōbēra kuza, bikubite imbere y’ibirenge vyawe, bamenye yuko nagukunze." 
Revelation3:10 Ko witondeye ijambo ryo kwihangana kwanje, nanje nzokurinda igihe co kugerageza, kigira kize mu bihugu vyose, kugerageza ababa mw isi." 
Revelation3:11 Ngira nze vuba: wumire ku co ufise, ntihagire ūgutwara igitsibo cawe." 
Revelation3:12 Ūnesha nzomugira inkingi yo mu rusengero rw’Imana yanje, kandi ntazosohoka ukundi, nanje nzomwandikakw izina ry’Imana yanje, n’iry’ umurwa w’Imana yanje, ni wo Yerusalemu musha, wururuka uvuye mw ijuru ku Mana yanje, kandi nzomwandikakw izina ryanje risha." 
Revelation3:13 Ūri n’ugutwi ni yumve ico Mpwemu abgira amashengero. 
Revelation3:14 Wandikire umumarayika w’ishengero ry’i Lawodikiya, ut’ Uwiyita Amen, icabona co kwizigirwa kandi c’ukuri, inkomoko y’ivyaremwe n’Imana, aravuga ibi," 
Revelation3:15 ngo Ndazi ibikorwa vyawe, yuk’ udakonje kandi ntubire. Icompa ugakonja cank’ ukabira!" 
Revelation3:16 Nuko rero kuk’ ur’ akazuyazi, udakonje ntubire, ngira nkudahwe." 
Revelation3:17 Kuk’ uvuga, uti Nd’ umukire ndatunze kandi nta co nkennye; ntumenye yukw ari wewe mutindi, wafutanye, ur’ umworo, ur’ impumyi, ugenda amēnya;" 
Revelation3:18 ndakugīra inama, ungurekw izahabu yakūwekw inkamba n’umuriro, ubone kuba umutunzi; ungureko n’impuzu zera, ubone kwambara, isoni z’ubgambure bgawe ntizigaragare; kand’ ungureko n’umuti wo gusīga ku maso, ubone guhumūka." 
Revelation3:19 Abo nkunda bose ndabakankamira, nkabakāngīra; nuko gira umwete, wihane." 
Revelation3:20 Ehe mpagaze ku rugi, ndaramukije. Umuntu ni yumva ijwi ryanje, akugurura urugi, ndinjira i we, dusangire." 
Revelation3:21 Ūnesha, nzomuha kwicarana nanje ku ntebe yanje y’ubgami, nk’uko nanje nanesheje nkicarana na Data ku ntebe yiwe." 
Revelation3:22 Ūri n’ugutwi, ni yumve ico Mpwemu abgira amashengero." 
Revelation4:1 Hanyuma y’ivyo ndāvye mbona mw ijuru urugi rwuguruye, kandi rya jwi nabanje kwumva rivugana nanje ari nk’iry’ inzamba, rirambgira, riti Dūga uze hano, nkwereke ibikwiye kuzobaho hanyuma y’ivyo." 
Revelation4:2 Ako kanya mba muri Mpwemu: kandi mbona intebe iteretse mw ijuru, mbona n’Ūyivyagiyeko." 
Revelation4:3 Uwar’ avyagiye yasa n’akabuyenge kitwa yasipi n’akitwa sarudiyo: kand’ umunywamazi war’ ukikije iyo ntebe, usa n’akitwa simaragido." 
Revelation4:4 Iyo ntebe yar’ ikikijwe n’izindi ntebe mirongwibiri na zine: kur’ izo ntebe mbona abakuru mirongwibiri na bane bazicayeko, bambaye impuzu zera, no mu mitwe yabo har’ ibitsibo vy’izahabu." 
Revelation4:5 Kandi kuri ya ntebe y’ubgami hava imiravyo n’amajwi n’imituragaro: kand’ imuri ndwi z’umuriro zākira imbere y’iyo ntebe, ni zo Mpwemu ndwi z’Imana:" 
Revelation4:6 kand’ imbere y’iyo ntebe hari nk’ikiyaga c’ibirahuri, gisa n’urubona: kandi hagati ahahanganye n’iyo ntebe no kuyikikuza har’ ibinyabugingo bine vyuzuye amaso imbere n’inyuma." 
Revelation4:7 Ikinyabugingo ca mbere casa n’intambge, ica kabiri casa n’inyana, ica gatatu cari gifise mu maso hasa n’ah’ umuntu, ica kane casa n’inkukuma iguruka." 
Revelation4:8 Ivyo binyabugingo bine bifise amababa atandatu‐atandatu, kandi vyuzuye amaso impande zose n’imbere mu nda: ntibiruhuka ku murango no mw ijoro, vyama bivuga, bit’ Uwera, Uwera, Uwera, ni we Mwami Imana, ashobora vyose, yamyeho, kand’ ariho, kand’ agira aze." 
Revelation4:9 Kand’ iyo vya binyabugingo bihaye uguhimbazwa n’icubahiro n’ishimwe Ivyagiye kuri ya ntebe, ni yo Ibaho ibihe bitazoshira," 
Revelation4:10 ba bakuru mirongwibiri na bane baca bikubita imbere y’Īvyagiye kur’ iyo ntebe, bagasenga Ībaho ibihe bitazoshira, bagaterera ibitsibo vyabo imbere y’iyo ntebe, bavuga," 
Revelation4:11 bati Mwami wacu, Mana yacu, birakubereye guhabga uguhimbazwa n’icubahiro n’ububasha, kukw ari wewe waremye vyose; icatumye bibaho kand’ icatumye biremwa, n’uko wabigomvye." 
Revelation5:1 Mbona igitabo mu kuboko kw’i buryo kw’Īvyagiye kuri ya ntebe, canditse imbere n’inyuma, kidombagijek’ udushashara ndwi, tukimatanije tudomyemw’ ikimenyetso." 
Revelation5:2 Mbona umumarayika w’inkomezi nyinshi asemereza ijwi rirenga, ati Ni nde bibereye kw azingurura kirya gitabo ngw amene ibikimatanije?" 
Revelation5:3 Ntihāgira uwo mw ijuru cank’ uwo kw isi cank’ uw’ i kuzimu ashobora kuzingurura ico gitabo canke kukirāba. 
Revelation5:4 Nanje ndizwa cane n’uko hatabonetse ūbereye kuzingurura ico gitabo canke kukirāba. 
Revelation5:5 Umwe muri ba bakuru arambarira, ati Nta co urira; eh’ Intambge yo mu muryango wa Yuda, Umunago wo ku gishitsi ca Dawidi, yaranesheje, ngw azingurure igitabo, amene ibikimatanije ndwi." 
Revelation5:6 Mbona hagati ya ya ntebe na vya binyabugingo bine no hagati ya ba bakuru, Umwagazi w’Intama ahagaze, asa n’uwishwe, afise amahembe ndwi n’amaso ndwi, ni vyo Mpwemu ndwi z’Imana, zatumwe kwama zija mw isi yose." 
Revelation5:7 Araza, agikūra mu kuboko kw’i buryo kw’Īvyagiye kuri ya ntebe." 
Revelation5:8 Amaze kwābīra ico gitabo, vya binyabugingo bine na ba bakuru mirongwibiri na bane baca bikubita imbere y’uwo Mwagazi, bafise inanga bose, n’inzavya z’izahabu zuzuye imibavu, ni yo gusenga kw’abera." 
Revelation5:9 Baririmba indirimbo nsha, bati Birakubereye kwābīra igitabo, no kumena ibikimatanije, kuko wishwe, ugacungurira Imana abo mu miryango yose no mu ndimi zose no mu moko yose no mu mahanga yose, ubacunguje amaraso yawe," 
Revelation5:10 ukabahindura ubgami bg’Imana yacu no kuba abaherezi bayo, kandi bazoba abami mw isi." 
Revelation5:11 Ndarāba, numva ijwi ry’abamarayika benshi bakikije ya ntebe na vya binyabugingo na ba bakuru: igitigiri cabo car’ amasinzi n’amasinzi, n’ibihumbi n’ibihumbi." 
Revelation5:12 Bavuga n’ijwi rirenga, bat’ Umwagazi yishwe abereye guhabga ububasha n’ubutunzi n’ubgenge n’ubushobozi n’icubahiro no guhimbazwa n’umugisha." 
Revelation5:13 Kand’ icaremwe cose co mw ijuru no mw isi n’i kuzimu no hejuru y’ikiyaga n’ibiri muri vyo vyose, numva bivuga, bit’ Īvyagiye ku ntebe bo n’Umwagazi w’Intama, umugisha ube uwabo n’icubahiro no guhimbazwa n’ububasha, ibihe bitazoshira." 
Revelation5:14 Kandi vya binyabugingo bine biravuga, biti Amen. Bano bakuru bikubita hasi, barasenga." 
Revelation6:1 Mbona Umwagazi w’Intama amena kamwe muri twa dushashara ndwi tumatanije ca gitabo: numva kimwe muri vya binyabugingo bine kivuga nk’ijwi ry’inkuba, kiti Ngwino." 
Revelation6:2 Mbona ifarasi y’igitare, kand’ ūyicayeko yar’ afise umuheto, ahabga igitsibo, agenda anesha, kandi ngo yame anesha." 
Revelation6:3 Kand’ amennye ica kabiri kimatanije ca gitabo, numva ikigira kabiri mu binyabugingo, kiti Ngwino." 
Revelation6:4 Haza iyindi farasi y’akagajo, ūyicayeko ahabga gukūra amahoro mw isi, ngo bicane: kand’ ahabga inkota ndende." 
Revelation6:5 Kand’ amennye ica gatatu kimatanije ca gitabo, numva ikigira gatatu mu binyabugingo, kiti Ngwino. Mbona ifarasi y’agafyiri: kand’ ūyicayeko yar’ afise umunzane mu minwe." 
Revelation6:6 Numva hagati y’ivyo binyabugingo bine nk’ijwi rivuga, rit’ Ingero imwe y’ingano n’idenariyo‐idenariyo, n’ingero zitatu za sayiri n’idenariyo‐idenariyo: arikw amavuta na vino ntugire ic’ ubikorako." 
Revelation6:7 Kand’ amennye ica kane kimatanije ico gitabo, numva ijwi ry’ikigira kane mu binyabugingo, kiti Ngwino." 
Revelation6:8 Mbona ifarasi ibenjutse; kand’ ūyicayeko yitwa Rupfu, Kuzimu na we aramukurikira; bahabga ububasha ku kigira kane c’isi, ngo babicishe inkota n’inzara n’urupfu n’ibikōko vyo kw isi." 
Revelation6:9 Kand’ amennye ica gatanu kimatanije ico gitabo, mbona musi y’igicaniro impwemu z’abishwe babahōra ijambo ry’Imana no gushinga intahe bari bafise." 
Revelation6:10 Batakambisha ijwi rirenga, bati Databuja wera w’ukuri, uzogeza ryari kudaca amateka no kudahōra abari mw isi amaraso yacu?" 
Revelation6:11 Umuntu wese muri bo ahabga imvune yera, babarirwa kumara iyindi misi baruhuka, gushitsa ah’ igitigiri c’abagurano bagenzi babo na bene Se, bagira bicwe nka bo, kizoshikira." 
Revelation6:12 Kandi mbona amena ica gatandatu kimatanije ico gitabo, isi iratigita cane: izuba ririrabura nk’igunira ry’ubgoya; ukwezi kwose guhinduka nk’amaraso:" 
Revelation6:13 inyenyeri zo kw ijuru zikorokera hasi, nk’uk’ umusukoni uzungagizwa n’igihuhuta ugahungurura insukoni zawo zitararunguriza:" 
Revelation6:14 ijuru ririzinga, nk’umuzingo w’igitabo kizinzwe: imisozi yose n’ibizinga vyo mu kiyaga vyose bikūrwa ahantu havyo." 
Revelation6:15 Abami bo mw isi n’abaganwa n’abakuru b’abagabisha b’abasoda n’abatunzi n’abanyenkomezi n’abagurano bose n’abidegemvya bose binyegeza mu masenga no mu bitandara vyo ku misozi; 
Revelation6:16 babarira imisozi n’ibitandara, bati Ni mutugweko, muduhishe inyonga z’Īvyagiye kur’ irya ntebe n’uburake bg’Umwagazi w’Intama;" 
Revelation6:17 kuk’ umusi uhambaye w’uburake bgabo ushitse, kandi ni nde ashobora guhagarara?" 
Revelation7:1 Hanyuma y’ivyo, mbona abamarayika bane bahagaze ku mfuruka zine z’isi, bafashe imiyaga ine yo kw isi, kugira ngo ntihagire umuyaga uhūha kw isi canke ku kiyaga canke ku giti cose." 
Revelation7:2 Kandi mbona umumarayika wundi adūga, ava i burasirazuba, afise ikidomesho c’Imana nzima, asemerera n’ijwi rirenga, abarira ba bamarayika bane bahawe kwonona isi n’ikiyaga," 
Revelation7:3 ati Ntimugire ico mugira isi cank’ ikiyaga cank’ ibiti, tutaradoma ikimenyetso mu ruhanga rw’abagurano b’Imana yacu." 
Revelation7:4 Numva igitigiri c’abadomwekw ikimenyetso, ngo n’ibihumbi ijana na mirongwine na bine, abādomwekw ikimenyetso bo mu miryango yose y’Abisirayeli." 
Revelation7:5 Abo mu muryango wa Yuda bākidomweko n’ibihumbi cumi na bibiri: Abo mu muryango wa Reyubeni n’ibihumbi cumi na bibiri: Abo mu muryango wa Gadi n’ibihumbi cumi na bibiri: 
Revelation7:6 Abo mu muryango wa Asheri n’ibihumbi cumi na bibiri: Abo mu muryango wa Nafutali n’ibihumbi cumi na bibiri: Abo mu muryango wa Manase n’ibihumbi cumi na bibiri: 
Revelation7:7 Abo mu muryango wa Simeyoni n’ibihumbi cumi na bibiri: Abo mu muryango wa Lewi n’ibihumbi cumi na bibiri: Abo mu muryango wa Isakari n’ibihumbi cumi na bibiri: 
Revelation7:8 Abo mu muryango wa Zebuloni n’ibihumbi cumi na bibiri: Abo mu muryango wa Yosefu n’ibihumbi cumi na bibiri: Abo mu muryango wa Benyamini bādomwekw ikimenyetso n’ibihumbi cumi na bibiri. 
Revelation7:9 Hanyuma y’ivyo mbona ishengero ryinshi, ata woshobora kuriharūra, bo mu mahanga yose n’imiryango yose n’amoko yose n’indimi zose, bahagaze imbere y’iyo ntebe n’imbere y’Umwagazi w’Intama, bambaye imvune zera, bari n’amashami y’ibigazi mu minwe:" 
Revelation7:10 basemerera n’ijwi rirenga, bat’ Agakiza n’ak’ Imana yacu ivyagiye kur’ irya ntebe n’ak’ Umwagazi w’Intama." 
Revelation7:11 Abamarayika bose bari bahagaze bakikije ino ntebe, bakikije na ba bakuru na vya binyabugingo, bikubita hasi bubamye imbere y’intebe, basenga Imana," 
Revelation7:12 bati Amen, umugisha no guhimbazwa n’ubgenge n’ishimwe n’icubahiro n’ububasha n’ubushobozi n’ivy’ Imana yacu ibihe bitazoshira. Amen." 
Revelation7:13 Umwe muri ba bakuru arambaza, at’ Aba bambaye imvune zera ni ba nde, kandi bavuye hehe?" 
Revelation7:14 Ndamwishura, nti Mugenzi, ni wewe wobimenya. Arambgira, at’ Aba n’abāvuye muri wa mubabaro mwinshi, kandi bamesuye imvune zabo bazezesha amaraso ya wa Mwagazi." 
Revelation7:15 Ni co gituma baba imbere y’intebe y’Imana, bakayikorera mu rusengero rwayo ku murango no mw ijoro: kand’ Īvyagiye kur’ irya ntebe izosanza ihema ryayo hejuru yabo." 
Revelation7:16 Ntibazoba bakigira inzara ukundi, kandi ntibazoba bakigira inyota ukundi, kand’ izuba ntirizobarabika cank’ indugumba yose," 
Revelation7:17 kuko wa Mwagazi ari hagati ahahanganye n’iyo ntebe, azobaragira, kand’ azobashōra ku masōko y’amazi y’ubugingo; kand’ Imana izohanagura amosozi yose ku maso yabo." 
Revelation8:1 Kand’ amennye ikigira indwi kimatanije ico gitabo, haba agacerere mw ijuru nk’igihimba c’isaha." 
Revelation8:2 Mbona abamarayika ndwi bama bahagarara imbere y’Imana bahabga inzamba ndwi. 
Revelation8:3 Haza umumarayika wundi, ahagarara ku gicaniro, afise icotero c’izahabu, ahabga imibavu myinshi ngw ayishire ku gusenga kw’abera bose kuri ku gicaniro c’izahabu kir’ imbere y’iyo ntebe." 
Revelation8:4 Umwotsi w’umubavu uva mu kuboko kw’umumarayika upfundukana n’ugusenga kw’abera imbere y’Imana. 
Revelation8:5 Umumarayika ajana icotero, acuzuza umuriro wo ku gicaniro, ashiburira mw isi: habah’ imituragaro n’amajwi n’imiravyo no gutigita kw’isi." 
Revelation8:6 Ba bamarayika ndwi bafise inzamba ndwi bagabiriza kuzivuza. 
Revelation8:7 Uwa mbere aravuza. Haza urubura n’umuriro bivanze n’amaraso, bishiburirwa mw isi. Ikigira gatatu c’isi kirasha, ikigira gatatu c’ibiti kirasha, ivyatsi bibisi vyose birasha." 
Revelation8:8 Umumarayika wa kabiri aravuza. Ikimeze nk’igisozi kinini caka umuriro gishiburirwa mu kiyaga; ikigira gatatu c’ikiyaga gihinduka amaraso; 
Revelation8:9 ikigira gatatu c’ivyaremwe vyo mu kiyaga bifise ubugingo kirapfa; ikigira gatatu c’amato kirahona. 
Revelation8:10 Umumarayika wa gatatu aravuza: inyenyeri nini iva mw ijuru iratibuka, yaka nk’urumuri, itibukira ku kigira gatatu c’inzūzi no ku masōko." 
Revelation8:11 Iyo nyenyeri yitwa Mururazi. Ikigira gatatu c’amazi gihinduka umururazi, abantu benshi bicwa n’ayo mazi, kuko yarurishijwe." 
Revelation8:12 Umumarayika wa kane aravuza. Ikigira gatatu c’izuba n’ikigira gatatu c’ukwezi n’ikigira gatatu c’inyenyeri birakubitwa, kugira ngw ikigira gatatu cavyo gicure umwiza, ikigira gatatu co mu bihe vy’umurango nticākirwe, no mw ijoro n’uko." 
Revelation8:13 Ndarāba, numva inkukuma iguruka yātiriye ijuru, ivuga n’ijwi rirenga, it’ Ibara, ibara, ibara riza kubonwa n’abari mw isi kubg’ ayandi majwi y’inzamba z’abamarayika batatu bahava bavuza." 
Revelation9:1 Umumarayika wa gatanu aravuza. Mbona inyenyeri itibukiye mw isi ivuye kw ijuru; ihabga urupfunguzo rw’urusumanyenzi rw’i kuzimu. 
Revelation9:2 Yugurura urusumanyenzi rw’i kuzimu, rupfundukamw’ umwotsi nk’uw’ itanure rinini, izuba n’ikirēre bicurishwa umwiza n’umwotsi wo mur’ urwo rusumanyenzi." 
Revelation9:3 Mu mwotsi havamw’ inzige zija mw isi, zihabga ububasha bgo gukora ivyo sikorupiyo zo kw isi zibasha gukora." 
Revelation9:4 Zibgirwa kutagira ico zigira ivyatsi vyo kw isi cank’ ikintu cose kibisi cank’ igiti cose, atar’ abantu batādomwekw ikimenyetso c’Imana mu ruhanga rwabo." 
Revelation9:5 Zihabga kutabica, ariko zihabga kubasesereza amezi atanu. Kandi kubabaza kwazo kumeze nk’ukwa sikorupiyo iyo iriye umuntu." 
Revelation9:6 Mur’ iyo misi abantu bazoba barondera urupfu, ariko ntibazorubona na gatoya; bazoba bifuza gupfa, urupfu rubahunge." 
Revelation9:7 Kand’ ishusho y’izo nzige yasa n’iy’ amafarasi yiteguriwe intambara, zari zambaye mu mitwe nk’ibitsibo bisa n’izahabu, mu maso hazo hasa n’ah’ abantu." 
Revelation9:8 Kandi zari zifise ubgoya bumeze nk’umushatsi w’abagore, amenyo yazo yari nk’ay’ intambge." 
Revelation9:9 Kandi zari zifise ibikīngira ibikiriza, bimeze nk’ivyuma, guhinda kw’amababa yazo kwari kumeze nk’uguhinda kw’imikogote ikwegwa n’amafarasi menshi yiruka ija mu ntambara." 
Revelation9:10 Kandi zari zifise imirizo nk’iya sikorupiyo, n’imbōyi, kandi mu mirizo yazo ni ho harimw’ ubushobozi bgo gusesereza abantu amezi atanu." 
Revelation9:11 Zifise umwami wazo, ni we mumarayika w’i kuzimu, mu Giheburayo yitwa Abadoni, mu Kigiriki yitwa Apoluwoni." 
Revelation9:12 Ibara rya mbere riraheze, eh’ ukundi kubona ibara kubiri guhava kuza hanyuma." 
Revelation9:13 Umumarayika wa gatandatu aravuza: numva ijwi riva ku mahembe ane y’igicaniro c’izahabu kir’ imbere y’Imana," 
Revelation9:14 ribarira umumarayika wa gatandatu afise inzamba, riti Bohora abamarayika bane babohewe ku ruzi runini Efurate." 
Revelation9:15 Abo bamarayika bane, bari biteguriwe iyo saha n’uwo musi n’ukwo kwezi n’uwo mwaka, babohorerwa kwica ikigira gatatu c’abantu." 
Revelation9:16 Igitigiri c’ingabo z’abarwanira ku mafarasi car’ ibihumbi amajana igihumbi kabiri: igitigiri cabo naracumvise. 
Revelation9:17 Kandi nerekwa ntya amafarasi n’abari bayicayeko. Bari bambaye ivyuma bikīngira ibikiriza, bisa n’ikibengebenge n’agafyiri n’amazuku: imitwe y’ayo mafarasi yari nk’iy’ intambge, mu kanwa kayo havamw’ umuriro n’umwotsi n’amazuku." 
Revelation9:18 Ikigira gatatu c’abantu cicwa n’ivyo vyago, ukw ari bitatu, umuriro n’umwotsi n’amazuku, bivuye mu kanwa kayo." 
Revelation9:19 Kuk’ ububasha bg’ayo mafarasi buri mu kanwa kayo no mu mirizo yayo: kukw imirizo yayo imeze nk’inzoka, na yo iri n’imitwe, kandi ni yo aryanisha." 
Revelation9:20 Abantu bārokotse, batishwe n’ivyo vyago, ntibihana ivyakozwe n’intoke zabo, ngo bareke gusenga abadayimoni n’ibigirwamana vy’izahabu n’ivy’ ifeza n’ivy’ imiringa n’ivy’ amabuye n’ivy’ ibiti, bidashobora kubona canke kwumva canke kugenda:" 
Revelation9:21 kandi ntibihana ngo bareke ubgicanyi bgabo, cank’ uburozi cank’ ubushakanyi cank’ ubusuma." 
Revelation10:1 Mbona umumarayika wundi w’inkomezi, amanuka ava mw ijuru, yambaye igicu, no mu mutwe yari yambaye umunywamazi, mu maso hiwe hasa n’izuba, amaguru yiwe asa n’inkingi z’umuriro." 
Revelation10:2 Yar’ afise mu minwe agatabo kazinguruye, ashinga ikirenge c’i buryo ku kiyaga, ic’i bumoso agishinga i musozi." 
Revelation10:3 Asemerera n’ijwi rirenga, nk’ukw intambge yivuga: asemereye, imituragaro ndwi ituragara amajwi yayo." 
Revelation10:4 Kand’ imituragaro ndwi imaze kuvuga nariko ngira nandike. Numva ijwi rivuye mw ijuru rimbarira, riti Matanisha ishashara udomemw’ ikimenyetso ivyo imituragaro ndwi ivuze, ntuvyandike." 
Revelation10:5 Umumarayika nabonye ahagaze ku kiyaga n’i musozi, amanika ukuboko kw’i buryo, agutunga mw ijuru," 
Revelation10:6 arahira Ībaho ibihe bitazoshira, yaremye ijuru n’ibirimwo, n’isi n’ibirimwo, n’ikiyaga n’ibirimwo, ati Ntibigitevye:" 
Revelation10:7 ariko mu misi y’ijwi ry’umumarayika w’indwi, ah’ azoba agira avuze inzamba, ni ho ibanga ry’Imana rizoba riheraherejwe, nk’uko yabariye abasavyi bayo ubutumwa bgiza, ni bo bavugishwa na yo." 
Revelation10:8 Rya jwi numvise rivuye mw ijuru nongera kuryumva rimbarira, riti Genda wābīre igitabo kizinguruye kiri mu kuboko kw’ umumarayika, ahagaze ku kiyaga n’i musozi." 
Revelation10:9 Nja ah’ uwo mumarayika ari, ndamubgira kumpa ako gatabo. Arambarira, at’ Enda ugatsontsomere, karakururira mu nda, ariko mu kanwa karagusosera nk’ubūki." 
Revelation10:10 Nābīra ako gatabo, ngakūra mu kuboko kw’umumarayika, ndagatsontsomera; mu kanwa kansosera nk’ubūki; mmaze kukarya mu nda hacika umururazi." 
Revelation10:11 Barambarira, bat’ Ukwiye kuzosubira kuvugishwa ivy’ amoko menshi n’amahanga menshi n’indimi nyinshi n’abami benshi." 
Revelation11:1 Bampa irenga rimeze nk’inkoni, bati Va hasi ugere urusengero rw’Imana n’igicaniro n’abarusengeramwo." 
Revelation11:2 Intangaro y’urusengero uyireke, ntuyigere, kuko yahawe abanyamahanga: kandi n’igisagara cera bazogisiribanga amezi mirongwine n’abiri." 
Revelation11:3 Kand’ abanshingira intahe babiri nzobavugisha, bazovugishwa imisi igihumbi n’amajana abiri na mirongwitandatu bambaye amagunira." 
Revelation11:4 Abo ni bo biti vy’imyelayo bibiri n’ibiterekwakw amatara bibiri, bihagaze imbere ya Nyen’ isi." 
Revelation11:5 Kand’ iy’ umuntu agomvye kubagirira nabi umuriro ubava mu kanwa, ugaturira abansi babo: kand’ umuntu ni yagomba kubagirira nabi uko ni kw akwiye kwicwa." 
Revelation11:6 Abo bafise ubushobozi bgo gukinga ijuru, ngw imvura ntikoroke mu misi yo kuvugishwa kwabo: kandi bafise ubushobozi ku mazi kuyahindura amaraso no kubabarisha isi icago cose, uko bagomvye." 
Revelation11:7 Kandi ni baheza gushinga intahe, igikōko kizodūga kivuye i kuzimu, kizobarwanya, kibaneshe, kibice." 
Revelation11:8 Imivyimba yabo izogangarara mw ibarabara ryo mu gisagara kinini, ni co mu buryo bg’impwemu citwa Sodomu na Egiputa, kandi ni ho Umwami wabo yabambge." 
Revelation11:9 Kand’ abo mu moko n’imiryango n’indimi n’amahanga bazorāba imivyimba yabo imisi itatu n’igihimba, ntibazokunda kw iyo mivyimba ihambga." 
Revelation11:10 Abari mw isi bazonezerwa, bazobītamba ku muvyimba, barungikiranire amashimwe, kukw abo bavugishwa n’Imana bātoneka abari mw isi." 
Revelation11:11 Iyo misi itatu n’igihimba ishize impwemu z’ubugingo zivuye ku Mana zibinjiramwo, baravyuka, barahagarara: ubgoba bginshi butera ababarāba." 
Revelation11:12 Bumva ijwi rirenga rivuye mw ijuru ribabarira, riti Ni mudūge muze ino. Badūga mu gicu baja mw ijuru abansi babo barorēra." 
Revelation11:13 Uwo mwanya isi iratigita, ikigiracumi ca ca gisagara kirasenyuka, ukwo gutigita kwica abantu ibihumbi ndwi, abarokotse baterwa n’ubgoba, bahimbaza Imana Nyen’ ijuru." 
Revelation11:14 Ibara rya kabiri riraheze: eh’ irya gatatu rigira rize. 
Revelation11:15 Umumarayika w’indwi avuza inzamba: mw ijuru hakurikira amajwi arenga, at’ Ubgami bg’isi buhindutse ubg’ Umwami wacu n’ubga Kristo wiwe, kand’ azohora ahangamye ibihe bitazoshira." 
Revelation11:16 Ba bakuru mirongwibiri na bane, bicara ku ntebe zabo imbere y’Imana, bikubita hasi bubamye, basenga Imana," 
Revelation11:17 bati Turagushimye, Mwami Mana ushobora vyose, uriho kandi wamyeho, kuko wābiriye ububasha bgawe buhambaye, ukima." 
Revelation11:18 Kand’ amahanga araraka, uburake bgawe buraza, igihe co guciramw’ amateka abapfuye kirashika, n’ico kugereramw’ abasavyi bawe, ni bo bavugishwa nawe, no kugerera abera n’abubaha izina ryawe, aboroshe n’abahambaye, n’ico guhonerezamw’ abahonnya isi." 
Revelation11:19 Urusengero rw’Imana rwo mw ijuru rurugururwa, mu rusengero rwayo habonekamw’ isandugu y’isezerano ryayo, hakurikira imiravyo n’amajwi n’imituragaro no gutigita kw’isi n’urubura ruhambaye." 
Revelation12:1 Ikimenyetso gihambaye kiboneka mw ijuru: umugore yambaye izuba, ukwezi kwari musi y’ibirenge vyiwe, mu mutwe yambaye igitsibo c’inyenyeri cumi na zibiri:" 
Revelation12:2 kandi yar’ akuriwe, atura akaborogo, kukw aramutswe, ababazwa n’ibise." 
Revelation12:3 Mw ijuru haboneka ikindi kimenyetso, igisato c’amahēro gisa n’ikibengebenge, gifise imitwe ndwi n’amahembe cumi, no mu mitwe yaco cambaye imigāra ndwi." 
Revelation12:4 Umurizo waco ukwega ikigira gatatu c’inyenyeri zo kw ijuru, uzishiburira kw isi. Ico gisato gihagarara imbere y’uwo mugore agira avyare, kugira ngo ni yavyara kirotse umwana wiwe." 
Revelation12:5 Avyara umwana w’umuhungu, ni we azoragiza amahanga inkoni y’icuma. Umwana wiwe arasahurwa, ajanwa ku Mana no ku ntebe yayo." 
Revelation12:6 Umugore ahungira mu bugaragwa, ah’ afise ahantu yateguriwe n’Imana, kugira ngo bamugaburirireyo imisi igihumbi n’amajana abiri na mirongwitandatu." 
Revelation12:7 Mw ijuru havyuka intambara. Mikayeli n’abamarayika biwe barwanya ca gisato: igisato kirwanana n’abamarayika baco. 
Revelation12:8 Ntibatsinda, kandi mw ijuru ahabo ntihaba hakiboneka." 
Revelation12:9 Ca gisato c’amahēro kirakororwa, ni co ya nzoka ya mbere, yitwa Murwanizi, irindi ni Satani, ni co kizimiza abari kw isi bose, gikororerwa kw isi, abamarayika baco bakororanwa na co." 
Revelation12:10 Mw ijuru numva ijwi rirenga, riti Noneh’ agakiza karashitse, gashikanye n’ubushobozi n’ubgami bg’Imana yacu n’ububasha bga Kristo wayo: kuk’ Umurezi wa bene Data akororewe hasi, yahora abarega ku murango no mw ijoro imbere y’Imana yacu." 
Revelation12:11 Na bo bamuneshesheje amaraso y’Umwagazi w’Intama n’ijambo ryo gushinga intahe kwabo, ntibakunda amagara yabo, ntibanka no gupfa." 
Revelation12:12 Nuko noneho munezerwe mwa majuru, namwe abayabamwo. Ibara rizobonwa n’isi n’ikiyaga, kuk’ Umurwanizi yabamanukiye, ari n’inzigo nyinshi, azi kw afise igihe gito." 
Revelation12:13 Kandi ca gisato, kibonye yuko gikororewe kw isi, gihīga wa mugore yavyaye umuhungu." 
Revelation12:14 Umugore ahabga amababa abiri y’inkukuma nini, kugira ngw agurukire mu bugaragwa ahantu hiwe, ah’ agaburirirwa igihe n’ibihe n’igice c’igihe, arindwa ico kiyoka." 
Revelation12:15 Ico kiyoka gisendanisha amazi nk’uruzi avuye mu kanwa kaco inyuma y’uwo mugore kugira ngo kimutwaze uruzi. 
Revelation12:16 Isi itabara uwo mugore, yasamika akanwa kayo, imira uruzi ca gisato casendanishije." 
Revelation12:17 Ico gisato kigirira wa mugore inzigo, kirīgīra ngo kirwanye abo mu ruvyaro rwiwe basigaye, bitondera ivyagezwe n’Imana kandi bafise ibishingira Yesu intahe." 
Revelation13:1 Gihagarara ku musenyi wo ku kiyaga. Mbona igikōko ciburuka kiva mu kiyaga, gifise amahembe cumi n’imitwe ndwi: ku mahembe yaco hārih’ imigāra cumi, no ku mitwe yaco hārih’ amazina y’amarogotano." 
Revelation13:2 Ico gikōko nabonye casa n’ingwe, amajanja yaco yar’ ameze nk’ay’ idubu, akanwa kaco kari kameze nk’ak’ intambge. Ca gisato kigiha ububasha bgaco, no kuja ku ngoma yaco, n’ubutware buhambaye." 
Revelation13:3 Muri ya mitwe yaco mbonamw’ umwe usa n’ūkomeretse akagīrīre: uruguma rwocishe rurakira. Isi yose ikurikira ico gikōko bagitangarira. 
Revelation13:4 Batazira ico gisato bagisenga, kuko cahaye ico gikōko ububasha bgaco; batazira na kino gikōko bagisenga, bati Ni nde ahwanye n’iki gikōko, kandi ni nde ashobora kukirwanya?" 
Revelation13:5 Gihabga akanwa kavuga ibihambaye n’ivyo kurogota: gihabga n’ubushobozi bgo gushishikara amezi mirongwine n’abiri. 
Revelation13:6 Giteranura akanwa kaco kirogota ku Mana, kirogota no kw izina ryayo, no kw ihema ryayo, no ku baba mw ijuru." 
Revelation13:7 Gihabga kurwanya abera no kubanesha, kandi gihabga gutwara imiryango yose n’amoko yose n’indimi zose n’amahanga yose." 
Revelation13:8 Kand’ ababa kw isi bose bazogisenga, umuntu wese atanditswe izina mu gitabo c’ubugingo c’Umwagazi w’Intama yatanzwe kw ikimazi uhereye ku kuremwa kw’isi." 
Revelation13:9 Namba har’ umuntu ari n’ugutwi ni yumve. 
Revelation13:10 Namb’ umuntu yagerewe gufatwa mpiri azofatwa mpiri; namb’ umuntu yicisha inkota akwiye kuzokwicishwa inkota. Aho ni ho ukwihangana kw’abera guserukira bo n’ukwizera kwabo. 
Revelation13:11 Kandi mbona ikindi gikōko gisokorotse mw isi: gifise amahembe abiri nk’ay’ umwagazi w’intama, kivuga nk’igisato." 
Revelation13:12 Kiganzisha ububasha bgose bga ca gisato ca mbere mu maso yaco, kigōbēra isi n’abayibako gusenga ca gikōko ca mbere, cakize uruguma rwocishe." 
Revelation13:13 Kandi gikora ibimenyetso bihambaye, kimanura umuriro uva mw ijuru utibukira kw isi mu maso y’abantu." 
Revelation13:14 Kizimirisha ababa kw isi ibimenyetso cahawe gukorera mu maso ya ca gikōko, kibarira ababa kw isi gukora igishushanyo ca ca gikōko cari n’uruguma rw’inkota, kigahava kikabaho." 
Revelation13:15 Gihabga guha ico gishushanyo c’igikōko guhūmēka, ngw ico gishushanyo c’igikōko kivuge, kandi cicishe abatazogisenga bose." 
Revelation13:16 Kigera ko bose, aboroshe n’abahambaye, n’abatunzi n’aboro, n’abidegemvya n’abagurano, bashirwakw ikimenyetso ku kiganza c’i buryo canke mu ruhanga:" 
Revelation13:17 kandi ko hatagira umuntu yemererwa kugira ic’ agura cank’ ic’ ashōra, atar’ ūfise ico kimenyetso, ni co zina rya ca gikōko cank’ igitigiri c’izina ryaco." 
Revelation13:18 Aho ni ho ubgenge buserukira. Ūfise ubgenge n’aharūre igitigiri c’ico gikōko. N’igitigiri c’umuntu: igitigiri caco n’amajana atandatu na mirongwitandatu na gatandatu. 
Revelation14:1 Kandi mbona Umwagazi w’Intama, ahagaze ku musozi Siyoni, ahagararanye n’abantu ibihumbi ijana na mirongwine na bine, bafise izina ryiwe n’izina rya Se yanditswe mu ruhanga rwabo." 
Revelation14:2 Numva ijwi rivuye mw ijuru, nk’iry’ amazi menshi asūma, kandi nk’iry’ inkuba ituragara cane: kand’ iryo jwi numvise ryari rimeze nk’iry’ abacuraranzi bacuraranga inanga zabo." 
Revelation14:3 Baririmbira indirimbo nsha imbere ya ya ntebe y’ubgami, n’imbere ya vya binyabugingo bine na ba bakuru. Nta muntu yashoboye kwiga iyo ndirimbo atari bamwe ibihumbi ijana na mirongwine na bine, bācunguwe ngo bakūrwe mw isi." 
Revelation14:4 Abo ni bo batandujwe n’icitwa umugore, kuko bābaye nk’inkumi. Abo ni bo bakurikira wa Mwagazi ah’ aja hose. Abo bācunguwe mu bantu, kugira ngo babe umushuzo ku Mana no kuri wa Mwagazi." 
Revelation14:5 Kandi mu kanwa kabo ntihābonetsemw’ ikinyoma: nta gasembga bagira. 
Revelation14:6 Kandi mbona umumarayika wundi aguruka yātiriye ijuru, afise ubutumwa bgiza butazoshira bgo kubarira ababa kw isi n’amahanga yose n’imiryango yose n’indimi zose n’amoko yose." 
Revelation14:7 Avuga n’ijwi rirenga, ati Mwubahe Imana, muyihimbaze, kukw igihe c’amateka yayo gishitse, musenge iyaremye ijuru n’isi n’ikiyaga n’amasōko y’amazi." 
Revelation14:8 Umumarayika wundi wa kabiri akurikirirako, ati Kirakomvomvotse, kirakomvomvotse, Babuloni, ca gisagara gihambaye, cateretse amahanga yose vino ni yo burake bg’ubushakanyi bgaco." 
Revelation14:9 Umumarayika wundi wa gatatu akurikirirako, avuga n’ijwi rirenga, ati Ni hagira umuntu asenga ca gikōko n’igishushanyo caco, akemera gushirwakw ikimenyetso mu ruhanga canke ku kiganza," 
Revelation14:10 uwo na we azonywa kuri vino, ni yo burake bg’Imana, yiteguwe idafunguye mu gakarabo k’uburake bgayo. Kand’ azobabarizwa n’umuriro n’amazuku imbere y’abamarayika bera n’imbere ya wa Mwagazi." 
Revelation14:11 Umwotsi wo kubabazwa kwabo upfunduka ibihe bitazoshira, kandi ntibaruhuka ku murango no mw ijoro, abasenze ca gikōko n’igishushanyo caco, umuntu wese yemeye gushirwakw ikimenyetso c’izina ryaco." 
Revelation14:12 Aho ni ho ukwihangana kw’abera guserukira, bitondera ivyagezwe n’Imana n’ukwizera Yesu." 
Revelation14:13 Numva ijwi rivuye mw ijuru rimbgira, rit’ Andika, ut’ Uhereye none hahirwa abapfa bapfira mu Mwami. Kandi Mpwemu aravuga, at’ Ego me, ngo baruhuke ubutame bgabo, kukw ibikorwa vyabo bijana na bo bibakurikiye." 
Revelation14:14 Kandi mbona igicu cera; no kuri kino gicu ūkivyagiyeko, asa n’Umwana w’umuntu, yambaye igitsibo c’izahabu mu mutwe, kand’ afise umuhoro ukarishe mu kuboko." 
Revelation14:15 Umumarayika wundi ava mu rusengero, asemerera n’ijwi rirenga, abgira ūvyagiye kur’ ico gicu, ati N’urungike umuhoro wawe, wimbure, kukw iyimbura rishitse, kand’ ivyimburwa vyo mw isi vyumye." 
Revelation14:16 Ūvyagiye ku gicu arekurira umuhoro wiwe mw isi, isi irimburwa." 
Revelation14:17 Umumarayika wundi ava muri rwa rusengero rwo mw ijuru, na we nyene afise umuhoro ukarishe." 
Revelation14:18 Umumarayika wundi ava ku gicaniro, ni we aganza umuriro, asemerera n’ijwi rirenga, abarira ūfise umuhoro ukarishe, ati Rungika umuhoro wawe ukarishe, uce inzabibu zo ku muzabibu w’isi, kukw inzabibu zawo zirungurije." 
Revelation14:19 Umumarayika arekurira umuhoro wiwe mw isi, aca inzabibu z’umuzabibu w’isi, aziterera mu bgato bunini bg’ukuraka kw’Imana." 
Revelation14:20 Ubgo bgato buganishirizwamw’ ibirenge inyuma ya ca gisagara, amaraso ava mu bgato, ashitsa stadiyo igihumbi n’amajana atandatu, agera ku mijiginya y’amafarasi." 
Revelation15:1 Mbona ikindi kimenyetso mw ijuru gihambaye, gitangaza, abamarayika ndwi bafise ivyago ndwi, ni vyo vy’iherezo, kuko mur’ ivyo ari ho uburake bg’Imana buheraherezwa." 
Revelation15:2 Mbona igisa n’ikiyaga c’ibirahuri kivanze n’umuriro; mbona abatabarutse banesheje ca gikōko n’igishushanyo caco n’igitigiri c’izina ryaco, bahagaze kur’ ico kiyaga c’ibirahuri, bafise inanga z’Imana." 
Revelation15:3 Baririmba indirimbo ya Mose umusavyi w’Imana, n’indirimbo ya wa Mwagazi, bat’ Ibikorwa vyawe birahambaye kandi biratangaza, Mwami Mana ushobora vyose; inzira zawe n’iz’ ukugororoka n’ukuri, Mukama w’amahanga." 
Revelation15:4 Ni nde atazogutinya ga Mwami, cank’ atazohimbaza izina ryawe? Kukw ari wewe wenyene wera, amahanga yose azoza akwikubite imbere, agusenge, kukw amateka yawe agororotse aseruwe." 
Revelation15:5 Hanyuma y’ivyo mbona huguruka urusengero rw’ihema ry’Ibishinga intahe rwo mw ijuru," 
Revelation15:6 hasohoka ba bamarayika ndwi bava mur’ urwo rusengero bafise vya vyago ndwi, bambaye impuzu zera zitanduye, zikayangana, kandi bambaye imikanda y’izahabu mu gikiriza." 
Revelation15:7 Kimwe muri vya binyabugingo bine giha bano bamarayika ndwi inzavya ndwi z’izahabu, zuzuye uburake bg’Imana ibaho ibihe bitazoshira." 
Revelation15:8 Rwa rusengero rwuzura umwotsi uva mu bgiza bg’Imana no mu bushobozi bgayo, kandi nta washoboye kwinjira mur’ urwo rusengero, gushitsa aho vya vyago ndwi vy’abo bamarayika ndwi vyaheraherejwe." 
Revelation16:1 Numva ijwi rirenga rivuye muri rwa rusengero ribarira ba bamarayika ndwi, riti Ni mugende, musuke kw isi izo nzavya ndwi z’uburake bg’Imana." 
Revelation16:2 Uwa mbere aragenda, asuka urwavya rwiwe kw isi, abantu bafise ikimenyetso ca ca gikōko, bagasenga igishushanyo caco, bafatwa n’ibisebe bikomeye bibi." 
Revelation16:3 Uwa kabiri asuka urwavya rwiwe mu kiyaga, gicika amaraso nk’ay’ ūpfuye: ikintu cose co mu kiyaga kiri n’ubugingo kirapfa." 
Revelation16:4 Uwa gatatu asuka urwavya rwiwe mu nzūzi no mu masōko, bicika amaraso." 
Revelation16:5 Numva umumarayika w’amazi avuga, at’ Uragororotse, uriho kandi wamyeho, Uwera, kuk’ uciye iryo teka." 
Revelation16:6 Bavishije amaraso y’abera n’ay’ abavugishijwe nawe, kand’ amaraso nyene ni yo ubahaye ngo banywe: birababereye." 
Revelation16:7 Numva igicaniro kivuga, kit’ Ego me Mwami Mana ushobora vyose, amateka yawe n’ay’ ukuri n’ukugororoka." 
Revelation16:8 Uwa kane asuka urwavya rwiwe mu zuba. Rihabga kubaburisha abantu umuriro. 
Revelation16:9 Abantu bababurwa n’indugumba nyinshi, barogota kw izina ry’Imana igaba ivyo vyago, ntibihana ngo bayihimbaze." 
Revelation16:10 Uwa gatanu asuka urwavya rwiwe ku ntebe y’ubgami ya ca gikōko. Ubgami bgaco bucura umwiza, uburibge butuma bahekenya indimi zabo," 
Revelation16:11 kand’ uburibge bgabo n’ibisebe vyabo bituma barogota ku Mana Nyen’ ijuru, kandi ntibihana ngo bareke ibikorwa vyabo." 
Revelation16:12 Uwa gatandatu asuka urwavya rwiwe mu ruzi runini Efurate. Amazi yarwo arakama, kugira ngw inzira y’abami bava i burasirazuba yitegurwe." 
Revelation16:13 Kandi mbona mu kanwa ka ca gisato no mu kanwa ka ca gikōko no mu kanwa ka wa muvugishwa w’ibinyoma, havamw’ impwemu zitatu zihumanya, zisa n’ibikere:" 
Revelation16:14 kukw izo ar’ impwemu z’abadayimoni, zikora ibimenyetso, zija ku bami bo mw isi yose, ngo zibakoranirize ku ntambara yo ku musi uhambaye w’Imana ishobora vyose." 
Revelation16:15 (Ehe ndaza nk’igisuma. Hahirwa ūba maso, akazigama impuzu ziwe, ngo ntagende amēnya, bakabona isoni z’ubgambure bgiwe.)" 
Revelation16:16 Zibakoraniriza ahantu hitwa Haru‐Magedoni mu Giheburayo. 
Revelation16:17 Uw’ indwi asuka urwavya rwiwe mu kirere. Ijwi rirenga riva mu rusengero kuri ya ntebe, rivuga, riti Karabaye." 
Revelation16:18 Habah’ imiravyo n’amajwi n’imituragaro, habaho no gutigita kw’isi guhambaye; nta gutigita kunganya n’ukwo ubuhambazi no gukomera kwigeze kubaho, uhereye ah’ abantu bākabereye kw isi." 
Revelation16:19 Ca gisagara gihambaye kigabanywamwo gutatu, ibisagara vy’abanyamahanga birasenyuka. I Babuloni hahambaye hibukwa imbere y’Imana, ngo hahabge agakarabo ka vino y’uburake bgayo bg’inkazi." 
Revelation16:20 Ibizinga vyo mu kiyaga vyose birahunga, kand’ imisozi ntiyasubira kuboneka." 
Revelation16:21 Urubura ruhambaye, ibuye rimwe ryarwo ririvye nk’italanto, rukoragurikira ku bantu ruvuye mw ijuru: ico cago c’urubura gituma abantu barogota ku Mana, kukw icago carwo gikomeye cane." 
Revelation17:1 Haza umwe wo muri ba bamarayika ndwi bari bafise za nzavya ndwi, avugana nanje, arambgira, ati Ngwino nkwereke iteka rizocirwa maraya w’agahebuza, yicaye kw iteraniro ry’amazi menshi." 
Revelation17:2 Uyo abami bo kw isi bāsambana na we, ababa kw isi bakaborerwa vino, ni zo busambanyi bgiwe." 
Revelation17:3 Anjana mu bugaragwa ndi muri Mpwemu. Mbona umugore yicaye ku gikōko gisa n’agahama, cuzuye amazina y’amarogotano, gifise imitwe ndwi n’amahembe cumi." 
Revelation17:4 Uwo mugore yambaye impuzu y’inyambarabami n’iy’ agahama, yari yisakaye izahabu n’utubuyenge tw’igiciro kinini n’imaragarita, afise igikombe c’izahabu mu minwe cuzuye ibihumanya n’imyanda y’ubusambanyi bgiwe." 
Revelation17:5 Mu ruhanga afise izina ry’akabanga, ryanditswe ngo BABULONI HAHAMBAYE, NYINA WA BA MARAYA, KANDI NYINA W’IBIHUMANYA VYO MW ISI." 
Revelation17:6 Kandi mbona uwo mugore aborewe amaraso y’abera n’amaraso y’abashingiye intahe ivya Yesu. Ndamubonye birantangaza ndumirwa rwose. 
Revelation17:7 Umumarayika arambaza, ati N’iki kigutangaje? Ndakubgira akabanga k’uriya mugore n’ak’ igikōko agenderako gifise imitwe ndwi n’amahembe cumi." 
Revelation17:8 Igikōko ubonye cariho kandi ntikikiriho, kandi kigira kidūge kive i kuzimu, kije kuranduka. Kand’ ababa kw isi batanditswe amazina yabo mu gitabo c’ubugingo, uhereye ku kuremwa kw’isi, bazotangara babonye ico gikōko yuko cariho kandi kitakiriho, kandi kizoboneka." 
Revelation17:9 Aha ni ho umutima w’ubgenge userukira. Imitwe ndwi, iyo ni yo misozi ndwi uwo mugore yicayeko." 
Revelation17:10 Kandi ni yo bami ndwi: abatanu bārakombowe, umwe ariho, uwundi we ntaraza, kandi ni yaza azoba ar’ uwo kumara igihe gito." 
Revelation17:11 Kandi ca gikōko, cariho kandi kitakiriho, ico ubgaco n’ūgira umunani, ariko kandi n’umwe muri ba bandi ndwi, kand’ azoja kuranduka." 
Revelation17:12 Kand’ amahembe cumi wabonye ni yo bami cumi batarīma, ariko bahabga kuganziriza hamwe na ca gikōko nk’abami nyene, kumara isaha imwe." 
Revelation17:13 Abo bahūza inama, baha ca gikōko ububasha bgabo n’ubutware bgabo." 
Revelation17:14 Abo bazorwanya Umwagazi w’Intama, uwo Mwagazi azobanesha, kukw ari we aganza abaganza n’Umwami w’abami, kand’ abari kumwe na we, bāhamagawe, bātoranijwe, bāyobotse, na bo bazobanesha." 
Revelation17:15 Arambgira, ati Ya mazi wabonye, maraya yicarako, ni yo moko n’amakungu y’abantu n’amahanga n’indimi." 
Revelation17:16 Ya mahembe cumi wabonye na ca gikōko bizokwanka uwo maraya, bizomuzingazinga, bimukobe, birye inyama ziwe, bimutongoze umuriro." 
Revelation17:17 Kukw Imana yashize mu mitima yabo gukora ivyo yagabiye, no guhūza inama, no gushira ca gikōko ku ngoma yabo, kugeza ah’ amajambo y’Imana azoshikira." 
Revelation17:18 Umugore wabonye ni we ca gisagara gihambaye, kiganza abami bo kw isi." 
Revelation18:1 Hanyuma y’ivyo mbona umumarayika wundi, amanuka avuye mw ijuru, afise ubutware buhambaye, isi ibonesherezwa n’ubgiza bgiwe." 
Revelation18:2 Asemerera n’ijwi rirenga, ati Kirakomvomvotse, kirakomvomvotse, Babuloni ca gisagara gihambaye, gicitse ikibanza c’abadayimoni, aharindirwa impwemu zihumanya zose, aharindirwa ibisīga bihumanya vyankwa vyose." 
Revelation18:3 Kukw amahanga yose yanyoye vino, ni zo burake bg’ubusambanyi bgiwe, kand’ abami bo kw isi bāsambana na we, abadandaza bo kw isi bātungishwa n’ubginshi bg’ibihinda vyiwe." 
Revelation18:4 Numva ijwi rindi rivuye mw ijuru, rivuga, riti Bantu banje, ni muve i we, kugira ngo mwoye gufatanya n’ivyaha vyiwe, mwoye guhabga ku vyago vyiwe." 
Revelation18:5 Kukw ivyaha vyiwe vyārundanijwe bigashika kw ijuru, kand’ Imana yibutse ukugabitanya kwiwe." 
Revelation18:6 Mumugirire ibihwanye n’ivyo yagiriye abandi, mumugerere kabiri ibikwiranye n’ivyo yakoze. Mu gakarabo yavangiyemwo, mumuvangiremwo kabiri." 
Revelation18:7 Nk’uko yihimbaza, akīgirira ibihinda, abe ari ko mumuha kubabazwa agashinyaguro no kuboroga. Kuko yibgira mu mutima, ngo Mvyagiye nd’umwamikazi, sind’ umupfakazi, sinzobona amaborogo n’akazirukanyo:" 
Revelation18:8 ni co gituma ivyago vyiwe vyose bizoza ku musi umwe, urupfu n’amaborogo n’amapfa, kand’ azotongozwa umuriro: kuk’ Umwami Imana amuciriyekw iteka ar’ uw’ ubushobozi." 
Revelation18:9 Kand’ abami bo kw isi, abāsambana na we, bagasangira na we ibihinda vyiwe, bazomuririra, bamuvugirize amarūru, aho bazobonera umwotsi wo kuyigizwa kwiwe," 
Revelation18:10 bahagaritswe kure no gutinya ugushinyagurirwa kwiwe, bati N’ibara, n’ibara, ewe wa gisagara gihambaye, Babuloni, wa gisagara c’inkomezi, kuko mw isaha imwe iteka uciriweko rigushikiriye!" 
Revelation18:11 N’abadandaza bo kw isi barakiririra, barakiborogera, kukw ata wukibagurira ibishōrano vyabo bizanwa mu bgato;" 
Revelation18:12 ibishōrano vy’izahabu n’ifeza n’utubuyenge tw’igiciro kinini, n’imaragarita, n’impuzu zera nziza, n’iz’ inyambarabami, na hariri, n’iz’ agahama, n’imbaho zose zimota neza, n’imbombovu zose z’ibintu vyabājwe mu mahembe y’inzovu, n’imbombovu zose z’ibintu vyabājwe mu biti vyiza vy’igiciro kinini, n’ivyacuzwe mu miringa, no mu butare, n’ivyabājwe mw ibuye ryitwa marimari," 
Revelation18:13 n’ibisosa vyitwa mudarasini, n’imbazi, n’imibavu, n’amavuta amota neza, n’isenga, na vino, n’amavuta ya elayo, n’ifu isetse neza, n’ingano, n’inka, n’intama, n’amafarasi, n’imikogote, n’imibiri y’abantu n’ubugingo bgabo." 
Revelation18:14 (Kand’ iyera ry’ukwifuza kw’ umutima wawe rirakuvuyeko; n’ibintu vyose biryoshe n’ibirābika neza biguhonnyeko, ntibazobibona ukundi.)" 
Revelation18:15 Abāshōra ivyo, batungishijwe n’ico gisagara, bazohagarikwa kure no gutinya ugushinyagurirwa kwaco, barira baboroga," 
Revelation18:16 bati N’ibara, n’ibara, ca gisagara gihambaye, cambaye impuzu zera nziza n’iz’ inyambarabami n’iz’ agahama, kandi cisakaye izahabu n’utubuyenge tw’ igiciro kinini n’imaragarita," 
Revelation18:17 kuk’ ubutunzi bungaho bukomvomvotse mw isaha imwe! Kandi nyen’ ubgato wese, n’umuntu wese ajabukirizwa mu bgato ahantu hose, n’abasoza, n’abatunzwe n’ikiyaga, bari bahagaze kure," 
Revelation18:18 kandi bakirāba umwotsi wo kuyigizwa kwaco barataka, bati N’ikihe cari gihwanye na kiriya gisagara gihambaye?" 
Revelation18:19 Biyorera imikungugu ku mitwe, bataka barira baboroga, bati N’ibara, n’ibara, ca gisagara gihambaye, catungishije ubutunzi bgaco abafise amato yabo mu kiyaga bose, kuko cakomvowe mw isaha imwe!" 
Revelation18:20 Ni biguhimbare, wa juru, namwe abera n’intumwa n’abavugishwa n’Imana, kukw Imana igiciriyekw iteka, igihōra mwebge." 
Revelation18:21 Umumarayika w’inkomezi araha ikibuye kimeze nk’igisyo kinini, agita mu kiyaga, at’ Uko ni ko Babuloni igisagara gihambaye kizotererwa kigenda imivuguvugu, kandi ntikizosubira kuboneka ukundi." 
Revelation18:22 Ntihazokwumvikana ukundi muri wewe ijwi ry’abacuraranzi n’iry’ abaririmvyi, n’iry’ abavuza imyironge n’iry’ abavuza inzamba; kandi nta muhinga w’umunyabuhinga bgose agisubira kuboneka muri wewe ukundi, kand’ ukuvuga kw’urusyo ntikugisubira kwumvikana muri wewe ukundi." 
Revelation18:23 Kand’ ukumurika kw’itara ntikugisubira kubonesha muri wewe ukundi, kand’ ijwi ry’umukwe n’iry’ umugeni ntirigisubira kwumvikana muri wewe ukundi. Abadandaza bawe bār’ abahambaye bo kw isi, kukw amahanga yose yahendahenzwe n’uburozi bgawe." 
Revelation18:24 Kandi mur’ ico gisagara amaraso y’abavugishwa n’Imana n’ay’ abera n’ay’ abishwe bo kw isi bose ni ho yabonetse. 
Revelation19:1 Hanyuma y’ivyo numva mw ijuru ikimeze nk’ijwi rirenga ry’ishengero ryinshi, riti Haleluya; agakiza n’ubgiza n’ububasha n’ivy’ Imana yacu," 
Revelation19:2 kukw amateka yayo ar’ay’ ukuri n’ukugororoka. Yaciriyekw iteka umwe maraya w’agahebuza, yononesha abari mw isi ubusambanyi bgiwe, kand’ imuhōye amaraso y’abagurano bayo." 
Revelation19:3 Rivuga ubugira kabiri, riti Haleluya. Kand’ umwotsi wiwe upfunduka ibihe bitazoshira." 
Revelation19:4 Ba bakuru mirongwibiri na bane na vya binyabugingo bine vyikubita hasi, bisenga Imana ivyagira kuri ya ntebe, biti Amen; Haleluya." 
Revelation19:5 Ijwi riva kur’ iyo ntebe rivuga, riti Ni mushime Imana yacu, yemwe mwese abagurano bayo, abayubaha, aboroshe n’abakomeye." 
Revelation19:6 Numva ikimeze nk’ijwi ry’ishengero rinini, n’ikimeze nk’ugusūma kw’amazi menshi, n’ikimeze nk’ijwi ry’imituragaro ihambaye, kivuga, kiti Haleluya, kuk’ Umwami Imana yacu ishobora vyose ihangamye." 
Revelation19:7 Tunezerwe, duhimbarwe, tuyihe icubahiro, kuk’ ubukwe bga wa Mwagazi w’Intama bushitse, umugeni wiwe ariteguye." 
Revelation19:8 Kandi yahawe kwambara impuzu zera nziza, zikayangana, zitanduye; izo mpuzu zera nziza ni zo bikorwa vyo kugororoka vy’abera." 
Revelation19:9 Umumarayika arambarira, at’ Andika, uti Hahirwa abatorewe gutaha ubukwe bga wa Mwagazi. Kand’ arambarira, at’ Ayo n’amajambo y’ukuri y’Imana." 
Revelation19:10 Nikubitishwa hasi imbere y’ibirenge vyiwe no kumusenga. Arambarira, at’ Oya sigaho; nd’umugurano mugenzawe, kandi ndi mugenzi wa bene So bafise ivyo gushingira intahe Yesu: Imana ba ari yo usenga. Kukw abashingira intahe Yesu baba bavugishwa na Mpwemu." 
Revelation19:11 Mbona ijuru ryuguruye, kandi mbona ifarasi y’igitare, ūyivyagiyeko yitwa Mwizigirwa, irindi ni Munyakuri. Aca amateka akarwana intambara mu bugororotsi." 
Revelation19:12 Inyonga ziwe n’imbeya z’umuriro, no mu mutwe yambaye imigāra myinshi, kand’ afise izina ryanditswe, nta wurizi atari we wenyene." 
Revelation19:13 Yambaye impuzu zājobetswe mu maraso, kandi yitwa Jambo w’Imana." 
Revelation19:14 Ingabo zo mw ijuru ziramukurikira, zicaye ku mafarasi y’ibitare, zambaye impuzu nziza zera derere, zitanduye." 
Revelation19:15 Mu kanwa kiwe havamw’ inkota ikarishe, kugira ngw ayikubite amahanga: azoyaragiza inkoni y’icuma. Kand’ aganishiriza ibirenge mu bgato vino y’uburake bg’inkazi bg’Imana ishobora vyose." 
Revelation19:16 Kandi ku mpuzu ziwe no ku kibero, afise izina ryanditsweko, ng’ UMWAMI W’ABAMI, ŪGANZA ABAGANZA." 
Revelation19:17 Mbona umumarayika ahagaze ku zuba; asemerera n’ijwi rirenga, abarira ibisīga vyose biguruka vyātiriye ijuru, ati Ni muze mukoranire amazimano menshi y’Imana," 
Revelation19:18 ngo murye inyama z’abami n’iz’ abakuru b’abagabisha b’abasoda n’iz’ abahizi n’iz’ amafarasi n’iz’ abayicarako n’iz’ abantu bose, abidegemvya n’abagurano, aboroshe n’abahambaye." 
Revelation19:19 Mbona ca gikōko n’abami bo kw isi n’ingabo zabo bakoraniye kurwanya ūvyagiye kuri ya farasi n’ingabo ziwe. 
Revelation19:20 Ico gikōko gifatwa mpiri, bo na wa muvugishwa w’ibinyoma, yakorera vya bimenyetso mu maso yaco, akabizimirisha abemeye gushirwakw ikimenyetso ca ca gikōko n’abasenga igishushanyo caco. Vyompi bitererwa bibona mu kiyaga caka umuriro n’amazuku." 
Revelation19:21 Abasigaye bicishwa inkota y’ūvyagiye kuri ya farasi, imwe ivuye mu kanwa kiwe. Ibisīga vyose bifunereza inyama zavyo." 
Revelation20:1 Mbona umumarayika amanuka avuye mw ijuru, afise urupfunguzo rw’i kuzimu, afise n’ikinyororo mu minwe." 
Revelation20:2 Afata ca gisato, ni co ya nzoka ya mbere, ni yo Murwanizi irindi ni Satani, akiboha ngo kimare imyaka igihumbi," 
Revelation20:3 agikororera i kuzimu, arahadadira, ashirakw ikimenyetso kikirumanya, kugira ngo nticongere kuzimiza amahanga, gushitsa ah’ iyo myaka igihumbi izoshirira: ni yashira gikwiye kubohorwa ngo kimare igihe gito." 
Revelation20:4 Mbona intebe z’ubgami, mbona abicara kuri zo, bahabga ubucamanza. Kandi mbona ubugingo bg’abaciwe amazosi, babahōra gushingira intahe Yesu, n’ijambo ry’Imana, ni bo batāsenze ca gikōko cank’ igishushanyo caco, kandi ntibemeye gushirwa ikimenyetso caco mu ruhanga canke ku kiganza. Baba bazima, bafatanya na Kristo kuganza imyaka igihumbi." 
Revelation20:5 Abapfuye bandi ntibaba bazima iyo myaka igihumbi itarashira. Ukwo ni kwo kuzuka kwa mbere. 
Revelation20:6 Ūri mu mugabane wo kuzuka kwa mbere arahiriwe kandi n’uwera. Urupfu rwa kabiri ntirugira ububasha ku bameze bartyo, ariko bazoba abaherezi b’Imana na Kristo, kandi bazofatanya na we kuganza, iyo myaka igihumbi." 
Revelation20:7 Kand’ iyo myaka igihumbi ni yashira, Satani azorekurwa ngw ave mw ibohero," 
Revelation20:8 azosokoroka aje kuzimiza amahanga yo mu mfuruka zine z’isi, Gogi na Magogi, kugira ngw ayakoranirize hamwe ku ntambara, igitigiri cabo ni nk’umusenyi wo ku kiyaga." 
Revelation20:9 Baradūga bakwira isi yose, bakikiza ah’ ingabo z’abera zishagaje, na ca gisagara gikundwa. Umuriro uratibuka uvuye mw ijuru, urabarigata." 
Revelation20:10 Kand’ Umurwanizi yabazimiza atererwa muri ca kiyaga caka umuriro n’amazuku, kirimwo na ca gikōko na wa muvugishwa w’ibinyoma, bazobabazwa ku murango no mw ijoro ibihe bitazoshira." 
Revelation20:11 Mbona intebe niniya yera, mbona n’Iyivyagiyeko, isi n’ijuru bihunga mu nyonga hayo, aho vyahora ntihaba hakiboneka." 
Revelation20:12 Mbona abapfuye, abahambaye n’aboroshe, bahagaze imbere y’iyo ntebe; ibitabo birazingururwa. Kand’ ikindi gitabo kirazingururwa, ni co gitabo c’ubugingo. Abapfuye bacirwa imanza z’ivyanditswe mur’ ivyo bitabo, zikwiranye n’ivyo bakoze." 
Revelation20:13 Ikiyaga kigarukana abapfuye bo muri co, urupfu n’i kuzimu bigarukana abapfuye bo muri vyo, bacirwa imanza zikwiranye n’ivy’ umuntu wese yakoze." 
Revelation20:14 Rupfu na Kuzimu batererwa muri ca kiyaga caka umuriro. Ico kiyaga caka umuriro ni co rupfu rwa kabiri. 
Revelation20:15 Kand’ umuntu wese atabonetse ko yanditswe muri ca gitabo c’ubugingo atererwa mur’ ico kiyaga caka umuriro. 
Revelation21:1 Mbona ijuru risha n’isi nsha: kukw ijuru rya mbere n’isi ya mbere vyari vyagiye, n’ikiyaga nticari kikiriho." 
Revelation21:2 Mbona umurwa wera, Yerusalemu musha, wururuka uva mw ijuru ku Mana, witeguwe nk’uk’ umugeni asharizwa umugabo wiwe." 
Revelation21:3 Numva ijwi rirenga, rivuye kuri ya ntebe, rit’ Eh’ ihema ry’Imana riri kumwe n’abantu, kand’ izogerēra muri bo, na bo bazoba abantu bayo, kand’ Imana ubgayo izobana na bo, izoba Imana yabo." 
Revelation21:4 Izohanagura amosozi yose ku maso yabo, kand’ urupfu ntiruzoba rukiriho, kand’ amaborogo no gutaka n’uburibge ntibizoba bikiriho: kukw ivya mbere bishize." 
Revelation21:5 Īvyagira kuri ya ntebe iravuga, iti Rāba vyose ndabihindura bisha. Kand’ it’ Andika, kukw ayo majambo ar’ ayo kwizerwa n’ay’ ukuri." 
Revelation21:6 Kand’ irambarira, iti Karabaye. Ndi Alufa na Omega, itanguriro n’iherezo. Ūfise inyota nzomuha kunywa kw isōko y’amazi y’ubugingo ku buntu." 
Revelation21:7 Ūnesha azoragwa ivyo, nanje nzoba Imana yiwe, na we azoba umwana wanje." 
Revelation21:8 Arikw ibijora, n’abatizera, n’abakora ibizira, n’abicanyi, n’abashakanyi, n’abarozi, n’abasenga ibigirwamana, n’abanyabinyoma bose, umugabane wabo uzoba mu kiyaga caka umuriro n’amazuku, ni co rupfu rwa kabiri." 
Revelation21:9 Haza umwe wo muri ba bamarayika ndwi, bari bafise za nzavya ndwi zuzuye ivyago ndwi vy’iherezo, avugana nanje arambgira, ati Ngwino nkwereke umugeni, umugore wa wa Mwagazi." 
Revelation21:10 Anjana ku musozi munini muremure ndi muri Mpwemu, anyereka umurwa wera Yerusalemu, wururuka uva mw ijuru ku Mana," 
Revelation21:11 ufise ubgiza bg’Imana. Ugukayangana kwawo gusa n’ukw’ ibuye ry’akabuyenge ry’igiciro kinini cane, nk’akabuyenge kitwa yasipi, kabonerana nk’icirore," 
Revelation21:12 uzigujwe n’urugo runini rurerure rufise ibirimba cumi na bibiri, no mu birimba harih’ abamarayika cumi na babiri, kandi hār’ amazina yanditsweko, ni yo y’imiryango cumi n’ibiri y’Abisirayeli." 
Revelation21:13 Ahahera i burasirazuba har’ ibirimba bitatu; ahahera i burārūko har’ ibirimba bitatu; ahahera i bumanuko har’ ibirimba bitatu; ahahera i burengerazuba har’ ibirimba bitatu. 
Revelation21:14 Urugo ruziguje uwo murwa rufise amatanguriro cumi n’abiri, yanditswekw amazina cumi n’abiri y’intumwa cumi na zibiri za wa Mwagazi." 
Revelation21:15 Uwavugana nanje yar’ afise irenga ry’izahabu ry’ikigeresho, kugira ngw agere uwo murwa n’ibirimba vyawo n’urugo rwawo." 
Revelation21:16 Uwo murwa ungana impande zose, uburebure bungana n’ubgaguke. Ageresha uwo murwa rya renga, ageramwo stadiyo ibihumbi cumi na bibiri: uburebure bg’umurambararo n’ubgaguke n’uburebure bg’igihagararo birangana." 
Revelation21:17 Agera urugo rwawo, rushikana amatambge ijana na mirongwine n’ane, y’ukuboko uciriye mu nkokora, nk’ukw itambge ritambishwa ukuboko kw’umuntu ringana, ni kw iry’ umumarayika ringana." 
Revelation21:18 Urugo rwawo rwubakishijwe yasipi, umurwa war’ izahabu ishize inkamba imeze nk’ibirahuri bishize inkamba nyene." 
Revelation21:19 Amatanguriro y’urugo rwa wa murwa yar’ asharijwe n’amabuye y’amoko yose y’utubuyenge tw’igiciro kinini. Ibuye ry’itanguriro rya mbere ryari yasipi, irya kabiri ryari safiro, irya gatatu ryari kalukedoni, irya kane ryari simaragido," 
Revelation21:20 irya gatanu ryari sarudonikisi, irya gatandatu ryari sarudiyo, iry’ indwi ryari kirusolito, iry’ umunani ryari berulo, iry’ icenda ryari topazi, iry’ icumi ryari kirusopuraso, iry’ icumi na rimwe ryari huwakinto, iry’ icumi na kabiri ryari ametusito." 
Revelation21:21 Kand’ ibirimba, ukw ar’ icumi na bibiri, vyar’ imaragarita cumi na zibiri: ikirimba kimwe cubakishijwe imaragarita imwe, birtyo birtyo. Irango rya wa murwa ryar’ izahabu nziza, isa n’ibirahuri bibonerana." 
Revelation21:22 Kandi sinabonye urusengero kuri wo, kuk’ Umwami Imana ishobora vyose na wa Mwagazi ari bo rusengero rwawo." 
Revelation21:23 Kandi wa murwa nturinda kwākirwa n’izuba canke n’ukwezi, kuk’ ubgiza bg’Imana ari bgo buwākira, kandi wa Mwagazi ari we tara ryawo." 
Revelation21:24 Kand’ amahanga azogendera mu muco wawo, abami bo kw isi bazozanay’ ubgiza bgabo." 
Revelation21:25 Ibirimba vyawo ntibijishwa na rimwe, kukw ata joro ribayo." 
Revelation21:26 Kandi bazozanay’ ubgiza n’icubahiro vy’amahanga. 
Revelation21:27 Kandi kuri wo nta ho hazogera ikintu gihumanya, cank’ ūkora ibizira akabesha, atar’ abanditswe mu gitabo c’ubugingo ca wa Mwagazi w’Intama." 
Revelation22:1 Anyereka uruzi rw’amazi y’ubugingo, rubonerana nk’icirore, ruva ku ntebe y’Imana na wa Mwagazi." 
Revelation22:2 Hagati y’irango rya wa murwa, hakurya no hakuno y’urwo ruzi harih’ igiti c’ubugingo, cera icumi na kabiri mu mwaka, kikera rimwe‐rimwe uk’ ukwezi gutashe. Ibibabi vyaco vyar’ ivyo kuvūra amahanga." 
Revelation22:3 Nta muvumo uzoba ukiriho. Intebe y’Imana na wa Mwagazi izoba muri wa murwa, abagurano bayo bazokwama bashashe," 
Revelation22:4 bazorāba mu nyonga hayo, izina ryayo rizokwandikwa mu ruhanga rwabo." 
Revelation22:5 Nta joro rizoba rikiriho, kandi ntibazorinda kubonesherezwa n’itara canke kwākirwa n’izuba, kuk’ Umwami Imana ari yo izobākira, kandi bazoba abami ibihe bitazoshira." 
Revelation22:6 Arambarira, at’ Ayo majambo n’ayo kwizerwa n’ay’ ukuri, kand’ Umwami, ni yo Mana igera impwemu z’abavugishwa na yo, yatumye umumarayika wiwe kwereka abagurano biwe ibigira bibeho vuba." 
Revelation22:7 Kand’ ehe ndaza vuba. Hahirwa uwitondera amajambo yavugishijwe yo mur’ iki gitabo. 
Revelation22:8 Ni jewe Yohana numvise ivyo, ndavyibonera. Mmaze kuvyumva no kubibona, nikubita hasi imbere y’ibirenge vy’umumarayika anyeretse ivyo, ngira ndamusenge." 
Revelation22:9 Arambarira, at’ Oya sigaho; nd’umugurano mugenzawe, kandi ndi mugenzi wa bene So, abavugishwa n’Imana, n’uw’ abitondera amajambo y’iki gitabo. Imana ba ari yo usenga." 
Revelation22:10 Kand’ arambarira, ati Ntumatanishe ishashara n’ikimenyetso amajambo avugishijwe n’Imana yo mur’ iki gitabo; kukw igihe kiri hafi." 
Revelation22:11 Ūgabitanya n’ashishikare agabitanye; uwanduye mu mutima n’ashishikare yandure; ūgororotse n’ashishikare agororoke; uwera n’ashishikare yezwe. 
Revelation22:12 Ehe ndaza vuba, nzanye ingero, kugira ngo ngerere umuntu wese ibikwiranye n’ivyo yakoze." 
Revelation22:13 Ndi Alufa na Omega, uwa mbere n’uwa nyuma, itanguriro n’iherezo." 
Revelation22:14 Hahirwa abamesura imvune zabo, kugira ngo babone kwēgēra ca giti c’ubugingo, kandi bace mu birimba bashike kuri wa murwa." 
Revelation22:15 Inyuma hazoba imbga n’abarozi n’abashakanyi n’abicanyi n’abasenga ibigirwamana, n’umuntu wese akunda kubesha akabikora." 
Revelation22:16 Jewe Yesu ntumye umumarayika wanje gushingira intahe mwebge ivyo, kubg’ amashengero. Ni jewe munago wo ku gishitsi ca Dawidi, nd’ umwuzukuruza wiwe, kandi nd’ ikinyenyeri gica ibibatsi co mu gaturuturu." 
Revelation22:17 Kandi Mpwemu bo na wa mugeni barahamagara, bati Ngwino. Kand’ uwumva n’ahamagare, ati Ngwino. Kand’ ūfise inyota n’aze, ūgomba ni yākīre amazi y’ubugingo ku buntu." 
Revelation22:18 Uwumva wese amajambo yavugishijwe yo mur’ iki gitabo ndabishingira intahe kuri we, nti Ni hagira umuntu azokwungurira kuri yo, Imana izomwunguka ivyago vyanditswe mur’ iki gitabo." 
Revelation22:19 Kandi ni hagira umuntu akūra ku majambo y’igitabo c’ibi vyavugishijwe na yo, Imana izomukūra ku mugabane wa ca giti c’ubugingo no ku wa wa murwa wera, vyanditswe mur’ iki gitabo." 
Revelation22:20 Ūshingira intahe ivyo, aravuga, at’ Ego me, ndaza vuba. Amen, urakaza, Mwami Yesu."
